<pb n="001"/>
<p>ṛjuvimalā-pañcikā</p>
<p><q>dravyāṇām</q> । atraivamākṣipati-yadi vṛttena saha saṃbandho'sti tadā'sau
kimiti na kīrtitaḥ । atha na tadā'sminneva sthāne kimityadhikāralakṣaṇasyārambha
ityanenābhiprāyeṇāha---<q>atha vṛttena saha saṃbandhakathanaṃ kimityatra tu na
kriyate</q> । sarvatra kṛtasya sambandhakathanasyātrākaraṇe heturvarṇanīya ityarthaḥ । uttaraṃ---
<q>sambandhābhāvāditi brūmaḥ</q> । kathaṃ tarhyasminneva sthāne adhikāralakṣaṇārambhaḥ ?
ata āha---<q>pañcalakṣaṇāpekṣo hyadhikāraḥ</q> pañcānāṃ pramāṇādīnāṃ lakṣaṇamapekṣate
adhikāraḥcintāprārambhāya na punaravagataya iti । āśayamabuddhvā codayati---<q>pañcalakṣa-
ṇāpekṣe hyapekṣā । evaṃ tarhi pañcāpi kīrtanīyāni</q> । pramāṇabhedaviniyo-
gopādānakramalakṣaṇaṃ vṛttaṃ idānīmadhikāralakṣaṇaṃ vartayiṣyāmaḥ ityevaṃ pañcāpi
kīrtanīyāni । pariharati---<q>na kīrtanīyāni</q> । evaṃ tarhi yasmāttairapi pratyekaṃ
saṃbandho nopapadyate । viniyogopādānakramāstāvat adhikārāpekṣā eva1 । grāhaka-
<note>1. pekṣaiva - mā.</note>﻿
<pb n="002"/>
pūrvako viniyogaḥ parārthe neṣyate । tathā sādhikārasya vidherutpattiviniyoga-
prayogākṣepaḥ । adhikārākṣepastu siddhe sati adhikāralakṣaṇasaṃbandhe bhavati iti
vakṣyāmaḥ । kramaḥ punaḥ prayuktyuttarakālabhāvī । adhikārapūrvakaḥ śās‍trabhedo'pi
nādhikāraṃ prati hetuḥ । abhinne'pi śāstrārthe śabdato'dhikārāvagateḥ । nanvabhinne'pi
śāstrārthe'nuṣṭhānasāmarthyābhāvādadhikāro nopapadyate । satyam । tathāpyadhikārapūrvakaḥ
śāstrabhedo'pi lakṣaṇasaṃbandhaśarīrāvagatiḥ śabdata eva bhavati । yadi paraṃ śāstrabhedaṃ
vinā na nirvahati anuṣṭhānaparyantatvādadhikārasyeti nirvāhe hetuḥ śāstrabhedaḥ adhi-
kārasyāvagame tu śabda eva hetuḥ । tathā pramāṇalakṣaṇamapi nādhikāraṃ prati,
sāpekṣe'pi hetuśabde <quote>‘devadatta gāmānaya’</quote> ityādiṣvadhikāradarśanāt । ataḥ pratyekaṃ
pañcabhirapi saṃbandho nopapadyate । nanvevaṃ samuditaiḥ saṃbandho bhaviṣyati tatrāha---
<q>na ca samudāyo nāma kaś‍cidarthāntarabhūto vidyate</q> । yadi samudāyo'rthāntara-
bhūto vidyate tadā pratyekamasaṃbandhe'pi kadācit samudāyenāpi saṃbandhaḥ saṃbhāvyeta ।
na caitadasti । tasmāt pañcānāmapi kīrtanaṃ nopapadyate । <q>yadi pañcabhirapi sambandho
nāsti kathaṃ tarhi pañcalakṣaṇāpekṣo hyadhikāra ityucyate । uttaraṃ---paraspa-
rāpekṣeṣu pañcasu parisamāpteṣu adhikārasyāvasara iti pañcalakṣaṇāpekṣo hyadhikāra
ityucyate । na punarhetutaḥ</q> । asyāyamarthaḥ---adhītavedasya prathamaṃ tāvat vedārthaji-
jñāsaivotpadyate । ataḥ codanālakṣaṇo'rtho dharma ityanena codanaikapramāṇakaḥ kāryarūpo
vedārtha ityukte punariyamapekṣā jāyate-kathamanapekṣā codanā pramāṇaṃ ? yena codanaika-
lakṣaṇa[ḥ/?/]kāryarūpo vedārtho bhavet iti । tataścānapekṣatvasādhakaṃ pramāṇalakṣaṇamārabdha-
vyam । ukte ca pramāṇalakṣaṇe punariyamapekṣā jāyate-kiṃ tatpramāṇaṃ bhinnamutābhinna-
miti । ataḥ dvitīyādhyāyena śāstrabhedaḥ pratipādyate । pratipādite ca śāstrabhede
śāstrārthā api bhinnāḥ । tatreyamapekṣā punarāpatati-kimete śāstrārthāḥ anyonya-
saṃbaddhā uta asaṃbaddhā iti tatra śeṣalakṣaṇena saṃbandhaḥ pratipādyate । pratipādite ca
śrutyādinibandhane śāstrārthānāṃ parasparasaṃbandhe punariyamapekṣopajāyate---kiṃ śrutyādi-﻿
<pb n="003"/>
bhireva parasparasaṃbandhaḥ utāparamapyasti kāraṇamasya ? tatropādānalakṣaṇaṃ aparamapi
kāraṇamiti tatpratipādanāya upādānalakṣaṇamārabdhavyam । aupādānikaviniyoga-
cintāyāṃ ca prakṛtāyāṃ aparamapyaupādānikaṃ sarvameva cintitam । upādānanibandha-
nāyāṃ ca prayuktau cintitāyāṃ kathamiyaṃ nirvartate nirvahati ekatvātkartuḥ anekatvācca
padārthānāṃ ityapekṣodaye kramato nirṇīyate । tatra ca kaḥ krama ādartavya ityapekṣāyāṃ
kramalakṣaṇāmārabdhavyam । evaṃ parasparāpekṣatvāt pañcānāṃ na tāvadadhikāraḥ eṣāmavasare
nipatitumarhati । kintu eṣu samāpteṣu kiṃ kramaparyante upadeśārthe1 adhikārī vidyate
neti jijñāsodeti । tataścādhikāralakṣaṇamārabdhavyam । evaṃ cintāsiddha‍yarthaṃ pañca-
lakṣaṇānyadhikāro'pekṣate yāvattāni na cintyante tāvadadhikāracintāvakāśa eva
nāstīti । na punarhetubhāvena pañcalakṣaṇānyadhikāro'pekṣate । tena saṃbandhābhāvāt
saṃbandho nocyate । anyatrāvasarālābhāt idānīṃ cāvasaralābhāt asminneva sthāne'dhi-
kāralakṣaṇamārabhyata ityākṣepapratisamādhānāya hetuhetumadbhāvenāpekṣā nāsti kintvava-
saralābhāyāpekṣeti darśayati---<q>na kramaparyanta upadeśo'dhikārasya hetuḥ ।
kintu kramaparyanta upadeśe kaś‍cidadhikārī vidyate neti cintā</q> । nanūpadeśa-
balenaivādhikāro'vagamyate upadeśasyādhikārāvinābhāvitvāt ityanenāśayena pṛcchati-
<q>kimanadhikāro'pyupadeśo vidyate</q> yena bhavānnopadeśasya adhikāraṃ prati hetu-
tāmāha । uttaraṃ-<q>bāḍhaṃ vidyate devadattaḥ kāṣṭhaiḥ sthālyāmodanaṃ pacatītyevamādiṣu
pramāṇāntarapramitārthaviṣayeṣu</q> pramāṇāntarapramitārthaḥ viṣayo yeṣāṃ vākyānāṃ teṣūpadeśo
niradhikāro'pi vidyate । <q>na tatra kaś‍cinniyujyate</q> । kathaṃ na niyujyata ityatrāha---
<q>pramāṇāntarapramitaviṣayatvādeva</q> । yasmāt pramāṇāntarapramita eṣāṃ viṣayaḥ tasmā-
dityarthaḥ । bhavatu pramāṇāntarapramitaviṣayatā tathāpi kimityadhikāraśūnyatā ।
<note>1. mā. apadeśārthe ।</note>﻿
<pb n="004"/>
adhikāraśūnyatābhāvāt kathamanuṣṭhānasiddhirityatrāha---<q>lakṣaṇāntareṇa hi pratītasya
svarūpasya śakteśca kathanamātrameva dravyādīnāṃ vartamānāpadeśaiḥ kriyate</q> ।
<q>arthādarthitvenopadeśasiddhiḥ</q> upadeśārthamanutiṣṭhati । nanu yadyarthādarthitvenopadeśārtha-
siddhiḥ kimarthaṃ tarhyadhikāra iha pratipādyata ityatrāha-iha <q>punarupadeśādeva śak‍tijñānaṃ
iti viśeṣaḥ</q> । upadeśavyatirekeṇātra śaktijñānaṃ nāstīti sādhikāra upadeśo
varṇanīyaḥ । anyathā śaktijñānābhāvenānuṣṭhānāsiddhiḥ । tasmādupadeśo'dhikāra-
vyabhicāritatvāt nāyamadhikāramavagamayatīti hetutvābhāvānnāsti saṃbandhaḥ । <q>tasmānna
saṃbandhābhidhānaṃ</q> bhāṣyakārasyeti । <q>kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ svargakāma evodāhni/?/yate na
punaḥ grāmakāmādayo'pīti</q> । sarveṣāmapyadhikārapradarśanārthaṃ sarvāṇyevodāharaṇīyānīti
bhāvaḥ । pariharati---<q>kiṃ vā sarvamevodāharaṇīyaṃ</q> yenaivaṃ pṛcchasi ? <q>nyāya-
siddha‍yarthaṃ tu ekamevodāharaṇīyaṃ</q> ekasminnapyudāharaṇe nyāyaḥ pradarśayituṃ śakyate
yataḥ । pratyutodāharaṇāntaramakiñcitkaram । ataḥ ekamevodāharaṇīyamiti । ākṣeptā
āha---<q>ucyate, satyamevaṃ atra punaḥ svargaśabdavācyanirūpaṇamukhena pūrvottara-
pakṣau nirūpayati bhāṣyakāraḥ</q> । tatra ekenāpyudāhṛtena sarvodāharaṇeṣu nyāya-
vyutpattirbhavati yadi sarvavyāpī vicāro bhavati । iha tu svargaśabdasya prītimad-
dravyavacanatayā pūrvapakṣo nirūpyate । rāddhāntaśca prītimātravacanatayā । <q>na ca
grāmakāmādiṣvetatsambhavati</q> prītyapagamepi grāme <q>grāmaśabdaprayogāt</q> । asyārthaḥ-
prītyapagame dravye svargaśabdasyāprayogāt prītivacanaḥ svargaśabda ityuktvā rāddhāntaḥ
kṛtaḥ । na cāyaṃ prakāro grāmakāme saṃbhavati ; prītiṃ vināpi grāme grāmaśabdaprayogāt
ato dravyamātravacano grāmaśabdaḥ iti rāddhānto na labhyata iti । <q>grāmakāmādiṣvadhi</q>-﻿
<pb n="005"/>
<q>karaṇāntaraṃ vā vaktavyam</q> yadyadhikṛtaviśeṣaṇamabhipretam । <q>sādhanābhidhānaṃ vā
dravyavacanatvāt grāmādiśabdānāṃ</q> yāgādisādhanatābhidhānamaṅgīkaraṇīyam । kartṛ-
viśeṣaṇābhidhāyakatvaṃ vā āśrayaṇīyam । <q>atrocyate sarvāṇyevodāharaṇīyāni ।
pradarśanārthaṃ tu svargakāmapadamudāhṛtam</q> । tulyanyāyatayā sarvāṇyevodāharaṇāni ।
vastutaḥ svargakāmapadaṃ tu pradarśanārthamudāhṛtam । <q>nanu ca kāmyamānābhidhāna-
nibandhanapūrvottarapakṣau na grāmakāmādiṣu saṃbhavata ityuktam</q> । kāmyamāno yaḥ
svargaḥ tadabhidhānanibandhanaṃ yadi svargaśabdo dravyavacanaḥ tadā pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ yadā prītivacanaḥ
tadā rāddhāntaḥ iti grāmakāmādiṣu na saṃbhavata ityuktaṃ dravyavacanatvāt grāmakāmādīnām ।
samarthayitā āha---<q>tadayuktam</q> । ākṣeptā āha---<q>kathamayuktam</q> । samarthayitā
āha-<q>itthamayuktam । kāmyamānatayā svargaśabdaḥ kāmyeṣu vartata ityuktam</q> ।
asyārthaḥ-prītivacanaḥ svargaśabda iti yaduktaṃ tenedamuktaṃ bhavati-kāmyamānatayā kāma-
nāvyāpyatayā kāmanāṃ prati pradhānatayā svargaśabdaḥ kāmyeṣu sraka‍candanādiṣu vartata
iti । prītirhi kāmyamānā bhavati । tena prītivacanatayā kāmyamānābhidhāyakatā
uktā bhavati । <q>evaṃ grāmakāmādiṣvapi draṣṭavyam</q> । grāmakāmādiṣvapi kāmyamāna-
tayaiva grāmaśabdo vartate । <q>na hyakāmyaṃ kāmanāyuktaṃ bhavatīti</q> grāmakāma ityatra
grāmaḥ kāmenecchayā yuktaḥ saṃbaddhaḥ pratīyate । sa ca kāmyamānameva bhavitumarhati ।
yata eva kāmyamānaṃ kāmanāyuktaṃ bhavati <q>ata eva deśavacanatāmabhyupagamya svarga-
śabdasya tathāpi kāmanāyogāt</q> prītimad‍dravyavacana <q>evāyaṃ svargaśabda iti
kṛtaḥ pūrvaḥpakṣaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ-pūrvapakṣavādinā prītimad‍dravyavacanaḥ svargaśabda ityukte
coditaṃ-upamānāt svargaśabdaḥ prītimad‍dravye prayujyata iti । punaśca samāhitaḥ
<pb n="006"/>
mukhyārthāntarābhāvāt nopamānena prayujyata iti । punaścoditaḥ-deśaviśeṣe śītoṣṇā-
dirahite svargaśabdaḥ prasiddha iti । parihṛtaṃ ca tādṛśe deśe pramāṇābhāvāt na tatra
svargaśabdo mukhya iti । punaścoktaṃ-yadyapi tādṛśopadeśo'sti tathāpi prītimada‍dra-
vyavacanaḥ svargaśabdo varteta । tatra cāyaṃ hetuḥ kāmanāyogo'tra svargaśabdārthasyāva-
gamyate । na ca prītirahitasya kāmanāyogo'sti । <q>rāddhānte'pi na hyasatyāṃ prītau
kāmanā vartate dravya iti prītiparameva</q> svargaśabdasya <q>prayogaṃ darśitavān na
punardeśo nirākṛtaḥ</q> । satyāṃ prītau dravye kāmanā pravartate ityanayaiva
yukta‍yā rāddhānte'pi svargaśabdasya prītiparameva prayogaṃ darśitavān bhāṣyakāraḥ na
punardaśo nirākṛtaḥ । yadi hi svargaśabdasyābhidhānabalenaiva prītivacanatā syāt
tadā prayat‍nena deśavacanatāṃ nirākṛtya prītivacanatā sādhitā bhavet । na ca
deśanirākaraṇe yatnaḥ kṛtaḥ । tasmāt kāmanāsaṃbandhabalenaiva prītivaca/?/natā
svargaśabdasya bhāṣyakārasyābhimatā । akṣarārtho'pyevaṃ varṇanīyaḥ---yasyaiva prīti-
sādhanasya dravyasya vaktā svargaśabdaḥ tadeva dravyaṃ yadā na prīteḥ sādhanaṃ bhavati
tadā svargaśabdena nābhidhīyata ityarthaḥ । evaṃ ca sati yathā svargaśabdaḥ kāmanāyogena
prītiparaḥ । <q>evaṃ grāmakāmādayo'pīti prītiviṣayatā</q> prītiḥ viṣayaḥ
pratipādyo yeṣāṃ te prītiviṣayāḥ teṣāṃ bhāvaḥ prītiviṣayatā tayā <q>prayuktāḥ</q> kāmanā-
yogāt <q>na puna</q>ryāgaṃ prati <q>sādhanatayetyuktaṃ bhavati</q> rāddhāntitā । tena sarvatra
tulyo nyāyaḥ । yata eva kāmyamānaviṣayo'yaṃ vicāraḥ na svargamātraviṣayaḥ <q>ata
eva svargaḥ sādhyo yāgo vetyupanyasya punaḥ kāmaḥ sādhya iti darśayati</q>
kāmyata iti kāmaḥ sāmānyena kāmyamātraṃ sādhyata iti vadāmaḥ । anyathā hi svargaḥ
sādhyata ityevocyeta । yadā sarvāṇyevātrodāharaṇāni tadā kiṃ prītiḥ svargaḥ uta
dravyaṃ ityanena granthena । <q>etaduktaṃ bhavati---kiṃ kāmaviṣayatayā svargaśabdaḥ</q>﻿
<pb n="007"/>
<q>prayuktaḥ uta kāmyamānatayā kartṛviśeṣaṇamiti</q> । kiṃ kāmyamānaviṣayatayā
kāmyamānāvasthāpratipādakatayā prayuktaḥ svargaśabdaḥ uta kāmyamānatayā kāmanāṃ
kartṛviśeṣaṇabhūtāṃ viśiṃṣan kartṛviśeṣaṇamiti । tatra prītiḥ kāmyamānā-
vasthā'bhipretā । kāmyamānatayā kartṛviśeṣaṇaṃ dravyamabhimatam । nanu ca dravyapakṣe
svargasyopasarjanatāmāha bhāṣyakāraḥ na kartṛviśeṣaṇa[tva]mityatrāha---<q>tadā hi</q> kartṛ-
viśeṣaṇatve hi kāme <q>kāmyaṃ svargādirupasarjanaṃ bhavati</q> । tenopasarjanatāprati-
pādanena kartṛviśeṣaṇataivoktā । yadyupasarjanatve kartṛviśeṣaṇatā tarhi siddhānto na
labhyata ityanenābhiprāyeṇa codayati---<q>nanu ca svargakāma ityatropasarjanībhūta
eva kāmaḥ</q> kāmyasvargādiḥ <q>pratīyate</q> । pariharati---<q>etadevātra vicāryate ।
kiṃ yathābhidhānaṃ</q> viniyoga<q>saṃbandhaḥ uta yathāviniyogamabhidhānamiti</q> ।
kiṃ svargakāmābhidhānānusāreṇa svargasya kāmanāyāśca saṃbandhaḥ, abhidhānaṃ hyetadanya-
padārthaparaṃ tadanusāreṇa ca saṃbandhe guṇataiva svargasya । uta yādṛśaḥ kāmyakāma-
nayorviniyogaḥ parasparasaṃbandhaḥ pratīyate tadanurodhenābhidhānamiti । kāmyakāmanayorhi
saṃbandhe kāmyaḥ pradhānabhūta iti । tenopasarjanataivātra vicāryate । tatra pūrvapakṣavādī
yathābhidhānaṃ viniyogamicchan upasarjanatāmāha । rāddhāntī tu yathāsaṃbandhamabhi[da]dhānaḥ
anupasarjanatāmāheti । atra codayati---<q>kiṃ yathāviniyogamabhidhāne bahuvrī-
hirayaṃ na bhavati</q> । ayamabhiprāyaḥ-yathāviniyogepyabhidhāne bahuvrīhirevāyaṃ bahuvrīhiścedu-
pasarjanatā duṣpariharā । yadi hi yathāviniyogapakṣe bahuvrīhirayaṃ na syāt tadaivānu-
pasarjanatā syāt । na caidasti । pariharati---<q>kena voktaṃ nāyaṃ bahuvrīhiriti</q> ।
codayati---<q>yadi bahuvrīhirupasarjanaṃ tarhi kāmaḥ kāmyaḥ padārthāntara</q>bhūtapuruṣa-
paratvādasya samāsasya । yata eva cārthāntarabhūtapuruṣaparatā asya samāsasya ata
<pb n="008"/>
<q>evākhyātagatayā kartṛsaṅkhyayā'sya saṃbandhaḥ yajeta svargakāmaḥ yajeran
ṛddhikāmāḥ</q> ityekavacanabahuvacanadarśanāt । yadā copasarjanaṃ kāmyaṃ <q>evaṃ ca sati
saṃśayo'nupapannaḥ</q> siddhāntavacanavyaktyabhāvāt । <q>na ca bhagavataḥ pāṇineḥ
svārthepi bahuvrīhismaraṇamasti</q> yena bahuvrīhipakṣe'pi kāmyameva pradhānaṃ bhavet ।
samādhātā āha---<q>ucyate</q> । <q>vayamapi svārtha eva na bahuvrīhiṃ vadāmaḥ</q> ।
<q>kintu parārtho'yaṃ bahuvrīhiḥ, uta svārtha iti</q> । samasyapadapratipādyābhyāṃ
padārthābhyāṃ paro yaḥ puruṣaḥ tadartho'yaṃ bahuvrīhiḥ, uta samasyamānapadapratipādya-
kāmyārthaḥ iti vadāmaḥ । ākṣeptā āha---<q>kathaṃ punaḥ parārthaḥ kathaṃ vā svārthaḥ</q> ।
samādhātā āha---<q>siddhārthastu parārtho bhavati</q> । yadi svargakāmādiśabdaḥ siddhārtho
bhavati tadā parārtho bhavati । <q>atha sādhyārthaḥ tadā svārtho</q> bhavati । sa evāha-
<q>tatredānīṃ na vidmaḥ</q> । <q>kiṃ siddhārthasyopādānaṃ</q> samuccāraṇaṃ <q>parārthatayā</q> uta
sādhyatayopādīyata iti । ākṣeptā āha---<q>anyapadārthaśca sādhyārthaśceti nanu
vipratiṣiddham</q> । sādhyaṃ hi anyārthaṃ na bhavati । tataścānyapadārthaśca sādhyārthaśceti
parasparaṃ viruddham । samādhātā āha---<q>nātra vipratiṣedhaḥ yataḥ sādhyopyasau</q>
svargādiḥ anyārtha eva puruṣārtha eva । tena sādhyārthatā anyārthatā cāvipratiṣiddhā ।
<q>uktaṃ ca</q> ṛṣiṇā <quote>‘phalaṃ ca puruṣārthaṃtvāt’</quote> iti phalasya puruṣārthatvam। <q>tasmādupa-
pannārtho'yaṃ</q> bhāṣyakārīyaḥ saṃśayaḥ---kiṃ prītiḥ svargaḥ uta dravyāmiti ।</p>﻿
<pb n="009"/>
<q>nanu caivamapi saṃśayo nopapadyate</q> yasmāt <q>kartṛviśeṣaṇamidaṃ pratīyate
ākhyātagatakartṛsaṅkhyāsaṃyogāt</q> - yajeta svargakāma iti । nanu cādhikāri-
viśeṣaṇe'pi svargasiddhāvastyeva svargakāmasya kartṛtvaṃ tenākhyātasaṅkhyāsaṃyogo bhaviṣyatī-
tyatrāha---<q>tadākhyātakartari ca saṅkhyāṃ smarati bhagavān pāṇiniḥ iti</q> ।
asyārthaḥ-yasminnākhyāte saṅkhyā śrūyate tasya ākhyātasya yaḥkartā tatra saṅkhyāṃ
smarati pāṇiniriti । <q>svarge ca sādhye svargasiddhau svargakāmasya kartṛtvaṃ na
yāgasiddhau</q> tena yāgagatayā saṅkhyayā yogo na syāt yadi yāge kartā svargakāmo na
syāt । tena yāgaṃ pratyeva svargakāmaḥ kartṛtayopadiśyate । kasmāt pāṇiniḥ (na)
smaratītyatrāha---<q>na cānyatra vyāpṛtasya ākhyātāntaragatayā saṅkhyayā
yogo bhavati - yathā pacatīti paṭhataḥ</q> । samarthaḥ padavidhiriti pāṇineḥ smaraṇam ।
svārthasaṃbandhaśca sāmarthyam । anyatra vyāpṛtasya ca ākhyātāntaragatayā saṅkhyayāṃ
saṃbandho na bhavati, yathā - pacatītyanayā saṅkhyayā paṭhato yogo na bhavati ।
tenākhyātāntaraga[ta](tā) saṅkhya[yā] anyatra vyāpṛtasya saṃbandho nāstīti pāṇine-
ranusmaraṇam । <q>iha tu yajeta svargakāma ityekavākyatā'vagamyate</q> । paraṃ na
parasparasaṃbandhaṃ vinā ekavākyatā bhavati । ataḥ kartṛviśeṣaṇam । <q>kasmāt siddhārtha
evāyaṃ bahuvrīhiḥ na sādhyārthaḥ ?</q> ākṣeptaiva yuktyantaramāha - <q>etadevātra yuktam</q>
siddhārthaṃ nāmeti । <q>na hi sādhyārthaṃ nāma prātipadikaṃ bhavatīti bhāvārthādhi-
karaṇe</q> bhāṣyakāreṇo<q>ktam । ato yāgasyai</q>vākhyatopāttasya <q>kartavyatātrāvasīyate</q> ।
<q>bhāvārthatvāt</q> sādhyārthatvāt <q>yajatiśabdasya</q> । yuktyantaraṃ cāha---<q>na ca
sādhyavādino'pi yāgena sahaikavākyatā nāsti</q> । sādhyamapi svargaṃ yo vādī
<pb n="010"/>
vadati tasyāpi mate yāgena saha svargakāmasyaikavākyatā na nāsti । api tvastyeva ।</p>
<p><q>asti cettarhyekasminneva vākye sādhyadvayāvagatirna</q> yujyate ।
atra kaściccodayati---<q>nanu yathā vrīhīn prokṣati iti saṃskāre vrīhigate
sādhye'pi prokṣaṇena</q> ākhyātopāttena <q>sādhyabhūtenāsyaikavākyatā yathā
tadvat ihāpi bhaviṣyatīti</q> । ākṣeptā pariharati---<q>maivaṃ vocaḥ tatra hi
kārakatayā vrīhayaḥ saṃbaddhāḥ saṃskārabhājo bhavantīti</q> । asyārthaḥ- yuktaṃ
<quote>‘vrīhīn prokṣati’</quote> ityatra । yasmāttatra prathamāvasthāyāṃ kārakatayā vrīhayaḥ prokṣaṇena
saṃbadhyante । tacca prokṣaṇaṃ paścāddrīhiṣu saṃskāramārabhate । tena bhāvisaṃskārayogi-
kārakatayā vrīhayaḥ prokṣaṇaṃ prati dvitīyāntena śabdenopādīyante । <q>iha punaḥ na
yāgasvargayoḥ</q> dvayorapi sādhyayoḥ <q>anyataḥ</q> pramāṇāntarāt <q>kriyākārakasaṃbandha-
siddhiḥ</q> yataḥ parasparasaṃbandhaḥ syāt । nanu mā nāma pramāṇāntarāt kriyākārakasaṃbandhaḥ
setsyati vedenaiva yūpaṃ chinattīti vadatā avasāyiṣyata ityatrāha---<q>nāpi yūpavadi-
haivāvasīyate</q> । pṛcchati---<q>kimiti</q> । nāvasīyate । <q>yadyutpādyasyāpi kāraka-
yogo bhavati</q> । utpādyasyāpi yūpasya cchede yadi kārakatayā saṃbandho bhavati, tadā
kimiti vede tadvadeva kriyākārakarasaṃbandho nāvasīyata ityarthaḥ । uttaraṃ---<q>yadi bhavati</q>
utpādyasyāpi kārakayogaḥ <q>bhavatu na punarutpādyasyā</q>sadbha‍ūtasya kriyāṃ prati	 kārakatā-
yogo bhavati । codayitā āha---<q>kathaṃ tarhi yūpaṃ chinattīti</q> । asati yūpasya
kārakatve dvitīyāntaṃ padaṃ dvitīyāyāḥ kārakavibhaktitvāt । samādhātā āha---
<q>chedanena saṃbaddhaṃ yūpaṃ karotītyarthaḥ</q> yūpaṃ chinattītyasya vākyasya । etaduktaṃ bhavati-
<note>1. mavatveva-mā.</note>﻿
<pb n="011"/>
atrāpi khadirādereva chedanasya saṃbandhaḥ । ta eva tu khadirādayaḥ chedanena kāraka-
tayā saṃbandhāt chedanena saṃskriyante । saṃskārayoginaśca yūpaśabdenocyante chedanena
yūpīkriyanta iti । yadi tatrāpi pramāṇāntarāvagata eva kriyākārakabhāvaḥ kathaṃ tarhi
codanālakṣaṇo yūpa iti prasiddhiḥ tatrāha---<q>alaukikatvāt</q> loke yūpaśabdavācyatayā
saṃskṛtānāṃ khadirādīnāmaviditatvāt <q>codanālakṣaṇo yūpa ityucyate</q> । abhi-
prāyamajānan pṛcchati---<q>saṃbandhaśca kriyayā alaukikaśceti kimidaṃ ?</q> kriyā-
kārakasaṃbandhasya sarvasya laukikatvāt । uttaraṃ---<q>yūpaśabdābhidheyatayā'laukikatvam</q> ।
vaidikaśabdaprayogavaśenaiva yūpaśabdasya svārthe vyutpatteḥ । na punaḥ chedanasaṃbandhitayā'-
laukikatvam । <q>ato'trāpi kārakasyaiva khadirādeḥ chedanena kiñcitkriyate</q> ।
ato vrīhīn prokṣatītyanena tulyatā । <q>svargasya punaḥ</q> sādhyabhūtasya <q>yajyarthaṃ prati
kārakatvamevālaukikam</q> । upasaṃharati---<q>tasmāt vrīhīn prokṣatītivat
saṃbandho nopapadyate yajeta svargakāma</q> iti । yathā vrīhīn prokṣatīti saṃbandha
upapadyate na tathā yajeta svargakāma ityatropapadyata ityarthaḥ । <q>na ca saṃbandhāntaraṃ
śabdavit smarati । smaran vā pramāṇābhāvāt</q> nirmūlasmaraṇānupapatteḥ <q>vihanyeta</q>
iti । siddhāntavacanavyaktyabhāvena saṃśayamākṣipyopasaṃharati---<q>tasmātsaṃśayamatra
devāḥ kariṣyanti</q> yadi kartavyaṃ maṃsyante ।</p>
<p>samādhatte---<q>atrābhidhīyate । syādetadevaṃ yadi pramāṇacatuṣṭayātagamya
eva saṃbandhaḥ syāt</q> । tena pramāṇacatuṣṭayenāvagatamapi śabda eva kiṃ saṃbandhāntaraṃ
bodhayati netīti yukta eva saṃśayaḥ ।</p>﻿
<pb n="012"/>
<p>ākṣeptā āha---<q>uktaṃ śabdasya prāmāṇyamanapekṣatvāditi</q> । tena tatprāmāṇya-
balenaiva saṃbandhāntaraṃ setsyatīti nādhikaraṇamārabdhavyam । samādhātā āha---<q>satyamuktaṃ</q>
prāmāṇyam । <q>tadevātrāvasīdati</q> । kathaṃ ? uttaraṃ---<q>adhikārasiddhau prayogasya</q>
anuṣṭhānasya <q>siddhiḥ prayogasiddhau</q> satyāṃ <q>upadeśasiddhiḥ</q> । kāryarūpaḥ upadiṣṭo
niyogārthaḥ sa siddhyatīti । anyathā anuṣṭhātaryasati kāryameva tanna syāt । tataścā-
kāryaṃ kāryatayā pratipādayan śabdaḥ pramāṇaṃ na syādityasminnadhikaraṇe adhikāralakṣaṇa-
saṃbandha[ndhā]sādhake sati prāmāṇyamevāvasīdatīti prāmāṇyanirvāhārthamidamadhikaraṇamārabdha-
vyam । ākṣeptā āha---<q>evaṃ tarhi pramāṇalakṣaṇamevedaṃ prāptaṃ</q> । na lakṣaṇāntaram ।
samādhātā āha---<q>bhavati ca lakṣaṇāntaramapi sat pramāṇalakṣaṇam pañcalakṣaṇa-
śeṣatvāt adhikārasya</q> । viniyogopādānakramalakṣaṇaśeṣatvaṃ utpādakatayā darśitam ।
veda prāmāṇyatadbheda lakṣaṇaśeṣatvaṃ tu tannirvāhakatayā, adhikāraṃ vinā pramāṇatvānirvāhāt ।
asati tannirvāhe tadbhedo dūrāpeta iti । yadi pramāṇalakṣaṇamidaṃ bhavati <q>kathaṃ tarhi
lakṣaṇāntaramidaṃ vyapadiśyate</q> ? samādhatte---<q>evaṃ vyapadiśyate satyapyadhi-
kāre pramāṇākṣepaḥ pramāṇalakṣaṇe samāhitaḥ</q> । ihedānīṃ <q>sa evādhikāraḥ upa-
padyate neti vicāryate</q> । etaduktaṃ bhavati - sāpekṣatayā śabdasyāprāmāṇyaṃ pramāṇalakṣaṇe
parihṛtam । iha tu sthitepyanapekṣatve'dhikārābhāvenākṣipya pratisamādhīyate । yadi
ca yāvadaprāmāṇyenaiva śabdasya adhikāra ākṣipyeta tadā''kṣepahetubhūtāprāmāṇyanirā-
karaṇenedaṃ na lakṣaṇāntaraṃ vyapadiśyeta । nacaitadevaṃ, tadāha---<q>na cāprāmāṇyenaivādhi-
kārākṣepaḥ kiṃ tarhi ? adhikārasaṃbandhānavagamāt</q> । ākṣeptā āha---<q>nanu
cānavagamo'pyaprāmāṇyameva</q> । tenānavagamenāpyākṣepaḥ aprāmāṇyenaiva । samādhātā
<pb n="013"/>
<p>āha---<q>satyameva</q>manavagamo'<q>dhikāre'prāmāṇyam na punaḥ śabdārthamātre</q>। tenādhi-
kārivyatiriktakāryamātrāvagamakatvāt asti prāmāṇyamiti nāprāmāṇyenākṣepaḥ । na
caiṃva tarhi yadyanavagame'pi prāmāṇyaṃ tadā kathaṃ pramāṇalakṣaṇe['] prāmāṇyaṃ nirākṛta-
mityatrāha---<q>pramāṇalakṣaṇe punaḥ śabdo'rthaṃ na spṛśatītyayamartho nirākṛtaḥ ।</q>
sarvathaivārthāsparśitve tadaprāmāṇyam । viśiṣṭārthāpratipādakatve tu arthāntarapratipādaka-
tayāpi prāmāṇyamupapadyata eva ।</p>
<p><q>tasmādupapanno lakṣaṇāntaravyapadeśaḥ । ataḥ pañcabhirlakṣaṇaiḥ kārya-
mātrāvagatiruktā na punarasyedaṃ kāryamityuktam । asatyāṃ caitasyāmavagatau
kāryamātrāvayatiḥ tathāpi bhavantī na tathā bhavati anuṣṭhānābhāvāt</q> ।
yāvadidaṃ mama kāryamiti nāvabudhyate na tāvat kaścit pravartate । ato yadyapi kārya-
metadityavagatirbhavati tathāpyasau kāryasyānuṣṭhānaṃ vinā kāryatvānupapatteḥ avagamyamāna-
śūnyatayā anavagatireva syāt । tasmādasyedaṃ kāryamiti siddhaye'dhikāralakṣaṇa-
mārabdhavyam । <q>nanu caturthe'satyapyadhikāre phalakalpanā uktā sa svargaḥ
syāt</q> sarvān pratyaviśiṣṭatvāditi । asyārthaḥ-kimartho'yamadhikāraḥ pratipādyate ?
yāvatā vināpyadhikāreṇa phalata evānuṣṭhānaṃ bhaviṣyati yathā <q>loke</q> । adhikāraṃ vinā
phalāvagatireva na syāditi cet, na, vināpyadhikāreṇa viśvajidādiṣu caturthe phala-
kalpanāyā uktatvāt iti । pariharati---<q>satyaṃ phalakalpanenoktā । adhikāra-
saṃbhave tu sā adhikāranibandhanaiva</q> na pramāṇāntaranibandhanā । nanvadhikāra
eva tatra tatra na śrūyate kathaṃ tannibandhanā kalpanetyatrāha---<q>aśrute'pyadhikāro</q>﻿
<pb n="014"/>
<q>vidyate ityuktam</q> tatraiva । tenāśrutepyadhikāre'nvitābhighānabalena klṛpte paścāttanni-
bandhanā phalakalpanā । <q>asaṃbhave punaradhikārasya kasyāśrutasya kalpanā</q> ।
yadi punaradhikāra eva na saṃbhavet kasyāśrutasya kalpanā bhavet । adhikārasambhave hi
adhikāriviśeṣaṇatayā phalakalpanā bhavet । tadasaṃbhave tu kasya kalpanā bhavati ।
nahi kāryaṃ phalamapekṣate yena phalatayā kalyeta svargaḥ । tasmādanyato'nuṣṭhāna[nā]siddhe-
radhikāro vaktavyaḥ । evaṃ tāvacchabdasya pramāṇyāt śabdaikagamyasaṃbandhaḥ asti nāstīti
saṃśayaḥ samarthitaḥ । punarākṣepamāha---<q>nanu cātra bhavanto vaiyākaraṇāḥ kecit
kartāramevādhikṛtaṃ manyante । yo yasmin kartṛtayā'vagamyate sa tatrādhikṛta
iti vadantaḥ । nādhikāro nāma kaścidarthāntarabhūtaḥ</q> kartṛtvāt । <q>saca kartā
kriyayā saṃbadhyate iti manyante</q> । tena kriyākārakasaṃbandha eva parasparasaṃbandhaḥ
nāparaḥ saṃbandhaḥ śabdenāpi pratipādyate । <q>brāhmaṇādayaśca kartṛtayā'vagamyante
smṛteḥ । dvijātīnāmadhyayanamijyādānaṃ iti</q> । manvādismṛtirapi brāhmaṇādīn
kartṛtvena pratipādayati nārthāntaratayā <quote>‘dvijātīnāmadhyayanaṃ ijyā dānaṃ’</quote> iti <quote>‘kartṛ-
karmaṇoḥ kṛti’</quote> iti kartari ṣaṣṭhīsmaraṇāt । <q>kartṝṇāṃ ca phalakalpanā ātmane-
padādibhirliṅgaiḥ</q> । kartṝṇāṃ hi phalakalpanā । na punaḥ kartṛvyatiriktānāṃ <quote>‘kartrabhi-
prāye kriyāphale’</quote> iti smaraṇāt । <q>ayamevāsau bādaripakṣaḥ</q> । bādarerapi sammato yaḥ
pakṣa iti । yaduktaṃ tṛtīye---<q>dravyaguṇasaṃskāreṣveva saṃbandhāvagamaṃ manyante na
yāgaphalapuruṣeṣviti । evaṃ ca kriyāsaṃbandha upapanno bhavati</q> yadi kartā
svargakāmaḥ evaṃ kriyayā saṃbadhyate <q>anyathā hyadhikṛtasya kriyayā saṃbandho durbhaṇaḥ</q> ।
avagamyate ca saṃbandhaḥ, anyathā hyekavākyatā na syāt । yatassaṃbandhāntaraṃ nāsti tena
<pb n="015"/>
<q>svargakāmādīni padāni kartṛviśeṣaṇānyeva <quote>‘bhinne juhoti’</quote> itivat</q> ।
yathā bhedenena darśapūrṇamāsakartā viśeṣyate tathā svargakāmādibhirapi । iyān viśeṣaḥ
homasaṃbandhārthaṃ darśapūrṇamāsakartā bhedanena viśeṣyate । svargakāmanayā tu nānyatra saṃbandha-
yitumiti । codayati---<q>nanu caivaṃ sati</q> kartṛniyamavidhānāt <q>kartrantara</q>bhūtānā-
mṛtvijā<q>manupraveśo na prāp‍noti</q> niyamena nivartitatvāt । pariharati---<q>na
prāp‍notu nāma । naitāvatā</q> kartrantarānanupraveśamātreṇa[ā] saṃbandhaḥ syāt । adṛṣṭa-
pūrvasya kalpanā''śrayituṃ śakyate । <q>vacanādvā</q> ṛtvigvaraṇabharaṇavidhānāt kartranta-
rānupraveśa <q>upapanno bhaviṣyati</q> yata eva ca kartṛparāṇyetāni <q>ata eva ca kāraka-
vibhakteranutpattiḥ । tiṅābhidhānāt saṅkhyāyāḥ prathamāyāścotpattiḥ ।
anyathāhi</q> kartṛvyatiriktasyā<q>dhikāriṇaḥ vibhaktyantaraṃ vā mṛgyaṃ śeṣalakṣaṇa-
ṣaṣṭhyā vā bhavitavyaṃ yajeta svargakāmasyeti</q> । yuktyantaraṃ cāha---<q>kartṛnirde-
śaścāyaṃ anvayavyatirekābhyāmavagamyate - yajeta svargakāmaḥ ijyate svarga-
kāmena iti</q>---anabhihitāyāṃ ākhyātena kartṛsaṅkhyāyāṃ tṛtīyānvayāt, abhi-
hitāyāṃ ca vyatirekāt । yadi hi kartari tṛtīyeyaṃ syāt tadaiva yujyate nānyathā
kartaryeveyaṃ tṛtīyeti kartṛnirdeśa evāyaṃ svargakāma iti । anyathāhi kartṛnirdeśo na
syāt । tadāha---<q>bhāvasādhanepi</q> svargakāmenejyate ityādau <q>tṛtīyā na syāt
akārakatvāt svargakāmasya । yatpunaridamuktaṃ</q> adhikāraṃ kartṛbhābā[va]vyatiriktaṃ
<pb n="016"/>
vinā <q>niṣphalaṃ karma bhavati na ca niṣphale pravartanta iti । tatra brūmaḥ karma-
svābhāvyāt</q> karmaṇo'yaṃ svabhāvaḥ yadabhūtaṃ kiṃcidbhāvayatīti । tatra yāgādikamapi
karmāśrutaṃ <q>kimapi bhāvayiṣyati । tacca</q> karmaṇā<q>mabhyudayāya</q> bhaviṣyatīti abhyudaya-
rūpaṃ kimapi bhaviṣyati <q>abhyudayaḥ(tvaṃ)</q> viśiṣṭaśarīrendriyādiprādurbhāvaḥ <q>nityeṣviva
bhavatpakṣe'pi</q> [yasya] svargakāmādīnyadhikāriviśeṣaṇāni tasyāpi mate jīvanādhikāre
phalāśravaṇe'pi karmasvābhāvyāt yathā kimapi phalamabhyudayarūpaṃ kalpyate tathehāpi
bhaviṣyati । evaṃ tāvat asatyapi vyatirikte'dhikāre phalataḥ pravṛttirityuktam । idānīṃ
vināpyadhikāraṃ vināpi phalaṃ pravṛttirbhaviṣyatītyāha-<q>kartavyatāvagamācca karmānuṣṭhānam</q> ।
yaddhi kartavyatayā'vagamyate tatra pravṛttiḥ <q>na punaḥ phalasambandhāt । phalasaṃbandhe</q>
hyaṅgīkriyamāṇe <q>pramāṇāntarāvagamyatā prāp‍noti</q> vedārthasya phalata eva kartavyatā-
vaṃgamāt । <q>tataścānapekṣatvāditi heturuddhṛta</q> unmūlito <q>bhavati sāpekṣatvaprasaṅgāt</q>
pramāṇāntarānavagamyamānārthatayā hi anapekṣatvam pramāṇāntarāvagamyārthatve tu sāpekṣatā
prāpnoti vedārthasya । tataścānapekṣatvaṃ prathamapāde uktam । upasaṃharati---<q>ataḥ karma
kartavyaṃ kartṛbhiriti anadhikāraḥ</q> karturevādhikāraḥ । evamākṣipte saṃśaye samādhātā
āha---<q>ucyate, nāyaṃ pūrvapakṣaḥ śreyān svargakāmapadaṃ hyasmin pakṣe yathā na
saṃbadhyate tathopariṣṭādvakṣyāmaḥ</q> । anyathānupapadyamānaḥ svargakāmaśabdaḥ saṃbandhāntara
mavagamayatīti bhāvaḥ । punarākṣeptā āha---<q>yadyevaṃ</q> yadi svargakāmaśabdo'nyathā nopa-
padyate <q>kathaṃ tarhi saṃśayaḥ- kiṃ dhātvarthaḥ sādhyatayopadiśyate uta kāma iti</q> ।
<pb n="017"/>
asyārthaḥ---ākhyātapadasaṃbandhāt yāgo'pi kartavyatayā pratibhāti, kāmanāsaṃyogāt
kāmo'pi । tatra kaḥ sādhyatayā saṃbadhyatāmiti sandehaḥ । kāmyata iti kāmaḥ
svargādiḥ । <q>nanu dhātvarthe sādhye</q> dūṣaṇamidamuktaṃ svarga<q>kāmapadamanyathā</q>
kartṛviśeṣaṇatvena <q>na sambadhyata</q> iti । samādhātā āha---<q>na na sambadhyate</q>, api
tu sambadhyata eva । kutaḥ? aṅgatayā hi <quote>‘samudraṃ manasā dhyāyet’</quote> itivat <q>kāmanaṃ
kartavya prāp‍noti</q> । yadi dhātvarthaḥ sādhyo bhavati tadā tadaṅgatayā samudrasya
dhyānavat svargādikāmanāpi kartavyā bhaviṣyati । tena svargakāmaśabdo'pi kāmanāme-
vāṅgatayā samarpayan saṃbadhyata iti । <q>nanvevaṃ satyubhayoḥ kartavyatā uktā bhavati</q> ।
dhātvarthakāmanayoḥ tataḥ kathaṃ saṃbandha ityarthaḥ । samādhātā āha---<q>na, satyamuktā,
guṇapradhānabhāvastvatra cintyate</q> । ekasya guṇatayā kartavyatā, aparasya pradhānatā ।
punaścodayati - yadi svargakāmanāpi sādhyā <q>kathaṃ tarhi siddhārthatayā svargakāma-
śabdasya pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । pūrvapakṣo'pi sādhyārthatayaiva</q> tathā । <q>bhūtaṃ bhavyāyopa-
diśyata iti ca kathaṃ bravīti</q> bhāṣyakāraḥ । samādhātā āha---<q>nāyaṃ doṣaḥ</q>yasmāt
<q>bhūtamevātropadiśyate । na cet pramāṇāntaraprāptamupādānasidhyarthaṃ kriyate</q> ।
anyathā upādānāsaṃbhavāt । <q>upadeśe tu bhūtameva</q> । tena saṃbandho'pyupadiśyate ।
sādhyasādhanabhāvena siddhārthatayā ca pūrvapakṣo'pyanupapannaḥ । bhūtavyapadeśaśca । yata
evamatra sandeho na---kiṃ yāgaḥ sādhyaḥ uta kāma iti । <q>ata eva caikādaśe
yadadhikaraṇaṃ tadapyapunaruktaṃ nyāyataḥ</q> । atra hi yāgaḥ sādhyatayā nopadiśyata
ityuktam ।। tatra sthite'pi yāgasya sādhyatvenānupadeśe svargakāmādeḥ kartṛviśeṣaṇatvaṃ
<note>1. avyavadhānasambandhata-mā.</note>﻿
<pb n="018"/>
nirākṛtam । tadatra ayaṃ mūlabhūtassandehaḥ---kiṃ svargakāmapadaṃ niyojyasamarpakaṃ
uta neti । tatra yadāhi niyojyaviśeṣaṇaṃ tadā kāmyamānasya sādhyatā svārthatā ca
kāmyamānatayā copādānaṃ yāgasya ca sādhanatā । kāryaviśeṣaṇa pakṣe tu kāmyasiddha‍yarthatā
parārthatā ca । kāmanāyāḥ sādhanatayopādānaṃ yāgasya ca sādhyateti । <q>evaṃ sthite
viśaye pūrvapakṣavādī bhūtaṃ bhavyāyeti pūrvapakṣitavān । śābdoktābhiśca
yuktibhiḥ</q> abhyuccayarūpābhiḥ । asyārthaḥ---ākhyātopāttatayā yāgaḥ sādhyatayā
pratīyate । na ca sādhyena sādhyasya saṃbandho yujyata iti bhūtārthatayaiva svargakāma-
śabdo'nvayaṃ yāti । tenātra kartṛviśeṣaṇataiva । vaiyākaraṇena ca yā yuktaya uktāḥ <q>na</q>
kartṛvyatiriktaḥ kaścinniyojyo nāmāstīti tābhiśca kartṛviśeṣaṇateti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>bhāṣyaṃ vyākhyātuṃ ākṣipati---<q>idamaparaṃ cintyata iti kathaṃ ? svarga-
śabdaḥ kiṃ prītivacanaḥ uta dravyavacana iti</q> । asyārthaḥ-yadi yāgassādhyaḥ
tathāpi kathaṃ dravyavacanatā svargaśabdasya । tathā yadi svargaḥ sādhyaḥ tathāpi kathaṃ prīti-
vacanatā । yo hi śabdaḥ svaśaktyā ca yadvacano'vagamyate tadvacana eva yuktaḥ na
punaḥ sādhyatāsādhanatābhyāṃ vyavasthāpyate । <q>tathā dvyaṣṭavarṣādyupanyāsaḥ deśāpa-
lāpo'bhyupagamaśca nātīvopayujyate</q> । yadi yāgasya sādhyatayā dravyavacanatā
svargaśabdasya, tadā kiṃ <quote>“dva‍yaṣṭavarṣāḥ striyaḥ svarga”</quote> ityevamādinā prayogopanyāsena ।
tathā deśāpalāpo'pi pūrvapakṣiṇo niṣprayojanaḥ deśasyāpi dravyatvāt dravyavacanatā hi
tasyābhimatā । tathā yadi deśo nirākṛtaḥ tadā abhyupagamaḥ kimartha iti ।
samādhatte---<q>nanu coktamasmābhiḥ kiṃ kāmaviṣayatayā svargaśabdaḥ prayuktaḥ uta
dravyaparatayeti</q> asyārthaḥ---nātra vācakatā cintyata iti । [kiṃ]tarhi ? prayogaḥ ।
tena sādhyatvāsādhyatvavicāraḥ tasya heturbhavati । yadā svargaḥ sādhyaḥ tadā prītipara-
tayā prayogaḥ yadā ca yāgassādhyaḥ tadā dravyaparatayeti prītiśabdaḥ । nacātra kāmya-﻿
<pb n="019"/>
mānāvasthā'bhipretā । <q>yadyevaṃ deśāpalāpe kiṃ prayojanaṃ ?</q> dravyaparatayā yadi
prayogaḥ pūrvapakṣavādino'bhimataḥ evaṃ tarhi deśāpalāpe kiṃ prayojanaṃ ? deśasyāpi
dravyatvāt । uttaraṃ---<q>sādhanasiddhiḥ</q> prayojanam । kāmanāyā yāgaṃ prati sādhana-
bhūtāyāḥ siddhiḥ prayojanam । <q>sa kila deśo jīvadbhirnopalabhyate । na cānupa-
labdhasyopādānopasarjanatā samudravadbhavati</q> । yathā samudrasyopalabdhasya dhyānopa-
sarjanatā saṃbhavati tathā'nupalabdhasya deśasya kāmanopādānopasarjanatā na saṃbhavatīti ।
<q>ato dvyaṣṭavarṣādyupanyāsaḥ peśalaḥ</q> । tasyopalabdhasyopādānopasarjanatvasaṃbhavāda<q>bhyupa-
gamepi deśasya । yadyapi kevalasukhaśravaṇādi</q>tyanayā yuktyā <q>tathāpyasmatpakṣo
na duṣyati iti pakṣasiddha‍yarthavacanameva</q> । deśasya svargatve kadācidasmākaṃ pakṣo
na siddha‍yatīti manyase tadapi nāstītyuktaṃ bhavati । tasyāpi kevalasukhaśravaṇārthāpatti-
siddhasya kāmanopādānopasarjanatvasaṃbhavāt । <q>sāmānyāvagame tu vyavahārāsiddheḥ
sukhasādhanatvamātraṃ parigṛhyata ityupasaṃhāraḥ</q> । kaściddeśo'stītyetāvatāpyavagamena
kāmanāvyavahārasiddheḥ sukha sādhanamātrameva ca kiṃ[na]gṛhyata ityupasaṃhāraḥ kṛtaḥ ।
<q>ataḥ pūrvapakṣavādī yāga evopadeśaṃ manyate</q> । yāgaḥ sādhyatayopādīyata ityarthaḥ ।
yata eva yāgaḥ sādhyaḥ <q>ata eva ca <quote>“bhāvārthāḥ karmaśabdāḥ tebhyaḥ kriyā
pratīyeta”</quote> iti samarthitaṃ bhavati । anyathā</q> cādīnāmapi sādhyārthaḥ syāt tadā
<q>ukto virodhaḥ</q> । saṃprati pūrvapakṣasāraṃ niṣkarṣayituṃ codayati---<q>nanu cāsmin
pakṣe yattat kimapi bhaviṣyati tathā bhaviṣyati । na hyakārakādhāraṃ kriyā-
<note>1. mā. tatra</note>﻿
<pb n="020"/>
<q>phalamupapadyate</q> । na cādhārabhūtaṃ phalasya karmāravyaṃ kārakamupalabhyate । <q>nanu ca
somaṃ yajatītyevamādiṣu kārakamupalabhāmahe</q> । devatā karmabhūtā yāge tadgataṃ phalaṃ
bhaviṣyati । nirākaroti---<q>tadidamayuktam navame nirākṛtatvāt prādhānyasya</q>
yadi yogaṃ prati pradhānabhūtā devatā bhavet tadā syādevam । navame nirākṛtaṃ devatā-
prādhānyaṃ vigrahādinirākaraṇena । itaśca devatāyāḥ prādhānyaṃ nāstītyāha---<q>nanu
anirjñātapuruṣārthasya sākṣāt praṇāḍikayā vā saṃskāro nopapadyata iti
saktvadhikaraṇe uktam</q> । sākṣāt praṇāḍikayā vā anirjñātapuruṣārtho'yam । tasya
saṃskāro nopapadyata iti savatvadhikaraṇe darśitam । <q>na ca devatā puruṣārthatayā kena-
cijjñāpitā । nanu ca devatā manuṣyān pālayantīti prasiddhiḥ</q> । tena puruṣārtha-
tayā devatā jñāpiteti <q>nirmūlatvāt vaṭayakṣaprasiddhivat nādaraṇīyetyuktaṃ navama
eva । nanu ca deśasyeva yāgopadeśaḥ pramāṇaṃ bhavitumarhati asyāḥ prasiddheḥ</q> ।
yathā deśaviśeṣasya sukhamātrāyatanasya svargapadābhidheyasya yāgopadeśaḥ tathā devatāyāḥ
manuṣyapālanakartṛtvasyāpi bhaviṣyati । tanmūlā ceyaṃ prasiddhiriti । sa evāha---
<q>avaśyaṃ caitaddeva</q>tāprādhānyaṃ nityārtha<q>mabhyupagamanīyam</q> । tatra hi kriyāphalamevābhyu-
dayo'bhyupeyaḥ । pariha rati---<q>naitadupapadyate upadeśo hi yāgaṃ kuryādityetāva-
tyarthe pramāṇaṃ na punaḥ puruṣasyopakārako yāga iti</q> ।
<pb n="021"/>
<p>codayati---<q>nanu cānuṣṭhānābhāvāt tathāpi bhavatūpadeśaḥ [na] tathā
bhaviṣyatītyuktam । na hyanupakārake kaścitpravartata ityuktam</q> । pariharati---
nanu cedamapyuktaṃ kartavyatāvagamāt pravartanīyaṃ nopakārāvagamāt sāpekṣatva-
prasaṅgāt iti</q> । yadā ca kartavyatāvagamamātreṇa phalaṃ vināpi pravṛttiḥ । <q>evaṃ ca
nityapratibandhako'pyayamapratibandhaka eva</q> । nityādhikāro bhavatā pratibandhako
darśitaḥ sa pratibandhaka eva na bhavati । tatra phalānabhyupagamāt । bandhaka upagraho
yadīti lokaprasiddhiḥ(?) । evamukte ca pūrvapakṣavādī svābhiprāyasāramāviṣkaroti---
<q>yadyevaṃ bhavatu tarhi sarvamevedaṃ nityavadanuṣṭheyaṃ phalamapi tathāpyasmatpakṣaḥ
siddha‍yatyeva</q> yāgaḥ kartavyatayopadiśyate kartṛviśeṣaṇaṃ ca svargakāmapadamiti । yato
yāgaḥ kartavyatayopadiśyate <q>ato na kāmaḥ</q> kāmyaḥ <q>svargādiḥ sādhyo bhavati
bhūtatayā'vagamāt</q> । yadi svargaḥ sādhyo na bhavati <q>kathaṃ tarhi nityaṃ kāmya-
miti yājñikā bhedenopadiśanti</q> sarvasya nityatvāt kāmo'syā nimittamiti ।
kāmyaṃ godva‍yaco'saṃkhyāparimāṇāśvāderyat iti yat । samādhatte---<q>nirmūlatvāda-
sadupadeśo bhaviṣyati</q> yājñikānām । punarākṣipati---yadi yāgassādhyaḥ <q>evaṃ
tarhi tadevedamāyātaṃ karturadhikāra iti</q> । sa evāha---<q>nirākṛtaṃ ca kartra-
bhidhāne svargakāmapadaṃ na saṃbadhyata</q> ityekādaśādye । samādhatte---<q>satyaṃ nirākṛtaṃ
nirupādānopasarjanatvaṃ</q>, nirupādāne kāme upasarjanatvaṃ nirākṛtam । <q>sopādā</q>-﻿
<pb n="022"/>
<q>nāyāṃ</q> tu kāmanāyāṃ <q>upasarjanatvaṃ</q> samudravat <q>sthāpitameva । guṇatvenābhi-
dhānāt</q> । kāmanāyāḥ karmaṇi guṇatvenābhidhānāt । pṛcchati---<q>kaḥpunarayoḥ</q>
sopādānanirupādānapakṣayo<q>rviśeṣaḥ</q> । ubhayatrāpi kartṛviśeṣaṇatvāt । uttaraṃ---<q>uktaṃ
sopādānatvaṃ nirupādānatvaṃ ca</q> । ekatra kāmanā upādeyā । anyatrānupādeyeti
viśeṣaḥ । praṣṭā āha---<q>satyamuktaṃ pratītau viśeṣaṃ pṛcchāmi । pratītau cet
saṃbandhopagamato viśeṣo'napekṣaḥ kiṃ viśeṣābhidhānena</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>satyaṃ yadi
viśeṣānapekṣaḥ saṃbandho'vagamyate । sa tvanupādāne nāvagamyata ityuktam</q> ।
tasmā dviśeṣo vaktavyaḥ । upasaṃharati-<q>tasmānna kartṛto'dhikṛtatvaṃ nāma pṛthagasti
kiñ‍cit । vaktavyo vā</q> kartṛtvādhikṛtatvayo<q>rviśeṣaḥ । nanu ca pravartamānaliṅā-
dibhiḥ pravṛttiḥ kriyate yathādarśitaṃ ṇijutpattau kurukurviti</q> । asyārthaḥ-pravartamānasya
pravartakalakṣaṇe prayojakavyāpāre ṇijutpadyate । tatra liṅādayaḥ prayujyamānā dṛśyante yathā
kurukurviti yathā । ato liṅādayo'pi pravartamānasyaiva pravṛttiṃ kurvanti । tena vede
pravṛttisiddha‍yarthaṃ kartṛtvātirekyadhikṛtatvaṃ nāma pṛthak vācyamiti । kurukurviti
saṃbhrame dvirvacanam । yata eva pravartamānasyaiva pravartane liṅādayaḥ <q>ata eva ca vedaivāsau
mayaitatkartavyamiti uyāyaṃ tu na veda iti bhāṣye'pyasti</q> । anena sāmānyena
pravṛttaḥ upāyadarśanena viśeṣe pravartata iti darśayan bhāṣyakāraḥ pravṛttapravartane liṅādaya
iti darśayati । <q>darśitaṃ ca <quote>‘abhicaran yajeta’</quote> iti samāmananti nābhicarita-
vyamiti</q> । anenāpi abhicāre tatsādhane ca sāmānyapravṛttau viśeṣe pravartata iti
darśitam । pariharati-<q>na tāvadidaṃ śakyate vak‍tum</q> pravartamānasyaiva pravartane
<pb n="023"/>
liṅādaya iti lakṣaṇāśravaṇāt (lakṣaṇe śravaṇāt) । vidhau hi liṅādayaḥ śra/?/yante ।
pravartakaśca vidhiḥ natvidamaparaṃ pravṛttasyāpravṛttasya ceti । <q>prayogavyabhicārācca</q> ।
prayoge vyabhicāra iti । apravṛttapravartane liṅādiprayogāt । etadeva vivṛṇoti-
<q>lakṣaṇaṃ tāvat pravartamānasyāpravartamānasya veti na viśeṣamācaṣṭe । prayogo'-
pyājñādiṣu apravṛttasyaiva dṛṣṭaḥ । nanu pratipannājñasyaiva liṅādayo bhavanti</q> ।
asyārthaḥ - yaḥ pratipannājñaḥ yenājñā pratipannā aṅgīkṛtā yadi sa eva taṃ pratyājñāṃ
dadāti । tena sāmānyena pravṛtasya ājñayā pravartana[ā/?/t]pravṛtteḥ pravṛttapravata/?/nājñāmapi
prayogamiti codayati(?) । pariharati---<q>na pravṛttapravartane prayogaḥ āmantraṇādiṣu
vyabhicārāt</q> । āmantraṇe hi apravṛttapravartane prayogo dṛṣṭaḥ । <q>ājñāyāmapyapravṛtta-
pravartana eva prayogaviśeṣe'pravṛttasyaiva pravṛttiḥ kriyate</q> । nanu sāmānyataḥ
pravṛtta eva viśeṣe pravartate । tatrāha---<q>na ca sāmānyataḥ</q> pravṛttiḥ <q>liṅādibhyo'-
vasīyate । viśeṣaniṣṭhatvāt</q> śabdārthasya । tena yā pravṛttirviśeṣaviṣayā liṅādibhiḥ
kriyate sā apravṛttasyaiva । yā tu sāmānyataḥ pravṛttā na tatra liṅādervyāpāra iti ।
nanu pravṛttimātraṃ liṅādibhiḥ viśeṣaviṣayasaṃbandhe hi viśeṣaniṣṭhateti । tatrāha---
<q>anvitābhidhānaṃ ca padānāmuktaṃ tadbhūtādhikāraṇe</q> । tena viśeṣaviṣayatānvitā-
meva pravṛttiṃ liṅādayo vadanti । <q>yatpunaridamuktaṃ ṇijutpattau kurukurviti darśayatīti
atrocyate---<q>na śabdaprayogamātrāt śabdārtho'vagantuṃ śakyate ananyathā-
siddhadarśanaṃ hi śabdārthaniyame</q> hetuḥ । vācakatāṃ vinā yasya prayogasya
<note>1. apravartasānasya ।</note>﻿
<pb n="024"/>
darśanaṃ nopapadyate sa prayogo vācakatāṃ niyamayati । yasya tu lakṣaṇayā gauṇyā
vā vṛttyā sāmānyavācitayā darśanaṃ tato na vācakatādhyavasānam । pravartakatā-
mātrābhidhāyakatayā ca pravṛttapravartane prayoga upapadyata eveti na tato
vācakatāyā niścayaḥ । kiṃñca sarveṣāmeva <q>kāraṇavatāṃ</q> kāryāṇāṃ yada<q>vyabhicāri</q>
tadeva kāraṇamuktami<q>tyuk‍tam</q> । tena vyabhicāritayā pravṛttapravartanamasya prayogasya na
kāraṇam । yacca yacchabdaprayoge kāraṇaṃ tat tadvācyam । ato na pravṛttapravartanam
liṅādīnāṃ vācyam । <q>nanu caivaṃ sati ājñādīnāmapyanaikāntika eva prayogaḥ</q>
ājñādīnāmapi apravṛttapravartanātmakānāṃ yaḥ prayogasso'pi vyabhicārī । ṇijutpattau
pravṛttapravartanāt । tasmādubhayorvyabhicārāt śabdārthaniyame kāraṇaṃ vaktavyam ।
pariharati---<q>idamucyate pravartanaṃ liṅādayo na vyabhicaranti sarvatrāvagateḥ
pravartamāne ca ṇijutpattiviṣaye apravṛtte cājñādau । ato'nvayavyatire-
kābhyāṃ tāvanmātrameva śabdārtha iti śakyate vak‍tum । yatpunaḥ <quote>‘vedaivāsau’</quote>
iti <quote>‘abhicaran yajeta’</quote> iti ca darśitaṃ tat sthite vyatirikte'dhikāre
kāmasaṃyuk‍teṣu prāp‍tyaprāptivivakṣayoktam । iha tu vyatirikto nāstī-
tyuktam । tasmādadarśanaṃ tat</q> । asyārthaḥ---etadadhikaraṇasiddhānte sthite
satyetaducyate kāmasaṃyukteṣu karmasu adhikārāpāditasādhanabhāveṣu phalābhiprāyeṇaiva
sāmānyataḥ pravṛttiḥ prāptā viśeṣatastvaprāptetyuktam । iha tvadhikāra eva kartṛvyati-
rekeṇa nāstītyākṣepaḥ । tenāyaṃ granthaḥ pratipakṣatayopanyasituṃ pūrvapakṣiṇaṃ prati na
<pb n="025"/>
śakya[ḥ/?/](m) । <q>yadi ca pravartamānasyaivāyamupadeśaḥ tadā upadeśārthataiva hīyate
asyedam sādhanamiti</q> siddhakarmaśaktisamarpaṇa<q>paratvāt</q> vākyasya । kasmāt punarevaṃ-
paratvepyupadeśasyārthavattā nāstītyāha---<q>na sādhanasvarūpe1 śābdaṃ pramāṇamastī-
tyuk‍tam, kiṃ tarhi ? anuṣṭhāna eva</q> । uk‍tamidaṃ codanāsūtre kārya evārthe
śabdasya prāmāṇyaṃ vyutpannamiti । vyutpattyapekṣaṃ ca śābdaṃ prāmāṇyamabhyupagantavyamiti
na sādhanarūpe prāmāṇyam । kintvanuṣṭhāna eva । <q>tasmādapravṛttapravatanamupadeśārtha
iti yuktam</q> । yata evāpravṛttapravartana eva liṅādīnāmupadeśakatvaṃ <q>ata eva ca
śabdavidaḥ pravartamānasya hetvabhidhānaṃ ṇico manyante । apravṛttasyaiva liṅā-
dīnām</q> । pravartamānasya hetoḥ pravartakasya(ā/?/pi) abhidhānaṃ ṇicā kriyate । apra-
vṛttasya pravartakābhidhānaṃ liṅādibhiriti śābdā manyante । anyathā ṇico liṅādīnāṃ
ca tulyamabhidhānaṃ syāt । yato'pravṛttapravartanameva liṅādyarthaḥ <q>tasmāt kartavyatāva-
gatirevānuṣṭhānahetuḥ na punaḥ phalābhilāṣaḥ</q> । kartavyatāvagatipūrvaṃ ca phalam ।
<q>tathā ca bhāvārthādhikaraṇe kuryādityuktvā svargakāmapadasaṃbandhāt svargaṃ
bhāvayedityuktam । na svargakāmaḥ svargaṃ kuryāditi</q> phalāvagamapūrvakaṃ kartavya-
tāvagamo noktaḥ । <q>avaśyaṃ caitadevaṃ</q> yathā vināpi kartavyatābhyupagamo bhavatītya<q>bhyupa-
gantavyaṃ, anyathā yāvajjīvādiṣvanadhikāraḥ syāt</q> । kartavyatāvagatirna syāt
ityarthaḥ । kutaḥ <q>sādhyāntarābhāvāt</q> । yadi kartṛtvātirikto'dhikāro nāsti sarveṣā-
madhikāraśūnyatayā samatvāt prayājādīnāmāgneyādīn pratyaṅgataiva na syāt । tadāha---
<note>1. mā. na sādhanabhūtaṃ</note>﻿
<pb n="026"/>
<q>nanu caivamaṅgasaṃbandho na prāp‍noti</q> । pariharati---<q>na prāp‍notyaṅgasaṃbandhaḥ
yadi śrutyādīni na pramāṇāni</q> । nanu śrutyādīnāṃ prāmāṇyamadhikārāyatta-
mityatrāha---<q>na caiṣāṃ prāmāṇyaṃ sādhyāntaraprayuktaṃ</q> nityeṣvapi sāṅgopadeśāt ।
yatrāpi phalaṃ nāsti nitye tatrāpi aṅgasaṃbandhāya(di) śrutyādītyabhyupagamāt । svargā-
dīnāmaphalatve'pi prayājādyaṅgasaṃbandho bhaviṣyati । etaccāpātamātreṇoktam । paramārthottara-
māha---<q>yadi ca na prāp‍noti</q> aṅgasaṃbandhaḥ <q>kiṃ kurmaḥ?</q> pramāṇānusāriṇo vayaṃ
yadi pramāṇato na yāgasaṃbandho bhavati na bhavatu । <q>uktaṃ cāsmābhiḥ</q> bādarimatānu-
vartibhiḥ <q>pṛthak prayojyā eva bhavantu prayājādaya iti । ye punaḥ dṛṣṭārthāḥ</q>
dravyaguṇasaṃskārā <q>niyamāyopadiśyante naivānaṅgaṃ karturadhikāre'pi</q> । tadidaṃ
bādarerapi sammatam । pūrvapakṣamupasaṃharati---<q>tasmāddhātvartha evopadeśaḥ na kāme</q> ।
yāga eva kartavyatāvagame'pi <q>kathaṃ nityeṣu</q> pratiṣedheṣu phalaśūnyeṣu <q>anuśāsyā iti</q> ।
anuśāsyā iti rūpasiddhau yat‍naḥ kartavyaḥ <quote>“etistu śāsvṛ”</quote> iti kyap bhavati ।
<q>saphale'pi cāpravartamānāḥ kaṃ daṇḍanumarhanti</q> ye phalāyopadiśyante na svarga
ityartha(?) । ayaṃ ca kriyāvākyārthapakṣo lokavyavahārānuguṇyāya । ye ca [phalāvagame
satyapi] na pravartante teṣāṃ kartavyam । <q>ataḥ pravṛttyavagatireva pravartane hetuḥ</q> ।
na phalam । pravṛttyavagame jāte'pi <q>apravartamānāḥ śrutamutsṛjanti kartavyaṃ na
kurvantīti । ataḥ sutarāṃ</q> tvatpakṣa eva <q>śās‍trasyānanuṣṭhāpakatvam</q> । asmatpakṣe
<pb n="027"/>
---<q>nanu ca kartradhikārapakṣe niyogo'narthakaḥ</q> । kathamanarthakaḥ ? uttaraṃ---<q>kartā hi
vyāpṛto vyāpṛtān vyāpārayiṣyatīti vā kārakavyapadeśaṃ labhate</q> । varta-
mānena bhūtena bhāvinā vā vyāpāreṇa kārakavyapadeśaḥ na punaḥ kālatraye'pi vyāpārā-
bhāve । vyāparanti iti prakṛtya(na)ntaraṃ bhauvādikam na punaḥ pṛṅ vyāyāme iti
taudādikaḥ । tataḥ kimityāha <q>tatra brāhmaṇādayo yāgādiṣu kiṃ vyāpṛtavanta
iti kartṛvyapadeśaṃ labhante । atha vyāparantīti athavā vyāpārayiṣyantīti ।
yadi tāvadva‍yāpṛtavantaḥ kiṃ niyogaḥ kariṣyati । atha vyāparantīti
tathāpyanarthaka eva</q> dvayorapi pravṛttatvāt pravṛrttthaṃ ca niyoga ityānarthakyam । <q>atha
vyāpārayiṣyantītyapyabhiprāyaḥ</q> । dūṣayati---<q>prāṅ‌niyogādvijñānamidam
kutaḥ ?</q> yasya niyogasaṃbandho'sti sa tadvaśāt vyāpārayiṣyatīti jñāyate । yasya
punarniyogasaṃbandho nāsti sa(ha)[na]vyāpāriṣyatītyetacchakyaṃ vijñātum । <q>niyogādeva
bhaviṣyatīdaṃ jñānamiti cet । na tarhi karturniyogaḥ</q> niyuktasya kartṛtvaṃ
<q>niyogasaṃbaddhasya kartṛtā prāp‍noti tasmāt karturadhikāro durbhaṇaḥ</q> । pariharati---
<q>nanu caivaṃ sati sarvakārakasaṃbandhāpalāpaḥ prāp‍noti</q> । prāṅ‌niyogasaṃbandhāt
tatrāpi kārakatvāyogāta । <q>kārakaśūnyāsu ca kriyāsu kiṃ niyogaḥ
kariṣyati । athānuṣ‍ṭheyatayā sarvakārakagrāmamavagamya tasya niyogo</q>﻿
<pb n="028"/>
<q>bhaviṣyatīti kartaryapi tulyam । evaṃ kartṛkartṛkaṃ yat karma tat tenaiva
kartavyamiti kariṣyamāṇābhiprāyeṇa</q> ca saṃbandhasiddhiḥ । yo yatra kartṛtvenāvagamyate
tattenaiva kartavyam । anyathā kartṛniyamāvagamabādhaḥ । tataśca kariṣyamāṇābhiprāyeṇa
kartṛtvena saṃbandhaḥ siddha‍yati । <q>ataḥ kartraradhikārepyanavadyam । avaśyaṃ caitat</q>
yatkartṛkaṃ yatkarma tat tenaiva kartavyamitya<q>bhyupagamanīyam</q> । siddhāntī kārakāṇāṃ
kārakātirekiṇīṃ daśāṃ nāṅgīkaroti yathā karturadhikāre'pi anavadyarūpāt । <q>teṣāmapi</q>
saṃbandhasiddha‍yarthaṃ hi yasmā<q>nnaivānyaḥ saṃbandho vijñāyate</q> viśiṣṭakārakaniyamavatīṃ
<q>niyogasiddhiṃ muktvā</q> । etaduktaṃ bhavati---yathā karaṇaviśeṣaniyamāt tadeva karaṇaṃ
tathā kartṛviśeṣaniyamāt sa eva kartā bhaviṣyati । upasaṃharati---<q>tasmādasaṃbandho
vā prāṅ‌niyogādabhyupagamanīyaḥ</q> । atha bhaviṣyadavasthāpekṣayā niyoganimittaṃ
kārakāṇāṃ saṃbandhaḥ tadā <q>tannimittaiva</q> sā <q>prāgapi</q> viniyogakartṛ<q>saṃbandhāvagati-
riti</q> । yadi punarekasyāpi kārakasya saṃbandho nābhyupagamyate tadā kārakaśūnyāsu
kriyāsu niyogānupapatteḥ niyogaikaviṣayasya <q>sthitaṃ prāmāṇyamuddharaṇīyam</q> । na ca
tadyuktaṃ sthitatvādeva iti । atha kaściccodayati---<q>nanu rājyādiṣu prāgadhi-
kārāt kriyākārakasaṃbandho dṛṣṭaḥ</q> । tena kimiti kariṣyamāṇābhiprāyeṇa saṃbandha-
siddha‍yā abhirucyate । kīdṛśe laukike prayoge ityatrāha---<q>evaṃkartṛke</q> rājye ।
madhye pṛcchati---<q>kathaṃkartṛke ?</q> viddaccharābhijanakartṛke bhavānadhikriyata ityevaṃvidhe
daṇḍanītyādiśāstravartini prayoge viśiṣṭakartṛviṣayaṃ prāguktvā adhikāraḥ k‍vaciducyata
iti । pariharati-<q>yuktaṃ rājyādiṣvatīteṣu</q> puruṣeṣu <q>tadguṇasya</q> vidhyādiguṇaśaktīnāṃ
<q>kartṛbhāvadarśanāt</q> । asyārthaḥ - rājyādiṣu yukta evāyaṃ prayogaḥ pūrvapuruṣāṇāṃ
<pb n="029"/>
yatkartṛkatvamavagataṃ tadabhiprāyeṇocyate viddaccharābhijanakartṛka iti । tathā saṃprati
na tasya tādṛśe viṣaye kartṛtvapradarśanāyedamucyate bhavānadhikriyata iti । tena yukta-
meva tatra bhūtakartṛpradarśanam । <q>iha punaḥ niyogādṛte puruṣāntaraṃ</q> kartṛtvena <q>na
śakyate vaktuṃ</q> tatpūrvakatvāt sarvapuruṣāṇāṃ pravṛtteḥ । tena bhaviṣyadabhiprāyeṇa kartṛ-
saṃbandhavarṇanam । <q>daṇḍanītyādiṣu punaḥ darśanāntarapūrvakatvādupadeśasyopapadyetāpi
anubhūtakartṛkepi viṣaye puruṣaviśeṣasyādhikāraḥ</q> । kartrantarakartṛke karmaṇi
kartrantarasaṃbandhānupapatteḥ na kartṛpratipādanamupapadyata iti kartṛtvātiriktatā adhikṛta-
syocyate ataḥ karturanyo'dhikṛta iti tatrāha---<q>tatrāpi ca arhatyarthakathana-
mātrameveti kartradhikāra eva; nādhikārāt kartṛtvam</q> । asyārthaḥ-viddaccharābhijana-
ityasyārthaḥ yatra rājye viddaccharo'bhijātaḥ kartṛtvamarhati tatra bhavataḥ kartṛtvamiti na
kartrantarāvarodhadoṣaḥ । ataḥ kartaivādhikṛtaḥ । (karturiti) <q>kartradhikāre ca svarga-
kāmitvaṃ kartṛviśeṣaṇaṃ na phalaviśeṣaṇamiti siddham</q> । evaṃ ca <q>sarvaṃ
sarvasyānuṣṭheyam</q> । yadi hi niyojyaviśeṣaṇāni svargakāmādīni padāni syuḥ
tadā bhedenaiva kāmanopādānāt sarvaṃ sarvasyānuṣṭheyaṃ na syāt । yadā tu
kartavyatāvagamamātreṇa kāmanāmaṅgabhūtāmupādāya karma kartavyaṃ tadā sarvaṃ karma sarvasya
puruṣasyānuṣṭheyam tathā bhāgaśo vidyopadeśo'yam । evaṃ ca bhāgaśaḥ bhāgena karmopa-
deśena <q>vidyopadeśo'yaṃ sarvapuruṣasya sarvakarmānuṣṭhānāt kṛts‍nasiddhiḥ</q> codita-
kṛts‍nārthānuṣṭhānasiddhiḥ । etaduktaṃ bhavati---sarvasya sarvānuṣṭhānaṃ vadan eka evānuṣṭhā-
teti darśayati । tenātmaikyapradarśanamidaṃ anuṣṭhānopadeśamukhena । <q>tadidamuktaṃ</q>---﻿
<pb n="030"/>
<q>sarvamidaṃ brahma bhāgaśa upadeśamukhena jñānato'nuṣṭhānataścopadiśyata iti</q> । tata-
stattvaṃ prakāśayediti vidhānāt । karmavidhīnāṃ tattvajñāne viniyuktatvāt jñānato
bhāgaśaḥ upadeśamukhenātmaikyamupadiśyate---sarvasya sarvamanuṣṭheyamiti aikātmyamanuṣṭhānata
upadiśyate । yata evāsmāt karmopadeśāt aikātmyamavagamyate <q>ata evodgāraḥ
kartradhikāravādināṃ <quote>‘asatye vartmani sthitvā tatassatyaṃ prakāśayet’</quote> iti</q> ।
sarvopadeśānāprayaṃ vidhiriti manyate । tatastattvaṃ prakāśayediti <q>sarvopadeśānāṃ</q>
tattvaprakāśanāyāyaṃ viniyogavidhiḥ, sarvopadeśāstattvaprakāśane viniyuktā ityarthaḥ । tena
tatvaprakāśane viniyuktatvāt karmopadeśapratibhāso'vidyaiva anyaparatvādvākyasya <q><quote>‘ta ime
satyāḥ kāmā anṛtāpidhānā’</quote> iti śruteḥ</q> । bhāgaśobhāgaśa upadeśo'nṛtamabhi-
pretaṃ tattvaprakāśane viniyuktatvāt । ato'nyaparādvākyāt karmopadeśapratītiranṛtamiti ।
tathā ca <q>rāgādinibandhanaśca vyavacchedo</q>'nṛtamabhipretam satyāḥ kāmādaya iti
śravaṇāt । tasmāt kārakādhikāradarśanāt adhikārāntaradarśanaṃ vyāmohaḥ । anena
prakṛtamupasaṃhṛtam । yata eva ca kartradhikāraḥ <q>ata eva ca dharmaśāstrakārāḥ paṭhanti-
kāmātmatā na praśasteti</q> kāmasiddhiṃ <q>phalasiddhimavaidikīṃ manvānāḥ</q> niṣphalatvāt
kāmanāyā(yāṃ) apraśastāṃ(statāṃ) kāmātmatāmāha । kāmyo hi <q>vedādhigamaḥ karma-
yogaśca vaidika</q> iti <q>jñāne karmaṇi ca viniyogaṃ manyate</q> । yadā aikātmya-
lakṣaṇatattvapratipattiparatayā sarvopadeśā viniyuktāḥ tadā vihitatvāt kāmyo vedādhi-
gamo vedārthādhigamaḥ । yadā ca (na) karmopadeśamātrapara[rā] bhāgaśa upadeśāḥ tadā
vede'pi vihitatvāt karmayogo'pi kāmya eva । <q><quote>“sarvaṃ khalvidaṃ brahma tajjalā-</q>﻿
<pb n="031"/>
<q>niti śānta upāsīta ityamumeva kartradhikārapakṣaṃ brāhmaṇavādo dyotayati ।</q>
kathaṃ dyotayatītyāha---<q>kāmye hi</q> kartavyatayā <q>upadiśyamāne na sarvakartṛsādhya
karma bhavati । bhedena</q> adhikāriviśeṣaṇabhūta<q>kāmadarśanāt । ataḥ sarva-
syaikyaṃ na siddha‍yati ।</q> sarvasya sarvānuṣṭhānapakṣe sarvo'nuṣṭhātā eka iti siddha‍yati
sarvasyaikyam । <q>tataśca puruṣa evedaṃ sarvamityādayo mantrārthavādā anupapannā
na syuḥ ।</q> nanu ca atrāpi pakṣe bhedavādānāṃ kā gatirityāha---<q>medavādāstu māgaśa
eva cedupadeśo yaḥ karmaviśeṣaviṣayaḥ tadāścita iti parihṛtam । ekatvaṃ
tu pāramārthike bhede kimāśritaṃ bhaviṣyati ।</q> yata eva kartratirekī niyojyo
nāsti <q>ata eva bhagavān pāṇiniḥ pacyādiṣu</q> dhātuṣu <q>kriyākārakavyatirekeṇa
na niyogārthe niyojyaṃ nāma karmāntaraṃ smarati । nanu 1yujirapi pacyā-
diṣveva paṭhyate</q> tena hi pūrvasyaiva yujeḥ karmasmaraṇāt pāṇininā niyojyo'pi
smṛta eva । pariharati---<q>satyaṃ paṭhyate na punaḥ yujeḥ karma yāgādiṣu karteti ।</q>
etaduktaṃ bhavati । pūrvaṃ niyojyasya sataḥ paścāt kartṛtvamiti na smarati । e(ka)ta-
marthamagṛhītvaiva punaścodayati---<q>nanu ca bhavataivedamuktaṃ kartā hi niyujyata iti ।</q>
evaṃ ca vadatā <q>tadidamuktaṃ bhavati yāgādiṣu kartā yujeḥ karmeti ।</q> paraharati---
<q>yadi yujeḥ sādhanaṃ kartṛrūpaṃ niyujyata ityucyate siddho naḥ pakṣaḥ</q> yadā kartuḥ
niyojyatvaṃ smarati tadā siddhaḥ eva pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ <q>kiṃ tarhi idamuktaṃ na smarati</q>
<note>1. tipūrvakayujerityarthaḥ---mā.</note>﻿
<pb n="032"/>
bhagavān pāṇiniriti । akārakābhiprāyaṃ taduktam ।</q> akārakabhūtaṃ niyojyaṃ
na smaratītyarthaḥ । etadeva vivṛṇoti---<q>tatra kāme sādhye pūrvaṃ tāvat niyogaḥ
tataśca niyogāt kartṛtvaṃ</q> niyoga <q>ityarthāntarāpattiḥ arthāntare cānavagatastati
rastītyuktam । tadidaṃ kāmināṃ phalāśaṃsanaṃ ākāśe bakabandhana(mivaṃ)-
prabhaṃ kāmināṃ moha ityuktam । tasmāt kartradhikāraḥ sūribhiruktaḥ bhūtaṃ
bhavyāyopadiśyate itya</q>nayā yuktyā । yata eva kāmopayogena[kāmo'pi niyogena na]
sādhyate <q>ata eva cākhyātabhedopyupapadyate kiñ‍cidguṇakarma kiñ‍citpradhāna-
karmeti । kāmye punassādhye sarvākhyātānāṃ guṇabhāvāpattiḥ</q> phalaṃ prati guṇa-
bhūtatvāt । <q>tataśca tāni dvaidhamiti sūtrārtho'nupapannaḥ syāt । nanu ca nityābhi-
prāyaḥ sūtrārthī bhaviṣyati ।</q> nityānāṃ phalābhāvāt । <q>na nityābhiprāyaḥ</q>
sūtrārthaḥ । <q>tatrāpi</q> nityeṣvapi <q>kāraṇaṃ arthāntarāpattidarśanāt <quote>“yaistu dravyaṃ
cikīrṣyata”</quote> iti guṇataiva prāp‍noti ।</q> asyārthaḥ---yadā kāmādhikāre yāgā guṇa-
bhāvenākhyātenocyante tadā nityādhikārepi guṇabhāvenaivākhyātenābhidhānaṃ kartavyam ।
anyathā'nekārthaprasaṅgāt । na ca guṇabhāvo nirviṣayaḥ kārakāṇāṃ viśeṣadarśanena
<pb n="033"/>
tadarthatayā guṇabhāvopapatteḥ । <q>asmatpakṣe punaḥ dravyaparatayā upadeśe guṇabhāvaḥ ।
kriyāpare hyupadeśe prādhānyamiti sūktam ।</q> nanu dravyacikīrṣāmātreṇa sūtrakāro
guṇabhāvamāha na punardravyaparatvenopadeśasya, tatrāha---<q>cikīrṣyata iti copadeśābhi-
prāyeṇa ।</q> yadeva hi śāstrālocanayā pradhānaṃ pratibhāti tadeva cikīrṣyate nānyaditi ।
tena yāgādiṣu kriyāparatve upadeśasya pradhānakarmatā । dravyaparatve tu guṇakarmateti
siddhaṃ dvaividhyam ।</p>
<p><q>atrābhidhīyate । sa nāma kartṛviśeṣaṇaṃ bhavati yasya viśeṣaṇa-
bhāva[ve]kāraka upapadyate । iha punaḥ prītyapagame tadeva tu dravyaṃ na svarga-
śabdābhilapanīyam ।</q> ataḥ[na] prītivacanaḥ svargaśabda iti । <q>kimato yadyevaṃ ?</q>
uttaraṃ---<q>idaṃ tato bhavati---iṣṭaṃ kāmasya viṣaya iti । tataḥ kiṃ ? neṣṭaṃ
paraniṣpattaye bhavati ।</q> iṣṭarūpā prītiḥ yāganiṣpattyarthā na bhavati । <q>iṣṭārthaṃ hi
sarvam ।</q> etadeva vivṛṇoti---<q>etaduktaṃ bhavati---iṣṭasaṃyukte hi vākye tadartha-</q>
katayaiva <q>hyanvayo'nyeṣāṃ padārthānām ।</q> atastathātra vākyārtho varṇayitavyaḥ
yathā iṣṭaniṣpattyarthaḥ itareṣāṃ padārthānāmanvayo bhavati । tatra yadi kartṛviśeṣaṇatā''-
śrīyate samudravadupasarjanatā svargasya syāt । niyojyaviśeṇatve tu vakṣyamāṇanyāyena
kāmyasiddhiparyantatvānniyojyabhāvasya iṣṭārthe padārthānāṃ [anvayo] bhavatīti niyojya-
viśeṣaṇatā svargasyāśrayaṇīyā । yadidamasmābhiruktaṃ <quote>‘neṣṭaṃ paraniṣpattaye’</quote> iti
tadidamuktaṃ---prītirūpatvāt kāmasaṃbandhācca iṣṭārthaścānvayo'nyeṣāṃ padārthānāṃ
<q><quote>“karmāṇyapi jaiminiḥ phalārthatvāt”</quote> <quote>“phalaṃ ca puruṣārthatvāt”</quote> iti ।</q>
﻿<pb n="034"/>
iṣṭatva deva phalasya na <q>kratvarthaṃ</q> phalamityartha । phalaṃ ca puruṣārthatvādityatra codayati---
<q>nanu ceṣṭaḥ svarga ityuktam</q> prītirūpatvāt kāmasambandhācca iṣṭārthaśca nvayo'nyeṣāṃ
padārthānāmityuktam । <q>sa ca puruṣārtha iti vipratiṣiddham ।</q> pariharati---
<q>apuruṣārthasya vā kathamiṣṭatā</q> icchāviṣayo hīṣṭa ityucyate । ātmasaṃbandhinī ca
prītiriṣṭeti nāpuruṣārthasyeṣṭatā । <q>evaṃ tarhi puruṣārthamevedaṃ sarvamityuktaṃ bhavati</q>
neṣṭārthatā । rāddhāntī parituṣṭa āśāste---<q>satyamevaṃ prājño'pyāyuṣmān
bhava ।</q> punaścodayati <q>iṣṭopanyāsastarhi kimarthaḥ ?</q> śāstrasya puruṣārthatvādeva
niyojyaviśeṣaṇatā svargakāmasyocyatāmiti bhāvaḥ । uttaraṃ <q>neṣṭārthatvādṛte
puruṣārthatā sidhyati</q> śāstrasya । puruṣārthenaiva śāstreṇa bhavitavyamiti nāsti pramāṇam ।
iṣṭatvādeva tu svargasya puruṣārthatā śāstrasya sambhavatīti sārtha eveṣṭopanyāsaḥ
yadidaṃ puruṣasya karmajanyaphalayogitayā karmaṇi śeṣitvam sa cāyamadhikāra
ityucyate ।</q> īśvaravacano hyadhikṛtaśabdaḥ । asmin grāme ayamadhikṛtaḥ īśvara
iti gamyate । tenaiśvaryamevādhikāraḥ karmaṇi । yata eva ca kasyacit karmaṇyapyaiśvarya-
masti <q>ata eva tulyepi kartṛtve svāmikarmakaravyapadeśaḥ ।</q> yadi kartṛtvāti-
riktaṃ svāmitvaṃ na syāt । tasmādadhikārādeva svāmivyapa/?/deśaḥ । parārtha karmakāritvācca
karmakaravyapadeśaḥ । atra codayati---<q>nanu ca yāge naiva karmakarassambhavati ।</q> svatyāga-
rūpatvena yāgasya svayameva karteti na puruṣāntarādyanupraveśassaṃbhavati । pariharati---
<q>na nāma padārthe</q> yāgamātre saṃbhavati । <q>śāstrārthe tu</q> adhikārasādhanībhūte yāge
anekapadārthopakṛte padārthāntarānuṣṭhānasiddhaye <q>saṃbhavatyeva</q> karmakaraḥ । <q>padārthāstu</q>﻿
<pb n="035"/>
<q>sāmarthyenāpi vyavatiṣṭheran ।</q> kañcideva kaścideva padārthaṃ karoti na sarvaḥ sarvam ।
<q>nanu ca bhāvārthāḥ karmaśabdā ityuktam ।</q> asyārthaḥ-bhāvārthāḥ karmaśabdā ityatra
bhāvārthānāṃ sādhyatvamuktam na ca sādhyadvayamekasmin vākye saṃbadhyata iti । <q>na ca
kāme sādhye yāge kartṛtvamupapadyata iti</q> kāmye svargādau sādhye yāge kartṛtvaṃ nopapadyata
iti yāge kartṛtvābhāvāt kartṛsaṃkhṅ‍yāvācinī yajeḥ parā kiñcidvibhaktirna yujyate । <q>kathaṃ
svargaśabde iṣṭavacane grāmādiṣvadhikārasiddhiḥ</q> grāmādiśabdānāmiṣṭavacanatvābhāvāt ।
anantaraṃ codyaṃ pariharati---<q>uktaṃ kāmaviṣayatayā svargādyuya/?/nyāso na kāma-
viśeṣaṇatayeti ।</q> etaduktaṃ bhavati-kāmaviṣayavacanatayā svargādīnāṃ siddhānto'bhi-
mataḥ, sacāyaṃ prakāraḥ grāmādiṣvaviśiṣṭaḥ iti । <q>nanu cānvayavyatirekau svarga eva
saṃbhavataḥ ।</q> pariharati---<q>uktamasmābhiḥ viṣayapradarśanārthāvanvayavyatirekau ।</q>
anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ hi prītivacanatayā svargaśabdasya kāmaviṣayatayā svarga ucyata
iti । <q>kāmasaṃyogāttu grāmādīnāṃ viṣayatvasiddhiḥ ।</q> na hyakāmyaṃ kāmanā-
marhatītyuktam । tasmātteṣvapi siddho'dhikāra iti । dvitīyaṃ codyamanubhāṣate---<q>yadapi
kāmye sādhye yāge kathaṃ kartṛtvamiti ।</q> pariharati---<q>kena voktaṃ yāge kartṛtva-
miti । yāge tvadhikāraḥ tatsiddha‍yarthaṃ cārthāt kartṛtvaṃ</q> īśvarataiva ।
niṣpattimantareṇa kriyāyāḥ phalabhāvo(ve) nopapadyata iti yāgasiddhau puruṣasya kartṛtvam ।
yata eva yāgepyarthāt kartṛtvaṃ <q>ata eva saṅkhyāniveśaḥ</q> । yadi svargasiddhau kartuḥ
sato yāge'dhikāraḥ tadā karturadhikāra ityucyate । yāge kartussato'dhikāro nāsti ।
kintu yāge'dhikṛtasya kartṛtvamiti tena nāsti doṣaḥ । lokavyavahārānusāritayā
<pb n="036"/>
svapakṣe'bhyuccayamāha---<q>loke'pi cānyatrādhikṛto'nyat sādhayati ।</q> tathā
<q>rājakarmasvadhikṛto'mātyaḥ svārthaṃ sādhayati । tatsiddha‍yarthaṃ tu rājakarmaṇi
kartṛtvam ।</q> prathamaṃ codyamanubhāṣya pariharati---<q>yadapi bhāvārthāḥ karmaśabdā iti
yatrādhikāraḥ</q> tebhyaḥ <q>phalāvagatirityuktaṃ bhavati ।</q> asyārthaḥ - yadidaṃ yāgasya
sādhyatvamuktaṃ bhāvārthāḥ karmaśabdā ityanena tenedamuktaṃ bhavati yeṣu yāgeṣu bhāvārtheṣvadhi-
kāraḥ tebhyaḥ phalāvagatiriti । etadeva vivṛṇoti-<q>tena sādhanena svārthamabhinirvarta-
yedityarthaḥ ।</q> tenādhikārī viṣayabhūtena bhāvārthena sādhanena svārthamabhinirvarta-
yedityarthaḥ । etaduktaṃ bhavati - bhāvārthaḥ sādhanatayaiva saṃbadhyate । sādhanasya hi
tādṛśaṃ rūpaṃ yat kartṛvyāpāraviṣayo bhavati । yathā paraśuḥ । udyamananipātanalakṣaṇo hi
kartṛvyāpāraḥ paraśuviṣaya eva na sākṣāt dvaidhībhāvaviṣayaḥ । tathāpi dvaidhībhāvassādhyaḥ
sādhanameva paraśuḥ । evamihāpi puruṣaprayatnasādhyau svarganiyogau । na ca tayoḥ
sākṣāt puruṣaprayat‍naviṣayatā । kintu yāgādeḥ sādhanasya tathā sati abhūtasvabhāvatvāt
bhāvārthānāmutpattiranena puruṣaprayat‍nena । na caitāvatā sādhanatvahāniḥ sādhyatvahāniḥ
sādhyatvāpattireva vā, niyogasya phalasya sādhyatvāvagamāt । tena sādhanabhāvāpattyaiva
yāgādeḥ kartṛvyāpāraviṣayatayā sādhyatā bhāvārthādhikaraṇe pradarśitā । kathaṃ punaḥ
anyaviṣayasya kartṛvyāpārasyānyasādhyatā bhavet ? uddiśya pravṛttatvāt । niyogaṃ phalaṃ
coddiśya kartṛtvavyāpāraḥ pravartate । nāntarīyakatayā tu sādhanībhūtabhāvārthaviṣayo
bhavati nāntarīyakakartṛvyāpāraviṣayatvādeva bhāvārthānāṃ anīpsitakartavyatā iṣyate ।
yata eva bhāvārthāḥ sādhanatathaiva saṃbadhyante <q>ata eva tṛtīyāsāmānādhikaraṇyāt
ud‌bhidādīnāṃ nāmatā uktā ।</q> anyathā hi tṛtīyāntānāṃ bhāvārthani(i)ṣṭhatvāna-
vagamāt icchāsāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ(na)syāt । yadi svarga eva sādhyaḥ <q>tarhi kimidamuktaṃ</q>﻿
<pb n="037"/>
<q>nāmnaḥ sakāśāt kartavyatā nāvasīyata iti । kena voktaṃ tadanyathā</q>,
prātipadikaṃ kartavyatāṃ nāvagamayatyeva । <q>kathaṃ tarhi kāmasya kartavyatā ?</q>
uttaraṃ---<q>iṣṭatvāvagamāt</q> iṣṭaviṣayatvādityuktam । nanu yadi niyojyo'sau vākyārthe-
'nvayī syāt tadā iṣṭatvāvagamāt niyojyaviśeṣaṇatayā'nvayaḥ syāt na cāsā-
vastītyāśaṅkya mūlayuktimāha---<q>avaśyaṃ caitadevamabhyupagantavyam ।</q> kartṛvyati-
rikto niyojyo'vaśyāṅgīkaraṇīyaḥ । <q>na hi kriyākārakasaṃbandhamātrāvagamā-
danuṣṭhānāvagatiḥ । devadattaḥ kāṣṭhaiḥ sthālyāmodanaṃ pacatītyevamādiṣu</q> varta-
mānāpadeśeṣu satyapi kriyākārakasaṃbandhe anuṣṭheyamityavagamābhāvāt । <q>nanu ca
liṅādibhyo'nuṣṭhānāvagatirbhaviṣyati ।</q> devadattaḥ pacet iti liṅādiyukta-
vākyaśravaṇe pravṛttidarśanāt anuṣṭhānāvagamaṃ ca vinā tadasaṃbhavāt liṅādibhyo'nuṣṭhā-
nāvagatirbhaviṣyatīti vijñāyate । <q>kasya liṅādayo'nuṣṭhānaṃ jñāpayanti iti ।</q>
asyārthaḥ-yadyapi liṅādayaḥ kāryabodhakatayā anuṣṭhānāvagamaṃ kurvanti iti yaśca
svasaṃbandhitayā'nuṣṭhānamavabudhyate sa pravartate । tena yasyānuṣṭhānaṃ jñāpayanti liṅādayaḥ
so'dhikārī tāvadaṅgīkaraṇīyaḥ । yadarthaṃ hi yatkarma tasya tatra kartavyatāvagatiḥ ।
yasya niyojyatvaṃ tasyādhikāritā । tena pūrvaṃ niyojyatvena devadattādīnāṃ saṃbandhaḥ ।
paścādadhikāritāyāmanuṣṭhānāvagatiḥ । tato'nuṣṭhānamiti ।</p>
<p><q>nanu ca kartarītyuktam ।</q> karturanuṣṭhānaṃ liṅādayo'vabodhayantītyuktam ।
pṛthak pariharati---<q>ayuktamuktam । itaretarāśrayaprasaṅgāt ।</q> yasyānuṣṭhānāvagatiḥ
tasya kartṛtā । yasya ca kartṛtvaṃ tasyānuṣṭhānāvagatirityuktam । <q>tathā ca karturni-
yogo'narthaka iti ।</q> yadi ca kartṛtvaṃ yāvatsampannaṃ kimaparaṃ kāryatvāvagamena ।
<pb n="038"/>
itaretarāśrayaṃ vivṛṇoti---<q>yadi hi niyogāt1 kartṛtvaṃ kartṛtve ca niyoga iti
itaretarāśrayāpattiḥ ।</q> tasmānniyoga eva pūrvamaṅgīkaraṇīyaḥ tato <q>niyogāt
kartṛtvaṃ mantavyam । niyojyāvagatistu anyataḥ evāyamatra ।</q> niyojyo
nāma kāryasya boddhā kāryaṃ prati boddha‍ṛtayā svargakāmādaya upādīyante । loke ca
saṃbodhanavibhaktiyogāt boddha‍ṛtayā'nvayo devadattādīnām । tena lokavyavahārānu-
sāreṇāpi niyojyo vākyārthānvayīti siddham । yadīṣṭasaṃbandhānniyojyaviśeṣaṇa-
samarpakatā evaṃ tarhi <q>yāvajjīvādiṣu kathaṃ ?</q> siddhāntī pṛcchati---<q>kathaṃ vā'tra
na bhaviṣyati ?</q> pūrvapakṣī tvāha---<q>siddhavadupadeśājjīvanasya</q> yadi sādhyatayā
jīvanamupadiśyate tadā sādhyatvāvagamāt tadānuguṇyena niyojyaviśeṣaṇaṃ syāt ।
yadā tu siddhavajjīvanamupadiśyeta tadā na niyojyaviśeṇatā । rāddhāntaikadeśī
vadati---<q>tvayaiva tarhyuktaṃ na jīvanaṃ kartṛviśeṣaṇatayā'nveti siddhatvādeveti ।</q>
dūṣayati---yadi tāvat siddhatvādeveti niṣpannatvādevetyabhiprāyakaṃ <q>ayuktamidaṃ siddha-
meva hi kārakaṃ viśeṣaṇatayā'nveti na sādhyam ।</q> atha siddhatvādavagatatvāditi
mataṃ tatrāha---yadi nāma viśeṣaṇaphalamatra na sambhavati <q>na punaranvayo'pi anvayācca
phalāvagatiśśābdī, na phalavato'nvayaḥ sāpekṣatvaprasaṅgāditi ।</q> yadi phalamava-
gamyānvayo varṇyate tadā phalāvagamāpekṣaṃ vedasyāvabodhakatvamiti sāpekṣatā syāt ।
<q>tasmāt kathamatrādhikāro</q> jīvanādiṣviti <q>vaktavyam</q> ।</p>
<p><q>ayamucyate---yāvajjīvamiti yāvacchabdo nānveti kartṛviśeṣaṇa-</q>
<note>1. tanniyogāt</note>﻿
<pb n="039"/>
<q>pakṣe । kathaṃ ? na yāvajjīvaṃ prayogassaṃbhavati</q> phalārthino yāvajjīvaṃ prayogassaṃ-
bhavati । (yadi)<q>vītāyāṃ phalecchāyāmaprayogāt ।</q> yadi jīvanaṃ kartṛviśeṣaṇaṃ bhavati
tadā svargakāmādhikārānupraveśitā, nādhikārāntaram । naṃ ca phalārthitayā yāvajjīvaṃ
prayogassaṃbhavati । yadi (jīvi)hi vītāyāmapi phalecchāyāṃ prayogaḥ syāt tadā
jīvanaṃ prayoge vyāpyeta । na caitadasti । tasmādyathā jāvanavyāptiḥ prayoge (na)syāt
tathā vācyam । nimittabhūte ca jīvane vyāptirupapadyata iti nimittatvameva jīvana-
syābhyupeyam । <q>tacca</q> jīvananimittaṃ[ttatvaṃ] <q>adhikṛtasaṃbandha upapadyate ।</q> adhi-
kārāyattatvādanuṣṭhānasya na kartṛsaṃbandhe nimittatvopapattiḥ । <q>kartṛsaṃbandhe hi yāvade-
voktaṃ yajeteti tāvadeva jīvatā yaṣṭavyamiti ।</q> tena na nimittatvopapattiḥ ।
nanu mābhūnnimittatvaṃ kimetenetyatrāha---<q>yāvacchabdānupapattirdarśitā ।</q> asati
nimittatve (na)kartṛviśeṣaṇaniyojyaviśeṣaṇasandehe niyojyaviśeṣaṇataiva nyāyyā prāthamyā-
dityāha-<q>na ca prākkartṛtvasaṃyogāt niyojyāparijñāne kartṛtvasiddhirityuktam ।</q>
api ca kartṛviśeṣaṇapakṣe ānarthakyāt <q>pakṣāntarāvalambenāpi (na) prayojana-
vattā vaktavyeti nyāyavido manyate ।</q> tenārthavatī niyojyaviśeṣaṇatā''śravaṇīyā ।
yathā avaśyāśrayaṇīyatayā niyojyaviśeṣaṇatā(yā) svargakāmādīnām । <q>na tarhi
iṣṭatvādadhikārasiddhiḥ ।</q> rāddhāntī āha---<q>na nāma</q> yadyapyavaśyāśrayaṇīyatayā
niyojyaśravaṇaṃ tathāpīṣṭatvaṃ adhikāriviśeṣaṇatve na na hetuḥ, api tu hetureveṣṭatvena । na
hi akriyārthatā akriyārthatvena cādhikāriviśeṣaṇamiti neṣṭam । paraniṣpattaya iti
syāt kriyārthatā । akriyārthatve ca tadarthataiva kriyāyāḥ tadarthā ca kriyā niyojya-
viśeṣaṇatve bhavatīti niyojyaviśeṣaṇatvaṃ niścīyate । upasaṃharati---<q>iti siddho
<pb n="040"/>
<q>naimittike nitye cādhikāraḥ । yatpunaridamuktaṃ 1sādhanatvenetareṣāmiva kāra-
kāṇāṃ kartṛtvasiddhiriti ।</q> yathā karaṇādīni kārakāṇi sādhanatvenāvagamyante
tathā kartāpi sādhanatvenaivāvagamyate । <q>ataśca kriyāsaṃbandhitayaiva niyojyāva-
gatiriti ।</q> anubhāṣya dūṣayatiḥ---<q>ayuktamidaṃ, anuṣṭhānato'pi kriyāsaṃbandho-
'vagamyate saṃbandhāntarasyāvidyamānatvāt ।</q> asyārthaḥ---karturhi kriyāsaṃbandho
'nuṣṭhānanibandhanaḥ । na cānuṣṭhānāvagatiṃ vinā'nuṣṭhānamasti । na cādhikāraṃ
vinā'nuṣṭhānāvagatiḥ karmaṇi । na ca svasaṃbandhikāryabodhaṃ vinā'dhikāraḥ । tena
niyojyatā prāgāśrayaṇīyā । <q>tasmāt yathoktameva nyāyyam ।</q> iṣṭatvāvagamāt
svargādeḥ, iṣṭārthatayā ca sakalapadārthānvayāt niyojyaviśeṣaṇatā svargakāmāde(ryu)ruktā,
tāmakṣamamāṇa āha---<q>karmaṇi niyujyamānasya</q> svargakāmasya <q>kāmasiddhau yāgaḥ
karaṇamiti kasya śabdasyātra nimittabhāvaḥ ?</q> asyārthaḥ-lokavyavahārānusāri-
tayā karmaiva kāryatayā liṅādibhiravagamyate । niyojyo'pi ta deva kāryamavabudhyate na
karmaṇyeva niyuktiṃ tathā ca sati karmaṇi niyujyamānasya svargakāmasya kāmasiddhau
kāmyamānaphalasiddhau yāgaḥ karaṇamiti kasya śabdasyātra vyāpāraḥ ? na kasyacidapīti
bhāvaḥ । tena niyojyaviśeṣaṇatve'pi neṣṭārthatayā sakalapadārthānvaya iti na tadbalena
niyojyaviśeṣaṇatayā niścīyate । tadeva prapañcayati-<q>yajeteti yajistāvat</q> yāga-
mātramācaṣṭe, na punastasyānyasaṃbandhitām । <q>vibhaktirapi tatrākhyātī yāga-
sādhanaṃ kartāraṃ</q> vaiyākaraṇamatyā <q>tadantargatāṃ vā saṅkhyāṃ</q> mīmāṃsakamatenācaṣṭe <q>na
punaryāgasyānyārthatāmapi । svargakāmapadamapi ca svargaṃ puruṣasyeṣṭatayā jñāpa-</q>
<note>1. sādhyatvenetareṣāmiva</note>﻿
<pb n="041"/>
<q>yati na punaryāgaṃ prati prādhānyaṃ svargasya kāmasya</q> vā ityanādaraḥ । <q>vibha-
k‍tistu prathamā'vyatirik‍tārthaiva</q> na prādhānyāvabodhikā । <q>jyotiṣṭomādayastu
nāmatvāt yāgābhidhānaparatantrāḥ</q> tatsāmānādhikaraṇyena nāmamātrāvagamāt ।
<q>na ca yajeteti śabdaḥ yāgaṃ karaṇatvenācaṣṭe ityuktam । tasmānnirmūlamevedaṃ
yāgena svargaṃ sādhayediti</q> jñānam । <q>yo'pyatra niyogārthaḥ</q> kāryātmakaḥ <q>sa kāme
vā puruṣaṃ niyuṅk‍te yāge vā</q> । kāmo vā kāryatayā'vagamyate yāgo vā ।
<q>ato'nyataratra niyogamātrāvagatirbhaviṣyati na punastayoḥ parasparaṃ
saṃbandhāvagatiḥ</q> ।</p>
<p><q>nanu ceṣṭatvaṃ nānyathopapadyate yadi na yāgāt kāmasiddhirityuk‍tam ।
kvedaṃ dṛṣṭam ? iṣṭatvaṃ sādhanādṛte na bhavatīti । iṣṭatvādeva</q> icchāviṣaya-
tvādeva <q>tadiṣṭaṃ bhavati</q> । āśaṅkyati---<q>iṣṭaṃ sādhyatayā'vagamyata iti cet</q> ।
dūṣayati---<q>ayuktaṃ kena śabdenāsya sādhyatocyate । kāmasaṃbandhamātramavagamyate
svargasya na punaḥ sādhyaḥ siddho</q> vetyavagamyate । sādhyatvepi cānyasādhyasyaiva kāmanā-
yogo na viruddha‍yate । <q>tasmādvak‍tavyamatra nimittaṃ yena yāgasya kāraṇatā'vagamyate
varaṃ pūrvapakṣa evāstu</q> kartṛviśeṣaṇaṃ svargakāmanimittamiti bhāvaḥ । asyārthaḥ - loke
vyavahārānusāritayā karmaiva kāryatayā liṅādibhiravagamyate । niyojyo'pi tadeva
kāryamavabudhyate tena karmaṇyeva niyuktiḥ । tathā ca sati karmaṇi niyujyamānasya svarga-
kāmasya kāmasiddhau kāmyamānaphalasiddhau yāgaḥ karaṇamiti kasya śabdasyātra padaṃ
<pb n="042"/>
vibhaktiyogāt । upasaṃharati---<q>tasmādbhavatvadhikāriviśeṣaṇaṃ svargakāmapadaṃ,
bhavatu svargakāmo niyojyaḥ na punaryāgena svargaṃ sādhayediti</q> jñānaṃ bhavati
<q>nimittābhāvāt</q> ।</p>
<p>siddhāntī vadati---<q>atrābhidhīyate kāmyamānatvena svargaḥ puruṣaṃ viśina-
ṣṭītyuktam</q> । kāmī tu niyujyata ityetadapyuktam । <q>bhāvārthe ca niyoga ityetada-
pyuktam । seyaṃ niyoganiyojyaviṣayatayaikavākyatā na vā'yathārthatve
ekavākyatā saṃbhavati</q> । yasya yo'rthaḥ padasya tasya tamatikramyaikavākyatā na saṃbhavati
padārthānāmeva vākyārthatvāt । <q>niyogasiddhiśca vākyārthaḥ</q> kāryaṃ hi niyuñjānaṃ
[ñjat]puruṣaṃ niyoga ityucyate tasya siddhirvākyārtha iti codanāsūtre uktam ।
<q>tatra vāvat yadi yāgasya kartavyatā</q> ucyate <q>tadā niyojyārtho nānveti
niyoge</q> । sa hi svargaṃ kāmayate । yadi ca yāga eva kartavyaḥ svargakāmitayā
tarhi puruṣo niyoge nānveti api puruṣamātratayā । na ca puruṣamātraṃ svargakāmeno-
cyate । <q>atha kāmaḥ</q> svarga eva kartavyatayocyate, ananvito viṣayaḥ syāt
niyojyena । <q>tataścaikaniyogāvagatiḥ pīḍyeta</q> । yadyevaṃ tarhi yāga eva kartavyaḥ
ityatrāha---<q>yāgaprādhānye cokto doṣaḥ</q> niyojyānanvayalakṣaṇaḥ <q>tasmāt kāmapradhāna-
tayaiva ekaniyogasaṃbandhaḥ</q> । yāgena svargaṃ sādhayediti tvāśrīyamāṇe sarvānvayo-
papattiḥ । tadidamuktaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa---<quote>“api ca yasya svarga iṣṭaḥ syāt sa yāgamabhi-
<note>(1) m. s. ekasaṃbandhaniyojyasambandhāvagatiḥ</note>﻿
<pb n="043"/>
nirvartayedityasaṃbaddhamiva anyadicchatyanyat karoti”</quote> iti (6-1-3) asādhana-
bhūte kāmino niyojyatayā saṃbandho na syādityarthaḥ । nirnimittatāṃ kāmasya nirāka-
rīti---<q>padamatra nimittamiti śakyate vak‍tum</q> । svargakāmapadameva yāgasya sādhya-
tayāsvargamāha । yajeteti padameva svargasādhanatayā yāgamāha । nanvatraivaṃvidhārthatā na
pratīyate ityatrāha---<q>yattvabhidhānāvivekapratipādanamuktaṃ tadanvitābhidhānenaiva
pratyuktam</q> । anvitābhidhāyīni padānyuktāni tenānvayayogyatayā svargādipadānāmevaṃ-
bhūtārthatvamasti । <q>evaṃ tarhi tadbhūtādhikaraṇa evaitatparihṛtam</q> । tadbha‍ūtādhi-
karaṇe hi vṛddhavyahārasiddhārthābhidhāyakatayā upādānamityuktam । tenātrāsiddhā evaṃ-
vidhārthatā nopapadyate iti tenaivedaṃ parihṛtaṃ pratyuktamityasyārthaḥ । samādhatte---<q>asaṃbaddhaiva
padapadārthāvagatirityetāvatparihṛtam</q> । asaṃbaddhānyeva padāni padārthāścāsaṃbaddhā
eva ityetāvat tatra parihṛtaṃ bhabati । kuta ityāha---<q>pratibhāsyānyāpohāvāpoddhāra-
pratipakṣatayā tadadhikaraṇam । na punaḥ padaiḥ padārthamātrābhidhānapratipattaye</q> ।
nimittaśūnyapratibhāsamātraṃ saṃsṛṣṭavākyārthāvagatiriti । tathā anyāpohaviṣayo vikalpa-
mātrametaditi । tathā vidyamānapadārthāvāpoddhāreṇa vyutpannā vākyārthamavagamayanti
ityetāvatā pūrvapakṣaṃ nirākartuṃ tadadhikaraṇam । na punaḥ padairanvayavyatirekānu-
vidhayipadārthamātramabhidhīyate ityevaṃ param । tadanenānvayābhidhānāt anvayānavagati-
rnirākṛtā । <q>tasmādyāgena svargaṃ sādhayediti yuktam</q> । ato niyojyaviśeṣaṇatve
iṣṭārtha evānvayo nirvahatīti tadevāśrayaṇīyam । eṣā cātra darśanasthitiḥ---codanāsūtre
kāryaṃ vāvayārtho na siddhamiti sādhyate । tasya tu kāryasya svasaṃbandhitayā boddhā
niyojyo'stīti ṣaṣṭhādye vyutpādyate । kāmini ca niyojye kāmakāryayoḥ sādhyasādhana-
bhāvo'stīti bādaryadhikaraṇavyutpādyamevātrocyate, niyojyāvagamanibandhanatvāt । tacca
kāryaṃ kāmasādhanatvānvayayogyamapūrvaṃ kriyātireki ityapūrvādhikaraṇe sthāpyate । tena ca
<pb n="044"/>
kāryeṇa saha sādhanatayā bhāvārtho'nvayaṃ yātīti bhāvārthādhikaraṇe nirdiśyate । sādhanī-
bhūtaśca bhāvārthaḥ niyogamavacchindat viṣayo bhavatīti śabdāntarādhikaraṇe nirūpyata
iti । <q>kimidaṃ <quote>‘asādhakaṃ tu tādarthyāt’</quote></q> iti । <q>asādhakamidaṃ vākyaṃ</q>
syādityarthaḥ । yadi ca yāga eva kartavyatayā codyate tadā niyojyābhāvāt saṃbhūya-
kāritvāt padānāṃ naivedaṃ vākyaṃ kañcidarthamavabodhayet ।</p>
<p>nanu ca nimittatvakalpanāyāṃ na kasyacidekasya nimittatā śakyate
vak‍tumityuktam</p> । na padavyatireki vākyaṃ na ca kasyacit padajātanimittatā ।
tena nimittaśūnyeyamavagatiḥ । pariharati---yata evaikasya na nimittatā'sti <q>ata
eva sarvasyetyucyate</q> । parasparānvitābhidhāyitayā sarvāṇyeva padāni asyārthasya
nimittaṃ bhavanti, anyathā'nvitābhidhānānupapatteḥ । yadi sarvapadajātaṃ parasparānvayabodhe
nimittaṃ kathaṃ tarhi vākyādhikaraṇe pratipadanimittabhāva uktaḥ atrāha---<q>pada-
padārthavivecane hi pratipadanimittabhāva ityucyate</q> । anviteṣu padārtheṣu
ekaikasya padasya nimittabhāvo vṛddhavyavahāre vyutpannaḥ । tatpratipādanadvāreṇa
<q>vākyārthe punaḥ sarvameva nimittam</q> । vākyārtho hi anvitānekapadārthaviśiṣṭaḥ
sacaikasya padasya na śakyaṃ pratipādayitumiti sarvasya tatra nimittabhāva <q>ityuktaṃ tatraiva ।
niyoganiyojyasaṃbandhena kiṃ saṃbandhābhidhānaṃ</q> saṃbandhapratipādakaṃ śabdaṃ <q>smarati</q>
pāṇiniriti <q>yaduktaṃ tadayuktaṃ śakyate hi ṣaṣṭhīsmaraṇena sarvamidamupasahartum</q> śeṣaṃ
karmādibhyaḥ (pratipādakaṃ vyatirekiṇaṃ) vyatirekapratipādakaṃ smaratā sarvamevopasaṃhṛtaṃ
bhagavateti śakyate vaktum । paramārthatastu <q>abhidhānaṃ punaḥ saṃbandhiśabdānāmani-</q>﻿
<pb n="045"/>
<q>yatameva bhagavataḥ</q> pāṇineḥ sarvasaṃbandhaśabdo bhagavatā smaryata iti niyamo nāsti
<q>kṛttaddhitasamāseṣvadarśanāt</q> । santamapi kṛtaṃ kelimarābhiṃ(?) taddhitamapi yantrādi
samāsamapi adhītapūrvaṃ idaṃ bhagavānna smarati । atassatāmapi śabdānāṃ smaraṇādarśanāt
[a]smaraṇena na śabdābhāvo'rthābhāvo vā vaktuṃ śakyata iti । <q>evaṃ ca niyoga-
siddha‍yarthatvāt vākyārthasya phalataḥpravṛttirityetat parihṛtaṃ bhavati</q> । yadi hi
anyataḥ phalamavagamyeta tadā tadvaśenaivādhikāre siddhe pravṛttiriti niyoganiyojya-
saṃbandho nāvagamyate । yadā tu niyogasiddhiḥ kathaṃ syāditi vākyena vākyārthaḥ
pratipādyate tadā tadanuguṇakalpaneti na phalataḥ prathamapravṛttiḥ । yadi phalaṃ niyoga-
labhyameva <q>kathaṃ tarhi phalaṃ na vidhīyata iti tantre vyavahāraḥ</q> । uttaraṃ---
<q>niyogārthatve'vagate nimittacintāyāṃ</q> padārtho hi vākyārthapratipattau nimittam ।
tena taccintāyāṃ idamanyataḥ prāptaṃ <q>idamanyata eveti kalpanā, na punaḥ vākyārthe
kiñcit prāptaṃ nāma</q> niyogānvitatayā na kiñcit prāptaṃ nāma <q>dadhnā juhotītyatra
pradarśitam</q> । ekagranthenāha---<q>padavākyaviṣayamaviviktavijñānamatrākulīkaroti
mandadhiyaḥ</q> । padaṃ vākyaṃ ca ye viviktaṃ na jānanti teṣāṃ mandadhiyāmeṣā ākulatā
kathaṃ tadeva prāptamaprāptaṃ ceti । ye ca punaḥ padavākye vivikte jānanti te padārthā-
vasthāyāṃ prāptāyāṃ vākyāvasthāyāṃ cāprāptatāṃ niścinvantyeva । ekagranthenāha---<q>na padaṃ
nāma vākye kiñcidasti na padārthāḥ kecana vākyārthe</q> । vākyāvasthāyāṃ padaṃ
nāma nāsti । vākyāvasthāyāṃ padārthā nāma kecana na santi । kutaḥ ? <q>viśeṣāva-
gatirhi vākyārthaḥ</q> । arthaviśeṣo'vagamyamāno vākyārthaḥ <q>tadavagatihetuśca vākyam</q> ।
ato viśeṣāvagamāvasthāyāmavagamyamānatayā vākyārthe padārtho nāsti । viśeṣāvagama-
<note>1. sandhātuṃ</note>﻿
<pb n="046"/>
daśāyāṃ cāvagamakaṃ padaṃ nāsti । tena vākyārthe sarvamevāprāptaṃ padārthavibhāgaṃ darśayan
idamāha---<q>nimittakalpanāyāṃ tu padaṃ padārthāśceti vyapadeśaḥ</q> । kaścideva varṇa-
samudāyaḥ kañcidarthamanvayitayā''cakṣāṇo vākyārthe nimittībhavati । tena tadabhi-
prāyeṇa padapadārthavyapadeśaḥ । tena tāmāśritya prāptatayā yadi vākyārthadaśāyāṃ padārthā
nāma na santi <q>evaṃ tarhiṃ padapadārthajñānamanṛtamevetyuktaṃ bhavati śābdairiveti</q> ।
pariharati---<q>na nimittatā'nṛtamiti badāmaḥ । kintvavagamyamānāvasthāyāṃ</q>
viveko nāsti <q>vākyārthe avagamakatayā ca vākye</q> ।</p>
<p>yata eva padapadārthā nimittatayā santi <q>ata evoktaṃ</q> padebhya <q>eva hi padārtha-
pratyayaḥ padārthebhyo vākyārthasya</q> । prameyatvādekasya pratītyavacchitannaḥ pratyaya iti
<q>nimittanaimittikabhedāśrayam</q> । padāni svārthānanvitān vadanti vākyārthe nimittatāṃ
yānti iti nimittanaimittikabhedāśrayameva taduktaṃ, na punaḥ pramitau bhedaḥ ekasya
vākyārthasya prameyatvāt ekasya pratītyavacchinnasya pramāpakatvāt । <q>śābdaistu nimitta-
mapyapahnutamiti viśeṣaḥ</q> । kasmāt ? teṣāṃ hi mate pratyastamitāvayavavibhāgaṃ vākyaṃ
vācakam । mīmāṃsakamate tu padānyevārthadvāreṇa vākyārthamavagamayantītyuktaṃ tadbhūtā-
dhikaraṇe । <q>tadidaṃ vākyapadīyamityuktam</q> । vaiyākaraṇamate hi vākyameva kevalaṃ,
padaṃ nāma nāsti । tena tadbhūtādhikaraṇameva vākyapadīyamiti tatraivoktam । <q>vākyārtha-
mātṛkāyāṃ</q> cāsmābhiriti ।</p>
<p>atra codayati---yadi niyogo'nuṣṭhānākṣepakatayā'vagabhyate tadā niyojyaṃ
vinā'nuṣṭhānānupapatteḥ niyojya āśrīyate । na ca niyogo'nuṣṭhānākṣepakaḥ niyoga-
śabdāvagamyamānasya tadāha---<q>bhāva</q> .... .... .... to liṅādi । abhidheyasyāpi
yā'nuṣṭhānākṣepakatāvagatiḥ sā kālpanikī । anenābhiprāyeṇāha---<q>kiṃ nimittapūrvasya</q>﻿
<pb n="047"/>
<q>yajeḥ vidhyartho vācyaḥ iti</q> na tāvadvācya iti śakyate vak‍tum । vācyaścetkimi-
tyanuṣṭhānaṃ na pratipādayati । pariharati---<q>asti kiñ‍cidvācyam</q> । kiṃ tadvācyaṃ ?
<q>svarūpato vācyo na pramāṇata iti</q> viyogavaśena nidhyarthaḥ svarūpato vācyaḥ
na pramāṇataḥ । dharmamātraṃ niyogaśabdaḥ[bdena] ucyate । anuṣṭhānapramāṇabhāvāliṅgitastu
gharmī liṅādibhiḥ । kutaḥ punarayaṃ vibhāgo'vagamyate ata evetyatrāha---<q>kāryāva-</q>
gamyatvāt [yatra]pramāṇakāryamanuṣṭhānarūpaṃ avagamyane tatra pramāṇato'bhidhānaṃ, yatra tu na,
tatra s‍varūpato'bhidhānamiti vibhāgaḥ । yadi pramāṇabhāvo nāsti kathaṃ tarhi kṛdantenābhi-
dhānamiti tatrāha---<q>abhidhānasya padārthamātraniṣṭhatvāt</q> । padārthamātratayā svarūpa-
mātreṇābhidhānopapatteḥ na svarūpeṇa liṅādibhirabhidhānam । <q>tasmālliṅādibhireva
pramāṇato'bhidhānaṃ na kṛdantairiti niś‍cīyate । tathā vyavahāradarśanāt vyava-
hārapūrvakatvācca padārthāvagateḥ</q> liṅādiyuktavākye'nuṣṭhānadarśanāt kṛdantaśravaṇe
cādarśanāditi । <q>ataḥ kalpanāpakṣo'pi pratyuktaḥ</q> । uktena nyāyena kalpanārthe
pramāṇābhāvāt । <q>yadi ṣaṣṭhyā smṛtyupasaṃhāraḥ kathaṃ tarhi svargakāmo yajeta iti
prathamā</q> prātipadikārthamātranimittā prathamā niyojyasyātiriktatayā'tra na prātipadikārtha-
mātratā । ataḥ śeṣatvāt <q>ṣaṣṭhī vā syāt aśravaṇaṃ vā vibhakteḥ</q> yadi ṣaṣṭhyapi na
yuktā । <q>ucyate । naiva niyogāpekṣeyaṃ prathamā, kiṃ tarhi kārakāpekṣā</q> ।
niyogāpekṣāyāṃ (vi)niyojyaḥ prātipadikārthātirikta iti prathamā na syāt kartṛbhāvā-
pekṣāyāṃ cākhyātenaiva karturabhihitatvāt śuddhaḥ prātipadikārtha iti prathamopapattiḥ ।</p>﻿
<pb n="048"/>
<p><q>nanu ca</q> niyogāpekṣāyāṃ hi <q>niyojyapūrvakatvāt kriyākārakasaṃbandhasya
tatsaṃbandhinyaiva vibhakta‍yā bhavitavyam</q> । prathamopanipātiniyojyamātrāpekṣayā
nibhaktyā bhavitavyam , na paścādbhāvikārakāpekṣayā । <q>satyamāha bhavān</q> niyojyaḥ
prathamabhāvīti <q>kintu na liṅvācye niyoge vibhaktissaṃbhavati</q> । nanu ṣaṣṭhī
śeṣatvalakṣaṇā saṃbhavati tatrāha---<q>saṃbandhamātrāpekṣiṇī ṣaṣṭhī na vyāpāraviśeṣā-
pekṣiṇī</q> । asyārthaḥ - kriyākārakagarbhaḥ śeṣasaṃbandhaḥ । tatra kriyākārakabhāvaṃ
tiraskṛtya tad‌dvārā pariniṣpanne saṃbandhe ṣaṣṭhī prayujyate । na punarvyāpāraviśeṣasaṃbandhe
tasyāśeṣatvāt karmādirūpatvāt । <q>liṅādibhiśca viśeṣo'vagamyate</q> niyojyaniyo-
k‍tṛbhāvaḥ । yadi niyojyatayā svargakāmasyāvagatiḥ <q>tarhi</q> karmatvāt <q>dvitīyā bhavatu</q> ।
na, dhātunā <q>anupāttattvāt niyogavyāpārasya</q> । niyuktilakṣaṇo[ṇā]hi dvitīyā
na bhavati satyapi(na)[ca] vyāpāravyāpyatve । kuta ityāha-<q>dhātūpāttavyāpāre hi
dvitīyādayaḥ</q> । tadeva kuta ityāha---<q>bhāvāpekṣitvāt kārakābhidhānasya</q> ।
kārake hi dvitīyādayaḥ । bhāvāpekṣayā ca kārakāṇyabhihitāni vaiyākaraṇaiḥ । tathāpi
kimityāha---<q>dhātūpāttasya bhāvatāmicchanti</q> । dhātvarthādeva kuta ityāha---
<q>kevalaḥ śuddho bhāva ityabhidhīyate</q> iti vadantaḥ । tenādhātvartharūpatvānniyukteḥ na
bhāvarūpatvam । abhāvarūpatve ca na kārakatvam । akārakatve ca na dvitīyeti ।
<q>tasmāt paścādbhāvyapi kartṛbhāvo'tra vibhaktyutpatteḥ hetuḥ । prātipadikārtha-
mātratayaiva niyogasiddhiḥ</q>[ddheḥ] । vibhaktiṃ vināpi svargakāmaprātipadikārthaparyālo-
canayaivoktena nyāyena niyogasaṃbandhasiddhiḥ svargakāmādīnām । yata eva prātipadi-
kārthamātratayaiva niyogasiddhiḥ <q>ata eva cābhihite karturekatve na dvitīyāprasaṅgaḥ</q> ।
yadi kartā nābhihitaḥ syāt tadā paratvāt tṛtīyayaiva dvitīyā bādhitā satī na bhavet ।
abhihite kartari tṛtīyāyāmasaṃbhavantyāṃ yā dvitīyā bhavati tatreyamaparā yuktiḥ । prāti-﻿
<pb n="049"/>
padikamātravalenāpi karmatvasiddhiriti । ata eva ceti cakāro hetvantarasamuccaye ।
ata eva lakāreṇābhidhānasiddhiśca । yata eva niyojyatayā svargakāmaḥ svargakāmaprāti-
