padikaparyālocanayā pratibhāti ata eva lakāreṇābhidhānasiddhiśca । anyathā dhātureva
kāryamabhidadhat niyogamabhidadhyāt lokavyavahārānusāreṇa । svargakāme hi phala-
paryante niyojye tadanvayayogyatayā dhātvarthātiriktaṃ kāryaṃ lakāreṇābhidhīyata iti tatra
tatroktam । yadi hi svargakāmaprātipadikaparyālocanayā tasya niyojyatvaṃ na pratibhāsate
tadā niyojya āśrīyamāṇo'pi lokavyavahārānusārikriyākāryatvānurūpo jīvati navā
na phalaparyanta āśrīyate । ka[tata]ścāpūrvakāryābhidhāyikā[tā] liṅāderna syāt iti
darśanasthitiranusaraṇīyā ।</p>
<p>nanu svargasiddheḥ yāgātmakabhāvadvayasaṃbhavāt yadyapi yajeḥ kartṛtvamabhihiṃta
tathāpi svargasiddhau kartṛtvasyānabhihitatvāt tṛtīyā syādeveti tatrāha---<q>bhāvadvayo-
panyāsaśca pratyuktaḥ dhātvantarānupādānāt</q> । svargasiddheḥ dhātvantareṇānupādānāt
na tenāpi kriyākārakavibhaktiyogāḥ । nanu yadi kartṛtvamapi svargakāmasya tadā
kartṛviśeṣaṇatvamapi svargasyāsti । tena svargo'pi guṇabhūta iti tatrāha-<q>guṇapradhāna-
bhāvaśca kārakābhiprāyeṇetyetadapi parihṛtam</q> । kārakābhiprāyeṇa kevalaṃ guṇa-
pradhānabhāvaḥ svarganiyogayoḥ । niyojyadaśāyāṃ tu pradhānataiva svargasya guṇataiva yāgasyeti
na doṣaḥ । yata eva kārakāvasthāyāmiyaṃ vibhaktiḥ na niyojyāvasthāyāṃ <q>ata eva
kāmigatā saṅkhyā'tantram ākhyātagataiva nādrīyate</q> । yadi hi kāmigatā
saṅkhyā niyojyāvasthāyāmeva syāt tad‍balenaiva ekasyādhikāraḥ siddha‍yet nākhyāta-
gatāyā ādaraḥ syāt । yadā tveṣā adhikārapūrvakakartṛdaśāvasthaivāśrīyate tadā nādhi-
kāraniyamāyālamiti ।</p>
<note>1. mā. vyāpriyate</note>﻿
<pb n="050"/>
<p>yadi svargakāmo niyojyatayā saṃbadhyate na kartṛtayā <q>idamaparaṃ tarhi kathamakā-
minaḥ pravṛttirnāstīti</q> । yāvatā akāmino'pi pravṛttyā bhāvyam । nanu kāma-
sidhyarthatvātpravṛtteḥ kathamakāminaḥ pravṛttirāśaṅkyate ityatrāha---<q>niyogaparatvācchā-
strasya</q> niyogasiddha‍yarthā hi kāmitā na niyogaḥ kāmasiddha‍yartha ityuktam । niyoga
eva kāryatāprayojyaḥ । tasya kartrā vinā siddha‍yanupapatteḥ । kāmanāviśeṣaṇatvena
tasya lābhāt niyogārthā kāmitā । ato'kāmino'pi pravṛttiḥ syāt । pariharati---
<q>niyogārthasiddha‍yarthatvāt kāmanāyāḥ</q> । niyogārthasiddha‍yarthe vā kāmitve kathama-
kāminaḥ pravṛttiḥ ityāśaṅkyate ? codayitā''ha-<q>naivāśaṅkyate aṅgatā tu kāminaḥ
prāp‍noti</q> । niyogaṃ prati kāmino'ṅgatā prāpnotītyucyate na ceṣyate mīmāṃsakaiḥ ।
pariharati---<q>aviveko'trāparādhyate bhavataḥ । dhātvarthāpekṣo hyaṅgāṅgibhāvo
neṣyate</q> dhātvarthamapekṣya niyojyasyāṅgatā neṣyate dhātvarthasya pradhānatā[ca] । niyogā-
pekṣayā tu iṣyata eva । nanvevaṃ svargo guṇa eva syāditi tatrāha---<q>guṇapradhāna-
bhāvo'pi tadapekṣa eva,</q> dhātvarthāpekṣa eva <q>ukto</q> bhāṣye । <q>niyogasiddhau tu sarvaṃ
tadanuguṇamiti kena neṣyate</q> । niyogasiddhidaśāyāṃ tatsarvaṃ tadanuguṇamiti kasyātra
vipratipattiḥ ? yadi sarvaṃ niyogārthaṃ tadā parasparaniyogārthānāṃ tādarthyaṃ na syādi-
tyatrāha---<q>tādarthyaniyamastu pradarśitaḥ kuryādityādinā</q> । bhāṣye'pyāha
<quote>“kimapi bhāvayet”</quote> iti । bhāṣyamarthato vyākhyātam । yadi niyojyaviśeṣaṇāni tāni
<q>kathamidānīmetāni vākyāni <quote>“ta ime satyāḥ kāmā anṛtāpidhānāḥ
<quote>“sarvaṃ khalvidaṃ brahme”</quote>tyevamādīni</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>uktā anyaparāṇāṃ mantrārtha-</q>﻿
<pb n="051"/>
<q>vādānāṃ pratipattiḥ</q> । uktā anyaparāṇāṃ mantrārthavādānāṃ pratipattiḥ gatiruktā
gauṇī lākṣaṇikī vā । tenaiṣāmapi sā bhaviṣyati । <q>nanu cānyaparataivopaniṣa-
dvākyānāṃ nāsti</q> kāryapratipādakasya vākyāntarasyāśravaṇāt; uttaraṃ-yadi na kārya-
pratipādakaṃ vākyāntaramasti svataśca kāryāśravaṇaṃ tasya <q>tarhi siddhārthaparatvaṃ siddhārtha-
paratve ca</q> śabdasya <q>tatra prāmāṇyavyutpatteḥ</q> anuvādakatvamaṅgīkaraṇīyaṃ, anuvādaśca
pramāṇāntarāpekṣa iti pramāṇāntarāpekṣitaiva prāpnoti । codayitā āha---<q>tarhi
mṛgyatāṃ pramāṇāntaraṃ iti</q> । siddhāntyāha---yadi tatra praṇāṇāntaramasti tadā
<q>prāmāṇāntarasadbhāve vā kā no bādhā । śāstrārthastāvadayam yathaivopavarṇi-
to'smābhiḥ</q> । na ca siddhārthasya pramāṇāntarāpekṣatve sādhyārthasyāpi tadbhavitumarhati ।
apekṣākāraṇābhāvāt । itarasya tu siddhārthataivāpekṣāheturityukto viśeṣaḥ । coda-
yati---nanu vedāntārthaviṣaye'dvaite pramāṇāntarasaṃbhavāt tena pramāṇāntareṇa <q>śās‍trārtho
virudhyate bhedenāvagamyamānatvācca</q> śāstrārthasya । pariharati---<q>na khalu kaści-
dvirodhaḥ</q> kāryasiddhaviṣayatayā bhinnaviṣayatvena virodhābhāvāt tena pramāṇāntareṇa na
śāstrārtho virudhyate । siddhāntavādyevāha---<q>atha virodhaṃ manyase</q> viniyogasavya-
pekṣatvāt niyogasya viniyogaviṣaye ca pramāṇāntarāṇāmavatārāt । dūṣayati---<q>na
tarhi pramāṇāntaramasti</q> । kutaḥ ? <q>etasmādeva śāstreṇa virodhāt</q> pramāṇāntarasya
kalpayitumaśakyatvāt । kasmāt punaḥ pramāṇāntaratvaṃ nāstītyāha---<q>na cānumānā-
dṛte ekatā</q> sarvasya jagataḥ <q>śakyate vak‍tum</q> । tataḥ kimityāha---<q>āgamavirodhe
ca nānumānamātmānaṃ labhata iti naiyāyikāḥ</q> । nyāyavyavahāriṇaḥ yathā
<pb n="052"/>
yāgīyā hiṃsā na dharmaḥ hiṃsātvāditi । prakṛtamupasaṃharati---<q>tasmādvākyaśeṣāṇi bhavantu
upaniṣadvākyāni svatantrāṇi vā adhyayanamātraparyavasāyīni</q> । pramāṇāntarā-
bhāve siddhārthatayā vivakṣitārthāni । <q>nātra saṅkaṭaṃ kiñ‍cit</q> । pakṣadvaye'pi
rāddhāntasiddheḥ । <q>yatpunaḥ dharmaśās‍trakāraiḥ paṭhitaṃ <quote>“kāmātmatā na praśastā”</quote>
iti</q> । anubhāṣya pariharati-<q>paṭhitamevaitat । kenavoktaṃ na paṭhitamiti</q> । codayitā
āha---yadi paṭhitaṃ <q>bhavatu tarhi svargādīnāṃ na prāśastyam</q> mṛṣābhūtatvāt ।
rāddhāntyāha---<q>bhavatva</q>prāśastyaṃ <q>yadi sādhyatayā</q> svargādeḥ <q>pratiṣedhaḥ</q> svargo na
bhavatītyuktam evaṃ yadi pratiṣedhaḥ syāt । <q>atha tu ātmaguṇo'yamupadiśyate</q>
akāmātmakena puruṣeṇa bhavitavyamiti kāmanāpratiṣedhaḥ <q>yathā nahiṃsyāditi</q>
hiṃsātmaka<q>kriyāpratiṣedhaḥ</q> tadā <q>nānarthakyaṃ</q> prayojanavattvameva <q>svargādisiddheḥ</q> ।
<q>nirṇayastvanayoḥ tata eva</q> smṛtivākyapaurvāparyālocanayaiva <q>anveṣyaḥ</q> kriyāpratiṣedha
eva smṛtāviti bhāvaḥ । atra bhāṣyaṃ <quote>“vākyādevāsmādavagacchāmaḥ”</quote> ityādi
tadākṣipati---<q>yatpunaridaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa yāgaprādhānye'pi phalasiddhiṃ darśayatā
upanyastaṃ <quote>“kāṣṭhānyāhartukāmo'raṇyaṃ gacchet”</quote> iti</q> । <q>kathamatra kriyā-
prādhānyaṃ manyate pratyuta tumun pratyayāt</q> gamirevānyārthe vartate । <q>tasmādyathā</q>-
bhavatyayaṃ <q>dṛṣṭāntaḥ tathā vaktavyam</q> । asyārthaḥ---bhāṣyakāreṇedamuktaṃ kimarthamatīva
svargaprādhānye prayatyate yāvatā yāgaprādhānye'pi kāmyamānasya phalasya yāgāt siddhi-﻿
<pb n="053"/>
ravagamyata eva <quote>‘svargakāmo yajeta’</quote> iti । asmādeva vākyāt yathā kāṣṭhānyāhartu-
kāmo'raṇyaṃgacchet ityasmādeva vākyāt prādhānye'pi gamanasya gamanāt kāṣṭhāharaṇa-
siddhiravagamyate; yāgāt siddhiravagamyate eva svargakāmo yajetetyasmādeva vākyāt ।
yathā kāṣṭhānyāhartukāmaḥ(neyate ?) ityuktam । tasmāt gamirevāhartumiti tumun
śravaṇāt guṇabhūto vartate । <quote>“tumun ṇvalau kriyāyāṃ kriyārthāyāṃ”</quote> iti smaraṇāt ।
tasmādviṣamo dṛṣṭāntaḥ । samādhatte---<q>idamucyate kāmaśabdaprayogāt tumunnartho'trā-
nyārthe vartate</q> । <q>tathā caitadamarthyamavagamyata ityabhiprāyaḥ</q> । atyārthaḥ-āhartu-
kāma iti puruṣapradhānatvāt nirdeśasya tumunnartho gamiṃ prati guṇabhūto vartate । tena
gameḥ prādhānyamasti । prādhānye'pi ca gatyarthasya kāṣṭhāharaṇasya tatassiddhiravagamyata
iti dṛṣṭāntaṃ dadato bhāṣyakārasyābhiprāyaḥ । asya tu yāgaprādhānye'pi phalamavagamyata
iti pakṣasya <q>parihāraḥ satyaṃ</q> phalasiddhiravagamyate । sā tu <q>na śabdataḥ</q> । <q>kiṃ tarhi ?</q>
<q>prāmāṇāntareṇa</q> araṇyagamanasya kāṣṭhāharaṇaphalatvadarśanāt । na ca yāgasya svargaṃ-
prati sādhanatvamavagamyata ityataḥ kāmaprādhānya eva phalasiddherupapattiḥ । adhikaraṇārtha-
mupasaṃharati---<q>tasmādadhikṛtasya kartṛtvamiti siddham</q> । atrādhikaraṇe pūrvapakṣottara-
pakṣayoḥ saṃkṣepaḥ---tatra pūrvapakṣī na loke niyojyo nāma kaścidvākyārtho[rthe]nvayī
pratīyate । nanvasati niyojye kathamanuṣṭhānaṃ ? yāvaddhi karma anuṣṭheyatayā nāvagamyate
tāvanna prekṣāpūrvakāriṇo'nutiṣṭhanti । niyojyatve tu sati yasya niyogastasyādhikāraḥ ।
adhikṛtasya cānuṣṭhānāvagamāt upapadyate cānuṣṭhā(nāt)nam । ucyate । asatyapi
niyojyatve phalataḥ eva pramāṇāntaramadhigamya tatkarmaṇi phalarthino'dhikārāvagamāt
upapannamanuṣṭhānam । [na]niyojyatve kaścicchabdo'stīti ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntī manyate---satyamevaṃ loke tathāpi vede kāryapratipādakatvāt liṅā-
dīnāṃ, anuṣṭhāne ca sati kāryasya kāryatvopapatteḥ anuṣṭhānasiddha‍yarthamadhikāro'bhyupa-
gamanīyaḥ । na ca pramāṇāntarasamadhigataṃ phalamatrāsti yato'dhikāraḥ syāt । tasmā-
dadhikārasiddha‍yarthaṃ svargakāmādīnāṃ niyojyatvena saṃbandho varṇanīyaḥ । kaḥpunarniyojyo-
nāma ? yaḥ kāryato'vabudhyate sa niyojyaḥ । etena kāryaṃ prati boddha‍ṛtayā svarga-﻿
<pb n="054"/>
kāmādaya upādīyante । na cākāmopāyaṃ kāmī kāryatayā pratipattumarhatīti kārya-
kāmayorupāyopeyabhāvaḥ । na ca kālāntarabhāvini kāme yāgaḥ kāryatayā niyojye-
nānvayaṃ yātīti yāgātiriktakāryābhyupagamāt yāgastaṃ prati sādhanatvena saṃbadhyate ।
tataśca puruṣasya yatkāryaṃ tatsādhanaṃ yāga iti tatraiśvaryaṃ puruṣasyopapadyate । tataśca tatra
tatrānuṣṭhānāvagaterupapannamanuṣṭhānam । tatra nityeṣu kevalaniyogakāryatvāt tatsādhanatvena
yāgeṣu puruṣasyādhikāraḥ । kāmādhikāreṣu tu phalaparyantaṃ niyogasādhyatvāditi viśeṣaḥ ।
atra ślokā bhavantiḥ---</p>
<lg><l>loke kartṛtva(tat)saṃbandhaḥ puruṣaḥ phalasādhanam ।</l>
<l>mānāntareṇa vijñāya karmādhikurute svayam ।। 1 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>tato'nuṣṭheyatāṃ jñātvā svārthaṃ karmānutiṣṭhati ।</l>
<l>niyojyatvamatastatra tenāṃśenopayujyate ।। 2 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>loke tasya pratīstaya vedepyavagatiḥ kutaḥ ।</l>
<l>na hi vyutpattirahitaḥ śabdenārtho'bhidhīyate ।। 3 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>satyamevaṃ liṅādīnāṃ kāryārthatvaṃ na varṇitam ।</l>
<l>na cānuṣṭhānaśūnyasya kāryatvamupapadyate ।। 4 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>anuṣṭhānāvabodhācca karmaṇyaiśvaryabandhanaḥ ।</l>
<l>aiśvaryaṃ ca na yāgādau phaladarśanasaṃbhavaḥ ।। 5 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>tataḥ kāryamakāryaṃ syāt aiśvaryeṇa vinā nṛṇām ।</l>
<l>na ca kartṛtvamātreṇa karmaṇyaiśvaryasaṃbhavaḥ ।। 6 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>aiśvaryeṇaiva kartṛtvaṃ yāvatkarmasu dṛśyate ।</l>
<l>kārye boddha‍ṛtayā tatra kāmī saṃbadhyate yadi ।। 7 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>tadā kāryaphalaprāptiḥ kāryādhīnā'vasīyate ।</l>
<l>na ca kṣaṇāpavṛttena karmaṇā śakyate phalam ।। 8 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>kālāntare janayituṃ tasmātkāryaṃ tato'dhikam ।</l>
<l>tena kāryeṇa saṃbandhaḥ sādhanatvena karmaṇaḥ ।। 9 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>svakāryasādhane karmaṇīśvaraḥ puruṣastataḥ ।</l>
<l>tathā ca sati karmāpi samāsāditasādhakam ।। 10 ।।</l></lg>﻿
<pb n="055"/>
<lg><l>labdhānuṣṭhānamityevaṃ kāryaṃ kāryatvamṛcchati ।</l>
<l>pravṛttibījajātāyāḥ kāryavyutpattivīrudhaḥ ।। 11 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>niyojyatvaṃ phalāsaṅgi kumudaṃ vikasatyadaḥ ।</l>
<l>tena vyutpattiviraho na doṣayātra jāyate
siddho ve(do)de niyojyo'taḥ kārye boddha‍ṛtayānvitaḥ ।। 12 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>phalārthatvāt karmaṇaḥ</q></p>
<p><q>nanu tiryagādiṣu vedasya pramāṇataiva nopapadyate</q> । <q>keyamadhikāra-
cintā</q> । asyārthaḥ-yo niyoge kāryātmani boddha‍ṛtayā saṃbadhyate sa niyojyaḥ,
so'dhikārī । na ca tiryaścaḥ śabdārthe bodhaśaktivikalāḥ śabdaikasamadhigamanīye
kārye boddha‍ṛtayā saṃbaddha‍uṃ yogyāḥ । ataśca teṣāṃ na niyojyatvasaṃbhavaḥ । tathā devatā-
nāmṛṣīṇāṃ ca caitanya(lābhāt)ā/?/bhāvāt bodadhṛtvānupapattiḥ । atastiryagādiṣu
vedasya bodhakatvānupapatteḥ tiryagādīnāmadhikāro nopapadyata iti pūrvapakṣākṣepaḥ । <q>tathā
devatānāmṛṣīṇāṃ cādhikāre rāddhānto nopalabhyate</q> । etadeva vivṛṇoti---
<q>yadi tāvadadhikāradevatāḥ parigṛhyante ārṣeyavaraṇacoditāścarṣayaḥ tadā'nitya
saṃyogo vedasya kiṃ tadā'dhikāracintayā</q> । asyārthaḥ-yadi yāga[ge yā]evādhi-
kāre devatā uddeśyā indrādayaḥ tāsāmadhikāraśśaṅkyate, yadyārṣeyavaraṇacoditānā-
mṛṣīṇāṃ ca, tadā teṣāmanuṣṭhānābhyupagamo'vaśyaṃbhā[vī । nacā](naścavi) <q>śarīriṇā</q>-
manuṣṭhāto[namu]papadyate । śarīraṇaścedanityārthasaṃyogādanityā[eva](bhāve) vedāḥ ani-
tyānāṃ ca prāmāṇyameva nāsti kimadhikāracintayā । <q>atha tato'nye</q> devatātmā[naḥ]
1. Page 1355﻿
<pb n="056"/>
ṛṣayaścābhimatāḥ <q>kimityadhikāro vāryate yasmādṛṣayo brāhmaṇāḥ</q> ka(ta)thāsu
<q>śrūyante</q> । <q>indrādayaśca kṣatriyāḥ</q> te cādhikāriṇo yuktā eveti rāddhānto na
labhyate <q>tasmāt bhraṣṭapūrvapakṣottarapakṣamevedaṃ tatrālocanatayā pratibhāti</q> mīmāṃsā ।
tatrālocanatayā bodhasamartho'dhikārīti tiryagādīnāmadhikārāśaṅkā na yuktā । tathāpi
nityā devatā ityadhikāradevatānāmṛṣīṇāṃ cārṣeyavaraṇacoditātirekiṇāmadhikāraścinta-
nīyaḥ । sa ca teṣāṃ vārayitumaśakya iti । <q>yadi cātrāpi viṣṇukramake</q> yāge
<q>yāgamātrādhikārāśaṅkā sāpi kramaparyante</q> sthite <q>śās‍trā</q>rthe <q>nopapadyate</q> । krama-
paryantaṃ śāstrārthaḥ sthitaḥ tena viniyuktāṅgaparityāgena yāgāmātrādhikārāśaṅkā nopapadyate ।
yadi tāvat parihārāntarabhāgāya śaṅkā kriyate tadopapadyetādhikāśaṅkā iṣṭahetuḥ
parihṛtāvapi sa eva punarupanyastaḥ । kramaparyantaḥ śāstrārtho rāddhānte hetubhūtaḥ tasmāda-
pratiṣṭhaiveyaṃ cintā <q>viyatipadam</q> । samādhatte---<q>śās‍trārthajñānamevopanyastaṃ</q> tiraścāṃ
<q>kāmanāmukhena</q> । asyārthaḥ-yeya bhāṣyakāreṇa pāralaukikaphalakāmanā tiraścāmupanya1stā
tanmukhena teṣāṃ śāstrārthajñānamevoṃpanyastam । tacca prakaṭitam । ye tāvat pāralaukikaṃ
phalaṃ kāmayante te śāstrārthamapi boddhuṃ śak‍nuvantītyabhiprāyaḥ । śāstrārthajñānameva kāmanā-
mukhenopanyastamiti tacca prakaṭitam । na śāstrādṛte pāralaukikakāmanāṃ saṃbhavati । tena
saṃbhavacchāstrārthajñānāt tiryañcopyadhikāramarhantīti । <q>kathamṛṣidevatayoriti</q> pūrvokta-
smaraṇam । <q>atrābhidhīyate-atra kecit vedārthajñānapaṇḍitaṃmanyāḥ yāgānu-
ṣṭhānakṛtameva ṛṣitvaṃ devatātvaṃ ca manvate adhikāraśabdā indrādaya iti
vadantaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ-kecidevaṃ manyante indrāgnīśānādiśabdā adhikāriśabdāḥ
<note>1. mā upanyastam</note>﻿
<pb n="057"/>
adhikāriviśeṣaṇaśabdā ityarthaḥ । indratvādikāmo yāgādīnanutiṣṭhatīti । anu-
ṣṭhitayāgādiścendro bhavati sa punarindrabhūto'parapadalipsayā yajate karmabhiḥ devatābhāvo-
bhavatīti । atra cetihāsaṃ darśayati <q>tathāca śatakraturindraityaitihāsikāḥ</q> ।
ṛṣayaśca yajanta ityatrāpītihāsaṃ [darśayati]---<q>śaunakādayaśca</q> dvāpare <q>naimiśāraṇye
satramāsitavanta iti vadanti</q> । <q>nacaitāvatā karmajanyadevatāpratipādakatvena
anityasaṃyogo vedasya bhavatīti manyamānāḥ</q> । ayamarthaḥ-karmabhireva viśiṣṭaiḥ
puruṣā indratvādikaṃ labhante teṣāmeva devatābhāvaḥ । punardevatābhūtāḥ padāntaralipsayā
yajante । nacānityā (bhimatā)rthatā vedasya karmajanyānāmevānāditopapatteḥ parāvara-
rūpatvāt । <q>tadvyāmohāpanuttaye idaṃ likhitam</q> । <q>kathaṃ punaranena vyāmoho'-
podyate ?</q> <q>itthamapanudyate-yata indrādīnāṃ tāvadyāgādayo na saṃbhavanti
svātmani kriyāvirodhāt</q> । nahi sa evoddeśakaḥuddeśyaśca yujyate । yajamānatayo-
ddeśakaḥ devatātvenoddeśya iti nopapadyate ekasyāṃ kriyāyāṃ ekasya karmakartṛtvayoranupa-
patteriti । atra pūrvapakṣamāviṣkaroti-<q>nanu cendrābhimānino yajamānāḥ pūrvo-
tpannamindraṃ yajante</q> । <q>ṛṣyabhimāninaśca pūrvotpannān ṛṣīn vṛṇvate</q> ।
asyārthaḥ-ye'mī asmākamindratvenābhimatāḥ yajamānāḥ aparapadalipsayā yajante ।
tatpūrvotpannamindraṃ yajante । tena nāsti svātmani kriyāvirodhaḥ । evamṛṣiṣvapi ।
indrābhimānina iti । indra ityabhimānaḥ saṃmatiḥ pūrvapakṣiṇo yeṣāṃ te । indratvābhimatā
iti yāvat । siddhāntī dūṣayati---<q>evaṃ tarhi darśanābhimānānupapattiranyatvenā</q>-
pagatā । asyārthaḥ-yādṛśaṃ darśanaṃ bhavatāmabhimataṃ tasyānupapattiḥ devatāyajanta iti
<pb n="058"/>
bhavatāṃ darśanaṃ abhimānaḥ । na caivaṃ sati devatā yajate pūrvotpannasya devatātvāt idānī-
madhunātanasya yajamānatvāt । ye'pi na puruṣāste'pi na taṃ yajante tadijyameva
pūrvotpannamindraṃ yajeran । evaṃ ca yamebeṣṭvā pūrvotpanno'pīndro hūtaḥ sa evāparairapījyate ।
tataśca karmabhirutpannānāmanijyamānatvāt na devatātvaṃ syāt । ataḥ karmabhiḥ devatā-
bhāvo bhavatītyapi pakṣo nopapadyate । tasmāt karmajanyadevatā yajata ityetattāvat nāsti ।
tadāha---<q>tadbhāvo bhedaś‍cetyanupapattiranuṣṭhāne</q> । asyārthaḥ-adhunotpannasyendrasya
puruṣeṇejyamānatvāt devatābhāvaḥ svayaṃ cānyadevatāyājitvāt pūrvadevatāto bhedaḥ iti
nedamanuṣṭhānamupapadyate puruṣāṇāmapi taddevatādījyayājitvaprasaṅgāt । <q>ato devatā
devataiva ṛṣirapi ṛṣireva na punaḥ prāpyaḥ prāpako vā</q> । uktena nyāyena
karmotpannasyānijyamānatvāt avaraṇītvācca । karmabhirdevatābhāvaḥ ṛṣibhāvaśca na
bhavatīti svabhāvenaiva devatā'ṅgīkaraṇīyā । ṛṣirapi na punaḥkarmaprāpyaḥ nāpi
karmaphalaprāpakaḥ <q>yathā na prāpakaḥ tathā navame vakṣyāmaḥ</q> devatādhikaraṇe
phaladātṛtvanirākaraṇāt । <q>prāpyatā tviha niṣidhyate । yadapyukta kathamapi
[a] viṣṇukramake yāge'dhikāra iti sādhikārapūrvakatvāt prakaraṇādīnāma</q> ।
asyārthaḥ---sādhikārasannidhisamāmnātānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ tādarthye sati śrutyādibhistadīyeṣu
padārtheṣu viniyogaḥ kriyate । prakaraṇādīnāṃ tu svarūpe viniyoge cādhikārapūrvakatva-
meva । tenādhikāradaśāyāṃ viniyogasyānupapannatvam । yadyapyanuṣṭhānasamarthasyaivādhikāraḥ
tathāpi paṅg‌vādīnāmadhikāro na śakyate vārayitum a dhikāravaśenaiva tu viniyogaḥ pratya-
dhikāraṃ vyavatiṣṭhate---yadā yatsamartho'dhikārī tasya teṣāmaṅgānāṃ viniyoga iti ।
yata evaṃ kramaparyante'vasthite śāstrārthe yāgamātrādhikāramapekṣate na punarviśiṣṭasyaivā-
dhikāraṃ tatra kāmimātrasyaiva śaṅkopapadyate । <q>ato rāddhāntepyadhikārasiddheḥ</q>
nādhikṛtasya teṣāmaṅgānāṃ viniyoga iti avirodhāt <q>viniyogānyatvaṃ śakyate
kalpayitumiti nānupapattiḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---prakaraṇādayo'dhikāramātramapakṣente na
<pb n="059"/>
punaḥ viśiṣṭasyaivādhikāraḥ tatra kāmimātrasyādhikāreṇa labdhātmakaiḥ viniyogapramāṇaiḥ
viniyukteṣvaṅgeṣu tadaṅgayukte'nuṣṭhāne samarthasyaivādhikāraḥ kāmino niścīyate । yadi tāvat
viniyogānusāreṇādhikāriviśeṣe niścīyamāne'dhikāro'va(vi)ruddhyate [tadā]
yathādhikāraṃ viniyogāśrayaṇena nānārūpatā viniyogasya kalpyeta । nacaivamasti ।
na hi sāmānyaśrutiḥ viśeṣe'vasthāpyamānā śabdārthatāṃ jahātīti । <q>viṣayaṃ ca darśayan
nidarśitāveva pūrvapakṣottarapakṣo iti na punaḥ pradarśyata iti sthitamadhikaraṇam</q>
adhikārapūrvaka'/?/vādviniyogasya yathādhikāraṃ vyavasthāyāṃ sāmarthyānusāreṇa viniyoga iti
pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । anirdhāritaviśeṣeṇāpyadhikāriṇā (sādhikāriṇaḥ) sādhikāritvopapattau
viniyogasiddheḥ tadanusāreṇa ta(sa)tsamarthādhikāraviśeṣāśrayaṇaṃ nyāyyamiti rāddhāntaḥ ।
sa cāyaṃ vicāraḥ tiryakṣu devatāsu paṅgvādiṣu tulya ityaikādhikaraṇyam । śāstrārtha-
bodhasāmarthyābhāvapradarśanamabhyuccayaḥ tiryakṣu ।</p>
<p><b>।। liṅgaviśeṣa । svavatoḥ ।।</b></p>
<p>ekamatra-kiṃ puṃso'dhikāraḥ uta strīpuṃsayorapīti vicāre pūrvapakṣasūtram ।
aparaṃ tu-kiṃ saha yaṣṭavyaṃ uta bhedeneti vicāre siddhāntasūtraṃ, ekīkṛtyapaṭhan
evaṃ jñāpayati---pūrvādhikaraṇarāddhānta evādhikāraṃ vinā na nirvahatīti । etacca
vakṣyāmaḥ । pūrvapakṣamākṣipati---<q>nanu kartṛgata evātra vibhakta‍yarthaḥ</q> । <q>katha-
madhikāre s‍triyaṃ nivartayati</q> । asyārthaḥ---svargakāmo yajeta ityatra pūrvādhikaraṇe
idamuktaṃ kartravasthāyāmayaṃ vibhakta‍yartha iti । liṅgaṃ ca vibhakterevārthaḥ । tenādhikāra-
daśāyāṃ liṅgasyāpratītatvāt tadvaśena puṃsa evādhikāro na yukta iti pūrvaṃ-
pakṣākṣepaḥ । samādhatte---<q>ayamabhiprāyaḥ pūrvapakṣavādināḥ ekatvamiva</q>﻿
<pb n="060"/>
<q>saṅkhyāntaraṃ liṅgamapi liṅgāntaraṃ nivartayatīti</q> । yathā vibhakta‍yarthabhūtenāpi
ekatvena kartṛdaśāgāminā ekasyaivādhikāramāpādayatā saṅkhyāntaramadhikāre nivartyate
tathā liṅgāntaraṃ nivartyate । atra codayati---<q>nanu ca saṅkhyāpi naivādhikāre
saṃkhyāntaraṃ nivartayati kiṃ tarhi kartṛtve</q> । pariharati---<q>satyaṃ nādhikāre
nivartyate tathāpi tu kartṛtvāpatteradhikārasya liṅgamapi liṅgāntarasya na kartṛ-
tvamāpādayati</q> । asyārthaḥ-adhikāraḥ svāmitvaṃ kartṛtvena vipariṇamyate adhikṛtaḥ
kartā bhavatītyarthaḥ । tena kartṛtvāpattau saṃkhyā yā dṛśyate adhikāre'pi saiveti niścīyate ।
nādhikāriṇo'nyaḥ kartā । evaṃ liṅgamapi kartṛdaśāśritaṃ liṅgāntarayuktasya kartṛtāṃ
nivartayatīti । yadā ca liṅgāntarayuktasya kartṛtā nāsti tadā'dhikāro'pi tasya nāsti ।
yo hi nānutiṣṭhati kathamasāvadhikārī bhavati anuṣṭhānaparyantatvādadhikārasyeti ।
<q>puṃyuktamiti paṭhitam</q> । taiḥ <q>parikrayādibhiś‍cāsvatvadarśanamabhyuccayaḥ</q> avijñāte
garbhe hate bhrūṇahā bhavatītyavijñātagrahaṇaṃ nopapadyate yadi strīpuṃsayoradhikāraḥ । [a]vijñāta
grahaṇena hyevamucyate avijñāte garbhe hate kadācit pumānapi hanyeta tatra yajñasādhana-
vadhakāritayā bhrūṇahā bhavatīti । [yadi]strīpuṃsayorapyadhikāraḥ, tadā kimavijñāta-
grahaṇena(dyotyate) garbhamātravadhenāpi bhavatyeva bhrūṇahatyā । tathā''treyyabhyuccayaḥ ātreyīṃ
hatvā bhrūṇahā bhavatīti ।</p>
<p>āpannagarbhāmātreyīmāhuḥ । yadā punaḥ strīmātravadhenāpi bhrūṇahatyā bhava(tī)ti
[tadā kimātreyīgrahaṇeneti] darśayitumātreyīgrahaṇamupapannam । ta(dā)thā parikrayādi-
bhirasvatvapradarśanaṃ striyā abhyuccayaḥ । yathā krayavikrayayoginī strī svavatī na bhavati
gavādivat । ataḥ svādikrayāyoge svadravyatyāgātmake'samarthetyanadhikāriṇī ।</p>
<p><q>atrocyate---jātistu bādarāyaṇa iti</q> । <q>narajātimātramatrāpyadhi-﻿
<pb n="061"/>
<q>kriyate na liṅgādviśeṣagatiradhikārasyetyarthaḥ</q> । na jāteradhikāro'cetanāyāḥ
kintu tajjātibhājāṃ puṃsāṃ strīṇāṃ cādhikāraḥ । <q>nanu cāpannakartṛbhāvo na niyukta
iti saṅkhyāvat liṅgamapi liṅgāntaraṃ nivartayatītyuktam</q> । <q>satyamuktaṃ, tattva-
yuktam saṅkhyā saṅkhyātagatā karmaṇi saṃṅkhyāntaraṃ nivartayatīti yuktam</q> ।
<q>liṅgaṃ punaḥ aśrūyamāṇatvādayuktaṃ tannivartayatīti</q> । asyārthaḥ---yajetetyākhyāte
kartṛsaṅkhyā pratīyate tayā(tha) viṣayo viśeṣyate tenaikakartṛkaviṣaye ekasyaivānuṣṭhāna-
sāmarthyamiti tasyaiva tatrādhikāraḥ yathā rājajātīyasya rājasūye rājakartṛke । liṅgaṃ
punarākhyāte na śrūyate tena tadviśiṣṭastadviṣayo na pratīyate tena liṅgaviśeṣa-
rahite viṣaye strīpuṃsayoradhikāro ghaṭate । yattvidaṃ prātipadikagataṃ liṅgaṃ
tadadhikārapūrvakamidamavagamyate iti nādhikāraṃ nivartayitumarhati yathādhikārameva tu
varṇyate । <q>atassūktaṃ bādarāyaṇasyeti</q> । bhāṣya eva tāvat saṅkhyā saṅkhyāntaraṃ
nivartayati । <q>evaṃ tarhi sahaprayogo na prāp‍noti</q> saṅkhyāntarapūrvakamavagamyata
iti nivṛtteḥ । sahaprayoge hi strīpuṃsayoḥ dvitvasaṅkhyā syāt tataścaikasaṅkhyā
bādhyeta । sahaprayoge cāsati na striyā adhikāra upapadyate vidyāvirahāt
śadravaditi manyate । <q>tadidamuktam---sthitaṃ tāvadaparyavasitamiti</q> sahatva-
paryantatvāt stra/?/yadhikārasya yata eva sahatvaparyantaḥ stra/?/yadhikāraḥ <q>ataḥ</q> stra/?/yadhikāraṃ
nivartayituṃ <q>pṛthagadhikāraṃ pūrvapakṣavādī darśitavān</q> । <q>rāddhāntavādī tu naiva
kramaparyante viṣaye saṅkhyāvirodhaḥ iti manvānaḥ sahādhikāramuktavān</q> ।
asyārthaḥ kramaparyatoviṣayoḥ । tatra ca striyāmanupraviśantyāmapi saṅkhyāvirodho nāstīti
<pb n="062"/>
matvā sahādhikāramuktavān । yadi hi kramaparyanto viṣayo na bhavati kintu yāgapadārtha
eva tadā yāge kartrantarānupraveśena saṅkhyāvirodhaḥ syāt । yadā tvanekapadārthātmako
viṣayaḥ śāstrārthīṃbhūtaḥ tadā vyāpārāntareṇāpi kartrantarānupraveśaḥ saṃbhavatīti na saṅkhyā
viruddha‍yate । <q>kathaṃ punaḥ saṅkhyāvirodho nāsti</q> ? uttaraṃ---<q>sahiteṣu hi
dvivacanabahuvacane bhavataḥ</q> samāso vā; yathā devadattayajñadattau pacata ityādiṣu । <q>na
punassahārtheṣu</q> devadattena saha yajñadatto gata iti । iha tu strī sahabhāvenānupraviśati iti
<quote>“dharme cārthe na nāticaritavyā”</quote> । <quote>“yatkiñcitkartavyaṃ tadanayā saha”</quote> iti
vacanāt । yata eva sahiteṣu samāsaḥ <q>ata eva cetaretarayoge samāhāre ca samāsaṃ
manyante samāsavidaḥ</q> । <q>na punaś‍cārthamātre</q> itaretarayoge samāhāre ca dvandvaṃ
manyante yatra sahitabhāvaḥ । <q>na punaś‍cārthamātrepi</q> samuccaye'nvācaye ca । yadi
yatrāpi sāhityaṃ nāsti tatrāpi samāso bhavet tadā samuccayānvācayayorapi dvandvaḥ
smaryeta1 । <q>kaḥpunarabhiprāyaḥ</q> sahitabhāve samāsaṃ smaratāmityatrāha---<q>ayamabhiprāyaḥ
netaretarabhāvamanāpannayoḥ padārthāntarasaṃbandhaḥ</q> yatra hi sahitabhāvaḥ tatra hītaretara-
bhāvaḥ । sahayogitvamanāpannayoḥ aprāptayorna padārthāntarasaṃbandhaḥ api tu paraspara-
saṃbandhayoreva padārthāntareṇa saṃbandhaḥ । samāse ca samasyamānayorarthayoḥ parasparānu-
gamanapūrvakaṃ padārthāntarānugamanam । tena sahitabhāve yādṛśo'rthānāṃ saṃbandhaḥ tādṛśa
eva samāsenāpyucyate iti । sāmarthye ca sati samāsa iti yuktam । tatra samāso
yatra ca parasparasaṃbaddhayoreva padārthāntareṇa saṃbandhaḥ । tatra tulyadvārasaṃbandhāt dvibahutvopa-
patteḥ dvivacanaṃ bahuvacanaṃ na yuktam । tena samāso dvivacanabahuvacane । yatra itaretara-
savyapekṣayorarthāntarasaṃbandhaḥ tatra tadviṣayāṇyeva । <q>yatra punaḥ padārthāntarasaṃbandhāpekṣaḥ
cārthaḥ na tatra dvivacanabahuvacane bhavataḥ samāso vā</q> । yatra hyekasmin sambandhe
sati punararthāntarasaṃbandhaḥ kriyate na tatraikadvāreṇa sambandhaḥ yathā devadattaḥ pacati yajña-
<note>1. smaryate-mā</note>﻿
<pb n="063"/>
dattaśca iti । na hi tatra yathā devadattaḥ pākena saṃbaddhaḥ tathā yajñadatto'pi punaḥ
sambandhayituṃ śakyate । arthāntarāvaruddhe'rthāntarasambandhitvābhāvāt । tena tatra dvārā-
ntareṇa sambandho'vagamyate । ataścānityasambandhitvāt dvibahutvānupapatteḥ na dvivacana
bahuvacanopapattiḥ । samāsastu sāmarthyābhāve na saṃbhavati । samāse hi paraspara-
sahitānāmarthāntarasambandho'vagamyate iti । tathācārthāntarasaṃbandhānāṃ samuccayāvagateḥ
sāmarthyābhāvaḥ । iha ca patnī yajamānāvaruddhe prayoge paścātsahaśabdena sambadhyate ।
nāsau yajamānādbhinnena dvāreṇa yajamānāvaruddhe prayoge kartṛtvenānupraviśati । <q>tena</q>
tāmapekṣya na dvivacanabahuvacanopapattiḥ atulyasambandhitvāt । yatra sahitayoḥ kriyā-
sambandhaḥ tatra dvivacanabahuvacanopapattiriti । <q>tadidaṃ mahābhāṣyakāreṇa darśitam
sahitayoḥ kriyāsambandhābhidhāne dvivacanameva pradarśanārtheṣu vākyeṣu evamanu-
kṛtaṃ bhavati</q> । <q>anyathāhi anukāro'pi nopapadyata iti</q> । asyārthaḥ---sahitayoḥ
kriyāsambandhābhidhāne dvandvasamāse dhavakhadirau cchindyāt ityādau pradarśanārtheṣu vākyeṣu
vigrahavākyeṣu dvivacanameva prayoktavyam---dhavakhadirau ca iti । evaṃ dvivacanaprayoge
sati sahitakriyāsambandhābhidhāyi samāsapadamanukṛtaṃ bhavati । dvivacanadarśane hi
evamavagamyate---dvitvamastīti । dvitvotpattiśca parasparānvitayoḥ kriyāsambandhe bhavati ।</p>
<p>nanvevaṃ sati kathamekasmin dvivacanamucyate । sahitāvasthāyāṃ dvitvasaṅkhyā-
yogāt । dvitvaṃ ca sādhāraṇaguṇaḥ sahitāvasthālakṣaṇārthaṃ ca padadvayam । ata
evārthāntare kathaṃ vṛttiriti codyasyānavakāśaḥ । yadi punardvivacanena prayujyate tadā
anukāropi na syāt, sahitāvasthāyā adarśanādeva । sahabhāvena kriyāsambandhe'-
vagate yajamānasya tatpurassarā patnī kartṛtvena karmaṇyanupraviśantī yajamānādbhinnadvāreṇa
kartṛtāmanubhavati । <q>tadidamuktam---pratikārakaṃ kriyābheda iti</q> । anyā
kriyā, anyaḥ yajamānasya dvavyatyāgātmo yāgaḥ, madhyagaṃ ca dampatyoḥ dhanaṃ, kevalo
yajamānastyak‍tuṃ na śak‍noti । atyakte hi pat‍nyāḥ svāmyāt yajamānasyāpi svāmitva-
miti yāgānabhinirvṛttiḥ । tena pat‍nī anumatiṃ kurvāṇā yāge kartrīṃ । yajamānastu
sākṣāddevatāmuddiśya tyāgaṃ kurvāṇo yāge karteti । tadidamuktaṃ---<q>pratikārakaṃ
<pb n="064"/>
<q>kriyābheda</q> iti । na hi pat‍nyā anumatiṃ vinā yajamānasya kartṛtvopapattiḥ yāge ।
tena sāpi bhavatyeva yāge kartrī, vyāpārāntareṇānupraveśāt na dvitvabahutvopapattiriti
niravadyā । atka bhāṣyaṃ---<quote>“dvādaśe vā śate ṣaṭa‍pañcāśat”</quote> iti, tadidamākṣipati---
<q>dvādaśe vā śate ṣaṭa‍pañcāśaditi kimidaṃ</q> ? idaṃ kila bhaṣyaṃ rāddhānte yuktyantaramiva
darśayati dvādaśe vā śate ṛtvik‌parikrayārthe yajamānena ṣaṭa‍pañcāśaditi dīyate,
pat‍nyā ca ṣaṭ‍pañcāśaditi । etacca rāddhāntavirodhi । evaṃ hi tulyavyāpārā yajamānena
patnīti dvitvāpatteḥ ekavacanavirodhaḥ । ekadeśyāha---<q>vayamapi brūmaḥ kimidamiti</q> ।
ākṣeptā āha---<q>kimasadevedaṃ</q> ? samādhātā āha---<q>na</q> asaditi brūmaḥ bhāṣyānartha-
kyāpatteḥ । arthamāha---<q>dvādaśe śate yadi vibhāgaḥ syāt syādetadevaṃ</q> ekavacana-
virodha iti । iha <q>punaḥ anya eva pat‍nīvyāpāra iti sahārthatāṃ darśayati na
sahitārthatām</q> । asyārthaḥ---rāddhantavādī evaṃ brūte yadi dvādaśe śate ekena
ṣaṭpañcāśaddīyate apareṇāpi ṣaṭpañcāśaddīyata iti dānavibhāgaḥ syāta tadā ekavacana-
virodhaḥ syādityadhyāhāraḥ । patnī vyāpārastvanya evānumatilakṣaṇaḥ । tena sahārthena
pat‍nyā anupraveśena[śo na] sahitārtheneti । darśitaṃ cedamanumatilakṣaṇaḥ pat‍nīvyāpāra
iti । <q>anyatarānicchāyāṃ tyāga eva na saṃvarteta iti</q> । upasaṃharati---
tena śrutyā sahatvasmṛte<q>ravirodhāt saha kartavyamityasya vacanasya ayathārthatā
na śakyate'vagantum</q> । śrutivirodhe hi tathā syāt । na cāsāvasti । <q>evaṃ ca
pat‍nīśabdassamarthito bhavati</q> । yadi sahaprayogaḥ pat‍nyā na syāt tadā pat‍nyadhi-
kāro bhajyetaiva । tataśca yajñasvāmitvaṃ striyā nāstīti yajñasvāmistrīviṣaye <quote>‘patyurno-
yajñasaṃyoge’</quote> iti pat‍nīśabdo'samañjasaḥ syāt । karmaviśeṣāścāvekṣaṇādayaḥ samarthitā
bhavantīti । anyathā hi <quote>‘pat‍nyavekṣitabhājyaṃ bhavati’</quote> ityanupapannaṃ syāt । <q>liṅgamuktam</q> ।
<pb n="065"/>
<p><q>yatpunaridamuktaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa</q>---<quote>“tatra śrutisāmarthyāt yaḥ kaścit yayā
kayācit striyā saha saṃbhūya yajeteti prāpte idamucyate yastvayā kaściddharmaḥ kayācitsaha
kartavyaḥ so'nayā saha”</quote> iti । tena na śrutivirodhaḥ smṛteriti gamyate iti ।
<q>asya ko'rthaḥ</q> ? uttaraṃ---<q>nanu cāyamarthaḥ yayākayācit striyā saha kartavye-
prāpte udvāhaniyamaṃ darśayati</q> ityucyate । codayitā āha <q>yadyevamasaṃstarhyaya-
marthaḥ yasmātkartṛsaṃskāro vivāhaḥ na kratvarthaḥ</q> । <q>anyathāhi</q> yadi puruṣa-
saṃkāro na syāt <q>kratuprayuktameva syāt aṅgaṃ ca । na caitadevam</q>। kuta
ityatrāha---<q>kṛtādhānasya hi adhikāraṃ varṇayanti na kratvarthamādhānamiti
bruvantaḥ</q> । <q>yasmāt kṛtādhānasyādhikāraḥ</q> na punaradhikṛtasyāgnayaḥ <q>kṛtodvāhasya
cādhānaṃ</q> ato nādhikāriṇā puruṣeṇa kṛtatvāt nāsāvaṅgaṃ, śrūyatāmayamarthaḥ । yata eva
ca kartṛsaṃskāro'yaṃ <q>ata eva saṃskārapaṅktyāmudvāhaṃ paṭhati gautamaḥ</q> । pari-
harati---<q>satyamevametat । śāstrārthajño bhavān kathamanyathā'bhidhatte</q> । ākṣeptā
pṛcchati---<q>kastarhi bhāṣyārthaḥ</q> ? <q>so'nayeti tathāpi śruteravirodha</q> ityarthaḥ ।
yadyapi kartṛsaṃskāro vivāhaḥ śruterekavacanayuktāyā na virodhaḥ । <q>saṃskārārthāyāḥ</q>﻿
<pb n="066"/>
<q>striyā na virudhyata ityarthaḥ</q> । evamapi <q>sahatvamupapannaṃ bhavatīti manyate</q> ।
yāsau saṃskārāyotpannā patnī tasyā eva vacanāntareṇa sahakartṛtvaniyama iti nānupapanna-
mityakiñcit ।</p>
<p><q>sthitāduttaraṃ</q></p>
<p><q>atha kasmātsvāmitvaṃ na gauṇamityāśaṅkya adhikārāvirodhānna gauṇaṃ
bhavitumarhatīti rāddhāntaḥ</q> । yadi hyadhikāraśrutiviṃrudhyeta tadā tadvirodhādgauṇaṃ
svāmitvasmaraṇaṃ syāt । na cāsti virodhaḥ । <q>yathā cāvirodhastathā darśitam</q> ।</p>
<p><q>dvyādhānam । kathaṃ punaratrasaṃśayaḥ</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>yathaiva bhāṣye</q> kiṃ dvau
pumāṃsau ādadhīyātāṃ uta ekaḥ puruṣa iti । ākṣeptā āha---<q>na tathopapadyate</q>
saṃśayaḥ । <q>bhāṣye hi upapadagataṃ dvitvamupanyastam---vasānau iti</q> । <q>na caitat
pūrvapakṣāyālaṃ bhavitumarhati</q> । <q>kutaḥ ? vasanto brāhmaṇo'g‍nīnādadhīta ityeva-
mādiṣu ekatvaśravaṇāt</q> । tena kathaṃ dvayoḥ puṃsorādhānaṃ śakyate vak‍tum । nanu ca
puṃdvitvaṃ śrūyate vasānāviti । tena patnīsadvitīye puṃsyanupapatteḥ pumāṃsāvādhānasyeti
tatrāha---<q>na ca liṅgaṃ saṅkhyāmapabādhitumarhati utpattau śravaṇāt</q> । utpatti-
vākye śrutasaṅkhyā na liṅgena śakyate bādhitum । athānanyaparatvāt vākyasya liṅgaṃ saṅkhyā-
mapabādhata ityatrāha---<q>anyavidhānācca</q> । kṣaumavidhānaṃ cāvagamyate । ato'nya-
paratāpi śakyate vak‍tum । yataḥ prakṛte ādhāne ekakartṛviśiṣṭe puṃdvayaṃ vidhātuṃ na
<note>1. p 1364</note>﻿
<pb n="067"/>
śakyate । <q>ataḥ ādhānāntaraṃ vā vaktavyam</q> । atha prakṛtādhānāvagamāt ādhā-
nāntaraṃ vidhātuṃ na śakyate <q>kṣaumavidhānārthaṃ vo vasānāvityanūdyate dvitvaṃ yathā-
prāptaṃ</q> yādṛśameva dvitvaṃ prāptaṃ strīpuṃsaviṣayaṃ tādṛśamanūdyate । kṣaumaṃ vidhīyata iti nāsti
pūrvāśaṅkā ākṣepāntaraṃ cāha---<q>nanu cāsminnapi pakṣe ādadhīyātāmiti
dvivacanaṃ nopapadyate</q> pūrvaṃ hi sahabhāvena striyā anupraveśaḥ karmaṇītyuktam-sahabhāvena
dvivacanaṃ nopapadyata iti tata evoktam । tena ādadhīyātāmiti striyamabhipretya-
dvivacanānuvādo nopapadyate । tathā <q>vasānāvityapi</q> nopapadyate dvivacanam <q>vasana-
kriyāyaḥ pratyekaṃ parisamāptatvāt</q> । bhinnayorvasanakriyayorekaikasya kartṛtvāyogāt ।
samādhātā---<q>evaṃ tarhi</q> pakṣadvaye'pi doṣaṃ vadatā <q>bhavataiva saṃśayo'bhihitaḥ</q> ekasmin
pakṣe duṣṭe aparapakṣaṃ samādatte । ākṣeptā āha---<q>satyamabhihitaḥ saṃśayaḥ pakṣagrahaṇaṃ
tu na śakyate kartum</q> dvayorapi pakṣayorduṣṭatvāt । samādhātā āha---</p>
<p><q>bāḍhaṃ na śakyate kartuṃ; tvayaivedamabhihitaṃ aprāptameva dvitva-
mādhāne vasane ca</q> । <q>aprāptasya</q> cānuvādānupapatteḥ <q>vidhānādṛte</q> saṃbandhābhāvo
<q>na śakyate vak‍tumiti vidhānamebāśrayaṇīyam</q> । nanu ca yadyapi vidhānaṃ tathāpi
kathaṃ puṃsorvidhānaṃ yāvatā strīsadvitīyasya kimiti vidhānaṃ na bhavati iti tatrāha---
<q>vidhīyamāne ca dvau pumāṃsāveva vidhātavyau । kasmāt</q> ? uttaraṃ---<q>yugapadadhi-
karaṇavacanatāyāṃ dvandvasmṛteḥ</q> <quote>“yugapadadhikaraṇe dvandvaḥ”</quote> iti vārtikakāreṇa
yugapadadhikaraṇavacanatāyā dvandvaḥ smaryate । kā punariyam ? ucyate---<q>samasyamā</q>-
nānāṃ padānāṃ ye'rthāḥ teṣāṃ yadyugapat ekena padenābhidhānaṃ1 sā yugapadadhikaraṇa-
<note>1. bhisadanaṃ-mā</note>﻿
<pb n="068"/>
vacanatā । adhikaraṇaśabdena śabdasya vṛttiviṣayo'bhidhīyate---yathā dhavakhadirau
iti samāsāntargatayoḥ dhavakhadiraśabdayoḥ vā .... .... na tayorekaikena padena
dhavakhadirayorabhidhānam । nanu naitadupapannam saṃbandhagrahaṇānusāreṇa śabdo'rthamabhidhatte ।
na ca dhavaśabdo'rthadvaye gṛhītasaṃbandhaḥ । yadi cārthadvayamabhidadhyāt tadā padāntara-
prayogo'narthakaḥ । na ca lakṣaṇayā'rthadvayāvagamakatvaṃ, anupapattiṃsabandhayorabhāvāt ।
padāntaraprayogaścānarthaka ityuktam । seyaṃ yugapadadhikaraṇatā duḥkhā ca durupapādā
ceti । <q>atrābhidhīyate</q> - sahitabhāve dvandvo vartate । samasyamānapadānatirekī ca
samāsaḥ । tena ekaikameva prātipadikaṃ sahitāvasthāpannasvārthaṃ lakṣayati । svarūpa-
mātrāvasthite svārthe'bhidhānaśaktiḥ śabdasya, avasthāviśiṣṭāvasthā lakṣyate । sahita-
bhāvaścārthāntareṇa vinā na bhavatīti dvitīyapadārtho'pi tenākṣipyate । ataḥ siddhaṃ
yugapadanekārthapratipādakatvam । ata eva ca dvandve padadvaya(miti)[mapi]lākṣaṇikārtha-
miti vadanti । yaścāsāvartho lakṣyate tasya viśiṣṭasyāvagatiḥ padāntarāyatteti na
padāntarānarthakyam । <q>tadapavādtvāccaikaśeṣasyeti</q> । dvandvāpavāda ekaśeṣaḥ vṛkṣāḥ ।
<q>yadyevaṃ tataḥ kim</q> ? uttaraṃ---<q>idaṃ tato bhavati dvayoridamabhidhānaṃ tantreṇa
vasānau iti tatra ca dvau pumāṃsāveva pratīyete</q> । <q>arthāntarasya vācakābhāvāt</q> ।
vasānāviti tāvat aukārāntena śabdena ekaḥ pumān sadvitīyo'bhidhīyate । tathā
aparo'pi pumāneva tantrāvṛttyā'bhidhīyate । tatra dvitīyasyāpekṣāyāṃ pumāneva tantrā-
bhidhānenopasthāpito gṛhyate na strī tasyā vācakābhāvāt । <q>nanu cādadhīyātāmiti
dvivacanānupapattiḥ ākhyāte</q> puṃdvayasyotpattiśiṣṭaikakartṛkaviṣaye'nupraveśānupapatteḥ ।
pariharati---<q>bhavatvādhānāntaraṃ</q> yadyutpattiśiṣṭaguṇāvarodhaḥ । <q>kā naḥ pīḍā</q> ।
etaccābhyupagamyavādenoktam । kintu prakṛtādhānāvagateḥ ananyapareṇa vākyena
puṃdvitvameva vidhāsyate । viniyogaśeṣasya balīyastvāt । ādhānotpattau vyutpādana-
śeṣabhūtā saṅkhyeti । <q>nanu ca <quote>‘pumān striyā’</quote> iti smarati bhagavān pāṇiniḥ</q> ।
<pb n="069"/>
asyārthaḥ-yatra striyīva s‍trīsadvitīye'pi puṃsi aukārāntaśśabdaḥ sādhuriti । uttaraṃ---
<q>smaratyekaśeṣe puṃso vacanasya sādhutāṃ, na punaḥ stryabhidhānamaukārāntasya</q> ।
<q>taddarśitaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa</q> asyārthaḥ-yatra s‍trī ca pumāṃśca lakṣaṇāviśeṣaśabdenābhidhātu-
miṣyate tatra puṃvacanaśabdaḥ śiṣyate na s‍trīvacana iti pāṇininā smṛtam । na
punaraukārāntaśabdena s‍triyā abhidhānam । tena s‍trīvācakaśabdābhāvāt pumāneva
dvitoyo'pi gṛhyate tadidaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇāpi darśitam । <q>nanu ca</q> yadi pumāneva
dvitīyo'pi gṛhyate tadā sarvatra puṃsaḥ s‍trīsadvitīyasyā<q>prāpteḥ kathamekaśeṣaniyama
upapadyate</q> ? pariharati---<q>kenavoktamaprāptau niyama iti</q> ? codayati---
<q>yadi prāptau niyamaḥ bhavatu tarhi strī sadvitīyatā</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>bhavatu yadi prāptau
pramāṇamasti tacca nāstīti darśitam</q> । asyārthaḥ-yatra pramāṇāntareṇa dvitīyā
s‍trī pratīyate tatra saiva dvitīyā । yatra tu nāsti tatra śabdābhihitapumāneva dvitīya
iti । iha ca vidheyatvāt dvitīyo'pi pumāneva pratīyate । upasaṃharati---<q>ato
yugapadadhikaraṇavācakatvāt</q> dvayoḥ <q>puṃso(sayo)rvācako'yaṃ na niyamasya viṣaya
iti</q> । pumāṃstriyeti puṃvacanaśeṣaniyamasyāyaṃ viṣayo na bhavatītyarthaḥ । <q>tasmāt dvau
pumāṃsāviti yuktam</q> । yadi puṃdvayaparametadvākyaṃ <q>kathaṃ tarhi kṣaumaśabdo</q> vidheyārthaḥ
kathamanvīyata ityarthaḥ । uttaraṃ---<q>pradarśito'nvayaḥ</q> yaugiko'yaṃ kṣaumaśabdaḥ ṭukṣuśabde
ityasmānmapratyayāntaḥ kṣaumaśabdaḥ kṣaumavatī viceṣṭamānayorvāsasī । gauṇo vā kṣauma-
sadṛśatvāt tayormalīmasayorityanvayo darśito <q>bhāṣyakāreṇa</q> ।</p>﻿
<pb n="070"/>
<p>rāddhāntamāha---<q>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate । nāyaṃ dvayoḥ puṃsorvācaka iti
śakyate vak‍tum</q> । kasmāt ? uttaraṃ---<q>kṣaumapadavaiyarthyāt</q> apravṛttiviśeṣakaratayā
kṣaumapadavaiyarthyāt । nanu kṣaumaviśiṣṭavasanaṃ ādhānaṃ vā vidhāsyate tena nānarthakyaṃ
bhaviṣyati iti tatrāha---<q>vasanādhānayoś‍ca prāptatvāt । nanu ca pudvitvayukta-
mekatvamapi na prāptamityuktam</q> । tena guṇadvayaśravaṇāt ādhānāntaravidhirbhaviṣyati-
uttaraṃ---<q>satyaṃ puṃdvitvayuktamekatvamapi na prāptam । puṃyuktaṃ tu dvayamapi
prāptam । tataḥ kiṃ ? śrūyatāmidam । tatastadanuvādena kṣaumavidhānaṃ saṃbhavati
sadvitīyatvaṃ tu kevalaṃ mṛgyam</q> । sadvitīyapuṃviśiṣṭādhānānuvādena kṣaumavidhāne
saṃbhavati sadvitīyatvaṃ kevalaṃ mṛgyam । yo'sau pumān sadvitīyaḥ tasya kena sadvitīya-
tvamiti yadi paranveṣaṇīyaṃ tatra strī dvitīyā prāpteti tayaiva sadvitīyatvam । <q>nanu
tadeva</q> sadvitīyatvameva <q>vidhānādṛte na saṃbhavati ityuktam</q> । sahabhāvānupraviṣṭā patnī
atulyayoginī na dvitīyā bhavatītyuktam । pariharati---<q>na saṃbhavati yadyādhāna-
vasanagata evetaretarayogaḥ parigṛhyate । tathaiva ca dvandvotpattiḥ abhidhāśraya-
mapītaretarayogaṃ nānumanyante kriyāmātrāpekṣatvāt itaretarayogasya gargā
bhojyantāmiti prayogadarśanāt । devadattayajñadattaviṣṇumitrā iti ca
prayogadarśanāt</q> । asyārthaḥ---na saṃbhavati itaretarayogaḥ । pat‍nyā saha yadyādhānavasana-
gata evetaretarayogaḥ parigṛhyate yāvatā abhidhānāśrayamapi itaretarayogamanumanyante
eva । yeṣāmekābhidhānakriyānupraveśasteṣāmapi tadapekṣobhavatyevetaretarayogaḥ yathā gargā
bhojyantāmiti । dvivacanaprayogopapattau satyāṃ na prakṛtapratyayabādhanena ādhānāntaraṃ
bhavitumarhati । <q>nāpi viśiṣṭavidhānaṃ</q> bhujeḥ pratyekaparisamāptatvāt । abhidhānāśraya
<pb n="071"/>
itaretarayogaḥ । tenehāpyabhidhānāśrayamitaretarayogamāśritya strīsadvitīyatvaṃ grahīṣyate ।
ittha prayogopapattau vasānāvadadhīyātāmiti prakṛte cādhāne <q>kṣaumaśabdasya</q> mukhyārtha-
tyāgena <q>gauṇānvayo</q> rūḍhibādhena <q>yaugiko vā nābhyugantuṃ yuktaḥ । tasmāt</q>
pramāṇāntarasya vidyamānatvāt <q>sadvitīyaniyamaprayoga evāyam</q> ।</p>
<p><q>tasyā yāvaduktam ।।</q></p>
<p>nanu prayogacinteyaṃ kathamatra saṅgtetyāśaṅkyāha---<q>sthitaṃ strīpuṃsayossahā-
dhikāraḥ iti</q> । <q>idamidānīṃ sandihyate</q> । <q>kiṃ sarvaṃ yājamānaṃ pat‍nyā sahaiva
kartavyam yāgavat uta yajamānenaiva kṛtaṃ kṛtaṃ bhavatīti</q> । asyārthaḥ---yaḥ
pūrvamavikāra uktaḥ tasya sahaprayogena nirvāha iti sahaprayoga uktaḥ । tasyaivedānīṃ
viśeṣaścintyate । kiṃ sarvameva yājamānaṃ striyā sahakartavyaṃ yathā yāge dravyatyāgātmakaḥ
striyā saha kriyate tathā । na ca sarvaṃ striyā saha śakyate kartum, sammānādiṣu
kevalasyaiva yajamānasya kartṛtvam । na hi strīvyāpāraṃ binā puruṣasya sammāne kartṛtā
nopapadyate । nanu cānumatidvārā tatrāpi striyā vyāpāro bhaviṣyati । manda ! maivaṃ, tatra
hyanumatyā strī vyāpriyate yatra tadanumatiṃ vinā puṃsa eva kartṛtā nopapadyate yathā yāge ।
yatra punastadanumativyatirekeṇāpi kartṛtā tatra kathamanumatidvāreṇa pat‍nyāḥ kartṛtvam ।
anumatyāpi[tirapi]svavyāpāreṇa pravartamāne puruṣe kīdṛśīti na jñāyate । tasmāt
kevalayajamānakartṛkeṣu sahabhāvo na śakyaḥ saṃpādayitumiti sahādhikārākṣepa evāyaṃ
samādhīyate । nanvevamapi kṣaumādhikaraṇe hyevamāṅkyate sahayogepi dvivacanaṃ prāpnoti-
yathā <quote>‘ādadhīyātāṃ’</quote> iti । atha sahabhāve dvivacanaṃ na mṛṣyate puṃsorvidhistarhi
prāpnoti । tena kṣaumādhikaraṇaparyantena sahabhāve dvivacanaṃ nāstīti sthāpitatvāt
śrutyavirodhena sahādhikāra eva nirvāhyate । sa idānīmākṣepāntareṇākṣipya samādhīyate
<note>1. 1369</note>﻿
<pb n="072"/>
<q>kiṃ sarvaṃ yājamānaṃ pat‍nyā sahaiva kartavyaṃ uta yajamānenaiva kṛtaṃ kṛtaṃ bhavati</q> ।
<q>iti</q> । na sarvatra sahabhāvaḥ kintu keṣucideva । itarāṇi tu yajamānenaiva kṛtāni
[kṛtāni] । tatra pūrvapakṣavādī sahavacanaṃ sāṅgkratau manvānaḥ sahakartavyatāṃ yājamāneṣu
manyate yatkartavyaṃ tadanayā saheti smṛtyā ucyate । sāṅgaṃ ca kartavyam, naikadeśaḥ,
tasyāphalatvāt । tasmān sakalameya saha kartavyam । na caitacchakyate । tasmāt
sahaprayogābhāvāt tadbalabhāvinaḥ pat‍nyadhikārasya durghaṭateti manyate ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntavādī tu yatna tāvat vacanenaivaṃ puṃso'ṅgatvaṃ ṛtvijāmiva tatra
naiva s‍triyāḥ kartṛtvam</q> । <q>yatrāpi samākhyayā prāptiḥ tatrānyatareṇaiva siddha-
manuṣṭhānamiti viduṣi saṃbhavati na vidvattā śakyate kalpayitum</q>, anyathā-
<q>pyupapannatvādanuṣṭhānasya</q> । ayamabhiprāyaḥ-na pratipadārthaṃ1 sahabhāvaḥ sahavacanena prati-
padyate, kintu prayogaḥ, tasyaiva kartavyatvāt । yatkartavyaṃ, tat saha kartavyamiti kartavye
sahakartṛtā ucyate । kartā ca prayogeṇa saṃbadhyate, na prayojyena, prayogaścaikasmin
padārthe saha kṛte kṛto bhavati padārthasaṃpattyaiva prayoge kartṛtopapatteḥ । tatra yāge
ṛtvika‍parikraye ca dravyasādhye sahakartṛtvena prayoge sahakartṛtopapatteḥ na pratipadārthaṃ
sahabhāvena prayojanam । kintvekenāpi kṛte padārthe kṛtaḥ padārtha iti na punaḥ kartavyaḥ ।
tatrāpi yatra vacanenaiva puṃso['va]gatā <quote>‘yajamānena saṃmitā auduṃbarī bhavati’</quote> ityeva-
mādiṣu, yathā ṛtvijāṃ, tatra striyā naiva kartṛtvam । yatrāpi yajamānasamākhyayā prāptiḥ
samākhyayā liṅgaviśeṣānavadhāraṇe'pi tatrāpi vidvatsādhye viduṣi puruṣe saṃbhavati
avidyāyāḥ striyā naiva kartṛtvam । nanu yadyasau tatra kartrī na bhavati kathaṃ tatrādhikāra-
siddhiriti atrāha---<q>anyathāpyupapannatvādanuṣṭhānasya</q> । yathāvabo2dhitānuṣṭhānasiddhau
<note>1. prātipādikārthaṃ-mā</note>
<note>2. bodhikānu-mā</note>﻿
<pb n="073"/>
hi adhikārassidhyati । sahavacanenaiva sahaprayogaḥ [gaṃ]pratipādayatā ekameva pat‍nī....
yajamāna bodhikā । tatra yajamānenādhi[pi]kṛtaṃ kṛtamiti siddhatyeva pat‍nyadhikāraḥ ।
tasmāt puruṣārtheṣu vidvattā kartṛtvaṃ ceti । yatra vā pratipadavidhānaṃ anyena kṛte'nyasya
saṃskārābhāvāt adhikārasaṃskāreṣu 2striyāḥ kartṛtvam । yatra punaḥ sākṣātkartṛtvaṃ
vihitaṃ tatrāpi vidvattā kartṛtvaṃ ceti । nanu caivaṃ tatra vidyāprayuktiprasaṅgāt adhikāra
eva striyā na yuktaḥ । ucyate । sahavacanena striyāstāvadadhikāraḥ śṛṅgagrāhitvena
pratīyata eva । taṃ prati prayuktikalpanā na doṣaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>।। cāturvarṇyam ।।</q></p>
<p><q>nanu cātra bhedaṃ cintayā trayāṇāmevādhānamityuktaṃ dvitīyādhyāye</q> ।
ādhānabhedagataṃ cintayatā sūtrakāreṇa trayāṇāmeva varṇānāmādhānamityuktam । <q>na
cānāhitāgneradhikāraḥ saṃbhavati kṛtādhānasya</q> traivarṇikasya kṛts‍nānuṣṭhānasamarthasya
<q>vidyamānatvāt</q> । <q>ataḥ kimanenādhikaraṇena ? atrocyate</q> । <q>abhyupagamyā-
pyanadhikāraṃ vak‍tuṃ nimittārthatayā ādhānaśrutīnāṃ atraivarṇikānāṃ āhitāgni-
tvamabhyupagamyāpi avidvattayā'nadhikāraṃ vak‍tuṃ śūdrasyedamadhikaraṇamārabhyate</q> ।
<q>tathā hi darśayati---yadyapi nimittārthānyādhānaśravaṇāni tathāpyanadhikāra-
śśūdrasyeti</q> । bhāṣyakāro naimittikeṣvapi teṣu śakyata eva śūdraparyudāso vak‍tumi-
<note>2. 1376</note>
<note>1. kriyākartṛtvaṃ-mā</note>﻿
<pb n="074"/>
tyanenaiva granthena । <q>kiṃ punaranvāruhyavādasya prayojanam</q> ? ayabhiprāyaḥ-śūdrasyā-
nadhikāraḥ prayojanam । tattu anāhitāgnitayā siddhameveti kimapareṇa kāraṇāntareṇa
uktena । <q>ucyate</q> । <q>idamasti prayojanam upanayanepyanadhikārapradarśanam</q>
upanayanepyanadhikāraṃ pradarśayitumabhyupagamaḥ । upanayane'nadhikārasya na prayojanaṃ
anagnisādhyeṣu mantravatkarmasu śūdrasyānadhikārapradarśanam । <q>yadyu(pyu)</q>panayane'nadhikāra-
pradarśanārthametat tadā <q>upanayanamevodāharaṇīyam</q> । (śrūyate)tatkiṃ śūdrasyāpi
bhavati neti <q>na śakyate cintayitum</q>-upanayane śūdrasyādhikāro vidyate neti ।
pariharati---<q>na tat udāhartuṃ</q> upanayanaṃ na <q>śakyate</q> । <q>kimiti ? brāhmaṇasya hi
śrūyate---aṣṭavarṣa brāhmaṇamupanayīta</q> iti brāhmaṇasyopanayanaṃ śrūyate । tatkiṃ śūdrasyāpi
bhavati neti [na]śakyate cintayitum sākṣāt brāhmaṇābhisaṃbandhitvena śravaṇāt ।
kiñca siddhānte'pi upanīyādhyāpanaṃ cācāryakaraṇavidhiprayuktaṃ na svātantryeṇodāhartuṃ
śakyate aprayojakatvāt svataḥ । atrocyate । yadi upanayane'dhyayane vā kiṃ śūdrasyā-
pyadhikāro vidyate athavā traivarṇikānāmevādhikāra iti cintyate, tadā rāddhānte
traivarṇikānāmevādhikāra iti varṇayitavyam । na ca tadyuktam । svātantryeṇādhikārā-
bhāvādubhayoḥ yasmāt dvayamapyetat ācāryakaraṇavidhiprayukta(tā)tayā paraprayuktānuṣṭhānasya
labdhatvāt niradhikāratvamubhayoḥ । kasmāt punaḥ arthajñānakāma evādhikārī na
bhavatīti atrāha---<q>nacārthajñānakāmasya tadityuktam</q> arthavādādhikaraṇe adhyayana-
virodhena ca । <q>kasmāt ? upanayanādhyayanayoḥ svato niradhikāratvāt
adhikaraṇāntaramukhenaivātra vicāraśśakyate kartumiti suktam</q> । yata eva
<pb n="075"/>
śūdrasyopanayane'nadhikārapradarśanārthamidamadhikaraṇaṃ <q>ata eva bhāṣyakāreṇa etatpradhāna-
metadadhikaraṇaṃ darśayitvā jyotiṣṭomādiṣu anāhitāgnitayaivānadhikāra
ityupasaṃhṛtam</q> । asyārthaḥ-asminnadhikaraṇe upanayane śūdrasyānadhikāra iti prati-
pādyate । jyotiṣṭomādiṣu agnisādhyeṣu anāhitāgnitayāpyanadhikārassiddha‍yatyeva ।
tadarthamidamadhikaraṇaṃ na bhavatīti darśayatā bhāṣyakāreṇa jyotiṣṭomādiṣu anāhitāgnita-
yāpyanadhikāra ityuktamante ।</p>
<p>idamatrādhikaraṇe vicāryate-kimupanayanamadhyayanāṅgaṃ uta ācāryakaraṇavidhyaṅga-
miti । yadyadhyayanāṅgaṃ tadā kāmaśrutiprayuktamadhyayanaṃ śūdrasyāpi kāmaśrutiṣvadhikāraḥ ।
athācāryakaraṇavidhyaṅgamupanayanaṃ tadā ācāryavidhiprayuktamadhyayanaṃ traivarṇikānāmeva kāma-
śrutiṣvadhikāra iti । tatra pūrvapakṣavādī manyate-svādhyāyo'dhyetavya ityasya sannidhau
śrutaṃ aṣṭavarṣaṃ brāhmaṇamupanayīteti upanayanaṃ copanīyamānasannidhānakārakatayā tadarthaṃ
pratibhāti । tasya ca kāryākāṅkṣā'sti । kimanenopanayanasahakṛtena kartavyamiti ।
tathā svādhyāyo'dhyetavya iti kartrapekṣāsti । tenopanīta evādhyayane kartā । adhyayanaṃ
ca vidyāprāptyartham । prāptayā ca vidyayā kāmaśrutiṣu vidyāsādhyāsu prayojanam ।
ataḥ kāmaśrutaya eva vidyāṃ prayuñjānā adhyayanaṃ upanayanaṃ ca tadaṅgabhūtaṃ prayuñjate ।
anupāttavidyānāṃ ca kāmaśrutiṣu vidyāprayojikāsu adhikāra iti kāmitvāviśeṣāt
śūdrasyāpyadhikāraḥ syāt । sa cādhikāra upanayanaparyanta iti । upanayane cāpyadhi-
kāra iti svāmitvaṃ śūdrasya । nanu cātmanepadaprayogāt upanayīteti tasyācāryakaraṇe
vartamānādupanayatervidhānāt ācāryakaraṇavidhyaṅgamevopanayanaṃ prayuñjāna ācārya-
karaṇavidhiḥ adhyayanamapi prayokṣyate । upanayanasya hi upanīyamānāsattidvāreṇācārya-
karaṇavidhyupakārakatā syāt adhyāpanena cācāryo bhavati । na cādhyāpanamadhyayanaṃ vinā
bhavati । pratīyate copanītakartṛkamadhyayanaṃ tenādhyayanaṃ kurvāṇameva māṇavakamupasādayat
upanayanamaṅgamiti bhavati adhyayanaṃ prati ācāryakaraṇavidheḥ prayuktiḥ । tataśca yeṣā-
mevopanayanaṃ teṣāmevādhyayanaṃ teṣāṃ vidyāvatāmadhikāra iti śūdrasyānadhikāra iti ।</p>
<p>ucyate । syādetadevaṃ yadi ātmanepadādācāryavidhyarthatā upanayanasyāva-
gamyate । kintvācāryakaraṇasaṃpattiḥ । sā pārārthenāpyupapadyata eva । kathaṃ punarupanīya-
mānamāṇavakārthatā upanayanasyāvagamyate ? tadāsattiphalatvāt । yo'pi hi ācārya-
karaṇavidhyarthatāmupanayanasyāha [tasyāpi] gamyate kintvācāryakaraṇasampattissā parārthena
so'pi māṇavakāsattiphalakameva tadicchati । gatameva tatphalaṃ tasyaiva । yasyaiva ca
<pb n="076"/>
yatkarma tattadarthameva tadyuktaṃ pratyāsatteḥ na punarācāryārtham । evaṃ copanayanaṃ tadaṅgameva ।
tena ca māṇavakasya saṃskāro'narthaḥ adhyayanavidhyavidyamānatvāt । na cādhyaya-
namanarthakaṃ kāmaśrutiprayuktatvāt । ato'dhyayanāṅgatvādupanayanasya kāmaśrutiprayukta-
madhyayanasya śūdrasyādhikāro mantravatsvapi karmasviti ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntī tvāha---aṣṭavarṣaṃ brāhmaṇamuyanayīteti ātmanepadaśravaṇāt ācārya-
karaṇasaṃpādakamupanayanaṃ upanīyamānāsattilakṣaṇakārakaphalamavagamyate । tataścopanayane
ācāryakaraṇasya yujyata eva kartṛtvaṃ, ekakartṛka[ta]yā ācāryakaraṇopanayanayoraṅgā-
ṅgibhāvo'vagamyata iti ācāryakaraṇavidhyarthamevopanayanam । yacca yasyāṅgaṃ sa eva tat
prayojayati iti ācāryakaraṇavidhiprayuktamupanayanaṃ tanmukhenādhyayana ca । tataścānyavidhi-
prayuktavidyālābhāt kāmyaśrutayo na vidyāṅgaṃ prayuñjate ityācāryakaraṇavidhyaṅgatvāt
upanayanasya ca tatprayuktatvāt । adhyayanavidhibhyaḥ śūdrasya mantravatsvanadhikāro vidyā-
virahāditi sthitam ।</p>
<p><q>।। trayāṇām ।।</q></p>
<p><q>nanu ca dravyaṃ na prayuṅkte karmavidhirityuktam</q> । <q>tasmādadhikāro[re] na
ghaṭata eveyaṃ cintā</q> । <q>yathāsthite karmabhede'nāhitāgneḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---caturthā-
dhyāye idamuktam kāmaśrutayo dravyaṃ na prayuñjata iti । tena adravyaḥ kiṃ adhikriyate
neti cintaiveyaṃ nopapadyate rāddhāntasyāsaṃbhavāt । yadi hi adravyo'pyadhikriyate tadā
adhikāre sati vidhayo'pi dravyārjanaṃ prayuñjīran । na ca prayuñjata iti sthitam ।
ato'dravyasyādhikāro nāstīti phalataḥ caturthe pratipāditam jīvanārthopāyārjitadravya
evādhikriyata iti arthādupapadyate yataḥ । yathā dvitīye karmabhede sthite prāpakeṣu
ādhānavidhiṣu satsu anāhitāg‍neradhikāre niraste śūdrasyādhikāracintā ghaṭate tatheyaṃ
<note>1. p 1381</note>﻿
<pb n="077"/>
cintā na ghaṭata iti vaidharmyadṛṣṭānto'yam । kathaṃ tathā na ghaṭata ityatrocyate---
<q>na cānyat prayojanamasti upanayanavat</q> caśabdo hetau । yathā pūrvādhikaraṇe
upanayanaṃ prayojanamasti tatheha prayojanaṃ nāsti yena kṛtvācintānyāyena cintā syāt ।
ataḥ na śakyamevedemadhikaraṇaṃ adhikāracintāyām । samādhatte---<q>ucyate yata eva
dravyaṃ na prayuñ‍jate karmavidhayaḥ ata eveyamadhikāre cintopapadyate</q> । yadi
karmavidhayo dravyaṃ prayuñ‍jata iti syāt tadā'dravyasyādhikāropapatteḥ pūrvapakṣābhā-
vāt neyamadhikāracintopapadyate । yatastu dravyārjanaṃ karmavidhayo na prayuñjate
ata eveyaṃ pūrvapakṣasaṃbhavena cintopapadyate । <q>kathaṃ ? kimanāhitāgnimiva karma-
śrutayaḥ śak‍nuvanti adravyaṃ nirasituṃ uta neti</q> yathā anāhitāgniṃ karmaśrutayaḥ
nirasyanti tathā kimadravyaṃ nirasyanti uta neti । kiṃ punarnirāse bījamiti atrāha
<q>dravyopādānamanākṣipantya iti</q> । yadi dravyopādānaṃ(mā)nākṣipanti tataḥ pūrvopātta-
dravyamadhikurvate anyathā dravyopādānākṣegprasaṅgāt । <q>tatra pūrvavādino'bhiprāyaḥ-
anāhitāgnimivādravyaṃ dravyopādānamanākṣipantya karmaśrutayaḥ adhikartuṃ na
śak‍nuvanti</q> iti । <q>tasmādanadhikāro'dravyasyeti</q> ।</p>
<p><q>atrābhidhīyate---na śakyata etadanāhitāgnimiva adravyaṃ nirūpa-
yitum</q> । asyārthaḥ---svābhāvikī śaktiradhikāriviśeṣaṇaṃ; adravyasyāpi ca
dravyasādhyakarmānuṣṭhānaśaktirasti adravyasyāpi dravyaṃ bhavatyeva । yadi punarevaṃ nirūpayet
asya dravyaṃ na bhavatyeveti tadā'tyantamaśakyatvādadravyasyānadhikāraḥ syāt । yathā
<pb n="078"/>
śūdrasyāgnivirahiṇo'tyantāśakteranadhikāraḥ । <q>tatra hi śūdrādijātiravacchedikā
vidyate evaṃ</q> jāteragnayo na santīti <q>iha punaḥ ādānamaniyataṃ kadācidupādatte</q> ।
<q>kadācinnopādatte sa eva</q> । tena svābhāvikī puruṣāṇāṃ dravyatāśaktirasti । <q>tasmā-
nnaikāntato dravyanirāsassaṃbhavati</q> । tena svābhāvikī śaktiḥ[a]dravyasyāpi tāva
dadhikāro'sti । <q>adhikṛtasya jīvanāyeva karmaṇopyupādānaṃ prāptaṃ</q> yuktamityarthaḥ ।
<q>nanu copādānaśeṣanirāsaḥ</q> caturthādhyāyoktaḥ <q>evaṃ samud‍vṛtto bhavati</q> । pariharati-
<q>noda‍dhriyate</q> । <q>nimittatvena hi asmābhiridamucyate</q> । <q>na śeṣitayā</q> prayojana-
bhūtatayā puruṣasya jīvanamiva dravyopādāne karmāpi nimittaṃ na punaretadeva śeṣītyarthaḥ ।
yata eva śeṣatā dravyārjananiyamasya neṣyate <q>ata eva tatrāpyuktam karmārjitamapi
ārjito vrīhireva</q> । <q>ihāpyuktam jīviṣyati vinā dhanenetyanupapannam iti</q> ।
caturthe hyevamuktam vrīhibhiryajeteti vrīhimātramaṅgatayā vidhīyate, na punaḥ pratigrahādyapi ।
tena karmārthamapi laukikabhojanakarmārthamapi yadi vrīhirupārjyate tadā vrīhibhiryāgo bhava-
tyeva tena vaiguṇyaṃ nāsti । tathā atraivādhikaraṇe uktaṃ <quote>‘jīviṣyati vinā dhanenetyanu-
papannaṃ’</quote> iti । tena jīvanopārjitena yakṣyata ityuktam । nanu cedamayuktaṃ---jīviṣyati
vinā dhanenetyanupapannamiti । etatkilānenoktam । yo jīvettasya jīvanānupapattyā
dravyamasti tena yāgaḥ kariṣyata iti । taccānupapannam---dravyeṇāpi vinā pratiniyata-
karmakāle jīvanasaṃbhavāt । tathā kratvanaṅgenāpi dravyeṇa kodravādinā jīvanopapatteḥ ।
tathāpi kenāpi jīvato nāvaśyaṃ dravyamasti tena nirviṣayamevedamadhikaraṇamiti pṛcchati-
<q>kimanenoktam</q>---iti । uttaraṃ---<q>idamanenoktam aniyatamidamupādānaṃ na
nirāsāyālamiti</q> । etaduktaṃ bhavati-jīvato dhanābhāva ityanupapannam । vyabhicārāt
tenāniyatamupādānam । ato'dravyasyāpi śaktirastīti nādhikāranirāsaḥ । adhikara-﻿
<pb n="079"/>
ṇārthamupasaṃharati---<q>tasmājjīvanāyeva karmaṇopyupādāne yatnaḥ kartavyaḥ</q> । adra-
vyasyādhikāro[re]dravyārjanaprayok‍tṛtvaṃ karmaṇāṃ prasajyate । taccaturthe nirākṛtamiti
pūrvaḥpakṣaḥ । adravyasyādhikāre caturthoktavirodho nāsti । śeṣatā hi tatra pratiṣiddhā na
punaḥ prayojanatāpi bhojanādivat prayuktiriti rāddhāntaḥ adravyasya svābhāvikī
śaktirastītyadhikāro yukta(me)eveti siddhametat । svābhāvikaśaktipratipattyarthaṃmeva
cātra niyatatā dravyavattāyā uktā ।</p>
<p><q>।। aṅgahīnaśca ।।</q></p>
<p>pūrvapakṣamāha---<q>kiṃdharmā ?</q> - asyārthaḥ - na tāvat adravyadharmā śakyate vak‍tuṃ
akalyāṇāṅgaḥ । yasmāt adravyasyāpi dravyasaṃbhavayogyatā dravyavattākālavadaviśiṣṭā,
akalyāṇāṅgasya tu rogavattayāśaktirapagataiva ।</p>
<p>auṣadhādiprayoge punaḥ śaktirutpādya iti tasyāmavasthāyāṃ śaktirupagateti nādravya-
tulyatā । tasmānna jñāyate kiṃdharmā aṅgahīna iti । rāddhāntamāha---<q>adravyadharme-
tyarthaḥ</q> । <q>sa eva hi kadācidaṅgahīno bhavati kadācit kalyāṇāṅgaḥ</q> ।
asyārthaḥ---yo na rogeṇa kāryaṃ prati vyāpṛtaḥ sa eva tasya cikitsāyāṃ satyāṃ punaḥ
kāryaṃ kurvan‍nupalabhyate । tathā ca rogeṇa naiva śaktiḥ nāśitetyavagamyate । ciki-
tsāyāṃ satyāṃ kāryadarśanāt । tena śakteḥ satyā eva pratibandhabhūto rogaḥ cikitsa-
yā'panīyata iti kalpyate । kaḥpunarniścayaḥ nāśotpādau na staḥ pratibandhāpagamāveva
kevalau iti ? ucyate । vināśo nāma ātyantikopalabdhivicchedaḥ । sa ca
śakternāsti punaḥ kāryeṇopalambhāt । utpādopyatyantānupalabdhasya punarupalaṃbhanaśaktiḥ ।
prāgatyantānupalabdharogasya purataḥ kāryeṇauvopalambhāt iti । tataśca tirohitaśakterapi
<note>1. p 1382</note>﻿
<pb n="080"/>
śaktirastīti yukta evādhikāraḥ ityadravyadharmaiva cititsyarogaḥ : <q>tasmādadhikṛtena
satā cikitsādiṣu yatnaḥ kartavyaḥ dravyopādānavat</q> । yasya punarapratisamādhe-
yaivākalyāṇāṅgatā [sa]śakyate nādhikṛta iti vak‍tuṃ śūdravat । śaktināśaśca ātya-
ntikopalambhavicchedaḥ । yathāhi tatra śūdratvaṃ nirāsahetuḥ nityāvagamyatvāt tadvada-
pratisamādheyatvamapīti tulyam । yathā śūdrasyāśaktiḥ atyantamanapāya t jāteḥ tathā-
naṣṭaśaktikāṅgyogitvamapīti । yadā putaḥ pravṛttayāga evāṅgairhīyate tadā kathaṃ ?
yāgaṃ kurvāṇasya(kasya) akalyaṅgatā vartate yadā tadā cikitsāvā abhāvāt katha-
madhikāra iti । ya eva dravye'pyupāyaḥ sa evātrāpi bhaviṣyati yayā prabṛttaprayoga-
madhya eva yo dravyarahitaḥ tasya yathā'dhikāro'napagataḥ tathā'kalyāṇāṅgasyāpīti bhāvaḥ ।
sa cābhyupāyaḥ pratinidhāvupadiśyate ।</p>
<p><q>।। atryārṣeyasya ।।</q></p>
<p><q>nanu kimidaṃ bhinnaṃ vākyaṃ uta ekamiti cintanīyam</q> । atra kila
bhāṣyakāraḥ prathamaṃ tāvadidaṃ cintayati <quote>‘ārṣeyaṃ vṛṇīte’</quote> iti sāmānyeta vidhiḥ
tena prāptānyekasya dvayostrayāṇāṃ ca varaṇāni ekaṃ vṛṇīte ityādibhiḥ pradarśyante ।
tathā <quote>‘na caturo vṛṇīte’</quote> <quote>‘na pañcātipravṛṇīte’</quote> ityābhyāṃ caturṇāṃ atītapañcānāṃ ca
varaṇaṃ pratiṣidhyata iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ <q>rāddhāntastu</q> ārṣeyaṃ vṛṇīte ityārṣeyavaraṇacodanā ।
trīn vṛṇīte iti tatraiva saṅkhyāvidhānam । <quote>‘ekaṃ vṛṇīte’</quote> iti cāvayutyānuvādaḥ ।
<quote>‘na caturo vṛṇīte’</quote> na pañcātipravṛṇīte’ iti nityānuvāda ityetattāvadatra na cinta-
nīyam । kutaḥ ? arṣeyaṃ vṛṇīte ityukte dvayostrayāṇāṃ ca varaṇaṃ prāptameva । upā-﻿
<pb n="081"/> 
dānaśeṣatvādekasaṅkhyāyāḥ । tena dvitvasya tritvasya cāvaśyaṃ vidheyatvameva yuktam ।
tayośca vihitayorekatvasya prāptirnāstīti tadapi vidheyam । tathā ekatvadvitvabahu-
tvānāṃ vidhānato viniyogaśeṣatvāt caturādīnāṃ prasaktireva nāstīti kathaṃ pratiṣedha
iti । tasmādidamatra cintanīyam---ārṣeyavaraṇe codite kimekatvādīni trīṇyapi
vidadhati bhinnānyetāni । [ni] yogaśeṣatvāt caturādīnāṃ prasaktireva nāstīti kathaṃ
pratiṣedha iti । tasmādidaṃ śāstrāṇi uta tritvavidhāyakamekamidaṃ śāstramiti ।
tatrāvayutyānuvāde <quote>‘ekaṃ vṛṇīte’</quote> <quote>‘dvau vṛṇīta iti tasyaiva stutyarthau । tathā ca na
caturo vṛṇīta iti lāghavena stutyartho nityānuvāda iti । tathā caitadeva
darśayan bhāṣyakāraścodayati---<quote>“nanu caikaṃ vṛṇīta ityapi viśeṣavacanamasti”</quote> iti
prathamaṃ yadbhāṣyakāreṇopanyastaṃ tat mandāpyāśaṅkā nirākaraṇīyetyanenābhiprāyeṇa । tasmāt
kimidamekaṃ uta bhinnamiti cintanīyam । <q>tacca śāstrabhedābhedopayogi, nādhi-
kāropayogi</q> । tena lakṣaṇasaṅgatirnāstītyarthaḥ । samādhatte---<q>satyamevaṃ sa tu bhedā-
bhedo'pyadhikāra eva viśeṣamādadhāti ityadhikāra eva cintyate</q> । asyārthaḥ---
yadyapi śāstrabhedābhedāvapi bhavataḥ tathāpyadhikāralakṣaṇa eveyaṃ cintocitā । yasmāt
bhede sati ekārṣeyasya cādhikāro bhavati abhede tu tryārṣeyasyaiveti । evaṃ sati
bhavati manuvat bharatavat amukavat iti yajamānasyārṣeyaṃ vṛṇīteti । tenaivaṃ
prayogakāle yajamānasyārṣeyāṇi varaṇīyāni-manuvat bharatavat śāṇḍilyavat asitavat
devalavat ayaṃ devadattaśarmā yajata iti । tatra yasya yābanta ārṣeyāḥ tāvantastasya
varītavyāḥ । tatra ekatvadvitvayorapi vidhiḥ syāt, tadaikārṣeyadva‍yārṣeyāṇāmapi adhi-
kāro bhavati ārṣeyavaraṇāṅgopasaṃhāro samarthatvāt । ārṣeyavaraṇaṃ hi kathaṃbhāvā-
vasthayā vihitaṃ syāt na samuccayena, asaṃbhavāt । yo hi ekārṣeyo yajamānaḥ tasyai-
kārṣeyavaraṇaṃ vihitam । dva‍yārṣeyatryārṣeyayostu yathāyathaṃ dva‍yārṣeyatryārṣeyavaraṇaṃ na punaḥ
sarveṣāmeva sarvāṇi varaṇāni vihitāni, tathāvivasya yajamānasyāsaṃbhavāt । yadā
punaḥ tritvameva kevalaṃ vidhīyate tadā tryārṣeyāṅgayukte karmaṇi tryārṣeṃya eva
yajamāno'dhikārī syāt ityadhikāraviśeṣāpādakatvāt <q>yāvatsaṅkhyākalpaneti ।</q>
asyārthaḥ---ekaṃ vṛṇīte ityevamādīnāṃ laḍantatvāt sākṣādvidhirna śrūyate । na ca
vidhimantareṇa tritvādīnāmanuvādatvenopapattiriti vacanāni tvapūrvatvāditi <q>vidhiḥ
kalpayitavyaḥ</q> । na ca kaścidviśeṣo'stīti <q>yāvatsu saṅkhyā</q> tāvatsu vidhireva
<q>kalpayitavyaḥ । ityevaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate । na yāvatsaṅkhyaṃ</q> vidheya<q>kalpanā
<pb n="082"/> 
<q>bhavitumarhati । kutaḥ ? parasparasaṃbandhāvagateḥ</q> । yadi parasparasaṃbandhaḥ saṅkhyā-
śabdānāṃ na syāt tadā bahavo vidhayaḥ kalpyeran । avagamyate tu parasparasaṃbandhaḥ ।
<q>tatra yasyāḥ saṅkhyāyā vidhāvāśrīyamāṇe naikavākyatā'paipi tadvidhīyata
iti nyāyāt</q> triṣu ca vidhīyamāneṣu anuvādopapatterekavākyopapatteriti । atra
codayati---<q>nanu ca yuktaṃ <quote>‘na caturo vṛṇīte’</quote> <quote>‘na pañcātipravṛṇīte’</quote> iti
triṣu vidhīyamāneṣu anuvādopapatteḥ ekavākyatvaṃ vidhānābhāvādeva varaṇā-
bhāvasya prāptasyānuvādaḥ <quote>‘<q>ekaṃ’</quote> <quote>‘dvau'</quote> iti tu nānuvādo ghaṭate । aprāptatvā-
dbhinnānyetāni vākyānītyuktam ।। ata eva pañ‍cānāṃ varaṇaṃ nyāyyameveti
manyāmahe</q> । yadi hyekavākyatvaṃ bhavet tadā <quote>‘na caturo vṛṇīte’</quote> <quote>‘na pañcāti-
pravṛṇīte’</quote> iti anāvṛttavākyaśravaṇāt pañcānāṃ na varaṇaṃ kalpyeta । yadā kalpyeta tadā
tadarthamapi vākyaśeṣasyāvṛttyā sakṛcchravaṇaṃ bādhyeta । yadā tu bhinnāni vākyāni
tadā vākyaśeṣasya sakṛcchravaṇabādhe siddhe pañcavidhisaṃbandhitayāpi āvṛttiḥ kalpyamānā
nānupapanneti pañcānāmapi varaṇaṃ nyāyyamevetyuktam । kathaṃ punaḥ pañcānāmapi varaṇa-
prāptirāṅkyate ? itthaṃ, naño'nuvāda upapannataro bhavati na caturo vṛṇīte na
pañcātipravṛṇīte iti । yadi pañcānāmapi varaṇaṃ na syāt tadā <q>itthaṃ nañarthasya</q>
varaṇābhāvasyā<q>nuvāda upapanno bhavati</q> pañcānāṃ tu varaṇābhāve sati pañcatikrameṇa
varaṇābhāvānuvādo nistātparyaka eva syāt । ataḥ pañcānāmapi varaṇaṃ nyāyya- 
meveti । <q>atrocyate---uktamasmābhiḥ sakalapadaikavākyatā । nanu ca ekaṃ
dvau iti anuvādāsaṃbhavāt anupapannaivetyuktam</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>na nāma triṣvanu-
<note>1. ms. na kathañcittvanuvādaḥ</quote>﻿
<pb n="083"/> 
<q>vādaḥ na ca saṅkhyā saṅkhyāntare'nuvartata iti nyāyāt</q> । nāmaśabdo'ṅgīkāre ।
etaduktaṃ bhavati---na saṅkhyā saṅkhyāntare vartata iti nyāyena tritve ekatva-
dvitvayorabhāvādanuvāda āñjasyena na ghaṭate ityaṅgīkurmaḥ । <q>yatpunaridaṃ nañ-
vākyaṃ tatkena saṃbadhyate sarvaissaṅkhyāvākyairaviśeṣāditi cet । siddhā
tarhyekavākyatā</q> । yadi sarvaiḥ saṅkhyāvākyaiḥ naña‍vākyasya saṃbandhaḥ tadā siddhā
ekavākyatā syāt । <q>yasmāt na naña‍vākye'sya pratyekaparisamāptau
pramāṇamasti । kathaṃ nāsti</q> ? uttaraṃ---sakṛcchravaṇāt pratyekaparisamāptau pramāṇaṃ
nāsti । <q>yadi hi</q> sakṛcchravaṇepi pratyekaparisamāptiḥ <q>syāt</q> tadā <q>ekatvādīnā-
mapi</q> <q><quote>‘na caturo vṛṇīte’</quote> <quote>‘na pañcātipravṛṇīte’</quote> iti pratyekameva
syānnaño'bhyāsaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---ekatvādīnāmapi kṛte naño'bhyāsaḥ syāt ।
tataścaivaṃ syāt ekaṃ na vṛṇīte na trīn vṛṇīte iti । bhavatvevaṃ, kā naḥ pīḍeti ।
atrāha---<q>niṣprayojanaśca saḥ</q> । prayojanaśūnyo'bhyāsaḥ syādityarthaḥ । kiñca
<q>nañarthaparatvādekādīnāṃ caturṇāṃ atītapañcānāṃ ca</q> sarveṣāṃ vihitapratiṣiddhatayā
<q>vikalpaḥ prāp‍noti</q> । nanu pramāṇabalena vikalpaḥ prāp‍nuvanna doṣa iti manyamānasya
matamāśaṅkate---<q>bhavatviti cet । na pakṣāntarāvalambanenāpi parihāro bhavati
iti naño'bhyāsakalpanānyāyyā</q> । abhyāsakalpanāyāṃ vikalpaḥ prāp‍noti ।
so'nāvṛttyāśrayaṇena parihriyate । tena prāmāṇikatvaṃ vikalpasya vadituṃ na śakyate ।
<q>yāvāṃś‍ca śrutasyotsarge doṣaḥ tāvānaśrutavākyasyāvṛttikalpanāyām ।
tasmādāvṛttiḥ kalpayituṃ [na]nyāyyeti nyāyavido vadanti । tasmādvaramava-﻿
<pb n="084"/>
<q>yutyānuvāda evāśrayaṇīyaḥ sāmañ‍jasyāt</q> । sakṛcchravaṇādityarthaḥ । anyathā
hi sakṛcchravaṇādbādhitaṃ syāt । nanvevamapi bhavatveko vidhiḥ vākyaśeṣasya sakṛdanu-
mānānuguṇyāt sa tu trayāṇāmeveti kutaḥ ityatrāha---<q>trayāṇāṃ ca na saṃbhavati</q>
ekasya dvayorvā vidhāvāśrīyamāṇe trayāṇāmanuvādo na saṃbhavati । trayāṇāṃ tu vidhā-
ne'vayutya ekasya dvayoścānuvādo ghaṭata iti । <q>atastrayāṇāmeva (vā)vidhānam</q> ।
adhikaraṇārthamupasaṃharati - <q>atastrayāṇāmeva varaṇaṃ tryārṣeyasya cādhikāra iti
sthitam</q> । etāvati vacane tāvadayaṃ śāstrārthaḥ । yadi punaraparāṇi vacanāni tadā
bhavatu atryārṣeyāṇāmapyadhikāra iti niravadyam ।</p>
<p><q>।। vacanāt ।।</q></p>
<p><q>atra pūrvapakṣavādī vidvatsādhyatvādādhānasya upanayanasādhyatvāt vidva-
dbhāvasya yepāmevopanayanaṃ teṣāmevādhānavidhirupapanno bhavatīti manvānaḥ
naisargikānāmevānena nimittena ādhānamiti varṇitabān</q> । asyārthaḥ---
traivarṇikānāmevopanayanaṃ yeṣāṃ copanayanaṃ teṣāmeva vidyā ācāryakaraṇavidhiprayuktatvāt
adhyayanasya । yeṣāmeva vidyā teṣāmevādhānaṃ yuktam vidvatsādhyatvādādhānasya । tataśca
traivarṇikānāmeva rathakaraṇena nimittena ādhānāntarametadvidhīyata iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
<q>ye punaḥ rathakārā brāhmaṇādayaḥ teṣāṃ vasantādikālakramādhānavidhānaṃ
bhaviṣyati pāriśeṣyāditi sarvamupapannam । yatpunaratra bhāṣyaṃ traivarṇikānāṃ
<pb n="085"/>
<q>śilpopajīvitvaṃ niṣiddhamiti tadayuktamiva pratibhāti niṣedhātikramaṇādapyā-
dhānavidhānaṃ [na] naivopapadyate</q> ye pratiṣedhātikrameṇa śilpamupajīvanti teṣāmapyā-
dhānavidhānamupapadyata eva <q>puruṣārthatvāt pratiṣedhasyāgna‍yarthatvācca</q> ādhānasya
sādhyabhedena ādhāna-śilpopajīvitvapratiṣedhayoraṅgāṅgi[bhāvā]bhāvāt na pratiṣedha
ādhānāṅgaṃ, kiṃ tarhi ? puruṣārthaḥ । <q>na ca puruṣārthātikrameṇādhānasya vaiguṇyaṃ
śakyate vak‍tum</q> । yadi vaiguṇyaṃ syāt tadā atikrāntaniṣedhānāmādhānaṃ na syāt ।
na cāsti vaiguṇyamiti samarthante । <q>satyamevaṃ, aucityamaṅgīkṛtyaitaduktam</q>
ye ucitācārās‍traivarṇikāḥ te tāvat śilpopajīvino na saṃbhavantītyanenā-
bhiprāyeṇaitaduk‍tam । yata evaucityāśrayaṇenaitaduktaṃ na punassarvathā śilpopajīvi-
tvāsaṃvena <q>ata eva brāhmaṇādīnāṃ niyatakālataivādhānasya ādhānāntarā-
saṃbandhe heturuktaḥ</q> । vasantādikālataivādhānasya ādhānāntarāsaṃbandhe heturuktaḥ ।
sarveṣāmeva traivarṇikānāmaviśeṣeṇa vasantādikālakādhānaśravaṇānnādhānāntarasaṃbandho yukta
ityarthaḥ । iyamapi cābhyupagamyayuktireva । rathakaraṇena nimittenādhānāntarasaṃbhavāt ।
paramayuktimāha---<q>jātyantaropanyāsaśca traivarṇikanimittaḥ paramārthato heturuktaḥ</q> ।
rūḍhyaiva rathakāraśabdena jātyantarasyābhidhānaṃ yogabalenaiva traivarṇikānām । rūḍhiśca
yogādbalīyasīti । evaṃ hi smṛtiḥ---<quote>“māhiṣyeṇa karaṇyāṃ tu rathakāraḥ prajāyate”</quote>
iti vaiśyāṅganāyāṃ kṣatriyajo māhiṣya ityucyate । tadāhuḥ---</p>
<p><quote>“māhiṣyograu prajāyete viṭa‍śūdrāṅganayornṛpāt”</quote> । karaṇaśca śūdrāyāṃ vaiśyena
jātaḥ । taduktaṃ <quote>‘śūdrāyāṃ karaṇo vaiśyāt’</quote> iti । tena māhiṣyena karaṇyāṃ jātasya
rūḍhyā rathakāraśabdo vācaka iti tasyaivedamādhānam । <q>yat punaḥ aviduṣo nādhāna-
mityuktam asati vacane tadupapadyate vacane punaḥ kā nāmeyamanupapattiḥ</q>---yadā
<pb n="086"/>
śrṛṅgagrāhikayā rathakārasyādhānaṃ vihitaṃ tadā kācidanupapattirnāstītyarthaḥ । vidyāpi
tadbalena bhaviṣyatīti bhāvaḥ । yadā vidyāpyasti tadā vidyālābhāya <q>kimanupanayane-
nāpi teṣāṃ saudhanvanāṃ bhavatu?</q> uttaraṃ---<q>yadi vacanamasti bhavatu upanayanādikaṃ
asati vidhāne strīṇāmivādhānavidhānādevāyaṃ bhaviṣyati</q> । tāvanmātreṇai-
vādhānavidhānopapatteḥ nopanayanākṣepe sāmarthyamastīti । adhikāralakṣaṇamadhikaraṇamiti
lakṣaṇasaṅgatisiddhaye adhikāraviśeṣādhāyakenānena bhavitavyamiti pṛcchati---<q>kasya
punaratra rathakārādhāne'dhikāraḥ ? rathakārasyeti brūmaḥ । rājña iva rājasūye</q> । atra
codayati---<q>nanu cāyaṃ kartṛnirdeśo nādhikāranirdeśaḥ</q> varṣāsu rathakāra ādadhīta
iti rathakāraśabdaḥ kartṛnirdeśaḥ rathakārajāterupādeyakartṛnirdeśaḥ rathakārajāterupādeya-
tvānnādhikāranirdeśaḥ । ekagranthenāha---<q>yathaiva brāhmaṇādayo vasantādikālakeṣu
kartṛtvena nirdiśyante nādhikṛtatayā evamatrāpi</q> । rathakārādhikāravādyāha---yadi
brāhmaṇādayaḥ kartṛtvena nirdiśyante nādhikṛtatayā <q>evaṃ tarhi tatkartṛkeṣvādhāneṣu
kasyādhikāraḥ ?</q> ayamāśayaḥ---yathā brāhmaṇādīnāmadhikāraḥ tathā rathakārasyāpi
bhaviṣyati । adhikārāpavādyāha---<q>na kasyaciditi brūmaḥ</q> । adhikāriṇo'śravaṇāditi ।
rathakārādhikāravādyāha---<q>kiṃ tarhīdamuktaṃ traivarṇikānāmadhikāra iti</q> । apaśūdrādhi-
karaṇe traivarṇikānāmadhikāra ityuktam । tenopādeyāpi brāhmaṇādijātiḥ adhikāri-
viśeṣaṇameveti manyate । uttaraṃ---<q>svargakāmasya traivarṇikasya jyotiṣṭomādiṣva-
dhikāra ityuktam</q> । jyotiṣṭomādiṣu svargakāmo'dhikārīti sthitam । sa tu svargakāmo
brāhmaṇādirnānya ityuktam । na punarjātirevādhikāriviśeṣaṇam । adhikāravādyāha---
yadi niradhikāraṃ <q>evaṃ tarhi aṅgamādhānaṃ</q> kratūnāṃ syāt । itara āha---<q>nāṅgaṃ agna‍ya-﻿
<pb n="087"/> 
<q>rthatvāt</q> । asyārthaḥ---niradhikāratve'pyādhānasya na karmārthatvam agna‍yarthatvenāvagamāt ।
nanu karmārthāgnimukhena avadhātādivat karmārthatā na syāt ityatrāha <q>agnayo hi
karmārthāḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---agnayaḥ siddhāḥ santaḥ karmaṇi viniyujyante na puna-
rviniyuktānāmevotpattiriti tṛtīye pradarśitam । tena karmāsaṃbandhāgna‍yutpādakatvānna
karmārthatā ādhānasya । yadyanaṅgamādhānaṃ <q>kathaṃ tarhi traivarṇikasvargakāmo jyoti-
ṣṭomādiṣvadhikriyata iti śakyate vak‍tum anaṅgatvādādhānasya</q> । yadi
hi aṅgamādhānaṃ syāt tadā'traivarṇikasyāśakyatvāt traivarṇikasyādhikāraḥ syāt ।
uttaramāha---<q>anagnitvādatraivarṇikānāmanadhikāra ityuktam । na punaḥ traivarṇikā
evādhikriyanta iti</q> । asyārthaḥ---yadyapyanaṅgamādhānaṃ tathāpyatraivarṇikasyānadhi-
kāraḥ । asyārthaḥ---jātiradhikāriviśeṣaṇaṃ na bhavati ityevaṃvidhe'bhyupagame <q>sidhya-
tyeva jyotiṣṭomādiṣu adhikāraḥ</q> svargakāmādīnām । anupādeyaviśeṣaṇaviśi-
ṣṭānāmadhikāriṇāṃ vidyamānatvāt । <q>ādhāne punaḥ</q> tadvidhānasyāparasyāśravaṇāt jāte-
ścādhikāriviśeṣaṇatvābhāvābhyupagamāt <q>kasyādhikāraḥ</q> । na ca niradhikāraṃ
bhaviṣyatīti vācyam, niradhikārasya karmaṇo'nuṣṭhānāpatteḥ । ekagranthenāha---<q>sarva-
syeti prāpte jātyaṅgāsaṃpatteḥ traivarṇikānāmeva bhavati । yathā svārājya-
kāmasya kṣatriyasyaivādhikāro rājasūye śrūyate</q> । <quote>‘rājasūyena svārājyakāmo
yajeta’</quote> iti rājavyatirikte kartari rājajātyasaṃpratipatteḥ rājña evādhikāraḥ
tathehāpi brāhmaṇajātisaṃpattaye brāhmaṇādīnāmādhāne'dhikāraḥ । yadi brāhmaṇajāti-
saṃpattaye brāhmaṇādīnāmadhikāra ādhāne <q>evaṃ tarhi</q> atrāpi rathakārādhāne'pi <q>evaṃ</q>
jātyasaṃpatteḥ rathakārasyaivādhikāra <q>iti siddham</q> । tena sādhūktaṃ rathākārasyeti brūma
iti । <q>āhitāgnitayā ca jyotiṣṭomādiṣvadhikāro draṣṭavyaḥ</q> । yadā rathakāra
<pb n="088"/> 
ādhāne'dhikārī tadā agnimān jātaḥ agnimattā ca jyotiṣṭomādiṣvapi tasyādhikāra-
mākṣipati । ākṣiptādhikāranirvāhāya vidyā prayujyata iti labdhavidyo rathakāro jyoti-
ṣṭomādi kariṣyati । kathaṃ punaḥ karmādhikāraṃ vinā ādhānādhikāro na paryavasyati ।
svarūpamātreṇāpuruṣārthatvāditi । nanu ca brahmasāmādīnāmabhāvāt kathaṃ rathakārasya
jyotiṣṭomādiṣvadhikāra ityatrāha---<q>yāni punarviśeṣavacanāni rāyovājīyaṃ
ityevamādīti tānyasya na saṃbhavanti na punaradhikāraṃ nivartayitumutsahante</q> । 
yeṣāṃ brāhmaṇādīnāṃ viśeṣavacanamasti teṣāṃ viśeṣeṇa brahmasāmādīni । yeṣāṃ tu
nāsti teṣāmaniyamaḥ na punaradhikāra eva tāvannirākṛtaḥ । niradhikāravādī adhikā-
ravādinaṃ pṛcchati---yadi tāvat ādhāne'dhikāraḥ paryeṣaṇīyaḥ tadā <q>kiṃ punarādhāna-
vidheḥ viśvajita iva kalpya evādhikāro na bhavati</q> । asyārthaḥ---yathā viśva-
jiti agnividyāsādhye tadvattayā traivarṇikānāmevādhikāro nāṅgīkriyate jāteradhikāri-
viśeṣaṇatvānupapatteḥ, tathā ādhāne'pi na jātiradhikāriviśeṣaṇībhavitumarhati iti
kalpya evādhikāro yuktaḥ tatra dravyārjaṃnavat agna‍yutpādakādhāne agna‍yarthina eva
eeśvaryalakṣaṇādhikāraḥ kimiti na bhavati niyojyatā tvatra nāstyeva niyogābhāvāditi ।
uttaramāha---<q>bhavatu na kaściddoṣaḥ</q> tathāpyadhikaraṇasya lakṣaṇasaṅgatisti । rathakārasyai-
vāgna‍yarthino'dhikārāt । evaṃ tāvat adhikāra(na)maṅgīkṛtya paramatamuktaṃ saṃprati
svamatamāha---<q>kintvatrāvadhātādīnāmiva niradhikāramevedaṃ sa prayojanatvādanu-
ṣṭhānamicchanti</q> । asyārthaḥ---nātrādhikārakalpanayā prayojanaṃ niradhikāratve'pyanu-
ṣṭhānasiddheḥ agnibhiḥ prayojanabhūtaiḥ prayojanavattvāt । agnīnāṃ ca karmārthatvāt karmabidhayai
[vidhinaiva]vānuṣṭhānaṃ prayujyate iti kimadhikārakalyanayā prayojanam ? niradhikāramevā-
dhānam । na ca lakṣaṇasaṅgatirnāsti; ādhāne kartṛtayā rathakārasyāgnivattayā jyotiṣṭo-
mādiṣvadhikārapratipādanāt kartṛtaivādhāne rathakārasyānyathā nopapadyate svarūpamātrasyā-
gnīnāmapuruṣārthatvāditi । <q>śeṣamuktam</q> ।</p>﻿
<pb n="089"/> 
<p><q>।। sthāpatiḥ ।।</q></p>
<p><q>atrāpi vidvattāpekṣayā ādhānāpekṣayā ca pūrvapakṣavādī ṣaṣṭhīsamāsa-
meva nyāyyaṃ manyate</q> । asyārthaḥ-yadā sthapatiścāsau niṣādaśceti karmadhārayo gṛhyate
tadā niṣādasyaivādhikāra ityāpadyate । yadi ṣaṣṭhīsamāsastadā niṣādavyatiriktasya ।
tatra ca niṣādasyaivādhikāro na ghaṭate, vidyāvirahādagna‍yabhāvācca । ato vidyāpekṣayā
agna‍yapekṣayā ca ṣaṣṭhīsamāsa eva yuktaḥ । <q>bhavati hi kaścit traivarṇika eva niṣā-
dānāṃ svāmī</q> । sthapatiśabdaḥ svāmivacanaḥ <q>ato</q> vidyāgna‍yanurodhāt <q>tasyaiva
traivarṇikasyādhikāraḥ । atrābhidhīyate । nāyaṃ ṣaṣṭhīsamāsaḥ । kasmāt ?
uttaraṃ-ṣaṣṭhīsamāse hi niṣādaśabdo lakṣaṇayā sthapatau vartate । karmadhāraye punaḥ
svārtha eva padadvayaṃ</q> vartate । asyārthaḥ-yaḥ śabdaḥ śrūyate sa evārthapratipattau nimittaṃ
bhavati । na ca samāse niṣādasthapatau ṣaṣṭhī śrūyate । kintu niṣādaśabda eva kevalaṃ, sa
ca śrutyā jātiviśeṣaṃ pratipādayati । na tu jātiviśeṣasaṃbandhinam । ṣaṣṭhīsamāsa-
pakṣe ca niṣādasaṃbandhinaḥ kārye'nvayo na niṣādasya । tatra niṣādaśabdenaiva niṣādasaṃbandhī
sthapatiḥ lakṣaṇayopasthāpanīyaḥ । karmadhāraye punaḥ niṣādasyaivānvayaḥ । niṣādaśabdaśca
śrutyaiva niṣādaṃ śaknoti vaditum । śrutilakṣaṇāviśaye ca śrutirnyāyyeti karmadhāraya
<q>evāyaṃ na ṣaṣṭhīsamāsaḥ</q> । idānīṃ pūrvapakṣamāviṣkaroti---<q>nanu cedamanyāyyamucyate</q>
lakṣaṇāyā vartata iti yāvatā śrutyaiva jñāyata iti bhāvaḥ । kathamanyāyyam ?
taddarśayati---<q>vāvacanaṃ hi samarthayatā bhāṣyakāreṇa vākyavṛttyorekārthatvamabhyupa-
gataṃ bhagavatā pāṇininā</q> । samāsādhikāre <quote>‘ve’</quote>ti smṛtam । samāsa eva nityaṃ
<pb n="090"/>
mābhūt vākyamapi yathā syādityevamarthaḥ । tatra yadi samāsasya vākyasya cārthabhedo
bhavet tadā arthabhedādeva samāsena vākyasya nivṛttirnāstīti kiṃ vāśabdena iti
matvā bhāṣyakāreṇa vāvacanaṃ samarthayitukāmena vākyasamāsayorekārthatvamuktam ।
tatra yadi ṣaṣṭhīsamāse ṣaṣṭhyarthavācakaśśabdo nāsti tadā vākyasamāsayorekārthatva-
meva na syāt । asti caikārthatā । ato'nyāyyamevedaṃ lakṣaṇayā vartata iti ।
rāddhāntī tu vadati---<q>kena vā'nekārthatvamuktam</q> lakṣaṇābhyupagamepi anekārthatā
nāstīti bhāvaḥ । bhāvamabuddhvā pṛcchati---<q>nanvidamuktaṃ niṣādaśabdo lakṣaṇayā
vartata iti</q> । pariharati---<q>prayojanamaṅgīkṛtyaitaducyate</q>-<quote>‘kena vā'nekārthatva-
mukta’</quote>miti yadidamasmābhirucyate tatprayogamaṅgīkṛtya । <q>etaduktaṃ bhavati ।’</quote></q> । vākye
savibhaktikasya śabdasya, samāse vibhaktirahitasya ekasminnevārthe prayogaḥ । tena
vākyasamāsayorekārthatvamucyata iti । etadevāha---<q>atra ṣaṣṭhīsamāse sthapatau</q>
niṣādasaṃbandhini <q>niṣādaśabdaḥ prayujyate । tasya ca lakṣaṇayā prayogasiddhiḥ ।</q>
idamākūtaṃ---vākyasamāsayorekārthatvameva prakāśamānaṃ bhidyate । vākye vācaka-
vṛttyā'rthapratipādakatvaṃ, samāse lakṣaṇāvṛttyeti । codayati---<q>kiṃ lakṣayati ?</q>
niṣādaśabdaḥ । uttaraṃ---ṣaṣṭhyarthaṃ lakṣayati । nanu ca yadi ṣaṣṭhyarthaṃ lakṣayati <q>evaṃ sati
vyadhikaraṇasamāsānāṃ sādhutvānvākhyānamanupapannam । vācakaniyamārthaṃ hi
bhagavato'nuśāsanaṃ pāṇineḥ pravṛttam</q> । apabhraṃśānu1vācakaśabdayoḥ pravṛttayoḥ vāca-
kāneva niyamayituṃ bhagavataḥ pāṇineḥ śabdānuśāsanaṃ pravṛttam । <q>lakṣaṇāpakṣe ca nāyaṃ
vācakaḥ</q> tataścāvācakatvādanuśāsanaṃ na yujyate । anuśāsti cācāryaḥ । tenāva-
gacchāmo vācaka eva samāso'pīti । lakṣaṇāvṛttipakṣe ca vāvacanānarthakyaṃ prakāra-
<note>1. anuvācakāpabhraṃśayoḥ---mā</note>﻿
<pb n="091"/>
bhedenaiva vākyasamāsayoḥ prayogopapatteḥ । tena vāvacanasyārthavattvāt vācakatvamevā-
śrayaṇīyamiti । tadāha---<q>ata eva ca kātyāyano'pi vāvacanānarthakyamukta-
vāniti । tasmādvak‍tavyo viśeṣaḥ</q> samāsasyāpabhraṃśāt gāvyādeḥ yena [a]vāca-
katvepi samāso'nuśiṣyate na gāvyādayaḥ śabdā iti । na cāsti viśeṣaḥ anyo
vācakatvādṛte iti । rāddhāntī vadati---<q>nanu cāyameva viśeṣaḥ lakṣaṇayāpi
vyavahāro loke dṛśyate gaṅgāyāṃ ghoṣaḥ prativasati kūpena gargakūlamiti</q> ।
asyārthaḥ-yeṣāṃ loke prayogaḥ tadanuśāsanaṃ vyākaraṇam । lakṣaṇayāpi ca loke
vyavahāro'sti । tena lakṣaṇayā vṛttasyāpi anuśāsanaṃ [na]virudhyate । gāvyādayastu
loke na prayujyanta iti prayogāprayogāveva viśeṣaḥ । tenānuśāsanama[na]nuśāsanaṃ
ceti । atra pūrvapakṣī---<q>nāyaṃ prayogo'nuśāsanavirodhī</q> । asyārthaḥ-vācanikā-
nāmevānvākhyānāya yat pravṛttamanuśāsanaṃ tadayaṃ gaṅgāyāṃ ghoṣa ityādiprayogo na
ruṇaddhi । yadi hyayaṃ prayogo lakṣaṇayā vṛttasyāpyanuśāsanamāpādayet tato vācanikānā-
mevānuśāsanamiti viruddha‍yeta । asmin prayoge lakṣaṇāvṛttasyānuśāsanāpattiḥ । kutaḥ ?
<q>padāvadhikaṃ hi bhagavato'nuśāsanam</q> । tathāpi kimityāha---<q>bhavati ceha
nimittāvasthāyāṃ vācakamevedam</q> । asyārthaḥ-yasyā nimittāvasthā tasyāṃ nimittārthasya
vācakapadaṃ bhavati gaṅgāyāmityādipadam । etaduktaṃ bhavati - gaṅgāyāṃ s‍nātītyādau
yatredameva vadanti tatra nimittaṃ bhavatyeva vācakamidamiti vācakasyaivānuśāsanamiti
nānuśāsanavirodhaḥ । nanu ca lakṣaṇāpekṣamevānuśāsanamayaṃ prayoga āpādayati । lakṣaṇā-
vṛttādeva gaṅgāśabdādvibhaktyanuśāsanāt iti atrāha---<q>na ca vācakasaṃbandhinya eva
vibhaktayaḥ iti smarati, prātipadikāditi vacanāt</q> । vibhaktiḥ vācikaivānuśiṣṭā
prātipadikaṃ tu vācakavṛttyā vartatāṃ lakṣaṇayā vā vartatāmiti nātrāpekṣāsti । rāddhāntī
vadati---<q>asadidamuktaṃ na</q> vācakasaṃbandhinya eveti yasmāt <q>samarthaḥ padavidhiriti
<pb n="092"/>
smaran samarthāt prātipadikāt vibhaktayo bhavantītyapi smarati । kiñcānyat
sāmarthyamuktvā[rthyaṃ muktvā]svārthasaṃbandhaṃ</q> na ca lakṣaṇāmantareṇa gaṅgāpadārthasya
saptamyarthasya ca ghoṣaprativāsaviṣayiṇaḥ saṃbandho'sti । <q>tasmāt</q> lakṣaṇāvṛttyapekṣatvena vinā
<q>nānuśāsanaprasiddhiḥ</q> । ato lakṣaṇāvṛttasyāpyanuśāsanamiti । na <q>cāyamācāryasya
niyamaḥ padāvadhikamevānuśāsanamiti । vākyāvadhikamapi dṛśyate । <quote>“deva-
sumnayoryajuṣi kāṭhake”</quote> <quote>“janitā mantra”</quote> iti ca darśanāt</q> । vācakāvadhike
cānuśāsane gaḍgāyāṃ ghoṣa iti lākṣaṇikasyānuśāsanaṃ na sthāt । na ca vācakamevānu-
śiṣyate । tasmāt prayogamātrānuśāsanaṃ vyākaraṇamiti mantavyam । tenānuśāsanabalena
tāvadvācakatā na śakyate vak‍tum । <q>ato'tra</q> lakṣaṇāvṛttipakṣe <q>vaktavyo vāvacana-
samarthane hetuḥ । ayamabhidhīyate । abhidhānavyāpāramaṅgīkṛtya etadvāvacanaṃ
samarthitam nārthavyāpāraṃ</q> asyārthaḥ - lakṣaṇāyāmapi śabdo vyāpriyeta svārthamavāntara-
vyāpā[raṃ kṛtvā] । [<q>abhidhānavyāpāramaṅgīkṛtyaitadvāvacanaṃ samarthitam</q>] । etena
vācakavṛttau caśabda eva vyāpriyata ityāśritya vāvacanaṃ samarthitam । <q>nārthavyāpāra-
meva</q> । lakṣaṇām sādhutvānuśāsanena vā kasya asādhutvaśaṅkānivṛttiriti । nanu yathā
gāvyādayaḥ apabhraṃśāḥ tathā lakṣaṇāvṛttirapi gāvyādiṣvapi gośabdopalakṣitādarthaḥ
pratīyate । atrāpi lakṣitāyā eva ṣaṣṭhyā iti । tatrāha---<q>arthaścārthāntaraṃ lakṣa-
yati nābhidhāṃ</q> yadi lakṣyeta tadā apabhraṃśaḥ syāt । iha tvartha evārthāntaraṃ lakṣayati
na śabdaḥ śabdāntaram । <q>nanu ṣaṣṭhyartho lakṣyata ityuktam</q> । ataḥ ṣaṣṭhyāpi
<note>1. pā-su 7-4-38</note> <note>2. pā-su 6-4-53</note>﻿
<pb n="093"/>
lakṣyata ityuktameva । na hi ṣaṣṭhyā'nabhidhīyamānasya ṣaṣṭhyarthatā bhavati । tena...lakṣitaṃ
ṣaṣṭhyabhidhātuṃ na śak‍notītyarthaḥ । pariharati---yata eva ṣaṣṭhyartho lakṣyata ityuktaṃ
<q>ata eva suktaṃ yadi ṣaṣṭhyā'bhidhānaṃ lakṣyata ityuktaṃ syāt syāda‍doṣaḥ</q> ।
alakṣitāyāmapi ṣaṣṭhyāṃ .... .... .... .... .... ṣaṣṭhyarthaṃ ityucyate । ato'nyat
ṣaṣṭhyarthatvena darśanāditi bhāvaḥ । nanu ca lakṣaṇāpakṣe <quote>“tadbha‍ūtānāṃ kriyārthatvena samāmnāyaḥ”</quote>
iti virudhyate yathā yāni hi padāni yadarthapratipādakatayā lokaprasiddhāni tathābhūtānyeva
vākyārthaṃ pratipādayantītyuktam । tat tyaktaṃ syāt gaṅgādipadānāṃ kūlārthe prayogā-
bhāvāt ityatrāha---<q>kvaciccābhidhānaṃ nimittaṃ kvaciccābhihito'rtha</q> iti <q>tadbha‍ūtānā-
mityabhyupagamo na viruddha‍yate</q> ।</p>
<p>lakṣaṇāyāmapi prasiddhamevārthamabhidadhadeva padaṃ vākyārthamavagamayati । ayaṃ tu
viśeṣaḥ---kvacitsvena rūpeṇābhidhānaṃ kvacittenaivābhihito'rtha iti nābhyupagamavirodhaḥ ।
nanu yadi loke ṣaṣṭhyartho lākṣaṇikaḥ kathaṃ tarhi bhagavān ṣaṣṭhīprasaṅge hi lopānuśāsanāt
lopasya ṣaṣṭhyāśca samānārthatā syādeveti atrāha---<q>na hi bhagavato'nuśāsana-
virodhaḥ prayogānuśāsanaṃ hi vyākaraṇam । k‍vacidabhidhānena nirūpyate
k‍vacidekārthatayeti na kaścida‍doṣaḥ</q> । k‍vacidabhidhānavṛttyā prayogaḥ k‍vacillakṣaṇā-
vṛttyā prayogaḥ vyākaraṇe'nuśiṣṭaḥ । tenāyamarthaḥ---vākyasthāne'pi samāsaḥ prayoktavyaḥ ।
ekārthā ca lakṣaṇāvṛttirabhipretā abhidhānena sahaikaprayojanatvāt । yata evobhayathāpi
prayogaḥ <q>ata eva bhāṣyakāraḥ asmadāyatte prayoge kimityavācakaṃ prayokṣyāmahe</q>
iti । na hi aprasaktau avācakaprayogasya etadupapadyate tasmādavācakasyāpyasti prayoga-
siddhiḥ । yadyubhayorapi prayogaprasaktiḥ tarhi ko viśeṣo vācakāvācakaprayogayoḥ ?
<q>anenābhiprāyeṇa</q> pṛcchati---<q>ko'bhiprāyaḥ</q> ? uttaraṃ---<q>ayamabhiprāyaḥ---nānabhi-﻿
<pb n="094"/>
<q>dhānanimittatā yuktā prayok‍tumiti</q> । avācakaprayoge hi abhihito'rtho nimitta-
miti anabhidhānanimittatā na yuktā āśrayitum sākṣatsaṃbhave paramparāśrayaṇānupapatteḥ ।
nanvevaṃ vede'pi prāpnoti ityāha---<q>kaḥkhalvatra viśeṣaṃ paśyati</q> ? uttaraṃ---<q>imaṃ paśyati</q> ।
<q>ekārthanimitte hi kārye kāryasyānāditā</q> । kāryaśabdena prayoga ucyate ।
