tenāyamarthaḥ---vede prayoganimitta eva prayogaḥ tatra prayogasyānāditā । tenātra
vācako'vācako vā prayok‍tuṃ kiṃ kriyatām । tathaiva prayoktavyam । <q>asmadāyatte
punaḥkārye</q> śabdayoge <q>kimanyadabhidhānādṛte bhaviturhati</q> । adhikaraṇārthamupa-
saṃharati---<q>atassūktaṃ niṣāda eva sthapatiriti evamabhidhānanimittataiva
bhavatītyabhiprāyaḥ</q> । ṣaṣṭhīsamāsāśrayaṇe tu abhihitārthatimittatā । sāca na yuktā
prathamopanipātyabhidhānanimittatāparityāgena jaghanyārthanimittatānupapatteriti ।</p>
<p>iti ṛjuvimalāyāṃ</p>

<pb n="095"/>
<p>ṛjuvimalāyāṃ</p>
<p><q>ṣaṣṭhādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ</q></p>
<p><q>puruṣārthaika</q> । pūrvapakṣavyaktyasaṃbhavena saṃśayamākṣipati---<q>nanu ca svargakāmādhi-
karaṇa idamuktam</q>---<q>naiveyamādhikārikī saṅkhyā, kiṃ tarhi ? kartṛsaṅkhyai-
veyam bhāvāntarānupādānāt iti । evaṃ ca kathaṃ pariṣado'rthinyā adhikāra
iti saṃśayaḥ ।</q> asyārthaḥ - yadya dhikārikī saṅkhyā syāt tadā adhikāra eva
bahutve sati pariṣado'rthinyā adhikāraḥ syāt naiveyamādhikārikā saṅkhyā । <q>kiṃ
tarhi ? kartṛsaṅkhyaiveyamiti</q> svargakāmādhikaraṇe darśitam । kutaḥ punariyamādhi-
kārikī saṅkhyā na bhavati <q>bhāvāntarānupādānāt</q> । yāga eva kevalo bhāvānta
upāttaḥ । tadapekṣeyamākhyātagatā saṅkhyā । na ca yāge puruṣasya niyojyatvaṃ, kiṃ
tarhi ? kartṛtvam । tena kartṛtve saṅkhyaiveyaṃ na niyojyasaṅkhyā । yaśca niyojyassa
evādhikārī iti । adhikāriṇo'pi neyaṃ saṅkhyā tena saṃśaya evāyamanupapannaḥ ।
ucyate । <q>uparitane'dhikaraṇe ākhyātagatasaṅkhyā vivakṣitā sthāsyati ।
sthitāyāṃ ca kartṛsaṅkhyāvivakṣāyāṃ kiṃ yathākartṛtvamadhikāro bhavati ।
utānyathaiva kartṛtvamanyathācādhikāra iti</q> । etadeva vivṛṇoti---<q>na kartṛgatā
saṅkhyā adhikārepi itaretarayogamāpādayituṃ kṣametyarthaḥ । tatra pūrvapakṣa-
vādino'bhiprāyaḥ</q> । adhikārasya <q>kāmanāyogāt kartṛtvamukhena cādhi-
<note>1. 1387</note>﻿
<pb n="096"/>
kārāvāpteḥ 1adhikāra[śca bhāgena] itaravyāpta‍yā ca niyamyate । kāmitayā
cādhikāra iti pariṣado'rthinyā adhikāra ityuktam</q> । asyārthaḥ - yo'yamṛddhi-
kāmādhikārastasya kāmanāyogāt kāmanāsaṃbandhāt kāmanāhetutvāditi yāvat । yaśca
kāmanāhetuḥ so'dhikāraḥ । tatra kāmasya siddhiḥ avikārārthā । tasya prāptiḥ
karturmukhena kartuḥ phalaprāptirityarthaḥ । kartṛtve vā itaretarayoge phalamapi itaretarayuktā-
nām yathābhūtā phalāvāptiḥ tathābhūtaiva kāmanāpyāśrayaṇīyā । tena bhāgaśaḥ kāmanayā
pariṣadaḥ ṛddhikāmanā adhikāriviśeṣaṇam । yathābhūtā kāmanā tathābhūta evādhikāra
iti pariṣado'rthinyā adhikāra iti । <q>atrābhidhīyate । na kartṛtvaṃ karmaprāptiṃ
niyantuṃ śak‍noti । yathābhidhānamāptimavagacchāmo na punaryathāpadārthāntara-
saṃbandham</q> । yādṛśamabhidhānaṃ svargakāmādikaṃ tādṛśaṃ,[na]punaḥ svargakāmādipadāt
svargaikadeśakāmanā gamyate । kintu kṛtsnakāmanā । tena kṛtsna eva svargaḥ sarveṣāṃ
bhavati । na punaḥ padārthāntarabhūtakartranusāreṇa phalāvāptirvarṇanīyā । kutaḥ? <q>svargakāma-

na kartṛtvamapi atra nirapekṣatāṃ vihanti kartṝṇāṃ hyatra bahutvamavagamyate na
bahūnāṃ kartṛtvam । kimato yadyevaṃ</q> ? <q>etadato bhavati । kartāro bahavaḥ na
<pb n="097"/>
<q>bahavaḥ kartā</q> । adhiṣṭhānamātrabheda eva kartṛtvaṃ tu na bhidyata ityevaṃ na bhavati kiṃ
tarhi sahādhiṣṭhānena kartṛtvameva bhidyata ityarthaḥ । tena kārts‍nyenaikaikasya kartṛtvāt
ekaikasya kṛts‍naṃ phalamiti । yathā kartradhikāre'pi phalāvāptau na pariṣado'dhikāraḥ kiṃ

ścātra karteti । yuktiṃ cāha---<q>ekaikasya svātantryavivakṣāyāṃ</q> kartṛtvavivakṣāyāṃ
<q>ākhyāte saṅkhyāyogāt</q> saṅkhyāvācitvāt । kiñca yadyatraika eva kartā syāt tadā
ekavacanameva syāt na bahuvacanam tena bahavaḥ kartāraḥ । tathā'paramapi bhāṣyakāreṇoktam-
<q>śak‍notyekaikasya svātantryavivakṣāyāṃ---iti</q> । tato'pi gamyate ekaikaḥ karteti ।
ekaikasya svātantryavivakṣāyāṃ ākhyāte saṅkhyāyogāditi yaduktaṃ tadupapādayitumāha---
<q>nyāyyā ceyamavagatiḥ</q> kartāro bahava iti । yasmācchabdāt <q>vibhaktayo bhavanti</q>
tadarthasya saṅkhyāyogāditi yaduktaṃ tadupapādayituṃ <q>avagamayantīti</q> ।। utsargastā-
vadayam । <q>nacākhyātārthaḥ saṅkhyāṃ bhajate । asattvabhūtattvāt atastadākṣiptāni
vyāvṛttānyeva kārakāṇi saṅkhyāṃ bhajante tadavasthānāmevākhyātārthenākṣepāt
na kārakaśabdābhidheyāni</q> kārakāṇāṃ dravyāṇāṃ ye śabdāḥ tadabhidheyāni dravyamātrāṇi
na saṅkhyāṃ bhajante ityarthaḥ । <q>nāmavibhaktayaḥpunaḥ saṅkhyābhājaḥ prātipadikārthā
<pb n="098"/>
<q>eveti tadgatāmeva</q> prātipadikārthagatāmeva <q>saṅkhyāmabhinirvartayanti । ata evāgnī-
ṣomau devatā, devatātvaṃ hi kārakāvasthā, tasyāmavasthāyāmagnīṣomaprātipadi-
kādutpannā dvivacanavibhaktiḥ na saṅkhyāmāha kintu prātipadikāvasthāmātrāyā-
miti । ata evādhiṣṭhānamātrasya dvitvaṃ, devatātve punarekatvamiti</q> eta-
ddarśitam---satyaṃ hi vai devateti vadatā । nanu karmaśabdādapi vibhaktirbhavantī karmasaṅkhyā-
māha na kārakasaṅkhyāmityāśaṅkāmapākareti-<q>utpattau ceyaṃ saṅkhyā । ataḥ kārakagataiva
mantavyā । kimidamutpattāviti</q> ? ākhyātagateyaṃ saṅkhyā nopapadagatetyarthaḥ ।
tathāpi kimityāha---upapada<q>gatā hi karmagatāpi pratīyate sattvavadabhidhānāt
tisra āhutīrjuhotītivat</q> । ākhyātagatā tu asattvabhūtatvāt ākhyātārthasya
tadgatā saṃbhavantī tadākṣiptakārakagatā bhavati । evamapi samabhivyāhāro na dūrānta-
ritaḥ syāditi bhāvaḥ । <q>tasmādekaikasya svātantryamavagamyate svatantraḥ
karteti ca smaraṇāt</q> । tasmādekaikasya kartṛtvamiti । nanu bahutvaśravaṇāt sāpe-
kṣāṇāṃ kartṛtvamavagamyata ityatrāha---<q>bahutvaṃ punaḥ 1kartuḥ sāpekṣatāmāpādayati
na sāpekṣasya kartṛtvam । ataḥ kartrantaraṃ sāhityasaṃpattyarthamupādīyate ।
na kartṛtvasaṃpattyarthamanyopādānam</q> । yadyākhyātena sahasaṅkhyā na saṃbadhyate
<note>1. kartṛsāpekṣatāṃ</note>﻿
<pb n="099"/>
kintu tadākṣiptena kartrā <q>kathaṃ tarhi yugapadabhidhānaṃ ? kathaṃ ca ekaśeṣaḥ ?</q>
ye hi ekaśeṣeṇa yugapadabhidhīyante teṣāmeva vibhaktibhiḥ saṅkhyocyata iti
bhāvaḥ । pariharati---<q>mābhūt yugapadabhidhānaṃ yugapadākṣepo bhaviṣyati</q> tathāpi
yugapadavagamasiddheḥ । <q>ekaśeṣastu yadyabhidhānādṛte na saṃbhavati</q> śabdaviṣayatvaṃ

<q>na pariṣado'rthinyā adhikāra iti siddham</q> ।</p>
<p><q>।। prayoge ।।</q></p>
<p>atra bhāṣyaṃ---<quote>“nanu tṛtīye uktaṃ śāstraphalaṃ prayoktari”</quote> ityādi । tadākṣi-
pati---<q>kimidaṃ śās‍traphalaṃ prayoktarīti kastenāsya virodhaḥ ? kathaṃ vā
tenedaṃ labhyate</q> yadi hi tenāsya virodho bhavet punaruktatā vā tadā yujyeta <quote>‘nanu
ca tṛtīye uktamiti’</quote>। na caitad‌dvayamapyasti iti । samādhatte---<q>yadā prayok‍tṛtvaṃ
karmaṇi śabdārthaḥ tadā bacanasya vivakṣā prāp‍noti । vivakṣite vacane aviva-
kṣitābhidhānaṃ viruddham</q> । asyārthaḥ---śāstraphalaṃ prayoktarīti prayok‍tṛtvaṃ karmaṇi
śabdevocyata ityuktam । prayok‍tṛtve sati tasyopādeyatvāt saṅkhyāyā apekṣitatvena
vivakṣā prāpnoti । tataścāniyatasaṅkhyānāṃ yāgāśaṅkā virudhyata iti virodhāmi-
prāyeṇākṣepaḥ । yata eva virodhābhiprāyeṇākṣepaḥ atassamādhānakāle idamuktaṃ <quote>“tadevā-
kṣipyata”</quote> iti । <q>kathaṃ punarākṣepaḥ ? niyojyasya hi karmaṇi <quote>‘idamasya’</quote>﻿
<pb n="100"/>
ityevaṃ saṃbandho'vagamyate asyātreti vā</q> । niyojyasya karmaṇyaiśvaryamityadhikāra-
lakṣaṇasambandho'pi niyojyasyaiva nānyasya । yaśca niyojyassa evādhikārī sa eva
karteti । <q>ato yathāniyuktasyaiva saṅkhyāsaṃbandha iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</q> ।1 niyojyatve
saṅkhyā vivakṣitetyāha---<q>kāmimātratayā ca niyogaḥ na saṅkhyāpekṣa ityu-
ktam</q> । nanu svargakāma ityekavacanaśravaṇāt saṅkhyāyuktasyaivādhikāra iti atrāha---
<q>svargakāme ca vibhaktivacanaṃ bhāvārthānapekṣamityuktam</q> tadanukāritvāt svargakāmo
yajeta ṛddhikāmā yajeranniti śravaṇāt । nanu bhavatu saṅkhyāśūnyo niyoga iti
tathāpi kartā kimiti eko na bhavatītyatrāha---<q>niyojyasya bhāvārthasaṃbandhaḥ
kartṛtvamityetaduktaṃ na bhāvasaṃbandhasya niyoga ityarthaḥ । tasmānna bhāvagatā
saṅkhyā vibakṣāmarhati adhikārapadagateva</q> । yadi hi adhikārapadagatā vivakṣyeta
tadā liṅgamapi vivakṣitaṃ syāt iti striyā adhikāro na syāt । <q>kiñca phalasya
puruṣārthatāparyantaṃ caitadvākyamityuk‍taṃ</q> tṛtīye । <q>tatparatve ca vākyasya
kriyākārakasaṃbandho natarāṃ vivakṣyeta । nanu kriyākārakasaṃbandho'pya-
trāvagamyate । sa kathaṃ tyajyate</q> । yathā phalapuruṣārthasaṃbandho'vagamyate tathā
kriyākārakasaṃbandho'pi avagamyamāno'sau kathamiva tyajyata iti । uttaraṃ---<q>anya-
<note>1. mātṛkāyāṃ bhavannityadhikam ।</note>﻿
<pb n="101"/>
<q>paratvādbākyasya</q> । bhavatvanyaparaṃ vākyaṃ tathāpi kimityāha---<q>ekārthaṃ caikaṃ vākya-
mityuktam । ato viṣaṃ bhakṣayediti ca na vivakṣyate</q> । asyārthaḥ-vyutpattyabhi-
prāyeṇa śabdārthapratītiḥ । vṛddhavyavahāre'pi vyutpattiḥ । tatraikaṃ vākyamekamevārthamava-
gamayatīti vyutpattiḥ । tena arthāntaraparatve arthāntaraṃ na pratīyate vyutpattivirahāt
iti । ato na vivakṣitetyucyate । pratipattibhramastu sāmānyato dṛṣṭanibandhanaḥ syāt ।
yathākāmī prayoge syāditi । yadācaikaṃ vākyametadarthadvayaṃ pratipādayituṃ na śaknoti ।
<q>evaṃ ca iṣvasanadṛṣṭānta upapan‍no bhavati । liṅgamuktam । atrābhidhīyate ।
na karma vā saṅkhyāpyavivakṣitā śakyate vak‍tum</q> । yathā karma avivakṣitamiti
na śakyate vak‍tuṃ na tathā saṅkhyāpītyarthaḥ । <q>kutaḥ ? viśiṣṭa eva hi karmaṇyadhi-
kāro bhavati yathā dravyaviśiṣṭakarmaṇyadhikārāvagamāt na dravyāntareṇa kriyate
tathā kartṛsaṅkhyāviśiṣṭe karmaṇyapyadhikārāvagame na saṅkhyāntaramāśrīyate</q>
viśiṣṭaṃ yatkārakaṃ kartrākhyaṃ tasyā yā saṅkhyā tayā viśiṃṣṭa caitatkarma tena tadviśiṣṭatā-
saṃpattaye saṅkhyā ādaraṇīyetyarthaḥ । nanu ca bhavatu viśiṣṭaṃ karma tathāpi vākyaṃ
tatparaṃ na bhavati ityatrāha---<q>na ca svargaḥpuruṣasyetyevaṃparaṃ tadvākyaṃ kiṃ tarhi
asmin karmaṇi asyādhikāra iti</q> । bhavatvevaṃ tathāpi kimityatrāha---<q>adhi-
kāraścāyaṃ</q> vidhyarthaścāyaṃ <q>viśiṣṭakriyākārakasvārthaphalaprayuktaḥ pratīyate iti
sarvamanavadyam</q> । ekakartṛkakriyārtho yuktaḥ svārthaḥ phalasāghako vidhyarthaḥ pratīyata
ityarthaḥ । nanvevamapi adhikāriṇaḥ phalaṃ na prayok‍tuḥ ityatrāha---<q>evaṃ ca sati
prayok‍tuḥ phalamityetadapi siddham । adhikāryeva hi prayoktā</q> । tenādhi-
<note>1. vagamotmā - mā</note>﻿
<pb n="102"/>
kāriṇaḥ phalamucyamānaṃ prayok‍turbhavati । anyasyāprayok‍tṛtvāt । yadi niyogaparamidaṃ
vākyaṃ kathaṃ tarhi karmādīnāṃ tārtīyo viniyogaḥ ityatrāha---<q>karmādīnāṃ tārtīyo
viniyoga etasmādeva</q> niyogādeva । yadi niyogādeva phalasya puruṣārthatā
'vagamyate tadā <q>yatpunaridamuktaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa ātmanaḥparasya vā svargaṃ kāmayataḥ
svagarkāmapadābhidhānamaviśiṣṭam । ātmanepadācca liṅgācca</q> । śabdai(da)stu
śabdārthe niyojyasyaiva phalāvāptiruktā । <q>ādhāne ātmanepadakartṛkopanyāsācca
aṅgaphalānāmapi pradhānakartṛsaṃyoga uktaḥ । kimanenoktam</q> ? uttaramāha---
<q>sarvaviśeṣaṇaviśiṣṭaniyogāt sarvamidaṃ labhyate yadātmanepadaṃ kartṛgāmitāmava-
gamayati phalasya yacca svargakāmapadamātmasaṃbandhini kāme kāmitāmabhidhatta
iti</q> liṅgasthānīyamidamuktamiti bhāvaḥ । <q>pāṇinirapyayameva prayogo liṅgābhidhāne</q>
ātmanepadaliṅgābhidhāne <q>nimittaṃ yadevaṃ smarati yajate yajamāna iti bhavati
yajanti yājakāḥ</q> asminneva prayoge niyogasāmarthyena svārthatāṃ phalasya jñātvā svārthe
phalamātmanepadaṃ bhavatīti smaraṇaṃ anyathā nirmūlaṃ syāt । upasaṃharati---<q>ato yathā-
nimittamevā</q>tmanepadādi nimittānatikrameṇaiva <q>niyogādapyavagatirbhavatīti</q> liṅga-
tvena <q>nimittopanyāso bhāṣyakārasya</q> । adhikaraṇārthamupasaṃharati---<q>ato
vivakṣitā saṅkhyeti sūk‍tam pratipadvidhānaṃ tu prakṛtāvasaṃbhavāt utkṛṣyate
vākyāditi tṛtīye uktam</q> ।</p>﻿
<pb n="103"/>
।। prakramāttu ।।
<p><q>kathaṃ punaratra saṃśayaḥ ? katha vā na saṃśayaḥ ? phalaparyantaḥ kāmādhikāra
ityuk‍tam</q> । tatra yadi kāraṇāntareṇa <q>phalaprāptau satyāṃ nivṛttaḥ kāmaḥ</q> kathañcidvā
<q>anyato</q> doṣadarśanādeḥ <q>tadadhikāra eva nivṛtto bhavati । niradhikārasya
cānuṣṭhānaṃ na śabdāt nāpyanyato'vagacchāmaḥ । tasmādapratiṣṭhitamevemaṃ
saṃśaya paśyāmaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ-na nimittaparyantaḥ kāmādhikāraḥ kintu phalaparyanta
ityuktam । yadi nimittaparyantaḥ syāt tadā kāmanā utpannā satī nimittamiti
nivṛttāyāmapi kāmanāyāṃ prayogaḥ parisamā[pyaḥ](pta) syāt । phalaparyante tu kāmanā-
nivṛttau puruṣasya karmaṇyaiś‍varyanivṛttiriti kinnibandhanamanuṣṭhānam । ato vītāyāmapi
phalecchāyāṃ prayogaparisamāptisaṃbhāvanā'nupapanneti । <q>ucyate । idamatra saṃśayadvāram ।
kartavyatāpūrvakaṃ hi karmādīnāṃ phalapuruṣasaṃbandhamuk‍tavanto'dhikārajñāḥ</q> ।
asyārthaḥ-yo'yaṃ phalapuruṣayoḥ sambandhaḥ sa kartavyatājñānapūrvakaḥ na punaḥ phalapuruṣa-
saṃbandhajñānapūrvikā kartavyatāvagatiḥ । phalakāmasya hi puruṣasya vidhyarthaḥ kartavya-
tayā'vagamyamānaḥ kartavya eva na bhavati yadi phalasiddhirnākṣipatīti । evaṃ phala-
puruṣayoḥ sambandho'vagamyate na punaranyathā । tena phalapuruṣasaṃbandhāvagamāt prāgeva
tāvat kartavyatā'vagamyate । tathāpi kimityāha-<q>pravṛttaścet kartavyatāyāṃ kāritaḥ
śāstreṇetyavagacchāmaḥ</q> । kartavyatājñānena karmakartavyatāvagamanibandhane'nuṣṭhāne
pravṛttiḥ kartavyatāvagame jāte tanmātranibandhanatvāttadanuṣṭhānasya pravṛttaḥ puruṣaḥ śāstreṇaiva
<pb n="104"/>
pravṛttiyogyamarthaṃ jñāpayatā puruṣo'nuṣṭhānaṃ kāryate । nānyathā । tena kartavyatayā
vidhyarthaṃ bodhitavatā śāstreṇa kāritamevānuṣṭhānamiti । nanu copakramamātre bhavatu śāstrasya
vyāpāraḥ ityatrāha---<q>śāstraṃ copakramāderapavargaparyantasya svārthasyābhidhānam । ato
nāparisamāpyāvatiṣṭhate avayavaśo'navagamānniyogārthasya । nanvevaṃ tarhi
phalārthatā karmaṇo nopapadyata ityuktam</q> । iṣṭalakṣaṇaṃ hi phalam । yadā tadiṣṭaṃ na
bhavati tadā tatphalameva na bhavatīti pariharati---<q>pravṛttau tāvannimittatayā nānupapannam ।
pravṛttikāle kartavyatāvagamena prayojanam । tasyāṃ cāvasthāyāṃ satyāṃ kāmanāyāmadhikāra-
nimittatvāt upapannamanuṣṭhānam <q>pravṛttau cāparisamāptereva śāstraṃ karaṇamityuktam ।
ataḥ paramadhikārānuvṛttiḥ k‍vopayujyate</q> । nivṛtte'pyadhikāre nānuṣṭhānaṃ nivartata
ityarthaḥ । <q>tasmāt vītāyāmapi phalecchāyāṃ samāpanīyaṃ karmeti manyate । evaṃ
prāpte'bhidhīyate - satyamārambhaḥ apavargaparyantaḥ śāstrārthaḥ । satyaṃ cāvayavaśo
nāvagamyata</q> iti । <q>na punaradhikārādṛte śāstraṃ kāraṇamityavagantuṃ śakyate</q> ।
ayamabhiprāyaḥ-yasya vidhyarthaḥ kartavyaḥ tasyaḥ tatsādhake sāṅgapradhāne'dhikāraḥ । kāma-
nāyāṃ ca nivṛttāyāṃ na kāryo vidhyarthaḥ । puruṣasya kāryatayā'vabhāsipramāṇābhāvāt ।
akāryabhūte ca vidhyarthe tatsādhake'pyavikāro nivṛttaḥ । nivṛtte cādhikāre kinnibandhana-
manuṣṭhānam । <q>nanu pravṛttau nimittatayopapannamanuṣṭhānamityuktam</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>nāsādhyaṃ
nimittaṃ bhavitumarhati</q> । asyārthaḥ - yadaiva puruṣasya kāmanā vidyate tadaiva putrādikaṃ
sādhyam । sādhyaṃ ca sat tadadhikāranimittam nānyathā । tena yadyapi pravṛttidaśāyāṃ
<pb n="105"/>
kāmanāyā vidyamānatvāt sādhyatāyāṃ satyāmadhikāranimittatā putrādeḥ tathāpi vītāyāṃ
phalecchāyāṃ asādhyabhūtaṃ nādhikāranimittamiti nimittābhāvena adhikāranivṛttau
nāstyanuṣṭhānamiti । tasmādasādhyasya nimittatā nāstītyāha---<q>yathāpratipannameva hi
nimittaṃ nāpratipannaṃ sādhyanimittatayā pratīyate</q> । kāmanāviṣayasyādhikāra-
viśeṣaṇatvāt syādityuktam । <q>ataḥ pravṛttāvapi yāvannimittameva pravṛttiḥ
nimittābhāve vā uparamaḥ</q> । yāvadevādhikāranimittamasti tāvadeva satyadhikāre-
'nuṣṭhānaṃ kartavyam । tadabhāve ca nānuṣṭhānamastīti <q>nyāyavido manyante</q> । ayamatra
saṅkṣepaḥ---prārambhasamaye satyāṃ kāmanāyāṃ sādhyatayā putrādikaṃ avagamyamānaṃniyojya-
viśeṣaṇamastīti niyogaṃ tāvatpuruṣaḥ kartavyatayā'vabudhyate । tatsādhakatayā'vasāne'pi
pradhāne vikārāvagamo jātaḥ tadeva cānuṣṭhānaheturiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>notpannamātramadhikārajñānamanuṣṭhāne hetuḥ । kiṃ tarhi ? anuvartamānam । na
vītakāmasyādhikārajñānānuvṛttirastīti rāddhāntaḥ । <q>yatpunaridaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇoktam-
vedaivāsau mayaitatkartavyamiti upāyaṃ tu na vedeti</q>--- asyārthaḥ---pṛcchataścāyamāśayaḥ-
anena kila bhāṣyeṇaivamāha-svata eva puruṣaḥ phalecchayā'ṅge pravṛttaḥ iti । sa cāyamarthaḥ
ihānupayogīti । uttaraṃ---<q>ayamarthaḥ phalecchoparame tāvat śāstraṃ na pratyakṣī-
bhūtamasti</q> । asyārthaḥ - phalecchā kartavyeti vacanaṃ nāsti । yadi vacanaṃ syāt sādhye
karaṇabhāvo dhātvarthasya । asti cet akāraṇabhūte cet tadā phalecchoparame śāstrasya
pratyakṣībhūtatvāt phalecchoparama eva nopapadyate । na caivaṃ vacanamasti । <q>ato vītāyāṃ
phalecchāyāṃ avadhūtaśāstrārthāyāṃ na karaṇatā dhātvarthasyopapadyate</q> । icchābhāve
phalasyāniṣṭatvāt na sādhyārthaḥ na cādhikāra iti <q>sa eva śāstrārthābhāvo</q> bhāṣya-﻿
<pb n="106"/>
kāreṇānena darśitaḥ । <q>nanu caitat</q> bhāvārthādhikaraṇaviruddham yadidamucyate na
yāgaḥ kartavyatā codyata iti । <q>uttaraṃ-yathā na virudhyate tathā svargakāmādhi-
karaṇe darśitam । yatpunaridaṃ pakṣāntaropanyasanaṃ śiṣṭavigarhaṇāt parisamāpa-
nīyamiti tathā kimiti vigarhanta iti paricodya kimatra kāraṇāntareṇetya-
syaiva śiṣṭavigarhaṇasya samāptau kārāṇatoktā । tathā <q>mithyāsaṅkalpadoṣaśca
darśitaḥ । tadidamasamañ‍jasamiva pratibhāti । kathamasamañ‍jasam ? yadi
tāvat mithyāsaṅkalpadoṣaparihārāyaiva prakrāntaparisamāpanaṃ tarhi na śakyaḥ
śiṣṭavigarhaṇopanyāsaḥ ।</q> vināpi śiṣṭavigarhaṇayā mithyāsaṅkalpadoṣaparihārārthatvenaiva
siddheḥ । <q>atrocyate । mithyāsaṅkalpataivātra nāsti ।</q> kutaḥ ? <q>śāstrārthe hi
saṅkalpaḥ kṛtaḥ na ca vītecchasya samāpanaṃ śāstrārthaḥ ।</q> yathā śāstrārthonopapadyate
tathā darśitam । te tveva manvate । <q>vigarhayitāraḥ śiṣṭā evaṃ manyante । mithyā-
saṅkalpadoṣo'syāsti yo'yaṃ prakrāntaṃ na parisamāpayati iti matvā ca
vigarhante atastadvigarhaṇāt samāpanaṃ kartavyam ।</q> yadi mithyāsaṅkalpadoṣabudhyā
vigarhante nirmūlamidaṃ vigarhaṇaṃ paramārthato mithyāsaṅkalpadoṣābhāvāt । tenocyate
<q>kimiti nimūlamidaṃ vigarhaṇamāśrayante ।</q> iti । <q>kimatra mūlānveṣaṇena ।
idameva</q> śiṣṭavigarhaṇaṃ mahad‍duḥkham । nirmūlamapi tāvadbhavati śiṣṭavigarhaṇam । tacca
<pb n="107"/>
tathābhūtamapi । <q>duḥkhaparihārārthaṃ ca kṛtino yatnavanta iti suṣṭhūktaṃ - vigarhante
tāvacchiṣṭā iti ।</q></p>
<q>।। loke ।।</q>
<p>saṃśayamāṣyāmarthato vyācaṣṭe - yadidaṃ 2<q>sūtradhāraiḥ karma kriyate tatkiṃ
prārabdhaṃ samāpanīyaṃ uta vītāyāṃ phalecchāyāṃ tata evoparama iti ।</q> atra
bhāṣyakāraḥ śāstrīyatvaṃ vicārayati । tadākṣipati---<q>nanu śiṣṭavigarhaṇābhayāt
samāpanīya karma, na śāstrīyamiti । atastadevānusaraṇīyaṃ ki vigarhante
neti । kiṃ śāstrīyāśāstrīyatvānusaraṇeneti ।</q> asyārthaḥ---prakrāntaparisamāptau
śiṣṭavigarhaṇameva kāraṇaṃ na śāstrīyatvam atastadevānusaraṇīyam - kiṃ vigarhante
kramasādhyaparisamāpanaṃ uta neti kiṃ śāstrīyānusāreṇa । samādhatte---<q>ucyate - satyameva
yadi nirūpādhikameva tadvigarhaṇaṃ</q> bhavet tadā na śāstrīyānusāreṇa kriyeta । tena
idaṃ śāstrīyaṃ idaṃ prārabhya na parisamāpayati tasmāt mithyāsaṅkalpadoṣo'sti iti ।
evaṃ manvānāḥ <q>śāstrīyamiti kṛtvā vigarhante nāśāstrīyaṃ</q> atasta<q>d‍bhramāpanuttaye</q>
śāstrīyatvabhramāpanuttaye <q>vicāraṇīyaṃ</q> śāstrīyatvam । [a] (ya to vicāraṇīyameta-
dbhavati । tatra <q>devatāsaṃbandhāt prāyaścittavidhānena śāstrīyamiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
na hmaśāstrīyasya śāstrīyamaṅgaṃ bhavati vaiguṇyasamādhirvā । yatkhalu
<note>1. p. 1398</note>
<note>2. sūtrakāraiḥ-mā</note>﻿
<pb n="108"/>
<q>(a)śāstrīyaṃ tatra devatā aṅgaṃ sambhavati</q> śāstraikasamadhigamyatvāt devatābhāvasya ।
aśāstrīyasya yadaṅgaṃ tat anvayavyatirekasamadhigamyam । aśāstrīyasya vaiguṇyasamādhiḥ
aśāstrīya eva bhavati pramāṇāntarasamadhigamyatvāt । tena śāstrīyatvamavagamyate ।
śāstrīyaṃ cet tadā prakrāntāparisamāpane sambhāvyata eva śiṣṭavigarhaṇeti tannivṛttaye
samāpanīyameva gṛhādi ārabdhamiti ।</p>
<p><q>atrocyate । na śāstrīyamiti pramāṇamasti ramaṇīyārthatvāt praya-
tnasya ।</q> ato'nvayavyatirekamūlānyeva kṛts‍nāni sasūtrāṇi na vedamūlāni । <q>yadapi
cedaṃ smaranti sūtrakārāḥ brāhmaṇasyedaṃ gṛhādi rājña idamiti, yathācodi-
tasyānyathākaraṇe maraṇādipratyavāyaṃ smaranti tadapyanvayavyatirekamūlaṃ vaidya-
kādivat । yatpunaḥ prāyaścittaṃ devatāvidhānaṃ ca puruṣārthatvāt na gṛhādi-
karmārthamiti parihṛtam ।</q> asyārthaḥ---śāstramūlamevedaṃ prāyaścittādi tathāpi na
śāstrīyaṃ gṛhādyaṅgatvenāśravaṇāt prāyaścittādeḥ । kimarthaṃ tarhi smaraṇaṃ ? puruṣārtho['to]
na deṣa iti ।।</p>
<p>।। pratiṣedhe ।।</p>
<p><q>kimidaṃ niyogavyāpāracintanam kiṃ nañartho vidhīyate uta dhātvarthaḥ
tadviśiṣṭa iti । dvaitīyaniyogacintanamidam ।</q> kiṃ nañartho viṣayaḥ atha
<note>1. karmārambhaṇārthaṃ</note>
<note>2. 1399</note>﻿
<pb n="109"/>
nañarthaviśiṣṭo dhātvartha iti । bhavatu viniyogacintanaṃ ko doṣaḥ ? ākṣeptā āha---
<q>na khalu kaściddoṣaḥ pūrvottarapakṣayoḥ kintvasaṃbandho'dhikāralakṣaṇe ।</q> dvitīya-
cintārūpatvāt । samādhatte - <q>evaṃ tarhi adhikāracintaiveyam । kathamadhikāra-
cintā ? ittham । yadyatra nañartho vidhīyate tato bhakṣayatiḥ adhikāri-
viśeṣaṇam ato nañarthaviśiṣṭakarmavidhiḥ । tataḥ kalpyamadhikāri-
viśeṣaṇaṃ viś‍vajita iva । tatsiddha‍yarthaṃ cedaṃ balābalacintanamupanyastam ।</q>
nañarthe vā audāsīnyātmake vidhiviṣaye prakārāntareṇa sambandhamalabhamāno balāt
bhakṣayatiḥ adhikāriviśeṣaṇam । yadā tu karmāntaravidhiḥ tadā viśvajinna‍yāyena
kalpyamadhikāriviśeṣaṇam adhikāriviśeṣābhidhāyakatvāt asti lakṣaṇe saṅgatiḥ ।
<q>pūrvapakṣavādī bhāvārthāḥ karmaśabdāḥ ityutsargaṃ manvānaḥ viśiṣṭavidhiṃ manyata
iti ।</q> <quote>‘bhāvārthāḥ karma śabdā’</quote> ityatrādhikaraṇe bhāvārthānāṃ vidhiviṣayatvamuktam ।
na ca nañarthaḥ audāsīnyātmako bhāvārthaḥ tena vidhiviṣayatā tasya na yuktā । nanu
abhāvārtho dadhyādi <quote>‘dadh‍nā juhoti’</quote> iti vidhiviṣayaḥ ityāśaṅkyāha-<q>tadāśrita-
tvāccopapadavidheriti ।</q> bhāvārthāśrita evopapadapadārtho vidhīyate । <q>etaduktaṃ
bhavati ।</q> bhāvārtha eva tadanurakto vidhīyate prāptāprāptavivekena tu upapadavidhiḥ iti ।
tasmāt bhāvārthātmako'bhakṣaṇasaṅkalpa eva lakṣaṇayā vidhīyata iti yuktam ।</p>
<p><q>kiñca nañarthavidhāne'nuṣṭhānamāpadyate ।</q> yadi hi nañartho vidhīyate
tadā prasajyamānaṃ bhakṣaṇamevādhikāriviśeṣaṇamiti anuṣṭhānamāpadyate । <q>kathaṃ ? prati-
ṣiddhamapi hi yanna puruṣasyopakaroti abhyudayena duḥkhaparihāreṇa ca na tatra</q>﻿
<pb n="110"/>
<q>buddhipūrvakāriṇaḥ pravartanta iti laukikāḥ । tasmādayameva śāstrārthaḥ śreyān ।</q>
pravṛttyānu[rūpyāt] yadi phalamantareṇa pravṛttirnāsti tadā nañarthavidhipakṣe'pi tarhi
phalaṃ kalpyamityāha---<q>nanu ca nañarthavidhāne'pi pratyavāyakalpanā bhavatu kiṃ</q>
nañarthādeva pratyavāyaḥ uta niṣidhyamānāyāṃ kriyāyām iti vikalpya dṛṣayati---<q>kathaṃ
nañarthavidhau pratyavāyaḥ śakyate kalpayituṃ</q> nañarthādeva pratyavāyakalpanena
<q>natarāmanuṣṭhānaṃ prāp‍noti</q> pratyavāyahetorananuṣṭhāpakatvāt । <q>atha viṣayānuṣṭhānena</q>
bhakṣaṇānuṣṭhānena <q>pratyavāyaḥ kalpyate pratiṣedhānuṣṭhānenāsau parihṛto bhavati
lokavat iti । tadayuktam yasmānnañarthavidhistāvat nañarthe eva paryavasito
bhavati</q> na viṣayānuṣṭhānaṃ bodhayatīti । <q>viṣayānuṣṭhānaṃ tu laukikam । laukike
cānuṣṭhāne yadi na laukikāt</q> pramāṇāt <q>pratyavāyo'vagamyate kutaḥ anyataḥ
śakyate'vagantum ।</q> viṣayanibandhanapratyavāyakalpanāṃ vināpi vidheranubandhadvayāva-
gamāt na śakyate kalpayituṃ pratyavāyaḥ kāmapravṛttiḥ syāditi <q>tasmānnaivānyathā
puruṣārthatā upapadyate ityabhakṣavidhiḥ syāt ।</q> tasmin pakṣe viśvajita iti svarga-
phalatvena karmaṇaḥ puruṣārthatopapattiḥ ।</p>
<p><q>atrābhidhīyate - satyaṃ yadāha devānāṃ priyaḥ</q> abhakṣaṇavidhipakṣe puruṣārtha-
teti । <q>kintu nāsāvabhakṣavidhiḥ pratīyate yato bhakṣayatistāvat bhakṣaṇamācaṣṭe</q>
<note>1. na ñarthe ityarthaḥ</note>﻿
<pb n="111"/>
<q>nañapi nivāraṇaṃ nivṛttimāha</q> । audāsīnyamiti yāvat <q>padadvayenāpyabhakṣaṇa-
mevāsad‍bhūtaṃ gamyate । na ca tadvidhātuṃ śakyate akriyārūpatvāt । māna-
sastu vyāpāro na padāt</q> pratīyate <q>na vākyāt</q> pratīyate । apratītasya ca
vidheyatā nopapadyate । nanu abhakṣaṇavallakṣaṇayā saṅkalpo'vagamyate ityatrāha---
<q>anīkṣaṇādiṣu vrataśabdaḥ sākṣācchrūyate</q> । ato yukta tatra vratalakṣaṇā । vrataśabdasya
saṅkalpavacanatvāt tatsāmānādhikaraṇyāt । atra tu tathā vidhaṃ na kriñcidasti । atra tu
bhakṣayatiranyena sambandhamanubhavitumaśak‍nuvan <q>galepādukayā adhikṛtaviśeṣaṇaṃ
nañarthasya vā'bhāvārthasyaudāsīnyamayuktameva vidheyatvam</q> । kasyacicchabdasyā-
virodhāt । śabdāvirodhena hi bhāvārthaḥ nāniyogaviṣayatvamuktam na dhātvarthatvādeveti
<q>nibandhanakāraḥ</q> śabdabalavādī manyate ।</p>
<p><q>nanu cānuṣṭhānaṃ nopapadyata ityuktam</q> । samādhatte-<q>kimiti nopapadyate</q> ।
ekagranthenāha---<q>kiṃ kartavyatāvagamo nāsti ?</q> asyārthaḥ---yadi hi vinā phalaṃ
kartavyatāvagamo na syāt tadā syādeva phalāmāve'[na]nuṣṭhānam । asti ca phalaṃ
vināpi kartavyatāvagamaḥ । tasmāt <q>kartavyatāvagame sati kāmādayaḥ sambadhyanta
iti darśitaṃ bhāvārthādhikaraṇe</q> । tenāsti phalaṃ vināpi kartavyatāvagamaḥ । nanu
ca svargakāmādivat bhavatvatrāpi phalāvagamaḥ ityatrāha---<q>yatra te svargakāmādayaḥ
tatraivāmyudayaparyantaḥ kartavyatāvagamaḥ । yatra punaḥ na vidyate kastatra karta-
vyatāvagamamahnupate</q> । kartavyatājñānāccānuṣṭhānaṃ na phalāvagamādityuktam ।
<pb n="112"/>
tanmūlatvāt</q> kartavyatājñānapūrvakānuṣṭhānamūlatvāt <q>phalāvagateḥ ।</q> anuṣṭhānaparyante hi
kartavyatājñāne sati svargādiḥ kāmyamāna[ma]sya phalatvena saṃbadhyate nānyathā । yata
eva kartavyanājñānamātreṇānuṣṭhānasiddhiḥ <q>ata eva jīvanāderapyadhikāriviśeṣaṇatvaṃ
siddhaṃ bhavati । evaṃ kartavyatāmavagacchannapi yo nāma na karoti svargakāma-
codanāsvapi tasyākriyāṃ ko nāma vārayituṃ kṣama iti । yopi svarṇa-
mupalabhya mṛttiketi brūyāt kastasyottaraṃ dadāti ।</q> kartavyatāmapi yo nāma
akartavyatāmāha kastasyottaraṃ dadātīti । yadi kartavyatāmātreṇānuṣṭhānaṃ <q>kimiti tarhi
bhāṣyakāraḥ</q> śiṣṭavigarhaṇamupanyasyati । vināpi śiṣṭavigarhaṇamanuṣṭhānasiddheḥ । samādhatte
---<q>ayamabhiprāyo bhāṣyakārasya-yo'pi laukikaśāstrāvagatimavidvān phalā-
bhāve na karoti tasyāpi mūḍhātmano vidyata eva laukikaṃ śiṣṭavigarhaṇaṃ
pravṛttaye । tasmānnāyamaṣahnotuṃ śakyate vākyārthaḥ---kaḻañ‍jabhakṣaṇaṃ na
kuryāditi ।</q></p>
<p><q>।। tasmiṃstu ।।</q></p>
<p>adhyāyasaṅgatisiddha‍yarthaṃ saṃśayaṃ bhāṣyakārīyaṃ vyācaṣṭe---<q>idamatra cintyate
<note>1. p 1402</note>﻿
<pb n="113"/>
kimanugamanādinā ācāragaṇena jātamātro'dhikriyate uta upanīta eva ।</q>
evadeva vivṛṇoti---<q>etaduktaṃ bhavati - kiṃ jananamevādhikāriviśeṣaṇaṃ utopanaya-
namiti । tatra pūrvapakṣavādī pranyate - svargādestāvadadhikāriviśeṣaṇatā nopapadyate
dṛṣṭārthatvādācāragaṇasyādhānasyeva ।</q> yathā''dhāne'gnyarthe svargāderadhikāriviśeṣaṇatvaṃ
nāsti tathā'sminnapyācāragaṇe dṛṣṭārthenaivātrādhikāra iti na svargakāmasyādhikāraḥ
kalpyate । <q>tasmāt sāmarthyameva adhikāriviśeṣaṇam ।</q> yadi sāmarthyamevādhi-
kāriviśeṣaṇaṃ tadā jātamātrasyāsāmarthyāt kathaṃ jātamātrasyādhikāraḥ ucyata ityāha
---<q>nanu caivaṃ sati na jātamātrasyādhikāraḥ ।</q> pariharati---<q>etaduktaṃ bhavati
nopanayanamapekṣate iti ।</q> anupanītaparo'yaṃ jātamātraśabda iti yāvat ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate upanayanottarakālamevādhikriyata iti । kā yuktiḥ?
svādhyāyādhyayanottarakālaṃ hi vaidikaiḥ padārthaiḥ adhikriyate । vaidikaśca
pāṭhagaṇa iti smṛtipāde uktam । svādhyāyādhyayanaṃ tu upanītasya ।</q> tenopa-
nayanottarakālamācāreṣvadhikāra iti anena bhāṣyārthasvarūpamuktam । akṣiyati-<q>bhavatu
svādhyāyādhyayanamupanītasya । padārthāstu yathā yasyāvagamyante upanīta-
syānupanītasya vā tasyaiva te na bhavanti yathā niṣādasthapateriṣṭiḥ ।</q> atra
codayati-<q>nanu ca tatra</q> sthapatīṣṭau <q>svādhyāyavirodhāt</q> karmadhārayavirodhāt <q>evamabhyu-
pagatam</q> niṣādasyaivādhikāra iti । iha tu ācāragaṇe <q>svādhyāyāvirodhāt adhīta-﻿
<pb n="114"/>
<q>vedānāmevādhikāro bhaviṣyati kāmivat</q> yathā kāmināmadhītavedānāmevādhikāraḥ
tathehāpi । anyathā tatrāpyanadhītavedānāmadhikāranivṛttiḥ syāt । pariharati---<q>ayukta-
midaṃ</q> adhītavedānāmevādhikāra iti pramāṇābhāvāt । yattu kāmināmivetyuktam
tatrāha---<q>tatra hi adhītavedasaṃbhave na adhyayanaprayuktau pramāṇamasti viduṣāṃ
kāmināmityuktam । iha punaramantrasādhyatvāt ācāragaṇasya naitacchakyate
vak‍tuṃ</q>---anadhītavedo nādhikriyata iti yasmānmantraprayuktiratra nāsti ityuktam । tato-
'nadhītavedasyāpi adhikāro yuktaḥ । <q>kiñca na copanītamātra evādhītavedo
bhaviṣyati ।</q> yadyadhītavedasyādhikāraḥ yadyupa/?/nītamātra evādhītavedo bhavet tata evaṃ
syāt । na caitadasti । tasmādupanītādhikāre vaidikatva/?/pradarśanaṃ śaṅa‍kyameva । atrābhi-
dhīyate---<q>ayamabhiprāyo bhāṣyakārasya । prāgupanayanādvidhayaḥ pituḥ dārviho-
mikasya vopalabhyante । upanayanaṃ cācāryasya ।</q> ayamāśayaḥ---yāvantaḥ keci-
dvidhayo vaidikāḥ te sarve upanītasya sataḥ nānupanīto'dhikārīti piturevādhikāraḥ ।
<q>dārvihomikasya vā kartu</q>kāmasya । bālakasyopanayane ācāryo'dhikārī kartā
ca । <q>taduttarakāla tu saṃskṛtaviṣayā vaudikā vidhayaḥ śrūyante । tanmūlāśca
smārtā apīti te'pi taduttarakālabhāvina eveti bhagavān bhāṣyakāro
manyate</q> sarvatra hi dṛṣṭānusāryanumataṃ vaidikāśca vidhayaḥ pratyakṣāḥ upanītaviṣayāḥ smṛtyanu-
mitā api tathaiva bhavitumarhantīti bhāvaḥ । <q>tasmātsūktaṃ upanītasyādhikāra iti ।</q>﻿
<pb n="115"/>
<p><q>।। abhyāsaḥ ।।</q></p>
<p>kathamatra pūrvapakṣamāśaṅkate ? yathā kālāṅgatvāt karmaṇo vaiguṇyamāpadyate tasmādā-
gate kāle'nuṣṭhānaṃ kartavyam tatrāha---<q>asminnadhikaraṇe sarvaśaktyadhikaraṇe sthite
bhavati saṃśayaḥ kiṃ kālaśūnyaḥ śaucaśūnyaśca prayogo hi jīvananimittatayā
kartavyaḥ uta neti ।</q> asyārthaḥ---sarvaśakta‍yadhikaraṇe idamuktaṃ adhikārabalenāṅa‍ga-
tyāgenānuṣṭhānaṃ kartavyamiti । tadihāpi jīvananimittakaḥ prayogaḥ kimadhikārabalena
uṅgabhūtakālaṃ parityajya kartavyaḥ ata neta cintā । <q>tatra pūrvavādino'bhiprāyaḥ---
nimittabalenāṅa‍gatyāgo'bhihitaḥ tasmāt yāvannimittaṃ prayogaḥ ।</q> asyārthaḥ---
jīvananimitto jīvanādhikāraḥ kālābhāve'pi jīvanaṃ nimittabhūtamasti iti tadbalenāṅa‍ga-
bhūtakālaparityāgenānuṣṭhānaṃ kartavyamiti <q><quote>‘‘juhudhi juhadhi’’</quote> ityeva hotavyamiti ।</q>
kimiti juhudhi juhudhi ityeva hotavyamiti । ābhīkṣaṇyena hotavyamityarthaḥ । tathāhi
---kriyāsamabhihāre tavyapratyayārthe juhoterloṭ‌vidhīyate tasya sthāne hiśabdādeśaḥ
sa ca loṭa ādeśaḥ । tathāca sūtraṃ---<quote>‘‘kriyāsamabhihāre loṭ loṭo hisvau vā ca
tad‍dhvamoḥ tataśca <quote>‘ābhīkṣaṇye dve bhavataḥ’</quote> iti dvirvacanam । tathā <quote>‘yathāvidhyanu-
prayogaḥ pūrvasmin’</quote> nimittatavyapratyayāntasya juhoteranuprayoga iti । <q>nanu ca āhāra-
vihārakāle na śakyate prayogaḥ kartumiti ।</q> pariharati---<q>yathā śakyate
tathā'bhyasanīyaḥ</q> yena prakāreṇāhāravihārakāle ca prayogaḥ śakyate kartuṃ sa prakāra
āstheyaḥ । nanu ca śaucādi tyaktaṃ syāt atrāha---<q>śaucamapyaṅa‍gameva ।</q> ataḥ kāla-
<note>1. p. 1403</note>﻿
<pb n="116"/>
<q>śocaparityāgenāpi prayogaḥ kartavyaḥ ।</q> rāddhāntamāha---<q>atrocyate nābhyā-
sāpekṣaṃ śāstram śaktasyāpi nimittāvagamopapatteḥ ।</q> asyārthaḥ---yathā śakyate
tathā kartavyamiti yo'yamabhyāsaḥ tadapekṣamidaṃ śāstraṃ na bhavati । sarvāṅgopasaṃhāre
śaktasyāpi nimittāvagamopapatteḥ । yadi hi sarvāṅgopasaṃhāre śaktasyādhikāre jīvanasya
nimittatāvagamo nopapadyate tadā evaṃ syāt । nacaitadasti । tasmānnāṅgabhūtaśaucakāla-
[tyāge] pramāṇamasti । nanvadhikārabalena tyajyate ityatrāha---<q>pratipanne hi nimitte-
'ṅgatyāgo'bhihitaḥ tasminnadhikaraṇe ।</q> yādṛśaṃ nimittaṃ tādṛśe pratipanne sati
aṅgatyāgaḥ sarvaśakta‍yadhikaraṇe darśitaḥ । <q>iha punaḥ nimittameva nābhyāsāpekṣaṃ
pratīyate ।</q> jīvanamātrameva nimittatayā na pratīyate । yadi hi abhyasāpekṣaṃ śāstra
evaṃ tarhi nimittaṃ pratīyeta । tadā jīvanamātrameva nimittaṃ syāt śaucānapekṣam । na caita-
dasti abhyāsābhāve'pi nimitāvagamopapatteḥ । yadi hi jīvanaśruteranadhikārāt nābhyā-
sāpekṣaṃ śāstraṃ <q>evaṃ tarhi kālaśūnyaṃ kriyatām ।</q> kālasya puruṣaviśeṣaṇatvānupapatteḥ
aṅgamātratvāt tena tattyāgenāpi bhavatyanuṣṭhānam । <q>neti brūmaḥ</q> kālaśūnyaṃ nimittaṃ naiva
pratīyate <q>nityayuktatvāt kālasya ।</q> nityasaṃbandha[āt] kāle karmaṇi śaktasyādhi-
kārāt tatkālameva jīvanaṃ nimittaṃ anyasmit kāle tadupasaṃhārasamarthatvāt । atra
codayati---<q>nanu ca sarvāṇyevāṅgāni nityayuktāni ।</q> asyārthaḥ---sādhikāri-
sannidhau niravikāritayā śravaṇāt tadarthatvenopādīyante । na ca kaścidviśeṣaḥ kālasya
nityatvenopādānaṃ itareṣāmanityatveneti । tena sarveṣāṃ nityānvaye sati kimidaṃ
nityayuktatvātkālasyeti । pariharati---<q>satyaṃ nityayuktāni na punaraṅgāntara-
tyāgena pratīyante ।</q> yasminnapi kāle tāni na santi tasminnapi kāle puruṣasya
<pb n="117"/>
tadupasaṃhārasāmarthyamastīti satyadhikāre tattyāgenāpi yuktamanuṣṭhānam । <q>kālaḥpunaḥ
kālāntaratyāgena nimittamavagamayati śaucamiva ।</q> asyārthaḥ---sarvaśakta‍yaghi-
karaṇena aṅgatyāgenāpyanuṣṭhāne gauṇāvayavatve prāpte - aṅgaśāstrāṇāmatyantabādho nāsti ।
kālasya tu punaḥ tyāge atyantabādhāpattireva syāt niravayavatvāt kālasya śaucamiva ।
yathā tasyaiva śaucaṃ aśaucaparityāgena nimittamavagamayati tathetyarthaḥ । tasmādanyathānupa-
padyamānakālānurodhena nimittatā'vasīyate । yata eva kālānurodhena nimittatā'-
vasīyate <q>tasmānna kālaśūnyanimittamavagacchāmaḥ । na cānavagamanimittaṃ
bhavitumarhati ।</q> bhāṣyamākṣipati---<q>bhāṣyakārastu kālameva nimittamāha---
"na kālo guṇaḥ nimittaṃ hyetat’’</quote> iti । taccāyuktam jīvanasya nimitta-
tvāt ।</q> nimittatve kālasya <q>kāmye prayoge kālasyopādānaṃ na syāt anaṅga-
tvāt ।</q> samarthayate-<q>tasmādayamatra bhāṣyārthaḥ---na kālo guṇo nimittamanava-
cchindannityarthaḥ ।</q> nimittamanavacchindannityetadadhyāhṛtya bhāṣyagrantho vyākhyeyaḥ ।
nimittānavacchedako guṇo na bhavati kintu nimittāvacchedako guṇa iti yāvat ।
uktanimittaṃ hyetaditi yaduktaṃ tadātmakālīnajīvananimittatvābhiprāyeṇa । na sākṣā-
nnimittatvābhiprāyeṇa । etacca tasmādāśritakālasya yāvajjīvanaṃ prayoga ityanena
bhāṣyeṇa prakaṭīkṛtam ।</p>
<p><q>।। teṣāmautpattikatvāt ।।</q></p>
<p>kathaṃ punaratra pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ? yāvatā nimittasyāvṛttau naimittikasya
<note>1. p. 1404</note>﻿
<pb n="118"/>
<q>bhavitavyamiti āgate kāle iti yuktam । evamatra pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ---kālānu-
rodhena nimittāvagatiḥ aṅgaṃ ca kālaḥ sakṛdanuṣṭhānena kṛtamaṅgaśās‍tramiti
nimittamapi tathaiva, tadanurodhitvāt ।</q> asyārthaḥ---kālastāvadaṅgam sakṛccopasaṃhāre
kṛte kṛtamaṅgaśāstramiti na punaḥ punaraṅgaśāstramāśrayaṇīyam । kālānurodhe ca pūrvādhi-
karaṇe nimittasaṅkoco'varṇi । tena sakṛdupasaṃharaṇīyāṅgabhūtakālānurodhena nimittamapi
sakṛdeva । anyathā tadanurodhitā na syāditi kriyāvat । <q>rāddhāntastu naitadyuktam-
sakṛdevānuṣṭhānaṃ kartavyamiti । utpadyamānaṃ hi karma kālasaṃyuktamevotpanna-
miti tatkālīnaṃ jīvanamavagamayatīti nimittamityuktam na punarvidheyatāmapi
nimittasyāpādayati ।</q> asyārthaḥ-yadi nimittatvamasmābhiḥ pūrvādhikaraṇe kālasyoktaṃ
tat kālasya nityayuktatvāt tadupasaṃhārasamarthasyaivādhikārāt kālāntare ca niyamena
tadupasaṃhārāsāmarthyāt balāt tatkālameva jīvanaṃ nimittamavagamayatītyanayā yuktyā ।
na punaḥ nimittasya vidheyatāmapyāpādayati । <q>avihite ca</q> tasminnimitte avidheyabhūte
cetyarthaḥ । nimittāvṛttau kālopasaṃhārasāmarthye ca sati <q>kṛtaḥ śāstrārtha iti na
śakyate vak‍tuṃ,</q> punaradhikāravṛtteḥ । <q>tasmāt tatkālīnaṃ</q> pūrṇimāntarakālīna <q>jīvanaṃ
nimittabhūtaṃ punaḥ punaḥ śās‍trārthānuṣṭhānaṃ prayuṅk‍te । āgate āgate
kāle'nuṣṭhānaṃ kartavyamiti sūktam । liṅgamuktam ।</q></p>
<note>2. p. 1404</note>﻿
<pb n="119"/>
<p><q>।। tathāntaḥ kratu ।।</q></p>
<p>nanūktaṃ nimittāvṛttau naimittikasyāvṛttiriti । tena bhedanādyāvṛttau naimittikā-
nāmapi homādīnāmāvṛttiruktaiva । <q>kena punarviśeṣeṇa vā idaṃ punaratidiśyate
asati viśeṣe[na]tulyatā bhavati</q> api tu ekataiva syāt । ayamasti viśeṣaḥ ।
<q>kratvarthatvādbhedanādinimittānāṃ homānāṃ sakṛtkṛtenaiva prayogavacanopakāra-
siddheḥ kṛto'dhikāraḥ iti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate ।</q> asyārthaḥ-yadyapyetāni naimitti-
kāni tathāpyeṣāṃ kratvaṅgatvāt kratūpakārāyānuṣṭhānam । ekaścāyaṃ kratuprayogaḥ
sakṛtkṛtenāpi cāṅgena pradhānopakāranirvṛtteḥ nivṛttāvapi na punaranuṣṭhānam prayojanā-
bhāvāt । agnihotrādīnāṃ tu na prayogavaśenānuṣṭhānaṃ, kintu nimittabaleneti yuktaṃ
paunaḥ punyam ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntastu <q>satyamevaṃ kratūpakārāyaiva anuṣṭhānaṃ tathāpi punaḥ punarbheda-
nādyutpattau punaḥ punaradhikāraṃ vārayituṃ tāvadupakāro na kṣamaḥ । nanu
bhavatu punaḥ punaradhikāraḥ tathāpi niṣprayojanatvātkimadhikāraḥ kariṣyati ?</q>
nānuṣṭhānāntaraṃ prayojayituṃ śavanotīti bhāvaḥ । pariharati---<q>na niṣprayojanatā ।
adhikārāddhi prayojanaṃ na prayojanato'dhikāra ityuktam</q> anapekṣatvasiddhaye
pramāṇalakṣaṇe । asyārthaḥ-yadā adhikāraḥ āvṛttaḥ tadā vidhānamāvṛttam । yathāvihi-
tasya ca prayojanakalpanā । tena yāvadvāraṃ nimittamāpatati tāvadvāraṃ naimittikenānuṣṭhitena
kratūpakāro niṣpadyate nānyatheti kalpyate । <q>tasmādyāvadadhikāgmatrāpi prayogaḥ
iyāṃstu viśeṣaḥ yāvatpradhānaprayogaṃ hi saḥ । tadadhikāratvādasya agni-﻿
<pb n="120"/>
hotrādibhiḥ naimittikānām ।</q> iyān viśeṣaḥ te svatantrā eva prayoktavyāḥ
bhedanādihomāstu yāvat pradhānaṃ prayujyate tāvatprayoktavyāḥ pradhānādhikṛtasyaiva bheda-
nādihomeṣvadhikārāt । pradhānābhāve'dhikārābhāvāt ।</p>
<p><q>।। ācārāt ।।</q></p>
<p>nanu svargakāmādīnāmapi adhikāriviśeṣaṇatvāt adhikārāvṛttau prayogā-
vṛttiryukteti kathaṃ pūrvapakṣa ityāśaṅka‍yāha---<q>gurvanugamanādiṣu nāgamanamadhikāri-
viśeṣaṇamiti pūrvapakṣavādī</q> nimittasyāpi gurvāgamanādeḥ adhikāriviśeṣaṇatāṃ na
manyate pūrvapakṣī । nimittenāpi vākyārthe'nvayopapatteḥ <q>gurumāgatamabhyutthānena</q>
prīṇīyāditi vidhāṃna manyate । <q>sakṛcca kṛtaṃ prīṇanamiti kṛtaḥ śās‍trārthaḥ iti ।</q>
rāddhāntamāha---<q>na hi adhikāriviśeṣaṇatvādṛte nimittatā saṃbhavatīti tadva-
dityatideśaḥ ।</q> asyārthaḥ-anuṣṭhānaṃ prati nimittabhāva eva adhikāriviśeṣaṇatvena
vinā na saṃbhavati adhikāramātranibandhanatvāt anuṣṭhānasya । tasmāt yāvat nimittaṃ
tāvat adhikāriviśeṣaṇamiti balādaṅgīkaraṇīyam । ata eva sūryasaṅkāntyādeḥ[diḥ]
puruṣasaṃbandhābhāvāt asaṃbaddhasya ca viśeṣaṇatvānupapatteḥ adhikāriviśeṣaṇatvāsaṃbhavānna
nimittam । api tu kālatayaivānvayaḥ s‍nānādīnāmiti mantavyam । tasmādāgamana-
syādhikāriviśeṣaṇatvāt āvṛttāvadhikārāvṛtteḥ punarabhyutthānaṃ kartavyamiti ।</p>
<p><q>।। brāhmaṇamya ।।</q></p>
<p><q>nanu cātra pūrvapakṣa eva nopapadyate na hi vacanamadṛṣṭvā pūrvapakṣaḥ</q>﻿
<pb n="121"/>
<q>vacanena rāddhānta iti yuktam</q> nyāyaparatvādasya śās‍trasyeti । <q>atrocyate ।
yāvajjīvanādīnāmadhikāriviśeṣaṇatvānupapatteḥ adhikāriśūnyatayā viśva-
jidādivadadhikāro'pyadhyāhāryaḥ</q> iti pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ । <q>kā
yuktiḥ ? uttaraṃ-aniṣpādyasya vastuno adhikāriviśeṣaṇabhāvo nopapadyate ?
kasmāt ? sādhyaṃ siddhaṃ vā pāralaukikatayā saṃbadhyate</q> । yāvatkiñcit vākye
sādhyaṃ siddhaṃ vā śrūyate tatsarvaṃ tāvat kriyayā saṃbadhyate । <q>tataḥ kiṃ ? idaṃ tato
bhavati-siddhaṃ niṣpādakatayā sādhyaṃ phalatayeti, jīvanaṃ siddham । tasmātsādhana-
bhāva eva yukta iti manyate</q> । sādhyasya tu phalatayā'nvitasyānyathā phalatvānupapatteḥ
adhikāriviśeṣaṇatā bhavati । tena svargāderadhikāriviśeṣaṇatā na jīvanāderiti ।
<q>rāddhāntastu-ṛṇadarśanamavaśyakartavyatāṃ sūcayati । jīvanamadhikāriviśeṣaṇa-
tayā jñāpayati</q> । anyathā'vaśyakartavyatvānupapatteḥ । <q>nanu siddhasya sādhana-
bhāvādṛte saṃbandho nopapadyate iti kimatra darśanaṃ kariṣyatīti</q> nirmūlaṃ darśana
vyāmoha iti yāvat । <q>atrocyate-uktamasmābhiḥ svargakāmādhikaraṇe na kartu-
rniyoga iti</q> । yadi kartuḥ niyogaḥ syāt tadā jīvanaṃ kartṛviśeṣaṇaṃ syāt । yadā
tu niyojyasya sataḥ adhikāriṇaḥ kartṛtvaṃ tadā'nayā niyojyaviśeṣaṇameva jīvanam ।
nanvevamapi 2kartṛviśeṣaṇatā na saṃbhavatītyanvayo na saṃbhavati ityāśaṅkyāha-<q>nayojya-
<note>1. adhikārakalpanā viśvajin‍nyāyena---mātṛkā.</note>
<note>2. kriyāyāṃ---mā.</note>﻿
<pb n="122"/>
<q>ścāyaṃ yāvacchabdādityuktam</q> svargakāmādhikaraṇa eva । kartṛviśeṣaṇatāyā anupa-
pattiśca avyavacchedakatvāt svargavat । yathā svargasya kartṛviśeṣaṇatā na saṃbhavati
ityekādaśādye nirūpitam tathā jīvanasyāpi nājīvan kaścitkaroti । yacca sādhya-
tayā'nvitasya svargasya paścānniyojyaviśeṣaṇatvamiti tadapi nopapadyata iti darśayati---
<q>niyogācca sādhyaṃ</q> svargādiṣvapi niyojyaviśeṣaṇasyaiva sato'rthātsādhyatvamiti
darśitam । <q>tasmānna sādhyatā niyoge niyojyaviśeṣaṇatve hetuḥ</q> । nanu ca
bhavatu niyojyaviśeṣaṇatā jīvanasya tathāpi kathamavaśyakartavyatetyāha---<q>niyojya-
viśeṣaṇaṃ cādhikāriviśeṣaṇamityuktam</q> niyojya evādhikārī bhavatīti ।
adhikārasyāvaśyakartavyāt anuṣṭhānamāvaśyakamiti <q>ṛṇadarśanasāmañ‍jasyaṃ cānyathā
nopapadyata iti</q> tadanusārādapi niyojyaviśeṣaṇatvameva yuktam । <q>tasmānnityānyevai-
tāni karmāṇi nimittanityatvāditi siddhaṃ</q> darśanaṃ mūlasaṃbhavānna vyāmoha ityarthaḥ ।
<q>athavā ṛṇavākye brāhmaṇaśabdaśravaṇāt brāhmaṇasyaivādhikāro</q> viśeṣaṇādadhikārā-
vagamāt <q>vidhyuddeśe brāhmaṇaśabdaśravaṇābhāvāt । asya cārthavādasyānyārthatvāt</q>
vidhyantaraśeṣatvāditi yāvat । <q>yathā'dhikāraṃ vyākhyānaṃ yuktam naitadvaśenādhi</q>-
<note>1. p. 12 ayaṃ mantrārtho brāhmaṇasya tu somavidyāprajamṛṇavākyena---mā</note>﻿
<pb n="123"/>
<q>kāraḥ</q> । ayamāśayaḥ-yāvajjīvanacodanāyāmeva vākyaśeṣabhūtamarthavāda[gataṃ] brāhmaṇapadaṃ
[yadi]syāt tadā vākyasya saṃbhūyakāritvāt tadanurodhenāpi adhikāripadaṃ vyākhyāyeta
vākyāntaraśeṣatvāt । tannirapekṣārthabodhakatvāt yājavajjīvacodanāyā brāhmaṇasyaivādhi-
kāravarṇanaṃ na yuktam mūlāpekṣatvāt । darśanasya mūlabhūtayāvajjīvanānusāreṇa brāhmaṇa-
grahaṇamupalakṣaṇatvena varṇanīyamiti ।</p>
<p>iti mahopādhyāyaśrīśālikanāthakṛtāyāṃ ṛjuvimalāyāṃ pañcikāyāṃ</p>
<p><q>ṣaṣṭhādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ</q></p>﻿
<pb n="124"/>
<p>ṛjuvimalāpañcikā</p>
<p>।। ṣaṣṭhādhyāsya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।</p>
<lg><l>।। 1 ।। sarvaśaktau pravṛttiḥ syāt tathābhūtopadeśāt ।। 1 ।।</l></lg>
<p>asminnadhikaraṇe gambhīrasya nyāyamahāhṛdasya upari bahavo laghudhiyaḥ plavanta
iti nyāyavicārameva tāvadāditaḥ ārabhāmahe---</p>
<p>tatra tāvat <q>kecit</q> evaṃ codayāṃbabhūvuḥ---yathā jīvanādikamadhikāri-
viśeṣaṇaṃ tathā sakalasāṅgapradhānakarmakalāpānuṣṭhānasāmarthyamapi । tatra yastāvat
kārts‍nyena yatprayogamupasaṃhartuṃ prabhavati tadviṣayo nāyaṃ vicāraḥ---kiṃ aṅgatyāgenāpya-
nuṣṭhānaṃ kartavyaṃ uta neti । yastu na prabhavati tasyānadhikāra eva śūdrasyevāgnihotrādau ।</p>
<p><q>yadapi</q> caike samādhānadhiyā'bhidadhati na-pravṛttāvevedaṃ yathāśaktyanuṣṭhāna-
mucyate । kintu pravṛttasya । tena sarvāṅgopasaṃhārasāmarthyenādāvadhikṛtasya yadyantarā
śaktiḥ vyāpadyate tadā prāktanādhikāradārḍhyenānuṣṭhānaṃ parisamāpyata eva । ata eva
nityeṣvagnihotrādiṣu śūdrādīnāṃ nānuṣṭhānam । adhikārasamadhigamasamaya eva teṣāma-
śaktatvāditi ।</p>
<p><q>tadapi</q> jātuṣamivābharaṇaṃ vipratipannajanamanīṣānalaśisvā[yāṃ] vilīyate ।
tathāhi---adhikāriviśeṣaṇayogāt adhikārī, pravartate ca । āprayogāpavargaṃ
cādhikāranuvṛttiranuṣṭhānasamāptaye'bhyupagamanīyā । anyathā hi nivṛtādhikārasyānuṣṭhānaṃ
na śabdataḥ, nāpyanyataḥ pramāṇāt syāt । tatra madhye prayoge'pi satyāmaśaktau śakte-
radhikārāṃśaniveśitvānnivartata evādhikāraḥ । nivṛttādhikārasya ca kinnibandhanamārabdha-
prayogaparisamāpam । śiṣṭavigarhaṇābhayāditi cet; tarhi naimittikakāmyayoḥ na kaści-
dviśeṣaḥ । nimittaparyanteṣu cedamadhikaraṇamityācāryāḥ । tasmādārambhasamaye prayoga-
madhye vā śaktivirahiṇāmadhikārābhāvādanuṣṭhānamayuktamiti ।</p>
<p><q>yadapi</q> kaścidāha---yannityaṃ kartavyaṃ tat sarvāṅgayuktamiti asaṃbhavānnityeṣu
yathāśaktyanuṣṭhānameva śāstrārthaḥ । tena sarvāṅgopasaṃhārasāmarthya vināpi nityeṣvadhikāra
iti</p>﻿
<pb n="125"/>
<p>tadidaṃ mīmāṃsātantramanādriyamāṇasya svamanīṣikākalpitam । tathāhi---
yathāviniyogamadhikāra iti nyāyasyāvagatirnāsti । tena jīvato'pi yaccoditaṃ tat
yasyaiva coditaṃ tat tasyaivāvaśyakartavyamiti nānyasya । nityānvitāṅgayuktaṃ ca karma
anuṣṭhānopasaṃhārasamarthasyaiva tadavaśyaṃ kartavyam; aśaktasya kimāyātam । na cāsaṃ-
bhāvyo'yaṃ śāstrārthaḥ kadācit sarvāṅgopasaṃhāraśaktisaṃbhavāt । anyathā kāmyānāṃ
karmaṇāmanavakāśatvāpātāditi yāvat । yatkiñcidetat । yadi ca yo yāvacchaknoti
nityakarmaṇi tasya tāvadeva coditamiti syāt tadā śūdrādīnāmagnividyāviyo-
gitvāt tadrahitamevānuṣṭhānaṃ coditamiti teṣāmapyagnihotrānuṣṭhānaṃ syāditi sakalācāra-
virodhaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>tathedamapare</q> vadanti---iha ca nimittaparyanteṣu phalaṃ nāstīti na tatprayukta-
manuṣṭhānaṃ tathāpi niyogasiddhiṃ prati vivādābhāvāt svasiddha‍yarthaṃ niyoga evānuṣṭhāna-
mākṣipatīti samāśrayaṇīyam । anyathā tadasiddheḥ । niyogasiddhistu yathācoditakṛts‍nā-
nuṣṭhānalabhyeti kṛts‍nasyaivānuṣṭhānamākṣipati na vikalasya । na cedamāśrayituṃ yuktam-
kadācitsakalasya sādhakatvaṃ kadācidvikalasyeti । sakalasyāpi kalāpasyādhikāra-
vidhinā yugapadga‍ṛhītatvāt । tathā gṛhītasya sādhakatvakalpanāt । yadi vikalasyāpi
sādhakatvaṃ tadā aṅgavat pradhānamapi parityajya kimityanuṣṭhānaṃ[na]syāt ।</p>
<p>api ca kāmyeṣu karmasu kasmādvikalānuṣṭhānaṃ neṣyate । phalāsiddheriti cenna,
niyogāyattatvātphalasiddheḥ । niyogādeva kālāntarabhāviphalamiti mīmāṃsakapravarāḥ
pratipedire । yadi ca vikalādeva niyogasiddhiḥ atrāpi kiṃ na syāt । athātra
sakalasādhyatvaṃ niyogasyāśrīyate, nityeṣvapi kimayaṃ niyogo rājājñāyā nirvāsitaḥ ?
tadidamadhikaraṇaṃ śraddhāvipralabdhamatīnāmevādaraṇīyamiti ।</p>
<p>atra prabhākarasevāhevākajaḍimānamāracayanti । satyaṃ śaktiradhikāri-
viśeṣaṇaṃ tathāpyeṣā cintā yujyata eva । dvidhā hi pumāṃsaḥ tirohitaśaktayaścāti-
rohitaśaktayaśca । tatra[ye]atirohitaśaktayaḥ teṣāṃ yadyapi śaktirasti[tathāpi](teṣāṃ)te
pratibandhakavaśāt śaktiphalamanuṣṭhānaṃ na labhante । kathaṃ punasteṣāṃ śaktirastīti gamyate ?
phalagamyā hi sā phalābhāve kiṃ tasyāṃ pramāṇam ? atrātridhīyate---ya eva prāk
kāryaṃ kuvan‍nupalabdhaḥ sa eva punarantarā na kṛtavān । punaśca kāraṇāntarasamupanipāte
kurvan‍nupalabhyate । tatra kiṃ śakternāśotsādau kalpyeyātām uta tirodhānatadvigamāviti ।
<pb n="126"/>
tatra dharmikalpanāto dharmakalpanā laghīyasīti pūrvaśaktivinaśapurassaro na śaktyanta-
ropajanaḥ kalpyate । kintu antarā kāryānudayadarśanāt pratibandhameva manyāmahe ।
punareva kāryodayadarśanāt tadapagama eva kalpanāmarhati । tasmādanuṣṭhānābhāve'pi
tiraskṛtā śaktirastīti sugamametat । tatra śakteradhikāriviśeṣaṇatvāt tirohi-
tāyāmapi ca sadbhāvāviśeṣāt tirohitaśaktīnāmapyadhikāro bhavatyeva । anuṣṭhānā-
tprāgbhāvinī hi daśā puruṣasyādhikāraviśeṣaṇam nānuṣṭhānameva, tasyādhikārāyattatvāt,
prāgadhikārādasaṃbhavāt । tena śaktirevādhikāriviśeṣaṇam । sā ca tirohitaśaktī-
nāmapyasti ityukto'dhikāraḥ । ye tu svabhāvata evoktāḥ śūdrādayaḥ atyantocchinna-
śaktayaḥ nāndhādayaḥ teṣāṃ śaktyabhāvādeva nādhikāraḥ । tatra ye tirohitaśaktayaḥ
teṣāmadhikāre sati kasyacidaṅgasyānuṣṭhānābhāve sati kimadhikāradārḍhyasadbhāvādanuṣṭhānaṃ
bhavatu uta aṅgāsadbhāvādananuṣṭhānaṃ (teṣāṃ śakta‍yabhāvādeva nādhikāraḥ । tatra ye
tirohitaśaktayaḥ teṣāmadhikāre sati) iti cintā । sā ceyamupakrame prayogamadhye ca
tulyā ।</p>
<p>tatra pūrvapakṣavādī manyate---yadyapi pratibaddhaśaktīnāmadhikāro bhavati tathāpyasau
nivartata eva sādhanavaikalyāt । kṛts‍nānuṣṭhānasampādyo nimittaparyante viniyoṃgaḥ
pratīyate । yadā ca kṛts‍namanuṣṭhīyate tadā vikalatvāt sādhanasya niyogasiddhirnāsti
tadabhāvācca na puruṣasyādhikāraḥ । niyojyasaṃbandhiniyogalakṣaṇe kārye sādhanatayā
karmaṇāmadhikāra ityutpannāpyadhikārapratītiḥ vilayamupaiti । yadi nitye vikalādapi
niyogasiddhiḥ tadā kārye'pi tathā syāditi । tathā pradhānaparityāgenāpi anuṣṭhānaṃ
prāpnoti aṅgaissaha sādhanatve pradhānasyāpyaviśeṣāditi ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntī tvāha-satyamadhikāro yāvadadhikāravidhinā prayujyate tāvataiva vini-
yogārthanirvṛttiḥ na yāvadviniyuktaṃ tāvataiva; bādhavat । sarveṣāmaṅgatve satyapi keṣā-
ñcidaṅgānāṃ bādhe yāvantyevādhikāravidhinā'nuṣṭhāpyante tāvadbhireva tatsiddhiḥ tathehāpi
adhikāravidhireva sādhanabhāvamupakalpayati na pramāṇāntaram । tena yāvatprayuṅkte
tāvataiva tatsiddhiṃ gamayati । yathāsaṃbhavinaśca prayuktiḥ nāsaṃbhavinaḥ । tena satyadhikāre
yāvatsaṃbhavaṃ prayuktāṅgasampādya evādhikāravidhiḥ nimittaparyanteṣviti kalpyate ।</p>
<p>yattūktaṃ---kāmyo'pi tathā syāditi । tatra brūmaḥ-kāmye phalaparyantānvayitvāt
adhikārasya phalaṃ prati karaṇībhūta eva yāgādirviṣayaḥ । nacetikartavyatārahitasya
<pb n="127"/>
phalaṃ prati karaṇatā'sti । kṛts‍nā cetikartavyatā । tenaikadeśābhāve'pi itikartavyatayā
śūnyatayā karaṇatvānupapatteḥ akaraṇībhūtasya viṣayatvamiti । itikartavyatāvirahe kevala-
viṣayāt viṣayābhāve ca niyogābhāvāt tadabhāve cādhikārābhāvāt nānuṣṭhānasiddhiḥ ।
ata eva pradhānaparityāge'pyanuṣṭhānaṃ syāditi nāśaṅkanīyam । nityeṣu phalāntarā-
bhāvāt na karaṇībhūtasya viṣayatvamiti itikartavyatāvirahe kevalaviṣayapratyabhijñānāt
niyogāpatteḥ adhikāro yuktaḥ । tadbalena cānuṣṭhānamapīti granthārthaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>nimittaparyantamatrādhikāraṃ cintayatyācāryaḥ</q> iti kāmyeṣu neyaṃ cinteti
darśayati । cintāsvarūpamāha---<q>kimaṅgairanupasaṃhniyamāṇaiḥ nimittatvamevāpaiti</q>
kimaṅgairanupasaṃhniyamāṇaiḥ kṛts‍nānuṣṭhānasādhyasya vidhyarthasya asiddheḥ adhikārābhāvā-
jjīvanādeḥ (na) nimittatvamevāpaiti satyapi tasminnananuṣṭhānāt । [u]ta nimittatvaṃ
nā(।nnā)paiti anupasaṃhniyamāṇairapyaṅgaiḥ uktena nyāyena niyogena niyogārthasiddheradhikāre
sati nimittatvamanuṣṭhāne yujyata eva ।</p>
<p>svavacanameva vivṛṇoti---<q>etaduktaṃ bhavati-kimadhikārāvagamo bhavati ।
utādhikārānavagamāt kathañ‍cidanuṣṭhānamiti</q> ।</p>
<p>yadā'dhikārāvagamo bhavati tadā nimittatvamevāpaiti । yadā tu adhikārāna-
vagamāt kathaṃcidanuṣṭhānaṃ tadā nimittatve nāpaiti । nanu ca yadā'ṅgānuṣṭhānāsaṃbhavaḥ
tasyādhikāra eva nāsti । yasya cādhikāraḥ tasya ca kṛts‍nānuṣṭhānameva saṃbhavatīti
cinte/?/yaṃ na jñāyate kīdṛśī[ti] tadāha---</p>
<p><q>nanu ca saṃśaya evāyamaprakaṭīkṛtārthaḥ iti । ayaṃ prakaṭyate-sarvāṅga-
viśiṣṭe karmaṇi adhikṛtasya kadācit prayogaśaktau sāmarthyānapagame'pi
cinteyamiti viṣayaviśeṣapradarśanenaiva saṃśayo vyākhyātaḥ</q> ।</p>
<p>yasya sāmarthyaṃ nāpagataṃ tasya sarvāṅgaviśiṣṭe karmaṇyadhikṛtasya prayoga[ā]śaktau
kiṃ nimittatvamevāpaiti uta neti cintā । kathaṃ punaḥ sāmarthyānapagamo'śak‍tiśca ।
śaktireva hi sāmarthyam । tena sāmarthyamanapagataṃ aśaktiśceti parasparaviruddham ।
samādhatte---</p>
<p><q>daivānmānuṣādvāpi tiraskārādaśak‍tiḥ na punarājānataḥ, svabhāvaśak‍ti-
rastyeveti sāmarthyānapagamo varṇyate</q> ।</p>﻿
<pb n="128"/>
<p>daivādrogādeḥ mānuṣāt abhighātādeḥ śak‍testiraskāra iti aśaktirityu-
cyate । etattu prāguktameva । tasmāt kadācidaśaktiriti sūktam । nanu tiraskārepi
śakteḥ anadhikāra eva atrāha---</p>
<p><q>sāmarthyaṃ cādhikārahetuḥ nopadhānavyapekṣam</q> ।</p>
<p>sāmarthyaṃ svābhāvikamevādhikāriviśeṣaṇaṃ na punaḥ upadhānasāpekṣam । upadhāna-
śabdena upādhibhūtaṃ vastvabhimatam । pratibandhāpagamaṃ cikitsādi । apratibandha ca
sāmarthyaṃ nādhikārehatuḥ kiṃ tarhi svābhāvikam । na hi kāryāt prāk apratibandhatā
śakteḥ śakyate vak‍tum । kāryaṃ cānuṣṭhānameva । tena satyanuṣṭhāne apratibandhaśakti-
niścaye sati adhikāraḥ, adhikāre cānuṣṭhānamiti itaretarāśrayatā syāt । tasmāt
svābhāvikī śaktiradhikāriviśeṣaṇam । adhikṛta eva pratibandhavigamāvapi tathā ।
yathā nayanācchādanapakṣmavigamaḥ(mau) ājyāvekṣaṇādiṣu iti bhavati saṃśayaḥ---
kimupadhānādrogādeḥ pravṛttiśaktirivādhikāro'pi virudhyate uta upādhinirapekṣatvāt
apravṛttāvapyadhikṛta eveti । atra pūrvapakṣavādī paśyati---</p>
<p><q>satyamanupādhikamevājānataḥ svabhāvata eva yatsāmarthyamanupādhikaṃ
anapekṣitapratibandhavigamaṃ adhikārahetuḥ kintu pravṛttyarthatvāttasya upādhi-
vihatāyā api pravṛtteḥ hetorakiñ‍citkaraṃ vidyamānamapi</q> ।</p>
<p>asyārthaḥ---sāmarthyasya pravṛttiḥ prayojanam । tatra yadi satyapi sāmarthye
pravṛttirnāsti tadā vidyamānaṃ akiñcitkaram । tasmin satyapi pratibandhavaśena
pravṛttyanupapatteḥ । asatyāṃ pravṛttau kṛts‍nānuṣṭhānasya saṃpādanīyasya vidhyarthasyāsiddheḥ
nivartata evādhikāraḥ । tasmāt sarvāṅgopasaṃhāreṇaiva [aṅgīkaraṇī]yā pravṛttiḥ । atrai-
vādhikārakāryasya niyogasyābhirnivṛttiḥ naikadeśaprayogāt anyathā ko viśeṣaḥ phala-
paryanteṣvadhikāreṣu ? asāvapi phalaparyanto'dhikāraḥ anaupādhika eva upādhinira-
pekṣa eva । na ca pravṛttyaśaktau kāryakṣamo bhavati, tathābhūte sakalāṅgayukte'dhi-
kṛtatvāt ।</p>
<p><q>atrābhidhīyate । phalaparyante viśeṣaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ nimittaparyanteṣvadhi-
kārānapa(va)gamo varṇyate pravṛttāvaśaktāvapi । yadi pravṛttāvaśak‍tiḥ kathaṃ
tarhi varṇyate ? itthaṃ varṇyate । anaupādhike adhikārāvagame hi nimittatva-</q>﻿
<pb n="129"/>
<q>mapahnotuṃ śakyam । bhavati hi aśak‍terautpattikyāḥ śūdrādīnāṃ nādhikāraḥ
na punaḥ svābhāvikasāmarthyavaśenopajātasyādhikārasya pratibandhavaśenāśak‍te-
radhikāravighātaḥ(m)</q> ।</p>
<p><q>tasmādanapagatādhikārasya yathāśaktyanuṣṭhānamanuṣṭhānavido manyante evaṃ
yathāśaktyanuṣṭhānaṃ nityeṣvasti</q> ।</p>
<p><q>ata evātra nityādhikāre gauṇo mukhyaśca śāstrārtha ityācakṣate
mīmāṃsakāḥ</q> ।</p>
<p>codayati---</p>
<p><q>kimidaṃ kūśmāṇḍabhūtaṃ pralapyate asaṃbandhaṃ, ekadeśasya śāstrārthasya
gauṇatvaṃ mukhyatvaṃ ceti</q> ।</p>
<p>pariharati---</p>
<p><q>bhavānevātra pralāpī</q> ।</p>
<p>na mīmāṃsakāḥ pralāpinaḥ । kathamiti pṛcchati । uttaraṃ---<q>avihanyamāne
hi aśaktāvapyadhikāre yāvacchaktyā cānuṣṭhāne pratīyamāne arthākṣipte ca
saṃbhavati śrautāpāye ca nopadānaṃ virudhyate</q> ।</p>
<p>nanu yadi śrautaṃ tyajyate tadā'paramapi kimiti na tyajyate ityatrāha---</p>
<p><q>yāvadaśaktistāvannopādīyate । tathāpi śakyatyāgeṣu na kiñcana
pramāṇamasti śakyopādāna [iva] iti</q> ।</p>
<p>anena hi yathāśaktyavagamo hetuḥ । <q>tena kiñcittyājyaṃ kiñciccopādātavyam ।
punaścodayati---<q>gauṇasya kimāyātam</q> ।</p>
<p>bhavatu arthasya kimāyātaṃ ? yadyapyarthānnīvārādi upādīyate tathāpi kathaṃ
gauṇatvaṃ ?</p>
<p>pariharati---</p>
<p><q>tadeva hi ārthamabhyupagamya na śakyate upādātuṃ</q> yāvat gauṇatā vrīhi-
śāstrārthasya nocyate tāvannīvārāṇāṃ nopādānaṃ saṃbhavati । nanu ca kiñcidvikala-
vrīhiśāstrārthagrahaṇenāpi karmasiddheḥ kartha gauṇatetyatrāha---</p>﻿
<pb n="130"/>
<p>na hi nīvārāṇāṃ na pratītyā bhūyo'vayavasāmānyamupapadyate । nīvārāneva
hyupā/?/dadānaḥ bhūyovayavasāmānyopādānaṃ śaknoti kartuṃ nānyathā । nīvāreṣu vopādīya-
māneṣu siddhaṃ gauṇatvam । tasmātsupṭhūcyate gauṇo mukhyaśca śāstrārtha iti ।</p>
<p>anyatra kathamiti atrāha---</p>
<p><q>ārādupakārakāṅgahāne'pi kasyaciccopādānāt sadṛśabuddhirbhavati</q> ।</p>
<p>abhinne'pi dharmiṇi yathā[loke](yoge)kasyacidanekaguṇasaṃbhṛ(bhū)tasya dṛṣṭasya
punaḥ kālāntare kaiścidga‍uṇairviyuktasya draṣṭāro bhavanti vaktāraḥ sa ivāyaṃ dṛśyata iti ।
avasthāvato'bhede'pyavasthānāṃ bhinnānāṃ sādṛśyamupapadyata eveti । tasmādubhayaṃ siddhaṃ
gauṇamukhyatā yathāśaktyanuṣṭhānaṃ ca । darśanamuktam । <q><quote>‘tadeva yādṛk‌kīdṛk‌ca
hotavyaṃ’</quote> iti vacanamidaṃ kasmānna bhavati yena darśanamucyate</q> । uttaraṃ---
<q>(sa)[na] yādṛk‌kīdṛk‌śabdārthau vidhātuṃ śakyete vihitāpekṣatvādanayoḥ</q> ।</p>
<p>vihitadravyamapekṣya yādṛk‌kīdṛk‌śabdārthau vidheyau nānyathā । tatra yadi tāvat
dravyaṃ viśiṣṭameva vihitaṃ tadā na yādṛk‌kīdṛk‌śabdārthau vidhātuṃ śakyete । atha
dravyamātraṃ vihitaṃ na viśeṣaḥ tadāpi prāptatvādvidhānaṃ nopapadyate । tasmāt nyāyānu-
vādāviti sūktam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 2 ।। kāmyeṣu caivamarthitvāt ।। 8 ।।</l></lg>
<p>nanvekādaśe darśitaṃ kāmādhikāre sakalāṅgopasaṃhāra eva kartavya iti ।
kimaparamiha cintyata iti । atrāha---</p>
<p><q>iha vikṛtayaḥ udāharaṇam । ekādaśe yadadhikaraṇaṃ tatprakṛtiviṣayam</q> ।</p>
<p>iha tu vikṛṣu cintā kena viśeṣaṇena ? uttaraṃ---</p>
<p><q>na hyatrāṅgopadeśaḥ । kiṃ tarhi ? kāryato hi saṃbandhaḥ</q> । vikṛtiṣu
aṅgāni nopadiśyante । kintu kāryeṇa karaṇopakāralakṣaṇenābhisaṃbadhyante ।</p>
<p><q>kaścaivaṃ sati viśeṣaḥ ? ayamasti viśeṣaḥ । upadiṣṭe hi karmaṇyadhi-
kāraḥ । upadeśāvagatipurassaro'tideśaḥ । vikṛtiṣu ca pradhānamātra-
mevopadiśyate । ataḥ kāryābhisaṃbandhānāmaṅgānāṃ kadācidanuṣṭhānāśakteḥ
adhikāro nivartate iti śakyate vak‍tuṃ upadeśaviṣayatvādadhikārasya</q> ।</p>﻿
<pb n="131"/>
<p>upadiśyata ityupadeśaḥ । evaṃ caupadeśikasyādhikārasya na saṅkocaḥ kṛto
bhavati । kriyatāṃ ko doṣa ityatrāha---</p>
<p>na hi kāryeṇa karaṇopakāralakṣaṇena prākṛtān padārthānatidiśatā
pramāṇabhūtenopadeśasya saṅkoco nyāyyaḥupadiṣṭārthasiddha‍yarthatvāt kāryasya ।
upadiṣṭo'rthaḥ kathaṃ nāma siddha‍yedityevamarthaṃ kāryaṃ pramāṇamāśrīyate । tena
yadarthameva yajjātaṃ tasya tena saṅkoco[na]nyāyyaḥ । na hi guṇānurodhena
pradhānaṃ saṅkocamarhati ।</p>
<p>idamatrākūtam-yadyapi sāṅgapradhānaviśiṣṭasya niyogasya kāryabhūtasya tadanuṣṭhāna-
yogyameva saṃbandhībhavitumarhati । ākāṅkṣasannidhiyogyatānāṃ sambandhahetutvāt ।
tathā ca bhavatu nāma tathāvidhasyaivādhikāra iti ayogyasya nādhikāraḥ । yastu śakta
eva1tirohitaśaktiḥ kiñcidātideśikamaṅgamupasaṃhartuṃ na śakroti tasyāpi vikṛtiṣu
kāmyāsvapi nānuṣṭhānamanupapannam । na ca tatraivaṃ śakyate vak‍tuṃ - phalaṃ prati karaṇī
bhūteṣvadhikārāt setikartavyatākasya ca karaṇatvāt aṅgābhāve karaṇatvānupapatteḥ
viṣayatvābhāve cādhikārāsaṃbhavāt ananuṣṭhānamiti, upadiśyamānaviṣayatvādadhikārasyeti ।</p>
<p><q>atrābhidhīyate---yadi kāryanirapekṣo'dhikāraḥ phalaparyanteṣu syāt
syādetadevam ।</q></p>
<p>asyārthaḥ---phalaparyanṣu karaṇībhūteṣu adhikārāt setikartavyatākasya karaṇa-
tvāt kāryeṇa ca pramāṇena vinā vikṛtiṣvitikartavyatāyā abhāvāt kāryasamarpiteti-
kartavyatānvayalabdhakaraṇabhāva evopadiṣṭe pradhāne sādhikāra iti atideśikopa-
saṃhāreṇānuṣṭhānam । yadi paraṃ phalaparyanteṣvapi karaṇopakāranirapekṣa evādhikāraḥ
syāt tadaivātideśikasyāpi aṅgasya tyāgaḥ syāt । na caitadasti tadāha---<q>yathā ca
sakārya eva sakaraṇopakāra eva upadeśopadiṣṭe pradhānepyadhikriyate phalārthī
tathā ekādaśe vakṣyāmaḥ ।</p>
<p>kāmyanimittādhikārayorviśeṣamaparamāha---</p>
<p><q>yathā ca nimittaparyanteṣu nimittāpagamo mābhūditi viguṇamapi
kartuṃ yuktam ।</q></p>
<note>1. atirohita---mā</note>﻿
<pb n="132"/>
<p>anuṣṭhānaṃ prati nimittatayā pratīyate । yadi cānuṣṭhānaṃ na kriyeta nimittatva-
mevāpaiti । na ca tadyuktam । [ato]viguṇamapi kartuṃ yuktam । anuṣṭhānaṃ prati nimi[ttaṃ]
phalāvagatiḥ ananuṣṭhāne'pi 1phalāvagamāvirodhāt । pratyuta viguṇānuṣṭhāne sā phalā-
vagatirna saṃbhavati sādhyatvāt phalasya sādhyasya setikartavyatākakaraṇāyattatvāt iti
sarvāṅgopasaṃhāra eva atrāpi vikṛtiṣvapi nyāyyaḥ ।</p>
<lg><l><q>।। 3 ।। kriyāṇāmāśritatvāt dravyāntare vibhāgaḥ syāt ।। 11 ।।</q></l></lg>
<p>nanu ca gauṇamukhyatveśāstrārtha ityuktam । na punastatpratyayādṛte'nuṣṭhānaṃ
saṃbhavati । yadi mukhyaśāstrārthaikadeśo'pi nānugṛhyate tadā kimananuṣṭhānene । gauṇā-
vagatāvapi tadityevānuṣṭhāne hetuḥ । tasmāt tatpratyaye yatraḥ kartavyaḥ ।</p>
<p>pūrvapakṣamāha-<q>nanu cānumānīkī kriyetyuktam । svarūpāgrahaṇe tu kathaṃ tatpratyayaḥ</q> ।</p>
<p>anumānena kriyā'vagamyate anumānācca svarūpāvagame ca pratyabhijñāyā anu/?/-
pattiriti kathaṃ kriyāyāṃ tatpratyaya iita ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntamāha---<q>śāstrāvagamyatayā tatpratyayābhidhānaṃ na svarūpeṇe-
tyadoṣaḥ ।</q> yadyapyānumānikī kriyā tathāpi tasya dravyāntareṇa kriyāyāḥ tenaiva
śabdenābhidhānam auṣādhikatvena śāstrāvagamyatayā tatpratyayaḥ na punaḥ svarūpeṇetyadoṣaḥ ।
śāstrāvagamyatvaṃ cānuṣṭhānahetuḥ na svarūpāvagatiriti sūktaṃ śāstrārthānanvayitvam । <q>nanu
svarūpe pratyabhijñānaṃ kimiti nocyata iti</q> suhṛdbhāvena kathayati । svarūpa-
pratyabhijñānaṃ tu na pratyakṣādṛte'stīti prathamapāde uktam buddhikarmaṇī abhihite-
'pratyakṣe iti ।</p>
<p>atra yadi śāstrāvagamyatayā tatpratyabhijñābhidhānaṃ <q>kathaṃ tarhi sve sve
prameye(na)[tena]tena pramāṇena pratyabhijñāpyastītyuktam ।</q> bhavati pratyakṣeṇa
pratyakṣagrāhye śāstrāvagamye ca śāstreṇetyāpatitam । pariharati---</p>
<p><q>naitadevam darśanāntarasya smaraṇapūrvikā hi pramitiḥ pratyabhijñetyuktam ।
pūrvadarśanānusandhānena pratītiḥ sā pratyabhijñā tadevedamiti ।</p>
<note>1. phalāpagama-mā</note>﻿
<pb n="133"/>
<p>anumānādiṣu punaḥ na darśanāntarapūrvikā pratītiḥ, viṣaye liṅgādimātrabhāvya-
manumānādikam । tena pūrvadarśanānusandhānaṃ tatra nāstīti । pratyakṣaṃ tu pūrvadarśana-
saṃskārasacivendriyajanyatayā pūrvadarśanānusandhānenotpadyata iti yuktaṃ pratyabhijñānam ।
ato viṣayāntarānavagatimātram । <q>atrocyate । na, pratyabhijñābalasyaivaṃjātīya-
kasyopādhibhūtatvāt ।</q> śabda eva paraṃ tatra pravartate na punaḥ pratyabhijñā'stīti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 4 ।। śrutipramāṇatvācchiṣṭābhāve nāgamo'nyasyāśiṣṭatvāt ।। 13 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nanu sarvaśaktyadhikaraṇe'yathābhūtamapi kartavyamevetyuktam ।</q> tena
vrīhyādīnāmapi parityāgenānuṣṭhānamuktameva । ataḥ kathamatra pūrvapakṣāśaṅkā ? uttaraṃ---
<q>tenaivamuktam ।</q> yathāśrutamapi kartavyamityetāvaduktam । yadi śrutāntarāsaṃbhave'pi
śrutāntaraṃ kartavyamevetyuktam athāpyetadadhikaraṇaṃ na kartavyam vrīhiśrutyarthāsaṃbhavepi
puroḍāśaśrutyarthaḥ kartavya eva ।</p>
<p>ekadeśī samādhatte---<q>evaṃ tarhi prayojanamidaṃ tasyādhikaraṇasya ।</p>
<p>dūṣayati---<q>prayojane'rthyamāne pūrvapakṣeṇa kiṃ ?</p>
<p>kṛta evātra pūrvaḥpakṣaḥ । tena prayojanamidaṃ na bhavati । paramasamādhātā āha---
<q>ya[dī]daṃ sarvaśaktyadhikaraṇasya prayojanamātraṃ na bhavati evaṃ tarhi kartavya
evātra pūrvaḥpakṣaḥ ।</q> sa evāha---<q>uk‍taṃ dvitīye śāstrāntaratayā dravyavidhayo
nāvagamyanta iti ।</q> nirapekṣasādhyabhede[vā]'nubandhamede vā śāstrāntaratā bhavati ।
na dravyavidhīnāṃ pradhānavidhikāryānapekṣaṃ kāryāntaramasti । na cānubandhabhedaḥ । tena
śāstrāntaratā tāvanna śakyate vak‍tum । tathā dvādaśe vakṣyāmaḥ । <q>kāryeṇa vikalpaḥ
na śāstrāntaratayā ।</q> kāryeṇa vikalpo vakṣyate । sa na śāstrāntaratayā bhavati ।
śāstrāntaratve hi vikalpānupapatteḥ । kutaḥ ? kāryānyatve hi śāstrānyatvaṃ nānyathā ।
tena śāstrānyatve sati balāt kāryānyatvāpattiḥ । ekārthāstu vikalperannityuktaṃ[na]
nānārthānām । tena śāstrāntaratā tāvat dravyavidhīnāṃ nāsti ।</p>
<p><q>bhavatvevaṃ tataḥkim ? idaṃ tato bhavati---āgneyo'ṣṭākapālaḥ
<quote>“vrīhibhiryajeta”</quote> iti caikaṃ śāstram</q> ekaśca śāstrārthaḥ kāryasyānantarasya śrutya-
ntarasya tyāgo'yam yasya śrutyantarasya tyāgena śrutyantarārtho'nuṣṭhīyate ।</p>
<p>upasaṃharati---<q>tasmādyuk‍taṃ yatsamidho yajatītyeva</q>mādyarthaparityāgenā-
gneyo'ṣṭākapāla ityasyārthasyānuṣṭhānam । anubandhabhedena śāstrabhedāt śāstrāntaratyāge-﻿
<pb n="134"/>
nāpi śāstrāntarārthasyānuṣṭhānaṃ yuktam । yuktameva । vrīhibhiryajeteti punaśśāstrānta-
rānupapatteḥ tadabhāve nānuṣṭhānamiti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate ।</p>
<p><q>atrābhidhīyate---satyaṃ nedaṃ śāstrāntaram puroḍāśaśāstrāt vrīhi-
bhiryajeteti ।</q> yata eva śāstrāntaraṃ na bhavati <q>ata evānuṣṭhānaṃ puroḍāśa-
śrutyā'stīti śrutadravyaparityāge'pi anuṣṭhānamucitam ।</q></p>
<p>yadi puroḍāśaśrutyaiva dravyamākṣipyate <q>kiṃ tarhi vrīhibhiryajetetyanena
kriyate ।</q></p>
<p>uttaraṃ---<q>niyamo vrīhīṇām ।</q> puroḍāśaniyogāṅgatve nirjñāte niyoga-
siddha‍yarthatayā vrīhīṇāmevopādānam anyasādhakatānavagamāt । avihiteṣu vrīhiṣu
kiyāmātrasiddhaye yatkiñcid dravyamupādīyata iti niyamaḥ prayojanaṃ bhavati । na hi
niyamaḥ śāstrārthatvaṃ (kāmaṃ) vihanti puroḍāśavidheḥ । yadi hi niyame sati puroḍāśavidheḥ
śāstrārthatvaṃ vihanyeta tadā niyamābhāve puroḍāśaśrutyartho nānuṣṭhīyeta । na cāyaṃ(a)
śāstrārthatāṃ vihanti । kutaḥ ? niyamo hi anirjñāte kārye ātmānaṃ labhate । na ca
śāstrādṛte kāryāvagatiḥ । tasmātsiddhaṃ niyamābhāvepyanuṣṭhānam । niyamanirapekṣatvā-
tkāryasya niyamamantareṇāpi śāstrasyārthavattvāt । kathaṃ niyamanirapekṣatetyatrāha---
<q>niyamena hi tadapekṣyata iti ।</q> atra na tena niyamaḥ । tasmādaśāstrāntaratve'pi
tadabhāve niyamābhāve'nuṣṭhānasiddhiḥ । yatpunardravyāntaravidhānumaktam tatparihṛtam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 5 ।। na devatāgniśabdakriyamanyārthasaṃyogāt ।। 18 ।।</l></lg>
<p>kena punaḥ prasaṅgetedamadhikaraṇamāyātam । yadi tāvat dravyaguṇacodanā-
bhāve'pi śāstrāntaramapi pradhānaṃ kartavyamityucyeta pūrveṇaivādhikaraṇena gatamidam ।
athaiṣāmabhāve'kartavyatāmeva manyate tat pūrvādhikaraṇena sarvaśaktyadhikaraṇena ca
viruddham । pūrvādhikaraṇe hi pradhānaśāstrārtho'nuṣṭheya ityuktam । tathā sarvaśaktyadhi-
karaṇena ca viruddham prayājādikarmābhāve'pi pradhānaṃ kartavyamiti sarvaśaktyadhi-
karaṇe pratipāditam । ucyate । sāmānyaṃ taccikīrṣā hi ityanena sadṛśe pratinidhau
prāpte tadapavādārthamidamadhikaraṇam । keṣu cinneṣyate sadṛśapratinidhiḥ yeṣu ca neṣyate
tānīmāni pratyudāhriyante---na devatāgniśabdakriyaṃ ityanena sūtreṇaiva sadṛśapratinidhya-
pavādo'yam । ata eva karmāpyatrodāharaṇam । tatrāpi pratinidhyabhāvasya saṃbhavāt ।
<pb n="135"/>
yeṣāṃ tu mate pūrvādhikaraṇokte dravyāntaropādāne tatpratiṣedhārthamevedamadhikaraṇaṃ teṣāṃ
mate karmodāharaṇamasaṃbaddhaṃ syāt ।</p>
<p><q>nanu ca devatābhāve'pi ananuṣṭhānameva pradhānasyāpi manyante kecit ।</q>
tena pratinidhyapavādamātratā tvatra nāstīti । kintu karmaṇo lopapratipādanārthameva ।
kecichabdaṃ prayuñjānaḥ asminnarthe'nāsthāṃ darśayati । etacca vakṣyāmaḥ । samādhatte-<q>nānta-
rīyakametadbhaviṣyati ।</q> devatāpratinidhau pratiṣiddhe nāntarīyakametadbhaviṣyati
karmāpi tyājyameveti । kathamidaṃ nāntarīyakamityatrāha---<q>yuktyantarābhidhānāt
devatāvirahe karmārthatyāge anyārthasaṃyogāt iti ।</q> ato mūlādhikaraṇayukteḥ
yuktyantarasya bhāṣyakāreṇoktatvāt । atraiva pratipādayiṣyāmastadyuktyantaram । tatra
pūrvapakṣavādī sadṛśacikīrṣāṃ manyate । tāvatā ca lābhena kiyānapi śāstrārtha-
ssaṅgṛhīto bhavati ।</p>
<p>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---<q>na devatādiṣvetatsaṃbhavati yo hyuddeśassūrya iti ।</q>
upādīyamāneṣu [nīvāreṣu]vrīhyavayavasāmānyalābho labhyate । naivamatra kiñcillabhyate ।
<quote>‘vrīhibhiryajeta’</quote> iti vrīhīṇāṃ sādhanabhāvo'vayavaparyantaḥ tena sādhanībhūtasādhāraṇā-
vayavalābhena tatra śāstrārthaikadeśānugrahaḥ । devatāyāṃ tu tannāstīti । na hi bhāsva-
ratvādiguṇaparyanto'tra śāstrārthaḥ iti ।</p>
<p>nanu āhavanīye juhoti ityayaṃ śāstrārthaḥ agna‍yantare'pyupādīyamāne
prāyeṇānugṛhyata evetyatrāha-<q>evamāhavanīyādiṣvapyagniṣu na dravyāntare kiñ‍jit
sādṛśyaṃ sādhāraṇarūpamuglabhāmahe ।</q> codanālakṣaṇatvādāhavanīyaśabdavācyasya
svarūpasya । ādhānādijanyasyātīndriyasyāhavanīyaśabdavācyatvāt tasya kaścidbhāgo
dravyāntaropādānenānugṛhīta iti nāsti pramāṇam । atha śabdamātramupādīyate na
mantrasādṛśyaṃ kiñcidupāttaṃ bhavati । mantratayā copādānaṃ na śabdatayeti vyarthaṃ śabda-
mātrasyopādānam ।</p>
<p>evaṃ karmasvapi sādṛśyābhāvānna kiñcitsādṛśyamupādātuṃ śakyate । karmaṇāma-
tīndriyāṇāṃ sādhāraṇamasādhāraṇaṃ vā rūpamavagantuṃ na śakyata iti sādṛśyābhāvānnānyo-
pādānam । ida nīṃ devatābhāve tadyuktyantaramāha---</p>
<p><q>devatāyāṃ punaḥ dravyāntare upādīyamāne āstāṃ tāvat sādṛśyaṃ,
devatātvamapi nāstīti । ko'bhiprāyaḥ evaṃ vadato bhāṣyakārasya ? aya-</q>﻿
<pb n="136"/>
<q>mabhiprāyaḥ-tadabhāve kevalaṃ karmānuṣṭhānamapi naiva saṃbhavatīti manyate ।</q> devatā-
bhāve yāgasyāniṣpatau kevalaṃ karmānuṣṭhānamapi na saṃbhavati ।</p>
<p>nanu ca <quote>‘agnihotraṃ juhotīti’</quote> ityavagamāt śāstrārthasya devatāviśeṣābhāve
sāmānyataḥ siddhe kimityananuṣṭhānam ? yathāha devānāṃ priyaḥ-yadi devatātvaṃ nāma
sāmānyamasti, prāgviśeṣacodanāyāḥ tacca nāsti caiva hi, yasya viṣayaścodyate saiva
tasya devatā nānyetyuktam । ataḥ sāmānyena devatā nāsti svarūpato viśeṣato'pi
tāvat devatā bhavati śabdamātropakāriṇī hi setyuktam । kutaḥ tasyāṃ sādṛśyaṃ
sāmānyaṃ vā ? yadi devatā sā । tathā mantre śabdāntaropādāne na kiñcitsādṛśya-
mupalabhāmahe, varṇasaṃhatyātmano mantrasyāpi kāryata upagamāt । svabhāvato hi varṇāḥ
parasparavilakṣaṇā eva । teṣāṃ mantrabhāvaḥ kāryasamadhigamya eva sa varṇasaṅghātāntare
upātte'nugṛhīta iti na śakyate vak‍tum kramānyato nāsti । <q>evaṃ tarhi devatāyā
vinā yāgānupapatteḥ agnihotraṃ juhotīti śāstrārthaḥ parityakto bhavati ।</q> uttaraṃ-
<q>coditāgna‍yabhāve yadi na śakyate saṃpādayitumiti tadā kimanyada-
tastyāgācchreyaḥ ।</q></p>
<p>yadiśabdaṃ prayuñjāno'trāpyanāsthāmāha । yadi devatābhāvepi yāgānapāyaḥ tadā
bhavatvanuṣṭhānam । atha yāga eva na saṃvarteta tadā bhavatu tyāgaḥ[kimetena] (kiṃ naitena)
nirbandhena । tasmānna kevalaṃ sādṛśyaṃ nāsti devatāyāṃ sāmānyamapi nāstīti, tadabhāve
cānuṣṭhānamapi nāstīti । tadidaṃ nāntarīyakam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 6 ।। pratiṣiddhaṃ cāviśeṣeṇa hi tacchrutiḥ ।। 20 ।।</l></lg>
<p>pūrvapakṣamāha---</p>
<p><q>sādṛśyalābhāt sādhāraṇāvayavalābhāt sadṛśapratinidhiriti taccikīrṣā
hīti vakṣyāmaḥ । tena māṣā api pratinidheyā iti ।</q></p>
<p><q>nanu ca pratiṣedhaḥ śrūyate na māṣā yajñasambandhāḥ kartavyā iti । tena
kathaṃ pratinidhiriti ।</q></p>
<p>pariharati---</p>
<p><q>satyaṃ śrūyate yatra bhāṣā ityeva sambadhyante tatrāsau pratiṣedhaḥ । iha
punaḥ śrutadravyasadṛśā iti pratinidhīyante na bhāṣā iti ।</q></p>﻿
<pb n="137"/>
<p>ayamāśayaḥ---yatra bhāṣāṇāṃ yajñasaṃbandhaḥ tatrāsau pratiṣedhaḥ । kutaḥ ? yajña-
saṃbandhapratiṣedhāt iha tu bhāṣāṇāṃ yajñasaṃbandho nāsti । śrutasaṃpādakatayā iha bhāṣāṃ
nāntarīyakāḥ । tasmānnātra pratiṣedhaḥ kramata iti pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>atrābhidhīyate । satyaṃ sadṛśā iti pratinidhīyante te na bhāṣā iti
na punaḥ bhāṣabhāvo'pahnotuṃ śakyate ।</q> yadi bhāṣabhāvo'panhūyeta tadā pratiṣedho
nāvataret । na ca tasyāpahnavo'sti । sa evāha---<q>pratinidhau bhāṣabhāvo na
vivakṣitaḥ</q> iti । etadapi satyaṃ, kintu pratiṣedho bhāṣabhāvaviṣayatayā bhāṣabhāvasya
bhāṣatvasya viṣayatayā bhāṣajātyāśrayatayā pratiṣedho vārayituṃ na śakyate । nanu bhavatu
bhāṣajātyāśrayatayā yajñasaṃbandhastu nāstīti atrāha---</p>
<p><q>tasya ca nāntarīyakayajñasaṃbandhānapahārāt saṃbhavo na nivārayituṃ
śakyate ।</q></p>
<p>nanu ca vikalpaḥ prāpnoti vihitapratiṣiddhatvāt tataśca kathamekāntenānu-
pādānamiti atrāha---<q>na cātra vikalpo'pyāśaṅkyate śrutasaṃbhavamātrākṣepāt
pratinidhānasya ।</q> ye śrutasya dravyasyāvayavāḥ teṣāmākṣepo'vaidhaśrutasya viṣayasya
saṃbhavāt । pratiṣedhasya śrautasya ca bhāṣatvasya pratiṣedhaviṣayasya saṃbhavāt bhinnaviṣayatvānna
vikalpaḥ । tasmāt pratiṣedhātikramāt bhayāt na pratinidheyā bhāṣā iti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 7 ।। tathā svāminaḥ phalasamavāyāt phalasya
karmayogitvāt ।। 21 ।।</l></lg>
<p>adhikāriṇamācikṣipsuḥ pṛcchati---<q>kasyāyaṃ pratinidhiḥ kartavyatayā
cintyata iti ।</q> kimayaṃ pratinidhirupādeyo neti cintyate ।।</p>
<p>uttaraṃ---<q>yasya karmaṇyadhikārastadīya iti ।</q> ākṣeptā āha---<q>evaṃ cet
svāmyapacāre ko'nyaḥ pratinidhatte ।</q> yadi svāmyevāpacaritaḥ kastarhi pratinidhi-
mupādatte । ekagranthenāha---<q>tadidaṃ bālajalpitamiva pratibhāti ।</q> samādhatte---
<q>astyatra pratinidherviṣayaḥ pat‍nīyajamānayoranyatarāpacāre'nyataraṃ pratinidhātuḥ
nīvāravat ।</q></p>
<p><q>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---adhikṛtayoḥ sahatvaṃ karmaṇi ।</q> pratyekamadhikṛtayoḥ
strīpuṃsayoḥ pratyekameva prayoge prāpte sahatvaṃ coditam । <q>tataḥ kiṃ ? idaṃ tato bhavati ।</q>﻿
<pb n="138"/>
adhikṛtaḥ karma kurvan yajamānākāratāmāpannaḥ । na karturadhikāra ityuktam ।</q>
adhikṛtasya sataḥ kartṛtvam tatrāyaṃ sahabhāva ityuktaṃ bhavati ।</p>
<p>codayati---<q>satyamevaṃ kārakamātravyāpāraḥ anyatagapekṣitaḥ ।</q> śakyate
ca kārakamātravyāpāro'nyenāpi saṃpādayitum । pariharati---<q>sahatvaṃ tābhyāma-
pekṣitam na sahitabhāvaḥ ।</q> adhikāravaśaprāpte'nuṣṭhāne sahatvamātramapekṣitaṃ, na
sahakartṛtvaṃ karmaṇaḥ । kasmāt sahabhāvo'pekṣito na sahitatvamiti atrāha---<q>netare-
tarayuktayoḥ kartṛtvaṃ kartṛtve ca sahabhāvaḥ ।</q> ekavacanaśravaṇāt netaretarayuktāḥ
kartāraḥ । kintu kartṛtva eva sahabhāvaḥ patnīyajamānayoḥ । tasmāt nādhikārādṛte
pratinidhānaṃ saṃbhavati । adhikārāyattaprayogasahatvasiddhaye pratinidhānamiti nādhikāra-
mantareṇa tatsiddhiḥ । adhikṛtaścenmukhya eva na pratinidhiḥ tasmādapratinidheyā svāmitā ।
so'yaṃ kāryabhūtasahaprayogāsapatteḥ na pratinidhiḥ । sahatvameva parityajya anuṣṭhānaṃ
kimiti na bhavatīti nāsyādhikaraṇasya viṣayaḥ । tathā'dhikṛtenāpariṇetrāpi sahatvamiti
strī na yajatītyapi ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 8 ।। bahunāṃ tu pravṛtte'nyamāgamayedavaiguṇyāt ।। 22 ।।</l></lg>
<p>satreṣvidānīṃ cintyate-<q>kiṃ kasyacidapacāre pratinidhāya satriṇaḥ prayogaṃ
parisamāpayanti uta neti ।</q> kasya citsvāmino'pacāre kiṃ svāminoḥ svāminaṃ
pratinidhāya satraṃ samāpayanti uta neti cintā । pūrvapakṣamāha-<q>na hyasvāmī yajamāno
bhavatītyuktamadhastāt । pratinidhīyamānaścāsau yathā na svāmī tathā
vakṣyāmaḥ । tasmādatrāpi pūrvavat pratinidhānābhāvāt</q> <quote>‘ye yajamānāsta
ṛtvija’</quote> iti vacanāt yajamānairevārtvijyaṃ karma kartavyam । svāmī ca yajamāno bhavati
yo hi phalabhāgī sa yajamāna ucyate । na cāsvāmī phalabhāgī । asvāmī cāyaṃ
pratinidhīyamāna iti uttarādhikaraṇe vakṣyate । tasmāt puruṣāntare'pi pratinidhīyamāne
tatkāryāsiddheḥ pūrvavadatrāpi pratinidherabhāvaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>atrocyate---atra hi sahitatvamapekṣyate na sahabhāvamātraṃ itaretara-
yuktānāṃ kartṛtvena śravaṇāt । ataḥ tatsiddha‍yarthaṃ itarakārakavat kartrantaraṃ
pratinidhātavyam ।</q> bahukartṛke karmaṇi ekaikasyādhikārāt kartṛtvamupādeyam ।
kathaṃ tarhi pratinivivācoyuktiḥ ? svāmisthāne nipātāt ।</p>﻿
<pb n="139"/>
<p>nanvevaṃ tarhi anadhikṛtamapyupādāya prayogaprārambhaḥ syāt । bhavatu na doṣaḥ
svāmini pravṛtte'pacārite puruṣāntaropādānamapi avaiguṇyānna‍yāyyamityucyate ।</p>
<p>nanvasvāmino yajamānatā nāsti । ayajamāne cānuṣṭhātari ārtvijyasyaiva
vaiguṇyaṃ syāt । ucyate । ye yajamānā iti pradhānakartṛtayaivārtvijyeṣu viniyogaḥ
[na]phalabhāgitaiva vivakṣitā । vākyabhedaprasaṅgāt । na cātmanepadāt tasyopādāna-
śeṣatā । yathānirjñātapradhānakartṛmātralābhena viśeṣaṇasyānapekṣitatvāt iti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 9 ।। sa svāmī syāt tatsaṃyogāt ।। 23 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nanu ca kartṛtvenopādānamityuktam । kathamatra svāmyāśaṅkā ?</q> yo
hyārabhya parisamāpayati sa phalabhāgī yaśca phalabhāgī sa svāmī । tena pratinidhīyamāna;
svāmī na bhavati iti kathaṃ svāmyāśaṅketi । samādhatte---<q>satyamuk‍taṃ, tathāpyāśaṅkā
kācidvidyata eva । adhikāramukhena kartṛtvamuktam । aiśvaryaṃ hi karmaṇi
pratītya kartṛtvaṃ bhajate puruṣaḥ । ato'nadhikṛtasya kartṛtā nopapadyata iti
pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</q> yadā'dhikṛtatvaṃ tadā kartṛtvaṃ, athānadhikṛtaḥ tarhi na kartṛtvamiti
bhāvaḥ ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntamāha---<q>satyaṃ, anadhikṛtasya kartatvaṃ nāsti । itaraiḥ punaḥ
kartṛtvamātramupādīyate saṅkhyāpūraṇāya । tasyāḥ karmaṇi śravaṇāt ।</q> ayamāśayaḥ-
adhikṛtakartṛtvamāpannaiḥ anadhikṛtasya sāmadānādibhiḥ śakyamāpādayituṃ, kartṛtvam ।
kartṛtvenetareṣāṃ prayojanam, tāvanmātreṇaiva saṅkhyāpūraṇāditi । tasmādārthakartṛtvamātra-
mevopādīyate śrautasyānupayogāt । ārthaṃ śrautamadhikṛtatvaṃm । tayorārthamevopādīyate ।
tasyaiva copayogāt । itarat śrautaṃ aupayogyeveti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 10 ।। sa taddharmā syāt karmasaṃyogāt ।। 26 ।।</l></lg>
<p>pūrvapakṣamāha---<q>yadyasau na svāmī sa kathaṃ svāmidharmeṇa saṃbaddha iti pūrvaḥ
pakṣaḥ ।</q> rāddhāntamāha---<q>bhavati saṃbandhaḥ । svāmino hi idamarthatayā''kṣiptaṃ
kartṛtvam । atastadarthāpatteḥ ।</q> kohi .... .... .... .... sūktam ।</p>
<p>asyārthaḥ---svāmyarthā ete saṃskārāḥ kartrādikāḥ pratipannāḥ । yaścāsāvekaḥ
kartā pratipannaḥ tasya sthāne bahavaḥ kartāraḥ pratītā iti । svāmināmaidamarthyena
svāmiṣvapi kartṛbhūteṣu taddharmatvamākṣipati । tasthānāpattyā taddharmā bhavantīti ।</p>﻿
<pb n="140"/>
<lg><l>।। 11 ।। sāmānyaṃ taccikīrṣā hi ।। 27 ।।</l></lg>
<p>pūrvapakṣamāha---<q>nanu ca śrutadravyāpacāre yathāśaktyanuṣṭhānaprāptau dravya-
mātropādānameva prāptam ।</q> na hi [sadṛśenāsadṛśenavā] (sadṛśasadṛśeṣā) samāptaukaści-
dviśeṣaḥ । rāddhāntamāha---<q>satyaṃ samāptau na viśeṣaḥ । upadeśatyāge tu
yāvatsaṃbhavaṃ nāsti pramāṇam</q> (apayāti) । <q>yāvatsu</q> upadeśalavo'pi labhyate
tad‌dravyamupādātavyam । jāterhi sādhanatā vyaktiparyantā । vyak‍terapi sādhanatā
avayavavyāpāraparyantā iti sādhanabhūtāvayavatyāge na kiñcit pramāṇamasti ।</p>
<p>nanu kāryasyobhayathāpi siddheḥ kimupadeśādareṇeti atrāha---<q>upadeśataḥ kāryā-
vagamāt</q> upadeśāvirodhena ca kāryata upādānaṃ kāryavido manyante । tasmātsūk‍taṃ
śrutasadṛśasyopādānamiti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 12 ।। nirdeśāttu vikalpe yatpravṛttam ।। 28 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>atra pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ---yāvacchrutasaṃbhavaḥ tattyāge pramāṇaṃ
nāstītyuktam । ato vaikalpikasyopādānameva nyāyyam ।</q> śrutasaṃpattyarthaṃ hi
sadṛśamupādīyate । yadapi tatsadṛśamupādīyate tat śrutasaṃpattyartham । śrutaṃ cenmukhyameva
saṃpadyate ko nāma gauṇīṃ sampadaṃ pratipadyate ।</p>
<p><q>atrābhidhīyate---prayogārthaṃ hi pratinidhānam । apacāre hi prati-
nidhiḥ । prayoge cāpacāraḥ । tasmāt prayogārthameva pratinidhānam । prayo-
gasya copāttamaṅgaṃ na śrutamātrameva ।</q> prayogasya hi śrute saṃbandhaḥ na prayogasya
anekaprayogasādhāraṇaṃ karma prayojyaṃ(karma) tatrānekaguṇasaṃbandho'pi yuktaḥ । kasmāt
prayogasya śrutamaṅgaṃ na bhavatītyatrāha---<q>śrutopādānamātrasādhyatvāt prayogasya
1ekaśrutopādānamātreṇa tasya siddheḥ anekaśrutasaṃbandhānupapattiḥ । prayoga-
saṃmpattyarthaścāyaṃ pratinidhiḥ na śrutasampattyarthaḥ ।</q> etaduk‍taṃ bhavati---na
śrutāvāgamasampattyartho bhavati । yadi hi tathā syāt tadā vaikalpikamapyupādīyeta ।
śrutānuṣṭhānasaṃmpatyartho hi saḥ । tasmādupāttasadṛśamevopādeyam, na vaikalpikaṃ tadānīṃ
tasyānaṅgatvāditi bhāvaḥ । abhāvavidhau hi pūrvaśrutābhāve paścācchrutamupādīyeta na
<note>1. etacchruto --- mā</note>﻿
<pb n="141"/>
tulyavidhau । yadi hi vrīhyabhāve yavānāṃ vidhiḥ syāt tadā vrīhyabhāve yavā
upādīyeran । na ca yavānāṃ vrīhyabhāve vidhiḥ । yavābhāve vā vrīhīṇām । kintu
tulyatayā yavā vrīhayaśca vihitāḥ ।</p>
<p>kasmātpunarabhāvavidhau paścācchrutasyopādānaṃ na tulyavidhau tatrāha---</p>
<p><q>prayogāpekṣo hi abhāvavidhirbhavati । prayoga evābhāvasambhavāt ।</q>
na prayojyate, abhāvānupapatteḥ nanu prayogasya prayojyādabhedāt prayojyārtho'pi prayogāṅga-
meva । tena prayojyāṅgabhūtasya vaikalpikasyāpi prayogāḍgatvamastyeveti tadupādānameva
yuktam । vikalpaśāstrārthāvāpteriti । anenāśayena pṛcchati---<q>kiṃ prayojyārthaḥ
prayogāṅgaṃ na bhavati ?</q> bhavatīti bhāvaḥ । uttaraṃ---<q>bhavati tu prayojyamukhena
netaravat prayogamukhena ।</q> yathā'bhāve vihitaṃ prayogamukhenaiva prayojyāṅgam । na
tathā vaikalpikam । kintu prayogaḥ prayojyasyaivāvasthāntaramiti prayojyāṅgaṃ prayogāṅgatāṃ
yati । tatra prayoge kṛtakṛtyatvāt dvitīyayopādānāt ekamevāṅgaṃ na sarvamiti
upāttasyaivāṅgatvāt tatsadṛśamevopādeyam । na vaikalpikam । prayoge tasyānaṅga-
tvāditi ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 13 ।। vacanāccānyāyyamabhāve tatsāmānyena pratinidhi-
rabhāvāditarasya ।। 31 ।।</l></lg>
<p>nanu abhāvidhipratinidhiniyamayoḥ na viśeṣamupalabhāmahe । tathāhi-abhāve
vidhirabhāvavidhiḥ । sa hi abhāve vidhiḥ upādānasāmarthyābhāve adhikāre ca līyamāne
kasyacitpratinidherupādānāprasakte'pi vidhiḥ na niyamaḥ । api tu vi(dhe)dhireva ।
yatra punaḥ aniyamenānekopādānasaṃbhave vidhānamekasya asau niyamavidhiḥupādāna-
sāmarthye satyadhikāre coditābhāve'nekapratinidhiprasaṅge'pi ekasya vidhiḥ niyama-
phalam । tatra saṃśaya upapadyate---kiṃ somopādānāsāmarthye etadvidhānaṃ utānekaprati-
nidhiprasaṅge niyama iti । <q>tatra pūrvapakṣavādī <quote>‘na vindet’</quote> iti asāmarthyamava-
gamyata iti manyate ।</q> na vindediti bhāvaḥ । ata idamavagamyate yadi somaṃ
labdhuṃ na śak‍nuyāditi । tena vedanasāmarthyaṃ nāstītyavagata ityuktam । na punarapacarita
ityetasmādavagamyate । ato'sāmarthyeṃ vidhirabhāve vidhireva ।</p>
<p><q>atrābhidhīyate । na śakyate'sāmarthyanirūpaṇam adravyavatkartuṃ na
vidyaḥ ko'sāvasamarthaṃ iti ।</q> yathā adravyādhikaraṇe uktam-avidyamānadravyasyāpi
<pb n="142"/>
dravyopādāne sāmarthyamasti iti । tathā anupāttasomasyāpi somalābhasāmarthyamastyeva ।
tena sāmarthyam । sarvapuruṣāṇāṃ sahajasāmarthyasaṃbhavāt saṃbhavati apacārābhāvāt ।
sa evāpacāro'nena vakṣyate । avedanena asāmarthyaphalatvāt abhāvasya, asāmarthyenā-
bhāvo lakṣyate । tasmāt sāmarthye'dhikāriṇaḥ somābhā(vaḥ)ve anekapratinidhau prasakte
niyamaḥ pūtīkānāmiti siddham ।</p>
<p>sthite'pyadravyādhikaraṇe sākṣācchabdenaiva asāmarthyoktitvāt asāmarthyasyāyaṃ
vidhiriti adhikāśaṅkā ।</p>
<p>asāmarthyābhāvāt lakṣaṇayā abhāva evārthādanena lakṣyata iti tannirākaraṇam ।
prayojanamuktam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 14 ।। na pratinidhau samatvāt ।। 32 ।।</l></lg>
<p>pūrvapakṣamāha---<q>kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ pratinidhisadṛśasya upādāne ?</q> mukhyo
gauṇaśca śāstrārtha iti bhrāntyā pratinidhisadṛśasyopādānamāha ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntamāha---<q>yasmānna pratinidhisampattyarthaḥ pratinidhiḥ kiṃ tarhi ?
śrutasampattyarthaḥ ।</q> śrutamevopādātukāmaḥ pratinighimupādatte tadupādāne'pi śrutaleśa-
lābhāt । tadarthaścet śrutasampattyarthaścet pratinidhiḥ tatsadṛśameva śrutasadṛśameva
dravyāntaramupādeyam । tasminnupādīyamāne śrutaikadeśānugrahāditi yuktam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 15 ।। syācchrutilakṣaṇe niyatatvāt ।। 33 ।।</l></lg>
<p>nanvabhāvavidhinirākaraṇatyedaṃ prayojanaṃ yatpūtīkāpacāre'pi somasadṛśamevopā-
deyamiti1 kimarthamidamadhikaraṇamārabhyata ityāśaṅkyāha---<q>yatprayojanamuktaṃ tade-
vedamākṣipyate</q> pūrvapakṣe yatra pratinidhiniyamaḥ śrūyate tenārabdhakarmaṇyapacarite(ka)[ta]-
sminniyam evādartavyaḥ । sa hi tatra śrutaḥ śrutasampattyarthaśca pratinidhiḥ ityuktam ।
<q>yatra punararthāt pratinidhānaṃ tatra śrutadravyasadṛśameveti yuktam, arthasyātrā(ta)-
sattvāt</q> ।</p>
<note>1. anupādeyaḥ - mā</note>﻿
