<pb n="143"/>
<p>ayamāśayaḥ---sarve hi dravyavighayo niyamārthā eva । tena somābhāve
vihitatvāt pūtīkasya tadapacāre tatsadṛśamevopādātavyam । somāpacāre tatsadṛśa-
miveti । evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---</p>
<p><q>yatrāpi pratinidhiniyamaḥ śrūyate tatrāpi na dravyasyāyaṃ niyamaḥ ।</q>
pūtīkasvarūpasyāpyayaṃ niyamaḥ । kintu tadgatā hi ye śrutadravyasadṛśāḥ śrutadravya-
sādhāraṇā avayavāḥ ta eva niyamyante । anyathā hi pūtīkasvarūpavidhiḥ syāt na
pratinidhiniyamaḥ aprasaktatvāt pūtīkasvarūpa(syā)grahaṇasya । pratinidhiniyamaścāyaṃ
pratipāditaḥ apekṣitavidhoḥ । yato'yaṃ pratinidhiniyamaḥ ato'trāpi arthena tulyaṃ
mukhyasadṛśamevopādātavyam । evaṃ tvatra nyāyyam---mukhyasadṛśamapi tadevopādātavyaṃ
yatra pūtīkasādhāraṇāḥ somāvayavā vidyante, na punaryatra pūtīkasadṛśāḥ somāvayavā
vidyante tadupādeyam । somāpacāre teṣāṃ niyatatvāt । tatsomāvayavasadṛśaṃ ca
pūtīkasadṛśaṃ copādeyamiti ।</p>
<p>atra cādhikaraṇe anapekṣitasādṛśyāḥ pūtīkā vidyanta iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
apekṣitavidhānāt tadgatāvayavā eva niyamyanta iti rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 16 ।। mukhyādhigame mukhyāmāgamo hi tadabhāvāt ।। 35 ।।</l></lg>
<p>yatra pratinidhiḥ prakṛtaḥ tatrottarādhikaraṇena mukhyasyāṅgīkāro vakṣyate । yatra ca
pratinidhyupādānaṃ na saṅkalpitaṃ tatra pūrvapakṣābhāvādanārabhyamevādhikaraṇamiti matvā''ha---</p>
<p><q>śrute dravye'pacarite pratinidhānārthaṃ pravṛttasya yadā mukhyādhigamo
bhavati tadā kiṃ mukhya evopādātavyaḥ uta pratinidhiriti</q> pratinidhisaṅka-
lpanāt pūrvapakṣavādī pratinidhirupādātavya ityarthaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>atrocyate</q> । satyamasau saṅkalpaḥ । kintvasāvakratvarthaḥ । yadyapi nīvārāssaṅka-
lpitāḥ tathāpi tattyāge'nṛtavaṃdanapratiṣedhātikramo nāsti । kratvarthaviṣayasaṅkalpatyāge
sa doṣaḥ । na ca nīvārasaṅkalpaḥ kratvarthaḥ nīvārāṇāmakratvarthatvāt । śrautasadṛśamātraṃ hi
tatra kratvarthatvām śrutairdravyairvrīhibhiḥ sādhāraṇā ye'vayavāḥ te tatra kratvarthāḥ na punaḥ
pratinidhidravyam । te ca mukhye upādīyamāne upāttā bhavanti । tena mukhyamevo-
pādeyam । vaikalpikānāṃ punaḥ vrīhyādīnāṃ śrutaviṣayatvāt saṅkalpasyāsāvapi kratvarthaḥ
iti kiṃ tatparityāge anṛtavadanapratiṣevātikramadoṣa iti yukto niyamaḥ ।</p>﻿
<pb n="144"/>
<p>yat(m‍/?/)saṅkalpitaṃ(ḥ)tadevopādātavyamiti sthite'dhikaraṇe duṣṭāśayaḥ pṛcchati-</p>
<p><q>kiṃ punaratra puruṣārthatvena mithyāsaṅkalpanā bhavet । śiṣṭāḥ svalvatra
pramāṇam</q> । yadi śiṣṭā īdṛśe viṣaye mithyāsaṅkalpadoṣaṃ smaranti । bhavatu mithyā-
saṅkalpadoṣaḥ puruṣasya tathāpi kratau mukhyamevopādātavyamiti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 17 ।। pravṛttepīti cet ।। 36 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>pravṛtte punaḥ karmaṇi pratinidhinā śrutadravyopalabdhau kiṃ śrutamevopādā-
tavyaṃ uta pratinidhinaiva samāptiriti</q> pratinidhau keṣucitsaṃskāreṣu pravṛtteṣucintā ।</p>
<p>atra pūrvapakṣavādī pratinidheḥ śrutasampattyarthatvāt tadevopādātavyamiti manyate
yathā pūrvādhikaraṇe ।</p>
<p>nanvatra kecana saṃskārāḥ kṛtāḥ punaḥ kartuṃ na śakyante । tena tadanugrahāya
pratinidhinaiva samāptiriti । nāyaṃ doṣaḥ । saṃskārāṇāṃ pradhānārthatvāt pradhānaṃ ca
prayogasampattaye । tena pradhānaṃ dravyamevādaraṇīyam । saṃskārāstu nīyantāmiti bhāvaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---upādānepyetaccintyate nopātte ।</q></p>
<p>upādānasamaya evedaṃ cintyate kiṃ śrutaṃ na iti । nopātte । tatra ca yathā-
viniyogamupādānamiti viniyogānurodhena śrutamevopādīyate । yatropādīyate yatro-
pādānasamaye viniyuktaṃ na labhyate tata upādātavye kimapyupādīyate । upātte ca
tasmin punarupādānāntarāsaṃbhavāt tenaiva prayogassaṃmpādanīyaḥ । upāttena prayoganirvṛttau
śrutamapyaśrutameva kṛtārthatvācchās‍trasya upādānaṃ hi śās‍trasya prayojanam । tacca
kṛtamiti । tasmāt pratinidhinaiva sampādayitavyamiti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 18 ।। dravyasaṃskāravirodhe dravyaṃ tadarthatvāt ।। 37 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>saṃskārakṣame pratinidhau mukhye cākṣame saṃskārāṇāṃ kasyopādānaṃ yukta-
miti । saṃskārāṇāṃ śravaṇāt saṃskārakṣamamupādeyaṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī</q>
pratinidhāvupātte dravyaśāstrārtho'pi anugṛhīto bhavati kevalaṃ vikalatvamātraṃ tasya । mukhye
upātte śrutasaṃskāratyāga eva1 tena saṃskāraśravaṇāt pratinidhirevopādātavya iti ।</p>
<note>1. tena na - mā</note>﻿
<pb n="145"/>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu---satyaṃ saṃskāraśravaṇaṃ kintu śrutasya saṃskāraśravaṇam ।
śrutābhāve punaḥ na ca saṃskārāḥ । śrutadravyāśritā hi saṃskārāḥ kratoraṅgam
tadabhāve teṣāmanaṅgataiva syāt । tasmāt śrutadravyamupādadataḥ yadi nāma
saṃskārā na bhavanti na bhavantu nāma tadabhāve'pi pradhānārthopapatteḥ ।</q> na hi
saṃskāro dravyasya dvāram । tena saṃskārābhāvepi dravyaśāstrārtho niṣpadyate । dravyābhāve
punaḥ na saṃskāraśāstrārthopapattiriti śrutasyaivopādānam । upādadatirūpasiddhau yat‍naḥ
kartavyaḥ, <quote>‘‘āṅodonāsya viharaṇe’’</quote> (pā. sū 1-3-20) ityātmanepadaprāpteḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 19 ।। arthadravyavirodhe'rtho dravyābhāve tadutpatterdravyāṇā-
marthaśeṣatvāt ।। 39 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nanu yatra punaḥ prayojanameva śrutena nopapadyate । tatra śrutamapyaśrutameva
prayojanārthatvācchrutasya</q> । ataḥ prayojanasiddhyarthaṃ samarthasyaivopādānamatreti pūrvādhi-
karaṇasya pratyudāharaṇamātrametat ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 20 ।। vidhirapyekadeśe syāt ।। 40 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nanu ca saṃskārābhāve'pi pradhānamupādātavyamityanenaitadgatam । kima-
bhyadhikamatra cintyate ।</q></p>
<p>asyārthaḥ - śeṣakāryāṇi dravyapratipattyarthāni dravyaṃ prati guṇabhūtāni । tena
tadabhāve'pi dravyamevopādātavyamiti । uttaraṃ---<q>idamabhyadhikam - puroḍāśasyā-
vadānaśrutayo bhavanti । na ca pradhanāmātrasaṃbhave puroḍāśatvopapattiriti
niyataparimāṇatvāt puroḍāśasya ।</q> asyārthaḥ - pūrvārdhādavadyatītyavadānaṃ puroḍāśe
śrutam । na ca dva‍yavadānamātraṃ puroḍāśo bhavati niyataparimāṇābhivyaṅga‍yatvāt puroḍā-
śākṛteḥ । tena puroḍāśe asamarthatayā nīvārā evopādātavyāḥ । puroḍāśānurodhena
vrīhīṇāṃ tyāgo yukta iti । tasmānnīvārāṇāmevopādānam । puroḍāśānurodhena vrīhīṇāṃ
tyāgo yukta iti । tasmānnīvārāṇāmevopādānaṃ pūrvapakṣavādī manyate ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhantastu satyaṃ puroḍāśasyāvadānaṃ, na punastat puroḍāśārtham ।
kiṃ tarhi ? kratvartham ।</q> puroḍāśo dva‍yavadānaṃ prati guṇībhūta eva nāpekṣyate ।
<pb n="146"/>
nanu bhavatu dvyavadānaṃ prati puroḍāśasya guṇabhāvaḥ vrīhīn prati pradhāna[bhāva] eva ।
vrīhayo'pi puroḍāśanirvṛttyarthāḥ । puroḍāśāstu dvyavadānārthāḥ । tena pradhānabhūta-
puroḍāśānugrahāya guṇabhūtānāṃ vrīhīṇāṃ tyāgo yukta iti ।</p>
<p>ucyate । puroḍāśaprakṛtidravyatayā'ṅgabhūtā vrīhyādayaḥ sākṣāt dva‍yavadāne
saṃbadhyante । tanmayatvāttasya । tena bahiraṅgatvāt puroḍaśasyaiva tyāgaḥ antaratvāṅga-
hvrīhīṇāmanugraha iti yuktaḥ । ataḥ puroḍāśo'pi yatra guṇabhūta iti yāvat
nāpekṣya(kṣa)te [tatra] kiṃ punaḥ śeṣakāryāṇyaprayojakāni । tasmāt pradhānamātra-
nirvṛtyarthā vrīhaya evopādātavyā iti । <q>darśanamuktam ।</q></p>
<p><q>iti ṛjuvimalāyāṃ ṣaṣṭhādhyāyasya</q></p>
<p><q>tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ</q></p>﻿
<pb n="147"/>
<p><q>ṛjuvimalāyāṃ</q></p>
<p><q>।। ṣaṣṭhādhyāsya caturthaḥ pādaḥ ।।</q></p>
<lg><l>।। 1 ।। 1śeṣād‌dvyavadānanāśe syāttadarthatvāt ।। 7 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nanu yasya havīṃṣi naśyeyuḥ ityādike vacane avadānanāśe dravyāntara-
vidhānārthe sati rpūvapakṣāśaṅkābhāvāt kathamidamadhikaraṇamārabdham ।</p>
<p>samādhatte-<q>asatyapi vacane nyāyādayamartho labhyata iti pradarśayitum</q> ।
vacanavyatirekeṇa hi dravyāntaramāgamayitavyam, na śeṣādavadeyamityayamartho nyāyenaiva
labhyate । tena caikasya dravyasya pūrvārdhaṃdvayaṃ vā saṃbhavatīti darśayitumidamadhikaraṇamārabdham ।</p>
<p><q>yadi nyāyenaivāyamartho labhyate vacanamidānīṃ kimartham ?</q> uttaraṃ---
<q>dravyaviśeṣādhānārthamiti brūmaḥ ।</q> nyāyataḥ puroḍāśāntarāgame prāpte dravyaviśeṣa-
syājyasya lakṣaṇayā aprāptasya vidhānārtham । yadi vacanametat nyāyata eva dravyāntarāgame
prāpte dravyaviśeṣavidhānārthaṃ <q>evaṃ tarhi <quote>‘nirdeśāt’</quote> iti sūtraṃ</q> (6-4-2)
<q><quote>‘yasya havīṃṣi’</quote> ityetannirdeśābhiprāyeṇa kathaṃ vyākhyātam</q> । na hyanena vacanena
dravyāntarāgamo nirdiśyate ।</p>
<p>samādhatte - <q>dravyaviśeṣavidhānaṃ tu śeṣāditi jñāpanārtham</q> । asyārthaḥ-
yadyapyetat dravyaviśeṣavidhānārtham tathāpi(vi)śeṣā(ṇā)nnāvadeyamiti jñāpayati । evaṃ
dravyāntaravidhānādeva । tena pūrvapakṣanirākaraṇārthametaduk‍tamiti bhāvaḥ । śeṣanirdeśastu
pratyukto bhāṣye śeṣakāryāṇāmaprayojakatvānna tadanurodhena dravyāntaramupādeyamiti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 2 ।। api vā śeṣabhājāṃ syādviśiṣṭakāraṇatvāt ।। 3 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>kathaṃ punaratra pūrvapakṣāśaṅkā śeṣādeva punaravadeyamiti । na hi
śeṣakāryāṇi dravyaṃ prayuñ‍jate</q> । yadi hi dravyaṃ prayuñjīran tadā tairdravyasya prayukta-
tvāt tadakaraṇe dravyopādānavaiyarthyāt punaravadānaṃ syāt । na caitadasti । samādhatte-
<q>sthita evāprayojakatve pratipattīnāmiyamāśaṅkā avirataśśās‍trārthaḥ śeṣasya
<note>1. 1429</note>﻿
<pb n="148"/>
vidyamānatvāditi</q> । na punaḥ prayojakatvamāśaṅkyate । pradhāne(tu tena)hute śeṣaḥ
sviṣṭakṛdādibhiḥ pratipādyata iti śrutam । tasya śās‍trārthasyāviratireva । tena
punaravadeyamiti ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu kāryārthatvācchās‍trāṇāṃ śās‍trārthānāṃ kṛtatvācca kāryasya
nānupapattiḥ śakyate vak‍tum</q> ।</p>
<p>yadyapi śeṣaśrutiraviśiṣṭā tathāpi kāryārthamanuṣṭhānaṃ dravyapratipattiḥ sviṣṭakṛdādīnāṃ
prayojanam । yacca dravyaṃ sviṣṭakṛdādibhiḥ pratipādyaṃ tat(da)vinaṣṭam tena pratipādya-
dravyābhāvāduparataḥ śās‍trārthaḥ । yadi paraṃ śeṣakāryāṇāṃ prayok‍tṛtvāt punaḥ karaṇaṃ tacca
nāstītyuktam । pratipattyantaravidhānācca punaradānaṃ na kartavyamiti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 3 ।। 1nirdeśāccheṣabhakṣo'nyaiḥ pradhānavat ।। 4 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>keyamadhikāre cintā kathaṃ vā nāsti ?</q></p>
<p>uttaraṃ - <q>śeṣacinteyaṃ ke bhakṣayitāra iti na punaḥ kasyādhikāra iti ।</q></p>
<p>samādhatte---<q>atrocyate - adhikāracintaiveyam । kāryaviniyuktakartṛ-
mato'dhikāraḥ utāviniyuktakartṛkasyāpīti</q> । etaduktaṃ bhavati - yajamānasyai-
vādhikāraḥ cintyate । kiṃ[ye]viniyuktā ṛtvijaḥ tadyuktasyaivādhikāraḥ uta kartrantara-
yuktasyāpīti ।</p>
<p><q>pūrvapakṣavādī tu aś‍vamedhādiṣvaśakteriti iḍāyāṃ na viniyuktakartṛ-
niyamādaviniyuktakartṛkasyāpyadhikāra iti manyate ।</q></p>
<p>asyārthaḥ-yadi viniyuktakartṛkasyaivāyamadhikāraḥ tadā'śvamedhe śeṣabhakṣaṇasyā-
śakyatvāt anadhikāra eva syāt । tathā <quote>‘yajamānapañcamā iḍāṃ bhakṣayanti’</quote> iti
vacanaṃ ṛtvijāmiḍābhakṣaṇe niyamārthaṃ <quote>‘iḍaiva taireva bhakṣayitavyā’</quote> iti । taccaivamupa-
padyate yadi vacanāntareṇānyasyāpi bhakṣaṇaṃ prasajyate । na ca tadvacanaṃ yajamānaprāptyarthaṃ,
tasyāpi kartṛtvena prāptatvāditi na punaḥ viniyuktavyatiriktānāṃ viniyoga iti
śakyate vak‍tum śrutyādīnāmabhāvāt ।</p>
<note>1. 1431</note>﻿
<pb n="149"/>
<p>[aviniyuktakartṛkasyāpyadhikāra iti śakyate vak‍tuṃ na punaraprakṛtānāṃ
viniyoga iti tadviniyoge śrutyādīnāmabhāva iti]</p>
<p><q>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---viniyuktakartṛkasyaivādhikāra iti । kutaḥ ?
na hyaśrutenādhikāraḥ śakyate vak‍tum । śrutaviṣayatvādadhikārāṇām</q> । yādṛśo
viṣayaḥ śrūyate tadanurūpo'dhikāro varṇanīyaḥ । ṛtvijāṃ ca karmakaratvenopādānāt
tatkartṛkabhakṣayukto viṣayaḥ pratīyata iti tadyuktasyaivādhikāraḥ ।</p>
<p><q>yatpunarvacanaṃ tatprāptyarthaṃ</q> karmakaratvena ṛtvijāmupāttatvāt bhakṣo'pi taireva
prāpto na yajamānena, tatprāptyarthaṃ vacanamupapadyata iti darśitam । <q>aśvamedhe punaḥ
tadvadevādhikāraḥ kāryārthaḥ punaranyopādānamiti nādhikārāntaraṃ prayuñ‍jīta ।
aṣi hi viniyuktakartṛkameva kāryamiti śabdādavagamyate</q> ।</p>
<p>etaduktaṃ bhavati-[vini]yuktasyādhikāraḥ tathāpi tāvanmātreṇaiva kāryasāmarthyāt
na sahāyatvenāprakṛtānāmupādānāditi ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 4 ।। arthasamavāyāt prāyaścittamekadeśe'pi ।। 10 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>ihaitāvacchrūyate <quote>‘bhinne juhoti’</quote> na punaḥ kṛts‍nabhinne ekadeśabhinne
vā iti । tatra saṃśayaḥ kiṃ bhinnasyaivayaḥ saṃskāraḥ uta bhedenāpagato'dhi-
kāra iti</q> । anena bhāṣyakārīyasya sandehasya karaṇe saṃdehaḥ kṛtaḥ । nanu ya[dya]tra
bhedanavato'dhikāraḥ tadā adhikārāntaratve sati darśapūrṇamāsāṅgatā na syāt । tataśca
prakaraṇabādha iti adhikṛtādhikārādaṅgatvasiddhiḥ ।</p>
<p>pūrvapakṣamākṣipati---<q>atrocyate - bhedanavato homaścodyate <quote>‘tasmāt bhinne
juhoti’</quote> iti</q> । bhedanamātramatra śrūyate na punaḥ parityaktasāmarthyasya aparityaktasāmarthyasya
vā bhedanavat iti viśeṣo'vagamyate । aviśeṣe ca parityaktasāmarthyasya saṃskārānupa-
patteḥ bhinnasaṃskārakatve niraste bhedavato homaścodyata iti vadāmaḥ ।</p>
<p>samādhatte --- <q>pūrvapakṣavādī tu kāryata eva viśeṣo'vagamyata iti manvānaḥ
samarthasaṃskāraṃ manyate । evamārādupakārakakalpanā ca kṛtā bhavati ।
adhikaraṇāśaṅkānivṛttiśca na vaktavyā bhavati</q> । ayamāśayaḥ-sannipatyopakārā-
dārādupakāratāṅgasaṃśaye sati sannipatyopakārāśrayaṇaṃ nyāyyam । antaraṅgatvāt ।
<pb n="150"/>
tena homasyāpi bhinnasaṃskāratvena sannipatyopakārakatvāśrayaṇaṃ nyāyyam । na ca
paratyaktasāmarthyaṃ saṃskāramarhatīti kāryaparyālocanayā parityaktasāmarthyaṃ bhinnaṃ pratīyate ।
saptamī tviyaṃ agāre gāvo vāsyantāmiti ca draṣṭavyā । tenādhikaraṇabhūtasyaiva
saṃskārāt tannivṛttirapi vaktavyā na bhavati । rāddhāntamāha---<q>atrocyate-satyamevaṃ,
kintu atra saptamīnirdeśāt na karmabhāvo bhinnasya</q> । na hi karmabhāve saptamī
bhavati । yattu <quote>‘agāre gāvo badhyantāṃ’</quote> iti tat pramāṇāntaratastathāvagamāt ।
atra tu na tathā । kintarhi nimittabhāva eva saptamīyam tena bhinnasya nimittatā ।
yuktyantaraṃ cāha---<q>saṃskāryatve ca na nityasaṃskārasya aṅgabhāvaḥ śakyate
pratipattum bhinnasyānityatvāt</q> । homastāvat nityamaṅgam । tadanurūpaṃ ca
ca dvāramāśrayaṇīyam । yadi ca bhinnasaṃskāro dvāraṃ syāt tadā bhodanasyānityatvāt
tatsamādhānadvāro homo'pi na nityaḥ syāt । atasso'yamananvayī śāstrārthaḥ syāt ।
nimittabhāve evam । nāyaṃ doṣaḥ । nityānityasaṃyogalakṣaṇo doṣo na bhavati sati
nimitte tvaṅgatvāvagamāt naimittikamevāṅgam na punaḥ saṃskārapakṣe nimitte'sati aṅga-
homa iti śakyate vak‍tum । na ca nimittamadhikāriṇāṃ mate upapadyata iti darśitam ।
tena bhedavato homaścānyata iti ।</p>
<p>codayati---<q>atha kasmādadhikaraṇasaptamyeveyaṃ na bhavati ।</q> uttaraṃ---<q>na
bhavati āhavanīyabādhaprasaṅgāt</q> ।</p>
<p>sarvahomeṣvāhavanīya[sya] prāptatvāt bhavatu bādha eveti cet tatrāha---<q>anyathā
vopapatteḥ</q> nimitte saptamī(te) tvenāpyupapattau na bādhaḥ śakyate vak‍tum । <q>atha
kasmānnimittanaimittikasaṃbandha eva na cocyate kimadhikāriviśeṣaṇena bheda-
nimittamiti</q> । etāvadeva kimiti pradhānahoma eva na jñāpyate kimityaparaṃ
homāntaramāśrīyate tatra ca bhedanamadhikāriviśeṣaṇamiti ।</p>
<p>uttaraṃ---<q>siddhaviṣayo hi saṃbhavati । na ca siddhaviṣaye vedasya pramāṇya-
mastītyukte bhavati</q> । yadi vede'pi siddhānuśāsanaṃ syāt tadā nimittanaimittika-
bhāvamātre vākyaṃ paryavasyet । na caitadasti anuṣṭhānopadeśakatvāditi homānuṣṭhāna-
vidhireva । homānuṣṭhāne cādhikāriviśeṣaṇasyaiva nimittatvamityaktam । tasmādbhedanavato
homaścodyata iti siddham । <q>śeṣamuktam</q></p>
<lg><l>।। 5 ।। kṣāme tu sarvadāhe syādekadeśasyāvarjanīyatvāt ।। 17 ।।</l></lg>
﻿<pb n="151"/>
<p>darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ śrūyate---atha yasya puroḍāśau kṣāyataḥ taṃ yajñaṃ varuṇo
gṛhṇāti । yadā taddhaviṣkaṃ karma santiṣṭhate atha tadeva havirnirvapet yajño yajñasya
prāyaścittiriti । tatrāyamarthaḥ-yasya yajñasya puroḍāśau kṣāyataḥ taṃ yajñaṃ varuṇo gṛhṇāti
yadā taddhaviṣkaṃ karma santiṣṭhate tadā tadeva haviḥ punarnirvaptavyamiti । yasya puroḍāśau
kṣāyata iti pūrvādhikaraṇanyāyena kṛts‍ne caikadeśe ca kṣāme nimittasya haviḥkṣāṇa-
lakṣaṇasya vidyamānatvāt । yasya puroḍāśau kṣāyata iti vacanavihitena naimittikena
bhavitavyamiti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । yadi kṣāmasaṃskārārthametat tadā ekadeśakṣāma eva
prāyaścittaṃ syāt na kṛtsnakṣāme । kṛtsnakṣāme'pi nimittasaṃbhavāttatrāpi yuktameva । na
ca kṛts‍nekṣāme ityapi viśeṣaḥ śrūyate । [ataḥ] ubhayasminnapi kṣāme prāyaścittaṃ
yuktam । taddhaviḥ [saṃsthā] vyapadeśo nirviṣaya evaitatsyāt (?) । <q>nanvevamapyeka-
deśakṣāma eva prāyaścittaṃ syāt । śabdaścaivamupapanno bhavati । yadi hi
akṛtsnakṣāme etadvacanaṃ syāt tadā taddhaviḥ santiṣṭhata iti saṃbhavati</q> ।
ayamarthaḥ-sarvadāhe tu dagdhe haviḥ saṃsthānānupapatteḥ taddhavirvyapadeśo na ghaṭate sarvadāhe
tu havirantaramupādāya prayoge kriyamāṇe taddhavirvyapadeśo nirviṣaya eva syāt ।</p>
<p>nanvaivamapi ekadeśadāha eva prāyaścittaṃ syāt na kṛts‍nadāhe । na hi tadā
taddhavirvyapadeśo ghaṭata iti । satyam । tata haviḥ yasya taddhaviḥ iti vyapadeśaḥ
ekadeśadāha evopapadyate । tathāpi ārtyadhikaraṇanyāyena yajñasaṃsthaiva nimittaṃ na punaḥ
tena haviṣā saṃsthānaṃ nimittaṃ, tenānyena [a]dahatāpi haviṣā kriyamāṇe naimittikaṃ
yuktameveti । kintu yadi sarvadāha evaitadvacanaṃ syāt tadā taddhaviḥ śabdāt
prāyaścittamityuktaṃ tadanvāruhyavādamātram ।</p>
<p>evaṃ prāpti'bhidhīyate---<q>aparihāryatvādekadeśakṣāṇasya sarvakṣāṇanimittaṃ
prāyaścittamiti yuktam</q> yasya puroḍāśau kṣāyata iti viśeṣavacanaṃ sarvadāha evopa-
padyate eka deśadāhe tu sarvasya saṃbhavāt viśeṣavacanaṃ nopapadyate । tasmāt kṛts‍nakṣāṇa-
prāyaścittamiti ।</p>
<p>atra codayati---<q>yāvatpākaṃ hi yā kṣāṇatā sā bhavatvaparihāryā
pākānaupayikī tu yā kṣāṇatā sā kimiti nimittaṃ na bhavati</q> । yāvatyā
kṣāmatayā vinā na pāka eva niṣpadyate tāvatī kṣāmatā'vaśyaṃbhāvinī mābhūnnimittam ।
yayā vināpi pāko bhavati tāvatī kādācitkā nimittamastu । sa caikadeśakṣāme'pi
<pb n="152"/>
saṃbhavati । laukikā api hi anīpsite pākānaupayike dāhe kṣāmaśabdaṃ prayuñjate
dagdho guḻaḥ dagdha odana iti । tenānīpsitaṃ pākānaupayikaṃ kṣāṇamiti ।</p>
<p>pariharati---[satyaṃ] <q>yathā bhavānāha, anīpsitaṃ pākānaupayikaṃ kṣāṇa-
mabhipretamiti । tadeva na jñāyate kiyadīpsitamiti</q> । tena īpsitapākā-
naupayikatvena viśeṣo jñātuṃ na śakyate । ākṣeptā āha---<q>kimiti na jñāyate ।
puroḍāśasiddhirapekṣitā । yāvatā pākena puroḍāśaḥ siddha‍yati tāvān pāka
īpsitaḥ</q> ।</p>
<p>samādhātā āha---<q>satyaṃ puroḍāśasiddhirīpsitā saiva tu na jñāyate
kiyatā kṣāṇena tu sidhyati kiyadanupayogīti</q> । ayamāśayaḥ - yāvatā pākena
puroḍāśaḥ siddha‍yati tāvānīpsitaḥ (tāvatānīpsitaṃ) tena yāvāneva puroḍāśasiddhi-
vighātakārī pākaḥ tāvānevānīpsitaḥ । sa ca sarvadāha eva । tāvatā hi puroḍāśa-
buddhirapaiti । laikike punaḥ loka eva pramāṇaṃ īpsitānīpsitatve । tatra niyamo
nāsti pratipuruṣamīpsitabhedāt । tasmāt suṣṭhūcyate---<q>aparihāryatvādekadeśa-
kṣāṇasya sarvakṣāṇa eva prāyaścittamiti</q> । tacchabdaparihārastūktaḥ anyenāpi-
haviṣā saṃsthāpyamānaṃ karma taddhaviśśabdena lakṣayituṃ śakyata iti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 6 ।। 1yathāśrutīti cet ।। 22 ।।</l></lg>
<p>nanu coddiśyamānasya viśeṣaṇamavivakṣitamiti grahādhikaraṇe uktam ।
tenaivādhikāriṇo'pi viśeṣaṇamavivakṣitamityuktam । tena punaruktatvādanā-
rabhyamevādhikaraṇam ।</p>
<p>pariharati---<q>satyaṃ kena voktaṃ na pratipāditamiti । yadi pratipāditaṃ
kiṃ tarhi anenedaṃ anena kimadhikriyamāṇaviśeṣaṇaṃ vivakṣyate neti
cintyate</q> । asyārthaḥ---uddiśyamānasya viśeṣaṇamavivakṣitamiti tatroktam ।
iha tu adhikriyamāṇasya viśeṣaṇamavivakṣitamiti pratipādyate । tena nāsti
paunaruktyamiti bhāvaḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu uddiśyamānaviśeṣaṇavivakṣābhidhāne nedamupalabhyata iti atrāha---
<note>1. 1438</note>﻿
<pb n="153"/>
<p><q>nacādhikāryuddiśyate । kiṃ tarhi karmaṇyadhikriyate । anyā adhi-
kāritā anyā coddiśyamānateti manyate</q> । vidheyasya viṣayatāpattiruddheśyatvaṃ,
karmaṇi svāmitvamadhikriyamāṇatvam । tena yatra vidheyārthatvenoddiśyate tadgatā sā
cintā । atra tu niyojyagatā cinteti viśeṣaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>atra pūrvapakṣavādī padadvayaviśiṣṭāmārtiṃ adhikriyamāṇaviśeṣaṇatayā
manvānaḥ padadvayaviśiṣṭārtiṃ nimittamityāha---yasyobhayaṃ havirārtimārcche-
diti</q> । ākhyātenārtirucyate । sā ca havirubhayapadābhyāṃ yugapat viśeṣyate
kraya ivāruṇaikahāyanībhyām । (te)viśiṣṭā cāsau puruṣaviśeṣaṇamiti । ubhayaviśeṣaṇa-
viśiṣṭā ārtiḥ nimittam । ṛcchatiśca dhātuḥ āṅpūrvaḥ ārtau vartate ārtiśabdo'pi
ktinnantaḥ tasmādeva vyutpādyate । upasargādṛti dhātau (pā. sū 6-1-11) iti
vṛddhau kṛtāyāṃ raparatve ca rāllope ilope; ārtimārcchediti tu yaducyate tadā odana-
pākaṃ pacatītivat draṣṭavyam । <q>rāddhāntavādī tu satyaṃ, sarvaviśeṣaṇaviśiṣṭo'dhi-
kārī gamyate । na punarekapadībhūtaiḥ viśeṣaṇaiḥ viśeṣyate samāsābhāvāt
ekapadībhūtāni etāni na bhavanti । tataḥ kiṃ ? idaṃ tato bhavati adhi-
kriyamāṇaviśeṣaṇaṃ hi phalatayā nimittatayā vā gamyate । na karmaṇaḥ
punaḥ punaḥ svaviśeṣaṇatayā</q> svasyātmanaḥ yā viśeṣaṇatā tayā nāvagamyate ।
viśeṣaṇamātramāha---<q>paryavasāyī na bhavatīti</q> । kintu karmaṇaḥ phalatvena
nimittatvena vā'vatiṣṭhate । taccedānīṃ phalaṃ vā nimittaṃ vā । yathaivādhi-
kṛtaviśeṣaṇatayā'vagataṃ tathaiva bhavitumarhati । svapadārthaprayuktaṃ ca viśeṣaṇatayāvagataṃ
na tatkāryādṛte śakyata ekīkartum । svakīye padārthe ca prayuktaṃ padajātaṃ adhikāri-
viśeṣaṇatayā'vagataṃ na śakyate kāryādṛte upādeyādṛte ekī kartum । yathā kraya upā-
deyatvena coditaḥ ekībhūtaviśeṣaṇaviśiṣṭo'vagamyate । na tathehāvagantuṃ śakyate
anupādeyatvādārteḥ । na cedaṃ kāryaṃ nimittaparyantatvādasyādhikārasya । na ca nimitta-
mupādeyaṃ bhavati । ato nedaṃ parasparasaṃbandhanimittatvenopādātuṃ śakyate । ekaṃ
cedaṃ vākyam । <q>tasmādanyataradatra nimittatvena pratipattavyam । nobhayam</q> ।
havirārtirnimittaṃ nobhayaṃ viśeṣyatvāddhaviṣaḥ । ānantaryācca । tena haviṣi
ārte nimitte ubhayapadamanuvādaḥ---<q>yadyekapadībhāvāvagamābhāvāt ubhayatva-
viśiṣṭaṃ havirnimittaṃ tadā kiṃ havireva nimittaṃ</q> ? uttaraṃ---<q>na ārtiviṣayabhūta-
miti brūmaḥ</q> ।</p>
﻿<pb n="154"/>
<p>nanu ca ārtirapi naiva haviṣā ekapadībhūtā kathaṃ tadviṣayabhūtasya viśeṣaṇatā ।
naiṣa doṣaḥ । bhāvāśrayatvānnāmnaḥ । na haviḥ[ṣaḥ] puruṣeṇa saṃbandhaḥ । abhāvārthānāṃ
kriyākārakasaṃbandhapūrvaka eva parasparasaṃbandhaḥ । parasparaṃ punaḥ nāma saṃbandhi । ekapadī-
bhāva eva hetuḥ tenārtisaṃbandhāt puruṣasaṃbandhaḥ । tenā[rta]rtimeva haviḥ puruṣasya
viśeṣaṇamiti ārtiviśeṣaṇībhūtameva haviḥ nimittamiti siddham ।</p>
<p><q>nanu vākyādapi parasparasaṃbandho nāmnāmavagamyate---yathā devadattasya
gāva iti</q> । pariharati---<q>bāḍhaṃ sa tu vaibhaktikaḥ । vibhaktiśca dvayoreva
saṃbandhamācaṣṭe, na punaranyenāpīti</q> । autsargikamidaṃ, tena havirārtyaiva saṃbadhyatāṃ,
nobhayatvena । tasmādārtiviṣayaṃ havirnimittaṃ viśeṣyā [tvā]dānantaryācca । ārtiviṣayamiti
napuṃsakanirdeśaḥ havirviśeṣaṇatvāt ।</p>
<p><q>nanu cobhayaśabde nimittatvena parigṛhyamāṇe haviṣo'pi anupraveśaḥ
siddho bhavati । ubhayatvasya nityasāpekṣatvāt । ataḥ sakalapadānuguṇyena
tathaiva sambandha āśrīyatām</q> । yasyobhayaṃ(haviḥ) ārtimārcchet kiṃ tadubhayamitya-
syāmapekṣāyāṃ havireva parigṛhyate ।</p>
<p>pariharati---<q>asaṃbandhajño bhavān padārthajātasya viśeṣaṇaṃ hi viśeṣya-
mapekṣamāṇaṃ viṣayatayā'pekṣate</q> nātmano'vacchedakatayā । ubhayatvaṃ saṅkhyā । sā ca
ārtiviṣayatayā bhavituṃ nārhati iti ārtiviṣayaṃ dravyamevāpekṣate । tena yadyubhayatvaṃ
havirapekṣate tathāpi viśeṣaṇatvena naivāpekṣate । kiñca ārtiviṣayatayā ārtiviṣayabhāve
ca tasya tadeva nimittaṃ bhavati tadāha---<q>na cedamavacchedakaṃ, apitu viṣayaḥ ।
viṣayaḥ punaḥ viśeṣaṇanirapekṣaḥ nimittatāmāpadyate iti havirārtimātrameva
nimittaṃ vyartha evobhayapadākāṅkṣopanyāsaḥ</q> । yadidaṃ haviṣo dravyatvena
ārtiviṣayatvaṃ nobhayatvasya tadidamuktaṃ---<q>mṛṣyāmahe na haviṣo viśeṣaṇamiti</q>
akāryatayā anupādeyatayā cādhikṛtaviśeṣaṇānāṃ yāvantaḥ parasparasaṃbandhāḥ pradarśyante
yāvatsaṃbhavatsaṃbhavatāmidameva nirākaraṇamityuparamyate samāsaṃ vinā parasparasaṃbandhānāṃ
viśeṣaṇatvānupapattiriti idameva nirākaraṇaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇāpīti iyatāmupanyāso nirā-
karaṇasya vyāptipradarśanārtha eva kṛtaḥ । na hi pramāṇādṛte nimittasamāhārassiddha‍yatīti
siddhaṃ havirmātraviṣayārtirnimittamiti ।</p>﻿
<pb n="155"/>
<lg><l>।। 7 ।। homābhiṣavabhakṣaṇaṃ ca tadvat ।। 24 ।।</l></lg>
<p>atrāpi dvayornām‍noḥ parasparasaṃbandho nāstīti adhikriyamāṇa-
viśeṣaṇatvepi pratyekaṃ nimittabhāvaḥ</p> । asyārthaḥ---abhiṣutya hutvā bhakṣayatī-
tyatra dvayoḥ vatvāntayornām‍noḥ parasparasaṃbandho nāstīti yadyapi vastusthityā parasparasaṃbandha-
yorapi puruṣaviśeṣaṇatvaṃ saṃbhavati tathāpi śabdasāmarthyānusāreṇa pratyekameva nimittabhāvaḥ
<quote>‘abhiṣutya bhakṣayanti’</quote> tathā <quote>‘hutvā bhakṣayanti’</quote> iti । tena ye abhiṣavamātre'pi
kartāraḥ te'pi bhakṣayanti । ye'pi homa mātre te'pīti । <q>na cobhayapadavadavivakṣā
saṃbhavati</q> । yathā ubhayapadamavivakṣitaṃ tathā'bhiṣave nimitte hutveti na vivakṣitaṃ
anuvādamātram । na ca śakyaṃ vak‍tuṃ haviṣo'nyasyobhayatvaṃ nimittaṃ bhaviṣyatīti ।
anyasyānupādānāt haviṣaścopādānāt tadviṣayatvamevobhayatve pratīyate । iha puna-
raviśeṣādubhayaṃ nimittam । abhiṣave nimitte homasya nimittatā na prāptā । tathā
home nimitte'bhiṣavasyeti nānuvādopapattiriti ।</p>
<p><q>nanu cābhiṣutya hutveti saṃbandho bhavati । k‍tvāpratyayasya samāna-
kartṛkārthatvāt dvitīyena vinā dhātvarthena tadanupapatteḥ</q> । tadavaśyāpekṣaṇīye
abhiṣutyeti bhavati । hutveti tu bhakṣayatītyetadapekṣam । tenābhiṣavahomayoḥ paraspara-
sahitayoḥ nimittatvamiti । pariharati---<q>satyaṃ kriyāntarāpekṣitā ktvāpratyayasya
na punaḥ ktvāntakriyāpekṣitā । tasyā apyanyaparatvāt । na hi dvayora-
pradhānayoḥ mithassaṃbandho yuktaḥ</q> । kintu sarvaṃ pradhānenaiva saṃbadhyate pradhānaṃ ca
bhakṣayatītyetat na tu hutveti । tasyāpi bhakṣayatītyetasmin guṇabhāvāt । tasmādaya-
mabhisambandhaḥ abhiṣutya bhakṣayati, hutvā bhakṣayati iti । <q>kramavidhānaṃ tvatra naiva
saṃbhavati prāptatvāt</q> । abhiṣutyaiva homaḥ prāptaḥ huta eva ca bhakṣaṇam pratipatti-
tvāt । nāpyabhiṣavahomayoḥ bhakṣaṇāṅgatvena vidhānam adhikṛtaviśeṣaṇatvāt । nāpi
svārthavidhānaṃ, abhiṣavasya <quote>‘somamabhiṣuṇuyāt’</quote> iti prāsatvāt । <quote>‘somena yajeta
iti ca homasya । tasmānnimittanaimittikavidhirevāyam । sa ca pratyekamiti
pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyate---samānakartṛkatāvagamāt ktvāntānāmabhiṣavahomayo-
ścānyataḥ prāptatvāt ekakartṛkatvasyaiva abhiṣutya hutveti codyate ।</p>﻿
<pb n="156"/>
<p>asyārthaḥ ktvāntena śabdena samānakartṛkatā ucyate । homābhiṣavau ca
samānakartṛkau siddhau । tena sa eva samānakartā ucyate । tenāyamarthaḥ sampadyate---
abhiṣavahomayoḥ dvayoḥ kartā bhakṣayati iti । atrāyaṃ pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>nanu ca dvayoḥ ktvāntayoḥ parasparasaṃbandho nāvagamyate । anyārtha-
tvāt vyatiriktavibhaktyantarayuktayoriva</q> । yathā aruṇayaikahāyanyeti ca
prātipadikāvyatiriktakaraṇatvābhidhāyitṛtīyāntayoḥ parasparasaṃbandho na bhavati । tathā
ktvāntayorapi na yuktaṃ, avyatiriktaprathamāntayorbhavatyeva saṃbandhaḥ na vyatirikta-
vibhaktyantayoḥ । pariharati---</p>
<p><q>satyaṃ, yatra pramāṇāntaraṃ nāsti tatra pradhānakriyayaiva ktvāntasya
saṃbandhaḥ । yatra punaḥ pramāṇāntarāvagatai(re)va tadviṣayatā na tatra viṣayānta-
rāvagatirbhavati pramāṇāntareṇa ekavākyalakṣaṇena</q>1, yatra ktvāntayorekakartṛviṣaya-
tā'vagatā na tatra kartrantarāvagati । yadi hi ekaviṣayatā na syāt tadā eka-
vākyatā na syāt । ekavākyatā cāvagamyate । tenaikavākyatvāt tayoḥ ktvāntayo-
rapi parasparasaṃbandhaḥ । yathā kṛṣṇasya devadattasya gāva iti । kintvekavākyatā-
balāt kṛṣṇaguṇasya devadattasyaiveti saṃbandho bhavati । evamatrāpi abhiṣutya hutveti
ekakartṛviṣayamevādhikāriviśeṣaṇamavagamayati ekavākyatvāt । adhikṛtamukhena ca
viśeṣaṇasya(ā)vidhyanvayāt siddhā samāhārasya nimittatā । samāhṛtaviśeṣaṇa-
viśiṣṭasyā dhikārāt siddhā samāhṛtayoreva nimittatā । na cobhayapadavat nivartayituṃ
sāmarthyaṃ nāstīti śakyate vak‍tum, bhinnadvāratvāt padadvayasyāsya kartarīti । tatra
punaḥ vidhidvārakameva padadvayamiti viśeṣaḥ abhiṣavahomayostvananyatantratvāt nivartayituṃ
sāmarthyamasti । abhayapadaṃ havirviṣayameva । tena havirmātrārtinimittaṃ na śak‍noti
nivārayitum । ayaṃ tu kevalasya nimittatāṃ śak‍notyeva vārayitumiti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 8 ।। 1punarādheyamodanavat ।। 26 ।।</l></lg>
<p><quote>‘yasyobhāvag‍nī anugatau’</quote> iti ubhayaśabdasyāgniviṣayatvāt havi(ṣu)
[ṣṣviva] naivaikasya vāraṇe sāmarthyaṃmastīti2 ekasminnapyanugate naimittikamiti
<note>1. lakṣaṇaṃ na- mā</note>
<note>2. sāmarthmaṃ nāsti - mā</note>
<note>3. p. 1447</note>﻿
<pb n="157"/>
pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । anugatasyāgnimātrasya sūryeṇābhyudayo'bhinimrocanaṃ ca
nimittatvena śrūyamāṇaṃ ubhayaśabdena nivartayituṃ na śakyate ubhayaśabdasyāgniviṣayatvāt ।
tena prāptasyāyamanuvāda iti । <q>rāddhāntavādī tu satyaṃ nimittabhāvo vārayituṃ na
śakyate naimittikaṃ tu ekasminnanugate nopapadyate</q> ubhayārthatvena jñātatvāt ।
jñātasya ca punarvidhānāt punarādheyameva tasya prāyaścittiriti । yadevādhānamagnyu-
tpādakatayā anugame naimittikamiti siddham ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 9 ।। 1pañcaśarāvastu dravyaśruteḥ pratinidhiḥ syāt ।। 28 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nirvapatisaṃbandhāt pratinidhiniyamaṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī</q> । aindraṃ
pañcaśarāvamodanaṃ nirvapet iti nirvapatiśravaṇāt sānnāyye vipanne ca dravyāntaraṃ
nirvapediti codyate । yadi hi karmāntaraṃ vidhīyate tadā tatra nirvāpasya codakaprāptasya
anuvādakaḥ syāt ।</p>
<p><q>kathamasminnapi pakṣe aindraśabdaḥ ?</q> yadyodanaṃ nirvapediti vidhīyate katha-
maindraśabdaḥ । na hi so'pi vidheyārtho'vakalpate vākyabhedaprasaṅgāt । uttaraṃ---
<q>prāptatvādanuvādaṃ manyate</q> । pratinidhīyamānaṃ dravyamaindrameva prāptaṃ indrasya tasmin
karmaṇi devatābhāvāt । nanu ca mahendro'pi[mahendrasyāpi] tatra devatābhāvāt; na
cendraśabdena mahendro'bhidhātuṃ śakyate । ataḥ kathamanuvāda iti tatrāha---</p>
<p><q>prāptatvānmahendraśabdāśravaṇamapi adoṣaḥ</q> nāvaśyaṃ sarvameva prāptamanuvadita-
vyamiti bhāvaḥ । <q>atrocyate । yataḥ prāptaṃ nāvaśyaṃ sarvamevānuvaditavyaṃ
vināpi tena vivakṣitārthasiddheḥ</q> । ata eva karmāntaramidaṃ; anyathā hi māhendra-
śabdavat aindraśabdo'pi na vaktavyaḥ syāt । uktaścāyam । sa ca yasmin pakṣe'rthavān
sa eva pakṣaḥ āśrayituṃ nyāyyaḥ । tasmādvidhānārthataiva nyāyyā ।</p>
<p>nanvevamapi nirvapatiśabdo'narthaka ityatrāha---<q>nirvapatiśabdastu pratya-
yoccāraṇamavaśyaṃ vaktavyamiti viśeṣaḥ</q> । aindraśabdassarvatrānarthakaḥ nirvapatiśabdastu
karmavidhānārthaṃ yo vidhissa vaktavyaḥ । tadarthatayāpyarthavāneveti ।</p>
<note>1. p. 1448</note>﻿
<pb n="158"/>
<lg><l>।। 10 ।। 1sa pratyāmanet sthānāt ।। 30 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>pañcaśarāva idānīṃ cinat‍te---kiṃ svatantraṃ karmāntaraṃ uta darśapūrṇamā-
sādhikṛtasyaiva tannāśe tatkāryasādhanamupadiśyate utāmāvāsyāṅgamiti</q> ।
sthite karmāntara[tve]hi cintopapadyate । idānīmiti vadan pakṣatrayamatra cintyata iti ca
darśayati । tena bhāṣye amāvāsyāṃ pratyāmanediti pakṣaḥ tadā[tathā]kiṃ karmāntaraṃ
svatantraṃ uta tadaṅgameveti draṣṭavyam । tatra pūrvapakṣavādī tāvat vinaṣṭasyāṅga-
bhāvo'narthakaḥ । ataḥ tatkāryasyaivedaṃ sādhanamiti manyate । svatantrapakṣo'pi mandatayā
nopanyastaḥ । <q>rāddhāntavādī tu svātantrye tāvadadhikārāntarakalpanaiva doṣaḥ</q> ।</p>
kāryakaraṇatve'pi pradhānaṃ pramāṇaṃ naivāṅgi aṅgatā punaḥ prakaraṇām‍nānādavasīyate ।
nanu vinaṣṭasya aṅgabhāvo'narthaka ityuktam । aṅgavināśādevāvināśo bhaviṣyati ।
haviṣi kila viparn‍na karmaṇo dravyāntareṇa kriyamāṇasya vaiguṇya saṃbhavati । tacca vaiguṇya-
maṅgavidhānādeva pratisamādhāsyate ।</p>
<p><q>nanu cānyathāpi idaṃ vidhānamupapannamityuktam । kāryakaraṇatayā
vidhānopapatteḥ sa śakyate'ṅgatayā vidhānam</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>na prakaraṇe'nyathoṣa-
padyate</q> । prakaraṇādaṅgataivāvagamyate । pratyakṣaśca prakaraṇapāṭhaḥ । kāryasvātantryayostu
kalpanopapadyate । tasmādaṅgataiveti yuktam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 11 ।। 2viśvajittvapravṛtte bhāvaḥ karmaṇi syāt ।। 32 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>āgurataḥ karma codyate । atra saṃśaya iti</q> । anena saviṣayatayā[tāṃ]
nyāyasya darśayati viśvajidvā bhavati anyadvā । sarvathā padāgūryamāṇasya karma codyate ।
tatrāyaṃ vicāraḥ---āgurata iti rūpasiddhau yatnaḥ kartavyaḥ । gurateranudāttettvāt
ātmanepadaprasakteḥ । saṃśayasvarūpamāha---</p>
<p><q>kiṃ yadāguritaṃ satrādi tatpravṛttau satyāmeva idaṃ karma uta aviśeṣeṇa
atha[a]pravṛttāveveti</q> । anenāviśeṣapakṣo yadyapi bhāṣyakāreṇopanyāsakāle manda-
tvānnopanyastaḥ tathāpi nirākaraṇadarśanādupādātavyaḥ iti darśitam । āguritamiti
<note>1. p. 1149</note> <note>2. p. 1451</note>﻿
<pb n="159"/>
śabdasādhutāyāṃ yatna āstheyaḥ । gurīdhātorīditvādiṭpratiṣedhopapatteḥ । viśeṣānu-
pādānādaviśeṣeṇa1 iti prāpte ucyate---</p>
<p>āgūryamāṇasya pravṛttau viśvajit iti । evamaṅgatā bhavati । na nimittaparya-
nto'dhikāraḥ kalpito bhavati । āgūryamāṇebhyaḥ pravṛtte karma vidhīyamānaṃ āgoraṇa-
nimittakaṃ bhavati । tacca na yuktam । adhikārāntarakalpanāprasaṅgāt । pravṛtte tasyeda-
maṅgamiti kalpanā laghvī । aviśeṣe punaḥ nimittaparyantatā । pravṛttyabhāvapakṣe'ṅgataiveti
vipratiṣiddham । svatantratāṅgatvayorvirodhāt ।</p>
<p><q>atrocyate---apravṛttasyai vedaṃ karmā''guramāṇasya codyate । āgūrya-
māṇasyāgoraṇaviśeṣārthatvāt na śakyate vidheyasyāṅgatā vak‍tum</q> । <quote>‘yaḥ satrā-
yāgurate sa viśvajitā yajeta’</quote> iti nāyamabhisaṃbandhaḥ <quote>‘satrāya viśvajitā yajeta’</quote> iti
vyavahitānvayaprasaṅgāt, kintu satrāyāgurate iti । tenāgoraṇaviśeṣaṇatvāt āgūrya-
māṇaṃ pratyaṅgatā caturthībalena vidhīyamānasya na śakyā sampādayitum । tena svatantra-
taiva nyāyyā ।</p>
<p><q>nanu cāsminnapi pakṣe āgoraṇasya nimittaparyantatā kalpanīyā ।
tadvaraṃ samabhivyāhriyamāṇasatrāṅgataivāśrīyatām । nimittaparyantatve'pi
svatantrādhikārāntaramāśrayaṇīyam</q> । aṅgatve tu tanna bhavatīti । uttaraṃ---
<q>nāyaṃ doṣaḥ āgoraṇasya samāptiparyantatvāt āgūryamāṇakāryaparyantataivā-
śrīyate</q> tasmāt pūrvādhikṛtakāryaparyantataiveti na kāryāntaraṃ kalpitaṃ bhavati । āgoraṇa-
mudyamanaṃ, udyamanaṃ ca samāptyartham samāptiśca kāryaparyantataivocyate udyamanaṃ ca tasya
bhavati । tena satratā kāryatayā pratipannā । tasya viśvajidvidhīyamānaḥ tatkāryaparyanta
evāvasīyate । ataḥ kāryāntarakalpanā nāsti । tadevaiśvaryaṃ viśvajitāpi puruṣasya
yataḥ sādhyate tasmādayameva pakṣaḥ śreyān viśvajitā satrakāryaṃ kuryāditi ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 12 ।। 2vatsasaṃyoge vratacodanā syāt ।। 34 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>keyamadhikāre aṅgāṅgicintā । yadi kālalakṣaṇā yadi vā śrautārthaḥ
ubhayathāpyaṅgapradhānacintaiva</q> । ekatra pakṣe śrutyā vatsasya vratāṅgatayā vidhiḥ ।</p>
<note>1. aviśeṣaṇaṃ-mā</note> <note>2. p 1452</note>﻿
<pb n="160"/>
anyatra pakṣe lakṣitasya ekakāla[sya]vratāṅgatayaiva vidhiriti viśeṣaḥ tena lakṣaṇe
saṅgatirnāstīti ।</p>
<p><q>atrocyate । śraute vatse vidhīyamāne vidhiḥ kālalakṣaṇāyāmadhi-
kāraḥ</q> । kathaṃ ? uttaraṃ---<q>ekatra vrate vatsaḥ codyate</q> pratyayā[amāvāsyā]ṅgatayā vā ।
anyatra vratinaḥ kālaḥ । kathaṃ punaḥ lakṣaṇāyāṃ vratinaḥ kālaścodyate ityatrāha---
<q>na kālaḥ karmaṇā saṃbadhyate । anapekṣitatvāt prayogāṅgaṃ sa ityuktam ।</q>
ekadeśaprayoga eva kālasyāpekṣaṇīyatvāt । tataḥ kimityāha---<q>prayogaścādhi-
kṛtasyeti</q> adhi(kṛtya)[tasya]sambandhaḥ prayogaṃ cikīrṣamāṇasya kālāpekṣāyāṃ kālo
vidhīyamāno'dhikṛtasyaiva sambandhitayā vidhīyate adhikāranibandhatvāt prayogasya ।
tenādhikāra cintāyāmasti saṅgatiḥ kālavidhāvadhikārasambandhitvāt । <q>śeṣamuktam</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 13 ।। 1kālaścetsannayatpakṣe talliṅgasaṃyogāt ।। 41 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nanu caiva puroḍāśānāmapi anapāyo hi kālasyetyuktam । kimatrā-
bhyadhikaṃ cintyate । na, paunaruktyamāśaṅkyate yo'pyeṣa puroḍāśaḥ paurṇamāsyā-
masti asomayājinaḥ tasyāmasatyapi agnīṣomīye puroḍāśe puroḍāśayormadhya-
vartikālaḥ upāṃśuyājasaṃbandhī vidyata evetyuktam । tadvadihāpi</q> । asānnā-
yyayājino vatsāpākaraṇābhāve'pi tatkālasyāpāyo nāstīti tasyāpi kālavidhiryukta
eveti siddha eva rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>kimarthamidamadhikaraṇamārabhyate ? astyatra viśeṣaḥ---adhikāramukhenai-
tatkālavidhānam</q> । adhikṛtasyaivāyaṃ kālavidhiruktaḥ । tatra pūrvapakṣavādī kālopa-
lakṣaṇapadārthayuktasyaivādhikṛtasyeti manyate । kālopalakṣaṇena vatsāpākaraṇena yukta-
syaivādhikāriṇaḥ kālavidhirayaṃ yuktaḥ । na hi anyasya tatkālo vidhātuṃ śakyate ।
tadabhāve tatkāla evāsau na bhavatīti bhāvaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntavādī tu - satyaṃ adhikṛtasyaivāyaṃ kālavidhiḥ । kālasaṃbhava-
mātre tvadhikṛto'yam</q> । tasya hi kālo vidhātavyaḥ yasya hi kālaḥ saṃbhavati tena
saṃbhava evā dhikṛto'yaṃ tasya kālavidhiḥ । sa ca kālo vatsāpākaraṇarahitasyāpyasti ।</p>
<note>1. 1454</note>﻿
<pb n="161"/>
<p>nanu ca vatsāpākaraṇayuktaḥ kālo nāstītyatrāha---<q>na punarupalakṣaṇamapya-
dhikāraṃ viśinaṣṭi । kutaḥ ? upalakṣaṇatvādeva । aṅgabhūto hi kālo'dhikāraṃ
viśinaṣṭi । na punarupalakṣaṇam । pratītimātrahetutvāt</q> । yadyupalakṣaṇamapi
kāryopayogi syāt tadā viśiṃṣyādapyadhikāram । nacopalakṣaṇaṃ kāryaupayikam । kiṃ
tarhi ? <q>upalakṣaṇāyaiva</q> । tadviśiṣṭakālaviśeṣapratipattyarthameva । na ca satā asatā
vā upalakṣaṇena kaścidviśeṣo'sti asya kālasyānyato'vagamāt । kasmāt ? anapāyo
hi kālastatrāpi siddhaṃ na kevalamekapuroḍāśe'yamiti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 14 ।। 1prastare śākhā śrayaṇavat ।। 43 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>atrāpi viniyogapratipakṣatayā'dhikāra eva cintyate</q> । aṅgavidhau
aṅgabhūtaśākhāvidhau viniyogaḥ । kālavidhau prastarapraharaṇakāle śākhā praharaṇaṃ prati
vidhīyamānā'dhikṛtasyaiva vidhiḥ । na punaḥ guṇārthe tṛtīyeyaṃ śaṅkyate । <q>upapada-
lakṣaṇā hīyaṃ na kārakalakṣaṇā । sahaśabdaśravaṇāt sahaprayoganibandhanaiveyaṃ
tṛtīyā na kārakalakṣaṇā । tena kathaṃ śākhāyāṃ guṇabhāvaśaṅkā</q> ।</p>
<p><q>satyaṃ upapadavibhaktiriyam aprādhānyaṃ tu anyathā nopapadyate</q> ।
tena guṇabhāvaṃ manyate । <quote>‘sahayukte'pradhāna’</quote> iti apradhānavācinaḥ prātipadikāt iyaṃ
tṛtīyā । tena śākhā apradhānabhṛtā guṇabhūtaivāvasīyate ।</p>
<p>atra codayati---<q>bhavatvatra prādhānyaṃ sahabhāve, mā bhūt prastare</q> । yadyapya-
prādhānye sahārtheyaṃ tṛtīyā, tathāpi tadaprādhānyaṃ sahabhāve ।</p>
<p>kimidaṃ sahabhāva iti? sa pradhānaṃ yasya tu prasiddha eva kriyāsaṃbandhaḥ, yasya na
tadapradhānaṃ tena praharaṇasaṃbandhaḥ śākhāyā ucyata iti । <q>bhavatvaprādhānyaṃ śākhāyāḥ
prastaraṃ pratiguṇībhāvo na yuktaḥ</q> । samādhate-<q>tatsiddhistviha na saṃbhavatīti hi
paśyan pūrvapakṣavādī sahabhāvamavivakṣitaṃ manyate</q> । śākhāyāḥ praharaṇasambandhasyāpi
aviditatvāt prastarasya viditatvāt sahabhāve'prādhānyaṃ na saṃbhavatīti avivakṣita
evātra sahabhāvaḥ । tasmāt kārakatayaivātra guṇabhāva upapadyata iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu---sahabhāvāvivakṣā na vibhaktibalena yuktā । vibhakta-
yo'pi vyatyayenāpi smaryante</q> । asyārthaḥ - yadi śākhāśabdaḥ tṛtīyānto gṛhyeta
<note>1. 1455</note>﻿
<pb n="162"/>
prastaraśabdaśca dvitīyāntaḥ tadā śākhāyāḥ aprādhānyāt anupapatteḥ sahabhāvo'vivakṣitaḥ
syāt । sā ceyamavivakṣā vibhaktibalena । na ca vibhaktiḥ sahaśabdamapi vivakṣitaṃ
kartuṃ śaknoti । vibhaktivyatyayenāpi prayogadarśanāt । tenātra vibhaktervyatyayena varṇanā
<quote>‘prastareṇa śākhāṃ praharati’</quote> iti । upapadyate cātra sahārthaḥ nopapadyamānasyāvivakṣā
yuktā । kiñca kṛtaprayojanā ca śākhā vatsāpākaraṇena । kṛtaprayojanānāṃ ca
pratipattau satyāṃ na kāryāntarakalpanā'vakalpate iti । prastarapraharaṇamapi kāryāntaraparam
na śākhāyāḥ (kāryāntaraṃ) kalpayituṃ śakyate - viniyuktaviniyogavirodhāditi ।
sahayoga evāyaṃ pratipattavya iti vibhaktivyatyaya ityevātra nyāyyaḥ । upakāraścātra
viparītaḥ tṛṇamayaprastaraḥ śākhāyāṃ dahyamānāyāṃ upakartumarhatīti śāsvāprastare prayojana-
muktam । pūrvapakṣe amāvāsyāyāmasannayatā śākhāupādeyā prastarapraharaṇāṅgatvapakṣe ।
pratipattipakṣe tu yatraiva sānnāyyāṅgabhūtā śākhā'sti tatraiva pratipādyā bhavatīti ।</p>
<p><q>iti ṛjuvimalāyāṃ ṣaṣṭhādhyāyasya
caturthaḥ pādaḥ</q></p>﻿
<pb n="163"/>
<p><q>ṛjuvimalāyāṃ</q></p>
<p><q>ṣaṣṭhādhyāyasya pañcamaḥ pādaḥ</q></p>
<lg><l>।। 1 ।। abhyudaye kālāparādhādijyācodanāsyādyathā
pañ‍caśarāve ।। 1 ।।</l></lg>
<p>atreyaṃ viṣayaśuddhiḥ---amāvāsyāyāmeva darśārthena vediḥ kriyate । agni-
praṇayanādikaṃ vratādikaṃ ca yajamānasaṃskāraḥ dadhyarthaśca dohaḥ । pratipadi darśaḥ pravartate
iti । eṣa tāvat pāramārthiko'nuṣṭhānaniyamaḥ । yasya tu yajamānasya kutaś‍cit
gaṇanabhramanimittā caturdaśyāmevāmāvāsyābuddhirupajāyate sā tasyāmamāvāsyāyāṃ karma
pravartayati । tasya candramasā havirabhyudīyate । tatredaṃ śrūyate <quote>‘yasya havirniruptaṃ’</quote>
iti । tena yajamānenābhyuditena haviṣā amāvāsyāyāmeva nimittādhikāraṃ parisamāpya
punastadahareva vedyuddhananādi karma kṛtvā pratipadyeva darśaḥ kartavya iti । abhyudaye-
[ṣṭiri]ti naimittikamidaṃ karmāntaraṃ vidhīyate । athavā tadevāpanītadevatāke iviḥ
punaḥ devatāntaraiḥ saṃyujyate iti ।</p>
<p>pūrvapakṣe niyogaḥ, rāddhānte tu adhikṛtasya prayogaviśeṣacodaneti । <q>adhi-
kāralakṣaṇena(ṇa na) karmasaṃbandhitā śās‍trasya</q> । anena adhikaraṇasya lakṣaṇasaṅgati-
māha । akṣarārthastu darśāt karmāntaraṃ vidhīyata iti । ayamatra pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । atra
ca viniyogo dvaitīyaḥ karmāntarasyādhikāre viniyoga upakrānto darśitaḥ । karmaṇaḥ
prayogaviśeṣo'yaṃ codyata iti rāddhāntaḥ । tatra ca prayogaviśeṣacodanā, prayogaviśe-
ṣaścādhikṛtasyeti adhikāriviśeṣāśrayatvāt adhikāralakṣaṇamevedamiti bhavati lakṣaṇa-
saṅgatiḥ । <q>nanu ca yadyapi pūrvapakṣe karmasambandhitā śās‍trasya tathāpi
kimityadhikāradvārā cintā na bhavatīti</q> ।</p>
<p><q>atrāha---karmasaṃbandhe hi adhikṛtadvārā cintopapadyate । tasmin
sati adhikārāt । tatra pūrvapakṣavādī karmāntaraṃ vidhīyata iti manyate ।
tredhā taṇḍulān vibhajet iti taṇḍulavibhāgo'trāvagamyate na dadhipayasoḥ</q>
asyārthaḥ । yadi(devataiva na)[devatābhyaḥ] haviṣāṃ vibhāgaḥ syāt tadā apanīta-
devatānāṃ haviṣāṃ devatāntareṇa saṃyogaḥ śakyate kartum । tataśca prakṛtānāmeva karmaṇā-﻿
<pb n="164"/>
mayamanuṣṭhānaviśeṣaḥ codyata iti rāddhāntasiddhirbhavati । iha tu taṇḍulān vibhajeta iti
taṇḍulavibhāgaḥ śrūyate na dadhipayasoḥ । evaṃ ca taṇḍulānāmevāyaṃ sthaviṣṭhādibhirviśeṣaiḥ
viśiṣṭo vibhāgo'vagamyate na devatāyāḥ । sthūlamadhyamasūkṣmatvādibhiḥ taṇḍulā
vibhaktavyā iti pratīyate । [na]punardevatābhyo vibhajediti । tataśca pūrvadevatābhyo'na-
panītatvāt na śakyate taddhaviḥ devatāntareṇa yojayitumiti । karmāntara vedaṃ vidhīyate ।
pūrvaṃ tu karmabhāvāt adhikārabhāvāt parityajanīyameva । dadhyādayastu laukikāḥ santaḥ
yadi karmāntare'pi vyāpriyante tadā na kaściddoṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>yuktyantaraṃ cāha---<q>caruśca dadhipayasossaṃyoge devatāvibhāge nopapadyate</q> ।
asyārthaḥ---ekendrādisaṃbandhitvena yadyapidaghnastaṇḍulānāṃ ca saṃyogaḥ tathāpi carutvaṃ
kathaṃ labhyate? tadapi na vidhīyate । vidhīyate cet tadā vihite karmaṇi guṇadvaya-
vidhānānupapatteḥ karmāntaravidhirevāpatati । na hi devatāntaraṃ carutvaṃ ca śakyate
vidhātumekena vākyena vihite karmaṇi ।</p>
<p>nanu saṃyuktayoḥ dadhitaṇḍulayoḥ pāke sati, tathā payastaṇḍulayośca pāke sati
carutvamarthaprāptameva sat anūdyate(saḥ)saptamyarthenetyāśaṅkyāha---<q>puroḍāśārtha---
tayā hi pākastatropadiṣṭaḥ । caroraśra(va)paṇāt</q> । darśapūrṇamāsopayogi yacchra(va)
paṇaṃ vihitaṃ tat prathanottarakāle puroḍāśākṛtike dravye sampan‍ne sati puroḍāśa-
saṃskārārthaṃ na taṇḍulānāṃ caroraśrapaṇāt । yadi tatra caruḥ śrūyate tadā taṇḍulānāṃ
pāko vidhī[yeta](yate) । tasmāt karmāntaravidhipakṣa evaitatsarvamupapadyata iti
pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>kathaṃ punaratra asmin pakṣe ātañcanābhyāsaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ । evamata
śruyate---<quote>“yadi bibhīyādabhimodeṣyatīti mahārātra eva havīṃṣi nirvapet phalīkṛtai-
staṇḍulaiḥ paryupāsīta ardhaṃ havirātañcanasya nidadhyāt, ardhaṃ na, yadyabhyudiyāt
tenātacya pracaret yadi na tena brāhmaṇaṃ bhojayet”</quote> iti । yaḥ khalu yajamānaḥ
āśaṅkate-pravṛttā'māvāsyā tatraiva kimatra caturdaśī uta pañcadaśīti । [sa tasyā](satyā)
meva rātrau vrīhīn‍nirupya avahatya, phalīkṛtya udīkṣamāṇa āsīta । sāyaṃdohana-
saṃpāditaṃ ca dadhi dvidhākṛtya ardhaṃ dadhi ekāntaritakariṣyamāṇasya kṛte anantaraṃ sāyaṃ
dohaṃ sampādya dadhyātañcanāya nidadhyāt । ardhaṃ caivameva sthāpayet । tatra yadyabhyudayaḥ
syādevameva sthāpitenārdhena dadhnā naimittikādhikāraṃ nirvartya nihitenārdhena dadhnā sāyaṃ
<pb n="165"/>
dugdhe payasi ātañcanaṃ kṛtvā dadhyutpādya anyedyuḥ darśamabhinirvartayet yadi tannābhyu-
diyāt yadevaṃ nihita(camevaṃnita)mardhaṃ dadhi tenārdhena dadhnā darśameva kuryāt । ātañcanāya
nihitaṃ ca dadhi ātañ‍canasyānarthakatvāt ātañ‍canenāsyāpa[sa]raṇīyaṃ brāhmaṇabhojanena
pratipādayediti । tatra ca yadi karmāntaramidaṃ naimittikaṃ bhavet । tadā yattaddadhyasti
taddarśārthabheveti (nanu) [na] darśārthenāpareṇa dadhnā kṛtyamastīti ātañ‍caṃna na kriyeta
tatrātañ‍canābhyāsadarśanaṃ nopapadyate । yadā tvetat tadevāmāvāsyākarma(a)pravṛttaṃ tatra
tadā anenaiva dadhnā darśārthopārjitena kartavyamiti aparedyuḥ k‍vacitprāptasya1 darśasya
kṛte ātañ‍canena prayojanamastīti yukta ātañ‍canābhyāsaḥ । pariharati---</p>
<p><q>vācaniko bhaviṣyatīti</q> । asyārthaḥ---yadyapi tad dadhyasti tathāpi
anyad‍dadhi ātacya pracaritavyamiti vācanikamevaṃ bhaviṣyatīti nyāyenaivāsmin
śās‍trārthe sthitam ।</p>
<p>atra kaściccodayati---<q>nanu cetarasmin pakṣe vācanika evāsau</q> ।
asyārthaḥ---yasminnapi pakṣe na karmāntaramidaṃ tasminnapi pakṣe caturdaśyāṃ janitasya dadhnaḥ
pratipadi kriyamāṇadarśaṃ prati ayogyatvāt vācanika eva viniyogaḥ । amāvāsyāyāṃ
hi janitaṃ dadhi darśe viniyuktam । <q>ataścātañ‍canābhyāsadarśanaṃ nopapadyate iti
itarasminnāpādanapakṣe'pi vācanika eva</p> । ayamarthaḥ---tenaiva dadhnā darśaḥ
kartavya iti । tatkena viśeṣaṇena ? prapañ‍cenedamucyate vācaniko'yamātañ‍canābhyāso
bhaviṣyatīti ।</p>
<p>pariharati---<q>satyaṃ tathāpi tūpādānāntarābhāvāt prāpta ityucyate
viniyoge tūbhayostulyam</q> । āpādanapakṣe hi viniyogamātraṃ tasya dadhnaḥ
na punarupādānam vācanikātañcanam । abhyāsapakṣe tu viniyogaḥ upādānaṃ ca
vācanikam---tena dadhyātañcanaṃ kartavyaṃ ityayamartho vācanikaḥsyāt । tathā
vidyamāne'pi tasmin dadhani dadhyantaramupādeyaṃ na punastenaiva dadhnā kartavyamityeta-
dvācanikameveti ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---devatāpanayo'yam</q> । kutaḥ? <q>vibhāgavākye
traividhyasyānyataḥ prāpteḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---nāyaṃ sthaviṣṭhādibhirviśeṣaiḥ taṇḍulānāmeva
<note>1. vidhiprāptasyeti yuktaḥ pāṭhaḥ</note>﻿
<pb n="166"/>
vibhāgo vihitaḥ, anyataḥ prāptatvāt । kintu devatāto vibhāgo haviṣaḥ, tasyānyataḥ
[to']prāptatvāt ।</p>
<p><q>kuto byastataṇḍulānāṃ traividhyena vibhāgaprāptiḥ ?</q> uttaraṃ---<q>devatā-
sambandhavidhānataḥ</q> । yadā sthaviṣṭhādīnāṃ bhedena devatātrayasambandhaḥ tadā arthā-
deva taṇḍulānāṃ pṛthak kalpanaṃ prāptam । ataḥ vibhajedityetāvadeva vidhīyate ।
na punastredhā vibhajet iti । tredhāśabdastu taṇḍulānāṃ nityaprāptaṃ traividhya-
manuvadati । sa cāviśeṣāt havirmātrasyaiva pratīyate na punaḥ taṇḍulānāmeva ।
devatābhyo vibhajedityukte jñāyata eva tatsambandhihaviṣo'pi vibhāga iti ।</p>
<p>tacca havirmātra na taṇḍulaśabdena viśeṣṭuṃ śakyate । vākyabhedaprasaṅgāt ।
uparitanāni ca vākyāni apanīte devatāntasambandhe devatāntarāṇīti na karmāntaramava-
gamyate । prakṛtānyeva ca dravyāṇi darśākhyena karmaṇā saṃbaddhāni devatābhyo viṣeśeṇā-
panītāni devatāntarairyuktānīti prakṛtakarmaṇi pratyabhijñānāt na karmāntaramavagamyate ।
na ca kālābhāvenādhikārābhāve karmasvarūpābhāvaḥ । naimittikādhikāre tānyeva karmāṇi
codyante । tataśca tasmin kṛte nimittādhikāre nityādhikāra1nirvṛttyarthaṃ bhūyastānyeva
karmāṇi kartavyānīti mantavyam । <q>nanu caruśabdaśravaṇaṃ nopapadyata ityuktam</q> ।
puroḍāśārthatvātpākasya tadvidhau ca vākyabhedaprasaṅgaḥ । yadi prāptakarmānuvādena vidhiḥ
guṇavidhiḥ karmasvarūpāśritaḥ syāt, tadā'nekaguṇavidhānādvākyabhedaḥ syāt । yadā tvayaṃ
kālabhrameṇādhikārabhrāntyā pravṛttasyābhyudayasyādhikṛtasya vibhāganimittako devatābhyo
vibhāge sati tasyaiva yāgasya prayogaviśeṣaścodyate tathāsati na vākyabhedaḥ । kathamityāha
---<q>sa evāyaṃ puroḍāśaḥ tāṃ tāmavasthāṃ nītaḥ</q> iti । anuvādo'yam । asyārthaḥ-
yo'sau puroḍāśaścoditaḥ tasya puroḍāśasvarūpatayaiva prayogo'pi prāptaḥ । samprati abhyudaye
nimitte abhyuditāvasthāyāmeva dadhisaṃyuktasya payassaṃyuktasya devatāpanayaṃ kṛtvā devatāntara-
saṃbandhaḥ kriyate । tasya ca tathābhūtasya peṣaṇaṃ na kartavyameva । prathanārthatvāt । tasya
prathanasya ca kartumaśakyatvāt stokatvāt taṇḍulānāṃ, prabhūtatvāt daghnaḥ payasaśca ।
tenātra(āpī) apiṣṭvaivāprathayitvaiva ca pākaḥ kartavyaḥ । 2tasyānapanīyatvāt kriyamāṇe ca
pāke'rthāccarutā । saptamyarthaśca sampadyata evetyanuvādoya'm <quote>“dadhani caruṃ”</quote> <quote>“payasi
<note>1. nivṛttyarthaṃ-mā</note>﻿
<pb n="167"/>
carum”</quote> iti । yata eva ca prayogaprakāracodanayā'nuvā(do)dānupapatteḥ prakṛtakarmānu-
praveśassiddha‍yati na punaḥ karmaṇi guṇavidhānena ca । ata evetyanuvādaḥ । <q>ayaṃ ca
bheda(ḥ)lakṣaṇe nābhedaḥ śakyate vak‍tumiti adhikṛtadvāramevedaṃ śabdārthavido
manyante</q> ।</p>
<p><q>bhedābhedalakṣaṇe hi dvitīye'dhyāye yadyeṣā cintā kriyate tadā karmasvarūpā-
śritatvāt tatraiva guṇavidhiḥ syāt । tatrānekaguṇavidhānāt vākyabhedaprasaṅgāt
karmāntaramevedaṃ syāt । adhikāralakṣaṇe tu cintāyāmadhikṛtasya prayogaviśeṣaścodyata
iti puroḍāśa evāyaṃ prayujyata iti pākasyāpanītatvāt arthaprāptaiva carutā saptamyarthena
sahānūdyata iti vākyabhedābhāvādupapadyata evābhedaḥ । tenādhikāralakṣaṇa idaṃ cintyate ।
tasmāt pañcaśarāvādibhyo vilakṣaṇamidaṃ naimittikamiti siddham । pañcaśarāvādibhyo-
havirārtyā karmaiva vinaṣṭamiti karmāntaraṃ codyate । iha kālāparādhe'pi haviṣo'vinaṣṭa-
tvāt karmaṇi avinaṣṭe prayogāntaramidaṃ naimitikaṃ codyate । tasyaivāyaṃ prayoga iti ।
prakṛtadravyapratyabhijñānena idamavagamyata iti sustham । śeṣamuktam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 2 ।। upāṃśuyāje'vacanādyathāprakṛti ।। 10 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>amāvāsyāyāmapyupāṃśuyājo vidyata iti kṛtvācinteyam । kathaṃ
punaratra pūrvapakṣā''śaṅkā yāvatā prayoga evedamuktaṃ tredhā taṇḍulān vibhajet
iti havirmātrasya vibhāga iti</q> । tenopāṃśuyājahaviṣo'pi devatāpanaya iti ।</p>
<p>uttaraṃ---<q>pratisamādhānadarśanāt pūrvapakṣāśaṅkā</q> । yathādadhipayaḥpuroḍā-
śānāmapanītāyāṃ pūrvadevatāyāṃ aparadevatāsambandhaḥ tatheha nāsti । na ca devatāṃ
vinā yāgo bhavati ityapanayaḥ eva(vaṃ)devatāyāḥ । tasmātpūrvapakṣī tāvatsamādhānama-
vibhāgaṃ manyate ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntastu---<q>vibhāgāviśeṣāt sarvatra vibhāgaḥ</q> । yatra samādhānaṃ tatra
samādhiḥ । yatra tu nāsti samādhānaṃ tatra vibhāgānta eva naimittikaḥ prayogaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>nanu ca devatāvibhāgānte yāgaḥ prayukto na bhavati । debatoddeśena hi
dravyatyāgo yāgaḥ । sa ca devatāyāmanuddiṣṭāyāṃ prayukto na bhavati</q> ।</p>
<p>pariharati---<q>kathaṃ śakyate vak‍tuṃ na prayukta iti ? vācanikatvāda-
syārthasya</q> । asyārthaḥ---ya evāsau yāgaścoditaḥ tasya devatāvibhāgātmaka eva
<pb n="168"/>
prayogaḥ kartavya iti vacanenedamucyate । tyāga eva tu devatoddeśo yāgaḥ । sa ca
upādhivigame'pi nānupapannaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>nanu yadyupādhirna pratīyate kathamavagamyate sa evāyaṃ yāga iti ।
prakṛtasyaiva prayogavidhānāt puroḍāśa iva carvavasthe</q> । yāgo'pi hi vibhāgānta
evāvasīyate prayoganiṣṭhatvādadhikāraśāstrāṇām । adhikāraśāstrāṇi tāvat prayoganiṣṭhāni
prayogameva codayanti । na prayojyaviṣayaśśeṣaḥ । tena yāgasyaivāyamīdṛśaḥ prayojyasya
prayogaśeṣo jñāyata iti na doṣaḥ । yathā puroḍāśa eva carubhūta iti । <q>karmasvarūpa-
vidhau hyayaṃ doṣaḥ</q> devatoddeśaṃ vinā yāgāsiddhilakṣaṇaḥ । nanu ca devatāpanaye sati
yākāciddevatā kathyata iti, atrāha---<q>na ca sāmānyena devatākalpanā vacanāva-
gamyatvāt devatāyāḥ</q> । etadeva kuta ityatrāha---<q>yā yasya haviṣaḥ codyate sā
tasya devateti sthiteḥ । tena devatābhāvaṃ</q> kalpayituṃ na śakyata iti । 1artha-
vibhāgānta eva prayogo vidhīyata iti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 3 ।। nirupte syāt tatsaṃyogāt ।। 12 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>niruptaśabdaśravaṇāt nirupta eva haviṣi udite naimittikamiti
pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</q> ।</p>
<p><q>nanu ca ārtyadhikaraṇenaiva gatamidam</q> । yathā ārtyadhikaraṇe ubhayatva-
viśeṣaṇamavivakṣitaṃ, kiṃ tarhiṃ havirmātrasyārtirnimittaṃ ihāpi havirmātrasya abhyudayo
nimittaṃ niruptagrahaṇamavivakṣitameveti pariharati---<q>na tena gatamidamadhikaraṇaṃ pravṛtta-
śabdasyāśravaṇāt</q> । na hi svarūpeṇa haviṣo'bhyudayaḥ saṃbhavati kiṃ tarhi ?
prabṛttasya । na cātra pravṛttaśabdaḥ śrūyate 1tena punaḥ śrutyavagatameva niruptatvaviśeṣaṇamastu
tasyaiva śrutatvāt ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntamāha---<q>satyaṃ pravṛttaśabdo na śrūyate tathāpi yasyābhyudi-
yāditi pravṛttyavagamāta na viśeṣaṇaviṣayameva vyavasthāpayituṃ kṣamam</q> ।
yasyābhyudiyādityukte pravṛttatvaṃ haviṣo'vagamyate । pravṛttaṃ hyabhyudayo bhavati । tenābhyudi-
<note>1. artha vibhāgataḥ- mā</note>
<note>2. kena-mā</note>﻿
<pb n="169"/>
yādityasmin‍neva pade pravṛttāvagamāt niruptaviśeṣaṇamaparanaimittikaṃ na viśeṣamava-
sthāpayitumarhati yasyābhyudiyāditi---[bhyupa]gamāditi । tasmāt pravṛttaśabde śrute
cāśrute ca na kaścidviśeṣaḥ । <q>darśanamuktam</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 4 ।। anirupte'bhyudite prākṛtībhyo nirvapedityāśmarathyaḥ
taṇḍulabhūteṣvapanayāt ।। 16 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nirupte'nirupteca abhyudite prākṛtībhyo devatābhyaḥ agnyādibhyo
nirvāpa iti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate</q> taṇḍulabhūtānāmeva devatāpanayaśravaṇāt । <q>nanu
ca pravṛttamātra havirabhyuditaṃ nimittamityuktam । tena pravṛttamātrasya devatā-
panayāt kathaṃ prākṛtībhyo nirvāpa iti</q> । pariharati---<q>satyamuktam</q> ।</p>
<p>nanu <q>naimittikaṃ tu taṇḍulameteṣviti vadāmaḥ</q> yadyapi pravṛttamātraṃ havirnimitaṃ
tathāpi devatāvibhāgātmakaṃ naimittikaṃ taṇḍulaśabdaśravaṇāt । taṇḍulāvasthāyāmeveti
prāga[na]panītatvāddevatāyāḥ prākṛtībhya eva nirvāpaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>atrocyate---naimittike'pi taṇḍulā atantramityuktam । vibhāga-
mātravidhānāt</q> । devatābhyo havirvibhajedityukte havirmātrasya vibhāgo'vagamyate
tena taṇḍulagrahaṇamavivakṣitamityuktam । abhyuditaṃ tu haviḥ vibhajanīyamiti śāstrārthaḥ ।
tasmāt naimittikebhyo nirvāpa iti rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 5 ।। vinirupte na muṣṭīnāmapanayastadguṇatvāt ।। 17 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>yadavasthasyaiva haviṣo'bhyudayaḥ tadavasthayaiva devatāpa(nna)nayo'stu
tatpūrvako devatāntarebhya eva nirvāpaḥ</q> ।</p>
<p><q>nanvevaṃ avaghāto'pi tarhi kimiti dadhipayasā yuktānāṃ na bhavati ।
ucyate । kṣodiṣṭhādibhedabhin‍nānāṃ dadhyādisambandhādavaghātottarakālameva
dadhipayassaṃsargaṃ kṛtvā pākaḥkartavya iti । vinirupte sāminirupte prākṛtībhya
eva nirvāpaḥ pravṛttaḥ । pariśiṣṭamapi muṣṭa‍yantaraṃ prākṛtībhya eva nirvaptavyam</q>
nirvāpe prākṛtīnāmevābhipravṛttatvāt । na ca padārthāntaraṃ muṣṭaya iti pañcame uktam ।
<q>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate-apanayanamavagamyate</q> durdarśassa(ma/?/)bhavati । tasmādvaikṛtīnāṃ
apanaye kṛte sati āpāditahavissambandhānāmuddeśenaiva nirvāpaḥ kartavya iti prāpte
rāddhānto'bhidhīyate---</p>﻿
<pb n="170"/>
<p><q>tūṣṇīṃ nirvāpaḥ kartavyaḥ apanayāvagamāt ekatvācca nirvāpasya (na
niruptapayassambhavaḥ) ।</q> asyārthaḥ - pūrvadevata muddeṣṭuṃ na śakyate । apanītatvāt ।
na devatāntaramapi yojayitu śakyate, caturmuṣṭinirvāpasyaikapadārthātmakatvāt । na ca
muṣṭa‍yantaraṃ pṛthak‌padārthaḥ । nacaikasmin padārthe devatādbayaṃ sambhavati, anyonyavirodhāt ।
na ca devatāvayavasya devatāsambandhaḥ ityanuddeśā parisamāptiḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 6 ।। sānnāyyasaṃyogānnāsannayataḥ syāt ।। 21 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nanu carvavasthasyāvidhānāt naivātra pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ sambhavati</q> । yadi sānnā-
yyādhikaraṇe carvavasthā vihitā syāt tadā sānnāyyābhāvena na syāt asānnāyyayājino
naimittikam । na carvavasthā vihitetyuktam ।</p>
<p>samādhate-<q>astyatra kācidāśaṅkā । nahyasati śṛte dadhani vā carvavasthā
puroḍāśasya sambhavati iti manvānaḥ sān‍nāyyayājina eva naimittikaṃ
sambhavatīti pūrvapakṣayati</q> । anuvādabhūtāpi carvavasthā sānnāyyayājina eva
sambhavatīti tasyaiva naimittikamiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntastu---<q>udakenāpi carvavasthāsaṃbhavāt nimittasya cāviśeṣa-
śravaṇāt naimittikasya ca devatāsambandhamātraparatvādadhikaraṇārtho na
vivakṣitaḥ iti</q> ।</p>
<p>yadyapi vivakṣitā carvavasthā, tathāpi udakenāpyasau sampadyata eveti aviśeṣeṇa
śrutaṃ naimittikaṃ na śakyate viśeṣeṇa sānnāyyayājinyavasthāpayitum । paramārthatastu
devatāntarasambandhamātraṃ naimittikam । adhikaraṇārthastvarthaprāpta iti । avivakṣitārthatvāt
carvarthasya yatrānuvādassambhavati tatrāsau bhaviṣyati । na punastabdalena vidhireva saṅkoca-
yituṃ nyāyya iti asannayato'pi naimittikamityuktam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 7 ।। sāmyutthāne viśvajit krīte vibhāgasaṃyogāt ।। 25 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nanu cāsannayato'ṣyuktameva । anantaraṃ tenaiva akrītarājakasyāpīti
labhyate kā atra abhyadhikāśaṅkā yā nivartyate</q> । yathā pūrvasmin adhikaraṇe
'viśeṣeṇa nimittaśravaṇāt asannayato'pi naimittikamityuktam । tathā'trāpi sāmyu-
tthānasyāviśeṣeṇa śravaṇāt akrītarājakasyāpi naimittikena bhavitavyamiti labdhameva ।
kimityadhikaraṇāntarāmbhaḥ ।</p>﻿
<pb n="171"/>
<p>samādhatte---<q>astyatrābhyadhikāśaṅkā-tatra hi taṇḍulaśravaṇāt adhi-
karaṇārthasyāvivakṣitatvāt yuktamasannayato'pīti । iha punaḥ akrītarājako
naiva śrūyate <quote>‘somamapabhajya’</quote> iti ca krītarājakāvagamāt vibhāgasya cānya-
trānupapatteḥ naimittikānurodhena nimittasaṅkocaṃ pūrvapakṣavādī manyate---yathā
ag‍nī ādadhīta iti ।</q> asyārthaḥ---taṇḍulaśabdaśravaṇāt auṣadhe'pi naimittikāva-
gamāt asannayato'pi cauṣadhasambhavāt, adhikaraṇārthasya vākyabhedaprasaṅgenāvivakṣita-
tvāt, arthaprāptatvāccāsannayato'pi naimittikamiti yuktam । iha punarakrītarājakasya
śravaṇameva nāsti । pratyuta naimittike somamapabhajya viśvajitā yajeteti śrūyate । tena
somavibhāgaviśiṣṭasya naimittikasya vidhānāt krītarājakasyaiva tathābhūtanaimittikānuṣṭhāna-
sambhavāt । yathā ca tatrodakenāpi carvavasthā asānnāyyayājino'pi śakyate vak‍tuṃ
tathā iha nākrītarājakena somavibhāgaśśakyata iti viśiṣṭanaimittikānusāreṇa krīte
rājani sāmyutthānaṃ nimittamiti kalpyate । yathā---yasyobhāvagnī anugatau
ityatra ।</p>
<p><q>atrocyate । satyaṃ, yuktamādhāne 1ekopāyatvena avagamāt ādhā-
nasya । somamapabhajyeti iha sarvadravyavibhāge prāpte lakṣaṇayā nāvagamyata
iti na nimittasaṅkocāyoktam ।</q></p>
<p>asyārthaḥ - yadi naimittikamevedaṃ somavibhāgaviśiṣṭaṃ syāt kiṃ yatra bahūnāṃ
sahapravṛttānāṃ madhye ekīkṛtadhanānāṃ sāmyutthāne prāpnotyevāyaṃ dravyavibhāgaḥ । sa ca
lakṣaṇayā somamapabhajyetyanūdyate । yo hi krītarājakastasyāpi somavibhāgaḥ prāptatvāt
na vidheya eva kintvanūdyata iti siddhe'nuvāde lakṣaṇāpi na doṣaḥ । tasmāt pravṛttā-
nāmutthāne viśvajiditi krītarājakānāṃ ceti yuktam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 8 ।। dīkṣāparimāṇe yathākāmyaviśeṣāt ।। 27 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>jyotiṣṭome bahūni dīkṣāparimāṇāni śrūyante । tatra saṃśayaḥ । kiṃ
tatra sarvaiḥ parimāṇaiḥ adhikriyante, uta ekenaiveti ।</q> anenādhikaraṇasyā-
dhyāyasaṅgatimāha । <q>yathāviniyogamadhikārāvagamāt sarvairiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</q>
<note>1. ekotpatyatvenānava-mā</note>﻿
<pb n="172"/>
sarveṣāṃ parimāṇānāṃ viniyuktatvāt sarvairevādhikāraḥ tadā dvādaśarātrīrdīkṣito bhṛrti
vanvītetyayaṃ 1[pākṣiko]dvādaśadīkṣa eva draṣṭavyaḥ ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntamāha---<q>dvādaśarātrīrdīkṣito bhṛtiṃ vanvīteti nityaśravaṇāt na
pakṣāntare upapadyata iti ।</q> dvādaśaparimāṇa evādhikāraḥ dvādaśarātrīrdīkṣitasya
bhṛtivananaṃ nityavadadhikāraśravaṇāt । parimāṇāntarapakṣe ca tadanupapatteḥ dvādaśapari-
māṇenaivādhikāraḥ । parimāṇāntarāṇi tu vikṛtāvutkṛṣyante ।</p>
<p><q>kathaṃ punaradhikāravaśāt viniyogotkarṣaḥ</q> yāvatā viniyogavaśenaiva tu
kimityadhikāro na varṇyata iti bhāvaḥ ।</p>
<p>pariharati---<q>adhikāraparyantatvādviniyogaśāstrāṇāmiti yuktam ।</q>
pradhānatvādadhikārasya tadanurūpo viniyogī nyāyya iti । tiryagadhikaraṇe tu adhi-
kārāvirodhāt yathāviniyogamadhikāravyavastheti darśitam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 9 ।। paurṇamāsyāmaniyamo'viśeṣāt ।। 30 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>dīkṣādhikāre paurṇamāsīśravaṇe saṃśayaḥ---kimaviśeṣeṇa yā kācit
paurṇamāsī grāhyā uta kācit viśiṣṭaiva caitrī māghī veti ।</q></p>
<p><q>tatra pūrvapakṣavādī aviśeṣaṃ manyate, vākyaśeṣasāmarthyayorvirodhāt ।</q>
vākyaśeṣe caitrīsaṅkīrtanāt caitrīpaurṇamāsīti pratibhāti । teṣāmekāṣṭakāyāṃ krayassampadyata
ityasya sāmarthyāt mādhīti । tena virodhāt anayoḥ parasparavyāghātenāsādhakatvāt
aniyama eva । yā kācitpaurṇamāsī grāhyā ।</p>
<p><q>aparastvāha---na hi sāmānyajñānaṃ vākyaśeṣaṃ vihantumarhati tena
caitryeva grāhyā ।</q> yadyapi paurṇamāsīśabdāt sāmānyajñānaṃ tathāpi vākyaśeṣāt
viśeṣo'vagamyate । nanu liṅgena krayasāmarthyena tadviruddhamityuktam । liṅgaṃ tarhi
niyāmakaṃ bhavatu yena tadapodyate ।</p>
<p>aniyamavādyāha---<q>etadeva na vijānīmaḥ anayoḥ vākyaśeṣasāmarthyayoḥ
kiṃ kena bādhyata iti ।</q> sundopasundanyāyena parasparamanayoḥ parāhatayoḥ
aniyama eva ।</p>
<note>1. yaḥpādaḥ - mā</note>﻿
<pb n="173"/>
<p>rāddhāntamāha---<q>ucyate । bāḍhaṃ jñāyate liṅgena vākyaśeṣo bādhyate ।</q>
sāmarthyaṃ hi adhikāre'bhyarhitam । vinā ca sāmarthyenādhikārābhāvāt । tena sāmarthyasya
valīyastvāt vākyaśeṣo'podyate । vākyaśeṣasya guṇavādenāpyupapatteḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu ca mādhyāṃ kāryasambandhinyāṃ caitryāḥ stutiranupapannā । tatrāha---
<q>vidheyāntarastutyarthatayaivāyamupanyāso jartilavat ।</q> yathā payovidhau jartilastutiḥ
tathā māghīvidhau caitrīstutiḥ । caitryeva sādhvī māghīṃ tvapekṣya nāpi jaghanyeti
tasmāt sāmarthyenaiva viśeṣagrahaṇam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 10 ।। dīkṣākālasya śiṣṭatvādatikrame niyatānāmanu-
tkarṣaḥ prāptakālatvāt ।। 38 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>iha pākādīnāṃ yāvaddīkṣākālaṃ paryudāsaṃ manvānaḥ pūrvapakṣavādī
anutkarṣaṃ manyate । dīkṣito na dadāti ityanena</q> yāvaddīkṣā puruṣasya śāstrataḥ
tāvat paryudāsaḥ pākādīnām śāstrataśca niyatakālaiva dīkṣā । tena 1dīkṣīnmoca-
nasya 2utkarṣepi pākādayaḥ kartavyā eveti ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu---nāyaṃ kālaparyudāsateti3 । yadi kālaṃ payudasyeta
bhaveyuḥ pākādayaḥ na tvayaṃ kālaparyudāsaḥ ।</q> dīkṣitasya hi atrānadhikāraḥ ।
dīkṣitatvaṃ cānuvartata eva [ā] avamṛthāt । tasmāt yāvat dīkṣitaḥ tāvat paryudāsa
eveti yuktaḥ pākādīnām ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 11 ।। tatra pratihomo na vidyate yathā pūrveṣām ।। 40 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>kālotkarṣe kiṃ pratihomāḥ kartavyā neti cintyate</q> ityanenākṣep‍tumanu-
bhāṣate ।</p>
<p>ākṣipati---<q>kathaṃ punaratra pratihomāśaṅkā ? dīkṣitaḥ paryudasta ityuktam ।</q>
asyārthaḥ---kartavyasya akaraṇe pratihomakriyā sambhavati । na ca dīkṣitasyādhikāraḥ
pākādiṣvasti । ato'kartavyānāmevākṛtatvāt na pratihomāśaṅkā yuktā । samādhatte---
<q>prāk‌pramādānniyataṃ nityaśāstraṃ manyate'</q>pramāda iva । asyārthaḥ-nityaśāstrāṇi
<note>1. dīkṣāmo - mā</note> 
<note>2. utkarṣopi - mā</note>
<note>3. paryudasyeteti - mā</note>﻿
<pb n="174"/>
homādiviṣayāṇi niyatāni prāk‌pramādāt । yāvat pramādo na nipatati । avabhṛtho-
tkarṣahetuḥ dīkṣitatvānuvṛttikāraṇam । tāvatpuruṣasya homādayaḥ kartavyā eva । yathā-
tataśca pramāde'pi āpatite dīkṣitena ye homādayo na kṛtāḥ te kartavyā eva santo na
kṛtāḥsyuḥ । tasmāt pratihomāḥ kartavyā iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu---satyamapramāde niyataḥ kālaḥ । anadhikārāttu dīkṣita-
syākaraṇameva homānām । adhikāradvāratvānniyamasya ।</q> asyārthaḥ---yasya
pramādo nāsti tasya homānāṃ niyataḥkālaḥ । yasya punaḥ pramādo nipatati tasya
dīkṣitatvenānadhikārāt pratihomānāmakaraṇameva adhikāradvāratvānniyamasya । 1<q>niyamo
hi homānāṃ adhikārivaśenaiva । yasya hi jīvanavato nityamadhikāraḥ tasya
nityamanuṣṭhānam । na cādhikāraḥ prāgeva bhavati ।</q> kintu aharaharadhikāro-
'pyāvartate । dīkṣitasya adhikāraḥ paryudasta iti adhikārābhāvānna homānāṃ karta-
vyateti kimu ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 12 ।। pratiṣedhāccordhvamavabhṛthādiṣṭeḥ ।। 42 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>dīkṣonmocanottarakālaṃ pramādādiṣṭyutkarṣe sati aparaṃ dīkṣitasya
pratihomaḥ kartavya iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</q> asyārthaḥ---<quote>‘dīkṣito na dadāti na juhoti
na pacati’</quote> iti dīkṣitasya paryudāsaḥ kṛtaḥ । kṛtāvabhṛthaśca unmuk‍tadīkṣo na
dīkṣitaḥ, yadyapi punarādheyasammiterṣṭina kṛtā । tenāparyudastatvāt pramādādiṣṭyutkarṣe'pi
homādiṣvadhikārāt ye homā na kṛtāḥ teṣāṃ pratihomāḥ kartavyā iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>etayā punarādheyasasmitayeṣṭyeti kramamātraṃ vacanam । tena kramānu-
grahāyodavasānīyāṃ kṛtvaiva pratihomāḥ kariṣyanta iti manyate ।</q></p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu satyaṃ nāsti paryudāsaḥ। adhikāro'pi naivāsti ।
adhikārāntaraśravaṇāt punarādheyasammitayeṣṭyeti ।</q> asyārthaḥ---jīvanamiva
kṛtodavasānīyatvamapi adhikāriviśeṣaṇānupraveśīti akṛtodavasānīyasyānadhikāraḥ ।
na tatrānadhikṛtasya niyamo'stīti na kartavyāḥ । samānakartṛkatā hi ktvāpratyayasyārthaḥ ।
na ca paraspara[ā]sambandhayoragnihotrodavasānīyayoḥ samānakartṛkatā sambhavati । tatra yadi
kṛtodavasānīyaḥ puruṣaḥ agnihotre'dhikārī bhavati tadā'dhiṣṭhānaikyenāpi tāvat
samānakartṛkatā nātīva dūrojjhitā bhavati । kramaparatve sā atyantabādhitā syāt ।</p>﻿
<pb n="175"/>
<lg><l>।। 13 ।। pratihomaś‍cet sāyamagnihotraprabhṛtīni hūyeran ।। 43 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>ekasmin kāle paryavasthitānāṃ pratihomānāṃ kramaniyamapramāṇā-
bhāvāt aniyama iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । rāddhāntastu yataḥpramādaḥ tataḥ prabhṛtyeva
kartavyā iti ।</q> atipannapratisamādhānamatipannakrameṇaiva kartavyamiti bhāvaḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 14 ।। prātastu ṣoḍaśini ।। 44 ।।</l></lg>
<p>1atra keṣāṃ citsāyaṃ, ṣoḍaśini prātariti vyavasthāpradarśanārthaṃ ca ṣoḍaśinaḥ
pṛthak grahaṇam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 15 ।। prāyaś‍cittamadhikāre sarvatra doṣasāmānyāt ।। 45 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q><quote>‘bhinne juhoti’</quote> <quote>‘skan‍ne juhoti’</quote> iti śrūyate । tatra sandehaḥ-
kiṃ nimittaparyanta evāyamadhikāraḥ uta kāryaparyanta iti ।</q> anena bhāṣya-
kārīyasaṃśayo vyākhyātaḥ । yadi hi bhedanavataḥ, svatantro'yamadhikāraḥ syāt ।
atha tu kāryaparyantaḥ, prakṛtakratūpakāraparyanto'yamadhikāraḥ tadā darśapūrṇamāsayoreva
bhedane sati homaḥ tadaṅgabhūtaḥ kartavya iti ।</p>
<p><q>asādhyatvādadhikāriviśeṣaṇasya nimittaparyanta evāyamadhikāra iti
pūrvapakṣavādī manyate ।</q></p>
<p>yatra hi sādhyamadhikāriviśeṣaṇaṃ bhavati tatra hi kāryaparyanto'dhikāro bhavati ।
atra tu na sādhyamadhikāriviśeṣaṇamiti na kāryaparyantatā yuktā । sā(tu)caivamanupakāra-
[ka]syāṅgasyānupapatteḥ sarvatra jyotiṣṭomādiṣvapi bhedanenaiva tatrāhitāgnerhomā bhavanti ।</p>
<p><q>nimittāviśeṣāt anāhitāg‍neḥ kimiti na bhavati ?</q> uttaraṃ---
<q>homavidhānāt । na hyāhavanīye homaḥ saṃbhavatīti ।</q> naimittikānurodhena nimitta-
saṅkocaḥ ādhānavat । nātra tirohitamiva kiñcidasti ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---kāryaparyanta evāyamadhikāraḥ ।</q> kutaḥ ? <q>darśa-
pūrṇamāsādhikārasyaiva prakṛtatvāt । niyogaikyāvagatirna śakyate'pahantum ।</q></p>
<note>1. ataḥ mā</note>﻿
<pb n="176"/>
asyārthaḥ-bhinne juhoti iti bhedanaṃ nimittatayā śrūyate । na sākṣādadhikāriviśeṣaṇa-
tayā । nimittabhāvastvadhikāraikanibandhane'nuṣṭhāne'nyathānupapanna iti arthādadhikāri-
viśeṣaṇatā kalpanīyā । darśapūrṇamāsādiniyogaśca sākṣācchrutādhikāraḥ । tatsannidhau
yanniradhikāramavagamyate tenāpi sa evānvitaḥ upanīyata iti ekaniyogatā tāvadava-
gamyate । kathaṃ ca sā bhavati ? yadi karaṇopakāraṃ nirvartayati (iti) nānyathā ।
tena kāryaparyantatvāddarśapūrṇamāsāṅgamevedam ।</p>
<p><q>nanu caivaṃ sati adhikāravirodhaḥ prāp‍noti yasmādanyadevādhikāra-
nimittam ।</q> adhikārasya nimittamadhikāranimittaṃ adhikāriviśeṣaṇaṃ bhedanam
anyacca kāryaṃ darśaṃpūrṇamāsopakāralakṣaṇam । svargādikaṃ adhikāriviśeṣaṇaṃ kāryaṃ caikameva ।
<q>ucyate । na virodhaḥ । adhikāro hi adhikāriviśeṣaṇaṃ niyojyatāmā-
pādayati । niyuktasya ca kāryamavagamyamānaṃ nādhikāraṃ niruṇaddhi ।
tasyaiva tadavagamāt ।</q> yadi kāryaṃ kalpyamānamadhikāriviśeṣaṇameva nirundhyāt tato
virodhāt na kāryamāśrīyate । avirodhe tu kāryakalpanā nānupapannā । tasyaivādhikṛtasya
kāryāvagamāt nādrīyetetyatrāha---<q>jīvane punaḥ kāryāntarānavagamāt nimitta-
paryantataiva yuktā ।</q></p>
<p>nanu kimiti 1nimittaṃ kāryamavekṣate । jīvane'pi kimiti na kalpyate ।
atha tu nāpekṣate kathaṃ tarhi yatra kāryaṃ svīkriyata ityanenābhiprāyeṇa pṛcchati---
<q>atha kasmānna parikalpyate kāryaṃ ? ucyate । na niyogaḥ kalpanāṃ viṣahate ।
niyogasiddha‍yaiva caritārthatvāt ।</q> jīvanādhikāre'pi (vi)niyogaḥ kāryabhūtaḥ
pratīyate । tenaiva caritārthatvāt na paraṃ kāryaṃ kalpyate । <q>pratīyamānaṃ(na)punarnā-
panhotuṃ śakyate svārthaviśeṣāt</q> yathā hi---niyogo'tra sādhyabhūtaḥ pratīyate tathā
karaṇopakāro'pi । tena pratīyamānasyāpahnavo'nupayuktaḥ । yasmāt kāryaparyanto'ya-
madhikāraḥ tasmāt darśapūrṇamāsādhikṛtasyaiva bhedanavato'dhikāraḥ, nāgnihotre
jyotiṣṭome vā । adhikṛtasyopadeśātideśayoḥ pramāṇayorabhāvāt ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 16 ।। vyāpannasyāpsu gatau yadabhojyamāryāṇāṃ tatpratīyeta ।। 48 ।।</l></lg>
<note>1. nimittakārya</note>﻿
<pb n="177"/>
<p>adhikaraṇamadhyāyasaṅgatiṃ darśayan kasya vyāpattyeti na vidma iti vadannava-
tārayati---<q>vyāpattimato'psu praharaṇaṃ śrūyate---<quote>‘vyāpannamapsu praharet’</quote></q> iti ।
vyāpattimataḥ puruṣasyādhikṛtasyāpsu praharaṇaṃ śrūyate । <q>na jñāyate kasya vyāpatti-
mata iti ।</q> kiṃ tat vyāpannaṃ yasya vyāpattyā vyāpattimān puruṣa iti na jñāyate ।
yadi vyāpattiradhikāriviśeṣaṇaṃ kathaṃ tarhi vyāpannasyaiva praharaṇam । ekamidaṃ
vyāpannapadaṃ nādhikāriṇaṃ (karma)viśeṣṭuṃ karma ca 1samarpayitumalamityarthaḥ ।</p>
<p>uttaraṃ-<q>tatkathamityapekṣāyāmadhikārāvagamāt</q> । asyārthaḥ-karmasamarpaṇārtha-
meva vyāpannapadamāmnātam । arthāt tasyādhikāriviśeṣaṇatvam । kena prakāreṇa ?
ucyate---tadva‍yāpannasyāpsu praharaṇaṃ kathaṃ sambhavati । yadi vyāpattimad‍dravya evādhikārī
bhavati evamarthādadhikārikalpanāyāṃ na doṣaḥ । atra ca vyāpannaśabdena kiṃ grahītavya-
mityajñānameva pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu---kiṃ taditi viśeṣānavagamāt yāvatkāryakāraṇatayā
kiñ‍ciddūṣitam ।</q> etadeva vispaṣṭayati---<q>śiṣṭānāṃ kāryaṃ pratyayogyaṃ kṛta-
mityartho vyāpannaśabdasya ।</q> yata evaṃ vyāpaṃnna atastadapekṣo'yamadhikāraḥ ।
śiṣṭānāṃ kāryaṃ prati ayogīkṛtaṃ dravyaṃ yasya tasya vyāpannapraharaṇamiti siddham ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 17 ।। vibhāgaśruteḥ prāyaścitaṃ yaugapadye na vidyate ।। 49 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>apacchede saṃśayaḥ-kimekaikenādhikriyate uta dvābhyāmapīti ।</q> anena
bhāṣyakārīyasya saṃśayasya kāraṇamupanyastam । yadyekaikenāpacchedenādhikriyate tadā
dvayoryugapat apacchede prāyaścittaṃ na kartavyam । 2ataḥ dvābhyāmadhikriyate ।
apacchedaśabdena cātra vibhāgaphalā kriyā'bhipretā ।</p>
<p>saṃśayamākṣipati---<q>nanu ca dūyoḥ kathaṃ saṃbhavaḥ?</q> dvayoḥ apaccheda kriyayoḥ
kathaṃ sambhavaḥ । ekaikevetyarthaḥ । samādhatte---<q>etadevātra vicāryate kiṃ yugapat-
kālayordvayoḥ ekatā bhavati, uta tatrāpi ekakālatāmātrameva । ekaikaiva
tatrāpyadhikāraheturiti ।</q> asyārthaḥ-phalapradarśanamukhenaitadevātra vicāryate kimekasmin
<note>1. samāpayituṃ</note>
<note>2. atha-mā</note>﻿
<pb n="178"/>
kāle ekaivāpacchedakriyā puruṣadvayasamavāyinī bhavati । tataśva tasyā ekena vyapadeṣṭu-
maśakyatvāt anyatarasya vyapadiṣṭe cāpacchede prāyaścittavidhānānna bhavitavyaṃ
prāyaścittena uta apacchedakriye nirapekṣayoreva puruṣayoḥ pratyekaṃ parisamāpte ।</p>
<p>yadi paramekakālamātravartinyau tataścobhābhyāṃ vyapadiṣṭāvapacchedau yugapat dvausta
iti bhavitavyameva prāyaściteneti ।</p>
<p><q>tatra pūrvapakṣavādī kālaikyādekamevāpacchedaṃ manyate ।</q> kālaikyanibandha-
no'yaṃ bhramaḥ ekaiveyamapacchedakriyā puruṣadvayasamavāyinīti manyate । ekadravyamaguṇaṃ
karmeti ca prakriyāmātraṃ padārthavidāmityavalopaḥ, anyatareṇa puruṣeṇa vyapadeṣṭumaśa-
kyatvāt ubhayādhiṣṭhānamekakartṛtvam । tasmāt dvābhyāmevāyaṃ vyapadiśyate ।<p>
<p>anyatareṇa puruṣeṇa vyapadiśyamāno'pacchedaḥ adhikāraheturityuktam । ato na
yaugapadye'dhikāraḥ ekayaiva kriyayā'numitayā phalopapatteḥ na kriyāntarānumāne kāraṇa-
mastīti gūḍho'bhiprāyaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>atrocyate---na dvābhyāṃ vyapadeṣṭuṃ śakyate'pacchedaḥ dva‍yadhiṣṭhānā
apacchedakriyā ekā na bhavati, itaranirapekṣatvāt kartṛbhāvasya ।</q> tasmādi-
taretarayuktayoḥ kartṛtvamiha na bhavati । kartṛtvābhiprāyeṇa nirapekṣatokteti siddhāntyabhi-
prāyamabuddhvā codayati---<q>kathaṃ punarapacchedo na dvitīyamapekṣate ।</q> apādānabhūta-
dvitīyānapekṣā'pacchedakriyaiva nopapadyata iti bhāvaḥ ।</p>
<p>uttaraṃ---<q>apekṣata eva dvitīyamapaccheda iti sanmātratayā'pādānatvena ।
na tu vyapadeśyasya ।</q> tathā na kartṛtayā'pekṣate । vyapadeśaścātra kartṛtayā'pekṣate ।
vyapadeśaścātra kartṛbhāveneti । vyapadeśyavyadeśatāniṣedhena kartṛtvaṃ niṣedhati ।</p>
<p><q>kathaṃ punaḥ pratyekamubhayasaṃpādye dve kriye kathyete ? ucyate । ekaikā-
pacchedadaśāyāṃ yādṛśamekaikagatatatphalaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tathābhūtameva dvayorapi avagamyata
iti dvayorapi kriyānumānamaviruddham ।</q> ataḥ samarthitamidaṃ bhagavataḥ kāśyapasya
sūtraṃ <quote>“ekadravyamaguṇaṃ saṃyogāvibhāgeṣvanapekṣakāraṇaṃ karma”</quote> iti । (1-1-17)
karmalakṣaṇam । tasmāt yugapajjñāpitāyāmapi siddhamekaikasyādhikārahetutvaṃ tattaddhaviḥ
prati ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 18 ।। tatra vipratiṣedhādvikalpaḥ syāt ।। 51 ।।</l></lg>﻿
<pb n="179"/>
<p>idamidānīṃ cinyate । kiṃ naimittikayorvikalpaḥ uta samuccaya iti ।
yadā sthitaṃ yaugapadye(na) nimittadvayamastīti tadā naimittikadvaye cintopapadyate kiṃ
samuccayaḥ uta vikalpa iti । tatra virodhāt vikalpa iti vadāmaḥ ।
sarvasvādākṣiṇyayoḥ virodhāt yugapadupasaṃhartumaśakyatvāt vikalpa eva nyāpya iti
rāddhāntaḥ । <q>atha kasmāt tadanurodhena naimittikāṅgadvayānurodhena nāvṛttiḥ
kalpyate pradhānasyaiva, tena dvayamapyupasaṃhariṣyate ।</q></p>
<p>pariharati---<q>nāṅgānurodhena ।</q> atha kasmāt dvirna pradhānasyāvṛrttiryuktā ? ।
pradhānaṃ hi aṅgasya prayojanaṃ nāṅgaṃ pradhānasya । tenāṅgānurodhena pradhānasyāvṛttirnopapadyate ।
aṅgatā caivaṃ vidhānāt naimittikānāmuktā vācanikyāṃ punaḥ tato dvitīyaṃ naimittikaṃ
bhaviṣyatīti cet । neti [brūmaḥ nā] pacchede(ḥ) [prāyaściyoḥ] samuccayaḥ, prathama-
prayogāṅgatvena(ā) nirjñānāt । yadeva hi prathamaprayogāṅgatayā vijñātaṃ tadeva punaḥ
ta(tra)tra kartavyam, na prathamaprayoge dvayoraṅgatā, kintvekasyaiva । tenāṅgatvād‌dvitīyasya
punasta(āva)[trāpya]pyananupraveśaḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu yathā vrīhiyavayordvayorapi viniyogādaṅgatā tathehāpi dvayoraṅgatā kimiti
na bhavati iti atrāha---<q>prayoge'pyadhikāradvārā viniyujyate na karmaṇītyuk‍ta-
mabhyudayeṣṭyadhikaraṇe ।</q></p>
<p>yatpunaḥ nimittasambandhenādhikāriṇamāśritya vidhīyate tatprayogāṅgatayaiva
vidhīyate । na ca prayoge dvayoranupraveśasaṃbhavaḥ । karmaṇi tu viruddhānāmapi sambhavo
bhavatyeva prayogabhedāśrayatvena । tasmādvikalpaḥ । ekaikasya viniyogādekāṅgateti ।
so'yaṃ śāstravikalpaḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 19 ।। paurvāparye pūrvadaurbalyaṃ prakṛtivat ।। 54 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>keyamatra bādhacintā ।</q> anenāsaṅgatiruk‍tā । <q>ayuktā ca sā</q> । anena
yuktiśūnyatoktā । adhikāre tāvadbādhasyānavasara eva । tenātreyaṃ cintā'saṅgatā ।
<q>kathamayuktā ?</q> uttaraṃ---<q>śāstrārthāvadhāraṇakāle hi bādhaścintyate । adhi-
kāradvārakamiṃda bādhacintanam । tacca prayoge । na caikasmin prayoge
viruddhadvayasyāvakāśo'sti tena śās‍trārthāvadhāraṇāyaiveyaṃ cintā । ko
bādhyatāmiti । na punaravadhṛte śāstrārthe bādhaścintyate dāśamikamiva ।</q>﻿
<pb n="180"/>
tathāpi kathamayuktatetyatrāha---<q>śāstrārthāvadhāraṇakāle hi nātra paurvāparyamasti
ekaikasya śāstrasya svārthabodhakatvāt prayoge tu ।</q> tatprayoge ca śakyāśakyatve
kṛtākṛtatve ca । atra tantraṃ prasaṅgo vā । ekagranthenāha---yuktaṃ tāvat kṛtā-
kṛtatve tantraṃ prasaṅgo vā । tantraṃ na prasaṅga iti śakyate vak‍tuṃ kṛtakṛtyatvena
hi tantraṃ bhavati । prasaṅgaśca punaraśakteḥ ।</q> aśaktiścātra na cintyate । nanu mā
(bhūt) bhūtāṃ tantraprasaṅgau bādho bhaviṣyatīti । atrāha---<q>bādho'pi cāvadhṛte śāstrārthe
naivopapadyate</q> tasya bādhitumaśakyatvāditi tṛtīye uktam । upasaṃharati---<q>tasmādanya
evāyaṃ prayoga[ā]śaktijaḥ prayogabādhaḥ । sa cādhikāre na saṅgataḥ yato'yaṃ
prayogabādhaḥ ।</q> tasmānnāyaṃ śāstrārthasya prāptasya bādho na viniyogo bādhyate ।
nāpyaprāptatvaṃ1 śakyate vak‍tuṃ śāstrārthasya yathā tṛtīye na prāptiḥ । tantraprasaṅgayorabhāvaḥ
pradarśita eva ।</p>
<p>samarthaṃyate---<q>bhavatyayamanya eva bādhaprakāro na kaściddoṣa iti ।</q>
ākṣipati---<q>kaḥpunarasyādhikāre prasaṅgaḥ ? ayamasti prasaṅgaḥ---adhikārastu
prayogāya bhavati na karmajñānāya ।</q> jñāte hi karmaṇyadhikriyate । tenādhikāra-
dbārakamidaṃ prayogāntaraṃ vidhīyate ityatraiva cintitatam ।</p>
<p>nanu yadyapi prayogāyādhikāraḥ tathāpi adhikāraśāstrārthāvadhāraṇakāle naiva
paurvāparya[ma]syāsti । tasmiṃścāsati kathaṃ bādhaḥ । maivaṃ bocaḥ, adhikāraśāstraṃ hi
pratiprayogamāvartate । karmajñānaśāstravat sakṛdevāvagatārtho bhavati । yasya ca prati-
prayogamāvṛttiḥ tasya pratiprayogameva śāstrārthāvādhāraṇa2naiva paurvāparye sati prayogopapattau,
prayogadaśāyāṃ tayoraśakyaviṣayaṃ yat dvayoradhikāraśāstrayoḥ ghaṭata evārthāvadhāraṇe
bādhyatā(mi)iti ।</p>
<p><q>atra pūrvaṃpakṣavādī anupajātavirodhitayā pūrvasyaiva satyārthatāṃ mene ।</q>
anupajāto virodho yasya tasyaiva satyārthatā । uttarasya tu tadviruddha evārtho nātmānaṃ
labhate । <q>rāddhāntavādī tu manyate---uttarasyāprāptāvayaṃ hetuḥ pūrvasyānupajāta-
virodhitā ।</q> 3prāptirhi uttarasya anupajātavirodhitāṃ pūrvasya viruṇaddhi na punaḥ
prayogam । iha ca na prāṅniroddha‍uṃ śakyate nimittasya vidyamānatvāt । aśakte tu
<note>1. aprāptatve-mā</note>
<note>2. raṇaṃ</note>
<note>3. aprā-mā</note>﻿
<pb n="181"/>
prayogaḥ paraṃ nivartate । tataścottara eva prayogaḥ pūrvasya bādhako yuktaḥ । aparaḥprayogaḥ
pūrvamabādhitvā (anena) na pratyetu śakyate na punaḥ pūrvaḥ paramabādhitvaiva na pratīyate ।
ato'nupajātavirodhitaivātra prayoge bādhyatve hetuḥ upajātavirodhitā bādhakatve ।</p>
<p>nanu pūrvādhikāre bhūte uttarādhikāraśāstrameva[na]pravartate ityatrāha---<q>pratiprayo-
gāvadhāraṇīyaṃ</q> cādhikāraśastramityuktam । ataḥ kālato'pi yatrāvadhāraṇaṃ daśame
tatropajātavirodhitaiva bādhakatve heturiti darśitam ।</p>
<p><q>yadyupajātavirodhitayā'yaṃ bādhaḥ tadā dāśamika evāyaṃ bādha iti
punaratrāsaṅgatiḥ</q> । pariharati-<q>satyaṃ hetuḥ na punardvārataḥ</q> । upajātavirodhitā yo'yaṃ
bādhe hetuḥ sā tulye tu dāśamika eva syāt dvārantu(stu)bhinnam । tatra hi prayojyāva-
dhṛtiḥ dvāre hetuḥ । iha na prayogāvadhṛtiriti viśeṣaḥ । prayojyāvadhāraṇaṃ prayojye'pi
tatra kṛtakāryatayā prayojyāntaraṃ bādhate । prayogaḥ prayogāntaraṃ aśakteḥ, adhikārā-
śrayā ca codanā prayogaviśeṣaḥ । codanā karmasvarūpacodaneti pradarśitam । tene-
haivāyaṃ bādhaścintanīya iti sarvamupapannam ।</p>
<p>tadayamatra saṃkṣepārthaḥ - pūrvaprayogaviśeṣaḥ sa tasminneva prayoge vidhīyate pratipakṣā-
bhāvāt uttaramapi vākyabalena prayogāntaraṃ pūrvopamardena viviyujyata iti prāptabādha
evāyam । yathā daśame'syāntarbhāvo na bhavati tathā'nantaramevoktamiti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 20 ।। yadyudgātā jaghanyaḥ syāt punaryajñe sarvavedasaṃ dadyāt
yathetarasmin ।। 55 ।।</l></lg>
<p>pūrvaṃ pratiharturapacchede sarvavedasadakṣiṇe prayoge prāpte <q>paścādudgāturapacchedaḥ
tasya balīyastvamuktam anantarādhikaraṇe । adākṣiṇyaṃ cāsya prayogasya
naimittikaṃ; punastataḥ pūrvavaddakṣiṇādānaṃ ca</q> । anena bhāṣyoktaviṣayaḥ spaṣṭīkṛtaḥ ।</p>
<p>tatra saṃśayaḥ । <q>tatra tad‍dadyāt yatpūrvasmin dāsyan syāditi vacana-
balāt kiṃ pratiharturapacchedanimittakaṃ sarvavedasaṃ dadyāt uta prakṛtameva dvādaśa-
śatamiti</p> । anenāpi saṃśayaḥ spaṣṭīkṛtaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>tatra pūrvapakṣavādī kratunimittakaṃ svābhāvikaṃ dāsyannityucyata iti
manvāno dvādaśaśataṃ dadyādityuktavān</q> । asyārthaḥ-yat pūrvasmin prayoge
<pb n="182"/>
deyatvena prāptaṃ taddeyamityukte yatsvābhāvikaṃ deyaṃ tadeva pratīyate nirapekṣatvāt ।
na naimittikaṃ nimittasāpekṣatvāt । sāpekṣanirapekṣayorhi nirapekṣe pratītiḥ śīghratareti
svābhāvikadvādaśaśatameva punastato dātavyam ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu prayogābhiprāyaṃ dāsyannityucyate, na karmābhiprāyam
asyārthaḥ-1atra pūrvasminnityanena pūrvaśavdena na karmocyate ekatvāt karmaṇaḥ pūrvā-
paravyapadeśābhāvāt । kintu prayoga ucyate । tenāyamarthaḥ-yatpūrvasmin prayoge
dātavyaṃ taddadyāditi । pūrvaprayoge ca prakṛtikarturapacchedanimittakaṃ sarvavedasameva teno-
ttarasyāṃ kratau deyam</q> ।</p>
<p><q>nanu ca pūrvadānābhiprāyametat, tatra dvādaśaśatamapyasti । yatkila
pūrvadāne deyaṃ tadabhipretyedamucyate yatpūrvasmin dāsyan syāt tad‍dadyāt
iti</q> । tatra pūrvaṃ deyaṃ dvādaśaśatamapyasti । pūrvaṃprayoge hi viniyogato dvādaśaśata-
mapyasti sarvavedasaṃ ca । ataḥ kathaṃ sarvavedasasyaiva dakṣiṇātvam ।</p>
<p>pariharati---<q>yadyapi dvayamasti tathāpi dvayoranugrahāt sarvavedasameva</q> ।
tasmin dīyamāne dvayamapi dattaṃ bhavati । dvādaśaśatādapyadhikābhiprāyaḥ sarvavedasa-
śabda uktaḥ । tenobhayānugrahaḥ । ūne hi ubhayānugraho na bhavet । etaccātrābhyupa-
gamyavādamātraṃ tathāpīti vacanāt । mūlayuktimāha---<q>na cātra pūrvatāmā-
tramabhipretam । kintu svaprayogābhiprāyaiveyaṃ pūrvatā sā ca sarvavedasa-
dakṣiṇaiva</q> । asyārthaḥ---yasyaiva prayogasya yaḥ punaḥ stutiḥ sa evātra prayogaḥ
pūrvaśabdenoktaḥ na pūrvatāmātram । dvādaśaśataprayogaśca pūrvataḥ । tadupamardena tu
pratiharturapacchedanimittakaḥ parataḥ sarvavedasadakṣiṇaḥ prayogaḥ । tasyaiveyaṃ punaḥ stutiriti
sarvavedasameva deyam ।</p>
<p><q>nanu sāpi sarvavedasadakṣiṇā tatra bādhitā</q>[na]kintu pūrvaprayoge bādhitā
(na punarastīti yukte prayoge) tatra taddadyāditi vacanāt sarvathā na bādhitā kintu
pūrvaprayoge bādhitā punastato deyā । tasmānnātra naimittikaṃ bādhitam । kālamātrasya tu
apahāṇyā pūrvaprayoge dakṣiṇā sā[na]tadānīmeva deyā । kintu punastutau deyā iti
<note>1. yatra-mā</note>﻿
<pb n="183"/>
kālamātrasyotkarṣaḥ । na dakṣiṇābādhaḥ । tataśca yaiva sā prāgbhāvī pratiharturapaccheda-
nimittā saivotkṛṣya dātavyeti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 21 ।। ahargaṇe yasminnapacchedastadāvarteta karmapṛthaktvāt ।। 56 ।।</l></lg>
