<p><q>prayogaviṣayatvādadhikārasya dvādaśāhaviṣayaṃ ca (yaśca) ekaṃ prayogaṃ
manvānaḥ sarvāvṛttiṃ pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । punaryajñena yajeta iti prayoga-
viṣayo'yaṃ naimittiko'dhikāraḥ prayogasyāvṛttimāha</q> dvādaśā[hā]<q>tmakaścāya-
mekaprayogaḥ iti</q> tasyaivāvṛttiriti pūrvapakṣavādyāha । <q>rāddhāntastu---karmaviṣaya-
tvādadhikārasya dvādaśāhe ca karmabhedāt pratikarma naimittikamiti karmaṇa
evāvṛttiḥ na karmagaṇasya</q> । yasminnimittamupapadyate tadīya eva prayogaḥ punarāvartate ।
ekakarmaṇi cedaṃ nimittaṃ, na karmagaṇe dvādaśāhe । ekaikānāṃ karmaṇāmavāntaraprayogāśca
bahava eva, tena karmaṇa ekasyaiva prayogāvṛttiḥ na karmagaṇasya ।</p>
<p>akṣarārthastu---karmaviṣayatvādadhikārasya adhikriyate'ne'neneti vyutpattyā nimitta-
madhikāraśabdenocyate । ataḥ karmaviṣayatvamadhikārasyaivoktam ।</p>
<p><q>iti ṛjuvimalāyāṃ ṣaṣṭhādhyāyasya
pañcamaḥ pādaḥ</q></p>﻿
<pb n="184"/>
<p><q>ṛjuvimalāyāṃ</q></p>
<p><q>।। ṣaṣṭhādhyāsya ṣaṣṭhaḥ pādaḥ ।।</q></p>
<lg><l>।। 1 ।। sannipāte'vaiguṇyāt prakṛtivattulyakalpā yajeran ।। 1 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>idānīmidaṃ śrūyate</q>-adhikṛta viśeṣāṇāṃ <q>śrūyate । tatra bahukalpeṣu karmasu
samānakalpānāmevādhikāraḥ uta bhinnakalpānāmapīti</q> । anubhāṣitamākṣipati-
nanu cādhikṛtaviśeṣaśravaṇe saṃśaya eva nāsti</q> । va[ā]siṣṭhādayo'pyadhikṛtatvenaivātra
sambadhyante, na kartṛtayā prathamopanipātitvādadhikārasya । tataśca nārāśaṃsakalpenaiva
teṣāmadhikārasiddhiriti । itareṣāṃ tanūnapātkalpeneti samānakalpānāmevādhikāro
yuktaḥ । na bhinnakalpānāṃ vaiguṇyāt । samādhatte---<q>satyaṃ kratvarthānapāyādbhavati
saṃśayaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---<q>prayājādayastāvatkratvarthā eva । na puruṣārthāḥ । kratoścaitadubhaya-
maṅgam । tataścaikānuṣṭhāne'pi kratoravaiguṇyam । avaiguṇye va kratoradhikārasiddhirapyadhi-
kṛtānāmiti । atra codayati-<q>kratvarthānapāye kathaṃ punassaṃśayaḥ</q> yāvatā bhinnakalpā-
nāmapyadhikāra ityayameva pakṣaḥ śreyāniti ।</p>
<p>uttaraṃ---<q>satyaṃ na saṃśayaḥ</q>, viparyayameva pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । kathaṃ ?
kratvarthaścennāpaiti na vaiguṇyaṃ śakyate vak‍tum । vaiguṇyāccādhikāravidhātaḥ svamanīṣi-
kayā । asmiṃśca pakṣe vasiṣṭhādiśravaṇamanuvādamātram । kratorvasiṣṭhādisambandhitvāt ।
yataḥ kratorekopādānatve'pi avaiguṇyenāyaṃ pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । evaṃ ca sati kāryasiddhiḥ
sāmānyamātratayā śirovaditi pradarśitam । yathā ṛtapeye ghṛtavratavidhānāt ghṛtaduhi
nivṛttāyāmanyayāpi gavā kāryasiddhiḥ । tathā'nyenāpi dvitīyena prayājenānyaprayāja-
kāryasiddhirityetāvanmātreṇāśiravaditi dṛṣṭāntaḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu aṅgāntarānupasaṃhāre vaiguṇyamityatrāha---<q>kāryārthatvādupadeśopa-
saṃhārasya tasya kāryasiddhāvanupasaṃhāre'pi adoṣa iti</q> । yadvā ubhayasaṃbhave
naikamapi nimittaṃ bhavatīti bṛhadrathantaravaditi pradarśitam । bhinnakalpodayapuruṣasambhave
vasiṣṭhādayo viśvāmitrādayaśca nimittaṃ na bhavanti ekaikasya nimittatvāt । <q>yathā
bṛhat rathantaraṃ ca pratyekaṃ nimittamiti ekasya na nimittatvamiti
naimittikavyāghātaḥ</q> । ayamabhiprāyaḥ---upadeśe'pi tāvadanupasaṃhāra uktaḥ । yadvā
<pb n="185"/>
upadeśa eva bhinnakalpānāṃ puruṣāṇāṃ samāhāraḥ nāstīti । kena punarviśeṣeṇā-
śiravaditi yasmāt yajamānasammitaudumbarī bhavati ityupanyastam । atrāpi
kāryasiddhistulyaiva । uttaraṃ---<q>satyaṃ, kintu parihāre'bhyadhikā śaṅkā'sti</q> ।
tāmanena dṛṣṭāntavyājenopanyasya parihartuṃ bhedena punarupanyāsaḥ । kā punarasau ? tāmāha---
<q>kārakatayaiva kimiti yajamānaśabdo na pravartate <quote>‘ṛtvigvat’</quote> tena(na)kratva-
ntaragatenāpi yajamānena sammānaṃ prāp‍noti</q> । yadā svāmitayā yajamānaśabdo
vartate tadā katvantaravartinā sammānaṃ na bhavati । tasyāsvāmitvāt । kartṛmātraparigrahe tu
tasyāpi kartṛtvāt tenāpi sammānaṃ śakyate kartuṃ tannirākaraṇārthaṃ dṛṣṭāntāntaro-
pādānam ।</p>
<p>nirākaraṇamāha---<q>na kartṛmātratayā grahaṇam adhikṛtamukhenopādāna-
sambhavāt । adhikārapūrvakameva kartṛtvamiti tatpurassarameva kartṛtvaṃ parigṛhyate</q> ।
tenādhikṛtena sammānaṃ kartavyamiti na kratvantaragatayajamānāntaraparigrahaḥ ātmanepadānu-
grahācca svāmyeva grāhyaḥ । na kartṛmātram । ato'dhikṛto yajamāna iti । sthitam ।
upādeyatvāt sammānaṃ prati bahavo na kurvantīti viśeṣo dṛṣṭāntenopādānasya । prathame
punaḥ śirovaditi vyākhyāne yathā puruṣaśīrṣamupadadhāti iti śravaṇāt smṛtibādhaḥ ।
tathehāpi kalpāntareṇa kalpāntarasya bādhaḥ iti । asminnapyaprāptireva draṣṭavyā nimitto-
pasaṃhāravat । kratvarthatve hi śavaśīrṣasya sparśane na pratiṣedhaḥ pravartate । tena dṛṣṭānte-
nātrāprāptireva draṣṭavyā । yathā nimittopasaṃhārapakṣe prāptau ca kalpāntarasya pramāṇaṃ
nāstīti ayukto'yaṃ pakṣaḥ । ata evāparitoṣāt dvitīyā vyākhyā kṛtā ।</p>
<p><q>atrābhidhīyate---nedamāśiravaditi śakyate vak‍tuṃ, nāpi nimittopa-
saṃhāravat</q> । etaduktaṃ bhavati-nāpi nimittopasaṃhāravadaprāptiḥ, nāpyāśiravaditi kṛta-
kṛtyatā sambhavati । kathaṃ tarhi ? adhikṛtaviśeṣaṇaṃ hi etat vasiṣṭhādīnāṃ bhṛgūṇāmiti
ca । tathāpi kimityāha---<q>adhikāradvāraṃ ca prayoge karmasvarūpe sambhavati-
tyuktam</q> । adhikṛtasambandhena prayogaviśeṣo'yaṃ vidhīyate na karmasvarūpam । tathā
ca prayoge kṛtakṛtyatāprāptirapi nāstīti samānakalpānāmevādhikāraḥ ekaprayogatvāditi
sthitam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 2 ।। vacanāt‍tu dvisaṃyogastasmādekasya pāṇitvam ।। 12 ।।</l></lg>﻿
<pb n="186"/>
<p>rājapurohitau sāyujyakāmau yajeyātāmiti śrūyate । tatra saṃśayaḥ---kiṃ
samāsārthāt dvivacanaṃ uta prātipadikārthāditi । yadi samāsārthadvitve dvivacanaṃ tadā
rājñaḥ purohitau dvau yajeyātāṃ (uta)prātipadikārthadvitve tadā rājā purohitaśca
yajeyātāmiti ।</p>
<p><q>nanu itarasminnapi pakṣe samāsārthādeva dvivacanaṃ dvandvo'pi hi samāsa
eva</q> । uttaraṃ-<q>satyaṃ samāsaḥ na tu samāsārthe dvivacanaṃ, samāsināveva dvivaca-
nārthena sambadhyete itaretarayuktau</q> । itaretarayoge hi dvayordundvaḥ । tatra samāsa-
vartibhiḥ padaiḥ svārthāḥ itaretarayuktā eva pratipādyante । na punaḥ padadvayena kaścidarthaḥ
pratipādyate । yadgataṃ tad‌dvitvaṃ hi vacanenocyate । yatra punaḥ samāsārtha eva dvivacanaṃ
tatraikavacanameva bhavati । yathā samāhāre । samāhāre hi yo dvandvaḥ tatra samāhniyamāṇa-
marthadvayaṃ samāhāralakṣaṇārthamucyate । tataśca tasyaikārthyāt ekavacanameva bhavati samāhāre ।
samāhāre hi yo dvandvaḥ tatra samāhriyamāṇe(ma)rthe dvivacanagrahaṇaṃ dvivacanopalakṣaṇārtham ।</p>
<p>nanvevamitaretarayogasyāpi ekatvādekavacanaṃ prāpnoti । na ca dṛśyate,
ke[te]nābhiprāyeṇa pṛcchati---<q>kimita itaretarayogo na samāsārthaḥ</q> yena tatraika-
vacanaṃ na bhavati । atha samāsārthe'pi tasminnekavacanaṃ na bhavati samāhāre'pi na
syāditi bhāvaḥ । uttaraṃ-<q>na samāsārtha iti brūmaḥ upādhimātraṃ hi sa tadā bhavati
samāsināvevetaretarayuktaḥ [ktau] samāsārthaḥ samāsasaṃjña</q>kābhyāṃ padābhyāmucyate ।
yata evetaretarayoge samāsināvevocyete, ata eva ca yugapadadhikāraṇatā ekaśeṣaśca
evaṃvidhaviṣaya eva na samāhāraviṣayaḥ ।</p>
<p>kathaṃ punaryugadapadhikaraṇavacanatā ? na tāvat vācakavṛttyā, sambandhagrahaṇā-
bhāvāt । padāntaraprayogavaiyarthyācca । na ca lakṣaṇāvṛttiḥ sambhavati anupapatterabhāvāt ।
svārthahānaprasaṅgācca । atrocyate । lakṣaṇāvṛttyā yugapadadhikaraṇavacanatā । tathā
hi - dhavakhadirau hi cchindhi ityatra dhavaśabdo dhavamātraṃ bravīti sa dhavārthaḥ, khadira-
sahitāṃ svāvasthāṃ lakṣayati avasthāvasthāvatoḥ sambandhāt । dvivacanaśravaṇaṃ cānupapadya-
mānaṃ lakṣaṇāhetuḥ । tarhi prātipadikārthadvitve sambhavati । na ca dvandve padadvaya-
vyatirekī dviśabdo'sti । samāsapade eva sahitāvasthasvārthamātrapratipādanapare । tadā
tayorapi pratyekaṃ dvitvābhāvāt kimāśritya ghaṭatāṃ dvivacanam । yadā tu samāsapade
itaretarayuktasvārthapratipādanapare bhavataḥ, tadā tathābhūtayorarthayoḥ dvitvaṃ samavetamiti dviva-﻿
<pb n="187"/>
canopapattiḥ । samāse tu pratyekapadābhihitayorarthayoḥ samāhāralakṣaṇatvādupapannameka-
vacanamiti na yugapadadhikaraṇavacanatāyāṃ pramāṇamasti । ekaśeṣe ca tantrābhidhānāt[na]
parasparasahitārthapratipattiḥ । itaretarayoge ca parasparasahitārthapratipattiriti tadapabā/?/da
ekaśeṣaḥ tadviṣaya eva, na samāhāraviṣayo dvandvaḥ pakṣe ।</p>
<p>yadā yugapadadhikaraṇabalāt idamāpadyate uktena nyāyena sahitavacanatā, evaṃ
cet purohitārthagatameva dvitvaṃ nyāyyam । anyathā hi purohitaśabdo rājanyapi
syāt । tatra lakṣaṇāprasaṅgaḥ syāt । kathaṃ punarekasminnevoccāraṇe purohite rājani ca
vartamānaḥ purohitaśabdo lakṣaṇayā vartata iti śakyate vak‍tum । <q>purohite tu śrauta
eva saḥ । na ca śrauto lākṣaṇikaśca sakṛduccārito bhavati</q> । pariharati---<q>satyaṃ
yugapadadhikaraṇaśravaṇabalādidamāpadyate । uktena nyāyena yadā sahitāvasthā-
lakṣaṇatvena yugapadadhikaraṇaṃ tadā śraute lākṣaṇike ca tātparyaṃ bhavati</q> ।
paramārthataśca yanna śrautārthaḥ lākṣaṇika eva । tathā ca darśitaṃ dhavasvadirau ceti । na hi
yugapadadhikaraṇavacanatāṃ vinā dvivacanamupapadyate । ataḥ śraute saṃbhavatyapi lakṣaṇāmaṅgī-
kṛtya heyatvenāyaṃ pakṣaḥ upanyasyate । yadyapi purohitārtho'pyasti tathāpi lakṣaṇā
prāpnotīti । anena doṣeṇa pūrvapakṣavādinā heyatvenāyaṃ dvandvapakṣa upanyastaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>nanu vasānau iti dvitvaṃ puṃstvaṃ ca eṣaśabdo vyabhicarati evamatrāpi
purohitadvitvaṃ caiṣaśabdo na vyabhicaratīti</q> dvitīya'rthe pratipādakatvāt
naiva lakṣaṇāprasaṅga iti । pariharati---<q>vacanābhiprāyaḥ । taduktaṃ puṃstvaṃ dvitvaṃ ca
aukārāntadvivacana na vyabhicaratītyuktam</q> । na prātipadikābhiprāyam ।
prātipadikasya hi yugapadadhikaraṇatvena vinā dvivacanānupapattiḥ । yathā rājapurohitaṃ
ceti । tena yatra dvivacanaṃ tena prātipadikena itaretarayuktaḥ svārthaḥ pratipādanīyaḥ ।
na ca lakṣaṇāṃ vinā tadupapadyate । tasmātsuṣṭhūcyate lakṣaṇeti । lakṣaṇātve heyo'yaṃ
pakṣa iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>nanu ṣaṣṭhīsamāsapakṣe'pi rājaśabdo lākṣaṇika eva ṣaṣṭha‍yarthalakṣakatat</q> ।</p>
<p>pariharati---<q>bhavati । kā no hāniḥ? purohitaśabdamaṅgīkṛtya lakṣaṇā-
tvena na hātavyo'yaṃ pakṣa ityuktam</q> ।</p>﻿
<pb n="188"/>
<p>nanu ca ṣaṣṭhīsamāsapakṣe'pi tasya lakṣaṇātvamanyaparatvādityāha---<q>uttarapada-
pradhāno'yaṃ ṣaṣṭhīsamāsa iti</q> ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---satyamevam । kintu ekatvāt purohitasya
ṣaṣṭhīsamāse'pi dvivacanānupapattireva sambandhiśabdatvāt purohitaśabdasya
dvayoḥ sambandhitvenābhāvāt</q> । asyārthaḥ---purohitaśabdo'yaṃ sambandhiśabdo-
'yam । na caikasya rājño dvo purohitau sambandhinau sambhavataḥ । tena ṣaṣṭhī-
samāse'pi arthābhāvāt dvivacanānupapattireva । tena varaṃ lakṣaṇaivāśrīyatāṃ dvivacanopa-
pattyartham ।</p>
<p>nanu ca viniyogadarśanāt dvau purohitau bhaviṣyataḥ yathā añjalividhānāt
dvau hastau vyāpāryete tatrāha---<q>yatpunarañ‍jalivat ityuktaṃ tadatra na sambhavati ।
asambandhitayaiva dvitīyasya sambandhino'bhāvāt । purohitaṃ vṛṇīta ityeka-
vacanaśravaṇāt</q> । nanu bhavatu sambandhiśabdaḥ purohitaśabdaḥ kāryāntare'pi niyoga
eva sambandhitāmāpādayiṣyati । yo yasya rājñaḥ tāni tāni karmāṇi karoti sa tasya
purohito bhavati iti sambandhidvayasambhavāt tatrāha---<q>utpattiśca sambandhe hetuḥ na
kārye viniyogaḥ etadapekṣatvādviniyogasya</q> । asyārthaḥ-paraṇotpannaḥ purohito
bhavati na punaḥ kāryāntaraviniyojyaḥ purohitatvāpekṣatvāt kāryāntaraviniyogasya ।
tadatra saṅgrahārthaḥ-viniyogataḥ purohitatvaṃ tasya tu varaṇenopasaṅgrahaḥ । tataśca
dvayorviniyogadarśanāt dvayoḥ saṅgrahaḥ viniyogārthatvāt saṅgrahasyeti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntastu purohitasya sataḥ viniyogānuvṛttita eva purohitatvam । utpattau ca
ekavacanaśravaṇāt eka evotpadyata iti dvayoḥ rājñoḥ sambandhinoḥ purohitayoḥ
sāyujyaṃ na bhavatīti pradarśitaṃ bhāṣye । tasmāllakṣaṇaivātra jyāyasī arthasambhavāt ।
<q>liṅgamuktam</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 3 ।। satrāṇi sarvabarṇānāmaviśeṣāt ।। 16 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nanu ca sarvavarṇānāmiti nopapadyate ārvijye yajamānaśravaṇāt</q> ।
asyārthaḥ-prakṛtau brāhmaṇakartṛkamārtvijyaṃ pratipannam । iha tu ārtvijye yajamānaḥ
kartṛtvenocyate <quote>‘ye yajamānāsta ṛtvija’</quote> iti śravaṇāt । yadyabrāhmaṇo'pi satre'dhi-﻿
<pb n="189"/>
kārī syāt tadā tasyārtvijye kartṛtve sati brāhmaṇakartṛtvaṃ bādhyeta । brāhmaṇe hyadhi-
kāriṇi na kaścidbādhyate । nacābādhenopadeśopapattau bādho nyāyya iti brāhmaṇānāme-
vādhikāro yuktaḥ satreṣu ।</p>
<p>na ceyaṃ vacanavyaktiratra cintyate-kiṃ ye yajamānāḥ ta ṛtvija iti
yajamānoddeśenārtvijyaṃ saṃskārakatayā vidhīyate uta ārtvijye yajamānāḥ kartṛtvena
vidhīyanta iti ।</p>
<p>tatra yadi yajamānasaṃskāraḥ tadā ārtvijyaṃ ṛtvigbhireva kartavyamiti sarva-
varṇānāmadhikāro bhavet । yadi tu yajamānānāmārtvijye kartṛtvavidhiḥ tadā brāhmaṇānāṃ
pūrvoktanyāyenādhikāra iti । tena prāpyavacanavyaktyāśrayaṇena sarvavarṇānāmadhikāraśaṅkā
yuktaiva । na ceyamiha cintā yuktā kartuṃ, adhikāralakṣaṇe'saṅgatatvādviniyoganirṇayasya ।
tasmādasaṅgatatvavādināṃ cintāṃ vinā pūrvapakṣo niryuktika iva pratibhāti ।</p>
<p>ucyate । <q>ayamabhiprāyaḥ pūrvapakṣavādinaḥ, yathādhikāramaṅgavacanaṃ
tatpūrvakatvāt svayaṃkartṛbhāvasya</q> । asyārthaḥ-yajamānānāṃ sakāmārtvijyavidhānāt
viniyogaḥ । yajamānānāṃ yajamānatā ca satyadhikāre । tena pūrvasiddhādhikāropa-
jīvitvāt ayamaṅgavidhānasya adhikāravaśena varṇanam[na] punaretadvaśenādhikāraḥ ।
adhikāraśca svarūpatastrayāṇāṃ nāma vibhāti । teṣāṃ cārtvijye'pi viniyoga iti
upadeśenātideśikī brāhmaṇakartṛtā bādhyate । tathā ca liṅgaṃ brahmasāmavidhāne
varṇatrayadarśanam ।</p>
<p><q>atrocyate</q>-kena voktaṃ yathādhikāramaṅgavacanam iti । kintu nādhikāro'dhi-
kārāntaraṃ nivartayituṃ kṣamaḥ bādhakāraṇābhāvāt asāvapyadhikāra eva brāhmaṇānāmārtvi-
jyamiti brāhmaṇakartṛkatvenārtvijyaṃ iti śrūyate । ārtvijyaśabdena ṛrtvikkarmāṇyucyante ।
<quote>“yadyat brāhmaṇakarma taduktaṃ....karma hīnena na kartavyaṃ”</quote> iti smaraṇāt kṣatriyavaiśyayoḥ
niṣidhyate । nāyamārtvijye niṣādādhikāro yathā nātikramyate tathā satreṣvadhikāro
varṇanīyaḥ । na cātra kratvarthatayā viṣayabhedenādhikāradvayāvirodhaḥ । dvayorapyadhikārayoḥ
puruṣārthatvāt । yadyapi ca satreṣu nāṅgāni ṛtvikkartṛkāṇi tathāpi tānyārtvijānyeva
prakṛtau teṣāmārtvijyena jñātatvāt taddevatāvat । idamadhikaraṇaṃ ārtvijye yajamāna-
māśritya varṇitam ।</p>﻿
<pb n="190"/>
<p>yatpunaratra bhāṣye ārtvijyena yajamānasaṃskāranirākaraṇaṃ tatpratikaroti---
<q>yadi paramārtvijyaṃ adṛṣṭāyaiva codyate svāminām</q> । asyārthaḥ-yadi svāmināma-
dṛṣṭāya saṃskārāyārtvijyaṃ codyate tadā evaṃ sati satre sarveṣāmadhikāraḥ syāt । na ca
tadastītyuktaṃ bhāṣye । tasmādadhikārānurodhena brāhmaṇānāmeva satreṣvadhikāra iti
siddham । darśanamahīne caritārtham । tatra varṇatrayasambhavāt ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 4 ।। vāsiṣṭhānāṃ vā brahmatvaniyamāt ।। 24 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nanu cedamadhikaraṇaṃ vacanamadṛṣṭvā pūrvapakṣaṃ kurvatāmanārambhaṇīyameva</q> ।
vaiśvāmitro hoteti vacane sati vāsiṣṭhānāmeva satramiti pūrvapakṣābhāvāt nedamadhikaraṇa-
mārambhaṇīyamevetyarthaḥ ।</p>
<p>samādhatte---<q>satyamevaṃ, kintvatra kalpāntarāśaṅkānirākaraṇāya pūrvapakṣa-
pradarśanam । kā punaratra kalpāntarāśaṅkā ?</q> vāsiṣṭhe brahmaṇi hotāpi vāsiṣṭha-
samānakalpa eva bhavatu vāsiṣṭho vā । ubhayathāpyavaiguṇyāt । tathā hotaryapi (vi)vaiśvā-
mitra eva tatsamānakalpo vā bhavatvityāśaṅkate-<q>dvayorvacanayorvidyamānatvāt kalpa-
dvayena bhavitavyamiti</q> । tannirākaraṇārthamidamadhikaraṇam । na punarvāsiṣṭhānāṃ
tatsamānakalpānāmevādhikāra iti tannirākaraṇārthametat । vasiṣṭhavacanasyānyārthatvena
niraste vāsiṣṭhe punarhotraiva niyamo bhavatīti siddhaṃ avāsiṣṭhānāṃ atatsamānakalpānāṃ ca
satram । vaiśvāmitratatsamānakalpānāmeva satramiti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 5 ।। vihārasya prabhutvādanag‍nīnāmapi syāt ।। 27 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>kathaṃ punaranāhitāgnyāśaṅkā ? sthite svāgniniṣṭhaṃ karma kartavyamiti
nyāye parakīyānāmagnīnāmāhavanīyatvābhāvāt</q> । samādhatte---<q>liṅgadarśanā-
śaṅkayā prasaṅgaṃ manvānasya pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</q> । sārasvate satre <quote>“pararathairvā ete
svarga lokaṃ yanti ye'nāhitāgnayaḥ satramāsate”</quote> ityanāhitāgnīnāṃ satradarśanāt ।
tathā <quote>“agnaye vivicaye puroḍāśamaṣṭākapālaṃ nirvapet yasyāhitāgneranyairagnibhiragnayaḥ
saṃsṛjyeran”</quote> iti saṃsargadarśanāt । āhavanīyenaiva kāryaniṣpatterapi anāhitāgnera-
pyadhikārāśaṅkā ।</p>
<p><q>atrocyate---nātra prasaṅga upapadyate tatkāryāparijñānāt</q> । yadi hi
āhavanīyakāryaṃ jñāyate tadā parakīyenāpi tatkṛtamiti prasaṅgaḥ syāt । na ca
<pb n="191"/>
tajjñāyate । homanirvṛttiḥ nāhavanīyakāryaṃ kiṃ tarhi agnidravyamātrasya । liṅgasya
parihāraṃ vakṣyati । 1<q>pātrāṇāṃ punaḥ svaiḥ ityaśravaṇāt pūrvapakṣavādī prasaṅgaṃ
manvāno yasya kasyaciditi bravīti</q> । asyārthaḥ---yathā svāgniniṣṭhakarma kartavya-
miti sthite prasaṅgo nāsti tadā[thā]tarhi yatra svairiti na śrūyate nāpi nyāyataḥprāpyate
tatra prasaṅgena bhavitavyaṃ yathā pātreṣu iti । pūrvopajīvanenotthānāt antarāgarbhiṇītvam ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntavādī tu satyamatra prasaṅgo vidyate sa tu dīrghakālatvāt satrāṇāṃ
āyuṣaśca parimāṇājñānāt anyairapi tadarthamutpannaiḥ kṛtameva tadbhavatīti pātrā-
ntaropādānameva nyāyyamiti । manyata iti sambandhaḥ</q> ।</p>
<p>satyamatra prasaṅgo vidyate sa tvayuk‍ta iti vākyaśeṣaḥ । kutaḥ ? dīrghakālatvāt
satrāṇāṃ, āyuṣaśca parimāṇājñānāt kadācit satrecet pravṛtte vyāpadyeta yo'tra
sthāyī tasya pātrāṇāṃ satre vyāpṛtānāṃ pratipattilopaḥ syāt । pratipattau vā satra-
kriyāvaiguṇyam । anyairapi ca satrārthamupāttaiḥ satraṃ kṛtameva bhavati ityanayā rāddhānta-
vādī manyata iti yojyam । ādhastyasya <q>liṅgamuktam prāyaścittamāpadi syāditi</q> ।
sārasvate darśanaṃ tu bhāṣye na parihṛtam ।</p>
<p>tatrāha---sārasvate darśanaṃ tu satre yadyanyathā nopapadyate tadā vacanaṃ
tarhi bhaviṣyati । na ca tāvatā sarvāṇi satrāṇyevānāhitāgnīnāmapi
bhaveyuriti bhāvaḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 7 ।। puruṣakalpena vā vikṛtau kartṛniyamaḥ syāt yajñasya
tadguṇatvādabhāvāditarān pratyekasminnadhikāraḥ syāt ।। 36 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>kathaṃ punaḥ adhvarakalpādiṣu sandehaḥ sāmānyenādhikāre śrūyamāṇe kiṃ
vaiśyasyaivādhikāraḥ uta trayāṇāṃ varṇānāmapīti saṃśayaḥ</q> । itthaṃ saṃśa(ye)[yaḥ]
kimadhvarakalpādiṣu adhikāro niyamyate sāptadaśyavacanena vaiśyasyaivādhikāraḥ uta
pāñcadaśyapratyāmnāyena sāptadaśyaṃ kratvarthatayā codyate iti । tatra pūrvapakṣavādī adhi-
kāraniyamaḥ sādhīyān iti manyate । sāptadaśyaṃ kila vaiśyanimittakaṃ tenaitadvacanenaivaṃ darśa-
<note>1. atra juhādīnāmaprayuktatvāt ityādhikaraṇārambho draṣṭabyaḥ । antarāgarbhiṇītvāt
na pṛthaguktiḥ ।</note>﻿
<pb n="192"/>
yati yathā sāptadaśyaṃ bhavati tathā kuryāditi । vaiśye cādhikāriṇi tadbhavati । tena vaiśya-
meva niyacchati । nanu pāñcadaśyapratyāmnāyena kratvarthatayā sāptadaśyavidhireva1 kasmānna
bhavatītyatrāha---<q>kratvarthe hi vaiśyakartṛke sāptadaśyasya codakaprāptatvānna vidhāṃna
sambhavatīti</q> । na cātra tatparyudāsaḥ śrūyate tena vidhivaiṣamyaṃ syāt ekasyaiva
vidheranuvādakatvaṃ ceti । tasmādadhikāra eva kasmānna bhavatītyadhikāraniyamaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu kratvarthena svarūpavidhiravagamyamāno nādhikāraṃ niyantuṃ
kṣamaḥ । nanu ca vaiśyakartṛke vidhānaṃ na sambhavatītyuktam</q> । samādhatte---
<q>na sambhavati yasmānna kāryataḥ prāptirūpaṃ vihanti</q> । kāryato hi nimittasāpekṣā
vaiśyakartṛke'pi prāptiḥ । upadeśastu nimitānapekṣatayā vidadhāti । yathā tryanīkāyāṃ
anyok‍teṣvāmnānaṃ guṇārthamityāśaṅkya nimittanirapekṣatayā aindravāyavāgra[tā]vidhānam ।
tena vaiśyakartṛke'pi vidhāyakatvameva । yathā ca tatra vaikṛte nimitta[ā]bhāvepyanuṣṭhānaṃ
bhavatīti vidhiprayojanaṃ tathehāpi brāhmaṇarājanyakartṛke prāptiḥ vidhiprayojanam ।
tasmātsarveṣāmadhikāra iti sthitam ।</p>
<p>evaṃ tāvat vacanaśravaṇenādhikaraṇasthitiḥ2 ।</p>
<p>ekaṃ prakṛtau saptadaśa vaiśyasyānubrūyāditi, aparamapi adhvarakalpāyāṃ saptadaśa-
sāmidhenīranubrūyāt iti । tṛtīyamāśritya vicāraṃ kurvanti taddūṣayati---<q>anārabhya
cintā tu na śāstrataḥ kāryato vopapadyata iti nādṛtā</q> । prākṛtavacanaṃ kāryataḥ
prāptāvupayujyamānaṃ cintanīyam । vaikṛtaṃ tu vacanaṃ śāstrataḥ prāptāvupayujyamānaṃ cinta
nīyam । vaikṛtaṃ tu punarārabhyavacanamiti taccintā nādṛtā bhāṣyakāreṇa ।</p>
<p><q>iti ṛjuvimalāyāṃ ṣaṣṭhādhyāyasya
ṣaṣṭhaḥ pādaḥ</q></p>
<note>1. vidhereva-mā</note> <note>2.sthitikam</note>﻿
<pb n="193"/>
<p><q>ṛjuvimalāyāṃ</q></p>
<p><q>ṣaṣṭhādhyāyasya saptamaḥ pādaḥ</q></p>
<lg><l>।। 1 ।। svadāne sarvamaviśeṣāt ।। 1 ।।</l></lg>
<p>viśvajiti sarvavedasaṃ śrūyate । vedasaśabdaḥ svaśabdasyārthe vartate । svaśabda-
ścāyaṃ jñātidhanādiṣvaviśiṣṭaḥ ātbhīyavacano'yaṃ svaśabdaḥ । ātmīyatvaṃ ca jñātidhanā
diṣvaviśiṣṭaṃ ityaviśeṣeṇa sarvatra svaśabdo vartate । na ca viśeṣe kiñcana pramāṇamasti
etaddeyaṃ etanneti । sarvaśabda śravaṇāt । tasmadyāvadasya svaṃ tāvatsarvamiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>atra ca sarvasyātmīyasya dānaśravaṇāt dadātiḥ parasvatvāpādane vartate na punaḥ
svatyāge tasyāśakyatvāt । atra codayati---<q>kaściddānā(dā)bhimānī । nanu
yathaivātmanaḥ svaṃ tathaiva parasmā āpādanīyam</q> । na ca pitrādayaḥ parebhyaḥ
pitṛtvenāpādayituṃ śakyante । <q>ucyate । svaṃ tāvaddeyam । dīyamānasya ca yathaiva
parasvatvāpattirbhavati tathaiva parikalpanīyam</q> । yena rūpeṇātmanaḥ svatā tenā-
pādayituṃ na śakyate [yena rūpeṇa śakyate] tenāpādayiṣyate । na ca kaścidvirodhaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu svaśabdastāvadayaṃ naikārthaḥ sambhavati svabhāvabhedāt ।</q>
asyārthaḥ---jñātidhanātmīyavacano'yaṃ svaśabdaḥ sa caikayā śaktyā na vartate । kiṃ
tarhi gośabdavadanekārthaḥ । anātmīye ca jñātau dhane ca prayogadarśanāt jñātiśabdavat
dhanaśabdavacca । tathā''tmani vartate ātmīye ca । nātmani śrautaḥ ātmīye lākṣaṇikaḥ
iti śakyate vak‍tuṃ viparītapakṣāṇāṃ sambhavāt । tasmādagṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatvādātmanaḥ
ātmīyasyāyaṃ vācakaḥ । na cāyamekārthavacanatayaiva caturṣvapi prayogaṃ labhate svārtha-
bhedāt । jñātiṣu jñātitvāt svatvaṃ dhane dhanatvaṃ ātmīye ātmīyatvaṃ ātmanyātma-
tvamiti naikaṃ sāmānyamasti sarveṣu anekārthaḥ svaśabdaḥ na ca yugapat sarveṣu vartate kintu
kadācitkvaciditi । tatra dadātiśabdasambandhāt dhanaviṣaya eva vartate । dadātirhi
svatyāge parasvatvāpādanātmake vartata iti darśitaṃ caturthe । dhanaviṣaye hi tathā
sambhavati tena sarvadhanaṃ deyamiti śāstrārthaḥ । tena pitrādayo na deyāḥ ।</p>
<p>yuktyantaramāha---<q>nacātmajñātyādiṣu yaḥ svaśabdārthaḥ sa śakyate parasmā-
āpādayitum । anyathā hi āpādyamāne na svaṃ parasmā āpāditaṃ bhavati ।
<pb n="194"/>
svaṃ sat parasmā āpāditaṃ na bhavati । kiñca viśeṣapramāṇaṃ cātra vidyate</q> ।
asyārthaḥ---yadyapi svaśabda ātmīyārthatayaiva jñātidhanādiṣu vartate tathāpyātmīya-
viśeṣe'pyatra pramāṇamasti । prakṛtau hi dhanaviṣayameva dānaṃ tasya ceyaṃ sarvatā vidhīyata
iti dhanaviṣayaiva sā sarvasvatā['va]tiṣṭhate । ātmīyamapi dīyamānaṃ dhanameva deyaṃ
nānyat prakṛtivaditi tasyaiveyaṃ sarvasvatā vidhīyata iti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 2 ।। na bhūmiḥsyāt sarvān pratyaviśiṣṭatvāt ।। 3 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>bhūmau svaśabdo bhavati</q> । bhogyaviṣayaṃ dhanaviṣayamityarthaḥ । tena deyā bhūmi-
riti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntamāha---<q>na tu sā parasmā āpādayituṃ śakyate sarvān pratya-
viśiṣṭatvāditi</q> । asyārthaḥ---bhūgolakaṃ gopatharājamārgajalādisamanvitaṃ kṛts‍nameva
dānuṃ na śakyate gopathādīnāṃ sarvān pratyaviśiṣṭatvāt yathā bhūsvāmī tatra svāmī
tathā'nyo'pi । gamanāgamanādibhogo hi tatra svāmitā, na paraṃ sa ca sarveṣā-
maviśiṣṭaḥ । laukikaṃ ca svatvaṃm । ye tu grāmādikaṃ dadati te'pi vāstukṣetrādika-
meva dadatīti mantavyam । grāmastu tadavacchedaka iti niravadyam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 3 ।। akāryatvācca tataḥ punarviśeṣaḥ syāt ।। 4 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>atrāpi prasajya pratiṣedhāśaṅkayā pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</q> । aśvā na deyā iti prasajya-
pratiṣedhaṃ manyate । tatra vihitapratiṣiddhatvāt vikalpena dānaṃ sarvadānameva prasajya-
pratiṣedhe kāraṇam । tathā sati pakṣe'pi tāvaddānaṃ bhavati । <q>paryupadāsena
rāddhāntaḥ । ekavākyatvabalenāśvavarjitaṃ ca sarvaṃ bhaviṣyati</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 4 ।। nityatvāccānityairnāsti sambandhaḥ ।। 5 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>atrāpi sarvaśabdānurodhena yāvadbhogyaṃ deyamiti manyate pūrvapakṣa-
vādī</q> । śayanāsanādīni yāvanti svaśabdavācyāni tāni sarvāṇi deyānīti ।
yasya sarvāṇi na santi tathāpi krītvā krītvā dātavyamiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntavādī tu vidyamānenaiva svena svato'dhikārasiddheḥ nāvidyamāno-
pādānamutsahate vidhiḥ kartum</q> । yāvadyasya dhanaṃ tāvataḥ sarvatvamucyate । sarva-﻿
<pb n="195"/>
śabdo'yaṃ prakṛtāpekṣaḥ vidyamānaṃ cādhikāriṇaḥ svaṃ prakṛtaṃ nāvidyamānamapi । tena
tasyaiva sarvatvamucyate । tāvatā ca dattenādhikārasiddhiriti nāparamapyavidyamānamapyu-
pādāya dātavyam । <q>na cātra dānacodanetyuk‍tam</q> । yadi hi svaṃ prati dānaṃ
codyeta tadā svaṃ dānena sambandhayitavyamiti bhavedapyupādānakalpanā । iha tu svena
dānaṃ kartavyamiti yathopāttenāpi kṛte kṛtameveti nopādānakalpanetyuktaṃ bhāṣye ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 5 ।। śūdraśca dharmaśāstratvāt ।। 6 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>dharmopanate cintā---bhogyatvāt deyabhāśaṅkya na dharmopanataḥ parasmai
śakyata āpādayituṃ tadadhīnatvāt dharmopanatasyeti rāddhāntaḥ</q> ।</p>
<p>asyārthaḥ---dharmopanatasya bhogyatvāt deyatāmāśaṅkya na deya iti siddhāntaḥ ।
sa hi dharmaśikṣārthaṃ yasmin‍nupanataḥ tasyaiva bhogyo nānyasya bhogyaḥ śakyate vak‍tuṃ tathā
tasyānupanatatvāt । sa hi dharmopanataḥ ucyate yo dharmaṃ bruvāṇasyopanataḥ paricāraka-
balena । tasmiṃśca svayameva kelavaṃ bhok‍tṛtvam na punaḥ paramapi pratyupādātuṃ śakyate ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 6 ।। dakṣiṇākāle yatsvaṃ tatpratīyeta taddānasaṃyogāt ।। 7 ।।</l></lg>
<p>idamidānīṃ sandihyate---<q>kiṃ yatprāk dakṣiṇākālāt svaṃ tadanyatra na
viniyujyate yo(dharmaḥ) yacca bhaviṣyatīti jñāyate tatsarvameva deyaṃ, uta
dakṣiṇākālavartyeveti</q> । mayā viśvajitkartavya iti jñānādanyatra na viniyukte tathā
pramāṇatayā yasya bhāvino nirṇayaḥ tadapi deyam । uta yatheṣṭaviniyuktaśeṣavartamānameva
deyamiti । tatra bhaviṣyadvartamānasarvasya bhūtavartamānasarvasya ca svaśabdārthatvāt
deyatāmāśaṅkya avyavasthānāt tatkālavartyeva deyamityavagamyata iti rāddhāntaḥ ।
vyavasthito hi śāstrārtho yuktaḥ tena vartamānameva sarvaṃ deyamiti rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 7 ।। aśeṣatvāt tadantaḥ syāt karmaṇo dravyasiddhitvāt ।। 8 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nanu ca tridhāvyavasthānādacintanīyamevedamadhikaraṇam</q> । samādhatte---
<q>satyaṃ tathāpi karmāpekṣo dānādhikāraḥ na dānāpekṣaṃ karmeti imamarthaṃ pradarśa-
yitumidamupanyastam</q> asyārthaḥ-vibhāgo nāstīti kṛtvā nyāyavyutpādanamevaitat
kiyace । tatra pūrvapakṣavādī dānāpekṣaṃ karmeti manyate । sarvasvaṃ hi sākṣāddeyatvenopa-﻿
<pb n="196"/>
deśena vihitaṃ bhavati । datte ca tasmin dravyasādhyatvāt karmaṇaḥ tadantataiva yuktā
na śeṣayitavyaṃ kiñcitkāryārthamiti śakyate vak‍tum teṣāṃ karmaṇāṃ codakaprāptānāmupa-
deśabādhe'samarthatvāt ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu karmānuṣṭhānārthaṃ sahāyānveṣaṇārthaṃ ca dānamiti pradhānabhūta-
karmānurodhena (na)dānaśāstraṃ varṇayitavyam</q> । tena kratvarthavyatiriktadravyameva sarvaṃ
deyamiti । dravyavibhāgastu udāharaṇāpekṣayā draṣṭavyaḥ । atrodāharaṇe tredhāvyavasthā-
panāt tadapekṣo'yamudāharaṇe'paro viśeṣa iti pradarśayituṃ vibhāga upanyastaḥ । na
nyāyāvalopitayā । tasmādanavadyam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 8 ।। ahargaṇe ca taddharmā syāt sarveṣāmaviśeṣāt ।। 14 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>kathaṃ punaḥ nāmnā dharmātideśe balīyasi dvādaśaśatāśaṅkā ?</q> saptamādye nāmnā
dharmāṇāṃ padārthānāmatideśo balīyāt liṅgena dharmātideśāt ityuktamiti pūrvapakṣo
nopapadyate । uttaraṃ---<q>gaṇadharmāpekṣayā । gaṇo hi gaṇasya dharmānapekṣate iti
gaṇāntaḥ pātina eva dharmo nyāyyaḥ apekṣitatvāt</q> । tena dvādaśāhika eva
vidhyanto yukto naikāhika iti । ekā ceyaṃ gaṇacodanā । tena gaṇadharmākāṅkṣā ।
tasmāt sarveṣāṃ dvādaśaśataṃ dakṣiṇeti tulyo dānādhikāraḥ । adhikāraśabdaṃ prakṣipya
lakṣaṇe saṅgatimāha ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu---satyamekā gaṇacodanā codanīyāstu bhidyante tadape-
kṣayā ca dharmagrahaṇam</q> । asyārthaḥ - yadyapyekā codanā tathāpi codanīyānāṃ karmaṇāṃ
bhedāt tadapekṣayācādhikāravidheḥ dharmagrahaṇaṃ karaṇānyapekṣya cādhikāravidhiḥ dharmān
gṛhṇāti । bahūni caitāni karaṇānīti tadapekṣayā pratyekaṃ dharmātideśaḥ tatra kasya-
cinnāmnā, kasyacilliṅgeneti । tasmāt nāmaiva balavat ।</p>
<p><q>kathaṃ punaritareṣāṃ dakṣiṇā</q> । yadi sarvasvaṃ ekasminnahani dakṣiṇā,
anyatra dvādaśaśataṃ ekayā ca dakṣiṇayā bhavitavyamiti daśame sthāpitam । ato
virodhāt kathamitareṣāṃ dakṣiṇā । <q>uttaranyāyāntaramidaṃ cintyate - vipratiṣiddha-
dharmāṇāṃ samavāye bhūyasāṃ syāt svadharmatvamityatra</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 9 ।। vikāraḥ san‍nubhayato'viśeṣāt ।। 18 ।।</l></lg>﻿
<pb n="197"/>
<p><q>nanu ca niyamavidhau sati sarvadānaṃ dvādaśaśatābhyadhikenaiva sarvasva-
dānenādhikṛta iti vaktavyam । kimidaṃ samena vetyucyate</q> । asyārthaḥ - bhāṣya-
kāreṇātra vidhāna evamucyate---dvādaśaśatādhikena tatsamena vā'dhikriyata iti । tadanupa-
pannam । yasmāt prakṛtau dvādaśaśataṃ vidhāyāha---evaṃ vā ṛtvija āgamayitavyāḥ
api vā sarvasveneti । evaṃ cokte dvādaśaśatādhikameva sarvasvaṃ pratīyate । yehi
dvādaśaśatena1 nānamante na tarāṃ te nyūnena । tenādhikaṃ sarvasvaṃ tacca viśvajiti
niyamyate । tenādhikenaiva sarvasvenāpyadhikāro na dvādaśaśatasamāneneti ।</p>
<p><q>atrābhidhīyate---samagrahaṇamānatyantarāpekṣayā na dvādaśaśatāpekṣayetya-
doṣaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---<quote>‘yo'yaṃ tat‍tulyayā dakṣiṇayā'dhikāra’</quote> ityūce sa ānantyanta-
rāpekṣayā tattulyamityanenābhiprāyeṇa tattulyādhikāra ityucyate । na dvādvaśaśatāpekṣayā
dvādaśaśatādhikameva kiñcit ānatitulyatvāttulyamityadoṣaḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 10 ।। aparimite śiṣṭasya saṅkhyāpratiṣedhaḥ tacchrutitvāt ।। 21 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nārthalopenātra pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---yadyatrāparimitaśabdena tāvat
yasya parimāṇaṃ nāsti tadavayavānusāreṇocyate na tasya dānāsambhavaḥ sarvasya dīyamānasya
parimāṇasambhavāt । athāvayarthatiraskāreṇa aparimitaśabdena bahūcyate tadā avaya-
vārthatyāga eva doṣaḥ । tenāvayavārthalobhena parimitaṃ na deyaṃ ityatrārthaḥ । asamartha-
samāsāśrayaṇe'pi avayavārthānugraha eva heturiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । <q>dānacodanāprakaraṇāt
śrutiścopapannatareti rāddhāntaḥ</q> । <quote>‘ekā deyā’</quote> ityādayaḥ dānacodanāḥ prakṛtāḥ
tatsamīpe ca aparimitaṃ deyamiti । tena dānacodanāsāhacaryāt iyamapi dānacoda-
naiveti mantavyam । tena aparimitaṃ deyamityevaṃ sambandhaḥ । samāsaśrutiścopapannatarā ।
samarthasamāso hi śrutita evāvagamyate । tena aparimitaṃ deyamityarthaḥ । aparimita-
śabdena bahūnyucyante ।</p>
<p>nanu caivaṃ sati avayavārthalopaḥ prāpnoti iti pūrvapakṣavāraṇam । rāddhāntamāha
---<q>prāptasya prāptirityapeśalam</q> । loke hi aparimitaśabdena bahūnyucyante
aparimitamasya dhanamiti bahviti gamyate । tenāvayavārthalopena darśanāt nāyaṃ doṣa iti ।
<q>tathā ca pravīṇādiṣu dṛṣṭam</q> । pravīṇakuśalaśabdānāṃ rūḍhitvaṃ dṛṣṭam । pravīṇa-
<note>1. dvādaśena-mā</note>﻿
<pb n="198"/>
śabdo hi na gauṇa iti śakyate vak‍tum । vīṇāvādanaguṇayogena hi vartamānaḥ
prakarṣa eva kevalena vyavatiṣṭhate । tasmāttatrārohan rūḍha ityucyate । evamapyaparimita-
śabdo'pyādhikya eva vartamāno rūḍha iti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 11 ।। aniyamo'viśeṣāt ।। 23 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>āpekṣikatvāt bahvarthasya sahasrasya prakṛtatvāt tadabhyadhikamiti
nyāyyam</q> । tatkilāpekṣitaṃ yatpratiyogyapekṣaṃ tasmin sannihite sambhavati tada pekṣa-
mevābhyadhikatvaṃ pratīyata iti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 12 ।। parakṛtipurākalpaṃ ca manuṣyadharmaḥ syādarthāya
hyanukīrtanam ।। 26 ।।</l></lg>
<p>atra cintyate---<q>kimevamadhikāravidhayo'thavā kratvarthānāmeva stuti-
riti</q> । māṣādīnāṃ saṅkīrtanaṃ kimadhikārapradarśanārthaṃ utāraṇyādistutyarthamiti
sandehaḥ । puruṣasaṃyogādadhikāra iti pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ । anyathā hi puruṣa-
śravaṇaṃ saviśeṣaṇamanarthakaṃ syāt bahvarthatvāddhi1 puruṣasaṅkīrtanaṃ gotraviśeṣeṇa sahitaṃ
stutimātratve'narthakaṃ bhavati । vikārārthatve sārthakamityadhikāravidhireva ।</p>
<p>nanu <quote>‘nivīṃta manuṣyāṇāṃ’</quote> ityanena tatrāpi puruṣasambandhāt vidhitvamāśaṅkya
stutitvaṃ darśitam ihāpi tathaiveti । neti brūmaḥ । tatra puruṣaviniyogaḥ kratuviniyoge
bādhitaḥ karmāntarāśrayaṇāt । kratuprakaraṇe kratureva kāryaṃ pratibhāti । tatra puruṣa-
dharmatvaṃ syāt tena puruṣasaṃyogo'rthavādamātram । iha punaradhikāramukhena kratvarthavighāta
upapadyate । adhikāre'pi nāṣādīnāṃ kratvarthatvāditi cintyate । ataḥ puruṣa-
śravaṇāt kratoścāvighātāt adhikāravidhirevāyam । viśeṣatastu tadgotrāṇāṃ sāmānyato
vā atadgotrāṇāmapi sāmānyata eva vā viśeṣasya stutyupayogitvāditi । yasmā-
dvārṣṇyenaivaṃ kṛtaṃ tasmādanyo'pi tatkuryāt iti sāmānyata evāyaṃ siddhiḥ ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---satyaṃ na kratunā virodhaḥ na punaradhikārāntaraṃ
pratyetumeva śakyate tadavagamāt</q> pākādaya evaṃ kurvantītyetāvanmātramatra śrūyate, na
<note>1. tvādi - mā</note>﻿
<pb n="199"/>
punaranyo'pyevaṃ kuryāditi tenādhikārāvagamāt āraṇyavyatiriktādhikārāntarāvagamāt
na māṣādiviṣayamadhikārāntaraṃ pratyetuṃ śakyate । nanu ca māṣapākādisaṅkīrtanamanartha-
kamityāśaṅkyāha - <q>viniyogasya ca viniyogāntareṇaikavākyatvāt</q> । stu-
tyarthatvāt āraṇyaviniyogenaikavākyatvāt stutyarthameva māṣamātre pākādikīrtanam ।
<q>ato na viṣayataḥ</q> na niyogata ityarthaḥ । viniyogo hi niyogasya viṣayaḥ tathāpi
niyogataḥ sākṣādvidhyaśravaṇāt nādhikārasya nānātvaṃ śakyateṃ pratipattum । tasmāt
stutireveti nyāyyam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 13 ।। sahastrasaṃvatsaraṃ tadāyuṣāmasambhavānmanuṣyeṣu ।। 31 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>kathaṃ punaratra trivṛta iti śravaṇāt saṃśabdārthāśaṅkā ?</q> asyārthaḥ---
yadyapi pañcāśataḥ trivṛtaḥ saṃvatsarā iti saṃvatsaraśabdaḥ śrūyate tathāpi trivṛta iti
śravaṇāt ahānyeva pratīyante trivṛcchabdo'hanyeva vartituṃ śak‍noti trivṛtstotra-
mukhena savanārthopasaṃhārāt ahareva pratīyate । saṃvatsaraśabdo'pi ahassveva
nāmadheyatvopapattyartho draṣṭavyaḥ । ataḥ kathaṃ saṃvatsaraśabdārtha ityāśaṅkate । <q>ucyate ।
dvādaśāhavadetat bhaviṣyati iti</q> । yathā dvādaśāhena yajeta ityatra trivṛdādayaḥ
śabdāḥ stotravacanā api ahardvāreṇa sambadhyante evamatrāpi pañcāśataḥ trivṛtaḥ saṃvatsarā
iti <q>yāvadbhiḥ ahobhiḥ trivṛdbhiḥ pūryate tāvatā trivṛtāmahnā trivṛtā iti
vyapadeśo bhavatīti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate</q> । asyārthaḥ-dvādaśāhena yajetetyatrāṃdhi-
kāravākye ahaśśabdaśravaṇāt utpattau trivṛdādayaḥ śabdāḥ ahānyevopalakṣayanti
tathāpi adhikāravākye saṃvatsara śravaṇāt utpattau trivṛdādayaḥ śabdāḥ yāvadbhirahobhiḥ
saṃvatsarāṇāṃ pañcānāṃ pañcāśatā pūraṇaṃ bhavati tāvatsu vartate । teṣāmapi stotra-
yogitvāt । ata eva cotpattāvapi saṃvatsara1śabdasāmānādhikaraṇāt trivṛdādi-
śabdānām । ataḥ sahasrasaṃvatsarayoginyadhikāre sthite sahasrasaṃvatsaraśravaṇāt nūnaṃ
keciddīrghāyuṣo vidyanta iti gandharvādyupanyāsaḥ । nahyāśaṅkanīyamarthaṃ vedo vidadhyāditi
nyāyāt vidhibalādeva dīrghāyuṣaḥ kalpanīyāḥ । evaṃ rasāyanakulakalpārghatṛtīyaśatādyu-
panyāsaḥ । tulyatvādadṛṣṭakalpanāyāṃ yadā drādhiṣṭhaṃ adṛṣṭānāṃ kalpanam । tathā rasā-
yanasyāpi jyoga‍jīvitatva[vakatva]kalpanaṃ tathā kulakalpanā ardhatṛtīyaśatapuruṣādhi-
kārakalpanā ।</p>
<note>1. śabdādasā-mā</note>﻿
<pb n="200"/>
<p><q>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---trivṛtaḥ saṃvatsarā iti hi śrūyate na trivṛtāṃ
saṃvatsarā iti</q> । yadi trivṛtāṃ saṃvatsarā iti śrūyate tataḥ trivṛcchabdena ahakena
saha sambandho'vakalpate । yadā tu trivṛta iti ahānyucyante tadā saṃvatsaraśabdena
mukhyasāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ na bhavatīti trivṛcchabdena vā trivṛtāṃ samūho lakṣaṇīyaḥ ।
saṃvatsaraśabdo vā gauṇyā vṛttyā ahassu varṇanīyaḥ iti cintāyāṃ vicāritatvāt
saṃvatsaraśabda evānirṇīyamānārthaḥ trivṛcchabdānuguṇyena lakṣaṇayā varṇanīyaḥ ।</p>
<p>tathāhi---sāvanenāpi saṃvatsaro'sti ṣaṣṭyadhikaiḥ tribhiranhāṃ śataiḥ । tathā
sāṅkrānto'pi bhavati ādityasya dvādaśarāśibhedanena । tathā nākṣatro'pi bhavati
dvādaśabhiḥ gaṇaparivṛttibhiḥ indoḥ । tathā cāndro'pi tithigaṇanāyāṃ ṣaṣṭyadhikaiḥ
tribhireva śataiḥ sarvatra cātra saṃvatsaraśabdo mukhyaḥ । tenāsau na jñāyate kva prayujyata iti ।
tena tadvaśena na padāntaravarṇanā, padāntaravaśenaiva tasya varṇanā । ityato na dvādaśā-
havadetadupapadyata iti saṃvatsaraśabdo'trāhassu nāmadheyopapattyartho draṣṭavyaḥ । pañca pañcā-
śatastivṛta ityetāvadevātra vidhīyate atra tu saṃvatsaraśabdasya vihitānvayitvāt ।
arthāntararūpe vṛttirdṛṣṭā । tasmāt siddho'dhikāro vinā kalpanayā sahastreṇānhāṃ
karmāṇi kartuṃ laukikānāmapi sāmarthyāditi sthitam ।</p>
<p><q>iti ṛjuvimalāyāṃ pañcikāyāṃ
ṣaṣṭhādhyāye saptamaḥ pādaḥ</q></p>
<pb n="201"/>
<p><q>ṛjuvimalāyāṃ</q></p>
<p><q>ṣaṣṭhādhyāyasya aṣṭamaḥ pādaḥ</q></p>
<p><q>।। 1 ।। iṣṭipūrvatvādakratuśeṣo homaḥ saṃskṛteṣvagniṣu syādapūrvo
'pyādhānasya sarvaśeṣatvāt ।। 1 ।।</q></p>
<p>atra bhāṣyakāreṇaivamuktam---pakṣāntaramapi vicārayiṣyatīti । yadi ca
pakṣāntaramasti kimiti nopanyasyate tatrābhiprāyamāha---<q>iha pakṣāntarānupanyāse
mandayuktikaḥ pakṣaḥ nānyapakṣapratipakṣatayopanyasanamityabhiprāyaḥ ।</p>
<p>atra bhāṣyakāraḥ evaṃ vicārayati---kiṃ pavamāneṣṭisaṃskṛteṣvagniṣu caturhotṛ-
homāḥ utāsaṃskṛteṣvapīti । tadasaṅgatamiti matvā samarthayamāna āha---<q>caturhotṛṣu
homeṣu kimāhitāgneradhikāraḥ utānāhitāgneḥ athavā aviśeṣeṇeti cintyate ।</q>
karaṇacintā tu bhāṣyakāreṇaiva kṛttā । tatrānārabhyāivanīyavidhānāt āhitāg‍neriti
pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । sarvahomeṣu āhavanīyayoga ityāhavanīyavataḥ sāgneradhikāraḥ । <q>kathaṃ
punaranāhitāgneriṣṭiriti vacanametasmin pakṣe ?</q> ato vacanenānāhitāgneriṣṭirbhava-
tīti bhāvaḥ । uttaraṃ---<q>yadagnisaṃyuktaṃ karma tanna bhavatītyabhiprāyaḥ ।</q> japānāmeṣa vādaḥ
anahitāgnereṣavā iṣṭiriti na homasya । eṣa vā anāhitāgneḥ kriyā yaduteṣṭiriti ।
iṣṭiśabdo'niṣṭiṣu gauṇaḥ praśaṃsārthaḥ । <q>aviśeṣāśaṅkā tarhi kathaṃ ?</q> uttaraṃ---
āhitāgneradhikāro na śakyate vārayituṃ avaiguṇyāt sarvahomānāṃ</q> na tasya
kiñcidvaiguṇyaṃ kleśāsādhyatvena tāvadadhikriyate । anāhitāg‍nestu vacanaṃ
bhaviṣyati iti ।</p>
<p><q>pitṛyajñavadapyanāhitāg‍ninā kārya iti ।</q> yathā tena dvayorapyadhikāro
bhavatviti yuk‍tā śaṅkā ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu yata eva cāviśeṣeṇa vidhānamāhavanīyasya ata
evādhikāriviśeṣaṇamāskanditumarhati ।</q> viniyogaviśeṣamiva pade juhoti vartmani
juhoti iti yathā । yadi hi caturhotṛhomānevādhikṛtyāhavanīyo vihitaḥ syāt
[syāt] āhitāgneradhikāraḥ । yatastu sāmānyenāhavanīyo vihitaḥ tato hi na
<pb n="202"/>
śak‍notyanāhitāgnervācanikamadhikāramāskandituṃ pade juhotīti viniyogāntaramiva ।
tena।[nā]hitāgnervācaniko'dhikāro yuktaḥ । eṣā vā anāhitāgneriṣṭiḥ iti vacanāt ।</p>
<p>atra ceyaṃ vacanavyaktiḥ---yaiścaturhetṛhomarūpeṣṭiḥ eṣā vā'nāhitāgneriti ।
yaduktaṃ āhitāg‍neravaiguṇyādadhikāro nivartayituṃ na śakyate anāhitāgna‍yarthaṃ tu
vacanamiti । atra brūmaḥ । uktaṃ ca nādhikāraviśeṣaṃ sādhāraṇavidhirāskandatīti ।
viśeṣeṇa cātra anāhitāgnerayamadhikāraḥ । tatra cāhavanīye juhotīti sāmānyavidhirnā-
vataratītyuktam । tasmāt vācaniko'yamadhikāro'nāhitāgneḥ । ato yatra cobhayasaṃyogaḥ
tatraivobhayoradhikāraḥ yathā piṇḍapitṛyajñe । tatra hi a[pya]nāhitāgninā kāryamiti
apiśabdenānvācayaḥ kriyate । atra tu sa nāsti । tasmādanāhitāgnerevaiṣo'dhikāra
iti siddham ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 2 ।। upanayannādadhīta homasaṃyogāt ।। 11 ।।</l></lg>
<p>iha māṇavakahomāścintyante, nācāryasya1, ācāryasyāhavanīyasaṃbhavāt ।
siddhāntābhāvaprasaṅgācca । māṇavakakartṛkāśca māṇavakahomā yeṣvācāryasyādhikāro na
śrūyate । iha cintyate---uktamādhastye'dhikaraṇe caturhotṛṣvanāhitāgneradhikāraśravaṇāt
āhavanīyavidhireva bādhita iti । iha punaḥ anāhitāgniśabdābhāvāt āhavanīyasya
ca sarvahomārthatvāt āhitāgnermāṇavakasya svakarmaṇyadhikāra iti tatsiddha‍yarthamādhānaṃ
kariṣyati । nanu cādhītavedasya gurukulānnivṛttasya kṛtadāraparigrahasyādhānamucyate
tatkathamanadhītavedasyādhānaṃ ? atrocyate । kramamātraṃ hi tat vākyāccāhavanīyasaṃyogaḥ
āhavanīye juhotīti । tenāhavanīyānugrahāt kramo bādhiṣyate । tadāha---
<q>vākyāṅgabhūtaṃ kramamapi bādhata iti punaḥ kramamātram ।</q> nanu ca saha pat‍nyā
ādhānaṃ śrūyate । asati sahabhāve kathaṃ taducyate । na cākṛtadārasya pat‍nī sambhavati ।
ucyate । kriyatāṃ dārasaṅgrahaḥ sahādhānasidhyartham । <q>nanu kathamanivṛttau gurukulāt
dārān kuryāt ।</q> gurukulanivṛttyantaraṃ dārakriyāvihitā yataḥ । pariharati---
<q>uṃkta kramamātraṃ taditi ।</q> tasmādāhitāgneradhikāraḥ aiśvaryalakṣaṇaḥ ।</p>
<note>1. nācāryatā - mā</note>
<pb n="203"/>
<p>atrocyate । nāyaṃ pakṣaḥ sambhavati । yasmānna dāropayamanamādhānaṃ prayuṅkte ।
yadi hyādhānena dāropayamanaṃ prayujyate tadā sahabhāvopapattaye syādapyupayananam । na ca
tadasti rāgasyaiva prayok‍tṛtvāt kṛtadāragrahaṇasya sambhavāt । atra codayati---<q>kena
voktaṃ prayujyata iti । rāgata eva tvasau kṛtadāra ityuktamasmābhiḥ ।</q> krama-
syānaṅgatvāt vākyācca durbalatvādityanayā yuktyā । pariharati---<q>satyamāha bhavān ।
kintvatrāsti kiñ‍cidvaktavyam ।</q> upanayanottarakālaṃ hi vaidike'dhikāra iti
pratipāditam, [na]prāgupanayanāt । tadā dārvihomikācāryāṇāṃ vidhaya ityuktam ।
tena māṇavakasya vaidiko'dhikāro nāsti । na cānadhikṛtadāraniyamassaṃbhavati । na cā---
kṛtadārasyādhānaṃ ityanāhitāgnerevādhikāraḥ । <q>nanu cāpatyānyārtheṣu dāreṣu niyamaḥ
dharmārthamiti na prāp‍nuyuḥ । tatra niyamābhāvāt ।</q> pariharati---<q>kṛtadārāṇāṃ
hi taddharmaniyamaḥ । na hi dharmārtho dārasaṅgrahaḥ । rāgaprayukto dārasaṅgrahaḥ</q>
na dharmaprayuktaḥ । tena dāraniyamaṃ vinā dārasaṅgraho nāsti । tasmātsiddhamanāhi-
tāgneḥ prāgaupanāyaniko vidhiriti ।</p>
<p><q>nanu ca prāgupanayanādadhikāra eva nāstīti tvayaivoktam ।</q> tena
māṇavakasya homa eva na sambhavatīti kuto'yaṃ vicāraḥ ? <q>uttaraṃ---bāḍhamadhikāro
nāstīti na punaḥ kāryato'pi nāstītyucyate</q> svādhyāyādhyayanavadaiś‍varyapakṣo'sti ।
niyojyalakṣaṇastu nāstītyarthaḥ । kārye cādhāne'nadhikārādanāhitāgneradhikāra
ityuktam । <q>ekatvānniyamasya na punaḥ dārasaṅgraha iti । satyamevam
dvitīyo dārasaṅgraho na syāt yadi tu vacanaṃ na syāt ।</q> punarādhānavadasti
tu vacanam dharmaprajāsampanne dāre nānyāṃ kurvīta anyatarābhāve kuryāditi vacanasyāpāyo
naivāstīti sthitiḥ । tena vacanāt dvirdārasaṅgraho na viruddhaḥ । <q>darśanamuktam ।
piṇḍapitṛyajñavaditi ca parihṛtam ।</q></p>
<lg><l>।। 3 ।। sthapatīṣṭiḥ prayājavadagna‍yādheyaṃ prayojayet
tādarthyāccāpavṛjyeta ।। 20 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>atrāpi (vi)nā''havanīyasya vidhiḥ śakyate bādhitumiti pūrvapakṣa-
vādī manyate</q> yasmānnātra māṇakasyeva ādhāne'nadhikāraḥ śakyate vak‍tum । ādhāne
sahabhāvadarśanāt (na)prāptireva prayājādiṣviva darśapūrṇamāsaprakṛtitvāt asya karmaṇasta-
<pb n="204"/>
dvidhānenāhavanīyasya prāpteḥ । tanmukhena cādhānākṣepādāhavanīyasyopāyatvāt । tasmādā-
hitāgnerevādhikāro niṣādasyeti । ucyate । <q>nādhāne tāvadadhikāritvaṃ paśyāmaḥ
vidhānābhāvāt ।</q></p>
<p><q>nanu darśapūrṇamāsaprakṛtitvenādhānasya prāptiruktā ।</q> pariharati---<q>satyaṃ,
agnīnāṃ tu sā prāptiḥ teṣāmaṅgatvāt । nanu ca anāhitasya tasyānaṅgatvāt
agnidvārā bhaviṣyatyādhānasya prāptiḥ ।</q> kratvākṣepakaṃ pariharati---<q>prakṛtāvapi
naivādhānamagna‍yarthamadhikārakaṃ, kiṃ tarhi ? viniyogataḥ tadagna‍yarthaṃ</q>, na
kratvadhikārākṣiptamādhānaṃ prakṛtau । kiṃ tarhi ? viniyogena hi krameṇa tadagna‍yarthamiti ।
na cādhikārādṛte viniyogo'tra labhyata iti । adhikāramapāsya viniyogo'tra
nāsti । kevalamadhikāramātraṃ nākṣipatyādhānamityasaṃskṛteṣvevāgniṣu sthitamidaṃ karma ।</p>
<p><q>nanu ca viniyukteṣvagniṣu adhikāra iti tanmukhenāpyadhikārasya
prāptiḥ । satyam । na(nu)tu punaradhikṛtasyādhāne viniyogānuṣṭhānam ।</q>
ādhānenāgna‍yupādānam । anadhikṛtaścāyaṃ niṣāda ityuktam । tena ādhānenāgnirna
siddha‍yati niṣādasyetyagnilopena karma kartavyam ।</p>
<p>atrāyaṃ pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ---</p>
<p>yadyapyanaṅgatayā ādhānamatideśena na prāpyate tathāpyatidiṣṭāhavanīyasiddha‍yarthaṃ
niṣādasyākṣepo bhaviṣyati ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntastu alaukikatvādāhavanīyasya niṣpatternākṣepakam । ato yatkartṛka-
mādhānamāhavanīyādyutpādakaṃ viniyogato'vagataṃ tatkartṛkenaivāhavanīyotpattiḥ nānyena,
mi/?/ṣādakartṛkasyotpādakatvenā1vijñānānnākṣepaḥ sambhavati ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 4 ।। avakīrṇipaśuśca tadvadādhānasyāprāptakālatvāt ।। 22 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>abakīṇiṃpaśau kaṃ viśeṣaṃ paśyati āśaṅkāhetubhūtaṃ tasyāpi dārābhāvāt
na sahādhānamupapadyate ।</q> uttaraṃ---<q>ayamabhiprāyaḥ---tasya dārāḥ saiva bhavatu
niyamātikramāt yayā sahāvakīrṇīṃ ।</q> dārā iti bahuvacanāt tadbhavati ityeka
<note>1. tvena vi-mā</note>
﻿<pb n="205"/>
vacanāt karma saiveti sambandhāt । tasmāt satsu dāreṣu āhavanīyasambandho naiva
bādhituṃ śakyata iti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntavādī tu atikrame nirharaṇāyaitatprāyaś‍cittaṃ niyamānusamba-
ndhāditi tādṛśasyādhikārādidamapi pūrvādhikaraṇavad‌draṣṭavyam ।</q> avakīrṇipaśurhi
avakīrṇinā kṛtadoṣanirharaṇena brahmacaryamevānusandhātuṃ ghaṭayituṃ vihitaṃ prāyaścittatayā ।
nivṛttasya ca pāpāt prāyaścittam । tena tāṃ parityajyaivāvakīrṇipaśuḥ kartavyaḥ । tena
tādṛśasyaiva brahmacāriṇa eva tyaktastrīkasyaivādhikārādidamapi māṇavakahomādhikaraṇena
tulyam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 5 ।। udagayanapūrvapakṣāhaḥ puṇyāheṣu daivāni smṛtirūpā-
nyārthadarśanāt ।। 23 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>kathaṃ punaratra smṛtivacane sati pūrvapakṣāśaṅkā</q> upanayanādiṣu saṃvatsarādi-
kālaniyamaśravaṇāt । aṣṭavarṣasyārthaḥ aṣṭavarṣaṃ brāhmaṇamupanayīteti śrūyate yasya pūrṇā aṣṭau
varṣāḥ so'ṣṭavarṣaḥ tena niṣekakakālādārabhya pūrve[rṇe]ṣvaṣṭasu varṣeṣu upanayanamiti noda-
gayanādismṛterādaraḥ sambhavatīti ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu vartamāneṣvevāṣṭasu varṣeṣu sa niyamo nātivṛtteṣvityavirodhaḥ ।</q>
yadi hi smṛtiḥ śrutiviruddhā syāt bādhyetāpi smṛtiḥ । na cāsti virodhaḥ ।
śrutāvapi vartamānepyaṣṭavarṣe upanayanaṃ śrūyate । tasyodagayanādiśrutyā saha virodho
nāsti । <q>sa hyaṣṭavarṣa ucyate ।</q> uttaraṃ---<q>aṣṭamo hi tasya varṣo'sti yadi paripūrṇaḥ
tena bhaviṣyatyevāṣṭavarṣaḥ । darśanamuktam ।</q></p>
<lg><l>।। 7 ।। yācñākrayaṇamavidyamāne lokavat ।। 26 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nopāttadravyasaṃbhave satyapyanyopādānaṃ yuktaṃ, adṛṣṭakalpanāprasaṅgāt
tadabhāva eva 1krayo vidhīyate bhṛtivananaṃ ceti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</q> asyārthaḥ-dravyo-
pādānārthaṃ hi yācñādi vihitam । asati dravye dravyopādānaṃ vihitaṃ kartavyaṃ na
satyeva । tasmāt prayojanālocanayā dravyābhāva evāyaṃ vidhiriti ।</p>
<p>1. tayorvi-mā</p>
﻿<pb n="206"/>
<p>rāddhāntastu---<q>satyamevaṃ yadi puruṣārthatvena vidhānaṃ syāt । kratvartha
evāyaṃ vidhiḥ । naca kratorupāttaṃ nāma kiñ‍cidasti ityasyaiva dṛṣṭārthatvam ।</q>
asyārthaḥ---kratvarthatvena yācñāvidhānaṃ kratuprakaraṇāmnānāt । na ca puruṣārthatvena prāk
kratvarthaṃ dravyamasti puruṣārthayācñayaiva hi kratvarthaṃ kriyate । tasmāt vidyamānasyāpi
yācñayaiva kratvarthaṃ dravyaṃ bhavati nānyathā, tenāsyaiva kratvarthasya sato dṛṣṭārthatvam ।</p>
<p><q>nanu yadi dṛṣṭārthatvaṃ tadā dṛṣṭasyānyena sambhave nityaṃ tarhi yācñā-
derupasaṃhāro na bhavati ।</q> atrottaraṃ---<q>na caitāvatā dṛṣṭārthatvenānupasaṃhāraḥ śakyate
vak‍tuṃ, sarvasya yugapadvidhānāt । aikaśabdyāditi vakṣyati । tasmānni-
tyavatkartavyam ।</q> asyārthaḥ-aikaśabdyāddhetoḥ sarvasya vidhiniṣpattyarthatvena yugapadvi-
dhānam । tena siddhe'pi dṛṣṭe'rthe vidhyarthasya yathācoditāṅgasādhyatvāt nityamupādānaṃ
kartavyam । tenāyaṃ yācñādividhiḥ vidhyarthaniṣpattyarthatvena yācñādivacanāt aprāpta-
vidhirevāstu । niyamastu prayojanamātram । asmin vidhau sati yācñādereva niyo-
gārthasiddhihetutvenābhyanujñānāt nityamupādānam । asati tu tasmin kriyāsaṃbandha-
sidhyarthamanyadupādīyeteti niyamaḥ prayojanaṃ vidheḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 8 ।। tathā bhakṣapraiṣācchādanasaṃjñaptahomadveṣam ।। 28 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>kaḥpunaratra viśeṣaḥ ?</q> uttaraṃ-<q>ayamasti viśeṣaḥ । puruṣārthadvāreṇānu-
praveśāt । saṃjñapanasya hṛdayādyutpattyarthatvaṃ manvānasya bhavati kācidāśaṅkā ।</q>
asyārthaḥ-kratvarthā api bhakṣādayaḥ puruṣārthadvāreṇa kratāvanupraviśantīti yatra paraṃ
puruṣārthopāyo nāsti tatraivaiṣāmaṅgabhāva iti bhakṣādiṣu tāvadāśaṅkā । saṃjñapanahome
tvevam---na saṃjñapanāṅgaṃ homo'vakalpate । prāyaścittasthānīyo hi sa śrūyate mantravarṇa-
śravaṇāt । pratyuta sādga‍uṇyāyattatvāditi ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhantastu---adhikāravidhinaikavākyatvāt prakaraṇavidhīnāṃ pūrva-
vadanuṣṭhānam ।</q> asyārthaḥ---prakaraṇe hi vidhīyamānaḥ śrūyamāṇaḥ adhikāravidhyarthaḥ
adhikāravidhiśca tatsambandhaḥ pratīyamānaḥ taireva sadbhirniścīyate । atastadanuguṇadvārā
kalpanīyatve(na) satyapi puruṣārthasiddhiḥ tena bhakṣādijanyapuruṣārthadvāreṇaiva vidhiriti
﻿<pb n="207"/>
parikalpyate tathā saṃjñaptahomo'pi saṃjñapanamātranimittataḥ, na vaiguṇyapratisamādhānārthaḥ ।
mantravarṇastu vidhyānuguṇyenaiva varṇanīya iti bhakṣāṇāmapi nityamanuṣṭhānam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 9 ।। anarthakaṃ tvanityaṃ syāt ।। 29 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>atrāpi tarhi adhikāravidhinaikavākyatvāt nityamanuṣṭhānaṃ tena
vinā vidhyarthāsiddheḥ ।</q> na cedaṃ vācyaṃ anuṣṭhīyamānamidaṃ prayojanaśūnyamiti
nānuṣṭheyamiti । yasmāt yaḥ sarvāṅgopasaṃhārasamarthaḥ so'pi kāmī bhaviṣyati । na hyanena
yatraiva prayojanamasya tasyaivādhikāraḥ ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntamāha-<q>ucyate । svārthaparityāgenaiva hi vidhānameva na pratīyate
dvāraniyamasyāpekṣitatvāt । na cāvihitasyānuṣṭhānaṃ yuktam ।</q> tasmādartha-
śūnyamevaṃvidhaṃ ananuṣṭhīyamānamapi nādhikāraṃ vihanti iti siddhamadhikāravidhirna vihanti ।
vināpi tena(āpi) adhikāravidhissidhyatyeva । nityavattasyāviniyuktatvāt । sati
dvāre tasya viniyogaḥ nāsatyapi । <q>yaccedamuktaṃ - yatra puruṣe dvāraṃ na sambhavati
tasyādhikāro mābhūditi tadayuktam । yathāviniyogamadhikāra ityuktam ।</q>
asya ca parārthasyānityadvārakatvāt anityamevārthāt viniyoga iti na śakyate
tadvaśenādhikāro nivartayitumiti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 10 ।। paśucodanāyāmaniyamo'viśeṣāt ।। 30 ।।</l></lg>
<p>lakṣaṇasaṅgatimāha---<q>idamatra cintyate - kiṃ sāmānyena paśumato'dhikāraḥ
uta chāgavata eveti ।</q> nanu viniyogamukhenāpi eṣā cintopapadyata iti kimityatraiva
cintyate ? tatrāha---<q>viniyoge punaś‍cintyamāne'viśeṣāt viniyogadvayasiddherna
śakyate viśeṣo'vadhārayitumityadhikāra eva cintyate ।</q> asyārthaḥ - na
viniyoge ghaṭate tathāmantrasyāpi chāgābhidhāyitayā । adhikāre tu parasparavirodhād‌dvaya-
mupasaṃhartuṃ na śaknoti । virodhe sati śakyate paśuviśeṣo mantrabalenāvadhārayitumityatraiva
cintā yuktā । tatra pūrvapakṣavādino'bhipāyaḥ---<q>sāmānyaśabdo'yaṃ paśuśabdaḥ
gavādiśabdavat । tena paśvākṛtimātrasya viniyogāt meṣādiṣvapi
jātyaviśeṣāt yaḥkaś‍citpaśurupādātavyaḥ ।</q> nanu mantravarṇena viśeṣe'vasthāna-
mityatrāha---<q>k‍vacicca viśeṣamantrasya arthavattvamupapannameveti na sāmānyaṃ
viśeṣe'vasthāpayitumarhati । yogādvā</q>---gamanayogādvā, varṇasāmānyādvā, akṣara-
﻿<pb n="208"/>
sāmānyādvā mantrasyaiva sāmānyārthatā yuktā । pramāṇāntaravaśena hi mantrasyārtho'vatiṣṭhate
ityuktam । viniyuktadvārasmārakatvāt mantrāṇāṃ yathāviniyogaṃt vaṇenā yuktaiva । tasmā
paśumato'dhikāraḥ ।</p>
<p><q>atrocyate । syādetadevaṃ yadyayaṃ paśuśabdaḥ sāmānyavacanaḥ syāt ।
kiṃ tarhi aupādhiko'yaṃ sarvapaśūnāṃ pucchavattvopādhikaḥ</q> śabdaśabda iva śrotra-
grāhyatvopādhikaḥ sarvaśabdānām ।</p>
<p>kasmādevaṃ bhavatītyatrāha---<q>pratyabhijñānābhāvāt</q> chāge hastini ca (na)pratyabhi-
jñānena sāmānyaṃ tāvannāsti tadabhāva eva śabdapravṛttimaupādhikīṃ darśayati । sa ca
vāladhirupādhiniyamaḥ । kathaṃ punaḥ pratyabhijñā nāstītyatrāha---<q>yathā ca pratyabhijñā
nāsti evaṃ prathamapāda eva darśitam</q> pūrvākārāvamarśābhāvāditi । yasmādayamaupādhikaḥ
sarvapaśūnāṃ pucchavattvopādhikaḥ śabdo vyaktivacanḥ । ato na viśeṣamantropasthāpi-
tamatikrāmati । tatraiva pravartate prayogaikyāt । ekādhikāravidhiparigraho mantrasya,
parigṛhītatbāt । tena ca viśeṣasya sannidhāpitatvāt ।</p>
<p>abhyupagamyāpi sāmānyavacanatāṃ brūmaḥ । viśeṣaniṣṭhataiva sāmānyā(pi)nāṃ
yuktā nityavanmantrām‍nānasāmarthyāt na mantrasya pākṣikatvaṃ yuktam । na ca sāmānyaṃ
viśeṣe'vasthāpyamānaṃ śabdārthatāṃ jahāti । yadyapi viniyogena virodhaḥ । tathāpi tasya
kāryānuguṇyāt viśeṣāvasthitireva nyāyyā । anuṣṭhānānuguṇo hi viniyogaḥ anuṣṭhā-
nārthatvāt anuṣṭhānaṃ ca mantrānvitamiti tadbaśena viśeṣāvasthāpanameva nyāyyam ।
na ca [rūḍhau]sambhavantyāṃ yaugikatvaṃ sambhavatītyuktam । tasmāt suṣṭhūcyate chāgo
vā mantravarṇāt iti । <q>śeṣamuktam ।</q></p>
<p><q>iti śrīśālikanāthamiśraviracitāyāṃ ṛjuvimalāpañ‍cikāyāṃ
ṣaṣṭhādhyāyasyāṣṭamaḥ pādaḥ
adhyāyaśca samāptaḥ</q></p>
﻿<pb n="209"/>
<p><q>ṛjuvimalāyāṃ</q></p>
<p><q>।। *navamādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ ।।</q></p>
<p>।। 1 ।। yajñakarma pradhānaṃ taddhi codanābhūtaṃ tasyaṃ dravyeṣu
saṃskārastatprayuktastadarthatvāt ।। 1 ।।</q></p>
<p><q>viśiṣṭakāryāvagamyatvādūhasya viśeṣātideśalakṣaṇaṃ hetuḥ ।</q> asyārthaḥ---
vikṛtau prākṛtānāṃ padārthānāmatideśena prāptau satyāṃ prākṛtāt kāryāt viśiṣṭaṃ
kāryamavagamyate । tatpramāṇakaścohaḥ । tena bhavati viśeṣātideśa ūhasya hetuḥ ।
atreyaṃ prakriyā-ūhyata ityanayā vyutpattyā vikṛtaprayoga ūhaśabdenocyate । sa ca
prākṛtāt kāryādanyasmin kārye'vagate'vagamyate । tathāhi---prakṛtāvavaghātādī-
nāmapūrvasādhanabhūtaviśeṣā1vrīhayo yavāśca kāryatvena pratipannāḥ । vikṛtau nīvāra-
dravyavatyāṃ apūrvasādhanabhāvāviśeṣāt atideśena prāptānāṃ nīvārā eva kāryatvenā-
vasīyante । tataśca teṣvavaghātādayaḥ kriyamāṇā vikṛtā bhavanti । kārakabhedena
kriyāvikārasyāparihāryatvāt ।</p>
<p>kathaṃ punarnīvārāṇāṃ kāryatvāvagamaḥ ? upadeśastāvada2pūrvaviśeṣagṛhītadharmāṇāṃ-
viśiṣṭāpūrvasādhanaviṣaya eva । nacā'tra pramāṇāntaramapi prakramate । ucyate । śābdaṃ
pramāṇaṃ dvivighaṃ, upadeśajaṃ kāryajaṃ ca ।</p>
<p>kaḥpunarupadeśaḥ ? kiṃ punaḥ kāryaṃm ? ucyate । upadeśo nāma granthasandarbhasya
pāṭhaḥ । kāryaṃ tu dvārabhūtam karaṇopakārādi । tatra granthasandarbhajaṃ darśapūrṇamāsābhyāṃ
yajeta svargakāmaḥ vrīhibhiryajeta yavairyajeta vrīhīnavahanti ityādiparyālocanayā'pūrva-
prayuktatāṃ sarvadharmāṃṇāmanusandadhatāṃ vrīhīṇāṃ yavānāṃ cāpūrvaviśeṣasādhanatvaṃ tulyamākalayatāṃ
vrīhiyavakāryakamavaghātādīti jñānamupajāyate । taccedamupadeśajam । śābdaṃ punaśca
<note>* saptamāṣṭamādhyāyayoḥ ṛjuvimalāmātṛkā kutrāpi nopalabdhā ataḥ navamādhyāyaḥ
mudrāpyate---</note>
<note>1. R viśeṣabhūtā</note>
<note>2. P pūrvaviśeṣagṛhītadharmāṇāṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="210"/>
1vikṛtyapūrvāntare dravyāntaravati codakaprāpteṣvaghātādiṣu iyaṃ jijñāsopajāyate---kathamete
prayoktavyā iti । tadarthaṃ ca kīdṛśaṃ kāryaṃ upadeśena prayujyata ityetannirūpyate ।</p>
<p>kiṃ darśapūrṇamāsāpūrvasādhanaviśeṣaḥ kāryatayā pratīyate, uta yasyāpūrvasyā-
vaghāto'ṅgaṃ tadīyasādhanaviśeṣa iti । tatra yadi darśapūrṇamāsāpūrvasādhanatā vivakṣitā
tadā nīvārāṇāṃ tadrūpatābhāvāt teṣāṃ kāryatā na syāt2 । atha tu yasyāpūrvasyāva-
ghāto'ṅgaṃ tadīyasādhanatāmātraṃ vivakṣitaṃ tadā'sti tadrūpatā nīvārāṇāmiti teṣāmapi
kāryatā vrīhīnavahantītyādibhireva pratīyate । tatra viśeṣāpūrvāṅgabhāvajñānamidaṃ
nāntarīyakaṃ darśapūrṇamāsāpūrvasādhanaviśeṣaḥ kāryabhūta iti । apūrvaviśeṣasambandhino
hi dharmasya tadīyaṃ kāryaṃ bhavitumarhati apūrvaidamarthyāvirodhāditi । nāntarīyakamapūrva-
viśeṣasādhanatvamavivakṣitat3 । yadīyo'vaghātastatsādhanameva kāryamiti codanārthaḥ ।
ataśca vrīhīnavahantītyanayaiva codanayā nīvārāṇāmapi kāryatvamavagamyate । tadidaṃ
kāryanirūpaṇajñānamupajāyata iti kāryajaṃ śābdam । tena nāpramāṇatvaṃ nāśābdatvaṃ
nopadeśatvamiti svayameva bhagavatā vivaraṇakāreṇoditamityanavadyam । ślokamapyudāharanti---</p>
<lg><l>prākṛtasthānapatitapadārthāntarakāryataḥ ।</l>
<l>ūhaḥ prayogo vikṛta ūhyamānatayoditaḥ ।। iti</l></lg>
<p>ākṣepyaṃ bhāṣyamanubhāṣate---<q>trividhaś‍coha iti ।</q> ākṣipati---<q>kimidaṃ
traividhyaṃ ?</q> vikṛtaprayogātmakatā mantrasāmasaṃskāraviṣaye tulyeti bhāvaḥ । samādhatte-
<q>ucyate---kāryabhedaṃ svasthāne vakṣyāmaḥ । tadbhedāyohyamapi prayogarūpaṃ
bhidyata iti tatraiva vakṣyāmaḥ ।</q> kāryapramāṇako hi prayogavikāraḥ sa pramāṇa-
bhūtakāryatraividhyāt trividho bhavati ।</p>
<p>tathāhi---avaghātādīnāṃ taṇḍulaprakṛtidravyaṃ kāryam, mantrāṇāṃ samaveto'rthaḥ,
sāmnāmakṣarāṇīti । tadvaśena ca trayāṇāmapi vikāro bhavatīti traividhyābhidhānaṃ bhāṣya-
kārasya prayājādiviṣaye ūho na bhavatīti darśayitum । na hi teṣāṃ kaścitprayoga-
vikāro'sti । anyadapyupoddhātādinetyanena bhāṣyamanubhāṣitam । ya(the)didamādyamadhi-
<note>1. p. vikṛtāvapū</note>
<note>2. nāsti</note>
<note>3. mavihitam</note>
﻿<pb n="211"/>
karaṇaṃ upoddhātena prasaktānuprasa(ktyā)ktaṃ īṣṭe bhuṅkta iti anūhasiddha‍yartha,
devatāprādhānyaṃ prasaktaṃ tatsiddharthamīśitṛtvaṃ, bhok‍tṛtvaṃ ca (tva)devatāyā anuprasaktamiti ।</p>
<p>atra bhāṣyakāreṇāgnihotrāditrayamudāharaṇaṃ gṛhītam । tatra tātparyaṃ pṛcchati-
<q>kiṃ kāraṇa ? kena punaḥ kāraṇenāgnihotrādaya evodāharaṇam ? yāvatā sarvāṇi
karmāṇi dharmavantyudāhāryāṇīti</q> ।</p>
<p>uttaraṃ---<q>kevalopadeśārthe hi pratiprakaraṇaṃ niyamātmake nirūpite'tideśaḥ
pravartate</q> । anyathā hi sarvatraivopadiṣṭatvāt dharmāṇāṃ sādhāraṇatā syāt, nātideśaḥ
syāt । atideśāvagatadharmaviṣayaścoha ityatideśasiddha‍yarthametānyevodāharaṇāni
nānyat । atra pauruktyaṃ saptamādyena saha paricodyottaravivakṣayaivedamapūrvaprayuktatvamucyata
ityarthaśaḥ parihāro dattaḥ । yaḥpunarayaṃ dvitīyaḥ parihāraḥ etena ceha prayojanaṃ ūhe
vivakṣite iti asāvayuktaḥ yasmāt tatrāpi saptamādye apūrvaprayuktatayaiva dharmāṇāṃ
pratiprakaraṇaṃ niyamaḥ siddha‍yati nānyathā । tenaitena cohaprayojanamityuktam । sapta-
mādye'pyasya prayojanattvāt । samādhatte---<q>nanu bhāṣye ayajiprayuktatve'pi sati
na pratiprakaraṇaṃ niyamaḥ siddha‍yatītyanyathāpi niyamaṃ darśayati</q> । tenāpūrva-
prayuktatā ekāntataḥ 1tatra na vyutpādyā । punarākṣipati---<q>yadeva bhāṣyakāreṇoktaṃ
tadeva na vidmaḥ kimidamayajiprayuktatvaṃ nāma</q> । yajeranyadayajiriti apūrvamevānya-
diti bhāvaḥ ।</p>
<p>samādhatte---<q>atrocyate । karaṇaprayuktatvaṃ ayajiprayuktatvamucyate</q> ।
yajeranyadayajiriti karaṇamucyate tena prayuktatvamayajiprayuktatvamucyate । 2nanu karaṇatā
kena(prayojakamata) [pramāṇena karaṇatvāvagamaḥ] atra āha---<q>kāryakaraṇasambandho'hyatra
niyogalakṣaṇaḥ</q> । sādhyabhūtena hi niyogena samabhivyāhāro'nyathā nopapadyate । yadi
niyogaḥ kāryabhūtaḥ karaṇabhūtaśca yajirna syāt iti kāryakaraṇatā niyogenāvasīyate ।</p>
<p>kathaṃ punaḥ karaṇaprayuktatve sati pratiprakaraṇaṃ niyama ityata āha---<q>karaṇa-
prayuktatve'pi ca niyogaviśeṣasambandha upapadyata eveti pratiprakaraṇaṃ niyama-
siddhiṃ manyate</q> ।</p>
<note>1. R tatrāpyūhyā</note>
<note>2. R kena pramāṇena prayojakatvaṃ ataḥ yajisvarūpamevāha-na kāraṇatā na ca tṛtīyāpi
vimaktirasti ya ākhyātapratyayasya na karaṇatāyāḥ smaryate ।</note>
﻿<pb n="212"/>
<p>asyārthaḥ-yajiprayuktatve hi darśapūrṇamāsābhyāṃ svargakāmo yajetetyanenādhi-
kāravantaṃ yajimuddiśya samidho yajatītyādibhiḥ samidānīnāṃ vidhānamiti pratiprakaraṇaṃ
niyamo na syāt । karaṇaprayuktatve tu darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmityadhikāravākyāvagataṃ karaṇaṃ
sannidhimātreṇāpūrvamiva dharmāṇāṃ grāhakaṃ tena viśiṣṭameva karaṇaṃ grāhakamiti viśiṣṭāpūrva-
sambandhāt pratiprakaraṇaṃ niyamasiddhiḥ । tena apūrvaprayuktatve karaṇaprayuktatve ca prati-
prakaraṇaṃ niyamasiddheḥ saptamādye apūrvaprayuktatā ekāntena na vyutpādanīyā । atra-
tvadhikaraṇe saiva vyutpādyate tāṃ vinā ūhāsiddheḥ । karaṇaprayuktatvehi dharmāṇāṃ vrīhayo'pi
karaṇabhūtā dharmān prayuñjata iti karaṇabhūtavrīhirūpatābhāve nīvārāṇāmavadhātādyūho na
bhavet । apūrvaprayuktatve tu vrīhisvarūpasyāvivakṣitatvādapūrvasādhanaviśeṣa eva vivakṣita
iti siddha‍yatyūhaḥ tena saptamādye idaṃ cintyate kiṃ yajiprayuktā utāyajiprayuktā iti ।
iha tu ayajiprayuktatvepi kiṃ karaṇaṃ prayojakamutāpūrvamiti cintyate---</p>
<p>tatra pūrvapakṣī karaṇameva svānugrahamapekṣata iti manyate । <q>rāddhāntī tu</q> karaṇa-
vat tadanugrahamapi kāryamevākāṅkṣati tasyaiva cikīrṣitatvāditi ।</p>
<p><q>atha kasmādidamevāyajiprayuktatvaṃ tat saptamādye siddhāntatvena na
likhitam ?</q></p>
<p>uttaraṃ-<q>asthāyitvādasyārthasya</q> । sāmānyenāyajiprayuktatvamasthāyi । kintva-
pūrvaprayuktatvameva sthāyi । sthāyī ca pakṣaḥ siddhāntatvenopanyasanīyaḥ śiṣyāṇāṃ bhrama-
nivṛttyartham । ato'yamevāpūrvaprayuktatāpakṣaḥ sthāyī saṃvyavahārārthamatrānīta iti hetora-
pūrvaprayuktatvamuktam । yadyayajiprayuktatvamasthāyi kimarthaṃ saptamādye taccintyata ityupanyastaṃ
tadāha---<q>asthāyinaḥ punarupanyāsaḥ kimarthaḥ ?</q> uttaraṃ - <q>punaruktiparihāraśca</q> ।
ca śabdastuśabdārthe । <q>kimetāvadeva prayojanam ?</q> uttaraṃ---<q>anyadastīti
hantipiṣṭa‍yadhikaraṇe vakṣyāmaḥ</q> । tatra pūrvapakṣaupayikamidam । athavā anyāmeva
cintāṃ ityetadbhāṣyakāreṇa yajinimittatānirāsārthamuktam । <q>tadayuktam---yaji-
nimittatve hyatideśo'pi na siddha‍yati na kevalamūhaḥ tasmādūhalakṣaṇa evāya-
mupanyāsa iti na śakyate vak‍tum</q> । asyārthaḥ---darśapūrṇamāsayajernimittatve
sati tadabhāve vikṛtau codakaprāptānāmapi sarvadharmāṇāmevānanuṣṭhānam bhedanābhāva iva
bhedanahomasya । tataśca kimatideśeneti atideśābhāvo'pi ।</p>
﻿<pb n="213"/>
<p>na kevalamūhābhāvaḥ tenohalakṣaṇa eva nedaṃ yuktaṃ cintayituṃ, atideśa-
lakṣaṇe'pi yuktā cintā । pariharati---<q>ucyate । satyamāha bhavān atideśo'pi
na siddha‍yatīti । saptamādyena tvadhikaraṇena idamapaunarukta‍yam</q> । asyārthaḥ---
na vayaṃ brūmaḥ ūhalakṣaṇa eveyaṃ cintopakāriṇīti । kintu punaruktatāparihāro-
payuktaḥ । apūrvaprayuktatve hi pratiprakaraṇaṃ niyamasiddhiḥ iti saptamādyena, iha tu yajerni-
mittatānirāsaḥ kṛtaḥ tenāpaunaruktyam । <q>kiṃ punarasya parihārāntarasya prayojanaṃ ?</q>
uttaraṃ---<q>idameva vakṣyamāṇaṃ prayojanam</q> । nimittāntare yajyantare prayuktasyāpi
codakaprāptasya dharmajātasya nimittābhāvādananuṣṭhānaṃ prāptaṃ tasyānanuṣṭhānasya vyudāso
vaktavya ityabhiprāyo varṇakāntaraṃ kurvataḥ so'yamananuṣṭhānavyudāsaḥ parihāraśca tenocyate-
tatreti vākyopanyāse । bhāṣyakāro varṇakakāyopanyāsānantaraṃ parihāradvayamekenaiva
varṇakena varṇitavān idānīṃ kiṃ yajiprayuktā utāpūrvaprayuktā iti cintyata ityevamādinā
bhāṣyeṇa ।</p>
<p>atra bhāṣya eva yāgaṃ kuryāditi yajisvarūpaprayuktatoktā । evaṃ yāgena
kuryāditi karaṇaprayuktatoktā । tṛtīyaḥ prakāro varṇa/?/kāntareṇa varṇitaḥ evaṃ
vetyādinā । bhinnaga ityuktamityasyārtha ityetat । <q>varṇakāntaraṃ bhāṣyakāreṇoktam</q> ।
bhāṣyoktā eva pūrvapakṣā iti yāvat ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 2 ।। saṃskāre yujyamānānāṃ tādarthyāt tatprayuktaṃ syāt ।। 2 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>ऩnu coktamapūrvaṃ prayojakam । nimittatve tvādye prayojakatvaṃ varṇakadvaye,
nimittatvaṃ ca tṛtīye varṇake'pūrvasyaivoktam । keyaṃ cintā ? kiṃ hantipiṣi-
prayuk‍taṃ prokṣaṇaṃ utāpūrvaprayuktamiti । ucyate । pūrvapakṣo'bhyadhiko'tra
vidyate । kathaṃ ?</q> uttaraṃ---<q>apūrvaṃ hi sādhyatayā sambadhyamānaṃ dharmāṇāṃ
prayojakaṃ bhavatīti śakyate vak‍tum</q> । asyārthaḥ - yadyapūrva sādhyatayā dharmaiḥ
saṃbaddhamavagamyate tadā taddharmāṇāṃ prayojakamiti śakyate vak‍tum । yathā ārādupa-
kārakeṣu teṣu prathamamadhikārāpūrvameva sādhyatayā'vagamyate nāvāntarāpūrvamiti tatra
tatroktam । iha punaḥ kriyānirvṛttireva kāryatvenāvagamyate prokṣitābhyāmiti tṛtīyā
nirdeśāt, kriyāpekṣatvāt karaṇabhāvasya । na ca pratīyamānāpi kriyāṃ prati sādhanatā
vivakṣitetyāha---<q>tadaparityāgenaivaidamarthyamuktam</q> । pratīyamānāvāntarakāryāpari-
tyāgena dharmāṇāmapūrvaṃ pratyaidamarthyamuktam <quote>“ye yatra śrūyante tatra bhavanti”</quote> ityatra ।</p>
﻿<pb n="214"/>
<p>nanu yadi kriyāniṣpattirevaiṣāṃ kāryaṃ tadā apūrvāsaṃsparśitve sati ānarthakyaṃ
prāpnoti niyamasya kriyāyāḥ puruṣaiḥ kāryatvenāvagamyamānatvāt । kiṃ tayā niṣpāditayā ?
pariharati---<q>evaṃ tarhi ānarthakyaparihārāyaivāpūrvamupayujyate । na punaḥ
sādhyatayā</q> । asyārthaḥ - na niṣprayojanā kriyāniṣpattiḥ । tatsiddhāvapūrvaniṣpatteḥ ।
tena prokṣaṇādīnāmapūrvasiddhirevārtho na punarapūrve sādhye[rvaṃ sādhyaṃ ?] yathā
dīkṣaṇīyāvāṅ‍‌niyamasya paramāpūrvaṃ prayojanam । na tu tadeva sādhyam । kasmādeva-
mityāha---<q>hantipiṣyorapūrvasambandhitayaiva prokṣaṇavidhāne parihṛta tadānarthakya-
miti nāpūrvaṃ kāryatayā parigṛhyate</q> । yau hantipiṣī apūrvaṃ pratisādhanabhūtau tayoridaṃ
prokṣaṇaṃ sādhanatvena grahītum [gṛhītam ।]</p>
<p>yaduktaṃ hantipiṣṭa‍yadhikaraṇopayogāya ayajiprayuktatvaṃ tadidamuktaṃ bhavati ।
avahantiprayuktatvena, sādhanībhūtāvahantiprayuktatvena parihṛtaḥ । ānarthakyenāpūrva-
prayuktatā śakyate vak‍tum yata evāvāntarakāryameva dharmāṇāṃ kāryaṃ ata eva ye yatra
śrūyanta ityupapannaṃ bhavati । anyathā'[vaghātādeḥ a]pūrvaprayuktatve satyavāntarakāryasya
kāryadvayavirodhenāvivakṣitatve sati ārādupakārakatvena sarvatraiva āgneyāgnīṣomīyopāṃ-
śuyājeṣu syāt prayājādivat । yasmādavahantiprayuktā avahantidharmāḥ tasmādavahantau
nakhanikṛttanenohitavyāḥ । yo nāma mandadhīḥ yathāśrutagrāhī taṃ prati udāharaṇa-
vyāptimāha---<q>sarvāṇyevaivaṃjātīyakāni pratīyamānāvāntarakāryāṇyudāharaṇāni
vrīhīnavahantītyevamādīni</q> । so'yamaṅgasya vrīhyāderdharmaḥ sannapūrvasyopakārako,
nāpūrvadharmo'ṅganāmupakārakaḥ । na caivaṃbhūtaḥ śabdo vidyate yadapūrvaṃ hantipiṃṣibhyāṃ
kriyate tatprokṣaṇena kartavyamiti । <q>yasmāt prokṣitābhyāmavahantīti śrūyate</q>
kriyāniṣpattireva kāryaṃ śrūyate ityarthaḥ । na cāvahantirapi sākṣādapūrvasādhanaṃ yena
tadyuktamavahantiyuktamapūrveṇa saha sāvayavatvena saṃbadhyate । tasmāt kāryāntarānupraveśināṃ
nādhikārakāryeṇa prayuktiḥ sambhavatīti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>atrocyate । nādhikāraprayuktimantareṇopādānasiddhirdharmāṇām । na
vā'nupāttānāmanuṣṭhānam</q> । asyārthaḥ-loke hi sarvasya śabdasyānuṣṭhānopādeyaparatā
dṛṣṭā । yadi vā'pūrvaprayuktatā dharmāṇāṃ na syāt tadā teṣāṃ niyogenopādānaṃ
anuṣṭhānākṣepo na syāt । anutpa(pa)nnānāṃ vā adhikārāpūrvānākṣiptānuṣṭhānānāṃ
anuṣṭhānaprayojanābhāvādanuṣṭhānaṃ na syāt ।</p>
﻿<pb n="215"/>
<p>atrāyaṃ bhāvaḥ-apūrvasādhanatā avahantyādīnāmeva । sā ca vinā prokṣaṇā-
dibhirna siddha‍yatīti tadarthatayā prokṣaṇādyākṣepaḥ । tasmāt sarvaṃ dharmajātamapūrvārtham ।</p>
<p><q>nanu caivaṃ sati viniyogavyavasthaiva na siddha‍yati[na ca avaha]ntyā-
dīnāmeva sāvāntarakāryasyāvivakṣāprasaṅgādityuktam</q> । pariharati---<q>kena
voktamavāntarakāryaṃ na vivakṣyata iti</q> । punaścodayati-<q>kathaṃ vā vivakṣāyā-
mavāntarakāryasya pradhānakāryasya prayojakatvam</q> । pariharati---<q>ucyate ।
avāntarakāryaṃ tāvat kiṃ pradhānāpekṣitaṃ sat kāryaṃ bhavati utānapekṣitaṃ tatra
yadyapekṣitaṃ satkāryaṃ tadā svarūpeṇa kāryatvābhāvāt pradhānakāryameva prayojakaṃ,
athānapekṣitaṃ tadā'vāntarakāryameva prayojakam ।</p>
<p>evaṃ saṃśayya nirṇayamāha---<q>pradhānakāryeṇānapekṣāyāmavāntarakāryataiva na
syāt</q> । tadavāntarakāryamucyate yat pradhānakāryānuguṇatayā kriyate yathā kāṣṭhānāṃ
pākaṃ kartuṃ pravṛttānāṃ jvalanam । na vā vācyamavāntarakāryatā mābhūditi । tanmātrasya
pradhānakāryatve'nuṣṭhānābhāvaprasaṅgāt । tadapekṣāyāṃ tu pradhānakāryāpekṣāyāṃ punastadarthatvena
pradhānakāryārthatvenāvagamāt । tadapāye pradhānakāryāpāye dharmasambandha eva na syāt ।
tenāvāntarakāryepa vivakṣite pradhānakāryasya prayojakatvāvidhānāt avāntarakāryamapi
pratīyamānaṃ vivakṣitam । atha tu upadeśavyavasthaiveyaṃ viniyoge naiveyaṃ vyavasthā-ye yatra
śrūyanta iti na punaḥ prayuktivyavasthā vrīhyādīnāṃ prayuktyā vyavasthaiveyaṃ na siddha‍yatīti
siddhamapūrvaprayuktatvam ।</p>
<p>yuktyantaraṃ vā'pūrvaprayuktatāyāmāha-<q>niyamavidhīnāṃ pradhānānupraveśaścaturthe-
darśitaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ-yadyavaghātādīnāmapūrvaṃ sādhyaṃ syāt tadā vidhānamavakalpate
pramāṇāntareṇāpūrvasādhanatvāparijñānāt । vrīhyādisvarūpasambandhitve tu vidhānameva nāva-
tarati prāptatvāt । na ca niyamārthaṃ vidhānaṃ aśakyatvāt । vināpyavadhātaṃ taṇḍulādi-
nirvṛttidarśanāt apūrvānupraveśitve tu niyamavidhiravakalpate taṇḍulanirvṛttyarthaṃ dalanā-
dyākṣipedapūrvaṃ vihite tadevāpūrva sādhanamiti tadevākṣipyata iti । evaṃ tahi niyama-
vidhīnāmapūrvameva kāryaṃ syādityatrāha---<q>tathābhūtopadeśena ca dvāraniyamastṛtīye
darśitaḥ</q> । vrīhyādisambandhibhūtā dyupadeśenaiva dvārasyāpi niyamastṛtīye darśitaḥ । tena
dvārakāryamapyāśrayaṇīyam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="216"/>
<p>upasaṃharati-<q>ataḥ prokṣitābhyāmavahantītyatra avahantidvāramapūrvaṃ kuryā-
diti śās‍trārthaḥ</q> । tasmāt tatkāryāpanne anyatrāpi dharmāṇāmūhasiddhiriti ।
aviruddhaśca vrīhīnavahantītyupadeśaḥ dvārasyāpi vivakṣitatvāditi sthitam ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ vā</q></p>
<p><q>ihedānīmapūrvārthatvātsarvadharmāṇāṃ paramāpūrvameva[rveṇaiva]prayuktaṃ dharmajāta-
miti pūrvapakṣavādī manyata iti sambandhaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---na laukikarūpārthatā
dharmāṇām vinā dharmaistasya sambhavāt । ato'pūrvārthatvāt dharmāṇāṃ paramāpūrvameva prayoja-
kam । nanvavāntarāpūrvamapyapūrvameva, tena tadapi prayojakaṃ syādityāśaṅkyāha---
<q>sādhikāraṃ vā'pūrvaṃ paramārthataḥ</q> । paramārthataḥ sādhikāramevāpūrvaṃ nānyat ।
etaduktaṃ bhavati---avāntarāpūrvāṇi nāma na santyeva । kintu sādhikārameva kevala-
mapūrvamasti । kuta ityāha-<q>tacchūnyānāṃ</q> adhikāraśūnyānāṃ <q>tadāpatteḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---
adhikāraśūnyānāṃ prayājādīnāmadhikārasannidhau śrutānāṃ tadrūpāpatteḥ । etaduktaṃ
bhavati - niradhikārebhyo yajibhyaḥ parato liṅādayaḥ śrutāḥ adhikārāpūrvamevānuvadantīti ।</p>
<p>nanvevaṃ [adhikāra]śūnyānāmapi yāgā eva dīkṣaṇīyādayo dharmajātaṃ prayuñca-
tāmityatrāha---<q>anāpannatadbhāvaiḥ svadharmaiḥ sambandhānna yāgāḥ svarūpeṇa dharmān
prayuñ‍jate</q> laukikatvāt dharmasambandhitvānupapatteḥ । (dūrotsāritatāṃ vāhana) nāvaghātā-
divat dvārakāryamatropalabhyate ārādupakāritvādeṣāṃ dīkṣaṇīyādyaṅgānām । tenā-
śaṅkāpi nāsti anyasya prayojakatvaṃ prati sākṣādapūrvasādhanatvādeṣāmiti । <q>atrocyate
---satyamuktamanāpannādhikārāṇāṃ na dharmasambandha iti kintu kāryatvamavi-
śiṣṭamavā</q>ntaraniyogasyāpi । sādhyamāna evāsau tadāpattiṃ labhate adhikārasādhanatāṃ
labhate । kuta ityāha---<q>na hi asādhyamānasya rūpamavaghātavallokataḥ siddham</q> ।
yathā laukikamavaghātādirūpaṃ tathā'vāntaraniyogasya rūpam tena tadapi sādhyaṃ vacana-
samadhigamyameva sādhyaṃ ca svabhāvataḥ setikartavyatākasya karaṇasya niṣpādyamiti vacanā-
davagamyate ।</p>
<p>nanu avāntaraniyoga eva nāstītyatrāha---<q>nadhikārāpattirbhedaṃ nirūṇaddhi
anubandhajam</q> kṣaṇikānāṃ yāgānāṃ sādhanatvānupapatteḥ avāntarāpūrvāṇyaṅgīkriyante anu-
bandhabhedabhinnānīti(māṃ)tadāpattyāpi bhedo na viruddha‍yate । <q>adhikāre tvabhedo</q>
﻿<pb n="217"/>
<q>varṇitaḥ</q> । adhikārāvasthāyāṃ tvabhedaḥ । etaduktaṃ bhavati - ekamadhikārāpūrvaṃ sādhyam ।
tatsādhanabhūtāni tu anubandhamedabhinnāni avāntarāpūrvāṇi yāvadanubandhaṃ bahūni
bhidyanta iti ।</p>
<p>nanu bhavantvanubandhabhedabhinnāni apūrvāṇi tathāpi kathaṃ dharmāṇāṃ tadarthatetyāha---
<q>anubandhajaṃ bhedamuddiśya dharmajātamavagamyata ityuktam</q> । yāvatyā vācā kāmayīta
tāvatyā dīkṣaṇīyāyāmanubrūyāditi vāṅ‌niyamo dīkṣaṇīyāyāṃ tāvat sākṣātsambandhaḥ
śrūyate । dīkṣaṇīyāsambandhena ca tatpratyāsannatadapūrvasambandho'vagamyate । tenānu-
bandhabhinnāpūrvoddeśena vidhānāt tadarthatā dharmajātasya ।</p>
<p>upasaṃharati---<q>tasmādadhikārāpatteravāntarāpūrvasyādhikārārthatā</q> । adhi-
kāraprayojanatā dharmāṇāṃ na niṣpādyatayā, avāntarāpūrvaṃ dharmaniṣpādyamiti siddhamavāntara-
niyogārthatvaṃ dharmāṇām । <q>niyogāvagamyasādhyeṣu</q> niyogena liṅgādinā'vagamyaṃ sādhyaṃ
avāntarāpūrvaṃ yeṣu vidyate dīkṣaṇīyādiṣvityarthaḥ । avāntarāpūrvābhāvāt avaghātā-
divat dīkṣaṇīyādiṣu paramāpūrvameva dharmāṇāṃ prayojakamiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>avaghātādivat dravyādidvāreṇa adhikāraidamarthyānupapatteḥ kṣaṇikeṣu dīkṣaṇīyādiṣu
avāntarāpūrvāṇyaṅgīkaraṇīyāni । tāni cā'laukikatvāt śabdāvagamyaniṣpattīni ।
dharmāṇāṃ vākyādibhirupanītānāṃ prayojanamuktam । uktepyarthe kasyacit mandadhiyo
vismṛtirmābhūditi bodhaparihāradvāreṇa uktamevārthaṃ smārayati---<q>nanu ca yāgo'pi
lokata eva siddhaḥ kimidamavaghātādibhirvaiṣamyamiti codyam</q> । parihārastu---
kāryaparyantatāmaṅgīkṛtyālaukikatvamuktam <q>ārādupakārakāṇāṃ nābhidheyatayā</q> । yāga-
śabdābhidheyatayā laukikatvam kintvavāntarāpūrvaparyantatveneti viśeṣo'vaghātādibhiḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 3 ।। phaladevatayośca ।। 4 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>kathaṃ punaratra saṃśayo yāvatā apūrvaprayuktataivātrāpi yukta</q> । uttaraṃ---
<q>mantrābhidhānasāmarthyācca taiḥ svarūpaprayuktataivoktā</q> । asyārthaḥ---mantrastāvat
śrutyā agnyādisvarūpaṃ svargādisvarūpaṃ cāha । tena mantraliṅgena svarūpaprayuktatā
pratibhāti । codanātaśca lakṣaṇā । mantrasyādhikāracodanayā parigrahītatvāt tadanu-
sāreṇāpūrvasambandhisvarūpalakṣaṇā bhātītyevaṃ saṃśayaḥ । punarākṣipati---<q>tadayuktam ।
na codanādṛte'bhidhānaṃ prāp‍noti karmasambandhitayā</q> । asyārthaḥ - yadi mantro'tra
﻿<pb n="218"/>
codanayā parigṛhyate tadā karmasambandhitayā mantreṇārthābhighānaṃ na prāpnoti । na
vā karmasambandhyabhidhānamatra cintyate, karmasambandhi vā'bhidhānaṃ codanānuguṇamiti
lakṣaṇaiva yuktā । tasmādayuktamevādhikaraṇamidam । karmasambandhitve hyapūrvārthatvamuktaṃ
sarvadharmāṇāmiti ihāpi tadeva yuktam । ato devatādvārakaṃ kāryābhidhānamiti
sthitameva ।</p>
<p><q>atrocyate---astyatra saṃśayahetuḥ । tathāhi-phalaṃ tāvanna karmārtha-
tayā codanāvākyepyavagamyate phalasya puruṣārthatvenāvagamāt</q> । tathāpi
kimityāha---<q>yathācoditaṃ ca mantreṇābhidhānamiti svarūpābhidhānāśaṅkā</q> ।
yatkhalu yathābhūtaṃ coditaṃ tat tathābhūtameva mantareṇābhidhātavyam । phalaṃ ca na karmārtha-
tayā coditamiti na tasya karmārthatvenābhidhānam kintu svarūpeṇaiveti svarūpābhidhānā-
śaṅkā । aprayukteśca karmārthatāṃ manyate । yadi karmārthamabhidhānaṃ na syāt tadā mantrasya
prayuktirna syāditi karmārthatā mantrasya । <q>tasmādupapannaḥ saṃśayaḥ</q> ।</p>
<p>atra pūrvapakṣavādī yathācoditamabhidhānaṃ nyāyyamiti manyate । <q>ayathā-
coditābhidhāne</q> yathā coditaṃ tathā'nabhidhāne hi mantrasyāṅgataiva nopapadyate । asama-
vetārthābhidhānāditi hetoḥ । devatāyāṃ punaḥ dātṛtvāśaṅkayā mukhyamabhidhānam ।
phaladātrī devatā । tena sāpi phalakoṭinikṣiptā na karmārthatayā coditā । tena
tasyā api svarūpeṇaivābhidhānamiti vakṣyamāṇaphaladātrī devateti vakṣyāmaḥ ।
tasmānna mantre lakṣaṇā kintu śrutyaiva svargā(nya)[dya]bhidhānamiti । <q>atrocyate-yuktamuktaṃ
yathācoditamabhidhānamiti । nanvevameva codatam । kathaṃ coditam ?</q> uttaraṃ
---<q>samantrakasya karmaṇaḥ idaṃ phalam</q> । asyārthaḥ - yadyapi phalaṃ karmārthaṃ na bhavati
tathāpi tāvat karmasambandhitayaiva cojitam । mantraśca karmāṅgabhūtaḥ anyathā prayuktya-
bhāvāt । <q>evaṃ sati karmadvārakamabhidhānaṃ mantrasya pratīyate</q> । asyārthaḥ-abhidhānasya
karmābhidheyaṃ yat tad‌dvārakamāgneyādikarmābhidhānaṃ mantreṇa pratīyate । <q>etaduktaṃ bhavati</q>
---svargaphalābhidhānadvāreṇa karmaivābhidhīyata iti । mantrakāryataḥ pratyutāyamevārthaḥ
śrauto vartate nimittāpekṣayā lakṣaṇetyucyate । yo hi kāryānvayyarthaḥ sa eva śabdārtha
iti । yadyapi nimittaṃ paramālocyate lakṣaṇeyaṃ tathāpi ayameva pratyuta śrauto'rthaḥ ।
mukhyastvartho niyogāsaṃsparśādaśruta eva śruteratatparatvāt । tasmānnimittāvasthāyāṃ na
lakṣaṇādoṣaḥ kāryapradhānatvānmantrābhidhānasya । viniyogaparyālocanayā yadeva mantrasya
﻿<pb n="219"/>
svakārye tadanuguṇamabhidhānaṃ, iha ca karmābhidhāne yo mantro viniyukta iti karmasambandhi-
tvena lakṣaṇayaiva tadabhidhānam । atra ca phaladātṛtayā phalāṃśanikṣiptāyāmapi devatāyāṃ
satyāṃ na tatprayuktatā'bhidhānasyetyuktam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 4 ।। devatā vā prayojayedatithivadbhojanasya tadarthatvāt ।। 6 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>idānīṃ dātṛtvādibhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ devatāṃ na viniyogārthāṃ manyate
pūrvapakṣavādī</q> । asyārthaḥ-havirdānena guṇavacanaiśca devataivārādhyate । yajerdevatā-
pūjārthatvāt । pūjāyāśca loke pūjyamānārādhanārthatvena darśanāt । tathā guṇavacana-
lakṣaṇāpi stutirloke rājñāmārādhanārthā dṛśyata iti । na ca phalakāmino niṣphalaṃ
devatārādhanamiti devatāyāḥ phaladātṛtvamavagamyate । na ca phalasyānīśānāyāḥ
tadupapadyata iti phalasyāpi seṣṭe iti kalpyate । na ca havira(nu)jñānā devatā
havirdānenārādhyate । na cācetanāyāḥ vigrahavirahiṇyāścaitatsarvamiti bhok‍tṛtvaṃ
caitanyaṃ vigrahavattā ceti sarvamarthādavagamyate । sarvathā yāvatā vinā'syārthasyāyogaḥ
tāvatkalpyate । tena pradhānabhūtā devatā na niyogārthā kintu saiva prādhānyenāvagamya-
mānā dharmajātaṃ svārthatayā gṛhṇatī prayojiketi । etadeva vivarītuṃ codayati---</p>
<p><q>nanu caivaṃ sati sāpekṣatvānmantrāṇāṃ bahu hātavyaṃ bhavati</q> । asyārthaḥ-
śabdastāvat vigrahavattādiṣu na pramāṇam । tasyāpūrve kāryātmani prāmāṇyā । tena
pramāṇāntarāpekṣairmantraiḥ vigrahavattvādiko'rtho vaktavyaḥ । na ca tatpramāṇāntaramastītya-
prāmāṇyāpatteḥ sthitaṃ prāmāṇyādi bahu hātavyaṃ bhavatyasmin pakṣe । pariharati---
<q>ārādhanasyautpattikatvaṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī</q>-asyārthaḥ-asminnadhikaraṇe rāddhānta-
siddhau satyāṃ apūrvaṃ vākyārthaḥ siddha‍yati । yadā tu devatārādhanamevopadiśyate tadā
tatraivautpattikamadhidhāyakatvaṃ ca śabdasya । idamatrākūtam---kāryapratipādakatā loke
śabdasya vyutpannā । tadeva ca kāmī kāryatayā'vabudhyate yatphaladānasamartham ।
ārādhanaṃ vā ārādhyadevatādvāreṇa phaladānasamarthamityārādhanameva kāryatayā śabde-
nābhidhīyata iti tatraiva śabdasya prāmāṇyam । yadā vā ārādhanaṃ śabdena pratīyate
tadā tadbalena vigrahavattādike pramīyamāṇe na kiñcidavahīyate smṛtyupacārānyārtha-
darśanāni caivamupapannāni bhavantītyabhyuccayaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>nanu caivamapi atideśo hīyate yaddhi devatāntarārādhanopāyabhūtaṃ na
tat devatāntare bhavitumarhati</q> asadṛśatvāditi bhāvaḥ । pariharati---<q>hīyatāmeva</q>
﻿<pb n="220"/>
<q>na kācit kṣatiḥ</q> । yata evātideśo hīyate ata evāha yaccāgnau havanaṃ na tat
sūrya iti</q> । sūryāgna‍yorasadṛśatvāt ।</p>
<p><q>kiṃ punaḥ karaṇaṃ sthito'tideśastyajyate ?</q> yāvatā sthitātideśānu-
guṇyāt ayameva pakṣaḥ kimiti na hīyate । uttaraṃ---<q>niyogasiddhau vākyārtha-
bhūtāyāṃ atideśo naiba tyajyate</q> । yadyarādhanenaivopapadyate kiṃ kurmaḥ etadadhi-
karaṇasiddhāntamaṅgīkṛtyātideśaḥ sthāpito nyāyabalāt । pūrvapakṣavelāyāṃ yadi
nopapadyate kiṃ kurmaḥ ? yata evāyaṃ doṣāvahaḥ pakṣo'ta eva tyājyatayopanyasta
ityarthaḥ । pūrvapakṣamupasaṃharati---<q>smṛtyupacārānyārthadarśanaiḥ pūrvapakṣavādī śrutyā
devatābhidhānamāha</q> ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhantastu codanātastāvat yāgeneti pratīyate</q> । asyārthaḥ-asyādhi-
karaṇasya pūrvapakṣadaśāyāṃ yāga eva devatāpūjātmakaḥ kāryatayā'vagamyate । yacca kāryatayā
phalakāmenāvagamyate tena phalaṃ siddha‍yatītyaṅgīkaraṇīyam । tena yāgena svargaṃ kuryāt
svargakāma ityayamarthaḥ svargakāmo yajetetyatra pratīyate ।</p>
<p>pratīyatāṃ kā kṣatirityāha---<q>pramāṇāntarābhāvācca dātṛtvādiṣu na vrīhi-
bhiryajetetivat vyavahitā yāgaśrutiḥ śakyate kalpayitum</q> । yadi hi
pramāṇāntareṇa phaladātṛtvaṃ agna‍yādīnāmavagataṃ bhavet tadā devatāvyavadhānena yāgasya
phalaṃ prati sādhanabhāvo'vagamyeta । na ca dātṛtvādiṣu pramāṇamasti । ārādhanabhūta-
yāgakartavyatopadeśa eva pramāṇamiti cenna, itaretarāśrayaprasaṅgāt । siddhe hi dātṛtve
ārādhanaṃ vākyārtho bhavati । ārādhane ca vākyārthe dātṛtvādikalpaneti । tasmāt
yāgasya phalakāminaṃ prati kāryatayopadeśo nopapadyata iti apūrvameva phaladānasamarthaṃ
kāryatayā śabdena pratipādyata iti tadeva vākyārtha iti siddham ।</p>
<p>yathā ca dātṛtvādiṣu pramāṇāntaraṃ nāsti tathoktaṃ bhāṣye । smṛtyādīnāṃ
tatrāprāmāṇyāt । tasmādapūrvasya vākyārthatvāt yāgasya ca tadviṣayatvāt yadaikasmāda-
pūrvaṃ tadā itarat tadarthamiti nyāyena devatāpi yāgārthā satī apūrvārthā । tasmādida-
mapi devatāsambandhi karmadvārakameva abhidhānakarmabhūtābhidheyadevatādvārakamapūrvasyaivābhi-
dhānamiti sthitat । <q>śeṣamuktam</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 5 ।। dravyasaṅkhyāhetusamudāyaṃ vā śrutisaṃyogāt ।। 11 ।।</l></lg>
﻿<pb n="221"/>
<p><q>sthite tvapūrvaprayuktatve(pi)viniyogasyāvirodhāt kāmāśaṅkāṃ nivarta-
yitumidadhikaraṇam ?</q> asyārthaḥ-hantipiṣyadhikaraṇe sarveṣāmevamādīnāmapūrvaprayuktatva-
muktam । <q>na ca</q> vrīhyādiviniyogavaśena tadākṣipyate ।</p>
<p><q>atrocyate - astyatrāśaṅkā ।</q> tāmāha---<q>yuktaṃ tābat prokṣaṇasya hanti-
piṣibhyāṃ saha sambandhe hantipiṣyoḥ bhāvyārthatayā kāryaparyantatvam ।</q>
asyārthaḥ---apūrvasambandho hi yasyāvagamyate tasyāpūrvaṃ prayojakaṃ bhavati । anyathā'ti-
prasaṅgāt । atra ca prokṣitābhyāmulūkhalamusalābhyāmavahantīti prokṣaṇasya yuktamapūrva-
sambandhitvam bhavyārthatayā hantipiṣṭyoḥ sādhyāntarānupraveśāt prokṣaṇasya ca tatsambandhi-
vāt । phaladevatayośca sādhyasambandhitvāt vyapadeśasyāpūrvasambandhitayaiva hi svargaḥ
phalamityucyate tathā'gnirapi devateti na svarūpeṇa tena tatsambaddhasyāpi mantrasya yuktama-
pūrvasambandhitvam tatsambandhitvācca tatprayuktatvaṃ ca । iha tu dravyasaṅkhyādayo na kārya-
paryantasvabhāvāḥ । nāpi sādhyasambandhitayaiva vyapadiśyante । ato na kāryasambandhitayā
dharmavidhānameṣāṃ bhavati ।</p>
<p>nanu saṃskāro'narthaka ityatrāha---<q>saṃskṛtānāṃ tu bhavati kriyāntare
viniyoga iti ।</q> nanu ca tṛtīye teṣāmarthena ityatra viniyuktānāṃ satāṃ vrīhyādīnāṃ
dharmaviniyoga ityuktam । kathamidamucyate saṃskṛtānāṃ satāṃ viniyogo bhavatviti ।
pariharati---<q>tadevedamākṣipyate ।</q> etadeva vivṛṇoti---<q>tatra tṛtīye ye yatra śrūyante
teṣāmeva dharmā iti viniyogavyavasthā pratipāditā ।</q> kāmāśaṅkāṃ nivartayitu-
mityatrāha---<q>iha siddhena kāryārthatvena virodhamāśaṅkyeti ।</q> kena hetunā tarhi
sā siddha‍yatītyatrāha-<q>virodhābhāvena śrutyādivyavasthoktā ।</q> iha punaḥ śrutyādi-
vyavasthāne'sati kāryagarbho nopapadyate ityākṣipyate ।</p>
<p><q>nanvevaṃ sati</q> yadi kā[rya](ryā)garbhatā nāsti tadā <q>ye yatra śrūyante itye-
tadebādhikaraṇamākṣiptaṃ bhavati ।</q> tathā ca sati pūrvapakṣābhāvenānārambhaṇīyatvāt ।
pariharati-<q>na sarvamadhikaraṇamākṣipyate dravyādiṣu punarākṣipyata</q> iti sambandhaḥ ।
kayā yuktyā ākṣepa ityatrāha - <q>kāryagarbhatā nāstīti virodhāśaṅkāpi nāstī-
tyanayā yukta‍yā ।</q> tasmādaviruddha eva vrīhīn prokṣatītyevamādiṣu viniyogaḥ ।</p>
