<p>nanu caivaṃ sati puruṣārthatā prāpnotyavaghātādīnām । yadi hi kratvarthānāṃ satāṃ
saṃskāraḥ syāt tadā kratvarthatā bhavet yadā tu saṃskṛtānāṃ satāṃ kratvarthatā
﻿<pb n="222"/>
tadānīmakratvarthadravyasambandhāt puruṣārthatā prāpnoti । uttaraṃ---<q>na prāp‍noti
puruṣārthatā ।</q> kasmādevamityāha---<q>śakyate vibhāgo'vagantuṃ amī kratvarthā
amī puruṣārthā iti ।</q> asyārthaḥ---ye vrīhyādayo niruptāsteṣāmeva prakṛtatvenāva-
ghātādisambandho'vagamyate nānyeṣām । ye niruptāste kratvarthāḥ anye cākratvarthā iti
śakyate vibhāgo'vagantum । ataḥ kratvarthavrīhisambandhānna puruṣārthatāvaghātādīnām ।
punarapi codayati---<q>nirvāpe kathaṃ ?</q> asyārthaḥ - nirvāpe tarhi kathamapuruṣārthatā ।
nahi tatrānyassaṃskāro'sti yatsaṃskṛtadravyasambandhāt apūrvārthatā syāt nirvāpasyā-
grimattvāt ।</p>
<p>pariharati---<q>tatrāpi nirvāpapṛthaktvāt siddhamapuruṣārthatvam ।</q> dvāvetau
nirvāpau staḥ yaḥ puruṣārtho yaśca kratvarthaḥ । kaḥpunaḥ kratvarthaḥ ? yaḥ kratvarthe dravye kriyate
yasya kratuḥ prayojanam tatkratvarthaṃ dravyam । tasmādaviruddha eva viniyogaḥ kāryeṇeti
akāryaprayuktatāṃ pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । atrocyate---<q>atrāpi kāryaprayuktataiba
nyāyyā ।</q> anyathā hi yadi kāryaprayuktatā na syāt tadā niyamaniyogo na sampāditaḥ
syāt । niyogo hi tadevānuṣṭhāpayati । yacca niyogasiddhāvaṅgaṃ yena ca vinā'ṅgasiddhireva
na syāt । tatra tāvat pūrvapakṣe avaghātādayo niyogasiddhau nāṅgabhūtāḥ । na ca tairvinā
aṅgasya kasyacidasiddhiḥ । avaghātādivyatirekeṇāpi puroḍāśasiddheḥ । tataścāva-
ghātādiniyamavidhiḥ nānuṣṭhitaḥ syāt । anuṣṭhānaparyantatā cā'vagamyate । tenāpūrva-
prayuktatā''śrayaṇīyā । yaccādhikārāntaraṃ vā kalpyaṃ avaghātādiviṣayaṃ, na ca sannidhānāt
kāryabhedo'vagamyamāno bhinna iti śakyate vaktum । adhikāravidhisannidhau niradhikāreṣu
śruteṣu sa evādhikāro buddhau viparivartata iti nādhikārāntarakalpanā śakyā । tasmā-
nnādhikārāntarakalpanāṃ sahate niyogo yathā sannihitādhikārapraveśo bhavati tathā varṇanīya-
miti tatprayuktataiva nyāyyā । tatprayuktatve ca vrīhiśabdo'pi tatsādhanaviśeṣalakṣaṇārtha
eva varṇanīyaḥ । yata eva prathamamapūrvagrahaṇaṃ paścāttadīyasādhanaviśeṣaviniyogaḥ ata
eva darśapūrṇamāsāvudāhṛtya viniyogavyavasthoktā grāhakapūrvakaṃ viniyogaṃ darśayitum ।</p>
<p>nanu viniyogavyavasthāyāmapūrvakāryatā virudhyate kāryadvayānupapatterityatrāha---
<q>kāryavirodhinī ca seti teṣāmarthenetyatra pratipāditam ।</q> avahantyādiṣvapi
naiva padārthānuguṇatā heturapūrvaprayuk‍tatve prokṣaṇādīnām । kintu niyamaniyogasiddhireva ।
tasmāt tulyatvāddhetoḥ na vaiṣamyam prokṣitābhyāmavahantītyasya vrīhīnavahanītyādinā ।
﻿<pb n="223"/>
tadevamihādhikaraṇe sannipatyopakārakāṇāṃ grāhakapūrvako viniyoga iti pratipādyate
ārādupakārakāṇāṃ tu saptamādye ityavahitena manasā1 brahmavidyevānusandheyam ।</p>
<p>iyamabhyuccayayuktiḥ । puruṣārthatā'vahantyādīnāṃ prāpnotīti sādhayituṃ pūrvapakṣoktaṃ
samādhānamanubhāṣya dūṣayati-<q>yadapi ca prakṛtalakṣaṇaṃ prakaraṇamaṅgīkṛtya kāryagarbhatā
'panīyate</q> tadapanayanaṃ niyamaniyogasiddherayuktamityuktam । nirvāpe cāsambhavāt prakṛta-
lakṣaṇasya prakaraṇasya । na hi tatra kiñcit prakṛtamasti yena kratvarthatā syāt ।</p>
<p><q>nanu nirvāpabhedādeva sambhava uktaḥ । sa eva</q> nirvāpabhedo bhinneṣu na sambha-
vati । na hi nirvāpatvāt kratvarthapuruṣārthabhedo vrīhīṇāmastītyasambhavaḥ prakṛtalakṣaṇasya
prakaraṇasya । nirvāpe ya eva vrīhayaḥ puruṣārthāsta eva kratvarthena nirvāpeṇa kratvarthāḥ
kriyante । pūrvapakṣāvasthāyāṃ tu nirvāpasyākratvarthatvāt na sambhavatīti puruṣārthadravya-
sambandhānnirvāpaḥ puruṣārthaḥsyāt । tasmin puruṣārthe prokṣaṇamapi prakṛtaniruptavrīhisambandhāt
puruṣārthamityanena krameṇa sarveṣāṃ puruṣārthatā । <q>śeṣamuktam ।</q></p>
<lg><l>।। 6 ।। deśabaddhamupāṃśutvaṃ teṣāṃ syācchrutinirdeśāt
tasya ca tatra bhāvāt ।। 20 ।।</l></lg>
<p>sthite apūrvaprayuktatve kiṃ dīkṣaṇīyāvāṅ‌niyamavat dharmasambaddhānā-
madhikāreṇaikatāpattiraṅganiyogānāṃ uta adhikārāpannānāmayaṃ dharmasambandha</q>
ityanena bhāṣyakārīyaḥ saṃśayagrantho vyākhyātaḥ । yadi hi dharmasambaddhānāṃ satāmavāntara-
niyogānāmadhikāraniyogasambandho dīkṣaṇīyāvāṅ‍‌niyamavat tadā avāntarāpūrvaprayuktatvaṃ,
athādhikāraṃ prati sādhanībhūtānāmevāyaṃ dharmasambandhastadā avaghātādivat paramāpūrva-
prayuktatvam । <q>tatra pūrvapakṣavādī yajñaikadeśasambandhaṃ manvānaḥ adhikāraikatāpa-
nnānāmayaṃ dharma iti manyate ।</q></p>
<p>asyārthaḥ---<quote>‘‘tsarā vā eṣā yajñasya tasmāt yatkiñcit prācīnaṃ tenopāṃśu
caranti’’</quote> ityatra yajñaśabdasya prācīnaśabdena saha sambandhaḥ anyathāhi tsarāśabdena
sambandhe arthavādapadaśeṣatā syāt । prācīnapadasambandhe tu vidhipadaśeṣatāsāmānyāt
pravṛttiviśeṣakaratvāt । tasmādyajñasya yatprācīnaṃ tenopāṃśu carantīti yajñasambaddhānāmevāyaṃ
<note>1. anūdyasanghe---A</note>
﻿<pb n="224"/>
dharma iti paramāpūrvaprayuktatāṃ pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । deśena hi tadāpattirlabhyata ityabhiprāyaḥ ।
<q>avāntaraniyogapare tu vākye deśaniyogasambandho'nyārthaḥsyāt ।</q> asyārthaḥ-
yajñasya prācīnamiti yo'yaṃ deśaniyogasambandhaḥ pratīyate tatra niyogasambaddhāvasthā-
nyavāntarāpūrvāṇi pratīyante । tena tadavasthānāmeva dharmasambandhaḥ । yadi svarūpamā-
treṇāvāntarāpūrvāṇāṃ dharmasambandhārthameva vākyaṃ syāt tadā sambandhāvasthā svarūpamātro-
palakṣaṇārthā satī anyārthā syāt । na ca svārthatve sambhavati anyārthatā nyāyā ।।</p>
<lg><l>।। 6 ।। praṇītādi tatheti cet ।। 23 ।।</l></lg>
<p>rāddhāntopakramamidamadhikaraṇam । tatra rāddhāntinā avāntarāpūrvaprayuktyarthaṃ
dṛṣṭānto dattaḥ । yathā praṇītāḥ praṇeṣyan vācaṃ yacchati iti vāṅ‌niyamo'vāntarā-
pūrvaprayuktaḥ tathedamupāṃśutvamiti ।</p>
<p>atra pūrvapakṣabhāṣyaṃ rāddhāntavādyuktavāṅ‌niyamavaiṣamyapradarśanārthaṃ yajñasya śrutatvā-
diti । yaktuṃ tatra vāṅ‌niyamasyāvāntarāpūrvaprayuktatvam yajñasambandhāśravaṇāt । iha ca
yajñasya prācīnamiti śratatvāditi । punaśca vāṅ‌niyamenaiva saha[sāmyo](svasyo)papattyarthaṃ
rāddhāntaikadeśe sthitvā <quote>‘‘nanvidānīmevoktaṃ’’</quote> ityuktam । yajñaśabdaśca yajñaṃ tanvāte
ityudāhṛtaḥ । <quote>‘‘yadadhvaryuyajamānau vācaṃ yacchataḥ tatprajāpaterhṛdayaṃ gatvā yajñaṃ
tanvāte’’</quote> ityarthavādagato yajñaśabda udāhṛtaḥ । yajñaṃ taniṣyantāvadhvaryuyajamānau vācaṃ
yacchata iti kena kena vākyārthapradarśanapareṇa ।</p>
<p>atra codayati---<q>naivopakrame yajñaśabda udāhṛtaḥ na cānantaramuktaḥ ।</q>
rāddhāntopakrame hi praṇītāḥ praṇeṣyan vācaṃ yacchati ityeva tadudāhṛtam tathānubhāṣyeṇa ।
sūtrepi praṇītāvaditi ? cet ityatrāpi yajñaśabdo noktaḥ kathamidamucyate <q>nanvidā-
nīmevoktaṃ yajñaṃ taniṣyantāviti ।</q> parihāramāha---<q>nanvidamacodyam ।</q> eta-
duktaṃ bhavati---nanvidānīmevoktaṃ svayā pūrvapakṣiṇā yatrāpi yajñaśabdaḥ śrūyate sa dharma-
vidhānāyaiva yuktaḥ pravṛttiviśeṣakaratvāt na stutaya iti । asti cātrāpyayaṃ yajña-
śabdaḥ <quote>‘yajñaṃ tanvāta’</quote> iti । idamatrābhipretam---nāyaṃ bhāṣye sambandho-nanvidānī-
meva yajñaṃ taniṣyantāvadhvaryuyajamānau vācaṃ yacchata ityuktamiti । kintu nanvidānīmevoktaṃ
tvayā yatra yajñaśabdaḥ śrūyate sa dharmavidhānāyaiva na stutaya ityadhyāhṛtena sambandhaḥ ।
punaścāsti cātrāpi ayaṃ yajñaśabdo yajñaṃ taniṣyantāviti tenātrāpi yajñasambandhāvasthā-
﻿<pb n="225"/>
nāmeva vāṅ‌niyamasambandha ityatrāpi paramāpūrvaprayuktataiva syādityevaṃ bhāṣyamuktvā puna-
rvaiṣamyābhidhānamaduṣṭam । satyamatrāpi yajñaśabdosti vidhiśeṣaśca । tathāpi vistāra-
sambaddho'sau । tena yajñaṃ vistārayituṃ vāṅ‌niyamaḥ kartavyaḥ । padārthasambandhe ca
yajñasya vistāra iti padārthasambandha eva yuktaḥ । sa paramāpūrvasambandhaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>kathaṃ punarasmin pakṣe vīpsāvagatiḥ ? yatkiñ‍cicchravaṇāt bahūn
prati vyāp‍tumicchā pratīyate sā'vāntarāpūrvārthatve'bakalpate । paramāpūrvārthatve
ca bhāgadharmo'yam । ekaścāsau bhāga iti vīpsāvagamo nopapadyate ।</q> uttaraṃ---
<q>arthaprāptatvādavivakṣetyabhiprāyaḥ ।</q> arthaprāptānuvādo'yamityarthaḥ । kathaṃ punaḥ
prāptirityāha---<q>deśasambandhepi hi padārthamukhenaivādhikārasambandha ityupapadyate
vīpsā ।</q></p>
<p>atra rāddhāntopakrame tasya ca tatra bhāvāditi sūtrāvayavaṃ vyācakṣāṇena sanni-
patyopakārapradarśanaṃ kṛtaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa । paraṃ na kevalārādupakārakasyaivāvāntarāpūrvasyāyaṃ
dharmaḥ । kintu tasya ca sannipatyopakārakasvāpūrvasyāyaṃ dharmaḥ tatra deśe dvayorbhāvāditi ।</p>
<p>tatra codayati---<q>nanu caibamapi sūtrārtho gacchatyeva ।</q> tasya cāvāntara-
niyogasya tatra bhāvāt tatprayuktamupāṃśutvamityarthaḥ sūtrāvayavaḥ । pariharati---<q>satyamevaṃ
sūtrārtho gacchati nirākaraṇīyastvartho nāsti ।</q> yannirākaraṇārtho'yaṃ sūtrāvayavaḥ
syāt । na cāsāvasti yannirākaraṇārthaḥ sūtrāvayavaḥ । tena mandaprayojanatā syāt ।</p>
<p><q>kathaṃ nirākaraṇīyo'rtho nāsti ?</q> uttaraṃ---<q>tasyāvāntarāpūrvasyābhāvo
vispaṣṭatvānna śakyata āśaṅkitum ।</q> yadi hi avāntarāpūrvasyābhāvāśaṅkā syāt
tadā tannirākaraṇārthaṃ sūtrāvayavaḥ syāt na cāsāvasti । yuktyantaraṃ bāhyaviśeṣeṇa
cāprāptirvaktavyā । na kevalamārādupakārakasya ubhayavidhasyāyaṃ dharma iti vaktavyam ।
yadi hi tathā nocyeta tadā kasya cinmandasya kevalārādupakārakadharmatvāśaṅkaiva syāt
iti yathābhāṣyameva sūtravyākhyānaṃ yuktam ।</p>
<p>idānīṃ rāddhānto'bhidhīyate---<q>dharmavatāmekatāvagatiryuktā । kutaḥ ?
ekatāpannānāṃ dharmasambandhe pramāṇābhāvāt ।</q> nanu ca yajñasya prācīnamiti sambandhāva-
gamaḥ pramāṇamupanyastam । pariharati---<q>tulyamavāntarāpūrvasambandhe'pi ekatvādya-
jñasya</q> prācīnamityupalakṣaṇārthametat । tenopāṃśu carantīti dharmavidheḥ tenopalakṣaṇatayā
﻿<pb n="226"/>
yajñasambandho nānupapannaḥ । yuktyantaraṃ cāha---<q>stutyā vā''nantaryeṇa sambandhāva-
gamāt ।</q> tasmādityanena śabdena vyavadhānādyajñaśabdaḥ prācīnaśabdena saha na
sambadhyate, kintvānantaryeṇa tsarāśabdenaivāsya sambandhaḥ । tena yajñasambaddhānāṃ
upāṃśutvaṃ na pratīyate ।</p>
<p>nanu stutisambandhe'pi śākunikadṛṣṭāntena yajñārthamevopāṃśutvaṃ pratīyate । yathā
śākunikasya tsarā śakunipratyayāya yajñasyāpi tsarā yajñaprāpta‍yarthaivetyāśaṅkyāha---
<q>dṛṣṭena cārthena stutyupapattiḥ ।</q> padārthadharmatve hi dṛṣṭenaivārthena yajñaprāpta‍yarthatvaṃ upāṃśu-
tvenāśithilaprayat‍nai sukhena padārthān aṅgabhūtānupakurvadbhiḥ sukhena yajñaḥ prāpyate ।
padārthasambandhābhāve tu adṛṣṭenopakāreṇopāṃśutvasya yajñaprāpta‍yarthatā syāt ।</p>
<p>rāddhānte'bhyuccayamāha---<q>avaśyaṃbhāvitvādyajñapadārthasambandhasya sākṣāddeśa-
sambandhasyāvidyamānatvāt varaṃ prathamaṃ padārthasambandha eva ।</q> yaccoktaṃ pūrvapadārtha-
sambandha eva । yaccoktaṃ pūrvapakṣe vīpsārtho'nuvāda iti tatrāha---<q>vīpsārthāvivakṣāyā-
mayameva doṣo yaduta tasya satyāṃ vivakṣāyāṃ avivakṣeti ।</q> atassiddhaṃ dharmavatā-
madhikārāpattiriti ।</p>
<p>atra bhāṣyakāreṇoktaṃ---<quote>‘‘nanu dīkṣaṇīyādiṣvanyadeva svarāntaramastī’’</quote>ti ।
tadasambaddham । na hi tat pūrvapakṣe rāddhānte vā upayuktam ityāśaṅkyāha---<q>nanu
dīkṣaṇīyādiṣvanyadeva svarāntaramasti vihitaṃ ityetena granthena yā'tra prāpta‍ya-
prāpticintā viniyogāviniyogacintā dīkṣaṇīyādiṣu pradhāneṣu viśeṣa-
vihitaṃ svarāntaramastīti naitadasambaddham ।</q> svarāntarāvaruddhe upāṃśutvasyā-
<q>viniyogaḥ ।</q> tadaṅgāpūrveṣu tu viniyoga iti sā kāryabhedasiddha‍yarthā । anyatra
tṛtīye siddhā saṃvyavahārārthaṃ likhitā । samyagrāddhāntena vyavahartumidamuktam । śeṣaṃ
saha prayojanenoktam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 7 ।। agnidharmaḥ pratīṣṭakaṃ saṅghātāt paurṇamāsīvat ।। 26 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>kimidaṃ kāryacintayā dravyāntaraṃ cintyate ?</q> asmin ṣaṭke kārya-
taścintā । tathā'sminnadhyāye tatsiddha‍yarthaṃ dvārakāryacintā kāryārthā । tena ṣaṭke
adhyāye ca neyaṃ dravyāntaracintā saṅgateti । uttaraṃ-<q>kāryasiddha‍yamarthamidaṃ dravyāntaraṃ
cintyata iti bramaḥ ।</q></p>
﻿<pb n="227"/>
<p><q>kiṃ tatkāryaṃ yadarthaiṣā cintā ?</q> uttaraṃ---<q>agniṃ prokṣatīti kimasya
pratīṣṭakaṃ kāryaṃ utaikameveti ।</q> yadi dravyāntaramasti tadā tadeva prokṣaṇīyamiti
ekaṃ kāryam । dravyāntarābhāve pratīṣṭakaṃ kāryam । tadā hi iṣṭakā eva prokṣaṇīyāḥ
tadarthaṃ dravyāntaracintā । pūrvapakṣamāha---<q>atra dravyāntaravidāṃ ye avayavebhyo'va-
yavibhūtaṃ dravyāntaraṃ vadanti vaiśeṣikāḥ teṣāṃ pakvāmasaṃyoge dravyāntaraṃ na
bhavatīti</q> rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<p>atra ceṣṭakāḥ pakvāḥ purīṣamapakvaṃ tena tatsaṃyoge dravyāntaraṃ nāsti । nacaivaṃ
pratyakṣaikabuddhiḥ kathamupapādanīyetyabhiprāyeṇāha---<q>kā punaratropapattiḥ pratyakṣabuddheḥ ?</q> ।
uttaraṃ---<q>samudāyālambanaivātrākṣajā</q> buddhiḥ pulakādiṣvava na punararthāntarāpekṣiṇī ।
avayavabhūtābhyaḥ iṣṭakāmyo'rthāntaramavayavidravyamapekṣya vā buddhirna bhavati yathā devadattā-
diṣviti vaidharmyadṛṣṭantaḥ । tasmānna dravyāntaram ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu bacanāttāvadavagamyate iṣṭakābhiragniṃ cinuta iti ।</q> anyathā
hi iṣṭakābhiścinuta iti syāt । yathāyamabhiprāyaḥ avyatireke'pi vyatirekaśabdaḥ-
prayujyate yathā śilāputrakasya śarīramityevamādiṣu iti । satyaṃ yatra spaṣṭa evābhāvaḥ tatra
hi dravyāntarābhāvāt vyatirekābhāvāt avyatirekabadbhāva eba nyāyyaḥ । iha punaḥ
devadattavat iṣṭakānirapekṣaiva citau buddhirutpadyate iti vyatirekavadbhāvakalpanā ।</p>
<p>yathāhi devadatte pāṇyādyavayavanirapekṣā ekabuddhiḥ avayavisadbhāve pramāṇaṃ tathā-
trāpyayamastīti nāvayavyanupapattiḥ śakyate vaktum । pakvāmasaṃyoge'pi dravyāntaramutpadyata
iti darśanabalādaṅgīkaraṇīyam । tena spaṣṭatvāt dravyāntarasya na vyatirekadbhāvakalpanā
kintu vyatireka eveti samāptamadhikaraṇam ।</p>
<p>yastu gautamamatāśrayaṇena sakalāvayavidravyāntarāpahnavaḥ sa vaiśeṣikairniṃrākṛto-
'smābhiśca <q>jātinirṇaye</q> । tadāha---<q>keśoṇḍrakanayaśca dravyāntaravidbhireva
pratyuktaḥ ।</q> yathā avidyamānaḥ keśoṇḍrakaḥ taimirikasyāvabhāti tathā'vayavyapīti yo'yaṃ
keśoṇḍrakanyāyaḥ sa vaiśeṣikairnirākṛtaḥ । yattvanumānamākarṣaṇamuktaṃ yatrāvayavī vidyate
tatraikasminnavayave ākṛṣyamāṇe avayavāntaramapi ākṛṣyate yathā devadattaḥ । iha ca
yaiveṣṭakā ākṛṣyate saivāyāti neṣṭakāntaramapi । tadākarṣaṇamatrānumānaṃ liṅgamuktam ।
tat sthāvareṣvanaikāntikatvāt pratyuktam । vṛkṣādau yaiva śākhā ākṛṣyate saivāyāti
﻿<pb n="228"/>
nānyeti । tena yatrāpyavayavī tatrāpyetadastīti naikāntato'vayavinirākaraṇe samartham ।
tasmādabhinnaṃ kāryaṃ prokṣaṇasyeti siddham ।</p>
<p><q>prayojanamuktam ।</q> paurṇamāsīnidarśanamapi yatpūrvapakṣiṇoktaṃ yathā caturhotrā
paurṇamāsīmabhimṛśediti pratyekamabhimarśanaṃ tathā'gnidharmeṇāpi pratīṣṭakaṃ bhā(ṣya)vyam ।
tadapi parihṛtam । yuktaṃ tatra dravyāntarānārambhāt, iha tu dravyāntaramārabdhamiti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 8 ।। pat‍nīsaṃyājāntatvaṃ sarveṣāmaviśeṣāt ।। 29 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>ūhacintāyāṃ kaḥprasaṅgo'valopasya ।</q> yadi sarveṣāmahnāṃ patnīsaṃyājāntatā
tadā parastāttanānāmaṅgānāmavalopa eva । yadā tu prāguttamādahnaḥ tadā nāvalopa ityava-
lopacinteyamūhalakṣaṇe na saṅgatā । bāghacintātprakatvāditi bhāvaḥ । <q>uttaraṃ---na
khalu kaścidavalopasya prasaṅgaḥ ।</q> kintu avalopa evātra na cintyata iti
hṛdistham ।</p>
<p><q>yadyavalopo'tra na cintyate kathaṃ tarhīdamadhikaraṇam । uttaram---
itthamadhikaraṇam । ayamupadeśo'valopasya uta kāryasyopasaṃhāra iti ।</q>
asyārthaḥ-kimaprāpta evāṅgalopo'yamupadiśyate atha kāryasya karaṇopakārasyopasaṃhāraḥ ।
sakṛdanuṣṭhitairaṅgaissiddhiḥ ।</p>
<p>nanvanyathaiva bhāṣye cinteti yo manyate taṃ pratyāha---<q>yadyayama[va]lopopadeśa-
stadā sarveṣāmahnāmaviśeṣāt pat‍nīsaṃyājāntatā । atha kāryopasaṃhṛtistataḥ
prāguttamādahnaḥ pat‍nīsaṃyājāntatā ।</q> uttame tu pat‍nīsaṃyājebhyaḥ(yasyāḥ)parastā-
ttanānāmapyanuṣṭhānaṃ sarvārthatvena ।</p>
<p>nanvevamapi kā'tra lakṣaṇe saṅgatirityatrāha---<q>upadeśe</q> avalopopadeśapakṣe
<q>yathopadeśaṃ kāryakalpanā ।</q> kāryaprāptirupadeśavaśena bādhanīyetyarthaḥ । tataśca
vikṛtiṣvapi tathaiva kāryam patnīsaṃyājāntaivāṅgarītiḥ । upasaṃhāre tu vikṛtiṣvapi
yathākāryameva tadantatā । sahānuṣṭhānasampattistadantatāyāḥ kāryam । tena yadupottamamahaḥ
tatra tatra tadarthaṃ tadantatā । dvirātra ekasyānhaḥ pat‍nīsaṃyājāntatā, trirātre tu dvayoriti
yathākāryamanuṣṭhānamityūhe saṅgatiḥ ।</p>
<p><q>tatra pūrvapakṣastāvadupadeśābhimānena ।</q> avalopopadeśo'yamityabhimānena
pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="229"/>
<p>nanṛpadeśena kathaṃ sarveṣāṃ tadantatetyatrāha---<q>na hyupadeśe kiñ‍cinniyāmaka-
mastīti sarveṣāṃ tadantatopadeśaḥ ।</q> itiśabdaḥ samāptau । <q>aparaḥ pakṣo
rāddhāntābhāsabhūtaḥ</q> bhavatvayamupadeśastathāpi asaṃsthitaśabdaśravaṇāt prāguttamādahnaḥ
patnīsaṃyājāntatā । evamasaṃsthiterhetutvamupapannaṃ bhavati । evaṃ śrūyate-pat‍nīsaṃyājā-
ntānyahāni santiṣṭhante na barhiranupraharati । asaṃsthito hi tarhi yajñaḥ ityasaṃsthā-
hetukā patnīsaṃyājāntatā kīrtyate । prāguttamādahno yajñasyāsaṃsthā । tena tatraiva
tadantatopadeśa iti ।</p>
<p><q>imaṃ rāddhāntābhāsamasaṃsthānasyārthavādatvena nirākṛtya punaraviśeṣa
uktaḥ ।</q> asyārthaḥ - pat‍nīsaṃyājāntatāstutiriyam । yadi hi pat‍nīsaṃyājāntatā
na syāt tadā cireṇa yajñassantiṣṭhate tena saṃsthito'pyasaṃsthitaprāyaḥ syāt । tasmāda-
valupyantāmaṅganīti । tenāviśeṣāt sarveṣāṃ pat‍nīsaṃyājāntateti ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu naivāyamavalopopadeśaḥ sambhavati । prāptatvāddharma/?/jātasya ।</q>
tadavalope prāptabādhaprasaṅgāt । na cābādhe sambhavati bādho nyāyyaḥ । mūlayuktimāha---
<q>aikaśabdyāda(dya)hargaṇasya dvādaśāhalakṣaṇasya kathamitikartavyatāvistāraḥ saṃhara-
ṇīya ityasyāmākāṅkṣāyāṃ</q> upasaṃhāravidhirevāyamavagamyate, nāprāptasyāvalopasyopa-
deśaḥ । dvādaśāhena prajākāmaṃ yājayedityekaḥ prayogavidhiḥ pratyahaṃ vihitamiti-
kartavyatākalāpaṃ yugapatprayuṅkte । tatprayuktyanusāreṇetikartavyatākalāpastāvat sahānuṣṭhā-
tavyaḥ । sa kena prakāreṇeti prakāraviśeṣākāṅkṣāyāṃ idaṃ vacanamupasaṃhārasya । upasaṃ-
hniyate sahānuṣṭhīyate yata itikartavyatākalāpo yena pat‍nīsaṃyājāntatāvasthānena
tadvidhiravagamyate । apekṣitavidhānāt । yadā vedaṃ pat‍nīsaṃyājāttatāvasthānaṃ iti-
kartavyatopasaṃhāraprayojanaṃ tadā prāguttamādahno vyavatiṣṭhate । evaṃ ca dṛṣṭārthaiva stuti-
rupapannā bhavati । <quote>‘‘pat‍nīsaṃyājāntānyahāni santiṣṭhante na barhiranupraharati asaṃsthito
hi tarhi yajñaḥ’’</quote> iti । yatrāsaṃsthā tatra pat‍nīsaṃyājāntatāvagamyate sā cānena
nyāyena prāptā samāptiḥ pramāṇapratipannatayaiva stutirupapannā bhavati । anyathā yathāva-
gamyamānārthābhāvenānupapannā syāt । vidhānaṃ ca viparītam । itarasmin pakṣe vākyena
vidhānam । ahnāṃ hi samāptirastyeva । tatra copapadārthavidhānaṃ syāt । asmatpakṣe tu
saṃsthānameva vidhīyata iti śrutyā vidhānam । <q>śeṣamuktam ।</q></p>
﻿<pb n="230"/>
<lg><l>।। 9 ।। abhyāsaḥ sāmidhenīnāṃ prāthamyāt sarvadharmaḥ syāt ।। 33 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nanu ca kāryaśūnyatvādṛco dharmasambandha eva nopapadyate । kathaṃ prayukti-
ścintyate ।</q> atra kilādhikaraṇe kimayaṃ ṛgdharmaḥ uta sthānadharma ityanena prakāreṇa
prayuktireva cintyate । ayamabhyāsaḥ ṛk‌prayukta uta sthānaprayukta iti । tacca na
yuktam । akāryatvādṛcaḥ । kāryaṃ hi dharmāṇāṃ prayojakaṃ bhavati nākāryamiti ।
ucyate । <q>kāryayogamaṅgīkṛtyaiṣā cintā na ṛṅ‍mātratayā ।</q> etaduktaṃ bhavati-
yāvatkāryamasyāssādhanabhūtāyāḥ kimayaṃ dharmaḥ, sāmidhenyanuvacanatayaiva uta prathamavacana-
tayaiveti । triḥprathamāmanvāheti yadi pravovā jāsambandho'bhyāsasya tadā darśapūrṇamāsādhi-
kāragṛhītatvāt yadetadīyaṃ pravovājāsādhyaṃ kāryaṃ tatra niviṣṭāyāstasyāḥ ayaṃ dharmaḥ
syāt । yadā tu prathamavacanasambandho'bhyāsasya tadā prathamavacanakāryaniviṣṭāyā iti ।</p>
<p>tatra pūrvapakṣavādī vadati---avaśyaṃ strīliṅgavivakṣā kartavyā । prāthamyamātra-
vivakṣāyāṃ hi padavarṇaṃdharmo'pyāśaṅkyeta ṛca eva dharmo na syāt । tena prathamoddeśena
vidhāne liṅgaṃ viśeṣaṇaṃ vivakṣaṇīyam । ato <q>liṅgenaiva saṃśayavyāvṛtteḥ vivakṣitaṃ
liṅgamityevaṃ</q> vadatīti sambandhaḥ । kena punarliṅgamabhihitaṃ vivakṣitamityāha---<q>striyā-
mabhidheyāyāmityapi pakṣo vidyate ।</q> tena pratyayenāpyate strītvam । tadevaṃ strītvasya
vivakṣitatvāt taddharmo'yam । ṛk‌strī, tasmāttaddharmo'bhyāsa ityevaṃ prāpte <q>abhidhīyate</q> ।</p>
<p><q>nātra liṅgavivakṣopapadyate, prāthamyasyānuvādāsambhavāt vidhāne ca
vākyabhedaprasaṅgāt ।</q> yadi striyamuddiśya dharmavidhistadā prāthamyaṃ tāvat nānṛdyate
aprāptatvāt । nahi prathamaiveyaṃ ṛk । na ca prāthamyaṃ vidhīyate vākyabhedaprasaṅgāt ।
tasmādvaraṃ strītvamavivakṣitamastu ।</p>
<p>nanu tadapi kathamanvīyata ityatrāha---<q>strītvaṃ punaḥ ṛgviṣayatvāt anu-
vacanasya nityaprāptatvāt anṛdyata ityadoṣaḥ ।</q> nanu padavarṇaśaṅkāpi prāpnotītyuktam
tena nāpi strītvamatra nityaprāptam । pariharati---<q>na padavarṇaṃśaṅkā arthaniṣṭhatvāda-
nuvacanasya ।</q> arthapratipattyarthaṃ hi anuvacanaṃ tena yadevārthaṃ pratipādayati tasyaivānu-
vacanaṃ vidhīyate । <q>vākyāccārthāvagatiḥ</q> anekapadasaṅghātātmano vākyādevārthāvagatiḥ
na punarekasmātpadādvā । tena vākyasyaivānuvacanaṃ prāptam vākyaṃ ca ṛk । tena prāptaṃ
strītvamanūdyata ityuktam । striyāṃ yatprātipadikaṃ vartata ityasyārtha ityanenābhiprāyeṇa striyāṃ
﻿<pb n="231"/>
yatpratipadikaṃ vartate tasmāṭṭābādaya ityuktaṃ viśeṣaṇabhūtatvācca strītvasyānuvacanasambandho
nāstītyāha---<q>na ca viśeṣaṇaṃ kriyayā sambadhyate kintu viśeṣyatayaiva</q> ।</p>
<p><q>nanu cābhidheyapakṣo'pyastītyuktam</q> । asyārthaḥ---yadyapi vastusthityā
laṅgasya viśeṣaṇatvaṃ pṛthak‌śabdābhidheyatayā sambandho bhaviṣyati saṅkhyāvaditi ।
pariharati---<q>tathāpi viśeṣaṇasvabhāvo naivāpaiti</q> । pratyayenāpi strītvamabhidhīyamānaṃ
prātipadikārthaviśeṣaṇatayaivocyate iti tasya kriyāsambaṃndhaḥ । tasmāt prāthamyenaivā-
bhyāsasya sambandho yuktaḥ । yuktyantaraṃ cāha <q>yuktaṃ caitat pañcadaśārthasampattyarthā-
vagateḥ</q> । samidhenīnāṃ hi pañcadaśatvasampattyarthe'bhyāse dṛṣṭārthatā bhavati । ataḥ sāmi-
dhenīprathamānuvacanakāryaprayukto'yaṃ dharmaṃ iti sthitam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 10 ।। iṣṭyāvṛttau prayājavadāvartetā''rambhaṇīyā ।। 34 ।।</l></lg>
<p>ādyamadhikaraṇam kimārambhaśabdena karmārambhaḥ karmānuṣṭhānopakrama ucyate uta
ide mayā kartavyamityadhyavasānamityevaprārambhaśabdasyārthaṃ vikalpya varṇitam । tatra karmo-
pakramaḥ śabdārtha iti pūrvapakṣayitvā adhyavasānaṃ śabdārthaḥ ekaṃ ca tat sarvadarśapūrṇa-
māsaprayogāṇāmiti rāddhāntitam । tadida pūrvācāryavyākhyānamayuktaṃ manvānena bhāṣya-
kāreṇa anyathā adhikaraṇaṃ vyākhyātam ।</p>
<p><q>kathaṃ punaridaṃ pūrvācāryavyākhyānamamayuktaṃ manyate</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>nāyamā-
rambhaśabdaḥ kasyacitpadārthasyaikasya pratiniyatasyādyāmavasthāmāha । kiṃ tarhi ?
sarvapadārthānāmeva ādyāmavasthāmācaṣṭe । tataḥ kiṃ ? idaṃ tato bhavati</q> ।
upāttasya sannighāvuccāryaprāṇaḥ tasyaivārambhamavagamayati । darśapūrṇamāsasannidhāvayamuccāryate
<quote>‘‘āgnāvaiṣṇamekādaśakapālaṃ nirvaped‌darśapūrṇamāsāvārapsyamāṇaḥ’’</quote> iti । tena tadārambha
mevāvagamayati । idaṃ mayā kartavyamityadhyavasānaṃ punaḥ sarvapadārthānāṃ sarvakarmaṇāmeva
nityanaimittikakāmyānāmāghānottarakālabhāvināṃ sādhāraṇatvāt naikasyādyāvasthā tayā-
'vagantuṃ śakyate । evaṃ hyasau puruṣasya saṅkalpo yāvadāgnisādhyaṃ me karmopanipatiṣyati
tanmayā kartavyamiti na punardarśapūrṇamāsamātraṃ kartavyamiti । tena sādhāraṇatvāt
darśapūrṇamāsārambhatayā nāvagantuṃ śakyate । ato darśapūrṇamāsārambha eva tadupakrama
eva tadī(yo'yaṃ)[yādya]padārthaprayoga evāyaṃ pratipattavyo'sādhāraṇatvāttasya tadārambha
tayā'vagamāt । nāghyavasānaṃ, <q>viśeṣādṛte vyavahārābhāvādadhyavasānasya</q> ।
﻿<pb n="232"/>
viśeṣābhāve darśapūrṇamāsārambho'yamiti vyavahārābhāvāt । tasmādadhyavasānanimittikā
nārambhaṇīyā । kintu ādyapadārthaprayoganimittikā । tataścāvṛttirevāpadyata iti na
rāddhāntasiddhiḥ ityevaṃ pūrvācāryavyākhyānamayuktam ।</p>
<p><q>nanu bhāṣya[vyākhyā]namapi gatārthamiva dṛśyate । kathaṃ</q> ? uttaraṃ---
<q>sarvameva hi nimittamadhikāriviśeṣaṇatayā'nvetīti bhedanādiṣūktam । katha-
mārambhaḥ śeṣitvenāṅkyate</q> । asyārthaḥ - bhāṣyakāro hyevaṃ vicārayati kimāra-
mbhaṇīyā darśapūrṇamāsayorādyapadārthaṃ samyañcaṃ karoti uta puruṣamārambhayogyamiti ।
tatrārambhasya nimittabhūtatvāt śeṣitvāśaṅkā nopapadyate । ukta hi ṣaṣṭhe । <quote>‘bhedanādīni
nimittabhūtāni na śeṣīṇī’</quote>ti । tena gatārthamidamadhikaraṇaṃ bhāṣyakārīyam । pariharati
---<q>astyatrāśaṅkā yadyayaṃ bhedanavadadhikāraḥ parigṛhyate tadā darśapūrṇamāsādhi-
kṛtaviśeṣaṇavat pratiprayogamāvartate ārambhaṇīyā yathā sati bhedane homaḥ</q> ।
asyārthaḥ - yathā bhinne juhotīti bhedanamadhikāriviśeṣaṇaṃ, yadi tathā''rambhaḥ syāt
tadā darśapūrṇamāsādhikṛ[taḥ] tena viśeṣaṇīyaḥ ārambhavān darśapūrṇamāsādhikṛtaḥ
ārambhaṇīyāṃ kuryāditi । yathā yo bhedanavāt darśapūrṇamāsādhikṛtaḥ sa homaṃ iti ।
tataścādhikārāvṛttau pratiprayogamārambhaṇīyā āvartate yathābhedanahomaḥ । pradhānādhi-
kārānupraveśāt avāntarādhikārasya tadāvṛttāvāvṛttiḥ । yadi tu svatantro'dhikāraḥ
syāt tadā ārambhaṇīyāyā āvṛttirna syāt । <q>athaivaṃ na kalpyate</q> darśapūrṇamāsādhi-
kṛtaviśeṣaṇaṃ na kalpyate tadā adhikārāntaratvāt kāryāntarakalpanā syāt ।
<q>bhavatviti cenna । darśapūrṇamāsaśabdasamabhivyāhārādadhikārāntarānavagatiḥ</q> ।
ekasmin vākye darśapūrṇamāsāvāgnāvaiṣṇavaṃ ca samabhivyāhniyete । tatra vākyena
sambandho'vagamyate । adhikārāntare ca sa bādhito bhavati । tasmānnādhikārāntarā
vagatiḥ । yata evaṃ nimittabhāvepyāvṛttiḥ tasmādvaramādyapadārthasaṃskāratayaivāyaṃ vidhiḥ
kalpitaḥ syāt kimavāntarādhikāreṇa । ārapsyamāna iti varaṃ śeṣiṇameva samarpayatu ।
yadārambhasaṃskārakaṃ tadārambhavataiva kriyata iti puruṣaśravaṇamanuvādaḥ kimavāntarādhikā-
reṇa vṛthā āśritena ।</p>
<p>nanu yadi tulyameva pakṣadvayepi prayojanaṃ kena viśeṣeṇāvāntarādhikārastyajyate
ārambhasaṃskāraḥ parapakṣaśca parigṛhyate tadāha---<q>kiṃ punaravāntarādhikāre gauravaṃ
yena sa tyajyate</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>na khalu kiñ‍cidgauravaṃ, kintvavāntarādhikāra
﻿<pb n="233"/>
eva na sambhabati । kathamasambhavaḥ</q> ? uttaraṃ---<q>nityatvādādyasya padārthasya
nāvāntarādhikārasambhavaḥ</q> । darśapūrṇamāsayorhi ādyaḥ padārtho nityabhūtaḥ anityaṃ
ca viśeṣaṇaṃ bhavati । tena tasyādhikṛtaviśeṣaṇāṃśo nopapadyate । bhedanādīnāṃ tu
anityatvāt yukto'vāntarādhikāraḥ teṣāmadhikṛtaviśeṣaṇatayā vidhānametadyuktamiti pūrva-
pakṣavādī manyate । ataḥ pratiprayogaṃ prayājavadāvṛttiriti yuktam ।</p>
<p>atrocyate---astyatrāvāntarāvikāraprayojanaṃ sakṛdanuṣṭhānarūpam । yathā ca
tatsiddha‍yati । na cedamadhikṛtaviśeṣaṇena bhavati ārapsyamāṇa iti puruṣaviśeṣaṇa-
tvāvagateḥ । tadāha---<q>spaṣṭaścāyamadhikāra iti</q> । nanu tathāpi kimityārambhaḥ śeṣī
na bhavatītyatrāha-<q>na ca nimittaṃ śeṣī(na)bhavitumarhati śeṣitve pramāṇābhāvāt</q> ।</p>
<p><q>nanu nimittametanna bhavati nityatvādādyasya padārthasyetyuktam</q> ।
pariharati---<q>satyaṃ na bhavati nimittaṃ yadyārambhaṇīyā bhedanahomavat karmāṅgaṃ
kalpyeta</q> । yo hyārambhaṇīyāmaṅgamicchati tena darśapūrṇamāsādāvārambha ityāstheyam
nānyathā'ṅgatvasiddhiryataḥ । yaśca darśapūrṇamāsādhikṛtaḥ tasya nedaṃ viśeṣaṇamupapadyate
avyabhicārāt । yastvārambhaṇīyāmaṅgabhūtāṃ necchati na tasya darśapūrṇamāsādhikāro
viśeṣaṇīyaḥ, kintu puruṣātram । na ca sarvaḥ puruṣo darśapurṇamāsārambhavāniti
vyabhicārādyuktaṃ viśeṣaṇam । svatantrādhikāra evāyaṃ na bhavatīti manvāna āha---
<q>kimiti cāsambhāvyamāne cāṅgatve svatantrādhikāre doṣa ukto darśapūrṇamāsa-
samabhivyāhārānnānavagatiruktādhikārāntarasya</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>satyaṃ svatantrādhi-
kāre kalpyamāne bhavatyayaṃ doṣo</q> darśapūrṇamāsasamabhivyāhārabādhātmakaḥ kintu avā-
ntarādhikāra evāyam । nāyamekāntato darśapūrṇamāsādhikārasaṃsparśyadhikāraḥ । kintu
tadupakārakatvādavāntarādhikāra evāyam । na cādyapadārthanityatayā'sya virodhaḥ ।
na cāstyeva nityatayā virodhaḥ । tathāhi---yadi darśapūrṇamāsasamabhivyāhāra
āditastadā tadaṅgamevārambhaṇīyā । tadaṅgatve vā ārambho'pi tadadhikṛtaviśeṣaṇaṃ
bhedanavat । na ca nityasya tadupapadyata iti śaṅkāyāmāha---<q>sarvatra cāṅgāṅgibhāve
niyogaikyaṃ kāraṇam</q> । aṅgaṅginorhi niyogaikye sati aṅgāṅgibhāvo bhavati anyathā
bhinnakāryatve aṅgāṅgibhāvānupapatteḥ ।</p>
<p>bhavatvevaṃ tathāpi kimityāha---<q>na cātra niyogaikye pramāṇamasti
aprakaraṇādhītatvādārambhaṇīyāyāḥ</q> । nanu ārambhasambandhamukhena astyeva tanniyoga-
﻿<pb n="234"/>
pratyabhijñānaṃ yathā parṇamayī juhūrbhavatītyanena abhiprāyeṇāha-<q>kathaṃ nāsti niyogaikye
pramāṇamiti</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>yadi hi svatantrasamabhivyāhṛtaṃ</q> ādyapadārtharūpaṃ ārambha
ityā[rambhaṇīya]yā sahānveti tadā syāt vainiyogikaḥ ādyena padārthena saha tanmukhena
viniyogaikye । iha punarārambhakarturupasarjanībhūtaṃ viśeṣaṇībhūtaṃ ādyapadārtharūpamārabha-
māṇa ityārambhaṇīyayā'nveti । tatrādhikārānvaye sambhavati kimiti vainiyogikaḥ
pirigṛhyate । adhikāriviśeṣaṇatayaivārambhānvayastadviśeṣaṇatvena darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ ।
<q>evamādhikārike sambandhe sati kimiti vainiyogikaḥ parigṛhyate ? prayojana-
bhedo nopapadyate tena parigṛhyata iti ceta ।</q></p>
<p>dūṣayati---<q>sutarāṃ sākṣātpratīyamānādhikāratyāge pramāṇaṃ nāsti ।</q>
na ca prayojanabhedo'pi nāstītyāha---<q>asti ca śabdārthe viśeṣaḥ sakṛt saṃskṛto-
'dhikārī sarvaprayogāṅgatāṃ labhate</q> । asyārthaḥ---adhikāriviśeṣaṇatghepyārambhasya
sādhyatvenaiva viśeṣaṇatvāt svargavat tatsiddha‍yupayogitvamārambhaṇīyāniyogasya । sadhi-
kāre vākye puruṣapradhānaḥ sambandhaḥ iti puruṣārthatvādārambhaṇīyāyāḥ puruṣasyaivārambho-
tpattyanuguṇaḥ saṃskāraḥ ārambhaṇīyayā kriyate । sakṛtsaṃskṛtaśca puruṣo darśaṣūrṇamāsāra-
mbhayogyo jāta iti nārambhaṇīyā''vartate । vainiyogike tu sambandhe[ke]valārambhasaṃskārā-
dārambhasya ca āvṛtterāvṛttiḥ syāt tadāha---<q>vainiyogike punaḥ sambandhe prati-
prayogamāvṛttiriti</q> । iha cedamarthasāram---anārabhyādhītā ārambhaṇīyā । tena
na tāvat sannidhānānniyogaikyam । nāpi parṇatāvat padārthānvayadvāreṇa । adhikāre
puruṣasambandhena puruṣārthatvādārambhaṇoyāyā na sākṣādādyapadārthasambandhaḥ । tena puruṣasyai-
vārambhayogyatāṃ utpādayantī saṃskārikā । na punaḥ kratvaṅgaṃ pramāṇābhāvāt ।</p>
<p>etenedamuktam---ye prayājādiṣvadhikāramāhuḥ teṣāṃ prayājādayo'pi puruṣārthā
eva bhaveyuḥ na kratvarthāḥ tatrārambhaṇīyāvat prayājādibhirapi apūrvodayānuguṇaḥ saṃskāraḥ
kriyate । tadvacca sakṛdanuṣṭhānaṃ teṣāmapi syāditi । dīkṣaṇīyā tu prakaraṇādhītā ।
tena dīkṣiṣyamāṇa iti prakṛtādhikṛtaviśeṣaṇameva । ato niyogaikyājjyotiṣṭo-
māṅgamiti । na ca puruṣasaṃskāradvāreṇāpi kratvanupraveśaḥ svatantrapuruṣasaṃskārāt
sakṛtsaṃskṛtasya sata uttarakālaṃ prayogāṅgatvāt ।</p>
<p><q>yadyevaṃ yadyārambhaṇīyā puruṣasaṃskārikā bhedanahomo'pi kasmāt puruṣa-
saṃskāra eva na kalpyate</q> । uttaraṃ-kalpyamāne'pi pratinimittaṃ <q>vyalīkotpattau
﻿<pb n="235"/>
punaḥ prasaṅgavijñānādāvṛttirevātra</q> । asyārthaḥ---bhinne juhotīti bhedananimitta-
doṣanirharaṇadvāreṇa puruṣaḥ saṃskartavyaḥ । nimittaṃ pratibhedanaṃ doṣotpatteḥ tannirharaṇārthaṃ
punaḥ homaprasaṅgavijñānamastītyāvṛttireva homasya । punaścedanuṣṭhānāviśeṣaḥ tenedaṃ codya-
macodyameva । tatrāpi saṃskāraḥ prakaraṇāt sākṣādadhikṛtasamabhivyāhā[rāt](yoṃ)
<q>bhedanādiṣu nimittānyathānupapattyā tu kalpitaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---na bhedanādīnāṃ
puruṣasambandho yena puruṣasaṃskārakatā syāt । kintu te kratvarthā eva । yadi teṣu sākṣā
dadhikāraḥ śrūyeta tadā bhavedevaṃ, kintu niradhikārā eva, bhedanādīnāṃ nimittatvena-
śravaṇāt । niradhikārasya ca prakaraṇādhītasya kratvarthatvameva । animittatā tu adhikā-
riviśeṣaṇatāmantareṇa na sambhavatīti kratvarthādhikṛtapuruṣaviśeṣaṇatā bhedanādīnāṃ
kalpyate ।</p>
<p>nanu puruṣasaṃskārakatvepi ārambhanimittatvādasyārambhāvṛttau kimityāvṛttirna-
bhavati puruṣasaṃskārabhedanahomavadityāśaṅkyāha---<q>iha punarnimittāntarotpāda eva
na bhavatīti nāvṛttiriti viśeṣaḥ</q> । kasmānnimittāntarotpādo na bhavadītyatrāha---
<q>abhinnatvādādyasya padārthasya</q> । eṣo'bhiprāyaḥ---ādyapadārthānuṣṭhāne yogyatā puruṣasya
ārambhaṇīyayā kriyate । ekaścāsāvādyaḥ padārthaḥ । tena taṃ prati yogyatā na bhinnā
yogyatotpattyarthatā ca puruṣasyārambhaṇīyānuṣṭhāne nimittam । ekā cāsau । tena nimittā-
vṛttyabhāvānnārambhaṇīyāvṛttiḥ । tatra punarabhinnasya bhedanamiti siddho nimittabhedaḥ ।
bhedanāntarotpannavyalīkabhedāt tannirharaṇārthaṃtāpi tatra bhinnaiva । tena puruṣasaṃskārakatve
tatrāvṛttirnimittāvṛtteḥ ।</p>
<p>tadidaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa prayogāntarepi saṃskṛta eva labhyate iti samāne'hanī-
tyapi siddhamiti darśitam । darśapūrṇamāsāvarapsyamāna ityatra lṭṛṭpratyayena anadyatanabhavi-
ṣyadvihitena yasminnevāhani darśapūrṇamāsau kartavyau tasminnevāhani kṛtayā''rambhaṇīyayā
ārambhayogyatā bhavatīti । taccāstyeva । yathā'sau sakṛdārambhaṇīyā kṛtā sā darśapūrṇa-
māsasamānāhassambandhinyeva । yathā caivaṃ tathā daśame yā dīkṣaṇīyādiṣvārambhaṇīyā-
śaṅkā samadhigatā sā somapūrvatvapakṣamāśritya । iṣṭapūrvatve hi saṃskṛtatvāt puruṣasya
nāśaṅkopapadyata ityanavadyam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 11 ।। arthābhidhānasaṃyogānmantreṣu śeṣabhāvaḥ syāt
tatrācoditamaprāptaṃ coditābhidhānāt ।। 36 ।।</l></lg>
﻿<pb n="236"/>
<p>atra kila samavetārthatve dṛṣṭārthateti manvān āha---<q>nanu ca dṛṣṭādṛṣṭārthatvaṃ
mantrāṇāṃ na sambhavatīti saṃśaya evāyuktaḥ</q> । yasmād <quote>‘arthaikatvādekaṃ vākyaṃ
sākāṅkṣaṃ cedvibhāge syāt’</quote> ityuktam । dṛṣṭādṛṣṭārthatve cārthabhedaḥ । tena mantraikyameva na
siddha‍yati । ekasya mantrasya dṛṣṭādṛṣṭārthatvaṃ nopapadyata iti rāddhāntavacanavyakta‍yabhāvāt
saṃśaya evāyamayuktaḥ ।</p>
<p>rāddhānte hi agnaye juṣṭaṃ nirvapāmīti samavetārtham pariśiṣṭamasamavetārtha-
madṛṣṭārthamiti prayojanabheda āpadyate । pariharati---<q>ucyate</q>---naivātra dṛṣṭādṛṣṭārthatayā
pūrvottarapakṣau yathāsaṅkhyaṃ kriyete । rāddhānte pariśiṣṭasyāpi nāsti adṛṣṭārthatvamiti
ekamantratvāvirodhaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>kathaṃ tarhi pūvottarapakṣau kriyete</q> ? uttaraṃ---<q>samavetārthatayā</q> । punaścodayati-
<q>nanu samavetārthatve sati dṛṣṭārthatvamasamavetārthatve tvadṛṣṭārthatvamiti tadevedaṃ
dṛṣṭādṛṣṭārthatvaṃ pūrvottarapakṣayoḥ</q> । pariharati---<q>naitadevam । satyaṃ samavetārthatve
dṛṣṭārthatvaṃ asamavetārthatve tvadṛṣṭārthatā na śakyate vastum</q> । kasmādityāha---
<q>na parārthasyābhidhānasya kāryāntarakalpanā śakyā</q> । stutyarthamapyabhidhānamarthaprati-
pattyarthameva nādṛṣṭārthaṃ śakyate kalpayituṃ pramāṇābhāvāt । etaccārthavādādhikaraṇe uktam ।
<q>yadi siddhānte'pi dṛṣṭārthatā kathaṃ tarhi samavetārthābhidhānaṃ pūrvapakṣavādī
manyate</q> । yadi hi siddhānte adṛṣṭārthatvalobhena yuktaḥ pūrvapakṣaḥ । uttaraṃ---<q>svārthā-
bhidhānalobhāt</q> । na hi svārthatve sambhavati pārārthyaṃ nyāyyāmiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
stutyarthatve hi pārārthyaṃ samavetadevatāprakāśakatve svārthatvaṃ śabdānāmiti svārthatvalobhena
samavetārthatvaṃ pūrvapakṣavādī manyate ।</p>
<p>atra codayati - <q>yuktaṃ svārthatvaṃ māntravarṇikasavitrādidevatākalpanāyāṃ</q>
savitrādipadaiḥ <q>tāsāmevābhidhānāt । gauṇakalpanāyāṃ tu kathaṃ ?</q> yathāhi gauṇyā
vṛttyā agnireva savitrādipadaiḥ pratyāpyate tadā kathaṃ svārthatā ? gauṇo hi śabdaḥ
parārtha eva । uttaraṃ---<q>atrāpi svārthaḥ prayoga iti siddhaṃ na śabdāntarārtham
stutyarthatayā savitrādipadānāmuccāraṇam</q> । kintu tānyeva devatāṃ pratipāda-
yantīti । tena gauṇapakṣe'pi prayogasya svārthatvameveti siddhaṃ svārthatvaṃ pakṣadvaye'pi ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---nātraikāpi kalpanā sambhavati । pārārthyenā-
pyekavākyatvāvagamāt</q> । devatāntarakalpanā gauṇakalpanā vā na sambhavati ।
﻿<pb n="237"/>
stutyarthatayāpyekavākyatvāvagamāt sarvapadānāṃ gamyatāmekavākyatā tathāpi kimityāha-
<q>gamyamāne caikavākyatve siddhaṃ mantrasya samavetārthatvamiti</q> । na pratipadaṃ samavetārtha-
pratipādakatā laghvīti sākṣātpratīyamānaikavākyatā na śakyate'panhotum । tadva-
[śe]na pārārthyameva nyāyyam yathā syonaṃ te <quote>‘ityatrānekavākyatāvagamyate tadā
tadanupraveśasamavetārthabhedena । tathā'trāpi bhavatu ityatrāha---<q>vidyamāne hyarthe vibhajya-
mānasākāṅkṣatvaṃ na nāmāpekṣyate</q> । kalpyamāne cārthe pramāṇābhāvānna tadapekṣatā
śakyate vak‍tum । na hi klṛptāmekavākyatāṃ kalpyo'rthabhedaḥ śaknoti vārayitum ।
syonaṃ ta ityatra bhedo na kalpyaḥ । bhidyamānatvāt sadanakaraṇapuroḍāśapratiṣṭhāpanayoḥ ।
ataḥ siddhaṃ pārārthye'pi keṣāṃcitpadānāṃ mantrasya samavetārthatvam ।</p>
<p>kathaṃ punaḥ savitrādipadānāṃ stutyarthatvamityatrāha---<q>pārārthyaṃ ca darśitaṃ
bhāṣyakāreṇa</q> । savitrādipadāni yajamānaparatvena stutau varṇitāni । tatra ca puna-
rāśaṅkitaṃ yadi yajamānaparāṇyetāni evaṃ tarhi yajamānāśraya ūhaḥ prāpnoti । tatra
ko heturityatrāha---<q>yajamānapakṣa ūhāśaṅkā prasavabalāt</q> । prasavo'nujñā yajamāna-
sambandhinī kīrtyata iti bahuyajamānaprasavakīrtanāya savitrādipade vacanohaḥ śaṅkitaḥ ।
<q>sā cohaśaṅkā'vivakṣāyāmapi prasavasyopapadyata eva prasavakīrtanamiti nādṛtā</q> ।
nirākṛtetyarthaḥ । yadi vivakṣitatā syāt tadā anyatrāpi kīrtanārthamūhaḥ syāt ।
avivakṣitatve tu naitatprakāśane prayojanamastītyanūhaḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 12 ।। guṇaśabdastatheti cet ।। 38 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>yadi savitrādayaśśabdāḥ nirvāpaikavākyatvādanyārthāḥ evaṃ tarhi
juṣṭāgniśabdāvapi anyārthāveva । tataścāsamavetārthatvaṃ asamavetārthatve cānūhaḥ ।</q>
asyārthaḥ---yadyapyagniḥ samaveta eva karmaṇi tathāpi yajñapatiṃ vardhānitivat
parārthatvāt mantreṇa samavetatvena nābhidhīyate । parārthatā ca nirvāpaviśeṣaṇatvenābhi-
dhānāt । asamavetārthatve ca yajñapatiśabdavadanūhaḥ ।</p>
<p>atra bhāṣyakāro'gniśabdasyaivānūhamāha na juṣṭaśabdasya । tatra kāraṇaṃ
pṛcchati---<q>kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇamagniśabdasyaivānūhaṃ bravīti । na juṣṭaśabdasyāpi</q> ।
uttaraṃ---samavetārthatvepyasambhavāt siddhānte pūrvapakṣe ca juṣṭaśabdenohaḥ</q> । tena
viśeṣābhāvāt tasyānūho nocyate ।</p>
﻿<pb n="238"/>
<p><q>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate</q>---satyaṃ nirvāpeṇaikavākyatvaṃ tathāpi devatā svārthatayaiva
nirvāpamākṣipantī tenaikavākyatāṃ yatīti na pārārthyaṃ śakyate vak‍tum । nirvāpeṇa
vinā yāgābhāvāt devatā svārthaṃ nirvāpamākṣipatīti na parārtho'gniḥ । apārārthye ca
samavetārthatvaṃ samavetārthatve ca vikṛtāvūha iti siddham । na ca ajuṣṭe juṣṭavacana-
mayuktaṃ nirvāpeṇa juṣṭateti । na prāṅ‌nirvāpādajuṣṭateti pariharati---<q>naivedamajuṣṭe
juṣṭavacanaṃ</q> kāryatvena juṣṭārthāvagamāt nirvāpeṇa juṣṭaṃ karomīti sambandhaḥ । na punaḥ
prāṅ‌nirvāpāt juṣṭaṃ santaṃ nirvapāmīti । yata evamabhisambandhaḥ ato'yamāśaṃsāyāṃ
bhūtavaccetyasya viṣayaḥ kāryasyāśaṃsanīyatvāt ।</p>
<p><q>।। evaṃ vā ।।</q></p>
<p><q>atra mukhye gauṇe vā'bhidhāne'sambhava iti kimadṛṣṭārtho bhavedayaṃ mantraḥ
dhānyamasīti taṇḍulāvāpe uta lakṣaṇayāpi tāvat samavetārthataiva nyāyyeti
cintyate</q>---dhānyaśabdena gauṇyā vṛttyā mukhyayā vā taṇḍulābhidhānāsambhavāt
taṇḍalāvāpe kimayamadṛṣṭārtho bhavenmantraḥ uta dhānyasambandhitvāttaṇḍulānāṃ dhānyaśabdo
lakṣaṇayā taṇḍulān pratipādayatīti samavetārtha evāyaṃ mantro bhavatviti cintā ।</p>
<p><q>tatra pūrvapakṣavādī prayogasyaidamarthyābhāvāt adṛṣṭārthatāṃ manyate ।</q>
asyārthaḥ---yadi lakṣaṇayā dhānyaśabdaḥ taṇḍulān pratipādayet tadā dṛṣṭārtho
bhavenmantraḥ lakṣaṇāpi prayogaidamarththajñāne sati bhavati । na cātra dhānyaśabdastaṇḍulaprati-
pādanaparatvena prayukta iti pramāṇamasti । tena lakṣaṇānupapatteradṛṣṭārtha eva mantra iti ।</p>
<p>kathaṃ punaḥ prayogaidamarthyānnāvagamyate dṛṣṭārthatetyatrāha---<q>prayogapradhāno hi
vākyārthaḥ tadabhāve</q> aśāvdyeva kāryakalpanā prāpnoti । prayogo hi vākyārthā-
vagame pradhānaṃ kāraṇam prayogābhāve taṇḍulaprakāśanaṃ kāryamiti śabdaśūnyaiva kalpanā ।
na ca viniyogo no(so)papadyate adṛṣṭenāpi dvāreṇa tadupapatteḥ । tasmādadṛṣṭārthataiva ।
idaṃ cātrabhipretam । viniyogena mantrasya tādarthyamavasīyate na padasya । padatātparya-
mūlā ca lakṣaṇopapattirityabhidhāyakatvenopayogābhāvāt adṛṣṭenaiva dvāreṇa viniyogo
mantrasyeti ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyate---nādṛṣṭārthatā sambhavati । kasmādityatrāha---<q>na hi lakṣaṇā
lokavatpratipattihetutayā vārayituṃ śakyate । yathā śālayo bhujyanta
﻿<pb n="239"/>
iti</q> । asyārthaḥ - yadi lakṣaṇā pratipattihetutayā vārayituṃ pāryate tadā adṛṣṭārthatā
syāt । nacaitatsambhavati lakṣaṇāyā api lokavyavahāre pratipattihetutvena darśanāt
śālayo bhujyanta itivat bhavati loke pratipattihetuḥ । atra tu na sambhavatītyatrāha
-<q>na ca sambhavantyāṃ lakṣaṇāyāṃ viniyogo'dṛṣṭakalpanāṃ sahate</q> । tasmāllakṣaṇayā
samavetārtha evāyaṃ mantra iti yuktā kalpanā ।</p>
<p><q>nanu ca prayogābhāvānna padavyāpāravattayā lakṣaṇā śakyate kalpayituṃ
viniyogena mantrasya tātparyāvagamo na padasya । tena dhānyapadaṃ lakṣaṇāvyāpāreṇa
taṇḍulāvagamakamiti na śakyate'vagantum । padavyāpāraścātra cintyate । kasmāditya-
trāha-<q>padavyāpārāśritaścohaḥ satyapi vākyaprayojanatve samavetaprakāśanasya</q> ।
yadi hi dhānyapadasyopyamānapratipādanaṃ vyāpāra ityavagataṃ bhavati tadā vikṛtau
māṃsasyopyamānasya dhānyaśabdenāvagamayitumaśakyatvāt māṃsaśabda ūhyate nānyathā ।
yata eva mantratātparyamātreṇa padavyāpārātmikā lakṣaṇā na siddha‍yati <q>ata eva keci
llakṣaṇaivātra vivakṣiteti manvānāḥ mṛgo'sītyūhaṃ manvate</q> । asyārthaḥ-yāvallakṣaṇā-
paryanto viniyogo na varṇyate tāvat padāśritā lakṣaṇā na siddha‍yati । tena
lākṣaṇikatvaṃ padasyecchatā evaṃ vaktavyam - lakṣaṇayopyamānaṃ vaktavyamiti viniyogārtha
iti । tataśca vikṛtāvapi mṛgo'sītyūhena bhavitavyaṃ na māṃsamasīti । atha tu lakṣaṇā
na vivakṣitā tadā mantratātparyāvagamāt dhinotīti dhānyamiti yaugikadhānyaśabdā-
śrayaṇena taṇḍulapratipādakatvopapatteḥ māṃsepi yogasya sambhavāt ūho na syāt ।
tadāha---</p>
<p><q>anūhaṃ vā manyate । kutaḥ ? arthavādadarśanāt</q> । dhinuhi devāniti
mantrārthavādadarśanāt । bhavatvarthavādaḥ tathāpi kathamanūha ityāha---<q>dhānyaśabda-
prayogasiddhistaṇḍuleṣvarthavādādeva</q> । arthadhādagatadevatādhinvanayogāt dhānyamiti
taṇḍulā ucyante tathā māṃsamapi tena prakṛtivikṛtyoryaugikatvādanūhaḥ ।</p>
<p>atrocyate---<q>mantraprayojanaṃ samavetaprakāśanamityuktaṃ prathame'dhyāye ।
atastadeva tāvatprayojanam</q> । yatpunarapadavyāpārādūho nopapadyata iti tadayuktam
kuta ityāha---<q>lakṣaṇāpi tadāśritaiva gaṅgāghoṣādiṣu darśanāt</q> । asyārthaḥ-
mantrasya samavetaprakāśanaṃ kāryamiti prayojane'vagate kathaṃ tatsiddha‍yatītyapekṣāyāṃ
pratipadaṃ śaktivimarśo bhavati । tatra tāvat dhānyapapadavyatirekiṇāṃ padānāṃ vā[na]
﻿<pb n="240"/>
prakāśanasāmarthyamasti dhānyaśabdasya tu lokaprasiddhalakṣaṇāvṛttyāśrayaṇena upyamāna-
taṇḍulaprakāśanadvāreṇāvāpapratipādakatā sambhavatīti tadāśritā lakṣaṇā''śrīyate ।</p>
<p>yasmānmantratātparyānusāreṇeyaṃ lakṣaṇā na punaḥ lakṣaṇaiva vivakṣitā tasmānnātra
lakṣaṇā vikṛtau, ātmāyattatvātprayogaptya ārṣeṇa dhānyaśabdena lakṣaṇayāpi māṃsasyābhi-
dhātumaśakteḥ tadyuktaṃ tāvat padāntaraṃ prakṣeptavyam । tatra mukhye sambhavati ko nāma
lākṣaṇikaṃ prakṣipet tadāhuḥ---</p>
<p><quote>‘ṛjumārgeṇa siddha‍yantaṃ ko'rthaṃ vakreṇa sādhayet’</quote> iti । ārṣe tu prayoge
kiṃ kriyatām ? । tathaiva prayoge yasyāmapi vikṛtau dhānyaśabdo lakṣaṇayāṃ varṇayituṃ
śakyate tasyāmapyanūha eva prakṛtāviva ārṣeṇaivābhidhānasiddheḥ । nāpyayaṃ yaugiko
dhānyaśabdaḥ śakyate rūḍhereva prayojanasiddheḥ rūḍhyā hi yaugikatve parihṛte tadāśritā
lakṣaṇaiva śreyasī na yaugikatvam । yatra tu lakṣaṇayāpi prayojana[ā]siddhiḥ tatra
bhavatyeva yaugikāśrayaṇam kāryapradhānatvānmantrārthasya yato'yaṃ dhānyaśabdo na yaugikaḥ
tasmāt stutimātramarthavādaḥ, na tu śabdapravṛttaye yogopasthāpakaḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu ca dhānyaśabdasya taṇḍulapratipādanaparatayā prayoga ityanavagame kathaṃ
lakṣaṇetyatrāha---<q>na cātra prayogeṇa prayojanam</q> । kasmādityatrāha---<q>samaveta-
prakāśane hi sa iṣyate</q> । samavetamarthaṃ padaṃ prakāśayatu ityetadarthaṃ prayoga iṣyate ।
taccānyenāpi prakāreṇa siddham । mantratātparyāvagamenāpi pūrvoktarītyā siddhamityatra
prayogaḥ । <q>yadi lākṣaṇiko'pi mantreṣu śabdasyārtho gṛhyate gauṇamukhyopa-
cārastarhi mandaprayojanaḥ syāt</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>na mandaprayojanaḥ, avagatau
tulyaprayojanatvāt</q> । gauṇatvamukhyatvāvagatyavasthāyāṃ tulyaṃ prayojanam । nimitte
viśeṣa ityuktaṃ tṛtīye । nimittāvasthāṃyāṃ viśeṣo mukhyasya nirapekṣaṃ nimittaṃ gauṇasya
1mukhyāvagatisāpekṣaṃ sādṛśyamiti gauṇamukhyayorviśeṣaḥ । imameva viśeṣaṃ darśayituṃ
gauṇamukhyavicāraḥ । anena viśeṣeṇa liṅgaviniyojye viśeṣo na punargauṇamukhyavicāre-
ṇaitaduktam mukhya evāvagatirheturnānya iti । tasmāllakṣaṇayāpi samavetārthatvaṃ mantrāṇā-
miti siddham ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 13 ।। codite tu parārthatvāt vidhivadavikāraḥsyāt ।। 40 ।।</l></lg>
<note>1. R mukhyā evā</note>
﻿<pb n="241"/>
<p><q>kathaṃ punariḍopahūteti iḍāmupahvayasveti śrutyā viniyuktasya mantrasya
kāryāntaraṃ yajñapativṛddhiprakāśanamāśaṅkyate</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>viniyoga evātra
cintyate । kiṃ yajñapatiṃ vardhānitīḍopāhvāne viniyuktaṃ neti</q> । asyārthaḥ---
pratīkenāyaṃ śrauto viniyogaḥ । tatra kiṃ yajñapatiṃ vardhānityapi iḍopāhvāne viniyoge
sati cintā ।</p>
<p>tatra pūrvapakṣī liṅgaprakaraṇābhyāṃ viniyogāntaraṃ manyate । yajñapatitvena yajamā-
nasya vṛddhiviṣayatvena yajñapatiṃ vardhāniti tāvat prakaraṇapāṭhāt prakaraṇino'ṅgam ।
śaknoti cedaṃ yajñapatiṃ vṛddhiviśiṣṭaṃ vak‍tum । asti ca tādṛśo yajñe । tatprakāśanaṃ
ca kratorupakārakaṃ protsāhajananāt । tena tatraivāsya viniyogo bhavati । <q>kathaṃ
punarupakramopasaṃhārayorantarnipatitaṃ vākyāntaraṃ kalpayituṃ śakyate paraspara-
sākāṅkṣatvena padānāmekavākyatvāvagamāt</q> ।</p>
<p>uttaraṃ---<q>viniyogavaśānmantrāṇāṃ yajuṣi kalpanā । vākyatvena nānya-
padākāṅkṣayā syonaṃ te sadanaṃ ithi pradarśitam</q>---asyārthāḥ---yajuṣi yā
mantrāṇāṃ vākyatvena kalpane yadekaṃ vākyamiti sā viniyogavaśāt yāvatāmekatra
viniyogaḥ padānāṃ tāvatāmekārthatvaṃ ekārthatve caikavākyatvaṃ na punaranyapadāpekṣayā
vākyatvakalpanā । yāvanti parasparāpekṣaṇīyapadāni tāvantyekaṃ vākyamiti vākyamiti saiṣā
kalpanā । yathā syonaṃ te ityatra satyapi sākāṅkṣatve viniyogabhedādbhinnavākyatvaṃ
tathehāpi viniyogavaśāt mantravākyabhedaḥ tasmādvibhāgaḥ vibhāgāt kāryabhedaḥ kārya-
bhedāccohabhedaḥ yajamānadvitve bahutve coho'nyathā cānūho yajñapatiśabde pariśiṣṭabhāge
iḍābhede nohabhedaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ prāpte abhidhīyate---spādetadevaṃ yadi viniyogāntaraṃ yajamāna-
vṛddhiviṣayaṃ syāt । iha tu kalpyam । na ca kalpyo'rthaḥ siddhasyārthasyā-
vivakṣāyāṃ heturbhavati</q> । asyārthaḥ---upakramopasaṃhārābhyāṃ iha tāvat yajñapatiṃ
vardhānityasya padanibandhanaikavākyatā'vagamyate iḍopahvāne ca śrutyā upakramopa-
saṃhārau viniyuktau । tadekavākyatayā tasyāpi tatraiva viniyogaḥ pratīyate ।
yajñapativṛddhau tu liṅgena viniyogaḥ kalpyaḥ । na ca klṛptaḥ kalpyena bādhituṃ
śakyate । tasmānmantrata eva mantramevālocya yadekavākyatvamavagamyate tadeva
yajuṣa ekavākyatve hetuḥ । yatsyonaṃ ta ityuktaṃ tatra prakaraṇena viniyoge sati
﻿<pb n="242"/>
liṅgenaiva yajuṣo vibhāgo bhedena sambandhaḥ । sadanakaraṇe pratiṣṭhāpane ca liṅgena
viniyogaḥ । ato yuktametat padākāṅkṣānirapekṣaṃ yajuṣo dvitvaṃ parikalpyate । iha
punaḥ liṅgaṃ prakaraṇaṃ ca śrauta eva viniyoga upapadyata iti siddhaṃ pārārthyaṃ iḍopāhvāna-
paratvaṃ ca । tataścānūhaḥ । kenāpi yajamānenopalakṣaṇasiddheḥ vidhivat । yajamāna-
sammitaudumbarītyekenāpi sammāne kṛtārthamiti pradarśitaṃ bhāṣye ।।</p>
<lg><l>।। 14 ।। vikārastatpradhāne syāt ।। 41 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nanu sūktavākādhikaraṇe phalamidaṃ āyurāśāsanaṃ āśāsyamānamāyuḥ
phalamityuktam । tenātra phalabhāgitayā na parārtho yajamāna iti kathamatra
pūrvapakṣaḥkriyate</q> ।</p>
<p>samādhatte---<q>satyaṃ phalamidaṃ, natu yajamānena sambadhyamānasyāsya
kaścidviśeṣo vidyate</q> । phalamapyetadyajamānena sambadhyamānaṃ na guṇatayā sambadhyate
tena ta yajñapatimityanena na kaścidviśeṣaḥ yasmāt nāvaśyaṃ phalavattvāya yajamānenā-
yurāśāsanaṃ viśeṣaṇīyaṃ kartṛtayaiva phalamabhisambadhyate tathāpi mantrārthopapatteḥ । na ca
phalavatā phalaṃ prati pradhānabhūtenāyurāśāsanaṃ viśeṣaṇīyaṃ kevalaṃ kartṛtayaivāśāsanānvaye'pi
mantrāvākyasyārthopapatteḥ । <q>ato yajamānasammitaudumbarīvaditi nānyo yajamāno
nāpi phalavattayetyasamavetaṃ manyate</q> । yathā yajamānasammitaudumbarī bhavatītyatra
anyo yajamāno na gṛhyate । na ca phalitayaiva samyadhyate, kintu kartṛtayaiva tathehāpi ।
<q>tena samavetasyāpi yajamānasya parārthatvenābhidhānānna samavetārthatvaṃ
mantrasya</q> । tataścānūho yajñapatiśabdavat ।</p>
<p><q>atrocyate---avaśyamatra 1phalitaivāśāsanaheturiti mantavyam</q> ।
asyārthaḥ---pha़labhāgitaivāśāsanahetuḥ tena yadyapi āśāsane kartṛtvaṃ tathāpi phala-
bhāgitayā prādhānyādapārārthyamityūhārham । <q>kutaḥ phalabhāgitaiva āśāsanahetuḥ ?</q>
uttaraṃ---<q>yatra hi anyataḥ phalāvagamaḥ tatra kartṛtayāpi mantrārtha upapadyata
ityuktam । iha tu mantrādeva phalakalpanā । sa cet phalavattayā na sambadhyate</q>
mantraścet phalavattāṃ na bodhayati tato mantrāt phalakalpanaiva vihanyeta । tadvidhāte ca
<note>1. phalatayaiva</note>
﻿<pb n="243"/>
haratau mantrasyāṅgatvaṃ nopapadyata ityuktaṃ tṛtīye । mantro hi phalaprakāśanena karmaṇyaṅgatāṃ
yāti । aphalatve tu kiṃ bodhayan aṅgatāmiyāt । tasmādaparārthatvādyajamānasya sama-
vetasya prakāśanaṃ tataścohasiddhiḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 15 ।। asaṃyogāttadartheṣu tadviśiṣṭaṃ pratiyeta ।। 42 ।।</l></lg>
<p>agneyī subrahmaṇyetyatra cintyate---kiṃ harivadādayo'pyatrohitavyā neti ।
tadarthamidaṃ cintyate---samavetārthā harivadādayaśśabdāḥ utāsamavetārthāḥ ।</p>
<p><q>kathaṃ punaḥ samavetārthāḥ kathamasamavetārthāḥ?</q> uttaraṃ---<q>yadīndrasya dravyasya
svarūpaṃ prakāśayanti tadā samavetārthāḥ</q> । yadi darbhaistṛṇīta haritairitivat guṇābhi-
dhānadvāreṇendra eva prakāśyate tataḥ samavetendraprakāśakatvāt samavetārthatvam । <q>atha
stutiṃ kurvanti tato na samavetārthāḥ</q> yadi harivattādikaṃ indraṃ stotumucyate tadā-
'samavetārthāḥ ।</p>
<p><q>tatra rāddhāntavādī stutimeva nyāyyāṃ manyate stutyaiva nigadārthopa-
patteḥ</q> । itarathā hi guṇaparatvena lakṣaṇā syāt । rāddhāntopakramo vyākhyātaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>pūrvapakṣyāśaṅkā punaḥ arthavādāt tatsvarūpāvagatyartho nigada iti
buddhirutpadyate</q> । indrasvarūpapratipattyartho'yaṃ nigadaḥ । kathaṃ punaḥ harivattādayaḥ indra-
mupalakṣayituṃ kṣamāḥ na hi teṣāmindrasambandho'vagataḥ yathā haritasya darbhasambandha iti ।</p>
<p><q>atrocyate-arthavādāt guṇasambandhāvagamāt bhavatīndrasvarūpāvagatiḥ</q> ।
kaḥ punarasāvarthavāda ityāha---<q>pūrvāparapakṣāviti darśitam</q> ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu arthavādo'pi tāvat stutyaivopapadyate svarūpaparatve'rtha-
vādataiva hīyeta</q> । yo'yamarthavādaḥ indrasambandhiharivattādipratipādanaparaḥ so'pi tāvat
stutyaivānvaye sati arthavādo bhavati । yadi pratīyamānārthasvarūpaparo bhavati tadā artha-
vādataiva hīyate । yasmāt stutyarthena vidhīnāmityarthavādatvamuktam । yadi cedaṃ vastu
yathāpratīyamānamevāśrīyate tadā ādimattā syāt kāṇvāyanādyarthapratipādakatvāt
ādimattāprasaṅgaśca vedasya syāt । tasmādayamartho yathāśruto na grāhyaḥ ।</p>
<p>evaṃ tāvadindrasyaivaṃrūpatā nāstītyuktamabhyupagamyāha---<q>tasmādyadyapīndraḥ evaṃ-
svarūpaḥ tathāpi harivattādayaḥ stutyarthā evamu[yu]ktāḥ । śrutistābhyāṃ</q>
﻿<pb n="244"/>
<q>hīdaṃ haratīti copapadyate</q> । indrasya harivattāṃ prati tābhyāṃ hīdaṃ sarvaṃ haratītyupa-
pattiryuktirucyate । tena harivattaiva yuktyā pratipādyata iti jñāyate । evaṃ cābhyupa-
gamyavādamātraṃ mūlayuktimāha । yatra punaḥ svarūpepi pramāṇābhāvaḥ tatra kimanyadataḥ
stuteḥ । yathā ca svarūpapratipattaye nālamarthavādaḥ tathā vyākhyātaṃ bhāṣye । tasmāt
harivadādīnāṃ noho'samavetārthābhidhānāt ।</p>
<p>atra bhāṣyakāreṇānūhaṃ darśiyitvā uktaṃ---<quote>‘‘tattvetanna rocayante yājñikāḥ’’</quote>
iti । tadākṣipati---<q>na rocayante iti kathane kiṃ prayojanaṃ siddhāntānupa-
yogāt । yājñikānuṣṭhānavirodhena ca pratyuta kṣatihetutvāt</q> ।</p>
<p>samādhatte---<q>evaṃ bacanārtheṣu vyāmoha upapadyate</q> । ato vipratipattau
jijñāseyamityarucipradarśanena yājñikānāṃ vacanārtheṣu vyāmoho'stītyucyate । ato
vipratipattau jijñāseyaṃ kriyata iti ।</p>
<p>nigadāntaravidhāne tu na doṣaḥ । athavā yajñikānāmarucipradarśanena nigadā-
ntarameva āgneyī subrahmaṇyetyatrāstīti pradarśayati । tena na kaściddoṣo nyāyasya ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 16 ।। asaṃyogāttadartheṣu tadviśiṣṭaṃ pratīyeta ।। 42 ।।</l></lg>
<p>athedamanyadudāhriyate---<q>nanvatra samavetatvepi guṇānāṃ mantrasya
stutyarthataiva nyāyyā śruteḥ । na ca stutyarthatve'dṛṣṭārthatvaṃ, prarocanayā
dṛṣṭārthatvopapatteḥ</q> । somavikrayiṇo hyekahāyanīstutau prarocanā jāyata eveti
dṛṣṭārthatvam । svarūpe punarabhidheye'ṅgīkriyamāṇe ekahāyanīmātrasya codatatvāt aco-
ditasvarūpābhidhāne'dṛṣṭaṃ kalpanīyam । tasmāt pūrvapakṣa eva nopapadyate । pūrveṇaivādhi-
karaṇena gatārthatvāt ।</p>
<p><q>atrocyate - ayamabhiprāyaḥ pūrvapakṣavādinaḥ sambhavati</q> । ekāhāyanī-
svarūpāpanhavaḥ śakyate kalpayitum । nanu adṛṣṭārthamekahāyanīsvarūpaparatvamityatrāha-
<q>yathāpratipannasya ca prayojanakalpanā</q> । yathābhūtaṃ vastu pratīyate ya[ta]thābhūtasya
prayojanaṃ kalpyaṃ na punaḥ prayojanavaśāt arthapratipattiḥ । tena yadi dṛṣṭaṃ nāsti
bhavatvadṛṣṭaṃ, kintvatra dṛṣṭamapyastītyāha---<q>bhavati ca svarūpādapi prarocanetyadṛṣṭa-
kalpanāpi parihṛtaiva sutarāṃ svarūpāvagameva vikreturbhavati prarocaneti</q> ।</p>
﻿<pb n="245"/>
<p>atra codayati---<q>stutāvapi prarocanā । svarūpāvagame punaḥ gauravādaraḥ
kiṃkṛtaḥ?</q> । pariharati---<q>ananyavyāpāratākṛtaḥ</q> । na hi svarūpaparatve sambhavati
parārthakalpanā ātmānaṃ labhate । svarūpāvagamapakṣe hi tasyai śṛtamityādipadānāṃ
svarūpaparatvam । stutau parārthastutiparatvam । na caitanna‍yāyyam । svārthaparatvasambhavāt ।
tasmātpūrveṇa vaiṣamyam pramāṇānavagamādindrasvarūpasya । iha tu pramāṇāntareṇa svarūpā-
vagamāt guṇipratipattyarthaṃ hi guṇavacanaṃ ityūha eva nyāyyaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu-nigadaprayogakāle ekahāyanīdaśāyāṃ nedaṃ svarūpameka-
hāyanyāḥ</q> । tena stutyarthamevāsadapyāropaṇam । <q>bhāvinīṃ pravṛttimaṅgīkṛtyocyata
iti cet</q> । dṣayati---<q>na prayogāṅgatvena svarūpapratipattirutpāditā</q> syāt
bhāvitvāvasthāyāḥ prayoganaṅgatvāt । aprayogāṅgatvepi svarūpapratipattiḥ stutaye
bhaviṣyatīti cet । dūṣayati---<q>stutyarthatvaṃ pratipannaṃ,</q> tarhi nigadasya siddhamasama-
vetābhidhānam ।</p>
<p>nanu sāṇḍasya nirālambanā stutiriti nopapadyate ityāha-<q>upapadyate ca
sāṇḍasyāpi stutiḥ garbhādhānamukhena śṛtādyutpattilakṣaṇaguṇayogaḥ</q> iha stuti-
rupapanneti hetoravikāro'nūha ityarthaḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 17 ।। liṅgaviśeṣanirdeśātsamānavidhāneṣvaprāptā sarasvatī
s‍trītvāt ।। 45 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nanu cātra prātipadikārthasyaiva pradhānatvāt naiva liṅgavacanānurodhena
saṅkoca upapadyate samānavidhānepi pāśasyeva</q> । yathā pāśasya prādhānyānnotkarṣo
mantrasya । tasmāt pūrvapakṣa evātra jyāyāniti ।</p>
<p><q>atrocyate - syādetadevaṃ yadi liṅgādvacanācca niṣkṛṣṭāntaraṃ sarvanāma-
śabdenābhidhīyate</q> । asyārthaḥ - sannihitavacanatvāt sarvanāmnāṃ yādṛśaṃ sannihitaṃ
tādṛśamevābhidhīyate । liṅgavacanayuktaṃ ca sannihitamiti tathābhūtameva prātipadike-
nāpyabhidhīyate iti viśiṣṭaviṣayatvāt prātipadikasyaiva viśiṣṭe viniyogaḥ । pāśe
punaryuktaṃ pāśamātrābhidhānāt ।</p>
<p><q>nanvatrāpi sarvanāmnā vacanaviniyuktena vibhaktirahitena sannihitamātraṃ
saṅkhyāliṅgaviyuktamucyate yadvastuvṛttena saṅkhyāvalliṅgavacca</q> । etaduktaṃ bhavati-
﻿<pb n="246"/>
yadyapi sannihitasya vastunaḥ saṅkhyāliṅge staḥ tathāpi sarvānāmamātreṇa vibhaktirahitena
paśutvamevocyate vibhaktyā tu saṅkhyāliṅgayorabhidhānam । tena prātipādikena meṣyā
api sannihitatvādabhidhānaṃ śakyate kartum । prātipadikaṃ ca liṅgādvalīyaḥ । tasmāt
prātipadikārtha evānena mantreṇābhidhīyata iti liṅgavacanānurodhena saṅkoco yuktaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate - satyamevaṃ saṅkhyāvalliṅgavacca yattadevābhidhīyate
sarvannāmnā</q> । nanu saṅkhyāliṅgavibhaktibhiśca saṅkhyā'bhidhīyate ṭābādibhiśca strītvaṃ
tathāpi tvatra[kiṃ]liṅgavaditi cintāyāṃ sannidhānādva‍yaktireva pratīyate na punaḥ paśutvam ।
<q>vyaktiścet sarvanāmnā pratīyate na liṅgavacanaviyuktā śakyate pratipattuṃ,
tasyāstadyuktatvāt pāśavat paśutvavacca</q> । yathā pāśatvaṃ pāśaprātipadikena
saṅkhyāliṅgarahitaṃ vaktuṃ śakyate evaṃ paśutvavacca, yathā paśutvaṃ paśuprātipadikena
vyaktimātraṃ liṅgasaṅkhyāviyuktaṃ sākṣācchabdena sannidhāpitaṃ prāsmai paśave agniṃ bharata
ityevaṃvidhe vākye pratyetuṃ śakyate tathā vyaktirna śakyate ।</p>
<p><q>nanu vyaktimātraṃ saṅkhyāliṅgayorāśrayabhūtaṃ pratīyatāṃ tasyāpi sanni-
hitatvāt</q> । pariharati - <q>keyaṃ vyaktimātratā nāma yā sarvanām‍nocyate</q> ।
uttaraṃ---<q>sannidhānāviśeṣāt sannihitavyak‍timātraṃ pratīyatāmiti</q> । yā vyakti-
rliṅgasaṅkhyānvitā tasyāḥ svarūpamapi sannihitaṃ, tena svarūpasyāpi sannidhānāviśeṣāt
bhavatyeva sarvanāmnā'bhidhānamiti rāddhāntī vadati । <q>sannihitaṃ cetsāmānyaṃ na tat
sarvanāmaprātipadikābhidheyam sannihitavacanatvāt sarvānāmnām</q> sannihitamātraṃ
yadi sāmānya tadā sarvanāmnā na śakyate vaktuṃ samānyasya vāstavasannidhānā-
bhāvāt । vyaktireva hi vāstavena sannidhānena sannihitā bhavati । sāmānyaṃ tu
śabdena sannidhāpyate । yadītyasaṃśayepi saṃśayavacanam । tasmāt vibhāgaśaḥ prāti-
padikenāśrayamātraṃ vibhaktyā saṅkhyā liṅgamiti vibhaktyartho na śakyate'navagantuṃ
ṛte paśuśabdasāmānādhikaraṇyāt । tacca nāsti । ataḥ sakalaprātipadikārthāvagateḥ
savibhaktikaprātipadikārthāvagatireva sannidhānopādhinānveti । vākye saliṅgasaṅkhyā
vyaktiḥ sannidhānopādhinā idaṃśabdenābhidhīyamanā asya vākyasyārthaḥ । ato na
strīliṅgayuktaṃ dravyamātraṃ vākyārthe'nvitatayā śakyate pratipattumityanimittamapadārthaḥ
sārasvatī । animittatve cāpadārthatve ca tādarthyaṃ mantrasya । tasmādyuktameva strītvāt
sārasvatī adhriguvacanamaprāpteti । tārtīyapaśvadhikaraṇapūrvapakṣaprayojanavicāro'yamityuktaṃ
bhāṣye । tena prayojanaṃ na vaktavyam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="247"/>
<lg><l>।। 18 ।। āmnātādanyadadhikāre vacanādvikāraḥ
syāt ।। 50 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>keyaṃ vādhacintā aprāpticintā vā ?</q> । anenāsaṅgatimāśaṅkate । yadi
irāpadena girāpadaṃ prāptameva bādhyate iti tadā dāśamikī cintā । atherāpada-
viniyoge sati girāpadasya prāptireva nāstīti cintyate tadā prāpticinteyaṃ tṛtīye
saṅgatā viniyogābhāvarūpatvāt । ubhayaṃ caitannopapadyate ūhalakṣaṇe । samādhatte---
<q>satyamevaṃ bādhaprāpticintehalakṣaṇe na saṅgateti kāryārthatve tacchāstraṃ na
prāpta‍yarthaṃ itīhaiva cintopapadyate</q> । asyārthaḥ - girāpadakārye guṇavacana irāpadamanena
śāstreṇa vidhīyate airaṃ kṛtvodgeyamiti । na punaḥ sāmni irāpadaprāpta‍yartham । tataśca
yajñāyajñīye sānni stutirūpaṃ kāryaṃ kartuṃ pravṛtte girāpadena vinā kartumaśakteḥ girāpade
ākṣipyamāṇe eva tatkārye irāpadaniyamāt tadevopādīyate । tena kāryavaśene-
rāpadayuktasāmaprayogo vikṛta ityūhalakṣaṇa evāyaṃ cintopapadyate । stutilakṣaṇakāryā-
deva hi girāpadaṃ prāpnoti nopadeśāt na girāpadaṃ sāmnyupadiṣṭaṃ tenerāpadamapi nopadi-
śyate । kintu tadapi kāryādevohyate ।</p>
<p><q>nanu sāmopadeśādṛgapi upadiṣṭaivetyupadeśādeva prāptiḥ</q> । sāmnaḥ
stutāvupadeśāt ṛcā vinā tadaśakteḥ sāmāpyupadiṣṭaiva[ṣṭameva] । pariharati---
<q>narca upadeśassambhavati prādhānyādakṣarāṇām । nahi pradhānaṃ guṇaṃ pratyu-
padiśyate</q> ।</p>
<p>kathaṃ punaḥ stutinirvṛttirityāha---<q>māṇavakavadetadbhaviṣyatīti vakṣyāmaḥ</q> ।
yathā ācāryakaraṇavidhinā upanayamaṅgabhūtaṃ prayuñjānena māṇavakaḥ prayujyate tathā ṛgapi
stutyā svasādhanaṃ sāma guṇakarmabhūtamākṣipatyeveti vakṣyāmaḥ । tasmāt kāryata eva
prāptiḥ ṛcaḥ padānāṃ cetīhaiva cintanīyam ।</p>
<p><q>nanu kāryato'pi prāptau bādha evāyaṃ aprāptirvā</q>, pariharati-<q>aprāptirhi
upadeśaviṣayā । prāptiviṣayaśca bādha iti nobhayamapyasti</q> । viniyogo hi
upadeśaviṣayastṛtīye cintitaḥ । aprāptasya ca bādho daśame । iha tūpadeśo nāsti
nāpi prāptirastīti । kasmādupadeśo nāstītyāha---<q>na cākṣarāṇi stutāvupadi-
śyanta ityuktam</q> ।</p>
﻿<pb n="248"/>
<p>nanvirāpadopadeśe kathaṃ girāpadasya prāptiriti pūrvapakṣa ityatrāha---<q>atra pūrva-
pakṣo1 na kāryaṃ sāma[mnaḥ]stuteḥ pṛthagbhūtaṃ [i]ṣṭamastīti</q> । irāpadaṃ hi kāryaṃ-
[rye]vidheyaṃ, kāryaṃ ca stuteranyadiha nāsti tatra sāmavidhānānnaiva padopadeśāvakāśo-
'sti । tenerāpadasya girāpadasya copadeśābhāvāt tulyatvaṃ tulyatve ca vikalpaḥ ।</p>
<p>kasmāt punastutāvavidhānamityāha---<q>sāmasādhyaṃ hi kāryamucyate । taccā-
sāmaviruddham</q> । tathāpi kathaṃ vikalpa ityāha---<q>na girāpadasyāpi tadapahartuṃ
śakyata iti vikalpaḥ</q> ।</p>
<p><q>atrocyate---satyamevaṃ sāmnaiva stutiḥ kāryā । tathāpi girāpadaṃ naivātra
bhavitumarhati niyatatvādirāpadasya । kva punarayaṃ niyamaḥ ? stutyabhidhāna
iti brūmaḥ</q> । stutirūpe guṇābhidhāne ayaṃ niyamaḥ irāpadenaiva guṇābhidhānaṃ kuryāditi ।
<q>nanvetadacoditaṃ stutāvityuktam</q> । asyārthaḥ---yadyakṣaraiḥ guṇābhidhānaṃ kāryamiti
codiṃta syāt tadā tatrākṣaraviśeṣaniyama ucyate । nacaitadasti sāmasādhyatvāt stute-
rityuktam ।</p>
<p>pariharati---<q>satyamacoditaṃ niyogānupraveśādādaraṇīyamirāpadavidhau</q> ।
asyārthaḥ---yadyapi sāmnaḥstutāvupadeśaḥ tathāpyārthamakṣarāṇāṃ sādhanatvaṃ na śakyate'pahnotum ।
tacca niyamavidhāvādriyate, tasyāpi niyogānupraveśāt । ato'rthaprāptasādhanabhāvā-
śrayaṇena niyamo'yaṃ kriyate vratavat । yathā payovrataṃ brāhmaṇasyeti arthaprāptaśarīradhāraṇā-
śrayaṇena payoniyamastathehāpi । ato na vikalpaḥ । irāpadasyāṅgatvāt tasyaivopādānaṃ
tena vinā stutiviniyogāsiddheḥ ।</p>
<p><q>yatyuna</q>ridaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa kva tarhi sāmānyopadiṣṭaṃ bhaviṣyatīti coditaṃ, tathā
sāptadaśyavadvikṛtiṣu girāpadasyāṅgatvāt tasyaivopādānaṃ tena vikṛtau nivekṣyata iti
parihṛtam । <q>tadayuktamiva pratibhāti</q> । kasmādayuktaṃ ? <q>upadeśādvikṛtāviti ca</q> ।
yasmātsāmānyopadiṣṭavidhāna upadeśa āśritaḥ sa ca nāstīt‍tuktam tathā vikṛtāviti
yaduktaṃ tadapyayuktam । kathamayuktatetyāha---(nyāhṛta) <q>tatparisāmādiṣu nopapadyate</q>
parisāmādīnāṃ vikṛtitvābhāvāt vikṛtau niveśau bhaviṣyatītyetattāvat parisāmādyabhi-
prāyaṃ nopapadyate teṣāṃ vikṛtitvābhāvāt । kratvantare punaḥsomavikāre kāryataḥ
<note>1. mā. nākāryaṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="249"/>
karaṇopakārataḥstuteḥ prāptatvāt tatraiva irāpadaniyamādirāpadameva । tena nāsti girāpa-
dānupraveśaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>atrocyate---sāmāvāntarakāryamaṅgīkṛtyaitaduktam</q> । sāmno hi stutiḥ
paramakāryaṃ, avāntarakāryaṃ tu parisāmādikāryamabhipretya vikṛtāvarthavadityuktaṃ bhavati ।
bhavati ca stuteḥ parisāmādikāryaṃ kratvantarbhūtaṃ tenātra vihitamirāpadaṃ parisāmakārye
na prāpnoti atastatrārthavattā bhaviṣyatīti sūktam ।</p>
<p><q>kathamupadeśaḥ samarthanīya</q> iti codyānubhāṣaṇam । sāmata eva sāmopadeśena
ya ākṣepaḥ sa upadeśo'bhimataḥ । nanvevamapi parisāmādiṣu vikṛtiśabdaḥ kathamitya-
trāha-<q>vikṛtiśabdaścānyatvābhiprāyaḥ</q> । anyatrārthavattā bhaviṣyatītyabhiprāyaḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 17 ।। apragāṇāncabdānyatve tathābhūtopadeśaḥ syāt ।। 54 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>kathaṃ punaratra saṃśayaḥ ? yāvatā apragītasya stutisādhanatvānupapatteḥ
pragāṇenaiva bhavitavyam</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>taddhitanirdeśādeva</q> । evadeva vivṛṇeti---
<q>pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ avikṛtādirāpadādayaṃ taddhitaḥ matau chaḥ</q> sūktasāmnoḥ
ityasminnadhikāre vimuktādibhyo'ṇ iti matvarthe sāmaviṣaye'ṇ‌pratyayo'yam । sa
cāvikṛtādirāpadāt । tasmādavikṛtamevedamirāpadam । yadi hi vikṛtaṃ prayujyate tadā
vikārānurūpastaddhitaḥ syāt । vikāre sati ā irā itiśabdarūpaṃ, tattu vimuktādiṣu
na paṭhitamiti matau cha iti cha eva syāt । na cāsāvasti । tasmādavikṛtamirāpadaṃ
prayoktavyamiti ।</p>
<p><q>kaḥpunaratra taddhitārthaḥ</q> । pṛcchataścāyamāśaḥ-vikārārtha evāyaṃ taddhitaḥ ।
gānarūpaśca vikāraḥ prāpta evānūdyata iti । uttaraṃ---<q>irāpadayuktaṃ gānaṃ kartavyaṃ
matvarthe'yama(ya)ṇ‌pratyaya ityarthaḥ । tasya pratipadoktatvāt lakṣaṇapratipadoktayoḥ
pratipadoktasyaiva grahaṇāt ।</p>
<p><q>nanu cāpragītatvādyoga eva gānayoga eva na sambhavati</q> । pariharati-
sambhavati tadyogaḥ, tatkāryakaraṇatvāditi</q> । ayamabhiprāyaḥ-sāmakāryakaraṇatvā-
ttasya bhavati sāmnastatsambandhitvaṃ tasmādapragītopadeśo'yaṃ taddhitāntopadeśena jñātaḥ ।
<q>rāddhāntavādino'pi taddhitanirdeśādeva svarūpamātropadeśānavagatiḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ-
﻿<pb n="250"/>
nāyaṃ vimuk‍tāditvāttaddhitaḥ । kintu tasya vikāra iti । yathā caivaṃ tathā'tra vakṣyāmaḥ ।
vikārataddhite'smin svarūpamātropadeśo nāvagamyate । gānapratyākhyānena svarūpamātro-
padeśo nāvagamyate । <q>ko'bhiprāya</q> iti pṛcchato'yamabhiprāyaḥ---bhavatu vikārataddhitaḥ
tathāpi apragāṇarūpo vikāro vidhāyiṣyata iti ।</p>
<p>uttaraṃ---<q>vikāravidhāne hi svarūpavidhānānupapattiḥ vikārasya svarūpasya
ca vidhāne vākyabhedaprasaṅgāt</q> । bhavatu tarhi vikāramātravidhānaṃ ityatrāha---
<q>na cāvihite svarūpe vikāramātravidhānamupapadyate</q> । nirāśrayasya tasyānupapatteḥ ।
na ca vācyamaupādānikaḥ svarūpavidhirbhaṃviṣyati irāpadavikāro hi asatīrāpadopadeśe
nopapadyata iti arthādirāpadākṣepa ityavaśyāśrayaṇīyaprathamopanipātisvarūpavidhinaiva
vidherupapatteḥ vikārasya gītisvarūpasya arthaprāptānuvādasambhavāt । tasmādvikārasyāyamanu-
vādaḥ । svarūpamātraṃ tu vidhīyate ।</p>
<p><q>kena punaḥ prāptasyānuvādaḥ ? kāryata eva</q> । na hyavikṛtaṃ sāmnaḥ kāryakaraṃ
bhavati । kāryaṃ hīrāpadaṃ vihitam । kathaṃ ca tatsāmakārye bhavati yadi pragītākṣara-
kāryaṃ bhavati । tasmāt kāryata eva gānaṃ prāptasanūdyate ।</p>
<p>kasmāt punaḥ avikārataddhito'yaṃ uktametat vimuk‍tāditvādayaṃ taddhita
ityatrāha---<q>vacanasaṃyogācca nārthāntare taddhita āśaṅkanīyaḥ</q> । na girāgireti
brūyāt iti prakramāt vacanamuccāraṇamavagamyate । tenerāvacanamiti vacanasambandhānna
vimuk‍tāditaddhito'yam । sām‍ni viṣaye hi sa taddhitaḥ । na cerāpadoccāraṇamātraṃ
sāma, kiṃ tarhi ? sāmāvayavaḥ । yaccoccāraṇaṃ gītātmakaṃ bhavati tacchabdavikārātma-
kamiti vikārataddhita evāyam । tasmādvikārānuvāda evāyam । yato'yaṃ
svarūpamātropadeśoṃ na gītiprakhyātaṃ ata evāvikṛtāt taddhitotpattiradoṣaḥ । pratyuta
vikṛtāttaddhitotpattireva doṣaḥ । vikṛtasya vikārābhāvāt ।</p>
<p><q>atha viśiṣṭavidhānaṃ kasmānna bhavati</q> apragāṇarūpavikāraviśiṣṭamirāpadaṃ
kasmānna vidhīyate । uttaraṃ---<q>sakṛttaddhitayorubhayoḥ sambandhāvagatiḥ</q> kriyā-
kārakayoriva kārye yasya vidhānaṃ tasya kutaścitkārye vidhānam yathā somena yajete-
tyadhikāra vidhau । tatra ca parasparānvayāvagame sati viśiṣṭavidhānaṃ yathā somena
karaṇabhūtena avacchinnāyā yāgakriyāyāḥ । iha ca stutikārye irāpadasya vidhānam ।
﻿<pb n="251"/>
na ca vikāro viśeṣaṇam । kintu vikāraṃ prati tasya viśeṣaṇatvam । tena kṛttaddhiteṣu
pratyayārthapradhāneṣu pratyayārthaviśiṣṭaprakṛtyarthavidhānaṃ nāsti viśeṣaṇaviśiṣṭabhāvānavagamāta ।</p>
<p>kiñca yugapadvidhānamapi kriyākārakavannopapadyate prakṛtiprāptisavyapekṣā hi
vikārā bhavanti । kāraṇakartṛnirdeśāśca ṇvulādayaḥ kriyāprāptisavyapekṣāḥ । prāptāyāṃ
prakṛtau tatsavyapekṣasya vikārasya viśeṣaṇatvena vidhānaṃ nāprāptāyām । tathā kriyāyāṃ
prāptāyāṃ ṇvulādayo'kriyāviśeṣaṇatvena kartrādīnyapayeyuḥ nānyathā । pratyayārthasyaiva
pradhānatvāditi nāsti viśiṣṭavidhānam । tasmāt prakṛtividhānameva nyāyyam na
viśiṣṭavidhānamiti ।</p>
<p>yat‍tu <q>prayojanaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇok‍taṃ praprapadaṃ praprīpadaṃ vā prayok‍tavyaṃ
pūrvapakṣe rāddhānte ca praprīpadameveti । tat pūrvādhikaraṇasyaiva pradarśitamiti
pratibhāti</q> । tattvayuk‍tamiheti bhāvaḥ ।</p>
<p>samarthayate---<q>yatpunarubhayorapyadhikaraṇayoḥ iti na doṣaḥ</q> । kimiti
punarirāpadaṃ parityajya anyatprayojanamuk‍taṃ tadāha---<q>kathamiti</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>tadge-
yamityupadeśena vikalpo nāpragītāśaṅkā</q> । upadiṣṭatvānna vikalpaḥ tadgeyaṃ āī
rācādākṣāsāi gānavidhānācca nāpragītāśaṅkā । praprapade punaḥ ubhayamidaṃ nirasanīyamiti
tadevādhikaraṇadvayasya prayojanam ।</p>
<p><q>iti śrīmahāmahopādhyāyaśālikanāthamiśrakṛtau
ṛjuvimalāyāṃ pañcikāyāṃ navamādhyāyasya
prathamaḥ pādaḥ</q></p>
﻿<pb n="252"/>
<p><q>।। navamādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।</q></p>
<lg><l>।। 1 ।। sāmāni mantrameke smṛtyupadeśābhyām ।। 1 ।।</l></lg>
<p>atra bhāṣyakāreṇa kiṃ gītiviśiṣṭaṃ mantravākyaṃ sāma uta gītimātrameveti
vicārya varṇakāntaramārabdham । kiṃ nityānyūhasāmāni utānityānīti । tatra varṇi-
te'pi kasmādvarṇakāntaramityatrāha---<q>atra dvitīyādhyāyacintayā sahārthāntara-
varṇanaṃ saptamādhyāyena sahāpaunaruktyakathanārtham । iha punaruttaravivakṣayaiva
parihāraḥ । atra pūrvottarapakṣāvaparihāryāveveti adhikaraṇāntaravarṇanā</q> ।
asyārthaḥ---yasmādiha navame uttaravivakṣayaiva punaruktiparihāraḥ atrāpi parihāre pūrvottara-
pakṣaracanā kartuṃ na yuktā । na ca tāva(sā)parihāryāvevetyadhikaraṇāntaravarṇanaṃ kartuṃ
śakyate, sūtrakāreṇa sākṣāt kṛtatvāt tasmādetaddoṣa1parihārāya varṇakāntaraṃ kṛtam ।</p>
<p>kasmātpunaratrottaravivakṣayaiva parihāro yāvatā dvitīyenādhyāyena sahānyathaiva
paunaruktyaṃ parihṛtam । dvitīye hi pragītepi mantravākye sāmti mantratrevidhyaṃ siddha‍yati ।
2tadarthaṃ ca gītiṣu sāmākhyetyuktam । tena naitena a(ta)tra prayojanaṃ gītimātraṃ sāmeti
tatrāha---<q>dvitīyena saha yadarthāntaravarṇanaṃ tatsaptamādhyāyacintayā saha[ā/?/]
paunaruktyārthaṃ</q>, saptamādhyāyacintayā tu yatpaunaruktyaṃ tasyottaravivakṣayaiva parihāraḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu nityānityavicāro'yamihāsaṅgata ityatrāha---<q>idaṃ cādhikaraṇamuttara-
cintārthamaupoddhātikamiti</q> । yadi nitya ūhaḥ tataḥ auk‌thikyamūhasāmasvarūpa-
nirṇayaprayojanaṃ sūtrajātaṃ jaimininā nārabdhavyam । prārabhyamāṇaṃ vā svarūpavarṇanāya yathā-
vasthitasvarūpakathanāya na kāryaupayikatayā kāryabhūtohopāyatvena na prārabdhavyam ।
atha tu kṛtaka ūhastato yathānyāyaṃ yathāvacanaṃ cohaḥ kartavya iti tatparamauk‌thi-
kyamārabdhavyam ।</p>
<note>1. R doṣabhayena</note>
<note>2. R traividhyasiddha‍yartha</note>
﻿<pb n="253"/>
<p>nanvanityatvepyavakāśo nāsti tasyāpi paṭhitatvāt ityatrāha---<q>ūhaśca tadanu-
sāreṇa nyāyānusāreṇa</q> paṭhito'pi tyaktavyo'paṭhito'pi paṭhanīya iti vyāmohasyāpi
sambhavādekāntataḥ pāṭhaparatantrairna bhavitavyamiti1bhāvaḥ ।</p>
<p>tatra svādhyāyavat chandogānāṃ nityavadupacāraṃ vyapadeśaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā cikīrṣita
ūha ityūhopadeśabhrāntyā anityatāparo'yamupadeśa iti bhrāntyā pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । cikīrṣito
hi kartumiṣṭaḥ iṣṭaśca[ā/?/]nitya eva bhavati । anityasya nyāyāpetatve'niṣṭatvasambhavāt ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntastu eke tāvadaukthikyaṃ jānanto'pi sāmohanaṃ pratyālasyāt anye-
nauktikyavidohitaṃ sāma paṭhanti । anye punaḥ aukthikyaśāstrāparijñānāccohituma-

ca(ktyā vā)grahaṇadhāraṇaviṣayā । tadidaṃ 2paṭhanaṃ svādhyāyavadupacārasya mūlam ।
nityavatpāṭhānnityabhramo'yaṃ chandogānāṃ cikīrṣita iti । pratyuta kāryatāmūhasya jñāpaya-
tyupadeśaḥ । kartumiṣṭatvābhidhānāt । yata evamanitya ūhaḥ tasmānna‍yāyāpetaṃ nohita-
vyamityāha । avakāśa3sambhavān‍nyāyaścintyate ।</p>
<p><q>।। karma vā vidhilakṣaṇam ।।</q></p>
<p>ihākṣepeṇa pravartata ityucyate bhāṣyakāreṇa । <q>kaḥ punarasāvākṣepaḥ ?</q> uttaraṃ-

prādhānyena nirdiśyate । evamatrāpīti hetau dvitīyopanyāsaḥ ।</p>
<p>yatpunaridamuktaṃ akarmakāle prayogāt <q>pradhānakarma sāmeti tadayuktamiti
manyante । kathaṃ</q>? uttaraṃ---<q>yadi prādhānyamṛco bruvate mīmāṃsakāḥ tarhi arthābhi-

<q>dhānavyāpṛtāyā eva ṛco guṇabhūtaṃ sāmeti bruvate</q> । asyārthaḥ---akarmakāle

anabhivyaktasyānabhidhāyakatvāt ।</p>
<p><q>atrocyate---aviṣayajño mātṛmān asyādhikaraṇasya । kathamaviṣa-

rakṣarābhivyaktirūpatvāt savadaivākṣarābhivyaktyarthatā avaghātādīnāmivāvahanyamānārthatā,
athavā sarvatra svapradhānataiva anīpsitakarmayuktānāmiva hiraṇyabharaṇādīnāmiti ।</p>
<p>tatra rāddhāntastāvat akṣaragrahaṇasyāpi kāryopayogitayā na śakyate'nīpsita

<q>manayā yuktyā prāp‍noti guṇabhāvaḥ sāmnaḥ</q> । kiñca karmakāle yadadhyayanaṃ tatrā-

<p><q>kalpite ca tasmin antaḥ prayoge'pi tadeva kāryamavailakṣaṇyāt ।

<p><q>nanu prādhānye'pi sāmnaḥ kimiti bahiḥ karmaṇi ca prayogaḥ</q> । uttara

<p><q>yadi pradhānaṃ sāma kathaṃ tarhi ṛgantarasambandhaḥ kavatīṣu ratha-

asyārthaḥ---yo'pi pradhānakarma sāmecchati so'pi dṛṣṭena rūpeṇa ṛk‌saṃskārakatvaṃ
sāmna icchatyeva । kintu saṃskārārthatā nāstītyucyate । tataśca ṛgantara-
sambandhepi pratyabhijñāyā abhāvaḥ yathā kṛṣṇaleṣu pākasya yasminneva dravye pratītāḥ
saṃskārāḥ tadgatā eva pratyabhijñāyante nārthāntaragatāḥ । yadyarthāntare pratyabhijñā nāsti
<q>kathaṃ tarhi śrapaṇavidhānaṃ kṛṣṇaleṣu pradhānapadārthasvarūpābhāve vidhirapi nopa-
padyata iti bhāvaḥ</q> । uttaraṃ-<q>idaṃ daśame vakṣyāmaḥ</q>, yathā vidhānaṃ taṃ saprakāraṃ daśame

﻿<pb n="256"/>
vakṣyāmaḥ । bhavati ca śrapaṇaśabdābhidheyatā kṛṣṇaleṣvapi । śrapaṇasya prākṛtasya
pāko na bhavati kāryābhāvenāpratyabhijñānāt । etaccodyaṃ pakṣadvayepi ।</p>
<p><b>atrocyate---yuktaṃ tatra pradhānārthasya anabhinirvṛttiḥ । iha punaḥ
ṛgantareṇāpi gītiḥ abhinirvartata eva</b> । asyārthaḥ---yuktaṃ 1tatra kṛṣṇaleṣu

tadidaṃ pākayajñavat3 dravyāntarepi pratyabhijñā'stītyuktam ।</p>
<p><b>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate-guṇabhūtaṃ sāma; kutaḥ ?</b> yasmādṛgakṣarāṇāmarthābhi-
dhānaṃ niyogasiddhāvanaupayikaṃ na śakyate vaktum । yadi hi arthābhidhānaṃ niyogasiddhā-
vanaupayikaṃ syāt tadā tadarthamṛgakṣarasaṃskāro na bhavet4 aupayikantu tanmātraprāmāṇyā-
bhidhānāt । uktaṃ mantrāṇāmapi prāmāṇyaṃ pramāṇalakṣaṇe । vastusvabhāvena cākṣarābhi-
vyaktiḥ saṃskāro'kṣarāṇāṃ pratīyate । idānīmākṣepahetudūṣaṇāyopakramate---<b>yā puna-
rdvitīyā sāmaviniyoge vā rathantaraṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ kuryāt ityevamādiṣu (a)praiṣe
cālaukike vaidike ca candraṃ gāyetyevamādiṣu dṛśyate । tatra yā tāvat
rathantaraṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ kuryāditi sā guṇabhūtasāmnyupapadyate । anyathā hi pṛṣṭhasambandho
na syāditi darśitaṃ bhāṣye</b> । pṛṣṭhaśabdena stutirūpaḥ kriyāviśeṣaḥ ucyate । yadi
rathantaraśabdo'pi pradhānakālakarmavacanaḥ syāt tadā pradhānakarmaṇaḥ karmāntareṇa sādha-
yitumaśakyatvādrathantarādibhiḥ sambandho na syāt । saṃskārakarmatve(hi)tu guṇābhi-
dhānasamarthākṣarasaṃskāradvāreṇa vyaktameva sādhanatvaṃ yathā'bhikramaṇasya prayājahome ।</p>
<p>yatpunaścandraṃ gāyeti tadviniyogavaśādavivakṣitamarthābhidhānaṃ praiṣe hi sāmaprayo-

avivakṣitaṃ tena yukto dvitīyānirdeśaḥ । <b>kiṇvamavahantītivadvikāraḥ</b> yathā kiṇva-

mavahantītyatra vidyamāno'pi kiṇvavikāro na vivakṣitaḥ tathehāpyarthābhidhānaṃ; nacaitāvatā

<p>yattu loke māṇake rathantaraṃ gāyetyevamādi tatra gātṛtvaparīkṣayā pradhānanirdeśaḥ
gātṛtvaṃ māṇavakasya paricikīrṣitamityadoṣaḥ । parīkṣamāṇasyaiva praiṣaḥ । tatra cārthābhidhāna-

vidhikāritameva । tasya ca svādhyāyavidheḥ puruṣārthatve satyapi nādṛṣṭārthatā, dṛṣṭo hi
tasyārthaḥ karmāvabodhanaṃ nāmeti nyāyāt । tatrākṣarāṇāmarthāvabodhārthamadhyayanaṃ gītestu
svarūpābhyāsāya । na hyanabhyastaṃ sāma karmaṇi prayoktuṃ śakyate । <q>ūhyānāṃ punarvacana-
prāpternyāyaprāpteśca saṅkaṭāvagamādanapetaśiṣyācāryasambandhasyaiva dṛṣṭārthasyaivā-
bhyāsasya naivādhikārāntaramastītyadoṣaḥ</q>-asyārthaḥ- ūhyānāṃ tu yadyapyanapetaḥ
1śiṣyācāryasambandhaḥ tathāpyabhyāso dṛṣṭārtha eva । vacananibandhanā hi yā prāptiḥ
nyāyanibandhanā ca sā saṅkaṭāvagameti । nyāyavacanavidā ūhitānāṃ sāmnāmabhyāsaḥ ।
ato na tatrāpi karmakāle punaḥ prayogepyadhikārāntarakalpanā । tena guṇakarmatvena(pi)
yukta eva bahiḥ prayogaḥ । tasmādga‍uṇabhūtaṃ sāmeti siddham ।</p>
<p>nanvevamabhyāsārthepi saṃskāre kṛte punassaṃskāro nopapadyata ityatrāha---<q>piṣṭapeṣaṇa-
nyāyastu viniyogāntarādabhyāsācca parihṛtaḥ</q> । karmakāle punaḥ prayogaḥ karmaṇi
viniyogāntarasyāvidyamānatvāt bahiśca prayogābhyāsāya । tadidamuktaṃ tāvatkāla-
manavasthānācchakyatvācceti । yadi bahiḥ prayoge(ku)kṛtaḥ saṃskāraḥ karmakālaṃ yāvadava-
tiṣṭhate tadā punarantaḥkarmaṇi prayogo na syāt aśakyo vā yadi bhavetsaṃskāraḥ na
caitadubhayamapyasti iti ।</p>

<p><q>nanu pradhānabhūtāsu ṛkṣu śrūyamāṇā saṅkhyā kathaṃ sāmasādhanatayā
śakyate'vagantum । yato grahe pradhānabhūte śrūyamāṇā na saṃmārgaṃ prati pradhāna-
bhūtā tathā trisaṅkhyāpi pradhānabhūtāsvṛkṣu śrūyamāṇā na sāmasādhanatayā
1. A anapekṣitaḥ
﻿<pb n="258"/>
<q>śaṅkituṃ yuktā</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>anyathā hi vidhānānupapatteḥ</q> yadi hi sāmarnivṛtau
saṅkhyā sādhanatvena nopadiśyate tadā vidhānameva na syāt । tenārthasādhanabhāva-
mṛcāmāśritya sāmni saṅkhyāvidhānamāśaṅki(śri)tam । tadāha---<q>na hi asādhana-
bhūtāsu ṛkṣu śrūyamāṇā saṅkhyā niyantuṃ śakyate</q> । nanu kiṃ tayā niyatayetyatrāha
---<q>aniyamyamānā ca kārye'nanvayinī syāt</q> guṇavacanena smṛtau sām‍nāmevaikā-
samāptipakṣaḥ । nanu grahaikatvavat bhavatu kāryānanviteti paramatamāśaṅka‍yati---<q>bhavatviti</q> ।
dūṣaṇamāha---<q>pratītāvapyananvitatā prāpnoti</q> । yathaikatvaṃ kārye'nanvitamapi pratītāva-
nvayi(ya)tathā trisaṃkhyā na syāt bahuṣvapi kriyamāṇassammārgaḥ ekasminnapi kriyate ।
sām‍nastu ekaikark‌samāptipakṣe nāstyeva trisaṅkhyāsambandhaḥ । imamevābhiprāyaṃ vivarītuṃ
codyaṃ tāvadāha-<q>nanu samāsātpratītāvanvayaṃ ko vārayati samāsapadatvādasya
tṛcaśabdasya</q> । triṅkhyāyā ṛk‌sambandho'vagamyata eva । grahasya caikatvasaṅkhyayā
samanvayo vibhaktiyogāt yathā grahaṃ sammārṣṭīti vibhaktiyogenaikatvaṃ grahasambandhi
pratīyate । tathā tritvamapi ṛk‌sambandhi samāsāditi । pariharati---<q>yuktaṃ tatro-
ddeśyo hi sa na klṛptakāryāpekṣaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---na grahamātrasambandhena pratītyanvayitvaṃ
kiṃ tarhi sammārgasambaddhāvasthāsambandhitvena । asti ca tatra sammārgasambaddhasyāpi
grahasyaikatvena sambandhaḥ । sammārgavidhau grahasyoddiśyamānatvāt pratyuddeśyaṃ ca vidhepa-
sambandhāt । yadi sammārgasya klṛptaṃ kāryaṃ syāt anekagrahavartyeva tadapekṣo'yamupadeśaḥ1
syāt tadā pratyekaṃ sammārgasambandho nāstītyekatvaṃ pratītāva(ya)nanvitaṃ syāt । na ca
sammārgasyānekavarti kāryaṃ klṛptamapekṣyāyamupadeśaḥ, <q>ayaṃ punaḥ klṛptakāryāpekṣo
viniyogaḥ</q></p>
<p>asyārthaḥ---stutiḥ sām‍naḥ kāryamavagataṃ ekaiva ca ṛk guṇābhidhānalakṣaṇāṃ
stutiṃ karoti nark‌samudāyaḥ । tataścārthāt stutisādhanabhūtasāmarnivṛttirekaikakāryaiva
(ca)tathābhūtark‌sambandhinī ca saṅkhyā samāsāt pratīyate । na ca klṛptamṛcaḥ
kāryamapekṣyāyaṃ trisaṅkhyāviniyogaḥ trisaṅkhyāsambandhaḥ tataśca (a)pratītāvapyananvitatvaṃ
tadāha---<q>na cet kāryeṇa saṅkhyā sambadhyate kathamasyāsambaddhamanvayaṃ pratīmaḥ</q>
vidhīyamānā hi saṅkhyā kāryānvayinī bhavati । yadyapi ṛca ekaikasyāḥ stuti-
sādhanatā tathā ca sati tritvasaṅkhyāviniyogavaśena sāmnā stuvīteti sāmaśabdaḥ
sāmāvayavalakṣaṇārtho vijñāyate । yadi punarevaṃ nāśrīyate tadā trisaṅkhyānanvayaḥ ।
<note>1. yamud‌deśaḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="259"/>
evaṃ ca śābdapratyāyyamekatvamāśrityoktam । <q>tatra punaḥ na vibhaktervacanamevaikaṃ
prayojanamiti nāntarīyakaḥ saṅkhyāsambandho darśitaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---yatparo hi
śabdaḥ sa śabdārthaḥ । grahaṃ sammārṣṭīti naikatvaparā dvitīyā kintu karmatvaparā tenā-
vivakṣito nāntarīyaka ekatvasambandhaḥ । <q>iha tu nirnimittatvādaśabdārthaḥ
prāp‍noti</q> । iha tu triśabdaprayoge nimittāntaraṃ nāstīti trisaṅkhyā-
sambandha eva vivakṣitaḥ । sa cānanvita ityaśabdārtha eva syāt anvitābhidhāyi-
tvācchabdasya । aśabdārthatve ca pramādanimittakastriśabdena1 saha samabhivyāhāraḥ syāt
pramādaśca puruṣāśraya iti pauruṣeyatvāpatteḥ sthitasya prāmāṇyasyoddhāraprasaṅgaḥ । tasmāt
satyapyṛcāṃ prādhānye (na) saṅkhyānurodhenārthalakṣaṇaḥ sādhanabhāvo varṇanīyaḥ । darśitaṃ ca
pradhānabhūtānāmapi arthaniṣpādakatvaṃ, pradhānamapi grahādi sammārgaṃ sādhayatyeveti vadatā ।
tadāha---<q>tasmāt saḍkhyāniyamamaparityajatā prādhānyamṛcāmabhyupagamanīyam</q> ।
ekena sām‍nā tisra ṛcaḥ saṃskāryā ityabhyupagamanīyam । yata evamataḥ sāmāvayavābhi-
vyaṅgyaṃ stutivākyaṃ manvāno rathantaraṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ bhavati iti rathantaraśabdena rathantarāvayava-
lakṣaṇayā aviruddhaṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī । ākhyātasambandhi vidheyamabhyupagataṃ bhavati
tṛce sāma kriyata iti sāmakṛtāveva trisaṅkhyopadeśāt । siddhānte(hi)tu stutau
saṅkhyopadeṣṭavyā, sāma kriyata iti sāmaśabdaśca lakṣaṇayā varṇito bhavati । sāma-
śabdena hi siddhānte sāmābhyāso lakṣaṇīyaḥ । tanna kṛtaṃ bhavati ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---naitadupapadyate sāmanirvṛttireva trisaṅkhyāyāḥ
kāryamiti</q> । kutaḥ ? upadeśapūrvakaṃ hi kāryāvadhāraṇam । bhavatvevaṃ tathāpi
kimiti sāmaniṣpattiḥ kāryā na bhavatītyatrāha---<q>mukhyaścāyamupadeśo rathantaraṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ
bhavati bṛhata pṛṣṭhaṃ bhavati iti</q> । mukhyaśabdena prathamabhāvyuktaṃ stutirhi sāmnaḥ
kāryamavagamyate paścādekaṃ sāma tṛce kriyata iti varṇanīyaḥ । bhavatu mukhyastathāpi
kimityāha---<q>pratya/?/caṃ stutiḥ parisamāpyate prāyaśaḥ</q> । prāyeṇaikargguṇābhidhānaṃ
karoti, nark‌sasudāyaḥ । prāyagrahaṇaṃ k‍vacidardhena k‍vacitpādena stutiḥ parisamāpyata
iti darśayitum । bhavatvevaṃ tathāpi kimityāha---<q>evaṃ sati stotrasādhanatve'vagate
sām‍na upadeśānnāvayavasya tatkāryamiti śakyate kalpayitum</q> । asyārthaḥ---
yadi hi prartya/?/caṃ stutiḥ parisamāpyate vyāsajya ca gānaṃ kriyate tadā rathantaraṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ
<note>1. tṛcaśabdena A.</note>
﻿<pb n="260"/>
bhavatīti rathantarāvayavo rathantaraśabdena lakṣayitvā pṛṣṭhasaṃjñake stotre viniyoktavyaḥ । na
caitacchakyate upadeśataḥ sāmakāryatayā stuteḥ avagatatvāt tatpūrvakatvācca trisaṅkhyo-
padeśasya । kathaṃ tatpūrvakatvamityatrāha---<q>kāryāpekṣaścāyamupadeśaḥ ekaṃ sāma tṛce
kriyata iti</q> । yo'pi sāmanirvṛttāveva tritvasaṅkhyopadeśamicchati tenāpi sām‍naḥ
kāryāvagamyo'yaṃ trisaṅkhyopadeśo vaktavyaḥ 1mānāntarāvagatakāryasya śeṣitvāt ।</p>
<p>nanu ca yadyapyayaṃ tatpūrvakastritvasaṅkhyāniyamaḥ2 tathāpi nirviṣayo'yamiti varaṃ
rathantarāvayavalakṣaṇā । tadāha---<q>nanu ca nirviṣayo'yaṃ niyama ityuk‍taṃ</q> sādhana-
tvenācodanādṛcaḥ । yadi ṛk stutiṃ prati sādhanatvena coditā syāt3 tadāśrayā
trisaṅkhyā stutau vidhīyeta । na caitadasti । pariharati---</p>
<p><q>atrābhidhīyate---nanu ca bhavatāpi pūrvapakṣiṇā'rtha eva sāmaniṣpattā-
vṛcaḥ sādhanabhāvaḥ trisaṅkhyāniyamaheturupanyastaḥ, mamāpi asāveva
bhaviṣyatīti</q> stutāvapi evamastyeva carcaḥ sādhanatvaṃ, yadyevaṃ kastarhi rāddhāntasya viśeṣaḥ
ityāha---<q>ayaṃ tu viśeṣaḥ upadeśānurodhinī kāryakalpanā kṛtā bhavati ।
