rathantaraṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ bhavatī</q>tyupadeśānurodhena sām‍na eva kṛts‍nasya stutiḥ kāryaṃmiti
kalpitaṃ bhavati । stutiniṣpannaścārthasādhanabhāvaḥ siddhāntinokta iti । pṛcchati---
<q>k‍va punarasāvārthasādhanabhāvaḥ</q> ? uttaraṃ---<q>stutāviti brūmaḥ</q> । stutau hi sāmaniyamaḥ
stotraniyamaśca paṭhitaḥ । sāmaniyamo rathantaraṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ bhavatītyādiṣu ṛṅ‌niyamaḥ kavatīṣu
rathantaramiti । stotraniyamaḥ pañcadaśa ārbhavaḥ pavamāna iti paṭhitaḥ । tatra yathā-
kathañcidaniyamāt stotrapūraṇe prāpte tadarthamidaṃ niyamavacanamityekaṃ sāma tṛce kriyata
iti pratyṛcaṃ gānamiti siddham ।</p>
<p>nanu sāma kriyata iti sāmaśabdo'bhyāsalakṣaṇārthaḥ syādaśratastutisambandhaśca
triśabdasyetyatrāha---<q>mukhyopadeśānurodhena ca kāryaniyamaniyogānāṃ svārtha-
siddherna lakṣaṇā padārthasambandho vā (na) doṣaḥ</q> । kārye ye niyamaniyogāsteṣāṃ
mukhyopadeśānuguṇyenārtho varṇanīya iti pūrvamuktam । tena lakṣaṇā padāntarasambandhaśca
na doṣaḥ । <q>sanidarśanaṃ prayojanamuk‍tam</q> ।</p>
<note>1. R. śāstrāvagata.</note>
<note>2. A. viniogaḥ</note>
<note>3. tadā'prāptā A.</note>
﻿<pb n="261"/>
<lg><l>।। 4 ।। tadabhyāsaḥ samāsu syāt ।। 21 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>tṛce gānaṃ kartavyamityetāvatsamadhigataṃ, samāsu geyaṃ viṣamāsu vā
geyamiti na śās‍traṃ bhavati</q> । viṣamatvepi trisaṅkhyopapatteḥ । tasmādaniyamaṃ
pūrvapakṣavādī manyate ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---satyaṃ vacanasyāyamagocaraḥ samāsveva geya-
miti । tathāpi samāsveva gānaṃ kartavyam</q> । kutaḥ ? uttaraṃ-(viṣamā) <q>asamāsveva
gāne kriyamāṇe aśruto vikāraḥ kṛto bhavati sāmnaḥ</q> । na ca vacanādṛte aśruta-
karaṇaṃ yuktam । yāvāneva śrutasyotsarge doṣaḥ tāvānaśrutakalpanāyāmiti samāsveva gānaṃ
kartavyam । vikārastu bhāṣyakāreṇa pradarśito laghīyasyāmṛci gīteḥ saṃśaraṇam ।
bṛhatyāṃ vileśa iti । <q>nidarśanamuktam</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 5 ।। naimittikaṃ tūttarātvamānantaryāt pratīyeta ।। 23 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nanūttarayorgāyatītyayamupadeśaḥ kimarthamiha cintyate ?</q> uttaraṃ---<q>ūha-
siddha‍yarthaṃ cintyate</q> । etadeva vivṛṇoti-<q>uttarāpaṭhiteṣu ṛgardhapādeṣu uttarayo-
rityanena gṛhyamāṇeṣu, prāgādhādikāryaṃ kartavyaṃ yonyuttarāsu naivaṃ syāt</q> yonya-
pekṣayā uttarāṇāṃ vyavahitānāmavyavahitānāṃ vā yathotpannānāmeva sambhavāt । tasmādaya-
mupadeśo vicārayituṃ yuktaḥ । tatra pūrvapakṣavādī uttarābhidhānamaviśiṣṭaṃ manyate yathā rūḍhi-
yaugikayorabhidhāne viśeṣaḥ tathātra na bhavati । ubhayoruttarāśabdasya rūḍhatvāt । satya-
maviśiṣṭaḥ padārthaḥ, 1abhidheyasyārthāntarāpekṣitvaṃ tu viśeṣaḥ । yonyapekṣamuttarātvaṃ
yonyavadhikagrahaṇaṃ uttarāsaṃjñikāstu nirapekṣā iti ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntavādī tu manyata</q> iti sambandhaḥ । <q>sāpekṣanirapekṣayośca nirapekṣaṃ
balīyaḥ</q> śīghrāvagamāt yatastasmāduttarāsveva gānaṃ kartavyamiti । <q>śeṣamuktam</q> ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ vā</q></p>
<p><q>yadyonyāṃ taduttarayorityatrottarāsaṃjñitā eva grāhyā iti sthitam ।
tathā samāsu geyamityapi sthitam । atredānīṃ kiṃ samāsu ityetadādaraṇīya-
muta uttarayoriti</q> । anenākṣep‍tuṃ saṃśayo'nubhāṣitaḥ । ākṣipati---<q>nanu caitadayuktaṃ
<note>1. R abhidhānasya</note>
﻿<pb n="262"/>
<q>cintayitum । yathāhi---uttarayorgeyamiti vacanaṃ, samāsviti nyāyaḥ na ca
nyāyo vacanamatikrāmati</q> । aśrutādikalpanaṃ hi nyāyo niruṇaddhi na vacanam । tena
vacanāt viṣamāsvapyuttarāsu gātavyam । tasmānnātra pūrvapakṣaḥ sambhavatīti ।</p>
<p>samādhatte---<q>astyatra pūrvapakṣāśaṅkā atijagatīṣu stuvata iti vacanaṃ
manyate pūrvapakṣavādī</q> । kutaḥ ? <q>na hyaprāptānuvādaḥ samkṣavati</q> । yadi hi uttarā-
daraṇaṃ tadā jagatībahutvamaprāptamityanuvādo na ghaṭate । tena vacanāni tvapūrvatvāditi
vacanamevedam । tathāpi ubhayathā vacanasambhave kena viśeṣeṇa samāsvityādriyate । tatrāha---
<q>sāmānyaṃ ca yadyonyāṃ taduttarayoriti vacanamatijagatīṣviti viśeṣadarśanam
tena yadāhavanīyanyāyena samāsveva gātavyam</q> । tasmānnirākaraṇīyā pūrvapakṣā-
śaṅkā । rāddhāntamāha---<q>seya nirākriyate pūrvapakṣāśaṅkāvacanamidaṃ</q> yadyonyāṃ
taduttarayorgāyatīti । uttarāsaṃsthitāśca gṛhyanta ityuktaṃ tena tatraiva geyam । yattvatijaga-
tīṣviti tadāvṛttyāpi bahuvacanamavakalpata iti na vacanakalpanāmarhati । ekaviṃśaḥ
ṣoḍaśī tṛce saptakṛtvo'bhyasyamāne saptadhā atijagatyāmāvartyamānāyāṃ bahuvacanaṃ ghaṭata
eva । klṛptavacanānurodhena hyeṣāpi kalpanā nānupapannā । tena vacanameva na bhavati
atijagatīṣu stuvata iti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 6 ।। prāgāthikantu ।। 25 ।।</l></lg>
<p>nanu prāgāthike nirdeśe sati cinteyamanucitetyāha---<q>kimatra cintyate ?</q>
uttaraṃ---<q>idamatra cintyate । kiṃ kakubhāvuttara iti pṛthak‌tvaniveśitvaṃ
saṅkhyāyā ādaraṇīyam</q> uta prāgāthikamiti nirdeśaḥ iti kakubhāvuttara iti
dvisaṅkhyā pṛthaktvaniveśinī । tenotpattikakubhorāgamaḥ pratibhāti । prāgāthikanirdeśācca
pragādha iti ।</p>
<p>tatra pūrvapakṣavādī pṛthaktvaniveśitvaṃ nyāyyam manyate । tenotpattikakubhorāgamaḥ
nirdeśastu laukikaḥ nirdeśa eva kevalo, na vastu vyavasthāpanāyālam ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntastu kakubhāvuttarākāraṃ sāmagānaṃ kartavyamiti kartavyatāmanuṣṭhānamevāva-
gacchāmaḥ । aparakakubhameva uttarāṃ kakubhaṃ kṛtvā gātavyamiti pratīyate । kakubhāvuttarā-
kāraṃ gānaṃ kartavyamityavyaye yathābhipretākhyāna iti ṇamul kārye vidhiḥ । <q>pṛthaktva-
niveśitvamupapadyate</q> । pragāthena kṛte ṛg‌dvaye pṛthaktvaniveśitvamupapadyate । <q>uttara-
yoriti vacanāttu uttarāsaṃjñitāḥ śakyante grahītuṃ ekatvādasya śāstrasya</q> ।
﻿<pb n="263"/>
<q>uttarayorgāyatītyekamidaṃ śāstram । ekasmiṃśca yathā saṅkhyāvagamaḥ tathottarāvagamepi iti
nobhayāvagame kāryataivāvagamyate । evaṃ ca prāgāthikamiti nirdeśa upapanno bhavati ।
tasmādeṣa pakṣaḥ śreyān । sanidarśanaṃ śeṣamuktam ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ vā</q></p>
<p><q>kaḥ punaratra pūrveṇa viśeṣaḥ ?</q> uttaraṃ---<q>tricchandā āvāpo mādhyandinaḥ
pavamāna iti vacanātikrama manyate</q> (utpatti bṛhatyostvā) pūrvapakṣavādī । yadi
yāsau raurave yaughājaye ca viṣṭāra paṅ‌ktiḥ tāṃ svīkṛtya prāgāthikaṃ kriyate । tadā
gāyatrī bṛhatī triṣṭup paṅ‌ktibhiḥ tricchabdastvaṃ śrutamatikramya(te) utpattibṛhatyostvā-
naya paneṅ‌ktiparityāgādupapadyata eva tricchandastvamiti pūrvapakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntastu paṅ‌kta‍yā bṛhatīkāraṃ gānaṃ kartavyamiti kāryatvenāpi bṛhatyāḥ
tricchandastvamupapannaṃ bhavatīti । yadi hi paṅ‌ktirūpatvenāsau stotre vyāpriyate tato
bhavet tricchandastvavirodhaḥ । nacaitadasti । tāmādāya pragādhena bṛhatīdvayaṃ sampādya
sāmaprayogāt । śeṣaṃ pūrvavat । nanu ṣaṣṭistriṣṭubho mādhyandinaṃ savanamiti liṅgaṃ
pūrvapakṣe'pyupapannaṃ trichandastvavat paṭhitapaṃktiparityāgāt । yadi hi ṛgantarāgamanena
trichandastvaṃ labdhaṃ tadā nāsti paṅ‌ktipragāṇamityāśaṅkyāha---<q>nāsyāsvānīyamānāsu
prakaraṇapaṭhitāḥ śakyante'prayojyatvena vak‍tuṃ, apragītatvameva kevalamāsāṃ
syāt na punaraprayogaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---prakaraṇapaṭhitānāṃ grāhakagṛhītānāṃ yadyapi
gānaṃ nāsti tathāpi laiṅgikaḥ kvāpi viniyogo bhavati । tena nāprayogaḥ savanagatark
parigaṇanā । na stotraparigaṇanāni na pūrvapakṣe liṅgānupapattiḥ apragītatve tricchanda-
sttvopapattiḥ stotragatachandogaṇanā neyaṃ, tena kāryāntaraprayoge'pi trichandastvādhirodhaḥ
iti upapannaṃ liṅgaṃ pūrvādhikaraṇe'pi tulyam ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ vā</q></p>
<p><q>atredānīṃ ko viśeṣaḥ ? uttaraṃ---ayamasti viśeṣaḥ</q> yadyonyāṃ tadutta-
rayoriti gāyatrībhyāṃ śāstraṃ sampannamiti nānuṣṭup‌kāraṃ gānakartavyatā'vagamyata iti
pūrvapakṣavādī manyate ।</p>
<p>ekaṃ sāma tṛce kriyata iti yadyonyāṃ taduttarayoriti ca gāyatrībhyāmeva śāstraṃ
sampannam । kimarthaṃ pragrathanenānuṣ‍ṭumaṃ kṛtvā gātavyamiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ? nanu cānuṣ‍ṭubhe
tṛce bhavataḥ ityasya virodhaḥ ekayāpyanuṣ‍ṭubhā tasyopapatteḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="264"/>
<p>rādhāntavādī tu manyate---kāryatvepi uttarayoriti saṃjñitvaṃ dvitvaṃ cāviruddha-
miti na kāryāvagamaḥ śakyate bādhitum śyāvāśvāndhīgave ānuṣ‍ṭubhe tṛce bhavata iti
śruteḥ tisro'nuṣ‍ṭubhaḥ pratīyante sambhavastu(su)tāsāṃ pragāthe nāstyeva । na ca kiñcidvi-
ruddha‍yate । tenānuṣ‍ṭuṃ kṛtvā gātavyamiti pratīyate । tasmādatrāpi prāgāthikaṃ gānam ।
<q>śeṣamuktam</q> ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ vā</q></p>
<p>atrādhikaraṇe kiṃ pragāthaḥ kartavyo neti cintyate । na kartavyo gāyatrībhyā-
meva tṛca uttarayoriti copapatteḥ iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>ānuṣ‍ṭubhe tṛce bhavata iti śruteḥ tisṛṇāmapyanuṣ‍ṭup‍tvāvagamāt kāryaḥ pragādha
iti rāddhāntaḥ । bhāṣye tu utpattyanuṣ‍ṭuvāgamābhidhāne varamāgamo na tu pragādha iti
pradarśayitum ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ vā</q></p>
<p>nanu cātrāpi catuśśatamaindrābārhatāḥ pragādhā iti codanāyāmeva śravaṇāt
pragādhenaiva bhavitavyam । kathamatra pūrvapakṣāśaṅkā । atrotyate - ṛk pragrathanenāpi
pragādhaśabda upapadyata eva tṛca uttarayoriti ca sarvamupapannaṃ bhavatīti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>dva‍yṛcānāṃ hi taccaturuttaraṃ śataṃ tenānyasmāt dva‍yṛcādekāmṛcamādāya tṛcaṃ
sampādya gānaṃ kariṣyati tena pragāthaśabdastṛcaśabda uttarayoriti copapadyate ।
kimaparaṃ pādapragrathanena ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntastu anyā anyā ṛco bhavanti tadeva sāmetyūhasya ca darśanāt
pādapragrathanenaiva gānaṃ kartavyam । pragādhatvasiddhaye hi tādṛśaṃ pragrathanaṃ yuktamāśrayituṃ
yena darśanavirodhona bhavati iti pādapragrathanenaiva gānaṃ nyāyyam । tṛca uttarayoriti ca
kāryepyārtha upapadyata evetyuktam । <q>śeṣamuktam</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 7 ।। arthaikatvādvikalpaḥ syāt ।। 29 ।।</l></lg>
<p>kathaṃ punargīterviniyuktatvādupāyāḥ samuccīyante ityāśaṅkate । yadi hi te'pi
viniyuktā bhaveyuḥ tadā samuccīyanta iti yāvat । na ca te viniyuktāḥ gītereva
﻿<pb n="265"/>
viniyuktatvāt । uttaraṃ---<q>na hi upāyānanupādāya gītiḥ śakyate upādātuṃ
ityupādānataḥ prāptiṃ manvāno gṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatayā samuccayamāha pūrvapakṣī</q> ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntastu---ayameva viśeṣaḥ yaduta eka evābhyupāya upāyāntaranirapekṣo
gītyupādānaṃ nirvartayati । nacopāyānugrahāya sāmopādānābhyāse pramāṇamasti ।
sakṛdupāttenāpi sāmnā kāryasiddheḥ । kāryaṃ ca dharmāṇāṃ prayojanaṃ nopāyāḥ । tasmāda-
gṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatvaṃ vikalpahetuḥ na samuccaye iti siddho vikalpaḥ ।।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ vā</q></p>
<p>nanu cedamadhikaraṇamanupapannārthamiti vakṣyate । yadi tāvadidaṃ vacanaṃ tadopa-
deśacinteyam nāsmin lakṣaṇe'syāvatāraḥ । atha vikṛtāvidaṃ vacanaṃ tato'narthakaṃ prakṛtau
stuteḥ sāmasādhanatvāvagamāt prakṛtivadeva sām‍nā stutiḥ prāpnoti । pratyuta
ṛgvidhānārthamevedaṃ yuktaṃ sāmnaḥ prāptatvāt ṛco'prāptatvāt ।</p>
<p>atrocyate-prakṛtau vikṛtau vā bhavatu parasparanirapekṣakāryanirvṛttyarthamidamadhi-
karaṇaṃ yadi ṛcāmapi stutau viniyogaḥ syāt tadā sāmanirapekṣameva kāryamṛcāṃ syāt
sāmaviniyogapakṣe ca ṛṅ‌nirapekṣasām‍na eva kāryamiti yadetadāpyate tannikaraṇārthamida-
madhikaraṇam ।</p>
<p>nanu ca yadyetadvikṛtau vacanaṃ tadā'narthakaṃ ṛgvidhānārthaṃ ca syāditi pūrvamuktaṃ
tatrāha---<q>na ca prakṛtivikṛtyorniyamaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---vikṛtāvapi yadi (vikṛtau)
stutau sāmavidhānārthametatsyāt tadā prakṛtigatāsvapi stutiṣu codakataḥ sāmaprāpti-
raviruddhā । vikṛtihiṃ pradhānabhūtātkarmaṇo dharmān gṛhṇāti prakṛtyaṅgāpūrvaṃ tu stuti-
viṣayaṃ vaikṛtastuterdharmagrāhīti na kutaścidviśeṣaḥ । tena prakṛtāvapi yatsāmnaḥ stuti-
darśanaṃ tadetadvacanapūrvakameveti nānarthakaṃ vacanam । na ca ṛgvidhānārthaṃ vacanam ।
kasmāt prakṛtivikṛtyorniyamo nāstītyāha---<q>yadeva yatrābhyadhikaṃ tadi-
tareṇākāṅkṣyate । prakṛtiliṅgaviśeṣādviśeṣo'vagamyate । naiva tasyāḥ
prakṛtirasti</q> । prakṛtigatasyāpi stotrāpūrvasya sādhanākāṅkṣā vaikṛtāpūrvasya sāmasādhanaṃ
vihitam । stutitvaṃ ca codanāliṅgam । tena yukto'tideśaḥ । yata eva paraspara-
nirapekṣakāryanirvṛttyarthamidamadhikaraṇaṃ ata evedamasmin lakṣaṇe contyate upadeśe
viśeṣābhāvāt । pūrvapakṣāvasthāyāṃ hi upadeśato vikalpo nāsti । śrutito viśeṣā-
﻿<pb n="266"/>
bhāvāt nāsyāṃ śrutau samuccaye vikalpe vā viśeṣaḥ, arthataśca viśeṣābhāvādubhayoḥ
sādhanabhāvasya samuccayenāpi ghaṭanāt aruṇaikahāyanīnyāyato vā dvārabhedena samuccayā-
virodhāt । kāryatastu vikalpa eva prāpnoti । ekaikasya viniyogenāṅgatvādekai-
kopādāne'pi tatsiddheḥ । tena kārye vikalpo'yamiti asmin lakṣaṇe saṅgatiḥ ।
kāryacintārūpatvāt । ūhasiddha‍yarthaṃ hi avāntarakāryacintā prastuteyam ।</p>
<p><q>api ca avāntarakāryacintā tannirākaraṇārthaṃ</q> vikalpanirākaraṇārthaṃ
ihaiva cintanīyam । tatraiva pūrvapakṣavādinā avaśyaṃ nindayaivāsurānvavāyasya nimittabhāva
iti kiṃ padāntarāpekṣayeti bhavatu vākyabhedaḥ । tasmāt pūrvapakṣavādī vikalpaṃ manyata
iti sambandhaḥ । yadi nindayaivāsurānvavāyasya vākyārthāvagame nimittabhāva iti niścayaḥ
syāt tadaikavākyataiva bhavet । yadi tu anindayā stutyā copapadyate tadā nāstiḥ
padāntarāpekṣāyāṃ pramāṇamiti vākyabhedāt ṛcāmapi stutau viniyogaḥ tathā
sām‍no'pi । tatra kāryasyaikaikasya sādhyatvādvikalpaḥ । vikṛtāvapi copapannārthamevedaṃ
vikalpapakṣe vacanaṃ, ṛco'prāptāyā eva vidhānāt । tadvidhāne ca sām‍na ekāntena
nivṛttirmābhūditi tasyāpi vidhānaṃ yuktaṃ tadāha-<q>ṛgvidhāne hi sāmnā stutirna
prāp‍noti</q> prakṛtitaḥ prāpterupadeśena vādhitatvāt । tasmādubhayaṃ vidhātavyam ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu syādetadevaṃ yadyaviśiṣṭo nimittabhāvaḥ syāt 1ayaṃ tu
gamyate viśeṣaḥ । ko'sau ?</q> uttaraṃ---<q>iti vakṣyamāṇaḥ</q> । kaḥ ? padārthāntareṇa
sāmnā stuvītetyanena hi sambandhitvena vikalpenāsākṣātkṛtatvādasya tadasaṃbandhitvam ।
ṛcā stuvīteti kalpanā । na cākalpanāyāṃ sambhavantyāṃ kalpanā sambhavatīti hetoḥ
sāmnaiva stutiḥ । <q>yadi sāmamātravidhānametat vikṛtāvidānīṃ kiṃ prayojanamasya
vākyasya ?</q> pūrvapakṣe tu pūrvoktaprakāreṇa vikṛtāvapyetadvacanamarthavat । uttaraṃ---
<q>nāvaśyaṃ prakṛtivikārabhāve niyama ityuktaḥ parihāraḥ</q> pūrvameva ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ vā</q></p>
<p><q>abhidhāne viśeṣānavagamāt pragītāpragītayorman‍trayoḥ pratīkena ca
vidhānāt aviśeṣaṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī</q> । asyārthaḥ---yathā stutau viśeṣaḥ
pragītenaiva stuteḥ sādhyatvāt 2tasyābhidhānaṃ tu nāpragītenaivopasthānātmakatvābhidhānāt
<note>1. idaṃ-mā</note>
<note>2. tasyā abhidhāne pragīte tulyaṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="267"/>
pragītena cāpragītena ca tulyam । ayaṃ sahasramānava iti (pragītena)pratīkena ṛco
viniyogāt tasyāścobhayāvasthatvādaniyamaḥ । yadi hi etayeti sarvanāmnā viniyoga-
stadā tasya prakṛtaparatvāt pragītāyāśca sāmavede prakṛtatvāt nāpragītayopasthātavyamiti
gamyate । pratīkena cāyaṃ viniyogaḥ । etacchabdastu pratīkopāttāyā ṛca eva
parāmarśakaḥ । yastvatra stutiśabdaḥ so'bhidhānopalakṣaṇayaiva, anyathā sāmnaiva syāt
ṛcāṃ stutāvacoditatvāt ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu etayeti viśeṣāvagamāt pragītayopasthātavyamiti yuktam</q> ।
---asyārthaḥ-etayopatiṣṭhata iti viniyogārthaḥ etacchabdaśca prakṛtaparaḥ sāmavede
ca pragītaiva sā prakṛtā । paścāt kayetyapekṣāyāṃ ayaṃ sahasramānava iti viśeṣasamarpaṇaṃ
pratīkenaiva । evaṃ vyākhyāyamāne etayeti pravṛttiviśeṣakaraṃ bhavati ।</p>
<p>nanu pratīkagrahaṇāt punarapyaviśeṣa ityatrāha---<q>pratīkagrahaṇaṃ tvaviśiṣṭameta-
yeti yā prakṛtā pragītopasthāpitā tasyā api viniyoge pratīkagraha-
ṇasyāviśeṣaḥ</q> ।</p>
<p><q>nanu ca sāmavede apragītāpi paṭhyata iti । ṛk‌pāṭhacodanāmu-
panyasyārthatayā pragāṇārthatayā na svarūpagrahaṇārthamṛk‌pāṭha iti nāpragītā
prakṛtā,</q> kintu pragīteti । āhavanīyopasthāne pragītāpragītayoḥ avikalpamuktavān ।
kutaḥ punaḥ apragītāyāḥ pragāṇārthamevātra pāṭhaḥ ityatrāha---<q>dṛṣṭe sambhavatyadṛṣṭa-
kalpanānupapatteḥ</q> । pragāṇanirvṛttirhi dṛṣṭaṃ prayojanam । na hyagṛhītānyakṣarāṇi sukhaṃ
pragīyante । tasmādyuktamanyārthatvam । ataḥ pragītayopasthātavyamiti sthitam ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ vā</q></p>
<p><q>kaḥpunaḥ gītyupāyaiḥ saha svarāṇāṃ viśeṣaḥ ?</q> uttaraṃ---<q>ayamasti
viśeṣaḥ svarāṇāṃ viniyogaśeṣatvam</q> । man‍tro viniyujyamānaḥ sasvara eva viniyujyate
jape nyūṅghe ca svaraniyamadarśanāt । yenaiva hi svareṇa man‍trāḥ paṭhitāḥ tenaiva svareṇa
jape nyuṅghe ca prayujyante । anyathāhi niyamo na syāt । nyūṅkhaśabdena ca nirantara-
paṭhitāḥ ṣaḍoṅkārā ucyante । yajñakarmaṇi japanyūṅkhayoraikaśrusyaṃ nāsti yajñakarmaṇyajapa-
nyūṅkhasāmasbiti paryudāsāt ।</p>
﻿<pb n="268"/>
<p>kena punarviśeṣeṇa japanyūṅkhyorupādānaṃ ye[na]tānyapi man‍trasvaraviśeṣeṇa
paṭhyante teṣāmapi tarhi svaraviśeṣeṇaiva prayogaḥ syāt । anyathā svarānarthakyāditi
tatrāha---<q>yeṣāṃ tu</q> nānenaiva prayogaḥ teṣāmudāttādayo'rthaniścayāyaiva । tāno yajñakarmaṇi
iti japanyūṅkhātirekiṇāṃ yeṣāmaikaśrutyena viniyogaḥ । tāna aikaśrutyam । teṣā-
mudāttādayo'rthaniścayāyaiva svādhyāyakāle । etacca na 1pūrvapakṣavādinā uktam kintu
suhṛdbhāvena granthakāreṇa ।</p>
<p><q>nanu viniyoge sati sutarāṃ nātra pūrvapakṣāśaṅkā aikaikaśyena vini-
yogāvagamāt samuccayāśaṅkā mandaiva</q> । pariharati---<q>na cātrā[nā]śaṅkā</q> ।
kintvāśaṅkaiva kārye'bhidhānalakṣaṇe svarāṇāṃ avaśyaṃ vyāpāradarśanāt । abhidhāna-
mātrāt varṇaviśeṣeṇāvadhānasiddheḥ । tenādṛṣṭārthatayā samuccaya eva yuktaḥ । <q>svarato'-
pyarthanirṇayamabhiyuk‍tā varṇayantīti2 rāddhāntaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ-yadyapyanabhiyuktā
lokāḥ svaraviśeṣeṇārthaviśeṣaṃ nāvadhārayanti, tathāpi paṇiniprabhṛtayo'bhiyuktāḥ svara-
viśeṣeṇārthaviśeṣaṃ varṇayantyeva । arthaviśeṣe svaraviśeṣānuśāsanāt <quote>“pade'padeśe”</quote>
<quote>“nivāte vātatrāṇe”</quote> ityādau । (pā. sū 6-2-7, 8)</p>
<lg><l>।। 8 ।। sāmapradeśe vikārastadapekṣaḥ syāt śāstrakṛtatvāt ।। 32 ।।</l></lg>
<p>atredānīṃ cintyate---kiṃ gītivat gītyupāyā akṣarābhivyaktyarthā uta
gītiniṣpattyarthā eveti । tatra yadi gītiniṣpattyarthāstadā yathāyonyuttarayorapi prayogaḥ ।
tatra yadi gītiniṣpattyarthā gītyupāyāḥ tadā yasmin gītibhāge viṣpādakatvena āī
bhāvaḥ kṛto yonau uttarāyāmapi tasminneva bhāge prayoktavya iti yathāyonyuttarayoḥ
gītyupāyānāṃ prayogaḥ । athākṣarābhivyaktyarthā gītyupāyāḥ tadā yathābhivyaṅgyaṃ prayogaḥ
yonau vṛddhaṃ tālavyaṃ āībhāvenābhivyaktamityuttarayorapi tadevābhivyajyate na yathāyoni
prayogaḥ ।</p>
<p>etaduktaṃ bhavati---kiṃ gītibhāgavaśena gītyupāyānāṃ prayoga uta varṇavaśeneti ।
tatra pūrvapakṣavādī gītyutpattyarthā upāyā iti manyate । kutaḥ ? gīterhyakṣarābhivyaktiḥ
<note>1. R. pūrvapakṣakālenoktam</note>
<note>2. upadiśantīti ।</note>
﻿<pb n="269"/>
prayojanaṃ nopāyānām । etadeva kuta ityatrāha---<q>yadyakṣarābhivyaktyarthā evo-
pāyā bhaveyuḥ kenedānīṃ gītirniṣpādyate aniṣpannāyāśca gīteḥ akṣarābhi-
vyaktyarthataiva hīyate</q> । tenopāyā gītiniṣpattyarthāḥ, gītirakṣarābhivyaktyarthā ।
ato gītyarthā evopāyā iti yuktam । tena gītibhāgavaśena prayogaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>atrābhidhīyate---yadyupāyā akṣarābhivyaktyarthā na bhavanti tadā
gīterakṣarābhivyaktyarthataiva na prāp‍noti</q> । kuta ityatrāha---<q>na hyakṣarāśritā
upāyā na santi । yadyakṣarāśritā upāyā na bhaveyuḥ tadā[kiṃ]gītiniṣpādi-
tākṣarāṇyabhivyañ‍jyāt</q> । āībhāvādayastu akṣarāśritāḥ । tatra yadyete abhi-
vyaktyarthā na bhavanti tadā'paro'bhivyañjako bhaviṣyati ।</p>
<p><q>nanu yadyupāyā akṣarābhivyaktyarthāḥ tadā gīteranutpattiḥ prāp‍notī-
tyuk‍tam</q> । pariharati-<q>iyamevotpattirasya yadutākṣarāṇāṃ abhivyak‍tiḥ svarāṇāṃ</q>
cānekopāyasamāhārātmikā gītiḥ sopāyairanavayavabhūtairniṣpādyate । ato'tra dṛṣṭe'rthe
sambhavati nādṛṣṭārthakalpanā nyāyyetyakṣarābhivyaktirevopāyaiḥ । darśitā cākṣarābhi-
vyaktyarthatā āībhāvena । tālavyamevāībhāvena niṣkṛṣyābhivyajyate ityanyeṣvapi bhāga-
vikāreṣu anekaghā'kṣarābhivyaktyarthatā । <q>kathaṃ tarhi lopāgamastobhādiṣu</q> ।
lopo hi anuccāraṇātmakaḥ sa kathamakṣarābhivyaktyarthaḥ । tathā āgamastobhāvapyakṣarānta-
rānupraveśātmakatvāt akṣarāṇāmanabhivyañjakau । uttaraṃ---<q>tatrāpyabhidhānātmataivā-
dṛṣṭāthaitaiva dṛṣṭārthatve na viśeṣaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---yadyapi lopādayo nābhivyañjakāḥ
tathāpyakṣarābhivyaktyarthā eva akṣarābhivyañjikāyā gīteḥ viśeṣāpādakatvāt । sa ca
tadāhito viśeṣo gīteradṛṣṭārthaḥ । tadāha---<q>teṣāmapyabhidhānavyak‍tāvevādṛṣṭārtha-
tvaṃ kalpayitavyam sviṣṭakṛdādīnāmiva dravyadevatāgatam</q> । tasmādvarṇavaśena
gānaṃ kartavyam, na bhāga1 vaśeneti siddham ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 9 ।। stobhasyaike dravyāntare nivṛttimṛgvat ।। 34 ।।</l></lg>
<p>nanu stobhasya lakṣaṇamuktvā stobhapradeśāpradeśacintā yuktetyatrāha---<q>idānīṃ
stobhaścintyate---pradiśyante neti । asyā eva cintāyā lakṣaṇasaṅgata-
<note>1. A. gīnivaśena.</note>
﻿<pb n="270"/>
<q>tvāt</q> । yadyonyāṃ taduttarayorgāyatītyanena vacanena yonisādhyastutikārye uttarayo-
viṃniyogaḥ । tacca stutyākhyaṃ kāryaṃ sāmasādhyamiti kāryeṇa sāmapradeśaḥ ūhātmaka-
stadviśeṣaśca stobhapradeśe iti stobhaprasaṅgena । stobhaśabdena yaducyate tadupariṣṭā-
dvakṣyāmaḥ ।</p>
<p>tatra pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ---<q>gītiśabdena stobhānāmanabhidhānāt ṛgakṣaraiśca saha
stutāvasambandhāt kāryārthatvāccātideśavākyasya na pradeśaḥ stobhānāmiti</q> ।
yadyonyāṃ taduttarayoriti yadidaṃ atideśavākyaṃ tatkāryārtham । yonikāryaṃ stutyākhya-
muttarābhyāmapi kartavyamiti । tatkāryaṃ yonyāpi gītiyuktayā kṛtamityuttarayorapi
tatsiddhaye gītirākṣipyate । tatra yadi stobhā gītiśabdābhidheyā bhaveyuḥ tadā stuti-
sādhanatvenopadeśāt stutisiddha‍yarthamākṣipyeran, yadi vā stobhaiḥ vinā ṛgakṣarāṇi na
stutiṃ kuryuḥ; na caitadubhayamastīti na pradeśaḥstobhānām ।</p>
<p>atrocyate---<q>gītyatideśādeva stobhānāmapyatideśaḥ svarāṇāmiva</q> ।
yathā svarāṇāṃ gītyatideśe gīti1bāhyānāmatideśastathā stobhānāmapi । <q>nanu ca stutya-
rthatvānabhidhānānniṣprayojanatā stobhātideśasya</q> । svarāṇāṃ tvarthapratītāvupayogāt
saprayojana evātideśaḥ । uttaraṃ---<q>satyamabhidhāne niṣprayojanatā gīti-
niṣpattireva prayojanaṃ stobhānāṃ tenābhidhāne nāsti prayojanam</q> ।</p>
<p><q>nanu cākṣarābhivyaktireva gītirityuktam । abhidhānārthaṃ cākṣarāṇya-
bhivyajyante । na ca taiḥ stutyabhidhānaṃ sādhyata ityuktam । tasmāt niṣpra-
yojanā gītirapi na niṣpādyā</q> । asyārthaḥ-stobhā na stutiṃ sādhayanti kintu
ṛgakṣarāṇyeva । gītiścākṣarābhivyaktirūpā stutau viniyuktā । tatra yānyakṣarāṇi stutiṃ
kurvanti tad‌dvāreṇa tasyāḥ stutisādhanatvam । sāca gītiḥ ṛgakṣaraiḥ vyaṅgyaiḥ
sampāditeti stobhasampādyo gītibhāgaḥ niṣprayojano naivottarayoḥ kartavyaḥ । <q>ucyate ।
satyamevaṃ yadi tāvadabhidhānākṣarābhivyaktyaiva sāmno guṇabhāvaḥ yadyarthābhi-
dhānākṣarābhivyakta‍yātmakasyaiva sām‍no guṇabhāvaḥsyāt tadā gītibhāgasya
syānniṣprayojanatā, kintu svādhyāya eva saṃskārakarmatā sām‍no vijñātā ।
bhavatvevaṃ tathāpi kimityāha---<q>atastathābhūtasyaiva karmaṇi viniyuktasya sāmnaḥ</q>
<note>1. R. vācyānā</note>
﻿<pb n="271"/>
<q>saṃskriyamāṇadvāreṇaiva kāryaṃ labdha(mapi)miti</q> karmaṇyapi nādṛṣṭakalpanā । yāvati
punarbhāge dṛṣṭaṃ na sambhavati tasya tasminnevādṛṣṭopakāraḥ kalpayitavyaḥ sviṣṭakṛdādīnāmiva
dravyadevatāgata ityuktam । tasmāda(ta)dṛṣṭārthatvāt kāryābhāvānna gītyaṃśāvalopaḥ
śakyate vak‍tum । anavalupte ca gītyaṃśe tanniṣpādakatayā stobhānāmapi pradeśo yuktaḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu yāvataiva bhāgena kāryaniṣpattiḥ tāvata eva pradeśo yukta ityatrāha---
<q>pradeśottarakālaṃ hi kāryaṃ, sām‍ni ca pradiṣṭe sati yāvato bhāgasya dṛṣṭaṃ kāryaṃ
nāsti tāvato'dṛṣṭaṃ kalpyate</q> ।</p>
<p>nanu stutikāryākṣepeṇa sāmapradeśa iti yāvata eva bhāgasya stutikāryatā1
tāvata evākṣepo yukta ityatrāha---<q>prakṛtyartha evāyaṃ pradeśo na kṛtakāryasya
prakṛtau vikṛtau</q> । asyārthaḥ---yatraiva karmaṇi sāmopadiṣṭaṃ tasminnevāyaṃ kāryeṇākṣepaḥ ।
tatra yatsāma tasyaivākṣepo yuktaḥ tathābhūtasyaivopadiṣṭatvāditi tataḥ stobhanivṛttyabhāvāt
<q>stobhanirvṛttyartha</q>sāmabhāgasyāpyatideśe ca kāryakalpanetyata upādānaṃ stobhākṣarāṇāṃ
sāmapadārthasiddha‍yarthaṃ na śakyaṃ vārayitum । tasmāt stobhapradeśasiddhiḥ । śeṣamuktam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 11 ।। adhikaṃ ca vivarṇaṃ ca jaiminiḥ stobha-
śabdatvāt ।। 39 ।।</l></lg>
<p>stobhapradeśaprasaṅgenedaṃ lakṣaṇamucyate adhikaṃ ca vivarṇaṃ ca jaiminiriti । tenā-
saṅgatirnāsti । ubhayopādānaprayojanaṃ bhāṣyoktamanubhāṣate---<q>bhavati kiñcidadhikaṃ</q>---
na vivarṇaṃ yathāśvādririti । tasya stobhatā mābhūditi vivarṇegrahaṇam । bhavati kiñcit
vivarṇaṃ nābhyadhikaṃ, yathā ognāī iti tannivṛttyarthamadhikagrahaṇam । idamākṣipāti---
<q>nanu cargakṣarebhyo'dhikaṃ adhikamityuktam । nacābhyāsasya ṛgakṣarebhyo'dhi-
katāstīti</q> । tenādhikamityetāvatyapi kṛte'bhyāsasya stobhatvāprasakteḥ tannivṛttyartha-
tvābhāvāt vivarṇatā kvopayujyate ? adhikatvādeva hi tat labhyate 3yāvadvivarṇagrahaṇena
sādhyam । atha vivarṇagrahaṇasya hyabhyāsasya stobhatvaṃ mābhūditi prayojanam । taccādhika-
grahaṇādeva labhyate abhyāsasya ṛganadhikatvāt ।</p>
<note>1. R stutikāritā</note>
<note>2. R yadvivarṇagrahaṇaṃ sādhyaṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="272"/>
<p>nanu bhavatyadhikaṃ śvādriḥśvādririti । naitadadhikam । na hyabhyāsādakṣarādhikyaṃ
bhavati । tenādhikasya stobhatvamityetāvatyapyukte nā/?/styabhyāsasya stobhatvaprasaktiḥ ।
samādhatte-<q>evaṃ tarhyabhidhānādhikyamātramabhipretaṃ nākṣarādhikyam</q> । abhyāsarahita-
syābhidhāyakatvāt (asyāpi cābhidhānādhikyamasti) abhyāsasyānabhidhānānanupraveśāt ।</p>
<p>nanu kimityabhidhānādhikyamevāśrīyata ityatrāha---<q>yuktaṃ caidevaṃ yadabhidhā
nādhikyamiti gṛhyate</q> । kasmādyuktamityāha---<q>abhidhānādevādhikyaṃ śakyate
vak‍tum nābhidhānanirapekṣādakṣarāṇāṃ parigaṇanāt</q> । na hi svarūpeṇādhikyamavagantuṃ
śakyate । abhidhānavaśena tu abhidhānānupayogino'dhikatvamiti śakyāvagamam ।</p>
<p><q>nanu chandastopyādhikyaṃ vijñāyata eva । satyamevaṃ, chandaḥparijñāna-
namapyabhidhānādṛte na śakyate vijñātum</q> । arthāvacchedena hi varṇān gṛhītvā
chandaḥparijñānaṃ śakyate kartuṃ nānyathā । tenābhidhānavyatirekeṇa ādhikyajñānaṃ nāsti
abhidhānādhikamevādhikam । tasmāt suṣṭhūcyate yadabhidhānākṣarebhyo'dhikavarṇāste
stobhā iti । evaṃ cocyamāne'bhyāsasyāpi stobhatvaprasaktirastīti tannivṛttyarthaṃ
vivarṇagrahaṇam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 12 ।। dharmasyārthakṛtatvād dravyaguṇavikāravyatikramapratiṣedhe
codanānubandhaḥ samavāyāt ।। 40 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nanu cedaṃ sthitaṃ kāryāpattyā dharmalābha iti । tena pūrvapakṣābhāvādanāra-
bhyamidamadhikaraṇam</q> । pariharati---<q>bāḍham</q> । ākṣeptā pṛcchati---<q>kimarthaṃ
tarhīdamadhikaraṇamārabhyate</q> ? uttaraṃ---<q>kāryāpattireva nīvārādīnāmasti nāstīti
cintyate । nanu kathaṃ punaratra kāryāpattāveva saṃśayaḥ</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>naivāraścaru-
riti śrūyate na punaḥ vrīhīṇāṃ 1sthāne nīvārā iti</q> । punarākṣipati---<q>yadi
vrīhīṇāṃ sthāne nīvārā na bhavanti kathaṃ punaranyathā naivāraścarurbhavatīti</q> । yathā
vrīhīṇāṃ taṇḍalanirvṛttyarthatā tathā nīvārāṇāmapi taṇḍulaniṣpattidvāreṇaiva nīvārāṇāṃ
carurbhavati । samādhatte---<q>arthāttarhīdamāpadyate na punaḥ kārye vidhissambhavati</q>
nānyathā nīvārasambandhaścarorbhavati ityarthāt vrīhikārye pāto nīvārāṇāṃ2 na punaḥsākṣā-
<note>1. R anyathā---</note> <note>2. R kārye āpattiḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="273"/>
cchabdenaiva tatkārye vidhānaṃ yathā paridhau paśuṃ niyuñjantīti । rāddhāntasammatyā
vaidharmyadṛṣṭānto'yam । na cārthaprāptaṃ tatkāryamiti śakyate vak‍tum । anyenāpi
prakāreṇa carornīvārasambandhasambhavāt nīvārakrītavrīhisādhyatvepi hi tatsambandhasambha-
vāt । yathā paṇasahasrakrītahemanirmite kaṭake sambhavanti vaktāraḥ paṇasahasrasyāyaṃ
kaṭaka iti । tasmāt kāryāpattyasambhavānna taddharmā bhavitumarhantīti pūrvapakṣavādino
'bhiprāyaḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu madhvaśanaghṛtāśane ṣaḍahāṅgameva na ṣaḍahanivṛttau vidhīyete kathamiyaṃ cintā ?
yadi ṣaḍahapravṛttau tayorvidhānaṃ syāt tadā'tra yukteyaṃ cintā kiṃ ṣaḍahakārye vidhirneti
tayostu ṣaḍahā[na]ṅgatvena kathamiyaṃ cintā । pariharati---<q>kimanayā'smākaṃ nirṇītayā
lakṣyāviṣayayā cintayā</q> । lakṣaṇānvākhyānaṃ tvatraiva ṣaḍahanivṛttau tayorvidhānamiti
kṛtvā cintyate tena nāsti doṣaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>kathaṃ punaratra madhvaśanaghṛtāśanayoḥ pūrvapakṣaḥ</q> yāvatā ṣaḍahanivṛttau tayo-
rvidhānamiti kṛtvā yadyeṣā cintā tadā tatkārya eva vidhānaṃ pratibhāti । uttaraṃ---
<q>saṃsthite ṣaḍahe nivṛtte ṣaḍahe madhvaśanaṃ ghṛtāśanaṃ ceti śrūyate । natu tatkārya
ityevam</q> । nakhāvayūtānāmityārthaṃ tuṣakaṇavimokaṃ kārye nakhānāṃ manyate । nacārthātta-
deva kāryamiti śakyate vak‍tum । anyenāpi prakāreṇa nakhānāmavapūte vyāpārasambhavāt
nakhairgṛhītvolūkhale'vahantuṃ nikṣepāt । paridhau paśuṃ niyuñjantītyatra kathaṃ pūrvaḥpakṣa ?
sākṣādyūpakārye vidhānāt । uttaraṃ---<q>atrāpi yanniyojanaṃ yūpe tatparidhau kartavya-
mityaśravaṇaṃ manyate</q> । niyojanāntaramevedaṃ kasmānna bhavatītyarthaḥ । airaṃ kṛtvodgeyamiti
na girāpadakāryamukheneti śrutirasti iti akṣarāntarasthānanipātenāpyudgānasambandhasaṃmbha-
vānna pāriśeṣyādapi girāpadasthāne nipātaḥ śakyate'vagantumiti pūrvapakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu naivāraścaruriti naivārasambandhe taddhita upapadyate'nyatra
prakṛtivikṛtibhāvāt</q> । asyārthaḥ---vaikṛto'yamupadeśaḥ sa carusthāne niyataḥ klṛpta-
kāryāśrayaḥ1 । klṛptaṃ ca prakṛtau vrīhikāryamiti na punaridaṃ(paraṃ)kāryāntaraṃ, tena
tatraivāyaṃ nīvārāṇāṃ vidhiriti prakṛtivikāralakṣaṇa evāyaṃ nīvārāṇāṃ carośca sambandha-
staddhitenocyate । tasmāt vrīhikāryāpattirnīvārāṇāṃ tadāpattau ca taddharmaprāptiḥ । tathā
<note>1. kāryāpekṣaḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="274"/>
madhvaśanaghṛtāśane na1 naimittikatayā saṃsthānasya sambhavato'nyatrādhikārānvayāt । yāva-
dadhikārānvayitā ṣaḍahasaṃsthānasya sambhavati tāvannaiva nimittatopapattiradhikāriviśeṣaṇa-
syaiva nimittatvasambhavāt । adhikāraśceha ṣaḍaha(hā)karaṇavataḥ satriṇaḥ tadārabdha-
kāryāntarepi । viniyogāntare [na]viṣayabhedabhinnaṣaḍahakāryāpattiradhikāraniyogalakṣaṇa eva
kāryāpattiḥ । tataśca prayojanaśūnyānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ paramāpūrvaprayuktānāṃ prāptiḥ । evaṃ nakhāva-
pūtepi kāryāpattiḥ? kuta ityāha---<q>avapūtatā ca phalena saha sambandhaḥ upapadyate'-
nyatra kriyākaraṇāt</q> । tasmādatrāpi kṛptakāryāśritatvāt vaikṛtānāmupadeśānāṃ
nakhānāmapi tuṣakaṇavimoka eva sambandhaheturiti kāryāpattiḥ । paridhau paśuṃ niyuñjantīti
niyojanasyāvidhānāt kimanyadato yūpakāryādavagamyate । yadi niyojanaṃ vidhīyeta
tadā na syādapi kāryāpattiḥ । na ceha niyojanaṃ vidhīyate prakṛtitaḥ prāptatvāt ।
tataśca yūpakāryāpattiriti taddharmaprāptiḥ ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ na girāgiretyanenaikavākyatvāt giraṇasya cāsambhavāt na
girāpadakāryādṛte dvayamupapadyata iti kāryāpattiḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---na giretyanena
saha airaṃ kṛtvetyasyaikavākyatvaṃ pratīyate । taccaivamupapadyate yadi girāpadakārya everāpadaṃ
vidhīyate tadā hi kṛtakāryatayā girāpadanivṛttiḥ । sā prāptā satī anūdyate anyathā
sāpi vidheyaiva syāditi vākyabhedaprasaṅgaḥ । tenaikavākyatvabalena girāpadakārya everāpadaṃ
kathaṃ nāma pratīyatāmityevamarthameva na girāgireti brūyādityucyate । na ca śakyamātma-
giraṇalakṣaṇadoṣo'bhidhīyata iti, asambhavāt । yadi ātmaśabdena śarīramevātma-
sambandhāllakṣaṇayocyate, yadi vā ātmaiva śrutyā ubhayathāpi giraṇāsambhavāt । tasmāt
girāpadakārya everāpadasya vidhāne dvayamidamekasmin vākye upapadyate । na girā gireti
brūyāt airaṃ kṛtvodgayamiti kāryāpattestaddharmalābhaḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 13 ।। tadutpattestu nivṛttistatkṛtatvāt syāt ।। 41 ।।</l></lg>
<p>paridhau punarākṣepaḥ anyārthasya sataḥ yatkāryāntarakaraṇaṃ na tat dharmaprāp‍tau hetuḥ ।
yadyapi yūpakārye paridhervidhānaṃ tathāpi viniyuktaviniyogavirodhāt paridherniyojanaṃ prati
aṅgabhāvo nāsti, nāpi niyojanadvāreṇa paśuyāgāpūrvaṃ prati ।</p>
<note>1. R omits na</note>
﻿<pb n="275"/>
<p>nanu 1puroḍāśakapālanyāyena kimiti adhiṣṭhānalakṣaṇayā viniyuktāvasthā-
parihāreṇāṅgatvenaivābhidhānaṃ nāśrīyate । atha śrutyanugrahāya kārakatāmātreṇa vidhānaṃ
puroḍāśakapālepi kimiti na syāt ।</p>
<p>atra prābhākarapravarāḥ pra(tyā)cakṣate-paridhau paśuṃ niyuñjantīti vikṛtāvidaṃ
vidhānaṃ nāśrīyate । atha śrutyanugrahāya klṛpte ca kārye vaikṛto vidhiḥ । klṛptaṃ pūrvasamba-
ndhyeva niyojanaṃ kāryamiti tatraiva tathābhūte sādhanatvamātreṇāpi paridhervidhānamupapadyate ।
tathābhūte hi tasmin sādhanatā paridhe2rna pramāṇāntareṇa samadhigamyate iti tatra vacanaṃ
bhavati pramāṇam । apūrvasya ca prayuktiḥ tena kārakatvamātreṇaiva apūrvasambandhi-
niyojane paridhervidhānaṃ(sādhana)viśeṣaṇaviśiṣṭatayā ca niyojanasya vākyenaiva pratipādya-
tvāt viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvena guṇapradhānabhāvamāśrityaikavākyatopapattiḥ । adhiṣṭhāna-
lakṣaṇādoṣeṇāṅgatvena vidhānaṃ nāśrīyate । puroḍāśakapālavidhānaṃ tu prakṛtāviti na
klṛptakāryāśrayo'sau vyapadeśaḥ, kintu padārthāpekṣaḥ tatra puroḍāśakapālo yadyapūrvaṃ prati
prathamamevaidamarthyenānvayaṃ na yāyāt tadā padārthasvarūpamātrasambandhyeva syāt । tathā ca
vākyasyāprāmāṇyaṃ prayuktyabhāvaśca । na ca tasyaidamarthyaṃ tadīyaidamarthyamantareṇa pramātuṃ
śakyate । na ca lakṣaṇāmantareṇārthāntaraṃ pratyaidamarthyena viniyogo ghaṭata iti
balādadhiṣṭhānalakṣaṇā āśrīyate । tatra tena siddhaṃ sādhanamātreṇa vidhānaṃ anaṅgatvaṃ ca
paridheḥ । yacca tadanaṅgasya sataḥ kāryakaraṇatvaṃ na tat dharmaprayuktau heturbhavatīti paridhau
punarākṣepaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>kasmāt ?</q> uttaraṃ---<q>aidamarthyanibandhanaṃ hi dharmajātaṃ</q> prakṛtāvupalabdham
ya eva hi niyogaṃ pratyaidamarthyāpannaḥ tasyaiva dharmasambandhaḥ prakṛtau dṛṣṭa iti vikṛtāvapi
tathaiva bhavitavyam । <q>tena nāṅge yūpakāryāpanne'pi dharmasambandhānupapattiḥ</q> ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntachāyayā codayati - <q>nanu caidamarthyamatra kāryārthaṃ naidamarthyārthaṃ---
asyārthaḥ - prakṛtāvaidamarthyaṃ vinā kāryakāritaiva nāvagamyata iti aidamarthyaṃ dharmasambandhaṃ
pratyāśritam । na punaraidamarthyameva dharmasambandhanimittam । iha ca kāryakāritāṃ vināpi
aidamarthyamavagamyata iti kimaidamarthyena । <q>pariharati-satyamevaṃ tathāpi naidamarthyamanta-
reṇa kāryasaṃsparśino dharmā bhavitumarhanti iti niyogavibhāgānnaidamarthyāpanne</q>
<note>1. puroḍāśakapālena tuṣānupavapatītivat</note> <note>2. R omits na</note>
﻿<pb n="276"/>
<q>dharmā bhaveyuḥ</q> tadā yaṃ pratyanaidamarthyaṃ tasya(vi)niyogāntarārthatvāt <q>niyojanaidamarthyaṃ
vinā paśuniyojanalakṣaṇakāryasaṃsparśino dharmā na bhaveyuḥ niyogaikyanibandha-
naśca dharmaniyama iti siddham</q> । asyārthaḥ---yadi dharmāṇāṃ pradhānānāṃ ca eka eva
niyogaḥ sādhyo bhavet tadā dharmaniyamo bhavati । anyathā hi aniyogārthatve dharmāṇāma-
niyamaḥ syāt । niyogārthānhi dharmānniyogaḥ prayuṅkte । yadi ca niyogasaṃsparśino
dharmā na bhaveyuḥ tadā teṣāmaniyogārthatve prayuktyabhāvaḥ prasajyeta । yata eva niyoga-
saṃsparśināṃ dharmāṇāṃ prayuktiniyamaḥ aniyogārthānāṃ cāprayuktiḥ ata eva paridhidharma-
viruddhānāṃ yūpadharmāṇāṃ takṣaṇādīnāmanavakāśaḥ । itarathā virodhino yūpadharmāḥ paśuyāgena
kimiti na prayujyante prayuktau viśeṣābhāvādityanenābhiprāyeṇāha---<q>anyathā hi
ko'yaṃ virodho nāma yūpadharmāṇāmananuṣṭhānahetuḥ । kathaṃ vā paridhyaidama-
rthyasya balīyastvaṃ yena yūpadharmāṇāṃ bādhaḥ paridharmaiḥ</q> । paridhyarthāḥ paridherdharmāḥ ।
yūpa/?/dharmāstu paridhau kriyamāṇā api na paridhyaidamarthyāpannā iti paridhidharmāṇāṃ balīya-
stvam taccobhayeṣāmapi svaniyogaprayuktatve sati nopapadyate । evaṃ ca sati yūpāyājya-
mānāyetyatroho na bhavati iti bhāṣyānubhāṣaṇaṃ ākṣep‍tum ।</p>
<p><q>nanu cedamayuktam</q> । kathamityāha---<q>ūhaḥ pratipādyate rāddhāntinā ।
tadabhāvaśca pūrvapakṣiṇo yuktiriti</q> । samādhatte---<q>anyāyya ūho na bhavatīti
1parihāraḥ । kathamanyāyyatvaṃ</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>sādhanabhāvena hi abhidhānaṃ
man‍trāṇāṃ pratipāditam । na ca paridhau niyojanasādhanatā'stīti parihṛta-
manyāyyamabhidhānamiti ayuktam</q> । asyārthaḥ---rāddhāntinā tūhamicchatā dharmoha-
vat man‍troho'pi vaditavyaḥ । tatra yūpāyājyamānāyeti paridhau mantre prayujyamāne
yūpābhāvāt yūpaśabdastāvanna prayojyaḥ । yadi paraṃ paridhiśabdaḥ sa ca prayok‍tumanucitaḥ
paridhiśabdena niyojanasādhanabhūtasyānabhidhānāt । sādhanabhūtaścārtho marntreṇābhi-
dhīyate । tadetad‌dūṣaṇaṃ paridhau yūpadharmāṇāmanūhe parihṛtaṃ bhavati ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate-atrāpyūhena bhavitavyam niyogaikye, niyogaikyaṃ
hi bhavati sambandhahetuḥ । upadeśena punaḥ kāryaprayuktatāṃ vārayati niyoga-
bhedaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ - upadeśena hi dharmāṇāṃ niyogaikyaṃ śeṣiṇo niyogaidamarthyasiddhau
<note>1. R abhiprāyaḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="277"/>
hetuḥ । atadarthatāpanne hi dharmāḥ sambadhyamānāḥ na niyogaidamarthyaṃ labhante, niyogaida-
marthyāpanneṣu sambadhyamānāstu labhante । kāryatastu dharmāṇāṃ prāptau niyogaidamarthyaṃ tāvat
pramitam । pramite tu tasminnanuṣṭhānāya kevalamāśrayāpekṣā sādhyaṃ cāśrayo dharmāṇāmiti
kāryaprayuktatā na śakyate vārayitum । tatkāryatā ca paridherupapāditā । tasmānna
dharmāḥ kartavyatayā śakyā vārayitum ।</p>
<p>idaṃ cādhikaraṇaṃ yūpakāryaprayuktā yūpadharmā na yūpotpattyarthā iti kṛtvā cintitam ।
yattvanabhidhāno(nāya)mantraḥ iti tatrocyate । kāryaprayuktatve sati sādhanāntarasyāvi-
vakṣitatvāt tathaivābhidhānamiti noho virudhyate,1 tathaivābhidhānasiddheḥ paridhānasādhanasyā-
vivakṣitatvāt niyojanasādhanasya vivakṣitatvāt yūpaśabdena tasyābhidhātuṃ śak‍teḥ nohaḥ
kartavyaḥ । <q>yadi paśuniyogo yūpadharmān prayuṅk‍te kathaṃ tarhi satvaktvādī-
nāmanugrahaḥ ?</q> uttaraṃ---<q>tathābhūtasya</q> paridhi1bhūtasya <q>yūpakārya upadeśāt</q> na svarūpa-
vighāte tatkāryasamarthamiti tadavirodhidharmāveśa iti yuktam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 14 ।। parārthena tvarthasāmānyaṃ saṃskārasya tadarthatvāt ।। 44 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>iha punaḥ kāryacodanāpi nāstīti1 pūrvapakṣavādī paridhinānyatvaṃ matvā
dharmā na bhavantītyāha</q> । etadeva vivṛṇoti---<q>tatra hi paridhau paśuṃ niyuñ‍jantī-</q>
tyatra paridheḥkāryaṃ coditam । iha punaḥ na dadhani caruścodyate kiṃ tarhi ubhayaṃ
dadhitaṇḍule pradātre । ato na kevalamaidamarthyameva nāsti api tu kāryamapi na codyata
iti vaiṣamyam paridhānāt । atrocyate । kāryaṃ hi dharmāṇāṃ prayojakaṃ na codanā, tadeva
hi kāryaṃ k‍vacit codanāt yathā paridhau paśuṃ niyuñjīteti । <q>k‍vacidaidamarthyādyathā</q>
prakaraṇādhīteṣu mantreṣu liṅgaviniyojyeṣu śeṣiṇāmaidamarthyaṃ, k‍vacidarthādyathā'traiveti na
kaścit kāryakāritve viśeṣaḥ । kāryataścātra prāptiruditā nābhidhānaviniyogābhyāmiti
kārye'bhidhānaviniyogābhyāṃ dharmāśrayasya na dharmasambandhaḥ, kintu kāryayogamātreṇeti
nātra praṇītādharmaprāptiravaidikīti śakyate vak‍tum । tasmāt kartavyāḥ praṇītādharmāḥ
dadhipayasoḥ ।</p>
<note>1. R yujyate</note>
<note>2. R paridhirūpasya</note>
<note>3. nāpyastīti</note>
﻿<pb n="278"/>
<lg><l>।। 15 ।। ekārthatvādavibhāgaḥ syāt ।। 46 ।।</l></lg>
<p>sthitaṃ kāryaprayuktā dharmā iti । bṛhatpṛṣṭhaṃ bhavati rathantaraṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ bhavatītyatra
kāryabhedo'sti nāstīti vicāryate । tatra pūrvapakṣavādī pṛṣṭhaśabdavācyaṃ dvayorapyekakāryaṃ
manvāna ubhayatrobhayavihitadharmāveśaṃ manyate vrīhiyavayoriva । yathā vrīhiyavayoreka-
kāryakatvāt kāryaprayuktatvācca dharmāṇāṃ ekatrāpi śrutā dharmā ubhayatra bhavanti tathā
atrāpi pṛṣṭhaśabdavācyasya dvayorbṛhadrathantarayorekatvāt tatprayuk‍tairdharmaiḥ ekaikatra śrutaiḥ
ubhayatra bhavitavyam ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu upadeśe tāvacchabdabhedo vidyate bṛhadrathantaramiti</q> । dharmo-
padeśe bṛhadrantaraśabdopādānāt śabdabhedastāvadasti । śabdabhedācca vyavasthā'vasīyate
dharmāṇām । <q>kāryamekamiti cet</q> । pariharati---<q>dṛśyate ca kāryabhedaḥ anyathā
kavatīṣu stutirgamyate anyathā bṛhadṛkṣu</q> । guṇābhidhānalakṣaṇā stutiḥ sā kavatīṣva-
nyena prakāreṇa । anyena bṛhadṛkṣu । tena vyāpārabhedastāvadavagamyate । <q>pṛṣṭhaśabdā-
bhidheyatvamekamiti cet</q> । pariharati---<q>nābhidhānato dharmaprāptirityuktam</q> ।
tenābhidhānaikyepi na dharmavyatikaraḥ । kiṃ tarhi ? kāryata eva dharmaprāptiḥ kāryataścobhaya-
bheda upalabhyate bṛhadrathantarayorityuktam । karṣaṇachedanayoriva parvavibhāgaphalayoḥ ।
na ca phalato dharmā bhavantīti nīvārādiṣu darśitam । kintu kāryataḥ । tasmāta sarva-
kāryabhede sambhavati bṛhadrathantarayoḥ lakṣaṇā ayuktā । ato vyavasthayaiva dharmāḥ kartavyāḥ
vrīhiyavayoḥ puroḍāśaniṣpattau na kāryabheda upapadyate ubhayoḥ puroḍāśanirvartakatvāt
<q>anyathā yavamayaḥ puroḍāśo'nyathā vrīhimaya iti tatrāpi kāryabheda iti
cet</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>na sva/?/bhāvaprayuktā dharmāḥ kintu kāryaprayuktā ityuktam</q> । svabhāva-
ścātra bhidyate na niṣpattau vyāpāraḥ vyāpāraprayuktā dharmāḥ abhidhānavyāpārānyatvaṃ ca bṛha-
drathantarayoḥ pradarśitam । anyathā kavatīṣu stutiḥ anyathā bṛhadṛkṣviti । ato
vrīhiyavābhyāṃ vaiṣamyaṃ bṛhadrathantarayoḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 16 ।। aprākṛte tadvirodhādva‍yavatiṣṭheran ।। 48 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>sāmāntarasādhane vikṛtiṣu pṛṣṭhe cintā । kimekasya dharmāḥ kāryeṇa
kartavyā utobhayadharmā iti</q> । kiṃ vikalpena dharmāḥ kartavyāḥ uta samuccayeneti
sandehaḥ । <q>atra pūrvapakṣavādī prakṛtau kāryabhedāt ihāpi tadvaditi na prāptibhedaṃ</q>
﻿<pb n="279"/>
<q>manvānaḥ kāryeṇecchati</q> । asyārthaḥ---prakṛtau kāryabhedāt bhedena prāptiṃ manvānaḥ
pūrvapakṣī ihāpi kāryeṇa prāptiṃ tadvati necchati । anyathā tadvadbhāva eva na syāt ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu---tadvati kāryaṃ prāpyate nopāyāḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---prakṛti-
vadvikṛtirapyupakāravatī na punaḥ padārthavatī upakārasādṛśyaṃ hyetat tadvaditi । <q>na</q>
padārthasādṛśyamiti । etaddaśamādye darśitam । bhavatvevaṃ tathāpi kathaṃ samāveśo dharmā-
ṇāmityata āha---<q>upāyataśca prakṛtau kāryānyatvamavagatam</q> । ṛgbhedāt prakṛtau
stutivyāpāralakṣaṇakāryabhedo'vagataḥ । na cehopāyabhedo'sti upāyāntaravidhānāt ।
stutau sāmāntaravidhānena prākṛtarṅ‌nivṛtteḥ ṛgantarāpekṣatvāt tasya caikatvāt ।
tasmānna kāryānyatvaṃ śakyate'vagantum । ananyatve ca kāryaprayuktāḥ kena vāryante nakha
ivolūkhalamusaladharmāḥ anyatra virodhāt । yadi paraṃ virodhādeva dharmāṇāmakaraṇam ।
ato'viruddhānāṃ samāveśa iti sthitam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 17 ।। ubhayasām‍ni caivamekārthāpatteḥ ।। 49 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>atrāpi kaṇvarathantaravat ubhayamubhayatra yojyata iti pūrvapakṣavādī
manyate</q> । etaduktaṃ bhavati---<q>yat prakṛtāvupāyadvayaṃ vijñātaṃ tasya kārye
ihopāyadvayaṃ vidhīyate</q> । etadeva vivṛṇoti---<q>bṛhatkārye bṛhadrathantare,
rathantara kāryepi bṛhadrathantare । tasmāt samāveśo dharmāṇām</q> ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu upāyasamāveśaḥ pratyabhijñānāt</q> । asyārthaḥ-yau tau vyāpārau
stutiṃ prati bṛhadrathantarayoravagatau tāveveha samāviṣṭau pratyabhijñāyete । tenopāyayo-
re va samāveśo na kāryayoḥ । na ca samāveśaprayuktā dharmāḥ kiṃ tarhi kāryaprayuktā
ityuktam । tena kāryabhedāt yathāyathameva dharmairvyavasthitairbhavitavyam । tadidamuktaṃ
bhāṣye <quote>“sām‍nāpi dṛṣṭamadṛṣṭaṃ vā kriyata”</quote> iti । <q>upāyārthasamāptirdṛṣṭakāryaṃ</q>
stutirvyāpāraviśeṣalakṣaṇā upāyārthasamāptirdṛṣṭaṃ kāryam । samāveśataḥ kimapyadṛṣṭam ।
na ca prākṛte kāryasambandhe'vagamyamāne kāryāntarasambandho dharmāṇāmupapadyata iti
vyavasthaiva nyāyyā ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 18 ।। pārvaṇahomayostvaprabṛttissamudāyārthasaṃyogāt
tadabhījyā hi ।। 51 ।।</l></lg>
﻿<pb n="280"/>
<p>atra sūtre pravṛttiśabdaśravaṇādbhrāntaścodayati । <q>nanu ceyamatideśacintā ।
kaḥprasaṅgo'syāḥ ?</q> । kimanena niṣphalenoktena । bādho'yaṃ nātideśa iti matvā''ha
-<q>astyatra prasaṅgaḥ kāryapradhānatvādatideśānatideśayoḥ</q> । etadeva vivṛṇoti-
<q>yadi hi prākṛtadevatārthatā homayoḥ tadā sauryādiṣvapravṛttiḥ । athārādupakāra-
katvaṃ tadā pravṛttiḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ - prakṛtāni yāni karmāṇyāgneyādīni devatābhūtāni
parvaśabdābhidheyāni tadarthatā tatsmaraṇārthatā pārvaṇahomayoḥ syād tadā vikṛtiṣu
apravṛttiḥ, athārādupakārakatvaṃ tadā pravṛttiḥ prayājādivaditi kāryanibandhane pravṛttya-
pravṛttī vicāryete iti tadarthaṃ homayoḥ dvārakāryaṃ cintyate---<q>kiṃ devatāsaṃskāraḥ
kāryaṃ uta karaṇopakāra eva prayājādivaditi । iha cādhyāye dvārakārya-
cintaiva kriyate tannibandhanatvādūhasyetyasti prasaṅgaḥ</q> । kaścitatvaviccodayati
-<q>nanvevaṃ sati bādhacintaiveyaṃ prāp‍noti kāryābhāvānnivṛttiriti । kimiti
bhavān samādhātā'natideśamāha</q> । pariharati---<q>satyamevametat tathāpi kārya-
svarūpamevātra nirṇīyate'rthādvādha ityūhāntaḥ pātinyeveyaṃ cintā</q> । anāsthayā
mayā nirbandho na kṛta iti samādhātā darśayati---<q>sarvathā kāryacintārūpatvāt
saṅgatiḥ । arthādbādho bhavatu anatideśo vā iti nāsmākamāsthā</q> ।</p>
<p>atra kecinmīmāṃsakāḥ tantre svātantryamicchantaḥ svabuddhilāghavamanākalayantaḥ
bhaṅgamāpādayāṃbabhūvuḥ । nanu karmasaṃskārakatvepi homayoḥ kimiti bādho yāvatā devatā-
ntarepi paśupuroḍāśavadūhena pārvaṇahomau kartavyāveveti ।</p>
<p>atra <q>prabhākarapādasevānirastasamastajāḍyāḥ</q> samarthanamāhuḥ---kāryaprayuktā
dharmā ityuktam । yaccāgneyādīnāmavāntarakāryaṃ paramāpūrvaniṣpattiṃ prati na tat sauryādī-
nām । ata eva ca prakṛtāvāgneyādīnāṃ nānyonyadharmasaṅkara iti ।</p>
<p>atra pūrvapakṣavādī kālavacanatvepi parvaśabdasya kālayogāt karmaṇi prayoga
upapadyata iti kālavacanatvaṃ manyate ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu niyogaikyaṃ na siddha‍yatīti samudāyavacanataiva nyāyyā</q> ।
karmavacanatve hi parvaśabdasya tatsaṃskārakatvāddhomayoḥ tanniyogaikyaṃ siddha‍yati । itarathā
tu na siddhiḥ । niyogaikyaṃ ca gamyate prakṛtatvāt । śakyate ca samudāyārthatvepi karma-
vacanatvepi kāle prayogo vak‍tuṃ karmayogāt । yadi vā parvaśabdo'yaṃ yaugikaḥ pṛṇāte
<p></p>
﻿<pb n="281"/>
rdānārthatvāt tatra bhāvasādhanatve karmavacanatā । adhikaraṇasādhanatve kālavacanatā । tatra
prakṛtatvātkarmāṇāmiha karmaṇyeva parvaśabdaḥ prayukta iti niścīyate । tadāha-<q>yogādvo-
bhayatra parvaśabdaḥ । vidhyanupraveśastu viśeṣahetuḥ</q> ।</p>
<p>nanu karmavacanatvepi kimityārādupakārakatvaṃ na bhavatītyāha---<q>prakṛtatvāccā-
rādupakārakatvanirākṛtiḥ</q> । prakṛtakarmaṇāṃ saṃskārārhatvāt ārādupakārakatvanirā-
kṛtiḥ । <q>śeṣamuktam</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 19 ।। ubhayoraviśeṣāt ।। 57 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>prasaktānuprasaktamidaṃ kāryacintāprasaṅgena</q> । pūrvādhikaraṇe homayoḥ
karmārthatvaṃ prasaktam । tadanuprasaktaṃ cedaṃ bhedena pārvaṇahomau kartavyāviti ।</p>
<p><q>kaḥpunaḥ pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ ?</q> uttaraṃ-<q>prakṛtārthaṃtve sati ekani-
yogakatvādubhayamubhayatreti manyate</q> । ubhayatrādhikāraniyogaikyāt tadarthatvāccobhayoḥ
ubhayatrobhābhyāṃ bhavitavyam ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu vyavasthāyāmapyekaniyogāvirodhāt na kāryaśūnyasyānu-
ṣṭhānaṃ yuktam</q> । amāvāsyādevatākasya hi amāvāsyāsaṃskārakatvaṃ pauṇamāsīdevatā-
kasya tatsaṃskārakatvam । yatraiva tatsaṃskāryaṃ tatraiva saṃskāreṇāpi bhavitavyam ।
nānyatra । tasmādva‍yavasthaiva nyāyyā । na ca dṛṣṭe sambhavatyadṛṣṭakalpanaiva nyāyyeti
kāryāntaravirodhaḥ । na hyekasyaiva kvacid‍dṛṣṭārthatvaṃ kvacidadṛṣṭārthatvaṃ yuktaṃ, yenāmāvā-
syāyāṃ dṛṣṭārthasya homasya paurṇamāsyāmadṛṣṭārthaḥ prayogaḥ syāt । tathetarasyāpī-
taratreti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 20 ।। prayāje'pīti cet ।। 55 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nāmadheyākṣepamātramidaṃ prakṛtaprasaṅgena</q> । asyārthaḥ---yathā pārvaṇahomayoḥ
prakṛtadevatārthatve vikṛtiṣvapravṛttiḥ tatheha prakṛtārthatvepi nāsti vikṛtāvapi kāryasambhavāt ।
tena nāmadheyamātramihākṣipyate prasaṅgena prakṛtatvāt । yathā pārvaṇahomayoḥ karmadevatā-
rthatvaṃ tathehāpi samidādīnāṃ devatārthatvaṃ saṃskāryatvaṃ ca ।</p>
﻿<pb n="282"/>
<p>rāddhāntastu iha na tathā kalpanāmarhati samidādīnāṃ devatārthatve pramāṇā-
bhāvāt । karmavacanatvepi dvitīyāyā upapatteḥ man‍travarṇasyāyathārthatve pramāṇābhāvāt ।
tasmādupādeyaivātra mān‍travarṇikī devateti siddhamārādupakārakatvam ।</p>
<p><q>।। iti śrīmahāmahopādhyāyaśālikanāthamiśrakṛtau ṛjuvimalāyāṃ
pañ‍jikāyāṃ navamasyādhyāyasya
dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ</q></p>
﻿<pb n="283"/>
<p><q>ṛjuvimalāyāṃ</q></p>
<p><q>navamādhyāye tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ</q></p>
<lg><l>।। 1 ।। prakṛtau yathotpattivacanamarthānāṃ tathottarasyāṃ tatau
tatprakṛtitvādarthe cākāryatvāt ।। 1 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nanu ca ākṛtyadhikaraṇe ākṛtiḥ śabdārtha iti darśitam</q> । rāddhā-
ntitam । <q>tasya caitadeva prayojanam</q> ।</p>
<p><q>tajjātiviśiṣṭe saṃskārābhidhānaṃ yathā syāditi</q> । saṃskāraścābhidhāna
catajjātiviśiṣṭa eva yathā syāt । vyaktipakṣe hi sādhanamātravacanatā । prakṛtau
vikṛtau ca sādhanabhāvāviśeṣādanūhaḥ tasmādākṛtivacanatvasyaitadeva prayojanam-<q>kimatra
pūrvapakṣe'bhyadhikaṃ kriyate ? vrīhiśabdena nīvārāṇāmabhidhānāśakteḥ tacchabda
eva prayoktavyaḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu caivaṃ sati yadi vrīhiśabdenāvrīhijātīyasyābhidhānaṃ nāsti
teṣāmarthenetyatrāpi pūrvapakṣo na yuktaḥ</q> । yadi vrīhiśabdenājyasānnāyyayora-
pyabhidhānaṃ syāt tadā ājyasānnāyyayorapi auṣadhadharmairbhavitavyamiti pūrvapakṣaḥ sambhā-
vyeta । kevalam vrīhijātīyābhidhāne tu na sambhavatīti । pariharati---<q>anyadeva hi
tatra nirākṛtaṃ anyastatra pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</q> । kiṃ nirākṛtamityāha---<q>dhātvarthakarma-
vivakṣāyāṃ prayogāṅgatā na prāp‍notītyāśaṅkya tatra nirākṛtam</q> । vivakṣite
dhātvarthasyaiva karmaṇi vrīhyādau prayojanatvena svīkṛte adhikāravidhyarthatā na syādavadhātā-
dīnām । ato dhātvarthakarma na vivakṣitaṃ kintvārādupakārakatvamevetyāśaṅkya tatra
nirākṛtam । iha punaḥ na kāryāntaramupalabhāmahe prākṛtānmantrakāryāt । prakṛtau hi
haviḥ prakṛtidravyābhidhānaṃ mantrakāryam । ihāpi tadeva, taccohamantareṇāśakyamityūhena
bhāvyam । na cāsamavetārthatvaṃ yena mantrārthasya vivakṣitatvepi asamavetārthatvamagni-
vrīhiśabdayorgamyeta । tadapi nāsti । yataḥ samabetārthatvaṃ agnivrīhiśabdayoḥ sthita-
meva । ataḥ vaktavyamatra nirākaraṇīyam ।</p>
<p><q>tadidamabhidhīyate । satyamākṛtivacanatvaṃ śabdānāṃ sthitaṃ, tathā-
pyatra sādhanabhāvenābhidhānāta prakṛtivikṛtyoścāviśiṣṭatvāt tadbhāvasya</q>
﻿<pb n="284"/>
sādhanabhāvasya <q>nohena bhavitavyam । śabdārthatve'pyākṛtistadavasthaiva bhavati
sādhanatvalakṣakatvāt</q> । asyārthaḥ---prakṛtāvapi vrīhiśabdena na svarūpaṃ prakāśitaṃ,
kiṃ tarhi sādhanaviśeṣaḥ sa ca vikṛtāvapyaviśiṣṭaḥ । anyathā hi ūho'pi na
syāt । tataśca prakṛtāvapyākṛteraprakāśyatvaṃ sādhanalakṣaṇopalakṣaṇatvāt । vikṛtāvapi
na nīvārajātiḥ prakāśyeti noho yuktaḥ । nanūpalakṣaṇatve'pi vrīhyākṛtervikṛtau
tadabhāvādupalakṣaṇatvānupapatterupalakṣaṇasamarthanīvārādijātiparyupasthāpanāya jātyantaravacanameva
nyāyyamiti vaktavyaṃ, yajjātīyaṃ hi coditaṃ tajjātīyamevopalakṣaṇakṣamaṃ vrīhijātiḥ
nīvāravyaktiṃ na lakṣayituṃ kṣametyanyatprayoktavyam । na vrīhijātivacanaṃ prayoktavyamiti ।</p>
<p>pūrvapakṣī samādhatte---<q>atrocyate-syādevaṃ yadi nāntarīyakasya vivakṣā
syāt svajātyabhidhānenopalakṣaṇīyaṃ sādhanamiti</q> । prakṛtāvidaṃ nāntarīyakaṃ,
prakṛtau hi tajjāteścoditatvāt sannikṛṣṭamupalakṣaṇamiti nāntarīyakabhābaḥ । yadi punaḥ
jātyantaracodanā syāt na tadopalakṣaṇaṃ nāntarīyakatayāpi syāt । prakṛtau hi
vrīhijātīyaṃ coditaṃ vrīhibhiryajeteti । mantre'pi tajjātivācaka eva vrīhiśabdaḥ prayukta
iti sannikṛṣṭajātirupalakṣaṇam । yadi punaḥ tatrāpyanyajātīyaṃ coditaṃ bhavet mantre(vā)ca
anyajātivācakaḥ śabdaḥ tadā na sannikṛṣṭasyopalakṣaṇaṃ bhavediti । tadevaṃ sampannaṃ
sannikṛṣṭasyopalakṣaṇatvam । na ca tadvivakṣituṃ nyāyyam । tena sannikṛṣṭasyopalakṣaṇatva-
siddhaye na sbajātivācakaśabdoho yuktaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>kathaṃ tarhi vrīhiśabdena nīvārajātīyasyābhidhānaṃ ?</q> uttaraṃ---<q>yathā-
kathaṃcit</q> abhidhānakalpanā aindrīvat । tasmānnāntarīyakamabhidhānamavivakṣitam ।
ataḥ prākṛtayoreva śabdayoḥ prakṛtau prayogadarśanāt vikṛtāvapyabhidhānaṃ kalpanīyam
tayoḥ kāryataḥ prāpteḥ । śabdāntarasya na punaḥ kāryataḥ(yā)prāptiḥ nāpi prayogata
ityanūhaṃ manyate । samavetārthatvaṃ punaḥ upodbalakamevāsya pakṣasya yasmātsādhanaṃ karmaṇi
samavetaṃ vyakteśca sākṣāt sādhanabhāva iti lakṣaṇārthaiva jātiḥ tena nāntarīyakatvājjāteḥ
avivakṣitatvānna nīvāraśabdaḥ prayoktavya iti ।</p>
<p>yuktyantaraṃ cānūhe darśayati---<q>viniyoge'pi ca śabdānāmevopadeśaḥ</q> ।
asyārthaḥ-mantrasya viniyogo varṇaparyavasāyī varṇātiriktasya tasyābhāvāt yathaivāsau
kāryārthatve'pi prakṛtau na pīḍitaḥ evaṃ vikṛtāvapyasau na pīḍanīya eveti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="285"/>
prakṛtāvapi kāryārthameva mantraḥ prayujyate । tatra yathā sa eva śabdaḥ prayujyate tathā
vikṛtāvapi sa eva prayoktavyaḥ aṅgabhūtatvāt ।</p>
<p><q>atrocyate---bhavitavyamūhena । kasmāt ? kāryāntare śaktyantara-
kalpanāyāmagnyādīnāmaindrīvan‍nyāyo na vidyate</q> । kāryāntare abhidheyāntare
śaktyantarakalpanāyāṃ agna‍yādiśabdānāṃ nyāyo nāsti yathendraśabde । <q>kathaṃ nyāyo
nāsti</q> ? uttaraṃ---<q>prakṛtāvivātra</q> mantreṇātra sādhanaprakāśanaṃ kartavyamipi prāptam ।
tadidānīmabhidhānāntarakalpanayā, uta śaktyantarakalpanayeti vicāraṇīyam । <q>tatra
śaktyantarakalpanā na nyāyyā klṛptaśakteḥ śabdasya, prayogāntare punaḥ
śaktyantarakalpanā</q> agna‍yādiśabdaḥ klṛptaśaktiḥ tasya mantraprayogāntare punaḥ śaktya-
ntarakalpanā na yuktā । kutaḥ ? <q>tāvanmātrasyāprayogāt । yadi tāvat
tāvanmātrasya prayogo(na)bhavet tadā balācchaktyantarakalpanā syāta । na ca
tāvanmātrasya prayogaḥ kintu mantrasya</q> । tathāpi kimityāha---<q>mantrasya puna-
rabhidhānāntaraprakṣepe'pi na kiñcit dṛṣṭādadhikaṃ kalpitaṃ bhavati</q> । nābhidhā-
nāntaraprakṣepe hi kiñcit kalpitaṃ bhavati । śaktyantarakalpanāpakṣe tu sa eva doṣaḥ ।
tasmāt gauravācchaktyantarakalpanāparihāreṇa śabdāntaraprakṣepa eva nyāyyaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>nanu ca mantratvameva hīyate । ūhapravaranāmadheyānāmamantratvamuktaṃ yataḥ</q> ।
pariharati-<q>na mantratvaṃ hīyate । nimittābhiprāyaṃ hi tadamantratvaṃ nābhidhānābhi-
prāyaṃ prakṣepyasya śabdasya</q> tadamantratvamuktaṃ na punarabhidhāyakasya vākyasya abhidhāyaka-
tvamautpattika ityatroktam । klṛptakāryatayā prāptiḥ kāryavaśena mantrasyārthavattvameva yuktaṃ
samudāyāpannasya pratyabhijñāyamānatvāt । yata eva ca nimittamātranāśe mantranāśo nāsti
<q>ata eva ca pratinidherabhāvaḥ</q> sakalamantranāśe hi pratinidheḥ ātmalābho na nimitta-
mātravināśe sakalamantravismṛteḥ na śakyate tatsadṛśo jñātumiti । nimittamātravināśe tu
tattvameva mantrasya । <q>tasmāt abhidhānāntaraprakṣepo nyāyyaḥ</q> na śakta‍yantarakalpanā ।
<q>kutaḥ? abhyāsāpekṣatvāt</q> śakta‍yantarakalpanā abhyāsāpekṣā । yadi hi agna‍yādipada-
syābhyāso(na) bhavet mantrāntargataṃ tāvatprayujyeta tathā kevalamiti । tathā kevalavacana-
prayoge śakta‍yantarakalpanā avaśyaṃ kartavyā । anyathā'bhidhānāśakteḥ । nacācoditā-
bhyāsaḥ kārayiṃtu śakyate yatra śabdasyopadeśa iti । satyaṃ, sa tu kāryārtha ityuktam ।
kāryataścātra prāptirnopadeśataḥ । <q>tasmādyathākāryamabhidhānam</q> kāryānatikrameṇo/?/bhidhānaṃ
﻿<pb n="286"/>
āśrayaṇīyam । kāryataścātra prāptiḥ, kāryaṃ cātra nīvāraprakāśanam । na ca tacchakta‍ya-
ntarakalpanayā yuktam । anyathāpi tatsiddherityūha eva nyāyyaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>yatpunaridaṃ antarāgarbhiṇīvyākhyānaṃ kṛtvā punarākṣepo'nyathā ca
vyākhyānaṃ tatra yadyākṣepaṇīya evāyamarthaḥ kimityupanyastaḥ</q> । kimiti
tatparatvena sūtravyākhyānaṃ kṛtam ।</p>
<p>uttaraṃ---<q>upanyastastāvat upanyasanīyatvādeva</q> nyāyyatvādeva । yadi
nyāyyaḥ, <q>ākṣepastarhi kasmāt ? uttarasūtrāsambandhaparihārāya</q> । 1uttarasūtramasambaddhaṃ
syādityetāvatā doṣeṇākṣepaḥ na punaranyāyyatayā । <q>yadyasmin vyākhyāne
uttarasūtrasambandho na syāt asūtritaṃ tarhi pūrvavyākhyānam</q> । pariharati-<q>na
cāsūtritaṃ anekārthasūcanāt sūtrasya । tasmātkauśalapradarśanamidaṃ ākṣepadvāreṇa
sūtrakāreṇa (sya)kriyate</q> । sūtrakāreṇātraivādhikaraṇāntaramapi sūtritamityekenaiva
sūtreṇānekārthasūcanāt mahatkauśalaṃ sūtrakārasya pradarśyate । <q>śeṣaṃ saliṅgamuktam</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 3 ।। laukike doṣasaṃyogādapavṛkte hi codyate ।। 9 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>prāsaṅgikamidamadhikaraṇam</q> । yadyekaṃ yūpamityadi vyavasthārthaṃ vacanamiti
pūrvamuktam । idānīṃ prasaṅgenedamadhikaraṇamāyātam । <q>tatrāviśeṣāt</q> yadyekaṃ yūpamupa-
spṛśediti aviśeṣaśravaṇāt । <q>ubhayārthatāṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī</q> । puruṣārthatāṃ
kratvarthatāṃ ca manyate । asti tvayaṃ viśeṣaḥ laukike'dhikārāntarakalpanā । 2tasmā-
dvaidika evāstu iti pakṣāntaram ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntamāha---<q>klṛpta evātrādhikāro doṣaśravaṇāt</q> । arthavādābhi-
hito'pi doṣaḥ puruṣārthatve āñjasyenopapadyate । yukta‍yantaraṃ cāha-<q>iṣṭaśabdasaṃyogācca
iṣṭottarakālasparśaviṣayameva prāyaścittaṃ manyate</q> । ucchrayaṇādayaśca neṣṭottarakālāḥ
aparāmapi yuktimāha---<q>aparihāryatvāccocchrayaṇāderna vināpīti śakyate kalpa-
yitum</q> । asyārthaḥ---tasmādyūpo nopaspṛśya iti pratiṣedho'yaṃ puruṣārtha evopapadyate ।
<note>1. A uttarasūtrasambandho na syādi ।</note>
<note>2. A alaukikavaidike</note>
﻿<pb n="287"/>
kratvarthapakṣe vikalpaprasaṅgāt । na ca vikalpo yuktaḥ ucchrayaṇādeḥ aparihāryatvāt ।
puruṣārthaścet pratiṣedhaḥ tadatikramaprāyaścittamapi puruṣārthameva । tasmāllaukika eva
sparśane'yaṃ mantraḥ । <q>yattarhīdamuktaṃ praharāneneti punargaṇya[punardaṇḍa]śabdaḥ saṃbadhyata
iti tatkathaṃ ?</q> uttaraṃ---<q>itthameva yathā śrūyate tathaivābhiprāyaḥ ।</p>
<p>praṣṭā vivṛṇeti---<q>nanu ca syonaṃ ta ityatrāpi ekavākyatāparihāraḥ
prāpnoti</q> । pariharati---<q>bhavatyeva vākyārthāvagame</q> । arthapratītikāle tadapekṣaka-
tvāt । prayoge tu prayogāvasthāyāṃ tu sa mantrānta(tya)[ram] ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 4 ।। anyāyastvavikāreṇādṛṣṭapratighātitvādavi-
śeṣācca tenāsya ।। 10 ।।</l></lg>
<p>dvitīyatṛtīyapakṣayossāmyaṃ manvāno bhedapradarśanāyāha---<q>pakṣacatuṣṭayamatro-
panyastam । ādyastvayaṃ pakṣo, bahuvacanānta evāvikāreṇa pravartatāṃ</q> eka-
vacanānto nivartata eva । dvitīyastu bahuvacanānto nivartate ekavacanāntaḥ pravartate ।
sa cohitavyaḥ । tṛtīyastūbhayorapi pravṛttiḥ bahuvacanāntasyāvikāraḥ ekavacanānto
vikṛtaḥ । caturthastu ubhayorapi pravṛttiḥ vikāraśceti । <q>kā yuktiścatuṣṭaye ?</q> uttaraṃ---
<q>prathamasya tāvat pakṣasyeyaṃ yuktiḥ vikṛtāva</q>bhidhānākāṅkṣāyāṃ yadyavikṛtamapi abhi-
dhānaṃ na śaknotyabhidhātuṃ tadā dhikāraniyogo niyuṅkte । sambhavati tvavikāreṇaiva bahuvaca-
nāntasyābhidhānaṃ, prakṛtau pāśamātravivakṣayā bahuvacanāntasya prayogāt sādhudṛṣṭiḥ[ṣṭam]
prakṛtivacca dvipāśakāyāmapi vikṛtau tenaivāvikṛtenābhidhānaṃ sambhavati । ekavacanā-
ntastu ekasaṅkhyākapāśābhidhāyitvāt vikṛtāvapi saṅkhyābhidhānāyohitavyaḥ
prāpnoti । na ca tadyuktaṃ avikṛtenaivābhidhānasiddherna vikāraṃ prayuṅkte ।</p>
<p>dvitīyasyeyaṃ yuktiḥ tāmāha---<q>ūhavādyāha</q>---anūhavādinā nāprāptirekavaca-
nāntasya śakyate vak‍tum । pāśamātrasya vivakṣitatvāditi tvayaivoktam । tataśca
prātipadikārtha(ma)sya sambhavāt bhavitavyamekavacanāntena mantreṇa । na ca tasyāvi-
kṛtasya prayogassambhavati, anvitasvārthatvāt । prakṛtau samavetārthatvāt sa cedeka-
vacanānto vikṛtaḥ tadā sampannamanvitābhidhānam । etadeva vivṛṇoti---<q>samaveta-
prakāśanamiti hetoḥ kimananvitābhidhānena</q> । bahuvacanānteneti vartate ।</p>
﻿<pb n="288"/>
<p>tṛtīye tviyaṃ yuktiḥ । tāmāha---<q>ayamabhiprāyaḥ । tvayaivokta
pāśamātrasamavāyānna śakyate mantro</q> vinivartayitumiti tena bahuvacanāntenāpi
mantreṇa bhavitavyam । <q>nanu cānanvitābhidhānānna tena prayojanamastītyuktam</q> ।
pariharati---<q>nānvitābhidhānanyāyaprāptiḥ</q> anvitārthābhidhāyyayamityanena rūpeṇa na
prāptiryena tadabhāvādaprāptiḥ syāt ।</p>
<p><q>kathaṃ</q> tarhi ? <q>samavetābhidhānena prāptikamityuktam</q> । tulyaścāyamartha-
samavāyaḥ ekavacanāntaśca bahuvacanāntaśca mantraḥ pratīyate । na prāptirvārayituṃ
śakyate । ananvitasya prakṛtāvivātrāpi sādhutā bhaviṣyati । ekavacanāntasya punaḥ
<q>svārthenaikatvenānvito yaḥ</q> samavetaḥ pāśaḥ <q>tadabhidhānātta</q>dadhāyakatvāt tathaivātrāpi
<q>sādhutvama</q>bhidhāne sādhuteti hetorno(n)haḥ ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu mantradvayaṃ vikṛtaṃ prayoktavyam । nanu cāsamavetābhidhāyi
bahuvacanāntamantra</q> [ityuktam] । [tasya kathaṃ]sādhutā bhaviṣyatīti bhāvaḥ । pariharati
-<q>satyaṃ śakyata iha dvipāśake karmaṇi noktam । nanu ca prakṛtivatkuryāditi
ihāpi tadvadeva prāp‍noti</q> । prakṛtau vivakṣitaṃ samavetārthaṃ syāt । na caitattatra
vivakṣitam । kuta ityāha---<q>satyaṃ śakyata iha dvipāśake karmaṇi noktam । nanu
ca prakṛtivatkuryāditi ihāpi tadvadeva prāp‍noti</q> । prakṛtau vivakṣitaṃ samavetārthaṃ
syāt nacaitattatra vivakṣitam । kuta ityāha---<q>tatra hi pāśamantrānvayādeva
pāśārtho vivakṣitaḥ vacanayogastu prayogasādhutāsampattyarthaḥ । nābhidhānā-
nvayaḥ । (na ca) yadi ca prayogo'yaṃ sādhuḥ tadā sādhutve sati atrāpi
kena prayogo vāryate</q> । pariharati-<q>nātra śakyate sādhutāṃ vak‍tum</q> । kuta
ityāha---<q>sādhutā hi prayogādbhavati । aprayukte'pi lakṣaṇādvā</q> । tatra prayoga-
stāvat bahubacanāntasya pāśayornāsti । (pedikaṃ)[vacana]lakṣaṇāpi chandasi vidyate supāṃ
supo bhavantīti । nacohaḥ cchanda ityuktam । tasmādapabhraṃśa evātra bahuvacanāntaḥ ।
tena sādhutvāya dvivacanānta ūhitavyaḥ । atra pūrvaprayogāt bhinnalakṣaṇamuktamiti
matvā codayati---<q>kathamaprayuktasya lakṣaṇamiti</q> । apratyakṣaprayogasyetyabhiprāyaḥ
yasyāpi prakṛtau pratyakṣeṇa prayogo na dṛśyate tasyāpi lakṣaṇadarśanāt sādhutvamavagamyata
ityarthaḥ । <q>ataḥ prakṛtau prayuktasya pāśadvayamātre vivakṣite mantrārthe kimiti
vacanārtha ādriyate</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>sādhutvāyeti</q> brūmaḥ । vibhaktiṃ vinā na kevalasya
﻿<pb n="289"/>
sādhutvam । tathāpi kimityāha---<q>asādhoḥ pratiṣedhāt</q> । tathā gatārthānāmapi
sādhutvāya laukikā vacanamādriyamāṇā dṛśyante devadattayajñadattābhyāmidaṃ kāryaṃ idaṃ
kṛtamityevamādiṣu । tasmāt sūktaṃ vikṛtayorapi mantrayoḥ prayoga iti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 5 ।। vipratipattau vikalpaḥ syāt samatvāt guṇe tvanyāyya-
kalpanaikadeśatvāt ।। 1 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>pāśamantradvayamudāharaṇam</q> । anena pāśamantrasamākhyāmutkarṣopayoginīmāha ।
<q>nanu codakaprāptaṃ bahuvacanāntapāśamantramāśritya vicāraḥ kṛtaḥ । nanu
prakṛtāvananupraviṣṭasya kathaṃ codakataḥ prāptiḥ</q> । ataḥ kathaṃ punarutkarṣāṃśaṅketyatrāha-
<q>arthāccedamadhikaraṇaṃ</q> ādhastyāt pūrvaṃ draṣṭavyam । etadadhikaraṇasiddhamevānupraveśaṃ
gṛhītvā sā cintetyabhiprāyaḥ । sākṣādasaṅgatatvācca pūrvamiyaṃ cintā na kṛtā । idānīṃ
pūrvādhikaraṇaprasaṅgena saṅgatiḥ । <q>atra pūrvapakṣavādī sakalavākyānvayābhāvāt
bahuvacanayuktasya mantrasyotkarṣaṃ manyate</q> । asyārthaḥ-liṅgaviniyojyo'yaṃ mantraḥ
tena yatraiva pāśabahutvānvitaṃ pāśonmocanaṃ prakāśyate tatraiva pāśamantrasamākhyayā
labdhasāmānyasambandho viniyujyate iti utkṛṣyaḥtava bahuvacanāntaḥ । nanu pāśavi-
muktyarthatvānmantrayoḥ bahuvacanaviniyuk‍tepi tasyārthasya sambhave notkarṣo nyāyyaḥ ।
<q>pāśavimoko'yaṃ mantrābhyāṃ prakāśyaḥ । bahuvacanāntenāpi mantreṇa śakyata
evāsau prakāśayitumiti kathamutkarṣaḥ</q> । pariharati---<q>satyaṃ pāśavimokārthaḥ
sa bhavati bahuvacanatyāgena tu</q> saḥprakṛtigatena । na cā (vā')nvitārthasya bahuvaca-
nasya tyāge pramāṇamasti । tasmādyatra karmaṇi sahānvayassamavetārtho'yaṃ mantraḥ tatrānena
mantreṇa bhavitavyam । athāpyavāntaravākyāśrayaṇaṃ syāt । na ca mahāvākye tada-
pāśrayaṇamastīti hetorutkarṣa eva nyāyyaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---prātipadikāśritaṃ hyatra bahutvaṃ pratīyate
vibhaktito'vagamāt na yathā saṅkhyāśabdādivat svatantram</q> । yathā saṅkhyā-
śabdena caturo muṣṭīnnirvapatītyevamādiṣu prātipadikasambandhanirapekṣā saṅkhyā vidhīyate
na tathā vibhakti[taḥ]pratīyate । vibhakti[śrutayaḥ]śrutyā'bhihitaṃ prātipadikāśritameva
svārthamāhuḥ । <q>tataḥkiṃ ?</q> uttaraṃ---<q>idaṃ tato bhavati</q> pāśārthāśrayi[yī] bahutvasyānvayaḥ
pratīyate । tathāpi kimityāha---<q>pāśārthaśca vimokasambandhitayā pratīya</q>-
﻿<pb n="290"/>
<q>māno'nena mantreṇa nābhidhīyata iti[na]śakyate vak‍tum । abhidhīyate cet
so'rthaḥ tadā tadarthatvānmantrasya tadabhi(dhāyakatvā)hito mantrārthaḥ yadi
viniyogāpekṣo mantrārtho bhavet</q> । yadi viniyogānapekṣo mantrārthaḥ, prātipadi-
kasthaliṅgasya prathamopanipātāt prādhānyāt prātipadikārthaviṣayasya vibhaktiliṅgāt
balīyastvāt ekasminnapi pāśe mantrasya viniyogāt bahuvacanamavivakṣitārthamantraphala-
miti niścīyate । viniyogataśca mantrārthāvagama ityuktam । anyathāhi kāryārthatā
mantrasya syāt । evameva yasya kasyacit anuvādaḥ prāp‍noti । tataśca sāpekṣatvaprasa-
ṅgādaprāmāṇyam । viniyogāyatte tu mantrārthe yāvatyeva viniyogaḥ tāvadeva prakāśyam ।
arthāntarasyollāpastu viṣabhakṣaṇavannāntarīyakaḥ ityanena nyāyena avivakṣita eveti
nāprāmāṇyam । tena viniyogāpannameva mantrārthāvadhāraṇam । yata eva prātipadikaliṅga-
nyāyenānutkarṣaḥ <q>ata eva prakaraṇamabhyuccayavṛttitayopanyastaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa</q> ।
yadi mūlayuktyantaraṃ na syāt tadā prakaraṇameva mūlayuktirbhavet । na ca tasya mūla-
yaktitvasambhavaḥ । śrutiliṅgavākyebhyaḥ aprabalatvāttasya । vākyabalenotkarṣo nyāyyo
yataḥ । kathaṃ punaḥ prakaraṇasyābhyuccayayuktitāpyastītyāha---<q>pratyakṣe hi kartavyatā-
vacanasambandhe'</q>dhikāravidhisambandhe <q>sambhavati nāpratyakṣeṇādhikāravidhinā
sambandho nyāyya ityabhiprāyaḥ</q> ।</p>
<p>upasaṃharati---<q>ata āśrayavaśādanuguṇavibhaktyarthaḥ pratipattavyaḥ</q>saṅkhyā-
śrayabhūtaikapāśānuguṇo vibhaktyartho vijñeyaḥ । <q>sa ca karmamātrapratipattiparo bhavati</q> ।
sahaikatvena ekasaṅkhyāyā avivakṣitatvāt karmamātrapratītiparo mantraḥ । yadi vā
saṅkhyā vivakṣitā tenaivaikatvena saha mantrārthaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>nanu sahapakṣe'rthāntaravacanatāpi kalpitā bhaviṣyati bahuvacanasyai-
katvamapi । bahuvacanasya vācyābhāva iti kalpitam</q> । tataścaikārthatvaprasaṅgo
bahuvacane'pi sambhavati । tataśca svāyattepi prayoge ekasmin bahuvacanaprasaṅgaḥ । pari-
harati---<q>na svāyatte prayoge prasaṅgaḥ aniyoge lokato'vagamāt</q> । ekatvādi-
niyamenaikavacanatādyavagamāt । tasmān prayogasādhutaivātrānabhidhānasādhutvam । kathaṃ
tarhi ekatvāvagatiḥ tatrāha---<q>karmamātravacanatvādapi ekatvasiddheḥ</q> karmamātre'vagate
nirapekṣatayā ekatvamavagamyate । dvitvādikā hi saṅkhyā apekṣābuddhinibandhanā । yata
ekasmin bahuvacanamavācakam ata eva ca lakṣaṇakārā api ekasmin bahuvacanamiti
﻿<pb n="291"/>
yat‍nāntaramārabhante । anyathā hi svabhāvasiddhatvādavācyaṃ syāditi । svabhāvasiddha-
tvānna na vācyatvam । kathaṃ tarhi bahuṣu vacanāprāptau ekasmin bahuvacanamiti smaraṇaṃ ?
prāp‍tyarthameva । tasmāt prayogasādhutaiveti arthe samanvayābhāvāt ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 6 ।। apūrve tvavikāro'pradeśātpratīyeta ।। 20 ।।</l></lg>
<p>iha punarekapat‍nīke prayoge svārthasambandhasambhavānna dvayorbahuṣu vā sādhutā
śakyate vak‍tum । pāśe hyananyagatitayā tathātvāśrayaṇam । iha tu gatirastīti na
prayogasādhutvāśrayaṇam ।</p>
<p><q>nanu cātrāpi prayogasādhutvāya bhaviṣyati</q> । pariharati---<q>na ekasmin
svārthasambhavāt</q> na [svārthe] sambhavati prayogasādhutā । tasmāt sādhutvāyaiva dvayoḥ
bahuṣu cohaḥ kartavyaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>atha kasmādekapat‍nīka evāsya prayogo na bhavati</q> । yathā vrīhipakṣe
syonaṃ te iti mantraḥ । tataścoktoho na yuktaḥ । pariharati---<q>naivamupapadyate sarvatra
prātipadikārthasambhavāt pāśavat sarvatraiva viniyogaḥ</q> । tatra hi yaveṣu samavetārtha-
taiva nāsti । iha punaḥ dvayoḥ bahuṣu ca patnīprātipadikasya samavetatvamasti iti na
vacanāntarānurodhena niyamaśśakyate vak‍tum । na ca samavetārthasambhave prayogasādhutā
vacanasyeti ūhena bhavitavyam । atrābhidhīyate---<q>na tāvadekavacanakārye dvitvaṃ
bahutvaṃ vā śrūyate nīvāravat</q> । yathā nīvārā vrīhīṇāṃ kārye vidhīyante tathā
ekatvakārye dvitvaṃ bahutvaṃ vā na śrūyate । <q>tataḥ kim</q> । uttaraṃ-<q>idaṃ tato bhavati ।
tadvatsamavetārthamiti na śakyate vak‍tum</q> । yathā prakṛtau vrīhiśabdaḥ samavetārthaḥ
tathaikavacanamapīti na śakyate vak‍tuṃ sarveṣāmekadvitvabahutvānāṃ samanvitatvāt । <q>nanu
ca prayogasādhutāpi na śakyate vak‍tum</q> । pariharati---<q>na śakyata eva vak‍tuṃ
prātipadikārthamātrasya sannahanayogāt dvayoḥ bahuṣu ca samavetārthānavagamāt</q> ।
asyārthaḥ---patnīprātipadikamātrasyāpekṣitasaṅkhyāviśeṣasya mantreṇa sannahanena yogāt ।
dvayoḥ pat‍nyoḥ bahuṣu vā ekatvābhāvāt ekavacanasya samavetārthatvānavagamāt ।
aviśeṣeṇaikasminnapi samanvayaśśakyate vak‍tum ।</p>
<p>ekatvapratipattyarthamidamekavacanaṃ na bhavati dvayoḥ bahuṣu ca tadabhāvāt । kintu sarva-
syāpi savyāpāratayā karmatvasambandhārthamiti । ataḥ prayogasādhutaivātrāpi iti na
﻿<pb n="292"/>
yopragavirodhaḥ । <q>nanu caikasmin samanvayo na śakyate parihartum</q> । pariharati---
<q>na śakyaṃ nāma prayogaviśeṣāt dvayoḥ bahupu cārthasamanvayāt prayogasādhu-
taivetyadoṣaḥ</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 7 ।। vikṛtau cāpi tadvacanāt ।। 21 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>atra svāyattaṃ prayogaṃ manvānasya pūrvapakṣaḥ</q> । yathā svāyatte karmaṇi
svāyattaḥ prayoga iti mattvā dvivacanamūhitavyam tathehāpi vikṛtau dvipat‍nyāmapi patnī-
śabde dvicanasyoha eva yuktaḥ svāyattatvātprayogasyeti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntastu prakṛtivat sādhutvasambhavāt [na]svāyatte prayoge pramāṇamastīti ।
yadi vaidikena prayogeṇa kāryaṃ na siddha‍yati tatra svāyattaḥ prayoga āśrīyate । pat‍nī-
śabdaścaikavacanānto dvitve bahutve ca siddhaprayoga iti na svāyattaprayogāvakāśaḥ ।
pāśe tu dvitve bahuvacanāntasya prayogādarśanādasti svāyattaprayogāvakāśaḥ । yatpunaḥ
bhāṣye tathaiva ca nāvivakṣā tadvacanenetyuktam । tadayuktam । pāśādhikaraṇavirodhāt
avivakṣitepi vibhaktyarthe yathārthameva vibhaktiḥ prayoktavyeti । tenātrāpi dvivacana-
bahuvacanayoreva prayogaḥ prāpnotīti pariharati---<q>yata evāyaṃ pakṣo dṛṣṭaḥ ata
evāthavetyuktvā</q> pakṣāntaramuktam pūrva[ā]paritoṣeṇa । tadva‍yācaṣṭe-<q>tadvadeva sādhutva-
sambhavāt</q> । yathā prakṛtau dvitvabahutvayorapi prayogāt ekavacanasya sādhutā pat‍nī-
śabde tathā vikṛtāvapyanūhaḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 8 ।। adhrigau savanīyeṣu tadvat samānavidhānāścet ।। 22 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>samānavidhānamiti kṛtvā cinteyam । anena viśeṣeṇa tadvadati-
deśo'yaṃ na viśeṣāntaraṃ vaktavyam</q> । samānavidhānaprayojanametadityarthaḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 9 ।। pratinidhau cāvikārāt ।। 23 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>pratinidhau vrīhikāryāpatteḥ mukhye ca vrīhiśabdasya samavetārthatvāta
ūhaṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī</q> । yadi pratinidhiḥ vrīhayaśca svātantryeṇopadiṣṭā bhaveyuḥ
tadā mantro na bhavedeva । vrīhikāryāpannaśya pratinidhiḥ vrīhiśabdaśca samavetārtha
iti yukta evohaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="293"/>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu na vrīhikārye nīvārā upadiśyante</q> । kintu vrīhyupadeśopa-
pattyarthaṃ kiñcidvikalaṃ vrīhyuddeśaṃ sampādayan nīvārāṇāmupādānam । na copadeśopapattau
kāryāpattiḥ tasmā eveti tadabhidhāna eva bhavitumarhatīti । tasmāt pratinidhāvapi
vrīhaya evetīha vrīhiśabdenaivābhidhānaṃ yuktam ।</p>
<p>samyañcamarthaṃ buddha‍yā coditi (?) tadevedamutpatitam । yadi pratipādyamapratipāditaṃ
nirākṛtaṃ ca । <q>adhyāsitatadbhāvo'dhyāropitatadbhāvo vā gauṇārtha iti</q> ।
adhyāso bhedāgrahaṇam । adhyāropo viparītakhyātiḥ । ubhayaṃ caitadayuktaṃ bhedena
nīvārāṇāmavagaterityuktam ।</p>
<p>svābhiprāyaṃ rāddhāntī vivṛṇoti---<q>nāyaṃ doṣaḥ bhūyo'vayavasāmānyenaiva
vrīhīṇāmevopapādanaṃ śaktitaḥ kṛtamiti</q> tadabhidhānameva vrīhiśabdena kriyata iti
[na]śabdāntarāpattiḥ । avayavaparyantatvādākṛteḥ sādhanabhāvasya । vrīhyabhāve'vikalā-
vayavopasaṃhārābhāvepi katipayavrīhyavayavasvīkārāya pratinidherupādānamiti vrīhitayo-
pāttānāṃ vrīhiśabdenaivābhidhānaṃ yuktam । na cādhyāropādhyāsau, tatpratyayādavayavāntara-
pratīteḥ । yadi tathaivāvayavo(pāyoḥ)pādānaṃ kimiti tasminnīvāropādānamiti tatrāha
---<q>tadva‍yatiriktasya vrīhyavayavavyatiriktasyātropādānaṃ</q> nāntarīyakam । tairvinā
vrīhīṇāmevopādānāśakteḥ ityadoṣaḥ । tasmānnāyamūhasya viṣayaḥ tatsthānāpattya-
bhāvāditi ।</p>
<p>atra pūrvapakṣavādī brūte---vrīhyapacāre'vaśyaṃ (a)mukhye karmaṇi dravyāntaropādā-
ne'vaśyaṃbhāvini sādṛśyena tad‍dravyopāditsāniyama iti । rāddhāntī tu upadeśenaiva
kevalaṃ sampādayituṃ sadṛśamupādīyata iti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 10 ।। saṃsargiṣu cārthasyāsthitaparimāṇatvāt ।। 27 ।।</l></lg>
<p>atra bhāṣyakāreṇaivamuktam---"nanu prakṛtāvapyanyāyanigada evāyam । dvayo-
ścakṣuṣorekavacanānto yataḥ tenoho na yukta" iti tadākṣipati---<q>yeyaṃ samavetārtha-
paricodanā naivāsāvanūhāyālam । kathaṃ ?</q>---uttaraṃ---<q>dvayorekavacanaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ
dvipaśukeṣu karmasu adhiṣṭhānabahutve asādhutaiva prāp‍noti pāśānitivat</q> ।
dvayoḥ pāśayoḥ pāśānityasādhu ekasmin darśanāt । tathā'tra dvayordarśanādekavavacanasya
bahuṣvasādhutā । <q>tasmānniṣprayojanaiveyaṃ paricodanā</q> । samādhatte---<q>ayamabhiprāya</q>-
﻿<pb n="294"/>
<q>ścodakasya । samavetatve punarūhaḥ kathaṃ syāditi</q> । asyārthaḥ---codakasyāya-
māśayaḥ---adhiṣṭhānabhedenāsamavetārthatvaṃ mayā coditaṃ, samavetārthasiddhaye pūrvapakṣavādī
tejasa ekatvaṃ nāsamavetārthatvamiti parihāraṃ vakṣyati । tathāpi dvipaśuṣvapi tejasa
ekatvāt samavetārthatvepi anūho bhavediti । evaṃ codanāṃ samarthya parihārabhāṣyaṃ
vyācaṣṭe---<q>tadidamayuktam । yadbhavatā coditamanyāyanigado'yamiti saṃsargi-
tvāttejasaḥ satyapyadhiṣṭhānabhede tatsamavetārthatvaṃ manyate </q>।</p>
<p>parihṛte codakaḥ svābhiprāyamāha---<q>ayamabhiprāyaḥ---eṣāmanayoriti vā
kṛte mantre asādhutā na śakyate vak‍tuṃ pāśānitivat iti</q> । vaidharmyadṛṣṭānto'yam ।
yathā pāśānityasādhutā dvayoḥ tathātrāsādhunā nāsti ekavacanāntasyāpi mantrasyeti
codanā । atra pūrvavādī sambandhibhedāt paśubhedāttejaso bhedaṃ manvānaḥ ūhaṃ vadati ।
tejodvaye tejobahutve ca ekavacanāntasyāsādhutvādūho yuktaḥ tejobhedaśca paśubhedāt ।
evaṃ pūrvapakṣite rāddhāntacchāyayā paricodayati---<q>adhiṣṭhānato vā kimiti
bhedo na vivakṣitaḥ</q> yadi sambandhibhedādbhedaḥ tadā adhiṣṭhānabhedādapi bhedaḥ
syāt । tataśca prakṛtāvapi kathamekavacanam । anyasya bhedepyanyasya bhedo nāstītya-
ṣṭhānabhedo na vivakṣitaḥ । tataśca paśubhedādapi bhedo na vivakṣaṇīya iti parihāra-
bhāṣyaṃ vyācaṣṭe---<q>anupādānādhiṣṭhānayoriti parihṛtam । asyeti punaḥ paśoḥ
rupādānamastīti</q> । asyārthaḥ---adhiṣṭhānanibandhano bhedo nāśrīyate tadavacchedena
tejaso'nabhidhānāt asyetyanyena tu śabdena paśorupādānāt paśvavacchedena tejaso'
bhidhānāt tannibandhano yukta eva bhedo vivakṣitum । tasmādūhaḥ ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntastu na śabdābhedādūho yuktaḥ । cakṣuśśabdasya yo'rthastejolakṣaṇa-
tasyābhedādekatvādūho na yuktaḥ । bhavatu sambandhinaḥ paśorbhedaḥ tathāpi na śabdānta-
rārthasya cakṣurādeḥ bhedo yuktaḥ । <q>śabdāntarārthasya paśorbhede yadi tejaso
nāsti[bhedaḥ] kathaṃ tasmin cakṣuḥ</q> [padaprayogaḥ] uttaraṃ---<q>adhiṣṭhānabhede lakṣaṇa-
yaiva</q> । bhinne'sminnadhiṣṭhānatvameva vivakṣitvā loka evaṃ prayuṅk‍te । cakṣuśśabda-
syādhiṣṭhānaparatvāt tatra tadabhidhitsāvagamāt । iha punaḥ sūryamasya cakṣurgamayatāditi
nādhiṣṭhānābhidhitsā'vagamyate prakṛtigāmitvādadhiṣṭhānakameva hi tadvacanam । nādhiṣṭhānasya
sūryaprakṛtitā kintu tejasa iti tatpuna[tpara]ścakṣuśśabda ityanūhaḥ । <q>liṅgamuktam</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 11 ।। ekadhetyekasaṃyogādabhyāsenābhidhānaṃ syāt ।। 29 ।।</l></lg>
﻿<pb n="295"/>
<p>idānīṃ cintyate---kiṃ yathā prakṛtau mantrārtho varṇitaḥ tathaiva vikṛtāvapi uta
prakārāntareṇāpi samavetārthānvayopapatteḥ varṇanīya iti । tatra [yadi]tathaiva vikṛtāvapi
tadā ekadhāsya tvacamācchyatāditi prakṛtau sakṛttvābhidhānāt vikṛtāvapi tadeva kartavyaṃ
ityabhyāsaḥ syāt ekadhaikadhā iti । anyathāpi yadi mantrārthavarṇanā tataḥ sahāyārtha-
tayā'nūha iti । tatra pūrvapakṣavādī viniyogāntara[vat] prayogāntarepi mantrasyārthāntaraṃ
na doṣāyeti manvānaḥ prakārāntareṇāpyanūhamuktavān । <q>nanu ca prakṛtivadityasyā-
rthāntarakalpanāyāṃ pramāṇaṃ nāsti [śaktyai] vopapatteḥ upadeśāntare tu pūrvasyānu-
papattikāraṇamarthāntaravarṇanena anyatrāpyanūho [bhavitā] tathā'nūha eva syāditi ।
pariharati---<q>ko'yamanūho nāma arthāntaravarṇanahetuḥ ?</q> uttaraṃ---<q>ārṣānugrahaḥ</q> ।
punaḥ pṛcchati---<q>arṣo nāma kaḥ</q> ? uttaraṃ-<q>svādhyāyakāle yatsvarūpam</q> । rāddhā-
ntyāha---<q>anugṛhītaṃ svarūpaṃ prakṛtau vikṛtau ca gauṇaṃ nāsti kāryatastu
tatprāp‍tyavagamāt yathākāryameva varṇanaṃ nyāyyam</q> । klṛptaṃ ca sakṛttvaprati-
pādanaṃ prakṛtau kāryamiti vikṛtāvapi tatsiddha‍yartha ūha eva yuktaḥ । upadeśe tu svarūpata
eva prāptiriti tadanurūpaṃ kāryam । bhavatu kāryataḥ prāptiḥ tathāpi kimityāha---
<q>kārye cārthāntaraklṛptau pramāṇaṃ nāsti prakṛtiklṛp‍tyaivopapatteḥ</q> । tasmādūha evātra
nyāyya iti nyāyavido manyante nārthāntarānugraham ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 12 ।। medhapatitvaṃ svāmidevatasya samavāyātsarvatra ca
prayuk‍tatvāt ।। 32 ।।</l></lg>
<p>atrobhayasya svāmidevatasya nimittatvopapatteḥ padārthatve ubhayaṃ svāmidevataṃ
mantrārtha iti manvānaḥ pūrvapakṣavādī prakṛtāveva bahuṣu dvivacanaika[vacana]darśanāt vikṛtā-
vapi prayogasambhavādanūhaṃ manyate । <q>nanu caikenaiva padārthena medhapatiśabdasya
nimittabhāvasya caritārthatvāt kathaṃ dva‍yarthatā mantrasya</q> ? yameva hi padārthaṃ upa-
sthāpayati medhapatiśabdaḥ sa evaiko mantrārtho yuktaḥ kathaṃ dva‍yarthatā mantrasya gṛhyamāṇa-
viśeṣatvāt । <q>dvayamapi medhapatiśabdenopasthāpyate</q> dviṣṭhānyapi vākyāni bhavantī-
tyabhiprāyaḥ । pakṣāntaraṃ tu satyaṃ dvayamupanyastam । yadi na gṛhyate viśeṣaḥ tatrobhayasya
nimittatvaṃ bhavadbhavet । gṛhyate tu viśeṣaḥ । svāmiparatve dvivacanaikavacanayorupapa-
tyā'rthau bhavataḥ । svāminyekavacanasya dampatyordvivacanasyopapatteḥ । na devatāparatve,
ekatvāddevatāyāḥ । tasmāt svāmiparo'yaṃ mantraḥ tadanusāreṇa cohitavyaḥ । devatā-
﻿<pb n="296"/>
paratvaṃ tu rāddhāntī manyate । evaṃ prātipadikārthoṃ na bhūtapūrvavṛttyā vyākhyāto bhavati ।
svāmino hi tad‍deyaṃ pratyāyitam । na ca bhūtapūrvaḥ sambandhaḥ[yuktaḥ] । na ca bhavatyarthe
bhūtapūrvāśrayaṇaṃ yuktam । yatpunaridaṃ gaṇābhiprāyamekavacanaṃ varṇitaṃ gaṇasyaiva devatātva-
miti smāritaṃ ekavacanāntasyānutkarṣārthaṃ tat pāśabahuvacananyāyenānutkarṣahetau
sambhavati ekasya hetoḥ kena hetunā ayaṃ sambhavati । abhidhānasādhutve prayogasādhutaivā
śrayituṃ na yuktam iti । pāśamantre hi bahuvacanasya prayoge sādhutā abhidhānasādhu-
tvā[t]sambhavati । agatikā gatiḥ । tenābhidhānasādhutvapradarśanāt gaṇābhiprāyameka
vacanaṃ varṇitaṃ, kiṃ prayojanamityāha---<q>ūhe ca viśeṣopapattiḥ prayogasādhu-
tvapradarśanārthatve bahiṣṭhadevatāsu prāp‍noti</q> । gaṇābhiprāyatve'bhidhānasādhutve sati
sa neti ।</p>
<p><q>nanu dva‍yadhiṣṭhānāyā devatāyā ekatvepi vacanamanupapannaṃ bhavati</q> ।
pariharati---<q>nānupapannaṃ ekena hetunā samavetārthatvena</q> । kutaḥ punassabhavetārthami-
tyāha---<q>dviṣṭhasyāpyadhiṣṭhānagataikyopapatteḥ</q> ।</p>
<p>nanu ca yadyapyadhiṣṭhānagatadvitvaṃ samavetaṃ tathāpi kārakagaṃ na bhavati tatprakāśane
mantrasyānarthakyaṃ ityatrāha---<q>samavetārthā</q>bhidhāne ca mantrasyārthavattoktā adhiṣṭhānamapi
smāritaṃ kārakaṃ smārayatyeveti bhāvaḥ । tasmāddevatāvaśādūhaḥ dvivacanāntasya adhiṣṭhāna-
bahutve ekatve cohaḥ ekabahutvayoriti sthitam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 13 ।। niyamo vā bahudevate vikāraḥ syāt ।। 41 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>atraikavacanāntamantrasya nivṛttiṃ manyate । ekavacanāntatayā ūhena
na tu pravartata eva । kathaṃ manyate</q> ? uttaraṃ---<q>dvitve hi ekavacanāntasyāyaṃ
prayoga iti bhrāmyato bahuṣu apabhraṃśaḥ sādhvekavacanamiti bahuṣvasādhutvā-
dūho yuktaḥ</q> ।</p>
<p><q>nanu saṃsargidevagaṇo devatetyuktam</q> । tenātrāpi tadabhidhāyakamupapadyata
evaikavacanam । pariharati---<q>syāt dvitva eva taditi manyate</q> । asyārthaḥ
-dvitve prayogaḥ sthitaḥ saṃsargokterityuktam । tenātrāpi dvitve vā saṃsarge vā tatraika-
vacanam na bahutva iti manyate । tasmāta bahuṣvapabhraṃśa eveti । nivṛttiḥ bhramaḥ yathā
pāśāniti dvayoḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="297"/>
<p>rāddhāntamāha---<q>pravarteta vā ekavacanāntameva</q> । kuta ityaha---<q>saṃsargo hyatra
vivakṣitaḥ (na ca) dvayoḥ bahuṣu vā saḥ</q> saṃsargamātraṃ hyatrāviśiṣṭam । sarvo hi
saṃsarga eka eva । tena tatra yuktamekavacanam । abhidhānavipratipattau hi
prayoganiyamo bhavati । na punassampratipattāvapi adarśanamātrāt anyābhidhāyino-
'nyatra punarabhidhānasampratipattiḥ yatraivābhidhāyakatvaṃ tatraiva prayogaḥ tatra tadvidha evānyatra
prayogadarśanamātreṇa niyamaḥ । kuta ityaha---<q>adya jātāyāṃ gavi gośabdasyā-
sādhutāprasaṅgāt</q> । na cāsādhutā tasmāt prakṛtivadatrāpyekavacanaṃ sādhu ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 14 ।। arthāntare vikāraḥ syāddevatāpṛthaktvāt ekābhi-
samavāyāt syāt ।। 43 ।।</l></lg>
<p>atra saṃsargamātrāviśeṣāt sādhutvaṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī । adhiṣṭhānasaṃsargo vā
bhavatu, devatāsaṃsargo vā । sarvathā tāvat saṃsargasyaikatvādekavacanaṃ sādhu iti ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu devatāsaṃsargaḥ [mantrārthaḥ] na saṃsargamātram</q> । aṅgatvāddeva-
tāgatasaṃsargo mantrārthaḥ na saṃsargamātram । tasyānaṅgatvāt । nanu anaṅgasyāpi samaveta-
tvādabhidhānaṃ yuktamityatrāha---<q>aṅge hi samavetārthābhidhānaṃ mantrāṇāmuktam</q> । na
sambhavamātreṇa । aṅge hīti <quote>‘nimittātkarmayoge’</quote> iti saptamī । tenāyamarthaḥ-aṅgārtha-
maṅgaṃ pratyāyayituṃ samavetārthābhidhānaṃ mantraiḥ kriyate । na punassambhavanmātrasaṃsargaḥ yāga-
bhedāt bhinneṣu yāgeṣu yā devatāḥ tāsāṃ saṃsargo na kvacit aṅgam । aṅgabhūtadevatārūpa-
prakāśakaścaikavacanānto mantraḥ । tasmāddevatābahutvādasādhvekavacanam । ata ūha
eveti siddham ।</p>
<p><q>nanu caivaṃ sati ākṛtyadhikaraṇākṣepaḥ prāp‍noti । kriyāviśeṣāṇāṃ
cābhidhānadarśanāt na tāvanmantrārthatā siddha‍yati</q> । asyārthaḥ---tathā kriyā-
viśeṣaṇatayaivābhidhānaṃ darśitam । evaṃ ca darśayatā akṛtyadhikaraṇamākṣiptaṃ bhavati ।
ākṛteḥ kriyāviśeṣaṇatvāsambhavāt anabhidhānaprasaṅgāt । samādhatte---<q>astyatra
viśeṣaḥ devatābhidhānatve prātipadikasya siddha eva ca nopapattyarthaṃ saṃsargasya
devatātvāśrayaṇam</q> । tena bhinnānāṃ yāgānāṃ yā eva devatāḥ tāsāṃ saṃsargo na
﻿<pb n="298"/>
devateti[na]man‍trasyābhidheyaḥ । tadabhidhāne man‍trasyā[na]nvayaprasaṅgāt । tatra punarā-
kṛtipratipattirevānvayahetuḥ sāmānyarūpeṇānvayāvagamāditi tatraiva prapañcenoktam ।
tasmānnāgṛhītaviśeṣaṇeti vā ito vā ākṛtyā samānāvevānvitā kriyāyāṃ na saṃsarga
iti siddhaṃ devatābhidhānamasaṃsargābhidhānam । tasmānnākṣepa ākṛtyadhikaraṇasya ।</p>
<p><b>iti mahopādhyāyaśālikanāthamiśrakṛtāyāṃ
ṛjuvimalāyāṃ pañ‍jikāyāṃ navamasya
tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ</b></p>
﻿<pb n="299"/>
<p><q>ṛjuvimalāyāṃ</q></p>
<p><q>navamasyādhyāyasya caturthaḥ pādaḥ</q></p>
<lg><l>।। 1 ।। ṣaḍviṃśatirabhyāsena paśugaṇe tatprakṛtitvādguṇasya pravibhakta-
tvādavikāre hi tāsāmakārts‍nyenābhisambandho vikārānna
samāsaḥ syādasaṃyogācca sarvābhiḥ ।। 1 ।।</l></lg>
<p>atra pañcapakṣā upanyasyante । pañcadhā mantrārthapratibhānāt । tatra paśupradhāno
mantrārtha ityekaḥ pakṣaḥ । saṅkhyāpradhāna iti dvitīyaḥ । vaṅkrīpradhāna iti tṛtīyaḥ ।
avivakṣita evetyaparaḥ, ṣaḍviṃśatisambandhitāparaḥ pañcamaḥ । asmiṃśca pañcame pakṣe
evaṃ sati sambandhitoktā bhavati ṣaḍviṃśatiṣṣaḍviṃśatiranayoreṣāṃ vaṅkraya iti ṣaḍviṃśati-
