pade'bhyaste paśubhyāṃ paśubhi[rvā]pratyekaṃ sambandhitā pratipāditā bhavati । vīpsā tu
vyāp‍tumicchā tena dvirvacanadarśanāt ṣaḍviṃśatisaṅkhyaiva paśusambandhitayā pratipādayitu-
miṣṭeti gamyate । yathā <quote>“puruṣaḥ puruṣo nidhanamupaiti”</quote> iti puruṣe ekavacanohaḥ
sthita iti pratīkānuvādo'yam ।</p>
<p>ṣaḍviṃśataya iti vacanohena saṅkhyāsvarūpasya gaṇanāvagamāt । saṅkhyā-
prādhānye1 pratītikaraṇatvenāviniyogādavivakṣaiva prāp‍noti mantrārthasyeti [a]vikāreṇaiva
prayogaḥ । yena hi mantreṇa smṛtaṃ kriyate[sa karaṇamantra] nayanakālatvādadhriguvacanasya
tenākaraṇatvādarthasmaraṇe'viniyogādavivakṣitārthamuccāraṇamadṛṣṭārthamityanūhaḥ । vaṅkrīprādhānye
samasya vacanam । samasya vacane hi vaṅkrīgaṇanā pratīyate । tena tāsāṃ prādhānyāvagatiḥ ।</p>
<p><q>kathaṃ punarviniyogavaśāt svīkṛte mantrārthe pañcadhā pratibhāyāt</q> ।
yāvatā yatraiva viniyogassa eva mantrārtho yuktaḥ । uttaraṃ-<q>prakaraṇamātreṇa viniyoga
mamanvānasya pañcadhā pratibhāti mantrārthaḥ</q> । prakaraṇamātreṇaiva mantrasya viniyogaḥ ।
na ca śrutyā, nāpi vākyena, samākhyayā, sthānena vā ।</p>
<p><q>nanu caitadayuktam---prakaraṇaviniyojyatve pañcadhā pratibhānaṃ uccāraṇa-
mātreṇaivāṅgatāsiddheravivakṣaiva nyāyyā । kvopayujyante'rthavikalpāḥ ?</q> pariharati
<note>1. nya-mā</note>
﻿<pb n="300"/>
---<q>satyamāha bhavān ācāryavānasi ! yadyapi prakaraṇaviniyojyatā tathā
pyarthālocanaṃ yuktameva</q> । kadācidālokyamāne mantrārthe kasmiṃścidarthe dṛṣṭārthatā
bhavatīti na liṃṅgaṃ prakaraṇena viruddha‍yate । prakaraṇasya sāmānyasambandhāpādakatvāt । 
liṅgasya ca viśeṣasambandhāpādakatvāt । liṅgena ca dṛṣṭārthe sambhavati nādṛṣṭārthaṃ
[pra]tyarthi(nī)bhavitumarhati mantrapadārthālocanena liṅgāt kvacilliṅgaviniyogo labhyo na
viniyogādityanekadhā mantrārthālocanā, tatra paśuprādhānye saṅkhyāprādhānyasambandhini
ca prādhānye'nyānuṣṭhāne kiñcidadṛṣṭenopakṛtam । yadi paśavaḥ pradhānaṃ yadi vā saṅkhyā
svarūpeṇa paśuviśiṣṭatayā vā pratipadyamānā pradhānaṃ tatprakāśanasyānupayogitvāt
(a)dṛṣṭopakāritā mantrārthasya na bhavatīti vaṅkrīyapradhānataivopakāriṇī । <quote>‘tā anuṣṭhyo
cyāvayatāt’</quote> iti sakaloddhāraṇāvagamāt vaṅkrīḥ anuṣṭhya prayat‍nena śamitāra ucyāvaya-
teti । anena sakaloddharaṇaṃ vaṅkrīṇāṃ pra(ā)tipadyate । <q>anaṣṭhānaṃ</q> anuṣṭhayā
prayatnaḥ parasyāstṛtīyāyā bhāvaḥ atassamasyameva vacanaṃ nyāyyam । etāvatīrvaṅkrī-
ruddharateti pratipādayitum ।</p>
<p>nanu atrāpi yugapaduddharaṇāśakteśca bahudhā vā'nupaklṛptameva samasyavacanam ।
yadi hi tāḥ samasya yugapaduddhriyeran tadā samasyavacanamupa(vṛta)padyata iti sūktaṃ
samasyavacanameva kāryamiti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 2 ।। aśvasya catus‍triṃśat tasya vacanādvaiśeṣikam ।। 17 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>atra pūrvapakṣaśaṅkā-kevalapadapratiṣedhabalena । [na]catustriṃśaditi brūyāditi
kevalaṃ catustriṃśatpadaṃ pratiṣidhyate । <q>na vaiśeṣikamevāsya vacanaṃ kartavyam ।
kathaṃ punarasmin pakṣe na vākyabhedaḥ ? catustriṃśatpadapratiṣedhāt ṣaḍviṃśati-
padavidhānācca vākyabhedaḥ prāp‍noti</q> । ṛk‌pratiṣedhe tu codakaprāptamantrānu-
vādo'yam ṣaḍviṃśatirityeva brūyāditi । tena[na]vākyabhedaḥ । uttaraṃ---<q>irāpadava-
dbhaviṣyati ityabhiprāyaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ-yathaiverāpade vidhīyamāne vākyabhedo na bhavati
tathā'trāpi nāsti ṣaḍviṃśatipadavidhāne prāpta eva catustriṃśatpadābhāvo'nūdyate ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu na kevala[pada]pratiṣedho'yam । kutaḥ ? brūyāditi
śravaṇāt</q> । asyārthaḥ---prasaktasya hi pratiṣedho bhavati ṛcaśca vacanaṃ prasaktam ।
na tu padamātrasya tasyārthapratipādakatvābhāvāt । tadāha - <q>na kevalaṃ padavacane</q>
﻿<pb n="301"/>
<q>arthapratipādane vyāpriyete</q> । vākyaṃ hi vacaḥ kāraṇamityuktam । tena prasakta eva
niṣidhyate natu padamātram ।</p>
<p><q>nanu cerāpadavadbhaviṣyati padasyāpi pratiṣedhaḥ</q> । pariharati-[na]<q>tathā'tra
sambhavaḥ</q> । kasmādityāha---<q>ṣaḍviṃśatirityeva pratīyāt ityukte na catus‍triṃśatpada-
pratiṣedhaṃ pratīmaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ-na girāgireti brūyādityanuvādo'yam । anuvādaśca
pramāṇāntareṇa varṇyamāno na doṣamāvahati । tena yuktaṃ tatra padamātroccāraṇānuvādaḥ ।
iha ṣaḍviṃśatipade vihitepi na catustriṃśatpadanivṛttiḥ prāptā tulyakāryatvābhāvāt---
<q>tatrāpi udgānapadasamabhivyāhārāt</q> । tatkāryānupraveśena airaṃ kṛtvodgeyamiti udgānena
gānāvayavenerāpa[dasya]sambandhaḥ । tenodgānakārakaṃ girāpadaṃ nivartate । iha punaḥ
vākyabhedādṛte naikakāryāvagatiriti vaiṣamyam । tena pratiṣedho yaktaḥ nānuvādaḥ ।
padapratiṣedho nāvagamyate ।</p>
<p>yuktyantarāṇyāha---<q>vākyabhedaścāyuktaḥ</q> ityuttarābhidhāyi । vaṅ‍‌kri(vi)<q>prati-
patteścādṛṣṭārthatvaprasaṅgaḥ</q> । yāvatyaśca vaṅkrayaḥ tāvatīḥ anuṣṭhyāditi ṣaḍviṃśatiśabdo
na śaknoti । tasmādṛca eva pratiṣedha iti sthitam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 3 ।। vaniṣṭhusannidhānādurūkeṇa vapābhidhānam ।। 22 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>atrāpi viśeṣaviniyogābhāvāt mantrārtha eva doṣo labhyata iti
tadartho vikalpate</q> । saiva dṛṣṭārthatvāśrayaṇa<q>hetuḥ gṛddhraṃ vapāṃ manyamānā vaniṣṭhuṃ
mārāviṣṭetyucyamāne'dṛṣṭārthatā mantrasya</q> । ulūkavacane hi adṛṣṭārthatā । vapoddharaṇa-
kāle viruddhatā ca vaniṣṭhoḥ lipitulyatvāt । yadyulūkaṃ dhyātvā vaniṣṭhurlevitavyetyu-
cyate tadā'dṛṣṭārthatā । atha ulūkasadṛśo vaniṣ‍ṭhurna lavitavya ityucyate tadā
viruddhārthatvādvaniṣṭhoḥ lavitavyatvāt । tasmātpadabhedamātra eva nyāyaḥ । urupadaṃ vistīrṇa-
vacanaṃ kapadaṃ ca samudāyalakṣaṇayā bhedovacanaṃ kaśaśabdopasthāpanamukhena bhedasvivapā-
lakṣaṇā । padabhede ca samāso bhavatu mā vā na kaścitprayojane viśeṣa iti । nirṇaya-
hetvabhāvādanirṇaya iti । yadi punaḥ svarādibhiḥ kaścidviśeṣārtho'virodhena sa āśraya-
ṇīya eva । tadabhāve punaḥna kiñcidvaiyarthyam । icchāto niyamaḥ । tathā cobhayaṃ pradarśitaṃ
bhāṣyakāreṇa ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 4 ।। praśasāsyabhidhānam ।। 23 ।।</l></lg>
﻿<pb n="302"/>
<p><q>atrāpi saiva vārtā mantrālocanena nirṇīyata iti</q> । pūrvasmin yā vārtā
saivātrāpi prayogakalpikā bhavatu 1prayogakalpanābhayāttu pūrvotthitā nirasyate । asivā-
cakatve hi asinā bāhūddhāraṇaprayogaḥ kalpayitavyaḥ nānyathā samavetārthaprakāśana-
mupapadyate । na ca prayogāntaraṃ kalpayiṃtu śakyate svadhitisādhanasya prayogasya klṛptatvāt ।
nanu ca prāśastye bāhvorvākyenābhidhīyamāne sūktabhāktvena tayoḥ devatātvaṃ prāpnoti ।
atrāha <q>prāśastyaṃ na punarbāhvordevatātvaṃ prakalpayati । kṛtsnoddharaṇatayāpyupapatteḥ</q>
kṛtsna ud‌dhriyate na sakṛt svoddhāraṇo mantraḥ tasya bhāvastattā । yadyapi mantrārthopapa-
tterna devatāpādakatvaṃ sambhavācca kṛtsnayorbāhvoḥ praśastatāyāḥ ayamevārthato nyāyaḥ । kathaṃ
punarasyabhidhānapakṣe ūho bhāṣyakāreṇocyate । ucyate । māntravarṇikādupapannam । māntra-
varṇiko'siḥ । tenaikasmin‍nasau praśasetyekavacanāntaṃ dvayoḥ bahuṣu ca dvivacanāntaṃ bahu-
vacanāntaṃ ca ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 5 ।। śyenaśalākaśyapakavaṣasrekaparṇeṣvākṛtivacanaṃ
prasiddhasannidhānāt ।। 25 ।।</l></lg>
<p>atrāpi dṛṣṭārthe sambhavati nādṛṣṭārthaṃkalpanā pratyarthinī yukteti kṛts‍noddhāraṇa-
taiva2nyā[yyā]śyenākṛtiḥ 1asya vakṣo yathā bhavati tathā kuruteti mantrārtho bhavet ।
kṛts‍noddharaṇārthatayā dṛṣṭārthatā bhavati । kṛts‍noddhāraṇe hi tathārūpatā vakṣasaḥ । nanu
kṛts‍noddhāraṇe kathaṃ dṛṣṭārthatetyata āha---<q>anyatra nyūnāvadānaprāpteḥ</q> । homārthaṃ hi
yadavadānaṃ kṛts‍noddhāraṇe sati anyūnebhyo bhavati । nanu[mā]bhūdanyūnāvadānākāṅkṣe-
tyatrāha---<q>atrābhidhānācca2 avadānaśruteḥ śyenādiśabdānāmubhayatra[prayogo]
na sambhavati</q> । ākāramātropalakṣaṇamitarasmin pakṣe yataḥ । <q><quote>“pakṣoktaṃ
prayojanaṃ”</quote> ityuktaṃ bhāṣye । viśasane ca tatprayojanaṃ kathitaṃ, nohe</q> ।
ūhe ca kathayitumucitam, anyathā lakṣaṇāsaṅgateriti paricodanā । parihārastu
<q>ayamabhiprāyaḥ īdṛśārthe yathābhidhānamupapadyate</q> । tathā (tā)evaṃ coditānyū-
nākāreṇādhrigurupavarṇito bhavati sarvasyādhrigumantrasyāvaiguṇyaṃ bhavati kṛts‍noddhāraṇa-
paratvāt ।</p>
<note>1. prayogakalpikāmavatu-mā</note>
<note>2. nyāyāditi ।</note>
﻿<pb n="303"/>
<lg><l>।। 6 ।। prāsaṅgike prāyaścittaṃ na vidyate parārthatvāt
tadarthe hi vidhīyate ।। 28 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nanu ceyamadhikāracintā । tasyāḥ kaḥ prasaṅga ūhalakṣaṇe ?</q> pariharati
---<q>kāryatastvadhikāranirṇayo nopadeśa[ta]itīhaiva cintyate</q> । yadā jyoti-
ṣmatyā agnireva kāryaṃ tadā agnihotrārthamuddha‍ṛtāgnyudvānavata evādhikāraḥ । yadā tu
naimittikamidaṃ karmānuṣṭhānaṃ tadā prāsaṅgiko'gnyudvānavato'pyadhikāraḥ । tena kāryata
evādhikāranirṇayo nopadeśāditi kāryacintāyāmūhacintā । <q>pūrvapakṣavādī ārtya-
dhikaraṇanyāyaṃ manvāna aidamarthyamuddharaṇena vivakṣitamiti pūrvapakṣitavān</q> ।
yathā ārtyadhikaraṇa ubhayatvamavivakṣitaṃ tathehāpyaidamarthyamudvānasyāvivakṣitam । tena
prāsaṅgikodvānepi naimittikameveti pūrvapakṣitam ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu kāryayogo'nyathā'gnihotre na syāta yadyaidamarthyaṃ
nādriyate</q> । asyārthaḥ-udvātāgninirmittaṃ nodvānamātraṃ udvātāgneśca puruṣasyāgnisamā-
dhānameva kāryam । tatra yadi prāsaṅgikepi agnāvudvāte prāyaścittaṃ syāt tadā tasyāgni-
hotrāsambandhātagnihotrasambandho jyotiṣmatyā na syāt tasmādagnihotrārthamuddha‍ṛtāgnyudvāna
eva ca tatra naimittikamiti ।</p>
<p>nanvadhikāriṇo viśeṣaṇamavivakṣitamityuktamārtyadhikaraṇe ityata āha---
<q>viśeṣaṇāvivakṣā ca upadeśa ukto na kārye</q> । tasmādvaiṣamyamārtyadhikaraṇena ।
vākyabhedādavivakṣitatoktā । kāryataścātrānupraveśaḥ । ato vākyabhedo nāsti । ato'-
nyārthe(vyābhā)prāyaścittam । nanvagnerudvānaṃ nimittaṃ nodvānavānityatrāha-<q>agniviśiṣṭo-
dvānanimittatā</q> yathānirastā tathā pradarśitaṃ bhāṣye yasyāgnirudvāta iti śravaṇādagnireva-
nimittamiti । tasmādudvānaparīto'gnirnimittamiti sthite yukto rāddhānta iti sthitam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 7 ।। dhāraṇe ca parārthatvāt ।। 29 ।।</l></lg>
<p>pūrvoktaṃ sarvamupapadyate nimittatayā[pro]ktam । tādṛśaṃ nāsti । kuta ityāha---
<q>kṛtārthasya hyatra</q> dhāraṇaṃ <q>akṛtārthaṃ ca nimittamityuktam</q> । akṛtārthasya samādhāna-
mapekṣitam apekṣitārthasamādhānārthamidam । (a)kṛtārthaścāgniratra yadarthamasau uddha‍ṛtaḥ
dhāryate tadanuṣṭhitameva । ataḥ parārthavadatrāstu । parisamūhanaparihārastūktaḥ prayogā-
ṅgatvena । prayogaḥ parisamūhanādīnāmaṅgatvāt ।</p>
﻿<pb n="304"/>
<lg><l>।। 8 ।। na tūtpanne codanā'prāptakālatvāt ।। 31 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>kālo'ṅgaṃ, na cāṅgābhāve pradhānaśās‍trārthānyatvaṃ tasmānnāṅgāntara-
nivṛttiḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ - yadyapi darśārthoddharaṇe agnihotrārthoddharaṇakālo na labhyate
tathāpi mantraḥ prayoktumucita eva । aṅgābhāvepi pradhānānuṣṭhānadarśanāt āgneyavat
yathā vrīhyabhāvepi āgneyaśāstrārtho na vidyata[lupyata]iti tadanuṣṭhānaṃ tathehāpi yuktam ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu satyamaṅga(ka)lopastathāpi nimittena tulyam</q> । kuta
ityāha---<q>kāle hi sati karma codyate na punaḥ karmaṇi sati kālaḥ</q> upādānā-
śakteḥ । tena tadabhāve adhikārābhāvānnedamagnihotrārthameva ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 9 ।। pradānadarśanaṃ śrapaṇe taddharmabhojanārthatvāt saṃsargācca
madhūdakavat ।। 32 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>payo na pākārthamiti</q> । atra punarbhede[rvede]śabdapramāṇakā vayaṃ śabdataśca
vākyārthatāṃ payaso vidmaḥ na dhātvarthatām । carurāditya iti ādityasambandhaścarora-
vagamyate na payasaḥ, tasya ca pākārthataiva yuktā । na ca pakvā āmāśśakyate
vak‍tuṃ yena śabdo vihanyeta । bhojanārthasyāpi(stā)pākasādhakatvasya loke darśanāt ।
athāpi nāntarīyakyapi pākāsiddhirna syāt sāmānyato dṛṣṭaṃ ca vede na kramata iti tatra
tatroktaṃ niyogārthastvananyaḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 10 ।। abhyudaye dohāpanayaḥ svadharmā syāt pravṛttatvāt ।। 41 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>।। 11 ।। apanayo vā'rthāntare vidhānāccarupayovat ।। 46 ।।</l></lg>
<p>śṛtaśabdaśravaṇāt prāyaṇīyena vaiṣamyam śrutisāmānyatvaṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī ।
śrapaṇaṃ hi havissaṃskāraḥ pratipannaḥ taddarśanāt । payaso haviṣṭvaṃ manyamānaḥ prāyaṇīya-
payasā vaiṣamyaṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī । abhyudayeṣṭitulyatvācca vākyānām ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntastu nāsati pradeyārthatve saptamyartho'pahnotuṃ śakyate iti yathāśrata eva
vākyārthaḥ abhyudayeṣṭau pūrvāvagatatvāt pradeyatāyāssaptamyarthāpahnavaḥ kṛtaḥ । iha tu tada-
bhāvānna yuktaḥ । [śṛta] śabdo'pi lakṣaṇayāpyanvita eva saptamyarthaḥ payomātra-
lakṣaṇataḥ śabda sa hi payasi haviḥ śravaṇānna[bha]vati । vṛtta ityarthaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="305"/>
<lg><l>।। 12 ।। śrayaṇānāṃ tvapūrvatvāt pradānārthe vidhānaṃ syāt ।। 45 ।।</l></lg>
<p>payasā maitrāvaruṇaṃ śrīṇātīti dṛṣṭārthālābhena pūrvapakṣavādī pradeyārthatāṃ
payaśśabdasya manyate । avarudhyaḥ tṛtīyāntasyāpi devatāsambandhaḥ । saptamyantasyeva
payasaḥ prāyaṇīye ।</p>
<p>rāddhānastu na brūmastṛtīyayā devatātvasyāvaruddhatayā deyatvena na sambadhyata
iti । kintu nityadeyasambaddhena somena saṃyogaśravaṇāt tadarthataivāvasīyate । maitrā-
varuṇaṃ gṛhṇātītyetaccodanānusāreṇa somamātrasyaiva devatāsambandhaḥ pratīyate । sa pratīta-
devatāsambaddhaḥ somaḥ śrayaṇārthamihānūdyate tena somārthaṃ payo na pradānārtham । kutaḥ ?
śrutyantare hi deyadravyopalakṣaṇāyaiva devatārītirvidhīyeta । yo vā dīyate vidheyāntarasya
saṃyogāt ta[sya] vidhāne cāvaśyopalakṣaṇīyatvāt । dvi....śe hi śeṣisamarpakaṃ
maitrāvaruṇapadam । tasmāt somasya dvitīyāsaṃyogāt somārthataiva payasa iti nyāyyam ।
<q>śeṣamuk‍tam</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 13 ।। paryagnikṛtānāmutsarge tādarthyamupadhānavat ।। 51 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>kathaṃ punaratra pūrvapakṣo devatāśravaṇe śakyate vak‍tum</q> । īśānāya parasvata
ālabhata iti devatāśravaṇādyāgaḥ vidhinaivādhigamyate । kathaṃ pūrvapakṣāśaṅkā ?
<q>devatāśravaṇasya ca samādhileśaṃ kaṃ punarasau</q> [manyate ?] uttaraṃ --- <q>tyāgādṛte
nānyadvidhātuṃ śakyata iti । rāddhānte rāddhāntasthāpanamadhye bhāṣyakāreṇa
śaṅkitavyo vikalpo draṣṭavyaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ - tān paryagnikṛtānutsṛjatītyatra tyāga
eva vidheyaḥ paryagnikaraṇaviśiṣṭaḥ vidheyāntarasyāsambhavāt । yadi hi īśānāya para-
svata ālabhata ityanena yāgo vidhīyate tān paryagnikṛtānutsṛjatītyatra na kiñcidvidheyaṃ
gamyate । paryagnikaraṇasya codakaprāptatvāditi bhāṣyakāreṇoktam । tasmādīśānāyeti
śabdamuccāryālambhaḥ kartavya iti vidhīyate । tadāha---<q>devatāśravaṇaṃ punaḥ svarūpā-
nvayi bhaviṣyati mantravadityabhiprāyaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---yāgavidhirevāyam । kutaḥ ? na hi arthānvaye
sambhavati svarūpānvayaśśakyate vak‍tum</q> । nanu ca śabde kāryasyāsambhavāt arthe
sampratyayo yuktaḥ । tatrārthe kāryaṃ vijñāyate । iha tu śabdo'stīti tatraiva kāryaṃ
bhavituṃ yuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="306"/>
<p>rāddhāntavādī vadati-kena voktaṃ yatra śabde sampratyayo'sti tatra na yuktamiti
kintviha śabda eva sampratyayo nāsti । na hyarthāvivakṣāyāṃ pramāṇaṃ śakyate'vagantum ।
yatrotsargamṛte vidhānaṃ na sambhavati tatra tatra darśitaḥ sambhavaḥ tadantāṅgarītividhānena ।
<q>śeṣaṃ sanidarśanamuktam</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 14 ।। ājyasaṃsthāpratinidhiḥ syāt dravyotsargāt ।। 56 ।।</l></lg>
<p>spaṣṭe'pi tadanenotsargavidhāne śeṣasaṃsthāpanaśabdāt bhrāntirupajāyate tadantaṃ
karma na bhavatīti । tataśca pakṣadvayasambhavāt tasyā bhrānterapanayāyedamadhikaraṇamārabhyate ।
na caivamapi sandeha eva yuktaḥ । kathaṃ pūrvapakṣādhyavasānamityatrāha---<q>pūrvapakṣo hi
śeṣasaṃsthāna [śravaṇāt]</q> etadvalena tadantāṅgarītividhānameva na sambhavati iti
kalpanīyā ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntastu parisamāpanīyamevaitadityuktvā punastaccheṣābhidhānaṃ viruddha‍yate ।
tena śeṣābhidhāne gauṇasamanvayaḥ । na ca parisamāptiḥ asamāptāvapi śakyate
vak‍tum । śabdābhidheyasya pakṣāntare'pyavyāghātāt । pūrvapakṣyāha---<q>yuktaṃ saṃsthānaṃ
karmāntarapakṣe । śeṣaśabdastu kathaṃ ?</q> rāddhāntyāha---<q>nanu sādṛśyādevetyuktaṃ
bhāṣye śeṣavaccheṣa ityarthena</q> । pūrvapakṣyāha---<q>satyamuktaṃ bhāṣye tadayuktamabhi-
hitam । śeṣaśabdaśrutibhānāt</q> । ekagranthenāha---<q>utsarge vā kaḥ pakṣapātaḥ</q> ।
sa eva kimityanyathā varṇitaḥ iti bhāvaḥ । rāddhāntī uttaramāha---<q>ayamasti pakṣa-
pātaḥ pūrvoktāpekṣonyaḥ śeṣaśabdaḥ</q> । na punaḥ pūrvoktaṃ śeṣamapekṣate । śeṣo hyavayavaḥ
pūrvamavayavinamapekṣate na punaḥ pūrvoktaṃ śeṣam । tasmānnirapekṣatvāt utsargaḥ śrautaḥ ।
tadapekṣayā tu śeṣaśabdo gauṇa iti nyāyyam । <q>sanidarśanaṃ śeṣamuktam</q> ।</p>
<p><q>।। iti mahopādhyāyaśālikanāthamiśrakṛtau
pañ‍cikāyāṃ navamasya caturthaḥ pādaḥ ।।</q></p>
﻿<pb n="307"/>
<p><q>ṛjuvimalāyāṃ</q></p>
<p><q>daśamādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ</q></p>
<lg><l>।। 1 ।। vidheḥ prakaraṇāntare'tideśātsarvakarma syāt ।। 1 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nanu ca bādhe satyūhena bhavitavyam</q> । anena bhāṣyoktamūhabādhalakṣaṇayo-
rhetuhetumadbhāvamākṣipati । yadi hi ūhe sati bādhaḥ syāt tarhi ūhasya bādhaṃ prati
hetutā syāt viparītaṃ tu vidyate bādhe satyūhena bhavitavyam ।</p>
<p>pṛcchati---<q>ka evamāha</q> - uttaraṃ---<q>evaṃ hyupalabhyate । nivṛtte'gniśabde
sūryapadaprakṣepaḥ</q> । agnipadasthāne sūryapadaprakṣepo yaḥ so'gniśabdasyānivṛttau nopapadyate ।
tasmādagniśabdabādhe satyūho bhavatītyupalabhyate । samādhātā āha-<q>upalabdhiścet
sāmni saṃskāre vā kimupalabhyate kasya nivṛttau kasya prakṣepaḥ</q> ? sāmni
saṃskāre ca kasyacidvādho na dṛśyate । tena sāmasaṃskārohastāvata bādhahetuko na
bhavati । ato bibhīṣikāmātrameva bādhapūrvaka ūha iti ।</p>
<p>ākṣeptāramāśaṅkyati---<q>mantre kathamiti cet</q> । parihāramāha---<q>tatrāpi
prakṛtivadabhidhānaṃ kuryāt ityanena hetunā yaḥ sūryapadaprakṣepaḥ so'gniśabdasya
nivṛttiṃ nāpekṣate</q> । kasmādityāha---<q>abhidhānasampattyartho hi[sūryapada]prakṣepaḥ
nāgniśabdābhāvanimittakaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ-yathā prakṛtau mantreṇābhidhānaṃ kṛtaṃ vikṛtāvapi
tathaiva kartavyamityevamarthaṃ sūryapadaprakṣepaḥ । nahi sūryapadamantareṇa prakṛtivadabhidhānaṃ
sampadyate । prakṛtau pradhānadevatābhidhānaṃ mantreṇa kṛtam । vikṛtau sūryaḥ pradhānadevatā,
nāsau sūryapadamantareṇa śakyate bodhayituṃ ityevaṃ sūryapadaprakṣepo mantre na punaragniśabdā-
bhāvanimittakaḥ tasya prakṣepaḥ । yadi hi agniśabdābhavanimittakaḥ syāt tadā bādha-
hetuka ūho bhavet na caitadevam । tasmānna viparīto hetuhetumadbhāvaḥ । <q>yadyevaṃ
bādho'pi tarhi nohanimittakaḥ tathābhidhāna1nirvṛttyarthaḥ 2prakṣepaḥ । tathā
saurye karmaṇyag‍neranabhidheyatvādagniśabdasya nivṛttiḥ na punarūhahetuko bādhaḥ</q>
<note<1. R sampattyarthaḥ</note>
<note>2. A prakṣepāt</note>
﻿<pb n="308"/>
uttaraṃ---<q>mā bhūdūhapūrvako bādhaḥ kā no bādhā?</q> na kiñcidasmākaṃ bādhyata ityabhi-
prāyaḥ । ākṣeptā---<q>kastarhi lakṣaṇasambandhaḥ yadi hetuhetumadbhāvo nāsti</q> ।
samādhātā āha---<q>kāryeṇohaḥ prāptaḥ kāryaśūnyamabhidhānaṃ kimanuṣṭhātavyaṃ neti
bhavati sambandhaḥ</q> ।</p>
<p>asyārthaḥ---yatprakṛtau padārthānāṃ kāryaṃ vikṛtāvapi tadeva kāryamiti kāryeṇa
haviḥ prakṛtidravyeṇa saṃskāryeṇa haviḥ prakṛtibhūteṣu kṛṣṇaleṣvevāvaghātasyohaprayojanaḥ
prāptaḥ । idānīṃ kṛṣṇalasaṃskāratvenāvaghātasya prayoge niścite kartavyo'vaghātaḥ kārya-
haviśśūnyo bhavati । tuṣavimocanakāryābhāvat ataścintā bhavati kiṃ kāryaśūnyasyā-
vaghātasyānuṣṭhānaṃ kriyatāṃ neti । tatra dvārābhāvat ananuṣṭhānamavaghātasyeti bādho
bhavati । eṣa ūhalakṣaṇabādhalakṣaṇayoḥ sambandhaḥ । etaduktaṃ bhavati - dvāralopanibandhano
bādhaḥ tena sākṣādūhasya hetubhāvo nāsti, kintu kṛṣṇalasāṃkaratvenāvaghātasya prayogaḥ
kartavya ityūhe niścite sati kṛṣṇale tuṣakaṇavimocanakāryābhāvādavaghātasya dvāralopa-
niścayaḥ । tataśca bādha iti bādhahetubhūtadvāralopaniścayahetutvādastyūhasya bādhaṃ prati
hetubhāva iti । tathā ca svayameva sūtrakāraḥ āgrayaṇe prākṛtānvāhāryasthānapatitayo-
rvāsovatsayoḥ anvāhāryadharmohaṃ darśayitvā dvārābhāvena pākasya bādhaṃ darśayiṣyati ।
<q>bhavanti cātra ś‍lokāḥ</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>vikṛtyapūrvatādarthye kratuśeṣatvasīmani ।</l>
<l>prākṛtānāṃ padārthānāmatideśātmake sthite ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>prākṛtasthānapatitavastvantaracikīrṣayā ।</l>
<l>prayoge vidite dvāralopaḥ śakyaviściyaḥ ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>dvāralopanimittaśca bādho'to hetusiddhaye ।</l>
<l>ūhāpekṣeti sambandho vyakta evohabādhoḥ ।।</l></lg>
<p>bādho nāmeti bhāṣyamarthato'nubhāṣya ākṣipati---<q>bādho nāmetyuktvā yanni-
ś‍citaṃ kāryavijñānaṃ tasya kāraṇāntareṇa</q> mithyābhāvo bādha iti bādhasvarūpamupa-
varṇitam । taccedaṃ vipratiṣiddhaṃ pramāṇavido manyante । na hi niścitajñānaṃ mithyā
bhavati । mithyābhāvo'pi jñānasyārthaśūnyatvam । na ca yadvijñānaṃ niścitaṃ tadartha-
śūnyaṃ bhavati । vijñānasya svamahimnaivārthopasthāpakatvāt । viśeṣeṇa tu mīmāṃsakānāṃ
﻿<pb n="309"/>
mate na hi vijñānaṃ mithyā bhavati yeṣāmagrahaṇanibandhanameva mithyātvam । mīmāṃsakā
hi bhedāgrahaṇarūpatayā vijñānasya mithyābhāvaṃ vadanti, na jñānarūpatayā । vivekā-
grahaṇāddhi smṛtijñānaṃ pratyakṣavyavahārapravartakatayā puruṣaṃ vyavahāre visaṃvādamāpādayat
vijñānaṃ mithyābhūtamityucyate । tenāgrahaṇanibandhanameva mithyātvam ।</p>
<p>yeṣāmapi mīmāṃsakaikadeśināṃ khyātireva viparītā jñānamevāyathābhūtaṃ te'pi naiva
niścitatvaṃ viparītatve heturiti bruvate । teṣāmapi śuktikāsvarūpaniścayo na rajatatva-
grahaṇe hetuḥ kintu śuktikāsvarūpāniścaya eva । tadetadāha---<q>teṣāmapi ajñāna-
vāsanā viparītatve hetuḥ</q> । ajñānena vāsanā saṃskāro'jñānavāsanā । śuktikā-
svarūpājñānena saṃskṛtasya rajatavijñānaṃ bhavati ।</p>
<p>yuktaṃ 1cājñānasyaiva mithyātvaṃ, tasyaiva jñānenāpanīyamānasya bādhyatvāt । jñānaṃ
tu na jñānenāpanetuṃ 2śakyate । tena bādhakābhāvānna jñānaṃ mithyeti yuktam । tadāha
---<q>jñānena cā'jñānaṃ vivartyata iti ajñānasyaiva yukto mithyābhāvaḥ । ato
niścitaṃ jñānaṃ mithyeti vipratiṣiddham</q> । kiñca prāmāṇye ca suparitiścitatvameva
hetutvena pramāṇalakṣaṇe svayamuditam । <quote>“jāgrato buddhiḥ supariniścitā kathaṃ viparya-
siṣyatī”</quote>ti । <q>tena yadvijñānaṃ niś‍citaṃ tanmithyetyabhidhīyamāne svavacana</q>-
virodhaḥ । tasmāt kathamidamevaṃsvabhāvaṃ bādhaṃ vadato bhāṣyamunneyamityāpa, saṃhāraḥ ।</p>
<p>samādhātā āha---<q>atrocyate । kathamidaṃ pramāṇavido manyante ।
niś‍citaṃ mithyā ceti vipratiṣiddhamiti</q> । nedaṃ vipratiṣiddhamiti bhāvaḥ । kutaḥ
ityāha---<q>śabdo'pi naḥ pramāṇamityuktam</q> । tathāpi kimityāha---<q>tasya ca
śabdasya prāmāṇyaṃ yairmīṃmāṃsakaiḥ viditaṃ na te'nyathā vadanti</q> । yasmācchabdena
niścitasyaivedaṃ mithyātvam । tena niścitaṃ mithyetyeva yuktam । <q>kathaṃ śabdena
niś‍citaṃ</q> ? uttaraṃ---<q>prakṛtau hi kathaṃ kartavyamityasyāmākāṅkṣāyāṃ itthaṃ
kartavyamityupadeśena itikartavyatā samarpitā । yathā'nayā bhavati tathettha-
miti kalpyate</q> । asyārthaḥ---prakṛtau niyoge kāryabhūte pratīte kathaṃ kartavyamiti
karaṇopakārākāṅkṣāyāṃ upadeśenetikartavyatā padārthasya saṃhatiḥ samarpitā । tataśca tāṃ
<note>1. R caiva</note>
<note>2. R apahno tuṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="310"/>
gṛhītvaivamupakāraḥ kalpyate - yathā yena prakāreṇa anayā padārthasaṃhatyopakārobhavati ।
tathā tena dvāreṇetthamiti kalpyate । klṛpte 1cetthaṃbhāve karaṇopakāre tadvaditi vikṛtā-
vatideśaḥ prakṛtivadvikṛtiḥ kartavyeti karaṇopakārasya padārthasaṃhateścātideśaḥ । tathāpi
kimityāha---<q>na cāprāptau tadvaditi śakyate vak‍tum</q> । yadyupakārasya padārthasaṃhateśca
vikṛtyapūrvaṃ pratyaidamarthyenāprāptiḥ syāt tadā prakṛtivadvikṛtiḥ kartavyeti vaktuṃ na
śakyate । tasmāt vikṛtyapūrvaṃ prati prāptirasti sopakārāyāḥ padārthasaṃhateḥ ।
tasmāt prākṛtaṃ padārthajātaṃ vikṛtyapūrve prāptamaṅgatvena sambaddhamityarthaḥ । yacca prāptaṃ
tanniścitam । tena niścitatvaṃ prasiddham । aniścitatvaṃ prasādhya mithyātvamidānīmāha
---<q>yasya tu tathā yena prakāreṇa prākṛtena dvāraviśeṣeṇetthaṃbhāvaḥ karaṇopakāro
na sambhavati tad‍dvārābhāvenākartavyatayā mithyetyavagamyate</q> । kathaṃ dvārābhāve
karaṇopakārāsambhava ityātrāha---<q>prakṛtāvapi ca dvāranibandhana eva itthaṃbhāvaḥ na
tādarthyataḥ</q> । caśabdo yasmādarthe । yasmāt prakṛtāvapi dvāranibandhana eva karaṇopa-
kāraḥ na tu tādarthyamātranibandhanaḥ prakṛtivacca vikṛtāvapyupakāraḥ tasmāt dvārabādhe
karaṇopakārāsambhavaḥ । karaṇopakārāsambhave cākiñcitkaratvādananuṣṭhānam । yadi
dvārabādhena karaṇopakāraṃ na janayati kathaṃ tarhi vikṛtau tasya niścaya ityāha---
<q>tādarthye(nā)cāyaṃ niścayaḥ</q> uktaḥ <q>yāvaduktaṃ tāvati śabdasya prāmāṇyāt</q> ।</p>
<p>asyārthaḥ---yadyapi 2dvārabādhena karaṇopakāraṃ na janayati tathāpi vikṛtyapūrvaṃ
prati tasyaidamarthyaṃ śeṣatvaṃ niścitam । tena śābdo niścayo'sti । aidamarthyamātre
śabdasya prāmāṇyāt । dvāraṃ punaḥ pramāṇāntarasiddhameva tuṣakaṇavimocanādikamavaghātā-
dīnām । śābda ca pramāṇamaṅgīkṛtyāyaṃ niścaya uktaḥ । yato dvāraṃ pramāṇāntaravedyamata
idamuktaṃ kāraṇāntareṇa mithyeti kalpyata iti । kāraṇāntaraśabdaṃ vivṛṇoti---<q>pramāṇā-
ntarabaśenetyarthaḥ</q> । ayamāśayaḥ---śābdena pramāṇāntareṇa tādarthyaṃ niścitaṃ pramāṇā-
ntareṇadvārābhāvena karaṇopakārajanakatayā mithyeti parikalpyate । anupakārakasyā-
tādarthyāt iti niścitaṃ mithyeti parika(lpitaṃ)lpyata iti siddham । kathaṃ punaḥ
pramāṇāntaravaśena śābdasya tādarthyasya mithyātvaṃ? śābdajñānena gṛhītaṃ tādarthyaṃ satya-
bhūtameva na tasya mithyātvaṃ śakyate vak‍tum । yadyapi tadānīmupakāraṃ dvārābhāvena sa
<note>1. R kalpite</note>
<note>2. A dvārābhāvena</note>
﻿<pb n="311"/>
padārtho na janayati, tathāpi prākṛtatvādupakārasya bhavatyevāsau tajjanyaḥ, prakṛtau tena
tasya janyamānatvāt । tenā(ā)tajjanyopakārasambandho vikṛtyapūrvasya । tasmātprākṛtasya
padārthasya luptadvārasyāpi avihatameva tādarthyam । <q>kathaṃ punaḥ pramāṇantaravaśena
śābdasya mithyātvaṃ ?</q> uttaraṃ-<q>yata eva mithyātvaṃ nāsti ata eva kāraṇā-
ntareṇa mithyātvaṃ na svata ityuktam ।</q> kāraṇāntareṇa dvāra(ā)niścayāt ।
tadabhāve tadānīṃ karaṇopakārājanakatvāt tādarthe satyapi atādarthyasādhāraṇīṃ karaṇopa-
kārājanakatāṃ pratiyato'nyatra dṛṣṭyā tādarthyasmaraṇamupajāyate tena luptadvāraṃ atadartha-
miti manyate । tena pramāṇāntareṇa dvārasya grāhyatvāt tadabhāve'tādarthyajñānamiva bhavati
na punaḥ śābdenaiva jñānenātādarthyamavagamyate tadeva spaṣṭayati---<q>paropādhikaṃ
mithyātvaṃ svatastu niścayaḥkena vāryate draṣṭṛtvamivātmanaḥ</q> । dṛṣṭāntaṃ vivṛṇoti
---<q>nopadhānādṛte na paśyatīti na draṣṭṛtvaṃ hīyate</q> । upadhānādindriyādi-
vyāpārādvinā suṣup‍tyādau viṣayaṃ na paśyatītyetāvatā ātmano draṣṭṛtvaṃ dṛk‌śaktiyogitvaṃ
na hīyate । astyeva dṛk‌śaktiḥ svābhāvikī apaśyato'pi । tathā kāryamupakurva-
to'pi upakārajananaśaktirastyeva luptadvārasyāpi prakṛtau darśanāt jāgraddaśāyāmivātmano
viṣayadarśanāt । tataśca tāvanmātrameva bādha iti ।</p>
<p>yadyevaṃ tadeva vaktavyaṃ dvārābhāvādbādha iti tadāha---<q>atha kasmādevameva noktaṃ
dvārābhāvo bādha iti</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>naivaṃ, pramāṇasya bādha ityuktaṃ bhavati । nanu
ca naiva pramāṇasya svato bādha ityuktam</q> । tena pramāṇasya bādhābhāvāt pramāṇabādho
vak‍tumeva na yuktaḥ । tena tasyānabhidhānaṃ na doṣa ityarthaḥ । pariharati---<q>upā-
dhito'pi bādho bādha eva sugandhiteva kāminīnām</q> । asyārthaḥ---dvārā-
bhāvāvagame tādarthye satyapi yadidamatādarthyasmaraṇamupādhiḥ tato'pi yobādhaḥ so'pi bādha
eva । yathā kāminīnāṃ sugandhidravyāṅgarāgavatīnāṃ śarīrasamavāyigandhāgrahaṇe smaryate
yathā aṅgarāgagatagandhagrahaṇe ca sugandhiteva bhavati । yadi sugandhiteva kāminīnāṃ
pramāṇasya bādhaḥ upacārastarhi ? upacārastu na pāramārthika iti tattve jñānena2
pāramārthiko bādho na bhavati । anyadīyamatādarthyaṃ smaryate yathā'ṅgarāgagataṃ saugandhya-
manubhūyate । tadeva tu saṃyuktasamavāyāt kāminīṣviva bhāsate ।</p>
1. R. ukto
2. A. tatve jñāne
﻿<pb n="312"/>
<p>pariharati---<q>na kārye upakāraḥ śakyate vak‍tum</q> । bādhakārye upacāro
nāsti । bādhakāryaṃ pāramārthikamananuṣṭhānātmakam । tatparamārthato bhavatyeva dvārābhāve'nu-
pakārakasyānanuṣṭhānāt । ato'pāramārthikepi bādhe kāryaṃ pāramārthikameva । yathā
saurabhe kāminīnāmapāramārthikepi saurabhakāryaṃ kāmukaprītirūpaṃ pāramārthikameva ।</p>
<p>1nanvevamapi bādhakāryameva pāramārthikaṃ na bādha iti pramāṇasya mithyābhāvo bādha
iti na vaktavyamityatrāha---<q>kāryārthaṃ ca svarūpavarṇanam</q> । yadidaṃ bādhasvarūpavarṇanaṃ tat
bādhakāryānanuṣṭhānasiddha‍yarthaṃ tadbādhakāryaṃ pramāṇasya mithyābhāve darśite satīti tadarthamau-
pādhiko'pi pramāṇasya bādha uktaḥ । <q>tasmātsuṣṭhūcyate niścitaṃ mithyeti ca
kārye vibhāgādarśanāt</q> bādhakārye'nanuṣṭhāne <q>vibhāgo</q> viśeṣo na dṛśyate । pāra-
mārthikaupādhikabādhayoryataḥ । tato niścitaṃ mithyeti ca sūṣṭhūktam2 ।</p>
<p><q>nanvaṅgabhūte3'nanuṣṭhite kimiti vaiguṇyaṃ na bhavati ? bādhakāryasyāpi
śābdatvāt</q> । upakārakaṃ kartavyamiti bodhayatā śāstreṇaivānupakārakamakartavyamiti
kāryata uktaṃ yataḥ । tadayamatra saṅkṣepārthaḥ---prākṛtasyāpi padārthajātasya vikṛtyapūrvaṃ
prati tādarthye niścite'pi yadidamaupādhikamapāramārthikamapi atādarthyajñānamutpadyate
tatphalato bādhakaṃ, tādarthyajñānaṃ phalato bādhyaṃ anuṣṭhānābhāvāditi ।</p>
<p>bhāṣyanubhāṣate---<q><quote>“tathābhyuccayaḥ yadidamiha bhavatīti vijñāne'paramapi
bhavatīti vijñānaṃ”</quote></q> iti । ākṣipati---<q>yata idamiha bhavatīti vijñāna iti ।</q>
kutaḥ ? uttaraṃ--- prathamaṃ prākṛtānāmevopakārasambandho'tideśataḥ । aparamapi bhavatī-
tyupadeśatau vaikṛtānām । etacca vikṛtiṣu । prakṛtau punaḥ naivāyaṃ vibhāgaḥsambhavati,
agṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatvāt aupadeśikasya sambandhasya । sarveṣāmevaupadeśikānāmaṅgānāṃ
yugapadevopakārasambandhāt ।</p>
<p><q>nanu yadi prathamamātideśikaṃ tadā ātideśikena nirākāṅkṣāyāṃ
vikṛtau kathaṃ paśvādaupadeśikāṅgasambandho bhavati</q> । yāsau vikṛtyapūrvasyopakāra-
janakapadārthākāṅkṣā sāpyatideśalabdhaiḥ prākṛtairevāṅgaiḥ pūriteti nirākāṅkṣatayā sākṣā-
dupadiṣṭāṅgasambandha upakāre na syādityarthaḥ ।</p>
<note>1. R nanu caivamapi</note>
<note>2. R suṣṭhūcyate</note>
<note>3. aṅgāntare A</note>
﻿<pb n="313"/>
<p>pariharati---<q>prakṛtau vā kathamaupadeśikāṅgasambandhaḥ</q> । ekagranthenāha---
<q>nākāṅkṣāta eva kevalāyāḥ sambandhaḥ śakyate vak‍tum</q> । sa kuta ityāha---
<q>niyogaikyaṃ hi tatrāṅgasambandhahetuḥ</q> । pradhānaniyogaparigṛhītatvaṃ aṅgasambandhahetuḥ ।
ākāṅkṣāto hi sambandhe kriyadbhirapyākāṅkṣā pūriteti sarvasambandho na syāt । <q>iha
ca vikṛtau tanniyogaikyamaviśiṣṭam yataḥ</q> । ataḥ <q>kārye</q> kāryadaśāyāṃ niyogaikya-
darśanāt dvayaṃ prākṛtaṃ vaikṛtaṃ <q>cāviruddham</q> । etacca vikṛtāvityatrābhyuccayādhikaraṇe
vakṣyāmaḥ । tadidamucyate---<q>anyadapi bhavatīti</q> ।</p>
<p><q>idānīṃ lakṣaṇārtho bādhaścintyate kiṃ luptakāryamapi prākṛtaṃ vikṛtau
kartavyaṃ uta nivartata iti । nanu ca kāryaprayuktā dharmā ityūhaṃ varṇayatā
sthāpitaṃ</q> kathaṃ tadabhāve kartavyatā śaṅkyate । uttaraṃ---<q>satyamevaṃ kāryaprayuktā dharmā
iti । atideśavākyasyārthabhedaṃ manvānasya bhavati saṃśayaḥ</q> । ayamāśayaḥ
---kāryasadbhāva eva saṃśayaḥ । yadi prākṛtameva dvāraṃ tadā kāryabādhaḥ । atha dvārāntaraṃ
tadā kāryasadbhāvaḥ dvārasaṃśayaśca atideśavākyasyārthabhedāt ।</p>
<p>kiṃ punastadatideśavākyaṃ kaśca tasyārthabheda ityatrāha---<q>tadvaditi । kimaṅgā-
pekṣaṃ sādṛśyaṃ utānuṣṭhānāpekṣamiti</q> । prakṛtivadvikṛtiḥ kartavyetyatideśavākyaṃ
vākhyātṝṇām । tena ca prakṛtisādṛśyaṃ vikṛtīnāmucyate । tatsādṛśyaṃ kimaṅgāpekṣamuta
karaṇopakārāpekṣamiti ।</p>
<p>etaduktaṃ bhavati---kiṃ padārthavattayā sādṛśyaṃ uta karaṇopakarāvattayeti । tatra
yadi padārthavattayā sādṛśyaṃ tadā kāryānapekṣāḥ prākṛtāḥ padārthā eva vikṛtāvati-
diśyante tadā teṣu karaṇopakārāntaraṃ kalpyam । tajjananārthaṃ ca padārthānāṃ dvāramā-
śrayaṇīyam । tatra yasya dṛṣṭaṃ dvāraṃ na sambhavati tasyādṛṣṭaṃ kalpyate । tataśca kāryābhāvo
na śakyate vaditum । atha tu karaṇopakāra eva prathamamatidiśyate paścāttajjana-
kākāṅkṣāyāṃ padārthā atidiśyante tadā yenaiva dvāreṇaṃ teṣāṃ prakṛtāvupakārasambandhaḥ
vikṛtāvapi tenaiva dvāreṇa । tadabhāvātkāryābhāvaḥ । tataśca bādha iti । tatra ca
pūrvapakṣavādī aṅgāpekṣaṃ sādṛśyamiti manyate ।</p>
<p><q>ko'bhiprāyaḥ</q> ? abhiprāyaṃ pṛcchataścāyamāśayaḥ---apūrvaṃ hi vaikṛtaṃ karaṇo-
pakārameva prathamamākāṅkṣati na kevalān padārthān । tataścopakārameva tadvadbhāvena
gṛhlātīti yuktam । uttaraṃ---<q>nahyaṅgāvamarśādṛte tadanuṣṭhānāvamarśa upapadyata iti</q>
﻿<pb n="314"/>
<q>nāgṛhītaviśeṣaṇānyāyena pūrvapakṣitam</q> । asyārthaḥ ---satyaṃ prathamamupakārāpekṣā,
kintu prakṛtāvapi upakārasya kalpyatvāt yaḥ prayājādibhirupakāro bhavati so'tropa-
kāra iti padārthapurassara evopakārāvamarśaḥ vikṛtāvapyupakārākāṅkṣāyāṃ padārthapurassarasya
tasyaiva buddhau sannidhānam । tatra prathamopanipātinaḥ padārthāneva vidhiḥ gṛhṇāti ।
yathā ākṛtiviśiṣṭapadārthābhidhānāśrayaṇapakṣe prathamopanipatitāmākṛtimeva śabdo
'bhidadhāti । nāgṛhītaviśeṣaṇā viśeṣye buddhiriti ākṛteḥ prathamāvagamāditi ।
evaṃ cet padārthāneva cedvidhirgṛhṇāti tadā'prākṛtakāryasyāpyanuṣṭhānaṃ pūrvāktayā nītyā
kāryaṃ kalpyaṃ kṛṣṇaleṣviva pākasyeti ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate ....nāṅgāpekṣo'yamatideśaḥ tadvadbhāvena vikṛtau
nāṅgānyatidiśyante, kintūpakāra eva । paścāt‍tu tajjanakākāṅkṣāyāṃ aṅgā-
nāmatideśaḥ</q> । kutastadvadbhāvena nāṅgānāmatideśa ityatrāha---<q>prakṛtāvapyanuṣṭhānā-
pekṣa evāṅgaiḥ sambandhaḥ । anyathā sambandha eva na syāt</q> । asyārthaḥ ---
sādhyabhūtasya vidhyarthānuṣṭhānāpekṣaiva prathamamupajāyate na punastadanapekṣayā'ṅgānāmapekṣā ।
tataśca yadyapyaṅgāni prathamamavamṛśyante tathāpi teṣāṃ tadānīmanapekṣitatvādupekṣaṇameva ।
paścādupasthitamapi anuṣṭhānameva svīkaraṇīyam । tasmin svīkṛte paścāt tajjanakā-
kāṅkṣāyāṃ anuṣṭhānajanakatayā prakṛtau pratipannasambandhānāṃ anuṣṭhānenaivopasthāpitānāṃ
padārthānāṃ svīkaraṇam na kevalaṃ vikṛtau, prakṛtāvapyanuṣṭhānāpekṣa evāṅgaiḥ sambandhaḥ ।
yadyapi niyogaṃ prati prathamamanapekṣitānuṣṭhānā eva padārthā aidamarthyamātreṇa sambaddhāḥ
tathāpi teṣāṃ pratipanno'pyasau sambandhaḥ upakārākāṅkṣayā vinā nāvakalpetetya-
pratītāveva sambandhapratītiriti kalpyate, niyogaikyāvagamādvā sarvasya karaṇabhāvaḥ1 ।
karaṇopakārākāṅkṣāṃ vinā niyogaikyena sambandhaḥ kalpyamānaḥ karaṇabhāvenaiva syāt ।
karaṇopakāralakṣaṇakāryāpekṣatve tu vidhyarthasya tajjanakatayaiva sambandhānnāyamasambandha-
lakṣaṇo doṣaḥ । yadi prakṛtāvapyupakārākāṅkṣayaivāṅgaiḥ sambandhaḥ kastarhi prakṛti-
vikṛtyorviśeṣa ityāha - <q>iyāṃstu viśeṣaḥ । tādarthyamātreṇānvitābhidhānāt</q>
prathamaṃ padārthasambandhe sati prakṛtau paścāt karaṇopakāralakṣaṇakāryaviśeṣāvagamaḥ ।
vikṛtau tasyopakāraviśeṣasyāvagamādaṅgānāṃ sambandhaḥ । upasaṃharati---<q>atastadva-
dbhāve gamyamāne pūrvāvagatamapyaṅgajātaṃ apūrvasambandhe svahetuṃ karaṇopakāra</q>-
<note>1. R ṇābhāvaḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="315"/>
<q>mapekṣata iti svahetvapekṣa evāyamartho grahītavyaḥ । yo'sau karaṇopakāra-
lakṣaṇo'ṅgasambandhahetuḥ tadapekṣa evāyaṃ prakṛtivadvikṛtiḥ kartavyetyayamartho
grahītavyaḥ ।</q> upakārasādṛśyameva tadvadbhāvenocyata1 ityarthaḥ । <q>padārthāpekṣitatve punaḥ
padārthāntarāṇāmapi anavasthaivetikartavyatākāṅkṣāyāḥ</q> ।</p>
<p>asyārthaḥ ---yadi padārthā evākāṅkṣyante tadā kāryasya akāryasya cāviśeṣe-
ṇākāṅkṣeti sarvapadārthānāṃ padārthāntarāpekṣāyāṃ anavasthaivetikartavyatāṅkṣāyāḥ । yadā tu
karaṇopakāra ākāṅkṣyate tadā kāryasyaivākaṅkṣā nānyasyeti yuktā vyavasthā ।
tadāha---<q>na kāryāt karaṇopakārādṛte vyavasthāpapadyate</q> । tasminnapekṣyamāṇe
vyavasthopapadyata ityarthaḥ ।</p>
<p>kiñca vikṛtiṣu codapadeśābhāvāt sambandhānavagatiḥ । yadi tu karaṇopakārā-
kāṅkṣā nāsti kathaṃ vikṛtiṣu prākṛtānāṃ padārthānāṃ sambandhaḥ pūrvapakṣepi hi karaṇopa-
kārāpekṣāyāmeva padārthāḥ karaṇopakāraviśeṣaṇatvenāvatiṣṭhante । tadabhāve tu teṣāmupa-
sthānameva nāstīti kathaṃ sambandhaḥ ? tasmādvikṛtiṣu sambandhaḥ prākṛtānāṃ padārthānāṃ
na syādityatrāha---<q>prakṛtau hi niyogaikyanibandhanaḥ padārthānāmupadeśa iti
saptamādye sthite</q> adhikārabhedādvikṛtiṣu durlabhaḥ sambandha iti । tasmādvikṛtyapūrvāṇāṃ
upakārākāṅkṣā āśrayaṇīyā । tasyāṃ cāśritāyāṃ upakāra eva prathamaṃ sambadhyate ।
ataḥ upakāralakṣaṇakāryānusāryeva vikṛtiṣu padārthānāṃ sambandhaḥ । tasmāt tadvadbhāvo-
'pyanuṣṭhānāpekṣa iti siddham । sarvatra karaṇopakāranibandhanameva <q>tādarthyamiti
darśayitumāha---yatrāpi śrutiliṅgavākyāni padārthānvayahetavaḥ santi
tatrāpyanapekṣe śabde kāryalakṣaṇa eva sambandhaḥ kiṃ punaḥ prakaraṇādīnām yeṣāṃ
kāryanibandhana evātmalābhaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---yatrāpi padārthānvayarūpo yaḥ sambandhaḥ
tasya hetavaḥ pratipādakāni śrutiliṅgāvākyāni santi tatrāpyupakāralakṣaṇa eva padārthā-
nāmaidamarthyena sambandhaḥ ।</p>
<p>kathaṃ punaḥ padārthānvayavyatiriktaḥ kāryalakṣaṇo'paraḥ sambandho'bhyupagamyata iti ?
atrocyate---anapekṣaḥ śabda iti yadyapi pramāṇāntarānna pramīyate tathāpi śabdenāva-
gamyata eva । yeṣāṃ punaḥ prakaraṇasthānasamākhyānāṃ kāryanibandhana evātmalābhaḥ
<note>1. R nāvagamyate</note>
﻿<pb n="316"/>
teṣāṃ sutarāṃ kāryanibandhana eva sambandhaḥ । karaṇopakāranibandhana eva padārthānvayo'pi
prakaraṇādiṣu padārthānvaya1 eva śrutyādīnāṃ vyavahāra iti tṛtīye darśitam ।</p>
<p>tasmānna kāryaśūnyaṃ prayoktavyamiti nivṛttistasyeti bādhavidaḥ । kṛṣṇaleṣu tu
upadeśādvaiṣamyam । upadeśabalenādṛṣṭārtho'pi kṛṣṇaleṣu pākaḥ kriyata iti ।</p>
<p>atra cāyaṃ saṃkṣepārthaḥ---ākāṅkṣāsannidhiyogyatā anvitābhidhānahetavaḥ ।
tatra prathamaṃ kathamiti vidheḥ karaṇopakārākāṅkṣā । prākṛtaścopakāraḥ pratyakṣavacanena
nāmnā codanāliṅgena ca sannidhāpyate । yogyaścāsāviti tadanvito vidhyarthaḥ
svaśabdenābhidhīyate । sā ceyamupakāraprāptiratideśo'nyadīyasyānyatra sambandhāt ।
aupadeśikī ca upadeśaprameyatvāt । yacca sākṣācchabdena vidhyarthaṃ pratyupādīyate
yacca vidhyarthena vākyaprameyena2 tatsarvamaupadeśikameva । upakāraśca vidhyarthenopasthāpanīya
eva prakṛtivat । prakṛtau vidhyartha evopakāraṃ kalpayitvopasthāpayati । vikṛtau tu
prakṛtiklṛptameva paraṃ vidhyarthānvitopakāraṃ vidhyarthaḥ sannidhāpayatīti । viśeṣaniyame
codanāliṅgādīnāṃ vyāpāraḥ ।</p>
<p>kiñca pratyakṣavacanopaneyo nām‍nopaneyaśca sutarāmaupadeśikaḥ, paṭyamānākṣara-
samarpitatvāt । codanāliṅgopaneyaḥ satyāṃ vidherākāṅkṣāyāṃ buddhistho bhavati nānyatheti
so'pi vidhyarthopaneya iti । evaṃ copadiṣṭatvamatidiṣṭatvaṃ ca viruddham upadeśaprameyatayo-
padiṣṭatvaṃ, anyadīyasyānyatra sambandhādatidiṣṭatvam । punaśca vidharupakāre labdhe
tajjanakākāṅkṣāyāṃ prakṛtāviva padārthāstenaivopakāreṇa tajjanyenopasthāpitā anvayaṃ
gacchanti ākāṅkṣāsannidhiyogyatānāmanvayahetūnāṃ vidyamānatvāt । anvayaśca
guṇapradhānabhāvamantareṇa na sambhavatīti vidhyarthaḥ pradhānabhūtaḥ padārthāśca guṇabhūtāḥ
pratīyante । tena guṇabhūtaprākṛtapadārthānvito vidhyarthaḥ svaśabdenābhidhīyate । tathā ca
sati padārthānāmapyatideśaḥ siddho bhavati ।</p>
<p>yadi hi padārthānāmapi vikṛtyapūrvasambandho na bhavet tadā teṣāṃ prakṛteranyatra
sambandhābhāvāt atideśo na syāt । darśitasteṣāmapi vikṛtyapūrvaṃ prati aidamarthyalakṣaṇaḥ
sambandhaḥ । yastu teṣāṃ vikṛtāvaṅgatāṃ necchati tasya dvādaśāhikavidhyantagrāhiṣu satreṣu
<note>1. R nvaye ca</note>
<note>2. R vākyamayena</note>
﻿<pb n="317"/>
jyautiṣṭomikāṅgaprāptirna syāt । dvādaśāhe teṣāmanaṅgatvāt anaṅgasya bādhānavagamāt ।
anaṅgasya ca ādhānapavamāneṣṭigodohanāderiva prāp‍tyabhāvāt । na ca pradhānacodanayā
prākṛtānāṃ prāptirasti । kintvanuṣṭhānajñāpanamātrameva । taccāviśeṣeṇaupadeśikānāṃ
prākṛtānāṃ ca । tataśca prākṛtebhyaḥ parato vaikṛtānāmanuṣṭhānaṃ na syāt । yadi
pradhānacodanāyā paṭhitā eva prākṛtā bhaveyuḥ tadā pradhānānantaraṃ teṣāmanuṣṭhānaṃ (a)pāṭhataḥ
syāt । tathā prasajyapratiṣedhābhyupagamena yaḥ prākṛtena saha vikṛtau vidhīyate sa na
syāt । yadi hi aṅgaṃ prākṛtaḥ padārthaḥ syāt tadā tulyabalatvādvikalpo bhavet ।
anaṅgatve tu anṛtavadanapratiṣedhavat ekāntataḥ pratiṣedha eva syāt pratiṣedhasyāṅgatvena
śīghraprayukteḥ । aṅge hyāśuprayuktiḥ । anaṅge tu aṅgaprayuktidvāreṇa vilambiteti । granthaśca
sarvatra padārthātideśamanabhyupagacchato viruddha‍yata1 ityalamatiprasaṅgena ।</p>
<p>na ca vācyaṃ kathamanyadīyāḥ padārthā anyatra sambadhyante viniyuktaviniyoga-
virodhāditi ca, yato viniyuktaviniyoge hi pratītivirodhaḥ । yadi tulyavat
vikṛtāvapi sambandho'bhyupagataḥ syāt tadā syāt pratītivirodhaḥ । yathā yad-
devadattīyaṃ tadyajñadattīyamiti । yadā tu tadvadbhāvenopakārasambandhaḥ paścāt tajjanaka-
tvāt padārthāḥ sambadhyante tadā na kaściddoṣaḥ । yathā upakāre tadvadbhāvena sambadhya-
māne na pratītivirodhaḥ anyathā hyupakāro'pi kathamanyadīyo'nyatra sambadhyeta ।
na ca vācyamupakāraḥ prakṛtāvaṅgabhūta eva na bhavatīti, asambandhaprasaṅgāt । na hyanyathā
tasyāpūrvasambandho ghaṭate । asati ca sambandho'nyadīyasyānyatra sambandha ityetadeva
na syāt । yaścāyaṃ padārthātideśaḥ sa kāryapramāṇako nopadeśaprameyaḥ । pāṭhena vā
vidhyarthena vā'nupasthāpitatvāt । na hi vidhyarthena padārthā upasthāpyante kintu kāryeṇa
upakārākhyena upadeśakāryapramāṇakena adhyāyaṣaṭkeṇa । yathoktaṃ aupadeśikī
pratītirvicāritā, idānīṃ kāryato'dhigatiścintyata iti kāryaṃ ca karaṇopakārādi-
kamabhipretaṃ, na niyogaḥ । 2niyogakārye gṛhyamāṇe caturthādhyāyacintāpi dvitīyaṣaṭke
syāditi ।</p>
<p>nanūpakārasyaupadeśikatvāttadupaneyāḥ padārthāḥ api kimityaupadeśikā na
bhavanti । ucyate । upadeśo hi vidhyarthapratipādako granthasandarbhaḥ na vidhyarthasāpekṣaḥ
bhavanti । ucyate । upadeśo hi vidhyarthapratipādako granthasandarbhaḥ na vidhyarthasāpekṣaḥ
<note>1. virudhyata</note>
<note>2. R niyogekārye</note>
﻿<pb n="318"/>
upadeśo bhavati । tena vidhyarthasāpekṣācchabdādyadevāvagamyate tadevaupadeśikam ।
yacca kāryeṇāvagamyate yaccopadeśena tadubhayamapi śābdameva । śābdatve tvayaṃ vibhāgaḥ-
kiñciccaupadeśikaṃ, kiñjicca kāryagamyamiti kṛtamatibahunā ।</p>
<p><q>kiṃ bhavati prayojanaṃ kathaṃ vā vaikṛtamudāhriyata iti ko'bhiprāyaḥ ?</q>
ekagranthenāha---<q>luptakāryaṃ nivartata iti prayojanamuditaṃ, tena prayojanaṃ tāba-
tsiddham । sarvāsu ca vikṛtiṣu kāryābhāvānnivṛttiriti</q> । udāharaṇamapi
(na)spaṣṭam । ataḥ kenābhiprāyeṇa prayojanodāharaṇapraśnaḥ । uttaraṃ---<q>ayamabhiprāyaḥ
yatra tāvatsvatantraṃ kāryoddeśena vā anyasya vidhānaṃ tata eva tatra nivṛttiḥ
sāmānyasya ko viṣaya iti</q> । asyārthaḥ---yatra na vidhānaṃ yathā ṣoḍaśinaṃ na
gṛhṇātīti, tathā kāryoddeśenānyasya vidhānaṃ yathā śaramayaṃ barhirbhavatīti tatra tata eva
nivṛttiḥ, na tatkāryābhāvena । yā punariyaṃ kāryābhāvena sāmānyena nivṛttiḥ tasyāḥ
ko viṣaya iti । viṣayājñānāduktāmapi nivṛttiṃ aviṣayajñatayā prayojanatvena amanya-
māno dvayaṃ 1tatra pṛṣṭavān । evaṃ pṛṣṭe ayaṃ viṣaya iti pradarśitam viṣaya-
prayojanadvayam ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ vā</q></p>
<p><q>kena punarviśeṣeṇedamadhikaraṇamārabhyate ?</q> uttaraṃ---<q>evaṃ tāvat sāmā-
nyaviṣayaṃ sūtramupavarṇitam । idānīṃ tu viśeṣeṇa varṇyate</q> । sāmānyaviśeṣa-
viṣayatayā'paunaruktyamiti bhāvaḥ । ākṣipati---<q>nanu sāmānyenaiva cintitam ।
ato'bhimatasarvaviśeṣā udāharaṇaṃ bhavanti kiṃ viśeṣacintayā</q> ? samādhatte
<q>astyasmin viṣaye viśeṣaḥ । kiṃ punarasau</q> ?---<q>pākavadaprākṛtakāryamapi
bhavatyevāvaghātādi ko'bhiprāyaḥ ?</q> uttaraṃ---<q>caruśabdaśravaṇāt pākasyaivā-
trāpi prāptiṃ manyat pūrvapakṣavādī</q> । asyārthaḥ---acarau caruśabdaprayogo'yaṃ
carudharmāḥ kāryānapekṣāḥ kathaṃ syuriti । kāryaṃ hi āgneyasya labdhameva । tadarthaḥ
caruśabdo bhavati । kintu kāryānapekṣo'carau carudharmātideśārthaḥ । tataśca pāko'pi
caruśabdaśravaṇādeva । pākavaccāvaghātādayo'pi bhavitumarhanti । yenābhiprāyeṇāpūrvaṃ
<note>1. adds barhirbhavatīti</note>
﻿<pb n="319"/>
pṛṣṭavān idānīṃ rāddhāntī tamabhiprāyamāha---<q>nanu ca ghṛte śrapayatīti vacanādeva
pākaprāptiḥ</q> । pariharati---<q>ghṛtārthaṃ tadvacataṃ na pākavidhānārthamiti manyate
pūrvapakṣavādī</q> । tasmāccaruśabdanibandhanaivātrāpi prāptiriti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntī pṛcchati---<q>kiṃ caruśabdaḥ kāryaprayuktatāṃ karaṇopakāra-
prayuktatāṃ vihanti dharmāṇām</q> । kāryaprayuktatvāvidhāte hi kāryameva prayojakamiti
bhāvaḥ । pūrvapakṣyāha---<q>vihanti kāryaprayuktatāmasmin‍nudāharaṇe । kathaṃ vihanti</q> ?
uttaraṃ---<q>caruśabdo'yaṃ viśadasiddhaudane prayuktaḥ, na cātra kṛṣṇaleṣu viklṛtti-
phalaḥ pacerarthaḥ pāko'sti</q> kṛṣṇaleṣu । tena viśadasiddhamadanīyametaddhavirbhavati ।
tasmādacarau caruśabdo'yaṃ caruvadityevaṃ gauṇo draṣṭavyaḥ । tataḥ caruśabdenaitaduktaṃ
bhavati - acarau carudharmāḥ kartavyā iti । dharmanibandhanaṃ sādṛśyam । kasmātpunargoṇa
ityatrāha---<q>anāñ‍jasatvācchrapaṇasya</q> । tena viśadasiddhirnāstīti paraśabdaḥ paratra
prayujyamāno gauṇaḥ । vācanika eva kimiti na bhavatītyāha---<q>na vacanaśatenāpi
śabdasya śaktyantarakalpanā bhavatīti tatra tatra darśitam</q> । tena tatra
mukhyo na bhavati pravṛttiviśeṣakaratayā dharmasādṛśyādanuṣṭhānaparo'yaṃ caruśabdo'gnihotra-
vaditi ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntabādī tu havissāmānyādapi caruśabdopapatteḥ śravaṇayogādvā
yāvadvacanaṃ vācanikamiti manyate</q> । asyārthaḥ---siddhasādṛśyenāpi caruśabdo-
papattiḥ । siddhaṃ ca sādṛśyaṃ haviṣṭevana śrapyamāṇatvena ca । pravṛttiviśeṣakaratā ca
prayojanamātram । agnihotrādiṣu tūpakārāpekṣāyāṃ apekṣitasamarpakatayā kāryasādṛśyā-
śrayaṇam । iha tūpakārākāṅkṣā pūritaiva1 pratyutānapekṣitā'vadhātādiṣu anuṣṭhānārtha-
tvenānapekṣitavidhitvam । tasmāt ya eva sākṣātpāko vihito vacanena sa eva kartavyo
nāvaghātādi ।</p>
<p><q>nanu vacanamevedaṃ śrapaṇavidhānāya nopapadyate । viklṛtterabhāvāt ।
tasya pacyarthatvāditi</q> codyamātram । uttaraṃ---<q>yathopapadyate vacanaṃ tathopariṣṭā-
dvakṣyāmaḥ</q> ।</p>
<note>1. A tvaritaiva</note>
﻿<pb n="320"/>
<p>evaṃ vā ।</p>
<p><q>atra ko viśeṣaḥ</p> ? uttaraṃ---<p>aniś‍cite bādhapramāṇāsambhavaḥ</q> ।
asyārthaḥ---kāryābhāve hi (hya)niścite bādhaḥ pramāṇavān । yatra tu kāryābhāvaḥ
sandigdhaḥ tatra niṣpramāṇako bādhaḥ । ākṣipati---<q>anuṣṭhānaṃ vā</q> kathaṃ ? yathā
kāryābhāvāniścayādbādho nopapadyate tathā <q>kāryasadbhāvāniścayādanuṣṭhānamapi । kathaṃ</q> ?
uttaraṃ---<q>nātideśo niścayamapekṣate prayogasya</q> । asyārthaḥ---yadyapi prayogo na
niścitaḥ pratipattitvādurukramejyāyāḥ । pratipattirhi dravyaṃ na prayuṅkte । kintu
dravyeṇaiva prayujyate । kādācitkaṃ ca dravyaṃ yat sph‌yāśliṣṭaṃ avamṛditaṃ ca । tenā-
niścitaprayogeyaṃ pratipattiḥ । tathāpi cāsyāṃ prākṛtānāmaṅgānāmatideśo niścita eva ।
tatra yadi viṣṇorāvāhanaṃ kriyate tadā yadyupanipatet urukramejyā tadā saguṇā bhavati ।
anyathā hyupanipatitā satī viguṇā syāt ।</p>
<p>atha nopanipatet tadā kṛtepi āvāhane na kācit kṣatirityarthaḥ । sandehe-
pyāvāhanaṃ kartavyam । ārthasandeho'pi pravṛttyaṅgam । yadyatideśaḥ prayoganiścayaṃ
nāpekṣate kiṃ tarhyapekṣata ityatrāha---<q>śāstraniścayānusārī hi saḥ niś‍citañca
<quote>“yadadho'vamṛdyet”</quote></q> iti śāstram । tena śāstrānusāreṇa tāvadidamekaṃ karma niścitam
tatra cātideśo'pi niścitaḥ । tasmātprayogāniścayo nātideśaṃ bādhituṃ kṣamate,
atidiṣṭaṃ cāṅgamiti kartavyamevāvāhanam । na cātra rājāmātyāmantraṇādivat dṛṣṭaṃ
kiñjidviruddha‍yata ityapratipakṣo'yamatideśaḥ ।</p>
<p>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---<q>satyamāha bhavān yadyatra śāstrārthādhikāro'pi
niścitaḥ syāt । yathāśāstraṃ niś‍citaṃ naimittikasvarūpaṃ śāstrārthaḥ pratipādya-
dravyanimittako'yaṃ pratipattāvadhikāraḥ aniścitaṃ caitannimittaṃ pratipādyadravyaṃ
tadanusāri ca śāstraṃ tathaiva</q> । yadyapi svarūpataḥ śāstraṃ niścitaṃ, (na)tathāpi
kratvadhikārapratipādakatayā tvaniścitamityuktam । <q>tasmādvādhavadatideśo'pi na
niścayādṛte śakyate vak‍tum</q> । yathā bādhaḥ 1kāryāvilopaniścayaṃ vinā na śakyate
vak‍tuṃ tathā'tideśo'pi adhikāraniścayaṃ vinā na śakyate । tasmādananuṣṭhānamevātra
jyāyaḥ tadidamuktam---<q>na cānārabdhe prayoge'ṅgaṃ kṛtamupakārakaṃ bhavatīti</q> ।
<note>1. R kāryābhāva</note>
﻿<pb n="321"/>
prayogānārambheṇānadhikāraṃ darśayati---<q>anadhikāre cānatideśaḥ tataścānaṅgasyānu-
pakārakatvam</q> ।</p>
<p>nanu nātra niścitasya bādhaḥ, aniścitamevedaṃ śāstramityuktaṃ tvayā । tataśca
niścitamithyātvalakṣaṇo'tra pratijñāto bādho na śakyate vak‍tum । ucyate । na ।
śāstraṃ niścite, kāraṇāntareṇānicaya ukto mithyābhāva eva । yadyapyetatsvarūpataḥ śāstraṃ
niścitaṃ tathāpi nimittāniścayādaniścitaṃ kāraṇāntaravaśena । nimittasya pramāṇāntara-
vedyatvāt dvāravat । yathā dvāraṃ pramāṇāntaravedyaṃ tadabhā(vo)ve mithyātvaṃ tathā nimittamapi
pramāṇāntaravedyaṃ tadaniścaye śāstrasyāpi adhikārahetutayā'niścitatvam ।</p>
<p><q>nanu mithyābhāvo bādha ityuktam nāniścayaḥ</q> tataśca pratijñātabādha-
svarūpabāhyatvādihāsaṅgatiriti bhāvaḥ । uttaraṃ---<q>aniścayo'pi mithyābhāva</q>
eva । kuta ityāha---<q>adhyavasāyahetuḥ pramāṇaṃ tadabhāvo mithyātvaṃ, abhāve ca
kāryāniścaye ca tulyamanadhyavasānamiti mithyātvāviśeṣādbādha eva । na
cāniścite'nuṣṭhānaṃ sambhavati iti</q> । asyārthaḥ---yadeva niścitaṃ sannānuṣṭhīyeta
tadananuṣṭhāne vaiguṇyaṃ pramāṇāyattatvāt viguṇabhāvasya । aniścite cānanuṣṭhīyamāne
vaiguṇyaṃ nāstīti ananuṣṭhānamevātrāvāhanasya yuktam । tasmānniścita eva śāstrārthaḥ
svarūpataḥ । upādhinibandhana evātrāpi mithyābhāva iti nimittānutpatteranārambhaḥ
urukramejyāyāḥ na punaraniścayācchāstrārthasya । tataḥ kimityāha---<q>ārambhaprayuktaṃ
cāṅgānāmanuṣṭhānam</q> । tasmānniścitamevāṅgānuṣṭhānam pradhānārambheṇāṅgānāma-
nuṣṭhānam । pradhānaṃ cādhikārābhāvānnārabdham । ato'ṅgānuṣṭhāne prayojako nāstīti
ananuṣṭhānamevāvāhanasyeti hetoḥ sūktam---<quote>“na cānārabdhe prayoge aṅgakṛtamupakārakaṃ
bhavati”</quote> iti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 2 ।। iṣṭirārambhasaṃyogādaṅgabhūtatvānnivartetārambhasya pradhāna-
saṃyogāt ।। 4 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>atrātmārambhāparityāgena dīkṣaṇīyāderaṅgatvamiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</q> ।
yadyapi jyotiṣṭomāṅgabhūtā dīkṣaṇīyādayaḥ tathāpi teṣāmārambho'styeveti ārambhā-
vaiguṇyāya ārambhaṇīyā kartavyā ।</p>
﻿<pb n="322"/>
<p>rāddhāntastu prayogāntaracodanaiveyam । yeyaṃ jyotiṣṭomena svargakāmo yajeteti
codanā sā prayogāntarasya codanā saumikasya naiṣṭikasya । prayogāpekṣaścārambha uktaḥ ।
sa padārthaḥ ādyo vā bhavatu audīsīnyādvā pracyutiḥ ubhayathāpi na dīkṣaṇīyāprayogā-
pekṣaḥ । kathaṃ teṣāṃ prayogo nāstītyatrāha-<q>jyotiṣṭomaprayogacodanaiṣā na dīkṣaṇī-
yāderyataḥ</q> । tasmālluptanimittamārambhaṇīyādi na kriyeta dīkṣaṇīyādyartham । api
cetyabhyuccayamātram nyāyavyutpattiparatvādadhikāraṇasya । ataḥ prabhṛti ca sthite nimitta-
dvārake bādhe tadbhāvamātraparīkṣaṇaṃ draṣṭavyam । nimittābhāvanibandhanatvāt nimittadvārako
bādha ityuktam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 3 ।। pradhānāccānyasaṃyuktāt sarvārambhānnivarte-
tānaṅgatvāt ।। 5 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>atrāṅgapradhānasādhāraṇaprayogacodaneti matvā pūrvapakṣavādī anvāra-
mbhaṇīyāṃ manyate</q> । pūrvatra hi pradhānasyaiva prayogo nāṅgānāmiti aṅgānāmārambhā-
bhāvāt tannimittamārambhaṇīyā na kartavyā । iha tvaiṣṭikānāmapi pradhānatvāt kartavyā-
'rambhaṇīyā । na ca jyotiṣṭomasyaiva prayogacodanā । etadeva vivṛṇoti---<q>nāya-
maniṣṭereva prayogaḥ jyotiṣṭomasyaiva । kiṃ tarhi ? sādhāraṇaḥ prayogaḥ
tenārambho'pi sādhāraṇaḥ tenārambhasya bhāvat kartavyā''rambhaṇīyā</q> ।
(na)[sa]ca jyotiṣṭomādīnāmavirodhamāvahati, kāṃsyabhojivadamukhyepīti nyāyāt ।
saumikadārvihaumikānāṃ hi kriyamāṇāyāmārambhaṇīyāyāṃ na kaścidvirodhaḥ । akriyamā-
ṇāyāṃ vā aiṣṭikānāṃ vaiguṇyam । yathā kāṃsyabhojinaḥ śiṣyasya kāṃsye'nupātte ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntaikadeśī pūrvapakṣamākṣipati---<q>kimidaṃ vacanaṃ na paśyati agniṣṭomaṃ
prathamamāharatīti</q> । anena kila vacanena anvārambhaṇīyākārye'gniṣṭomavidhānāt
śaravidhānādiva barhirāmbhaṇīyā nivartata iti manyat । samādhatte---<q>bāḍhaṃ paśyati
vacanaṃ, kintu phalārthasyaivāgniṣṭomasyāyaṃ prathamaprayogo abhidhīyate ।
nārambhaṇīyārthena vidhānamiti paśyati</q> kramamātravidhānaparamidaṃ vacanaṃ nārambhaṇīyā-
pratyāmnāyārtham ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---nārambhaṇīyā</q> kartavyā yasmāda<q>gniṣṭomārambho'yaṃ
prayoga uktaḥ</q> । asya granthasyārthamabuddhvā ārambhaṇīyākārye vidhānābhiprāyametaditi
﻿<pb n="323"/>
matvā codayati-<q>satyamuktaṃ nānvārambhaṇīyārthenāgniṣṭomavidhānamiti1</q> । rāddhāntī
pariharati---<q>kena coktamanvārambhaṇīyārthenāgniṣṭomavidhānamiti</q> । evamapyā-
śayamajānānaś‍codayati---<q>yadyārambhaṇīyārthena vidhānaṃ na sambhavati kimiti
tarhi aluptārthā ārambhaṇīyā na kriyate</q> । pariharati-iṣṭī<q>nāmagniṣṭomārambheṇā-
mbhāvalopāt</q> । asyārthaḥ---agniṣṭomasya 2prathamānuṣṭhānāt gṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatayā tasyai-
vārambhaḥ । tadārambheṇaivaiṣṭikānāmapi karmaṇāmanuṣṭhānamiti teṣāmārambhāvalopāt
ārambhaṇīyā na kartavyā । na cāgniṣṭomārambho'nvārambhaṇīyāṃ prayojayati । na cāsau
kṛtārambhaṇīyasya bhavatītyuktaṃ kāraṇāntarasyārambhaṇīyāṃ prati aprayojakatvena । tasmā-
datrāpyananvārambhaṇīyaka eva prayoga iti siddham ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 4 ।। tasyāṃ tu syāt prayājavat ।। 6 ।।</l></lg>
<p>atra pūrvapakṣamākṣipati---<q>nanu cārambhaṇīyāśāstre prakṛtivadvidhānaṃ
nānvārambhaṇīyākāryamatideṣṭuṃ kṣamam । kutaḥ ? anenaivārambhaṇīyākārya-
vidhānaśās‍treṇaiva kāryamavagacchāmo'traivātidiśāma iti</q> । bālakrīḍitamet ।
ātmāśrayadoṣaprasaṅgāt । tasmānnātra nirākaraṇīyamiva kiñcitpaśyāmaḥ ।</p>
<p>samādhātaikadeśyāha-<q>atrocyate aparisamāptadharmakaṃ vā darśapūrṇamāsānu-
ṣṭhānaṃ, kathaṃ tadvadityatideṣṭuṃ śakyate</q> । asyārthaḥ- ārambhaṇīyayaiva saha
darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ itikartavyatā kalpyate3 । tataścārambhaṇīyāṃ parityajya darśapūrṇamāsayo-
rupakāro nātideṣṭuṃ śakyate । tena prayājādyatideśābhyupagame ārambhaṇīyāpyatideṣṭa-
vyeti bhāvaḥ ।</p>
<p>ākṣeptā āha-<q>kathaṃ vā darśapūmāsopakāramapekṣate । anvārambhaṇīyāṅga-
kāryaṃ darśapūrṇamāsopakāramapekṣate । ātmāśrayadoṣaprasaṅgāt</q> । nyāyastāvadayaṃ
na kaściddoṣa iti । sa evāha---<q>kiṃ vā 4ātmapratyakṣasya hānam ?</q> yadyapi
<note>1. R nārambhaṇīyārthenetyuktam</note>
<note>2. A pradhānānu</note>
<note>3. A vakalpyate</note>
<note>4. R asma pra</note>
﻿<pb n="324"/>
aparisamāptadharmakaṃ darśapūrṇamāsānuṣṭhānaṃ nātidiśyate tathāpi asmākaṃ na kiñciddhīyate ।
samādhātaikadeśyāha---<q>yadyārambhaṇīyā nātidiśyate</q> tadā prayājāderapyanatideśaḥ ।
asampūrṇetikartavyatātideśāyogāt । iṣyate ca bhavadbhiḥ prayājāderatideśaḥ । tena
sa eva hīyate । ekagranthenāha---<q>tasmādanvārambhaṇīyāpi kartavyā । yadi
prayājāderatideśaḥ ārambhaṇīyā nātidiśyate tadā prayājādervā'natideśaḥ</q> ।
ākṣeptā āha---<q>varamanatideśo nyāyopapannaḥ prayājādīnāṃ na punarak‌lṛpta-
syopakārasyātideśaḥ</q> । ārambhaṇīyāyāṃ tu ārambhaṇīyākārye'tidiśyamāne
aklṛptasyaivopakārasyātideśa āpatati yathaitadvacanaṃ; sa cāyukta iti । parama-
samādhātā āha---<q>so'yaṃ <quote>‘āmrān pṛṣṭaḥ kovidārānācaṣṭe’</quote> ityāpatitam</q> ।
yathā kaś‍cicchūnyamānāḥ1 ke āmrā iti pṛṣṭaḥ tadvacanārthamabuddhvā āha---ime
kovidārā iti, tathaitatsakalamasmadvacanamabuddhvā coditaṃ bhavateti ।</p>
<p>samādhātā svābhiprāyaṃ prakaṭayati---<q>kṛtārambhaṇīyasya hi darśapūrṇamāsau
codyete, na punaḥ darśapūrṇamāsāṅgatvena codanā</q> । asyārthaḥ - nārambhaṇīyā
darśapūrṇamāsāṅgatvena codyate । kutaḥ ? (tataḥ)kṛtārambhaṇīyasyaiva hi puruṣasya darśapūrṇa-
māsau codyete । tena nārambhaṇīyāyāḥ darśapūrṇamāsāvikārāṅgatvam । <q>tataḥ kiṃ ?
idaṃ tato bhavati । na darśapūrṇamāsavidhyantātideśaḥ ārambhaṇīyāyāṃ śakyate
vārayitum । kutaḥ ? vināpyārambhaṇīyayā nirjñātopakāro darśapūrṇamāsa-
prayogo yataḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---aṅgānyeva gṛhītvā karaṇopakāraḥ parikalpyate ।
teṣāmeva tajjanakatvāt grāhakaidamarthyavaśenādṛṣṭamapi karaṇopakārakatvaṃ kalpyate ।
taccāṅgānāmeva grāhakaidamarthyam tenānaṅgabhūtānvārambhaṇīyāvyatirekeṇa nirjñātopakārāt
darśapūrṇamāsaprayogādārambhaṇīyāyāmatideśo na viruddha‍yate prayājādīnām । <q>nanu
cārambhaṇīyāpyevameva bhavitumarhati</q> । asyārthaḥ- yathā prakṛtau kṛtārambha-
ṇīyakena kṛtopakāraka ārambhaḥ iti ārambhaṇīyā prasajyate tathā ārambhaṇīyā-
yāmapyārambhaṇīyā prāpnoti । tataścāvyavasthādoṣeṇa vyavasthāsiddha‍yarthaṃ atideśatyāga-
eva yukta iti bhāvaḥ । pariharati---<q>satyametat ata evānadhikāramāśaṅka‍te
pūrvapakṣavādī</q> । yata evānvārambhaṇīyāsaṃskṛtena puruṣeṇa kṛta ārambha upakārako'ta
<note>1. R anyamanāḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="325"/>
eva dvitīyāmārambhaṇīyāṃ ārambhaṇīyāyāṃ anadhikāramāśaṅkate pūrvapakṣavādī, na
cānavasthetyupasaṃhāravyājena darśayati---<q>tasmāt sāmarthyato jyāyasīṃ vyavasthāṃ
manyate</q> । sarvāsvavasthāsu śaktireva niyāmikā । tena yāvacchaktyatideśo bhavati ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu---darśapūrṇamāsāvārabhamāṇa ityārambhaṇīyāyāmārabhamāṇo-
'dhikṛtaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---darśapūrṇamāsārambhapravṛttasyārambhaṇīyāyāmadhikārāt pṛthagāra-
mbhaṇīyāyāmārambho nāsti । tadāha---<q>ato'nanvārambhamārambhaṇīyāṃ prayok‍tu-
marhati । tasmānnādhikāramapekṣate ityā</q>mbhaṇīyatvaṃ nāpekṣata ityarthaḥ । tadidaṃ
kṛtārambhaṇīyatvaṃ niś‍cimapyārambhaṇīyāyāmadhikāre nimittanibandhanaṃ mithyātvaṃ gatam ।
ārambharūpanimittābhāve hi mithyābhāva ityarthaḥ ।</p>
<p>yaḥ punarayaṃ dvitīyaḥ parihāraḥ na tadeva śāstramarthadvayāya prabhavati ārambhaṇīyā-
kāryamavagamayituṃ tatra cātideṣṭumiti । aṅgatvābhyupagame na saḥ; aṅgatve hyārambhaṇīyā-
śāstramapyaṅgatvakalpanāyāṃ vyāpriyate । <q>nanu cāyamaṅgatvābhyupagamaḥ prayājādera-
pyatideśaṃ vārayati aparipūrṇadharmakasyopakārakasya anatideśāt</q> । pariharati
---<q>na, abhāvapradarśanamātraparatvāt</q> । ārambhaṇīyāyāmārambhaṇīyā nāsti ityetā-
vanmātraparametat । na cābhyupagame doṣāntarāpattiḥ । tasmātsūktam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 5 ।। karma ca dravyasaṃyogārthamarthābhāvānnivarteta tādarthyaṃ
śrutisaṃyogāt ।। 9 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>yūpotpattyarthatā asyā yūpāhuterna vidyata iti pūrvapakṣavādinaḥ</q> khale-
vālyāmapi yūpāhutiḥ kartavyeti vadato'bhiprāyaḥ । <q>kā yuktiḥ yūpānutpattyarthatve ?</q>
uttaraṃ---<q>takṣaṇādīnāmivotpattau na kaś‍cidva‍yāpāra upalabhyate । tasmāda-
dṛṣṭārthatayā parivyāṇādivat khalevālyāmapi yūpāhutiḥ kartavyā</q> । khadirā-
dayo hi yūpībhavanti । tatra ca yat khadirodiṣu vyāpriyate karma tasyaiva khadira-
saṃskāreṇa yūpotpattyarthatvaṃ yuktam । na ca yūpāhuteḥ khadirādau kaś‍cidva‍yāpāra
upalabhyate । tasmādadṛṣṭārthatayā parivyāṇādivat khalevālyāmapi yūpāhutiḥ kartavyā ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu satyaṃ na kaś‍cit dṛṣṭa upakāraḥ utpattāvupalabhyate
takṣaṇādiśabdena tūtpattyarthatāmavagacchāmaḥ yūpamaccheṣyatā hotavyamiti</q> ।
﻿<pb n="326"/>
kathaṃ ? acchośabdo hi āptumityasminnarthe prasiddha ityabhiyuktā upadiśanti । bhavatvā-
p‍tyarthatā । tathāpi kathamutpattyarthatetyāha---<q>utpattiścāptiryūpasya</q> । utpādayanneva
yūpamāpnoti yataḥ nānyena prakāreṇa । yato yūpotpattyarthatā'to na khalevālyāṃ kartavyā ।
ayūpe hi paśurbadhyata iti siddham । tena yūpe naiva prayojanamiti yūpārthā satī
na kriyate ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 6 ।। sthāṇau tu deśamātratvādanivṛttiḥ pratīyeta ।। 10 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nanu yūpasyotpādyatvena sarvayūpasambandhaṃ tadutpattyarthamityuktam</q> । yasya
yūpamaccheṣyateti yūpasambandho'vagamyate tadyūpotpattyarthaṃ yūpasyotpādyatvādityuktam । tena
sthāṇvāhutiryūpotpattyarthā । samādhatte---<q>satyamuktam tadevedamākṣipyate । kathamā-
kṣepaḥ ? sthāṇumātrasambandhāt sthāṇvāhuteḥ na yūpīyasthāṇusambandho'va-
gamyate</q> । kiṃ tarhi ? sthāṇumātrasambandhaḥ tataśca na yūpasambandho'vagamyate । asaṃyuktaśca
prakaraṇena gṛhyata ityārādupakārakatvam । idamatrākūtaṃ---saṃskāravaśena khadirādayo
yūpībhavanti । saṃskāraścāyaṃ laukikaḥ padārthaḥ saṃskārasambandhini vā kriyamāṇena
karmaṇā janyate । na ca sthāṇvāhutiryūpe yūpasambandhini vā kriyata iti asaṃskārikā ।
acchaśabdaśca kathañcidva‍yākhyeya iti । evaṃ ca yūpāhutirapyārādupakārikā ।
sāpi hi na yūpasambandhinī । atha yūpasamīpe kriyamāṇā yūpārthā । tatrāha---<q>kiñca
avaśyamevamabhyupagamanīyam yūpāhutiryūpasamīpe kriyamāṇatayā yūpasamba-
ndhinī na bhavatīti । anyathā yūpāhuterekādaśinyāṃ tantratā na syāt</q> ।
yadi yūpasamīpe kriyamāṇā yūpasambandhinī tadā samīpadeśabhedāt tantratā yūpāhuterna
syāt ।</p>
<p><q>nanu ca yūpāhutiryūpārthetyuktam । satyamuktaṃ tadevāyuktaṃ manyate</q> ।
tantratā vā hātavyā । yūpotpattyarthatā vā ityabhiprāyaḥ ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntastu---<q>accheṣyatīti vacanāt yūpārthaivāvagamyate sthāṇvāhuti-
riti ca yūpasambandhinyeva sthāṇau pratīyate</q> । na hi prakṛtaviśeṣaṇahāne pramāṇa-
masti । sthāṇuśabdo'yaṃ yaugiko vyaktivacanaḥ । vyaktivacanāśca sannihitāṃ vyaktiṃ
nātikrāmantīti yūpasambandhyeva sthāṇuḥ । nanu ca yadyapyasau(dāya) [na yūpa] sambandhī
tathāpi tato'pi yuktaḥ kathaṃ tatsambandhena yūpasaṃskāraḥ ityatrāha-<q>taruviyuktasaṃskāre'pi</q>
﻿<pb n="327"/>
<q>tadvataḥ saṃskāramicchanti laukikāḥ</q> yathā devadattaśiraso'vatāritāyāḥ srajaḥ
śucideśanidhānena saṃskṛtāyāḥ devadattasya saṃskāraḥ । laukikaścāyaṃ saṃskārapadārtho
'bhyupagato'vahantyādivat । śabdāttu niyamamātram । tena yūpasambandhisthāṇusambandhāt
sthāṇvāhuteryūpotpattyarthatā । yūpāhutestu antikadeśasyāvivakṣā । āpekṣikatvā-
dantikadeśasyetyuktam । tenaikatra kriyamāṇā yūpāhutiḥ kasalayūpāntikeṣu kṛtā
bhavati āpekṣikatvādantikedaśasya । tasmānna doṣastantratāyāḥ । yūpāntikeṣvapi
kriyamāṇāyāḥ yūpāhuteḥ tantratopapatteḥ tantratā yūpārthatāṃ na dūṣayatītyarthaḥ ।
<q>darśanamuktam</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 7 ।। prayāje ca tan‍nāyatvāt ।। 14 ।।</l></lg>
<p>svāhākāraṃ yajatīti dvitīyānirdeśāt devatābhidhānaṃ pūrvapakṣavādī manyate ।
yathā viṣṇuṃ yajatīti dvitīyānirdeśāt viṣṇordevatātvam tathā svāhākāraṃ yajatīti
svāhākārasyāpi । yuktyantaraṃ cāha---<q>karmābhidhānapakṣepi cārādupakārakameva
karmaṇaḥ prādhānyāt</q> । yadyapi svāhākāraśabdaḥ karmanāmadheyaṃ tathāpi dvitīyānirdeśāt
pradhānakarmāvagateḥ taddevatāsmaraṇārthatvam । tasmādva‍yatiriktārthataiva varam । yadi hi
sannipatyopakārakatā karmaṇaḥ syāt tadā tallobhenāvyatiriktārthatā yajatiśabdāt
svāhākāraśabdasyāṅgīkriyate । yadā tu karmanāmadheyatvepyārāpupakārakatā tadā
kimarthaṃ tadvyatiriktārthatā nāśrī('ṅgīkri)yate varaṃ vyatiriktārthataiva bhavatu । tathā sati
ko guṇa ityāha-<q>padabhedaścāsmin pakṣe nyāyyo bhavati arthabhedāt</q> । anyathā
hi arthābhede'pi padabhedābhyupagamaḥ kāryaḥ । na caitaducitam । anyāyaścānekaśabda-
tvamiti ।</p>
<p>nanvevaṃ kathaṃ svāhākārasya śabdamātrasyāgnyādiśabdaiḥ mantragatairabhidhānaṃ itya-
trāha---<q>agnyādīnāṃ ca śabdānāṃ guṇādapyabhidhānasiddhiriti samañ‍jasam</q> ।
guṇayoge na mukhyā vṛttirbhaviṣyati yadi vā gauṇīvṛttiḥ śaktyantarakalpanā vā
jyotirādipadānāmiva । yathā jyotirādayaḥ karmaṇyapi vartante tathā'gnyādayo'pi
svāhākāre tathā darśitaṃ bhāṣye । māteti śabdo mātaramapi vakti mātāramapi
dhānyādīnāṃ iti । yadi punaragnyādayo devatāḥ tadā1devatānāmagnyādīnāmapi
<note>1. A devatānāmapikalpanāt</note>
﻿<pb n="328"/>
vikalpaḥ syāt mantrasya vibhāgaḥ syāt । tatteddevatāprakāśakabhāgakalpanayā tadāha---
<q>anyathā hi devatāvikalpaḥ syāt1 mantravibhāgaś‍ceti</q> । tasmādetaditara-
prayājavadayamapyārādupakāraka iti sāhacaryamapyupanyastam । evaṃ pūrvapakṣitam ।
samprati codayati---nanu gauṇe sambhavati śaktyantarakalpanā na nyāyā । yatra hi
klṛptaśaktyanusāreṇārthāntarapratītyupapattiḥ tatra śaktyantarakalpanā na yuktā kāryasyā-
nyathāpyupapatteḥ । pariharati---<q>satyaṃ yatrānvayyavayavārthaḥ arthāntarasambandhasya
vā'nyatra vidhānam । ihatu ubhayaṃ nāstīti matvaivamuktam2</q> । dvivā hi
gauṇā bhavanti ye guṇayogādvartante yathā gārhapatye 3viniyogādindraśabdaḥ । sa ca
yatrāvayavārtho'nvayī tatra bhavati । tathā sādṛśyavaśena vartamāno gauṇaḥ yathā'g‍nihotra-
śabdaḥ kauṇḍapāyināmayanīye home । sa cārthāntarabhūtanaiyamikāg‍nihotrasambaddhasya
vidhyantasyānyatra kauṇḍapāyināmayanīye home vidhānādbhavati । iha tu tadubhayaṃ
nāstīti gauṇatvāsambhavāt śaktyantarakalpanāyāṃ māteti mātāramapīti yaduktaṃ bhāṣye
tadeva yuktam ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyeta---karmamātravidhānamidaṃ svāhākāraṃ yajanīti
na devatāviśiṣṭakarmavidhānam lāghavāt । nanu ca devatāvidhānamidaṃ
svāhākāraṃ yajatītyuktam</q> । pariharati---<q>na hi ajñātadevājñāpane'tra
pramāṇamasti । na dvitīyā devatātve4 smaryate</q> । nanu padayorvyatiriktārthataiva
devatārthatve pramāṇam; tatrāha---<q>jñāte hi devatātve vyatirekeḥ vyatireke ca
devatātvamiti</q> itaretarāśrayatā bhavati । viṣṇuṃ yajatīti codanāntareṇa devatā-
vāvagamānna doṣaḥ । tasmātkarmābhidhānamevaitadyukaṃ sāmānādhikaraṇyāt । <q>nanu ca
karmavidhānepi prādhānyameva karmaṇo'vagamyata ityuktam</q> । pariharati---<q>kena
vā vidhāne</q> vidhānāvasthāyāṃ <q>prādhānyaṃ neṣyate yāgo hyakarmakatayā svapradhāna
evotpattidaśāyām prayojane tu</q> prayojanakalpanāyāṃ tu <q>guṇabhāvo na avahantyādi-
vat svata eva guṇabhāva iti</q> । na ca vidhāne prādhānyaṃ pramāṇāntareṇāvagamyaṃ
guṇabhāvaṃ niruṇaddhi । tasmāt devatāsaṃskāratayā'tra dṛṣṭārthataiva yāgasyeti yuktam ।
<note>1. R mantravikalpavi</note> <note>3. avayavayogāt R</note>
<note>2. mātetivadyuktam A</note> <note>4. devatārthe R</note>
﻿<pb n="329"/>
<p><q>nanu ca devatāvikalpo mantravibhāgaś‍ceti prāp‍notīti coditam</q> ।
uttaraṃ---<q>na prāp‍noti saṃskāraviśeṣāt</q> । etadeva vivṛṇoti---<q>na gṛhyate hi
saṃskāre viśeṣaḥ । asyā devatāyāḥ saṃskāro'syā neti । atassarvadevatā-
saṃskāre'pekṣitatvāt prayogasya tathaiva devatābhāvo'pi iti nyāyyam</q> ।
asyārthaḥ-sarvāsāṃ devatānāṃ saṃskārasyāpekṣitatvāt prayogavidhinā sarvadevatāsaṃskāro
devatātvaṃ ca kalpyate (na) sarvasaṃskārānuguṇaṃ militānāmeva svāhākāre devatātvaṃ
kalpyate । <q>liṅgamuktam</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 8 ।। tathā''jyabhāgāgnirapīti cet ।। 16 ।।</l></lg>
<p>pūrvavadatrāpi dṛṣṭārthataiva devatāsaṃskāratvenājyabhāgasya nyāyyā ityāśaṅkya, na
dṛṣṭārthatā devatāyā apratyabhidhānāditi rāddhāntitam । yadi hi āg‍neye yā ca
devatāg‍niḥ saivājyabhāge'pīti pratyabhijñānaṃ syāt tadā syāt saṃskāratvam । na
cātra pratyabhijñānam । darśitā cāpratyabhijñā āvāhananigade । <quote>‘ag‍nimāvaha’</quote>
somamāvaha’ <quote>‘ag‍nimāvaha’</quote> iti paṭhitam । tatra yadyāg‍neyasya ag‍nirājyabhāge'pi
devateti syāt tadā prathamena ag‍nimityanena āgneyasya pradhānasya devatā prakāśyā ।
somamag‍nimityanena upāṃśuyājadevatā ag‍nīṣomau prakāśyau tatra ca kramaviparyayaḥ ।
devatāntarīye tvājyabhāgīye ag‍niṃ somaṃ ityājyabhāgayoḥ devate prakāśye tadanantaraṃ
ca pradhānadevatā ag‍niriti yuktam । kathaṃ tarhi devatāyā guṇabhāvaḥ ? uttaraṃ---
<q>bhūtatvāt devatāyā bhavyatvācca karmaṇa iti nyāyyatā guṇabhāvasyoktā</q> ।
nyāyyāṃ guṇabhāvo na vācanika ityarthaḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 9 ।। paśāvapīti cet ।। 19 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>atra pūrvapakṣavādī latāsome praṇīyamānāgnyabhidhānaṃ manvānaḥ artha-
vādādapratyabhijñāṃ manyate</q> । āsomaṃ vahantītyarthavādāt latāsomapraṇīyamānāgnya-
bhidhānaṃ agnisomaśabdayoḥ paśau manyamānaḥ puroḍāśe ca niyoga[ta]stadvacanatā
nāstīti pratyabhijñāyā abhāvaṃ manyamānaḥ pūrvapakṣavādī ārādupakārakaḥ paśupuroḍāśa
iti vadati । saṃskārakarmapakṣe utkarṣāśaṅkā'tra sautrāmaṇyāṃ vipratipannadevatāttvāt
paśūnāṃ puroḍāśānāṃ ca । yatra sampratipannā devatā tatra puroḍāśānāmutkarṣaḥ syāt ।
ārādupakārakatve tvanutkarṣaḥ guṇābhivātaṃ ca tulyam । yathā paśau guṇatvenābhi-
﻿<pb n="330"/>
dhānaṃ tathā puroḍāśe'pīti । kathaṃ tasyāḥ prādhānya mukhyā ca dharmaprāptiḥ anyathā
vaktavyeti guṇabhāve'g‍nīṣomayoḥ mukhyā ca dharmaprāptiḥ । guṇabhūtayoreva hyag‍nīṣomayoḥ
prakṛtau dharma upadiṣṭaḥ sa guṇabhāve mukhyo bhavati । prādhānye tu sati guṇakāryakaratvena
dharmaprāptirvaktavyā । sā kleśasādhyā parihṛtā bhavati । puroḍāśepi devatāyā 1guṇa-
bhāvāṅgīkaraṇena ।</p>
<p>tadidamuktaṃ bhāṣye---<quote>“parājite'pi hetuḥ kenacidviśeṣeṇānuprāṇyata”</quote> iti ।
so'yaṃ viśeṣaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu --- nājyabhāgavadapratyabhijñākāraṇamatrāsti । pratyabhijñā
cenna dṛṣṭārthatāhānaṃ sambhavatītyuktam</q> । viśeṣe tu pūrvapakṣānuprāṇanahetau tūk‍taḥ
parihāro'rthavādena । nanu 2cārthavādo'bhidhānānyatve heturuktaḥ parihṛto'rthavādāntareṇa
yaddaivatyaḥ paśuḥ taddaivatyaḥ puroḍāśa ityanena ।</p>
<p><q>nanu ca prakaraṇavaśādṛte saṃskārakarmatā na sambhavati</q> । asyārthaḥ---
3prakaraṇaniyogenāvamarśe saṃsparśe sati saṃskārakarmatā anyathā svatantrakarma kimiti na
bhavati । prakaraṇāvamarśaścet tadā sākṣādevopakārakatvam । tataścārādupakārakateti
gūḍhābhiprāyaḥ ।</p>
<p>pariharati---<q>kena coktaṃ sambhavatīti</q> vayamapi prakaraṇāvamarśādṛte saṃskāra-
karmatā na bhavatīti brūmaḥ । punaścodayati ---<q>evaṃ tarhi prakaraṇādārādupakārakataiva
bhavatu</q> । pariharati---<q>kiṃ na dṛṣṭe'rthe/?/ prakaraṇopakāraḥ</q> । ekagranthenāha---dṛṣṭe-
cādṛṣṭe ca prakaraṇasambandhasyāviśeṣāt na dṛṣṭārthaḥ śakyate bādhitumityukto hetuḥ
svāhākāre । tena dṛṣṭaprayojanānusāreṇa paramparayā prakaraṇopakārakatvāśrayaṇam ।
<q>śeṣamuktam</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 10 ।। carurhavirvikāraḥ syādijyāsaṃyogāt ।। 34 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>sthālyā mukhyārthatāṃ manvāno'nadanīyena dravyeṇa yāgavirodhāt 
kapālavikāraścaruriti manyate</q> । asyārthaḥ-sthā/?/lyāḥ pūrvasiddhatvāt tadvacana eva
<note>1. A aṃśe nira karaṇe guṇabhā/?/vaḥ syāt</note>
<note>2. R arthavādābhidhānatve hetu</note>
<note>3. prakaraṇena</note>
﻿<pb n="331"/>
caruśabdaḥ tadyogādodane vartate । tatrāpi sthālī na haviṣṭvena vidheyā anadanīya-
tvāt । anadanīyena ca yāge kriyamāṇe śiṣṭācāravirodhāt । pākādhāratvena
kapālasthāne sthālī vidheyā । darśana ca darśitamasya pakṣasya । uparitanapakṣāntaramāha
---<q>taddhitārthānupapatteḥ havirvikāra iti sthitam</q> । saurya iti taddhitena
devatā haviṣā sambadhyate na pākādhāreṇeti haviṣṭvenaiva sthālyā vidhānam ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntamāha---<q>odane'pi ca mukhyārthe sambhavāt tadyogācca sthālyāṃ
prayogopapatteḥ adanīyaśrutivirodhāśca । kvacit śrapayatīti carau śravaṇāt
odanena havirvikriyata iti sthitam</q> । asyārthaḥ - yadi sthālīvacanaḥ caruśabdaḥ
syāt tadā haviṣṭvaṃ tasyā vācyam । tataścānadanīyena yāgaḥ kriyeta iti śiṣṭā-
cāro bādhanīyaḥ । odanavacanatve tu nāsti śiṣṭācāravirodhaḥ iti tadvacana eva
caruśabda iti nirṇīyate । sambhavati tadvacanatā । tadyogena ca sthālyāmapi prayogo
ghaṭate । ādhāravacanatā śiṣṭācāravirodhena tyajyate । kvaciccaroḥ śrapaṇaṃ vidhīyata
ityodana eva haviriti sthitam । <q>śeṣamuktam</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 11 ।। sa kapāle prakṛtyā syādanyasya cāśrutitvāt ।। 45 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>atra yāvadviruddha‍yate tāvannivartate । na ca kapālasya kaś‍cidvirodhaḥ ।
kintu saṅkhyāyāḥ । tasmādaṣṭasaṅkhyāṃ parityajya kapāla eva caruḥ śrapaṇīya
iti pūrva pakṣaḥ</q> ।</p>
<p><q>na kapālaḥ prakṛtivadupakartuṃ śaknoti । taddhi pākahetuḥ, pākādhāra-
tvena prakṛtāvupakārakam</q> । odanaśca udakagatenoṣmaṇā pacyata ityarthalopādaprāptiḥ
kapālasyāpi saṅkhyāyā iva । idānīṃ pātraniyame prāpte yāsu sthālīṣu somāḥ syuḥ
te carava iti liṅgadarśanāt caruśabdābhidheyāyāśca pakteḥ sthā/?/lyāmevābhinirvṛtteḥ
saukaryāt sthālyāmeva paktavya iti sthitam । etacca suhṛdbhāvakathanamātram, na tu
sthālī viniyuktetyevaṃparaṃ tat । <q>śeṣamuktam</q> ।</p>
<p>kiṃ bhavati prayojanam ? yadi kapālavikāraścaruḥ yadi vodanena havirvi-
kriyata iti । atra sthālyāḥ punarhavirdhikāre ko viśeṣa iti na cintitam । sujñāna-
tvādavaghātādibādhasya ।</p>
﻿<pb n="332"/>
<p><q>।। evaṃ vā ।।</q></p>
<p>atra punaradhikaraṇe prayojanatve peṣaṇādilopaṃ vyākhyāya punaradhikaraṇāntara-
karaṇāt kvacit kiñcidapaneyamastītyabhiprāyaḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu ca mandaśaṅkā nāpaneyetyatrāha- <q>mandaviṣeṇāpītī darśitam</q> । yo
mandaviṣeṇa vṛścikena dṛṣṭo na mumūrṣati saḥ nācikitsyo yathā tathā mandāśaṅkāvyā-
kulitaḥ śiṣyo'pīti darśitaṃ bhāṣye । tatra bahuṣu anuṣṭhānasambhavaṃ anarthalopaṃ ca
manvānena pūrvapakṣitam । kvacidavirodhenānivṛttiḥ kvacidārthasyaiva codanārthatāṃ manyate ।
saṃvapa(caya)nādīnāṃ śakyatayā'nuṣṭhānasambhavamātreṇopakārakatvam । asti cātrānuṣṭhāna-
sambhavalakṣaṇo'narthalopa ityabhimānavān peṣaṇādīnāṃ dṛṣṭārthānāṃ avirodhāt piṣṭakamaya-
syāpi caroḥ darśanāt vyuddharaṇasya cārthasya vidheyatvabuddha‍yā pūrvapakṣitam ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu-na śakyatayā'nuṣṭhānam nāpyavirodhāt</q> । nāpyartho'ti-
diśyate kiṃ tarhi ? kāryato'nuṣṭhānaṃ dharmāṇāṃ tadabhāvācca nivṛttiḥ । vacanācca
kāryakalpanā । tenārthasya kārye karaṇopakāre'nanupraveśānnātideśa iti sūktam ।</p>
<p><q>।। iti śrīśālikamiśraviracitāyāṃ ṛjuvimalāyāṃ
pañcikāyāṃ daśamasya prathamaḥpādaḥ ।।</q></p>
﻿<pb n="333"/>
<p><q>ṛjuvimalāyāṃ</q></p>
<p><q>daśamādhyāyasya dvitīyāḥ pādaḥ</q></p>
<lg><l>।। 1 ।। kṛṣṇaleṣvarthalopādapākaḥ syāt ।। 11 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>kathaṃ punaratra pūrvaḥpakṣaḥ ? pūrvapakṣe'pi hi vacanamapi vidyata eva</q> ।
samādhatte---<q>na vacanaśatenāpi aśakanīyo'rthaḥ śakyate vidhātum</q> । kathama-
śakyatetyatrāha---<q>pacerhi viklṛttiḥ pradhāno'rthaḥ । na cāsau kṛṣṇaleṣu vidyata
iti kimatra vacanaṃ kariṣyati</q> । asyārthaḥ - mahābhāṣyakāreṇoktaṃ - pacerhi
viklṛttiḥ pradhāno'rtha iti । pradhāno mukhya ityarthaḥ । dṛśyate ca loke'pi pacyante
taṇḍulā iti viklṛttivacanatā pakteḥ । devadattaḥ pacatītyādāvapi taṇḍulasama-
vāyinyāmeva viklṛtau devadattaḥ kartā, tadadhīnatvāttasyāḥ । viklṛttiśca gandharūpa-
sparśarasādiviśeṣātmikā । tena puroḍāśādīnāmapi pākassiddho bhavati । na ca
taijasānāṃ kṛṣṇalādīnāṃ rūpādiviśeṣestīti pākasyāśakyatvānna vacanaśatenāpi
vidhānamupapadyate । ekagranthenāha---<q>atha tu santāpajananamātraṃ pākaḥ tathāpi
codakenaiva prāpnotīti vacanena kiṃ ?</q> viklṛttiphalako yo vyāpāraḥ sa eva yadi
pacerarthaḥ tataḥ prakṛtāvapi sa eva vidhīyate tataścodakenaiva kṛṣṇaleṣvapi prāpnotīti
vidhānamanarthakam । doṣāntaraṃ cāha---<q>avaghātādi ca durnivāraṃ tadā bhavati</q> ।
yadā vyāpāravacanatā dhātūnāṃ tadā hanterapi udyamananipatanamātrārthatvāt kartavyataiva
pratīyate ।</p>
<p><q>athocyate tuṣakaṇavimocanātmakaphalābhāvāt akaraṇaṃ pāke tulyaṃ
upadiṣṭepi pāke tulyaṃ phalābhāvādakaraṇam</q> । tasmādakartavyatāmeva manyamānasya
pūrvaḥpakṣaḥ । <q>vacanamidānīṃ kimarthaṃ yadi pākasyākartavyatā</q> । uttaraṃ---
<q>anarthakaṃ ca।</q> । avagamyamānārthatayā hi vacanamarthavat, na vacanenārthavatā bhavitavyamiti
pramāṇamasti ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu satyamāha bhavān phalābhāvāt na kāryataḥ prāptirastīti</q> ।
vacanaṃ punaḥ na nivārayituṃ śakyate । tena vācanikaḥ pāko bhaviṣyati ।</p>
﻿<pb n="334"/>
<p><q>nanu vacanaśatenāpyaśakanīyo'rtho na vidhātuṃ śakyata ityuktam</q> ।
pariharati---<q>etadapi satyam aśakanīyo'rthoṃ na vidhātuṃ śakyata iti</q> । punaḥ
pūrvapakṣī pṛcchati---<q>kathaṃ tarhi pākasya kartavyatā aśakanīyatayā vidhānā-
sambhavāt</q> । siddhāntītvāha---<q>śabdārthasya sambhavāt</q> । yo'sau viklṛttiphalako
vyāpāraḥ sa eva pacinocyate pūrvabhāvitvāt । tatkāryatayā lakṣaṇayā viklṛttau paceḥ
prayogaḥ pacyante taṇḍalā iti । evaṃ ca devadattaḥ pacatīti svasamavāyinyeva
vyāpāre devadattasya kartṛtvam । yaścāsau gandhādiparāvṛttihetubhūto'gnyavayavasaṃyoga-
phalako vyāpāraḥ sa eva yadi śabdārthaḥ kṛṣṇaleṣvapi sambhavati । teṣāmapyavayava-
saṃyogopalabdheḥ । uṣṇasparśānumeyo hi teṣvagnyavayavasañcāraḥ । tena śabdārtha-
sambhavāt pākastatra vidhātuṃ śakyate ।</p>
<p>nanu vihitasyāpi phalābhāvādananuṣṭhānaṃ kāryaprayuktatvāddharmāṇāmityatrāha---
<q>vihite śabdārthe dṛṣṭamadṛṣṭaṃ vā prayojanaṃ bhavati । yasya dṛṣṭaṃ prayojanamasti
tasya dṛṣṭameva prayojanaṃ</q> yathā prakṛtau pākasyāvaghātādīnāṃ ca । yasya tu dṛṣṭaṃ
nāsti tasyādṛṣṭaṃ kalpyate grāhakasambandhanirvāhāya । dvāreṇa vinā tadanupapatteḥ ।
yathā prakṛtāveva prokṣaṇasya । tatrāpi dvitīyāśravaṇāt tad‍dravyagataṃ taditi kalpyate ।
tenātrāpi kṛṣṇaleṣu ko'pi pākajanyaḥ saṃskāraḥ prayojanamityadhyavasīyate na punaḥ
dṛṣṭaṃ prayojanaṃ nāstīti vidhinivāraṇam । sambhavati ca śabdārthaḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu vidhānaṃ satyadṛṣṭaṃ prayojanaṃ vidhānameva prāk prayojanāvagamānnopapadyate
prayojanaparyante vyāpāre puruṣasya niyogādityāśaṅkyāha---<q>yāvat puruṣavyāpāra
eva hi vidherviṣayaḥ na phalopapattirapi</q> । svavyāpāre hi puruṣo niyujyate tena
tāvanmātre vihite adṛṣṭaphalakalpanā yuktaiva । viklṛttiśca phalaṃ paceḥ pacyarthasya na
punaḥ sa eva pacyartha iti pūrvamuktam । kathaṃ tarhi mahābhāṣyakārasya vacanamityatrāha-
<q>phalenāpi ca dhātvarthakathanaṃ dhātupāṭhe1 dṛṣṭam yathā gaḍivadanaikadeśe iti</q> ।
kriyāvacano hi dhāturiti gaḍirapi kriyāvacana eva kriyāmeva vadanaikadeśārambhalakṣaṇāṃ
vadati । tatphalena dhātvarthakathanam vadanaikadeśaphalake vyāpāre gaḍirityarthaḥ । evaṃ kaḥ
paceḥ pradhānārtha iti phalata eva vyākhyānaṃ vaktavyam viklṛttiphalo vyāpāra eva paceḥ
pradhāno'rtha ityarthaḥ ।</p>
<note>1. A dhātvarthapāṭhe</note>
﻿<pb n="335"/>
<p>etenedaṃ nirākṛtaṃ yadāha kaścit viklṛttimātrasa/?/ṅkalpaviśeṣaikāvalambinau
jñāyamānatadarthatvāt 1neṣṭāvanyābhidhāyināviti । tasmātsūktaṃ vacanāt kṛṣṇaleṣu
pāka iti ।</p>
<p><q>yattu vyāpāramātre dhātvarthe avaghātādyapi durnivāra/?/miti । atrocyate
prākṛtakāryābhāvādavaghātādīnāṃ nivṛttiḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ vyāpāramātre'pi dhātvarthe
tasya prakṛtau dṛṣṭameva dvāraṃ tuṣakaṇavimocanādi tatkāryasyaiva vikṛtāvapi prāptiriti
prākṛtakāryābhāvat avaghātādīnāṃ nivṛttiḥ । tathā pākasyāpi prākṛtakāryapuroḍāśa-
gandhādiparāvṛtterabhāvānnivṛttiḥ । paścāttu vācanikaḥ pāko'paro vidhīyate tasyādṛṣṭaṃ
dvāraṃ kalpyate । taduktaṃ yathopapadyate tathopariṣṭādvakṣyāma iti tadidamuktam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 2 ।। upastaraṇābhidhāraṇayosmṛtārthatvādakarma syāt ।। 3 ।।</l></lg>
<p>nanu ca vyakta eva rāddhāntaḥ kimarthamidamadhikaraṇamityātrāha-<q>atra nivṛtti-
hetavaḥ parīkṣyante । kimupastaraṇābhidhāraṇayoramṛtārthatvaṃ kṛṣṇaleṣu nivṛttau
hetuḥ svādim‍no'sambhavāt uta caturavattasyāp‍tyā iti caturavattāptivacana
nivṛttihetuḥ athavā saṃsargābhāvo nivṛttau heturiti rāddhāntābhāsanivṛttyartha-
midamadhikaraṇamityarthaḥ</q> ।</p>
<p>keciddhi manyante svādimaprayojanamupastaraṇamabhidhāraṇaṃ ca prakṛtau, kṛṣṇaleṣu
svādim‍no'bhāvānnivartata iti ।</p>
<p>tathānye manyante---caturavattaprayojanamupastaraṇamabhidhāraṇaṃ ca taccaturavatta
kṛṣṇalacatuṣkāvadānenaiva sampannamiti kāryābhāvannivartate ।</p>
<p>tathānyanmatam - upastaraṇābhidhāraṇe sruci havissaṃsarganivṛttyarthe । na ca kṛṣṇa-
lānāṃ sruci saṃsargo'sti tena tannivṛttyarthaṃ nopastaraṇamabhidhāraṇaṃ ca kāryamiti ।
tatraikamamṛtāhutisampādanaṃ nivṛttikāraṇamarthavādatvena parihṛtam । na hi svādimā
paramārthataḥ prayojanaṃ bhavitumarhati । anupayogitvāt । asvādunāpi yāgasiddheḥ ।
<q>dvitīyamapi nivṛttikāraṇaṃ parihṛtamiti</q> sambandhaḥ । kena hetunetyatrāha---
<note>1. R neṣṭāpattyā</note>
﻿<pb n="336"/>
<q>pradhānāvadeyaviṣayatvāccatussaṅkhyāyāḥ</q> । catvāri kṛṣṇalānyavadyatīti yeyaṃ
catussaṅkhyā sā yatpradhānaṃ haviravedayaṃ tadviṣayā nāvadānaviṣayā tena caturavattāvāptirekena
avadānena nāsti ।</p>
<p>nanu yadyapyekamavadānaṃ tathāpi tena caturāvattāvāptirarthavādādavagamyata ityatrāha
---āp‍tyarthavādasya catvāri kṛṣṇalānyavadyati tadekamavadānaṃ ityanena</q>
nirākaraṇamiti sambandhaḥ । tathā bhinnaviṣayāvagamāt saṅkhyāyā nirākaraṇam ।
catussaṅkhyā bhinnaviṣayā'vagamyate kṛṣṇalaviṣayā, nāvadānaviṣayā । tena 1stutimātra-
metat । kṛṣṇalacatuṣkāvadānābhyāsaśrutivirodhācca nirākaraṇam । catvāri
catvāri kṛṣṇalānyavadyati iti । avadānāntare sati abhyāsa upapadyate । yadi ca
kṛṣṇalacatuṣkāvadānenaiva caturavattasampattiḥ tadā'vāntaraprasaṅga eva nāsti ityabhyāsa-
śrutirviruddha‍yeta ।</p>
<p>nanu sviṣṭakṛdavadānāpekṣayā'bhyāsaśruterupapattirityatrāha-<q>pradhānasya cābhyāsaḥ
prakaraṇāt iti darśitam</q> । ato nirākaraṇaṃ pradhānāvadānaviṣaya evāyamabhyāsaḥ na
sviṣṭakṛdavadānāpekṣaḥ pradānasya prakaraṇaṃ yata iti bhāṣye darśitam । ato heto-
rāp‍tyarthatvādasya nirākaraṇam । tasmāt kṛṣṇalānāṃ strucyasaṃsarga evopastaraṇābhidhāraṇa-
yorbādhe(rabhāve)hetuḥ । tayossaṃsarganivṛttiprayojanatvāt । kasmāttadeva prayojana-
mityatrāha---<q>na ca dṛṣṭe saṃsarganirākaraṇe prayojane sambhavati prakṛtāvapi
kāryāntarakalpanā śakyate vak‍tumiti</q> yuktamuktaṃ asaṃsarga eva bādhaheturiti ।</p>
<p>nanu yadyupastaraṇābhidhāraṇaṃ nāsti tadā pradhānahaviṣṣu2 dva‍yavadāne sati
caturavattatvaṃ kathaṃ setsyatītyatrāha---<q>yatpunaścaturavattaṃ juhotīti tadāp‍tyā
sampāditamityadoṣaḥ</q> । catvāri kṛṣṇalānyavadyati caturavattasyāp‍tyai ityanenaiva
āptivacanena caturavattatāyā anugrahābhidhānāt ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 3 ।। bhakṣāṇāṃ tu prītyarthatvādakarma syāt ।। 13 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nanu bhakṣaṇaṃ dravyapratipattyarthaṃ prakṛtau । keyaṃ prītyarthaṃtā bādhahetutve-
nāśaṅkyate</q> । samādhatte---<q>satyaṃ dravyapratipattyarthaṃ kintu bhakṣaṇaṃ sat prati-</q>
<note>1. A stutiprasaṅga eva nāsti ।</note> <note>2. haviṣo R</note>
﻿<pb n="337"/>
<q>pattyartham</q> । svarūpāparityāgena pratipattyarthatetyarthaḥ । bhakṣaṇaṃ ca prītyavinābhūtaṃ,
abhyavahāryaviṣayaṃ hi talloke dṛśyate । yadeva pārthivaṃ rasavad dravyaṃ tadviṣayameva loke
bhakṣaṇamucyate । tacca prītyā tṛptirūpayā'vinābhūtam । tasmāttasyāḥ prīterabhāvāt
padārthasvarūpābhāvādeva bhakṣā nivartanta iti yuktamiti pūrvapakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu---vacanādbhakṣo bhavatīti</q> । tadākṣipati---<q>nanvevaṃ sati
vacanamapyanarthakaṃ prāpnoti aśakyārthavidhānāt</q> । rāddhāntī pariharati---
<q>nānarthakaṃ padārthamātrasya śakyatvāt</q> । prītyarthe'pi bhakṣe yo'sau vyāpāraḥ sa hi
bhakṣayatinā ucyate । tataśca tadvacanena vidhānaṃ bhaviṣyati । tasya kṛṣṇaleṣvapi
śakyatvāt । nanu cābhyavahāryaviṣayaṃ bhakṣaṇaṃ loke dṛṣṭam । tacca prītyavinābhāvi ।
na ca kṛṣṇaleṣu prītirastītyuktam । satyaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ na tu vidheḥ viṣayatāṃ pratipadyate ।
kintu vyāpāramātrameva । tacca kṛṣṇaleṣvapyasti । tadāha---<q>vidhiviṣayaṃ ca bhakṣaṇaṃ
kṛṣṇaleṣvapi vidyate</q> । viṣayaśabdena bhakṣaṇaṃ parāmṛśyamiti viṣayamiti napuṃsakanirdeśa
iti yuktaṃ vacanam । tacca kṛṣṇalaviṣayameva । na ghṛtaviṣayaṃ tasya guṇatvāt pradhānatvācca
kṛṣṇalānāmityuktaṃ bhāṣye ।</p>
<p>nanu ca ghṛtaviṣameva bhakṣaṇavidhānametaditi yuktam । tasmin bhakṣaṇe
cucchūṣādīnāmanuvādasambhavāt । hiraṇye tu bhakṣyamāṇe cucchūṣādīnāmaprāpteḥ tepi
vidhātavyā iti vidhigauravamityatrāha---<q>cucchūṣādīnāmanuvādāsambhavāt</q> । hiraṇye
śrapaṇādhārājyasaṃsṛṣṭe bhakṣyamāṇe prāptameva cucchūṣākaraṇamiti na viśiṣṭavidhi-
gauravāpattiḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 4 ।। ekadhopahāre sahatvaṃ brahmabhakṣāṇāṃ prakṛtau vihitatvāt ।। 17 ।।</l></lg>
<p>atra bhāṣyakāraḥ 1sakṛttvapakṣe codakaprāpte bhakṣāntarabādhaprasaṅgena sahatvapakṣa-
