māśritya coditavān । <quote>“nanu vācanika evāyaṃ bhakṣo na codakaprāpta”</quote> iti । tatra
punarevamuktavāt---dravyapratipattyarthatayā codakaprāpta evāyaṃ bhakṣaḥ । vacanaṃ cucchūṣādi-
vidhānārthamiti । tadākṣipati---<q>pūrvādhikaraṇe vācanikaṃ bhakṣamabhidhāya kathaṃ
pratipattyarthatvena punaḥ prāptirucyate । kathaṃ vā cucchūṣādīnāṃ anuvāda-</q>
<note>1. A. sakṛdbhakṣye</note>
﻿<pb n="338"/>
<q>mabhidhāya punarniyamo'bhidhīyate</q> । samādhatte---<q>nāyaṃ virodhaḥ sambhavati
prakṛtau yathā laukikasya bhakṣasyābhyavahāryaviṣayasya yat kāryaṃ prītirūpaṃ tasya</q>
darśanāt tadabhāvena vikṛtau na vidheyaprāp‍tirityadhastāduktam । vacanaṃ ca vidheya-
viṣayatayopapadyate pākavat । iha punaridamucyate yadi vikṛtāvetadeva vyāpāramātraṃ
vidheyam । vidheśca kāryakalpanā na padārthasya । sambhavati cātrāpi । prakṛtāvapi
tadvidheḥ kāryaṃ dravyapratirūpaṃ tasmānna bādhaḥ śakyate vak‍tum । tena bhakṣaścodakenaiva
prāpto 1na vedhayaḥ । cucchuṣādīnāmeva vacanaviṣayatvam । cucchuṣādīnāṃ cāni-
tyatvāt nityārthaṃ vacanaviṣayatāpi śakyate vak‍tumiti sūktam । etaduktaṃ bhavati---
yathā vikṛtau vyāpāramātrasya vidhānaṃ tathā prakṛtāvapyastu । tasya ca dravyapratipattiḥ
pradhānaṃ phalaṃ ānuṣaṅgikī puruṣaprītiriti codakato'styeva bhakṣaprāptiḥ । vacanaṃ tu
prakāraviśeṣaniyamārthaṃ vacanaviśeṣaniyamārtham । kathaṃ tarhi prāgvācanikī prāptiruktā ।
ata <q>āha---ādhastyamadhikaraṇamidānīṃ kimarthaṃ ?</q> uttaraṃ---<q>etadyukti-
prasiddha‍yartham</q> । etāmeva yuktiṃ prasādhayituṃ tadityarthaḥ । vyāpāramātrameva vidhiviṣaya
ityetatsādhane tatra tātparyam na punarvācaniko bhakṣa ityatra । tena nāsti doṣaḥ ।
yuktisādhanaṃ kimarthamityatrāha---<q>na hyaprasādhitā yuktiryuktirbhavati kāryākaraṇāt</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 5 ।। sarvatvaṃ ca teṣāmadhikārāt syāt ।। 18 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>kasyacidapariharaṇīyasya parihāravidhānaṃ sambhavatīti pūrvaḥpakṣaḥ</q> ।
yadyeṣā vacanavyaktiḥ yadbrahmaṇe pariharati tatsarvamiti tathāpi brahmabhāgabhūtasyāpi yasya
pariharaṇīyatvaṃ prāptaṃ tasya parihārarthaṃ sarvamiti vidhīyate2 । yo'pi brahmabhāgaḥ sa na
sarvo niyamena brahmaṇe deya iti na prāpta eva । ekadeśadvāreṇāpi tādarthyopapatteḥ ।
tathā yadi yadbrahmaṇe sarvaṃ tatpariharatīti vacanavyaktiḥ tathāpi apariharaṇīyapari-
hārārthameva pariharatīti vidheyamityarthaḥ । yadyeka evārtho vacanavyaktidvayepi kimarthaṃ
tarhi dvayamuktamityatrāha---<q>vacanavyaktipradarśanaṃ tu sambhavamātrakathanam</q> ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntastu---<q>sarvaśabdānupapatteḥ nāprāptavidhānaṃ sambhavatīti bhāgāpa-
naya eva</q> । asyārthaḥ---yadbrahmaṇe pariharati tatsarvamityasyāṃ vacanavyaktau sarvaśabdārtho
<note>1. R. na vidheyaḥ</note>
<note>2. R. vidheyaṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="339"/>
na vidheyaḥ prāptatvāt, yatkhalu brahmaṇe parihārārthaṃ tatsarvameva parihārārthaṃ prāptaṃ dravya-
pratipattyarthatvāt parihārasya yāvad‍dravyameva parihāro yuktaḥ yadi hi dravyaṃ guṇabhūtaṃ
syāt tadā ekadeśenāpi vyāpāre kṛtaḥ śāstrārtho bhavet । prādhānye tu dravyasya
yāvad‍dravyameva parihāro yuktaḥ । anyathā'nena saṃskāreṇa tasya varjanaṃ syāt ।
tathā yadbrahmaṇe tatsarvaṃ pariharati ityasyāmapi vacanavyaktau sarvapadārthasyānupapattireva
viśeṣyāparijñānāt । tasmāt sarvaṃ caruṃ brahmaṇe pariharati iti । yadi syāt yatsarvaṃ
pariharati tadabrahmaṇa iti anyataravacanavyaktyāśrayaṇena puruṣāntarabhāgānāmapanayo'yaṃ
vidhīyate asambhavaśca sarvaśabdārthasya sarvāsu vacanavyaktiṣviti darśitam1 ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 6 ।। puruṣāpanayāt svakālatvam ।। 20 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>kiyadanena bādhyat iti cintyate</q> । tatra pūrvapakṣavādī yāvacchravaṇa-
mabādhaṃ manvānaḥ pūrvapakṣitavān । sarvaṃ brahmaṇe pariharatīti śruteḥ ekasminneva kāle
pariharaṇaṃ pratīyata iti kālo'pi bādhyata iti pūrvapakṣitam ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntastu---<q>ekārthatvānniyogasya nārthāntaraṃ sambhavatīti apana-
yamātreṇa paryavasānam yadanyat tadavādhitatvāt kartavyam</q> । asyārthaḥ---
yadyapyekakālatā śrūyate tathāpi niyogasyānekārthavidhāyakatvāsambhavāt bhāgāpanayamātraṃ
vidhīyate । na kālo'pi । tena kālāntarāvidhānāt yathāprāptasya kālasyāvādhi-
tatvāt svakāla eva pariharaṇaṃ kartavyam ।</p>
<p>kasmātpunaḥ śrūyamāṇāpyekakālatā na vidhīyata ityatrāha---<q>na yāvadabhidhānaṃ
yāvadviniyogaṃ vā niyoga iti sthāpitam</q> । niyogasya pradhānatvānnābhidhāna-
viniyogavaśena varṇanam kintu niyogavaśenaiva tayorvarṇanaviti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 7 ।। ekārthatvādavibhāgaḥsyāt ।। 21 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>apanayamātrasya coditatvāt yadanyat tadabādhitamiti pūrvādhikaraṇa-
nyāyena vyādeśamapi prati abādhabuddhau prasaktāyāṃ nyāyoktiḥ</q> । kīdṛśī
<note>1. vyaktiṣu darśitaḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="340"/>
setyāha---<q>1satyetasminnapanayavacane yasyārthādapi</q> prayojanamapaiti tadapi na
kartavyamiti । prayojanāpanayena hyakaraṇaṃ tadyasya sākṣādvihite nāpaiti । yasya ca tadā-
kṣepalabhyena tasyāpi bādho nyāyyaḥ prayojanāpāyasya samatvāt । tasmādvyādeśasya na
prayojanaṃ puruṣāpanaye sati yebhyo yaddeyaṃ tattebhyo vyādiśyeta । na ca brahmavyatirekeṇā-
nyebhyo dānamastīti nāsti vyādeśasya prayojanam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 8 ।। ṛtvigdānaṃ dharmamātraṃ syāddadātisāmarthyāt ।। 22 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>atra pūrvapakṣo2niyataparimāṇatayā, vacanācca</q> । asyārthaḥ---puruṣāṇā-
mānateraniyatopāyatvāt niyataparimāṇavidhānaṃ nopapadyate । adṛṣṭārthatve tūpapadyate ।
tathā ānatyarthe dāne kiṃ vacanena । vināpi vacanena dānaṃ prāptameva । na ca niyamārthaṃ
vacanaṃ niyamasyaivāśakyatvāt puruṣānatīnāṃ aniyatatvādeva । tadāha---nahyānatyarthe
vacane kiñjitprayoja़namastīti manyate ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu niyame sambhavati nādṛṣṭārthatā śakyate vaditum
vratasyeva</q> । yadi dṛṣṭaṃ puruṣānatireva prayojanaṃ dānasya na syāt vacanānarthakyaṃ idaṃ
tāvadavaśyaṃ kartavyamiti niyamārthatvādvacanasya nānarthakyam niyamārthamapi vacanaṃ bhavatyeva ।
yathā payo vrataṃ brāhmaṇasyeti । niyamārthatā vacanamātreṇa dṛṣṭāntaḥ । anyanivṛttyartho
vrataniyamaḥ । ayaṃ tu ayoganivṛttyarthaḥ niyamenāpi niyogānāṃ arthavattoditā caturthe ।
tasmātparikrayārthaṃ dakṣiṇādānamiti sthitam । <q>liṅgamuktam</q> ।</p>
<p><q>kaḥ ihaḥ punaḥ prasaṅgo'syādhikaraṇasya bādhalakṣaṇe ?</q> uttaraṃ---<q>apari-
kretavyeṣu puruṣeṣu satre dakṣiṇā bādhyata iti prasaṅgaḥ</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 9 ।। śeṣabhakṣāśca tadvat ।। 29 ।।</l></lg>
<p>kathaṃ punaranyārthaṃ dravyaṃ parikrayārthaṃ manyate ? viniyuktaviniyogavirodhādi-
tyatrāha-<q>atrāpi dva‍yavadānopasaṃhāra some ca yāvaddhomaṃ yāgārthamiti manvānaḥ
parikrayārthatāṃ manyate</q> । yāgaṃ prati tādarthyaṃ na puroḍāśamātre kintu dva‍yavadānamātre
<note>1. A asatye....prayojanamudeti</note>
<note>2. aniyata A</note>
﻿<pb n="341"/>
(evopasaṃhṛtam) । some tu yāvadeva hūyate tāvatyeva 1pariśiṣṭamānatyarthamiti vini-
yuktaviniyogavirodhābhāvāt tena parikrayo yukta iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>kathaṃ punastāvatā dravyeṇālpīyasā parikraya ityatrāha---<q>bhavati ca yā
ca yāvatīva mātrā prīteḥ dravyeṣu bhakṣyamāṇeṣu</q> prītaye cānamante । tasmā-
dānatyarthā bhakṣāḥ ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---ānatyarthe hi dravyamupādeyaṃ prāp‍noti</q> ।
yadyānatyarthā bhakṣāḥ bhakṣaṇīyaṃ dravyaṃ ānatyarthamupādeyaṃ prāp‍noti । tataḥ kiṃ upātta-
dravyaviṣayā bhakṣāḥ śrūyante । yāgārthaṃ ca tadupādānam । kṛts‍nasyaiva yāgārthatvāt ।
ekadeśena tu vyāpāraḥ । na cānyārthasyānyārthatopapadyate । tasmādyāgārthasyaivāyaṃ
saṃskāraḥ pratipattirūpaḥ nānatyartha iti siddham । <q>sanidarśanaṃ śeṣamuktam</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 10 varaṇamṛtvijāmānamanārthatvātsatre na syāt
svakarmatvāt ।। 24 ।।</l></lg>
<p>nanu varaṇaṃ prārthanātmakamānatyarthameva kathamadṛṣṭārthaśaṅketyatrāhaḥ---<q>parikrayeṇaivā-
natiḥ siddheti varaṇamadṛṣṭārthaṃ manyate śratuvaraṇat</q> ।</p>
<p>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---na hi prayojanavataḥ sannidhau prārthanā dṛṣṭārthā śakyate
kalpayitum । uttarakālabhāvitvācca dakṣiṇādānasya na kṛtārthatā । <q>yadi pūrvaṃ-
kālabhāvi varaṇaṃ dakṣiṇādānaṃ tarhi tenaiva kṛtārtham</q> । pariharati---<q>nānatyarthatā
varaṇasya dānaṃ vihanti</q> । kuta ityāha---<q>tadanugṛhītaiva hyānatyarthatā
siddha‍yati prayojanavatī bhavati na kevalā</q> । kuta ityatrāha---<q>sammānapūrvakaṃ hi
satāṃ dānaṃ prayojanasiddhau loke dṛṣṭam</q> । yatra hi loke prayojanasiddha‍yarthaṃ satāṃ
dānaṃ tat sammānapūrvakaṃ dṛṣṭam । tena2sammānaṃ dānasyetikartavyatābhāvenopakārakaṃ
na dānameva nirākartumarhati । ṛtuvaraṇaṃ tu kṛtārthatayādṛṣṭārthamiti pratyuktam ।
varaṇabharaṇayoḥ kṛtatvānna varaṇāntaraṃ dṛṣṭārthaṃm3 ।</p>

<p><q>nanu parikraya ityuktam parikrīyate'nenati vyutpattyā parikrayaḥ ।
sa cātmani na sambhavatīti kathaṃ pūrvapakṣaḥ । pratiṣedhadarśanāṅkyā mandaviṣa-

na hyasatyāṃ prāptau pratiṣedho bhavatīti ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastūktaḥ । nāyaṃ pratiṣedhaḥ । kintarhi ? nityānuvādo-
'yamiti</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 12 ।। udavasānīyaḥ satradharmā syāt tadaṅgatvāt tatra dāna-
dharmamātraṃ syāt ।। 39 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>satrasamabhivyāhārānnādhikārāntara1kalpanā nyāyyā । phalavatsanni-
dhāvaphalaṃ tadaṅgamiti nyāyasiddheḥ</q> । satrādudavasāya pṛṣṭhaśamanīyena jyotiṣṭomena
sahastradakṣiṇena yajeran iti satreṇa sahaikasmin vākye tāvatpṛṣṭhaśamanīyaḥ samabhivyā-
hriyate । tena satrasannidhau tasya śravaṇaṃ phalavatsannidhau aphalaṃ tena sahaikādhikāram ।
ekādhikāratve ca phalavadaṅgatā । satraṃ ca phalavat; aphalaḥ udavasānīyaḥ । ataḥ
satrāṅgam । satrāṅgatve ca svayaṃ2kartṛtvena adṛṣṭārthameva sahasradakṣiṇāvacanam3 ।
kāmeṣṭau sārasvatasatrāṅgabhūtāyāṃ <quote>“aśvāṃ ca puruṣīṃ ca dhenuke”</quote> itivat । kiñca
yadyadhikārāntaramudavasānīye syāt tadā satrādudavasāyeti kālalakṣaṇā syāt ।
sā cāyuktā । tasmāt satrāṅgatve sati samānakartṛkataiva ktvāpratyayasyārthaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate - naitadyuktaṃ yadadṛṣṭārthaṃ sahasradakṣiṇāvacanamiti ।
yasmānna satrāṅgamudavasānīyaḥ । nātra satrasamabhivyāhāraḥ kintu satratyāga-
samabhivyāhāro'yam</q> । na hi yajeḥ ktāntatā śrūyate । kiṃ tarhi ? avasyateḥ
udavasāyeti । na cāvasyatiryāgamācaṣṭe vājapeyeneṣṭevativat । yadi cedamaṅgaṃ
satrasya syāt tadā satratyāga eva na bhavet । tataśca tyāgaśravaṇaṃ bādhyeta । tena
<note>1. R nādhikaraṇāntara</note>
<note>2. R /?/tsayaṃ kartṛkatvāt</note>
<note>3. R dakṣiṇāyanayaṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="343"/>
tyāgaśravaṇāt satrānanupraveśyetatkarmeti jñāyate । <q>tasmādutsṛṣṭasatrāṇāmadhikārā-
ntarametaditi siddham । dṛṣṭārthā ca dakṣiṇā bhavati</q> । tena dakṣiṇāśabdo na
pīḍyate । svatantrakarmapakṣe codakaprāptaparakartṛkatvābādhāt 1ānatyarthameva sahasra
dakṣiṇādānam2 ।</p>
<p>evaṃ sthite pṛcchati---<q>kimutsṛṣṭasatratā nimittaṃ tena nimittādhikāro-
'yam, kiṃ vā viśvajidvadadhikārāntarakalpanā</q> । yadyadhikārāntarakalpanā
tadā kālalakṣaṇeti manyate । uttaramāha-<q>nedamatra vicāryate anaṅgatvaṃ tāvatsiddham</q>
tatra yadi nimittādhikāro nyāyyaḥ tadā sa evāśrīyatām । athānyāyyastadā adhi-
kārāntaraṃ kalpyatām । na ca kālalakṣaṇādoṣaḥ tyāgasamabhivyāhāreṇānaṅgatvādudava-
sānīyasyeti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 13 ।। teṣāṃ tu vacanāt dviyajñavatsaha prayogaḥ
syāt ।। 41 ।।</l></lg>
<p>nanu kathamatra bahukartṛkatvamāśaṅkyate yāvatotsṛṣṭasatrāṇāmetadadhikārāntaram ।
teca bahava eveti prāptameva bahutvamanūdyate । na punarbahukartṛke karmaṇyadhikāra ityā-
śaṅkyāha---<q>atra yajeranniti bahuvacananirdeśāt padārthasya ca padārthāntareṇa
sambandhāt3 avagatāviva kārye'pi anvayaṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī bahutvasya</q> ।
asyārthaḥ - yajeranniti tāvadbahuvacananirdeśena4 bahukarteṛke viṣaye'dhikāraḥ pratīyate ।
na codavasānīyetyetadapekṣayā tadvahutvamanuvādabhūtamiti śakyā kalpanā । paripūrṇasya
padārthasya bahukartṛkayāgaviṣayavidhyarthātmakasyāvagatatvāt । yasmāt padārthāntareṇodava-
sānena sambandhaḥ । yadi bahutvamanapekṣyaiva kevalayāgamātraviṣayo vidhirudavasānena
sambadhyate tadā bahutvamanūdyata ityucyeta । yadā tu paripūrṇasya sataḥ padārthasyānyena
sambandhaḥ tadāpi bahukartṛkayāgaviṣayasya vidhyarthasyāvagatatvānnānūdyamānatā bahutvasya ।
ato yathā pratītau bahutvasyānvayaḥ tathā kārye'pīti bahūnāmevodavasānīye kartṛtvam ।
evaṃ bahukartṛkatve sthite svayaṃkartṛkatā śakyā cintayitum । anyathā hi ekakartṛkatve
śaktyabhāvādeva svayamṛtvikkāryatvaṃ na śakyetāśaṅkitumityantarāgarmiṇyupanyāsaḥ ।</p>
<note>1. dṛṣṭārthameva</note> <note>3. R sambandhāvagatāviva</note>
<note>2. ṇā vacanam</note> <note>4. R vacanaśravaṇāt</note>
﻿<pb n="344"/>
<p>tatra sthitaṃ tāvadaparyavasitamityuktvā ātmakartṛkaḥ prayoga iti pūrvapakṣitam ।
tadayuktamiva pratibhāti । yadi hi yajamānānāmevārtvijye vidhānaṃ syāt tadaitadyuktaṃ
pūrvapakṣayitum । na ca yajamānānāmārtvijyaṃ śrūyate । yadi hi udavasātāro
yajamānāḥ puruṣāntaraprayojyatayā śrūyeran tadā ārtvijye teṣāṃ śravaṇaṃ syāt । na
caitadasti tadāha---<q>na hyudavasānīye kartāraste paraprayojyatayā</q> puruṣāntara-
prayojyatayā <q>pratīyante</q> yena yāge tathābhūtā bhavitumarhanti । <q>nanu yajerannityanenā-
rtvijye'pi kartṛtvamucyata</q> ityatrāha---<q>na hi te yajanti । kiṃ tarhi ? yāja-
yanti</q> । ṛtvijo na yajante kiṃ tarhi yājayanti । yajeranniti ca yajane kartṛtā
pratīyate na yājane । <q>yadi yajane ṛtvijāṃ kartṛtā nāsti kathaṃ tarhi yajanti
yājakā iti pratyudāharaṇam</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>prayoge sati tad‍draṣṭavyam</q> । yadā prayojya-
yajamānavyāpāra eva yajiḥ prayojakaṛtvig‌vyāpāre yājane lakṣaṇayā prayukta iti
gamyate tadaitatpratyudāharaṇam । tatra yājakaśabda eva pramāṇam । yājakaśabdenartvijā-
mabhidhānam । ṇyantādyajeḥ ṇvulutpatteḥ ।</p>
<p>ayaṃ punaryajeranniti prayogaḥ svatantra eva kartaryupapadyate ātmanepadaśravaṇāditi
nartvijāmavagatiḥ । tena kathamārtvijye yajamānakṛtāśaṅkā iti । samādhatte---<q>satyaṃ
yathā bhavānāha । iha punaḥ satrasamabhivyāhṛtamudavasāne bahutvamiti tathā-
bhūtāśaṅkopapadyate iti tannirākaraṇāya pūrvapakṣitam</q> । asyārthaḥ---satre yathābhūtāḥ
kartāraḥ tathābhūtā udavasāne'pi pratīyante । ye evodavasāne kartāraḥ ta eva pṛṣṭhaśamanī-
ye'pi । satre ca svayamārtvijyakāriṇaḥ kartāra iti ihāpi tathābhūtā eva te kartāra
iti pūrvapakṣāśaṅkānirākaraṇāya pūrvapakṣitam ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntastu---<q>paricodanayaivoktaḥ । yeyaṃ prāk paricodanā kṛtā
yajamānānāmārtvijye vidhānaṃ nāstīti tayaiva hi rāddhānta uktaḥ</q> । na
tenāparakartṛkatā bādhitā iti prakṛtivaduvasānīyaḥ kartavya iti vacanaṃ parakartṛkatā-
prāpakamabādhitameva draṣṭavyam ।</p>
<p>yadi hi satraprakṛtitvaṃ syāt syādapi svayaṃ kartṛtvaṃ, na ca satraprakṛtitvaṃ
pṛṣṭhaśamanīyasya । tasmādṛtvijo varitavyā iti sthitam ।</p>
<p><q>kathaṃ punaravagamyamānā tathābhūtatā svayamārtvijyakāritā nirā-
kṛtā</q> । uttaraṃ-<q>prakṛtivadityuktam</q> । yathā prakṛtau parakartṛtā tathā pṛṣṭhaśamanīyepi
﻿<pb n="345"/>
iti yadidaṃ codakādavagamyate tadeva tathābhūtatvanirākaraṇe kāraṇamityuktam । tasmādyā-
vacchrutamevotsṛṣṭasatratvamādaraṇīyaṃ na punaḥ svayamārtvijyakāritvamiti ।</p>
<p><q>।। sthitāduttaram ।।</q></p>
<p><q>satyaṃ paripūrṇaṃ padaṃ padāntaramākāṅkṣati । pūrvāvagatastvatra prayogaḥ ।
sa cetaretaranirapekṣāṇāṃ bahūnām</q> । asyārthaḥ---udavasāyeti ktvāpratyayaśravaṇāt
udavasānaprayogastāvat pūrvamavagantavyaḥ pūrvāvagamye ktvāpratyayaprayogāt । sa ca
parasparanirapekṣabahukartṛkaḥ । ākṣipati---<q>bahavaścetaretaranirapekṣāśceti bhavato-
cyante । kiṃnibandhanaṃ tarhi bahutvam</q> । itaretarāpekṣatvanibandhanaṃ hi bahutvaṃ
nānyathā bahutvopapattiḥ । apekṣābuddhinibandhanatvāt । samādhātā āha---<q>satranibandha-
namiti brūmaḥ</q> । satre parasparāpekṣatvāt bahutvamupapannam । nirapekṣatā tūdavasāne
ekaikasya tatprayogāt ।</p>
<p>bhavatvevaṃ tathāpi kimityāta---<q>tathābhūtānāṃ ca pūrvaṃ grayogāvagamāt
uttaratrāpi tathaivāvasīyate</q> । asyārthaḥ---nirapekṣā bahava udavasānaprayoge pūrvāvagate
tāvat kartāraḥ pratīyante । samānakartṛkatā ca dvitīyaṃ prayogamantareṇa na syāt ।
yo'pi cāsau dvitīyaḥ prayogaḥ sa pūrvaprayogasamānakartṛkaḥ iti itaretaranirapekṣa-
bahukartṛka eva pratīyate । tasmādekakartṛkataivodavasanīyasya ।</p>
<p>nanu yajeranniti śravaṇāt dvitīyaprayogo bahukartṛka eva vidhīyata ityatrāha
---<q>yajimātraṃ tvanavagatamiti tadarthavidhānamavaśiṣyata iti tatraiva paryava-
sānam</q> । asyārtha---samānakartṛkatāvagamāt tāvat pūrvaprayogavilakṣaṇakartṛkaprayoga-
samarpaṇārthaṃ na vidhānaṃ, kintu anavagatadvitīyaprayogasvarūpamātrapratipādanārthamiti
tatraiva paryavasānam । na kartṛbahutve'pi vyāpāro vidheḥ । nanvevaṃ rājapurohitādiṣvapi
kimityevameva na syāt ityata āha---<q>rājapurohitādiṣu tu</q> prayogāntarānavagamāt
agṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatayā yajivadvacanārtho'pi vidheya iti vaiṣamyam । yathā yajyartho'na-
vagatastatra vidhīyate tathā vacanārtho'pi । iha tu vacanārtho na vidheyaḥ । pūrvaprayoga-
﻿<pb n="346"/>
samānakartṛkatvādeva tatkartṛsaṅkhyāvagamāt kevalaṃ yāgamātraṃ vidheyam । tasmāt
prakṛtivadekakartṛtvaṃ vivakṣaṇīyamudavasānīye । ataḥ pratyekaṃ prayoga iti sūktam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 15 ।। kāmeṣṭau ca dānasaṃyogāt ।। 44 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>atra pūrvapakṣavādī deyaviśeṣaṃ manvānaḥ aṅgeṣu parakartṛkatāṃ manyate</q> ।
asyārthaḥ - satrāṅgabhūtāyāmapi kāmeṣṭau codakaprāptaparakartṛkataiva । tataśca dakṣiṇādāne
codakaprāpte deyaviśeṣavidhānabhetat1 । na ca ye yajamānā iti vacanaṃ parakartṛkatāṃ bādhate
samarthaṃ ca ye yajamānāsta ṛtvija iti pradhāne vacanam । pradhānamātre'pi svayaṃ-
kartṛkatvavidherbahuvacanamupapannameveti nāṅgeṣu codakaprāptāṃ parakartṛkatāṃ bādhate । tasmāt
parikraya evāyaṃ <quote>“aśvāṃ ca puruṣīṃ ca”</quote> iti ।</p>
<p><q>atrocyate---prayogāṅgaṃ hi ānamanam ।</q> yadetadānamanaṃ tatprayogāṅgam ।
ekaścāyaṃ satraprayogaḥ aṅgavidhiḥ punaḥ padārthaviṣaya eva na prayogaviṣayaḥ । na ca
padārthāṅgaṃ dakṣiṇetyuktam । tasmādadṛṣṭārthaṃ vacanaṃ na deyaviśeṣavidhānārtham । eṣo'tra
tattvārthaḥ---yo'yamaṅgavidhiḥ sa padārthamātrasattāṃ jñāpayati । na prayogam । pradhāna-
vidhireva prayogajñāpakaḥ । sa cāviśeṣaṇāṅgapradhānānāmekameva prayogaṃ jñāpayati ।
prayogāṅgabhūtā ca dakṣiṇā । tatra yadyeṣā dakṣiṇā syāt tataḥ pratiprayogaṃ bhavet ।
na ca prayogāṅgaṃ bhavitumarhati । pradhāne svayaṃkartṛkatvābhidhānāt । tena neyaṃ dakṣiṇa ।
yuktā padārthamātrānaṅgatvāt । ato'dṛṣṭārthaṃ dānamiti niścīyate ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 16 ।। dveṣye ca cācodanāddakṣiṇāpanayaḥ syāt ।। 46 ।।</l></lg>
<p>nanu kathamanvāhārthe vihite dakṣiṇāntarāśaṅkhetyatrāha---<q>naimittikatvāt
dakṣiṇāvikāro nyāyya iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</q> nityāmanvāhāryadakṣiṇāṃ naimittikai-
kahāyanīvidhirbādhate । dakṣiṇāśabdaśca samarthito bhavati । dakṣakārī hi dakṣiṇā ।
yadi dveṣyo'pi ṛtvigbhavet tadā tasmai dīyamānā dakṣakāriṇī bhavati anṛtviji tu
dakṣiṇātva nopapadyate । na cādṛṣṭaparikalpanā । ṛtvije tu dveṣyāyābhyupagamyamāne
dāne naivādṛṣṭakalpanā ।</p>
<note>1. R vidhirayam</note>
﻿<pb n="347"/>
<p><q>atrocyate---narvije dānametat । smṛtivirodhāt । yadi hi dveṣyo
ṛtvigbhavati tadā bhavedidaṃ ṛtvigdānaṃ, na ca ṛtvik dveṣyaḥ</q> na dveṣaṇīya
ityarthaḥ । smṛtivacanāt ṛtvigācāryau nāticaritavyau iti । tena dveṣyasya-
rtvijo'bhāvāt nedamṛtvije dānam ।</p>
<p><q>nanu laṅghitaśāstrārthasya kadācit ṛtvigapi dveṣyaḥ sambhavati</q> ।
yata eva dveṣyasambhavaḥ ata eva pratiṣedhaśāstram । anyathā'prasaktau pratiṣevacanaṃ
nāvataret । pariharati---<q>śāstrācca tadviṣayadveṣanāśanaṃ 1yatrataḥ prāptam</q> । asyārthaḥ---
śāstrasthān gṛhītvā śāstravyāpāraḥ । na ca śāstrasthasya ṛtvigdveṣaṇīyaḥ । yaḥ punaḥ
śāstraṃ nādriyate tasya varaṇepyanadhikāra eva 2ucchṛṅkhalatvāt । etadevāha---
<q>na cecchāmtramanuvartate vṛṇoti vā kimiti</q> । śāstrāccet kṛtaniścayaḥ na tarhi
dveṣya ṛtvik । tasmāt dveṣyasyartvijo'sambhavāt nedaṃ naimittikamānatyarthaṃ dānamiti ।
śāstrāntaramadṛṣṭāyeti sthitam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 17 ।। asthiyajño'vipratiṣedhāditareṣāṃ syādvipratiṣedhāda-
sthnām ।। 47 ।।</l></lg>
<p>kathaṃ punarasthnāṃ yāgāśaṅgā acetanatvāt । na hyacetano yagaṃ kartuṃ śakrati ।
na cādhikāro'pyacetanānāmupapadyeta । boddhā hyadhikriyate । nāpi tāni niyujyante ।
ata eva tiraścāmanadhikāra ityatrāha---<q>atra śrutibalena abhidhānaviniyogayoḥ
niyogasya ca śaktyapekṣatvāt śrutāparityāgena yathā śakyate tathā niyo-
gārtho'nuṣṭhātavyaḥ iti pūrvapakṣavādino'bhidhānaḥ</q> ।</p>
<p>asyārthaḥ---nāsthnāmadhikāraḥ śakyate, aṅgatvādasthiyajñasya । asthnāṃ
yāge kartṛtvāśaṅkā abhidhānaviniyogayoḥ śrutibalena । asthīni yājayet ityami-
dhānaṃ tāvadasthiṣu śrautam । tathā yājanānvayo'pyasthnāṃ śrauta eva । tena yāga-
kartṛtā tāvadasthnāṃ śrautī । yo'pi cāyaṃ niyogārtho'sthikartṛke yāge'bhūtena yathā
śakyate tathā'nuṣṭhātavyaḥ yasmāt satre niyogaḥ śaktyapekṣaḥ । pradarśitā ca yathāśakti
<note>1. R. hānaṃ</note>
<note>2. ullaṅghitaśās‍tratvāt</note>
﻿<pb n="348"/>
śavadravyaṃ gṛhītvā puruṣāntareṣu yāgaṃ kurvāṇeṣu bhavati yāge asthāni kartṝṇīti pūrvapakṣa-
vādino'bhimānaḥ । liṅgaṃ ca darśitam । yajamānabhūtānāṃ stotrānte'sthnāmupasthitiḥ
asthīni yajamānāni darśayati ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---satyaṃ śaktyanurodhī niyogaḥ । kintu
abhidhānaviniyogayoreva śrautārtho na sambhavati</q> asthnāṃ yāge kartṛtvā-
sambhavāt । na ca parikradvārā kartṛtā parikrayābhāvāt । yadi hi tāni yājayataḥ
puruṣān parikrīṇīta sa tadā saṃbhavedapi parikrayaḥ । nacaitadasti । na cāsthnāṃ
svamasti yena parikrayaḥ syāt na ca tadviṣayā yathāśaktiḥ । na hyaśavatyanyaḥ
śāstrārtho bhavati ।</p>
<p><q>kathaṃ tarhi pratinidhau yathāśakti</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>sā niyogasyaiveti
varṇitā । niyogārtha eva yathā śakyate tathā'nuṣṭhīyate । sadṛśagrahaṇaṃ tu
abhidhānasampattyartham yathābhihitārthasampattaye</q> । na punararthāntarābhidhānasya
sampattaye । tasmādabhidhānaviniyogayoreva yathāśrutanimittasāmañjasyaṃ na sambhavatīti
gaṅgāyāṃ dhoṣa itivat lakṣaṇā āśrayaṇīyā । asthiśabdena asthimantaḥ jīvantaḥ
satriṇa eva lakṣaṇīyāḥ । ato yena saha satriṇaḥ pravṛttāḥ tadaṅgavatāṃ tadasthimatāṃ
kartṛtvamiti sāmañjasyam । tasmāt jīvatāmeva yāgaṃ iti yuktam । <q>liṅgaṃ punaḥ
tatsarūpaṃ yājamānakumbhopasthitisarūpaṃ vācanikamityuktaṃ bhāṣye</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 18 ।। yadi tu vacanāt teṣāṃ japasaṃskāramarthaluptaṃ seṣṭi
tadarthatvāt ।। 49 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>kṛtvācintopanyāso'yam pūrvādhikaraṇapūrvapakṣaprayojanakathanāya</q> ।
prayojanakathane punaḥ prayojanaṃ na vaktavyam, svayaṃ prayojanarūpatvāt । tatra ca japasaṃskā-
reṣṭīnāṃ yathāsaṅkhyaṃ bādhaḥ । keśaśmaśruṇo'rbhāvāt vāco manasaścābhāvāt nivṛttiḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 19 ।। kratvarthaṃ tu kriyeta guṇabhūtatvāt ।। 50 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>atrāpi svātantryābhāvādevāsthnāmaudumbarīsammānādāvapi kartṛtā
na sambhavatīti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</q> na hyasthīnyacetanāni svayaṃ kvacit kartṝṇi
vyāpriyante ityabhiprāyaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="349"/>
<p><q>abhidheyasambhavāt svātantryopapattiriti rāddhāntaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---
dhātvabhidheyavyāpārayogitā svātantryam, na punaḥ svayaṃ pravartamānatā । etadeva
vivarītuṃ pṛcchati---<q>kiṃ kriyāsampādanameva svātantryam</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>omityu-
cyate dhātvavacchinnavyāpāravyāptiḥ kartṛtve hetuḥ</q> । dhātunā yo'vacchinnaḥ
pratipādito vyāpāraḥ tadyogitā svātantryamiti saiva kartṛtve hetuḥ tathā ca svavyāpā-
rāpekṣaṃ kāṣṭhādivyāpārabhūtajvalanādyapekṣaṃ kāṣṭhādīni pacantīti vākyaṃ prayujyate ।
tasmādasthnāṃ kartṛtvasambhavāt abādhaḥ sammānānvārambhayoḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 21 ।। kāmyāni tu na vidyante kāmājñānādyathetarasyānu-
cyamānāni ।। 51 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>atra kāmābhāvepi yajamānasya vṛṣṭirbhavatīti ko'bhiprāyaḥ</q> ? yāvatā
satyeva yajamānasya <q>kāme kāmyamānena phalena bhavitavyam</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>ayamabhi-
prāyaḥ-na kāmanāyāṃ yajamāno'ṅga phalaṃ ca puruṣārthatvāditi prādhānyāt</q> ।
asyārthaḥ-yatra kāmanāyāṃ satyāṃ puruṣasyādhikāraḥ tatrādhikāriṇo'ṅgatā nāsti pradhāna-
tvādadhikāriṇaḥ । kāmanā cādhikāriviśeṣaṇamiti sāpi nāṅgamiti । tataḥ kimi-
tyāha---<q>aṅgābhāvena phalānutpattiḥ</q> । na punaranaṅge'pyupādīyamāne । tena
kāmanāyā vināpi phalena bhāvyam । tasmān nīcaistvādiguṇayuktāt sadomānāt
vṛṣṭyādiphalena bhavitavyaṃ asatyāmapyasyāṃ kāmanāyāmiti yuktam ।</p>
<p><q>kathaṃ tarhyasmin pakṣe ātmanepadam</q> ? asyārthaḥ-ātmanepadaṃ hi
kartṛgāmitāṃ phalasyāpādayati । yadi tu akāme'pi kartari phalaṃ bhavati na tarhi
kartṛgāmitā phalasya । bhogyatayā hi phalasya sambandho nānyathā । uttaraṃ---
<q>uktastāvadayaṃ nyāyaḥ । sthite ca nyāye yathāsambhamātmanepadameva kartṛgā-
mitāṃ phalasyāha</q> kintu adhikāraprāptāṃ dyotayati । tatra yatrādhikārataḥ prāptirasti
tatra bhavati kartṛgāmikriyāphaladyotakatā । yatra na sambhavati tatra mābhūta । 1pravṛttatvā-
ñcāsya <q>jīvadavasthāyāṃ iti siddhaṃ sādhyabhidhānaṃ pāṇineḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---
yadetat vṛṣṭyādi sadomānaphalamihāsthiyajñe na tat sākṣācchrutam । kintu
<note>1. A prāptatvā</note>
﻿<pb n="350"/>
āśrayasadbhāvena jyotiṣṭomataḥ pravṛttam । jyotiṣṭome ca jīvadavasthāyāṃ kartṛgāmi-
kriyāphalapratipādakamātmanepadaṃ prayuktam । sambhavati ca taditi sādhvabhidhānaṃ
pāṇineḥ ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---satyamanaṅgaṃ yajamānaḥ tathāpi kāmanāyāma-
satyāmadhikṛta eva</q> । adhikāre ca sati sādhanatvamadhigamyate karmaṇaḥ, adhikṛtasya
phalaṃ janayituṃ śaknoti nānadhikṛtasyaṃ । <q>kathamanadhikāraḥ ?</q> uttaram <q>kāmitā
hyadhikāre hetuḥ । tadabhāve nādhikāraḥ । tasmiṃścāsati asādhanaṃ karma ।
sādhanābhāvacca phalābhāva kimatrānaṅgacintayā</q> । etadukta bhavati---yadyapyadhi-
kārī nāṅgaṃ tathāpi pradhānasyāpi phalotpattau 1sādhanabhāvāt tadābhāvāt phalābhāva
iti । tasmātphalābhāvānnivṛttiḥ kāmyādīnāṃ sadomānādīnām ।</p>
<p><q>bhāṣye punarātmanepadopanyāso'dhikāralakṣaṇārthaḥ । adhikāravaśenaiva phalā-
bhāvaḥ2 । ātmanepadaṃ tu tadeva dyātayatītyātmanepadopanyāsaḥ</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 21 ।। īhārthāścābhāvāt sūktāvākavat ।। 52 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>kā punaratra viśeṣāśaṅkā</q> । asyārthaḥ---yathā phalābhāvāt kāmyānāṃ
nivṛttiḥ tathā sūktavākasya phalābhāvāt nivṛttireva yuktā । samādhatte---<q>nanu cārtha-
vādatvamuktam nedaṃ phalamāyurādikam kintu arthavādo'yam</q> । punarākṣipati---
<q>vidhyudeśāśeṣatvenāyuktaṃ tadarthavādatvam</q> । arthavādo hi vidhyuddeśaśeṣo bhavati ।
tadabhāvānnāyamarthavādaḥ । punassamādhatte---<q>anuṣṭhāne'pi protsāhanamarthavadityuktaṃ
catvāri śrṛṅgetyatra</q> । tenānuṣṭhānāvasthāyāmarthavādo'stviti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । rāddhāntastu
asamavāyinyarthe hi evam yathā catvāri śrṛṅageti । iha tu phalatayā samavāyo'rtha-
syopapadyata eva । tathā ca bhāṣyakāreṇa ha(da)ratiryajātiḥ māntravarṇikī devatādikā
vidhiḥ āyurādīni phalānīti darśitam । tasmāt sati phalatve phalābhāvāt
phalapratipādakasūktavākasya pūrvavadatrāpi bādhaḥ ।</p>
<note>1. R sādhanābhāvāt</note>
<note>2. phalabhāvaḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="351"/>
<lg><l>।। 12 ।। syurvā hotṛkāmāḥ ।। 55 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nātrādhikāraśśakyate vak‍tum । āyurādīnāmiva kāmānāṃ vidyamā-
natvāt । ṛtvijo hyarkakāminaḥ । tasmādbhavitavyaṃ hotṛkāmaiḥ</q> । yathā
hyāyurādīnāṃ yajamāna eva kāmyādhikārī na tathā hotṛkāmānāṃ ṛtvijāmapyadhi-
kārāt । tena santyeva kāmina iti bhavitavyaṃ hotṛkāmaiḥ ।</p>
<p>evaṃ prāpte <q>atrābhidhīyate</q>---satyamanadhikāro nāsti । viṣayābhāvāttu
nivṛttiḥ । yajamāno hi āśāsyaphalasya viṣayaḥ tadviṣayaphalakāmanā hotṝṇāmadhi-
kāre hetuḥ । na cāsthnāṃ phalaviṣayatā sambhavati, acetanatvāt tena nirviṣayakāmināṃ
adhikāranimittabhāvaṃ hotṛkāmāḥ pratipadyante । tasmādatrāpyadhikārabhāvāddhotṛkāmānāmapi
nivṛttiḥ ।</p>
<p>atra codayati-<q>viṣayādhikārayoḥ kaḥsambandhaḥ ? yena viṣayābhāvādadhi-
kārābhāvaḥ</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>bāḍhamasti sambandhaḥ । na nirviṣayā kāmitā adhi-
kāranimittabhāvaṃ pratipadyate । tasmādatrāpyanadhikāra eva । kimartha tarhi
idamuktaṃ pūrva satyamanadhikāro nāsti viṣayābhāvattu nivṛttiḥ yajamāno
hi viṣaya iti</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>adhikṛtāpekṣamidamuktam</q> । adhikṛtānāṃ hi ṛtvijāṃ
cetanavatāṃ kāmanāyogyānāṃ vidyamānatvābhiprāyeṇānadhikāro nāstītyuktam । paramārtha-
tastu satsvapi kāmayitṛṣu viṣayābhāvānna kāmanā kāmanābhāvādanadhikāra iti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 23 ।। sarvasvārasya diṣṭagatau samāpanaṃ na vidyate karmaṇo
jīvasaṃyogāt ।। 57 ।।</l></lg>
<p>atra bhāṣyakāra evaṃ cintayati---kiṃ taddiṣṭagatyantaṃ karmotsraṣṭavyaṃ uta samāpa-
nīyameveti । tatra kāraṇasandehamāha---<q>athedānīmidaṃ sandihyate kiṃ yāvaddiṣṭāṃ
gatiṃ na gacchati tāvadevādhikāraḥ । gate tvadhikārabhāvāt karmatyāgaḥ
uta mṛtasyāpyadhikārānuvṛttiriti maraṇādapyupari1 phaleṣvadhikāro'stīti</q> ।
tatra pūrvapakṣavādī pūrvapakṣitavāniti sambandhaḥ । kathā yuktyetyatrāha---<q>na kaścidevaṃ
śāstrādadhikāraṃ pratipadyate mṛtasyāpi mamātrādhikāra iti</q> । tasmāt yāvaddiṣṭāṃ
<note>1. R uparitaneṣvapi</note>
﻿<pb n="352"/>
gatiṃ na gacchati tāvadevedaṃ mayā kartavyamiti śāstrādavagamyate । ata <q>ūrdhva karmaṇo
nivṛttiḥ adhikārābhāvāt kāmyasyeva</q> (phalasyeva) yathā'dhikārābhāvāt kāmyaṃ
phalaṃ na bhavati tathā maraṇāduparitanenāpi karmaṇā na bhavitavyaṃ yadaiva tasya jīvanaṃ tadaiva
tasya karmaṇi kartṛtvamupapadyate kartṛtvaparyantaścādhikāra iti maraṇāduparitaneṣva-
nadhikāraḥ ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu āparisamāpteradhikārāvagamāt nādhikāranivṛttirava-
sīyate</q> । sāṅge pradhāne'dhikāraḥ pratīyate । <q>nanu mṛtena kartavyamiti pratīyate
mṛtasya kartṛtvānupapattirityuktam</q> । pariharati---<q>kena voktaṃ pratīyata iti ।
kathaṃ tarhi kartavyatoktā</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>jīvata eva sā kartavyatā jīvanneva
maraṇāduparitanānapi padārthānadhikaroti । jīvataiva ca tathā kartavyaṃ
yathā diṣṭāpannasya 1svāmyaṃ prati yata 'dhikāro nivartyate । kathaṃ vā
nivartate ? sambhāravidhāvāt</q> । jīvanneva sambhārasāmagrīmupadiśatīti śāstrāda-
vagamyate ।</p>
<p>yatpunarna sambhavati yājamānaṃ bādhastasyāsambhavādeva yathā'nyeṣāmasambhavatāṃ
jīvatyapi yajamāne । yathā satreṣu parikrayādīnām । sambhārasambharaṇena ca svāmināṃ
kartṛtvamiti nādhikāro nivartate । tadidamuktam---<q>asaṃśayaṃ jīvato mṛtasya ca
na kaścidviśeṣa iti । sambhāra/?/dvāreṇa kartṛtvādubhayoḥ</q> ।</p>
<p><q>yatpunaridamuktaṃ kathamavidyamānasya kartṛtvamiti । atrocyate ।
nāvidyamānatā । śāśvatatvādātmanaḥ tasya ca kartṛtvāt</q> । (yadā)<q>paraṃ mṛte
upāyāsambhavastuvoditaḥ sa sambharaṇopāyena parihṛtaḥ</q> । brāhmaṇāḥ samāpayata
me yajñaṃ iti praiṣasya caivaṃ dṛṣṭārthatopapannā yadi samāpanīyaḥ kratuḥ । anyathā'dṛṣṭārthatā
syāditi samāpanīyaḥ kraturiti sthitam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 24 ।। gate karmāsthiyajñavat ।। 59 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>kṛtvācintāprayojanamihānuṣṭhāne upayujyata iti atideśo viṣaya-
sambhavapradarśanārthaḥ</q> । kṛtvācintayā vyutpāditasya nyāyasyānuṣṭhāne phalaṃ darśayitu-
midamuktam ।</p>
<note>1. R ayaṃ pratīto'dhikāro</note>
﻿<pb n="353"/>
<lg><l>।। 25 ।। jīvatyavacanamāyurāśiṣastadarthatvāt ।। 60 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>idānīṃ yāvaddiṣṭāṃ gatiṃ na gacchati tāvanmaraṇavirodhinīṣu codanāsu
adhikāro vidyate neti cintyate</q> । anena bhāṣyakārasandehe kāraṇasandehaḥ
kṛtaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>tatra maraṇanimittatvādadhikārasya tadvirodhyadhikāro nivartata iti
pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</q> ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu niyatakālatvānmaraṇecchāyāḥ tatpūrvakālīneṣu nādhikāra
virodho'vagamyata iti bādhābhāvaḥ</q> । niyatakālamaraṇārthameva pūrvamāyurāśāsitavya-
miti nāsti virodhaḥ । ato nāyurāśiṣo nivṛttiḥ</p>
<lg><l>।। 26 ।। kriyā syāddharmamātrāṇām ।। 62 ।।</l></lg>
<p>ākṣeptuṃ sandehamanubhāṣate tāvat---<q>dvādaśāhamṛddhikāmā upeyuriti
śrūyate । tatra ṛtuyājyāvaraṇaṃ ātreyahiraṇyadānaṃ ca bhavati na bhavatīti
sandihyate</q> । akṣiti---<q>nanu ca sandeha evāyamayuktaḥ pūrvapakṣābhāvāt ।
nahyadṛṣṭārthasyārthalopaḥ śakyate vak‍tum</q> । asyārthaḥ---adṛṣṭārthemṛtuyājyāvaraṇaṃ
ātreyadānaṃ ca na tayossatrepi dvāralopaḥ śakyate vak‍tum, tatrāpyadṛṣṭasambhavāditi
pūrvapakṣāsambhavāt sandeho na yuktaḥ । samādhatte-<q>satyamevaṃ tathāpi laukikanyāyā-
nusāreṇa yadapyanyasmai dīyate sāma vā prayujyate tatrāpi bhṛtyānāṃ bhavatye
vānatiḥ sādhurudāro'yamiti manvānāḥ sutarāṃ tatkārye yatanta iti lopaṃ
manyate pūrvapakṣavādī</q> । asyārthaḥ---laukikanyāyānusāreṇārthasya lopaṃ manyate pūrva-
pakṣavādī । loke hi yadanyasmai dīyate dānaṃ sāmaprayogaśca tatrāpi bhṛtyānāṃ bhavatyeva
dātāraṃ pratyānatiḥ । tathāhi---bhṛtyāḥ sādhurayaṃ priyaṃvada udāro dānaśīlaśceti
matvā sutarāṃ tasya dāturyajamānasya kārye yatamānā dṛśyante । tataśca parapuruṣavartinorapi
sāmadānayoḥ ṛtvigānatireva prayojanam । na ca satre sāstītyarthalopānnivṛttiḥ
sāmadānayoḥ ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu---nānuṣaṅgikaṃ śāstraprayojanaṃ bhavitumarhatīti</q> । asyārthaḥ
---anuṣaṅgikī ṛtvigānatiḥ na śāstraprayojanaṃ bhavitumarhatīti na sāmadānayoḥ
﻿<pb n="354"/>
prayojikā bhavitumarhatīti । kintvadṛṣṭameva prayojanam । tadāha---<q>mukhyaśca śāstrārtho-
'dṛṣṭāyaiveti prakṛtau nirūpitam । tasmānna nivṛttiranayoḥ sāmadānayoḥ</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 27 ।। guṇalope ca mukhyasya ।। 63 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>sahaivāgnihotrahavaṇyā nirvāpaśāstraṃ parisamāpyate</q> । asyārthaḥ-agnihotra-
havaṇyā havīṃṣi nirvapatīti nirvāpaśāstraṃ agnihotrahavaṇyā saha samāpyate । tathāpi
kimityāha---<q>na ca śāstrārthasya vibhāgo vidyate</q> । śāstraikye śāstrārtho'pyekaḥ ।
padārthā hi vibhaktāḥ na tu śāstrārthaḥ । agnihotrahavaṇyā vinā śāstrārtha eva nāstīti
pavamāneṣṭiṣu nirvāpasyākaraṇaṃ manyate pūrvapakṣavādī । kevalo'pi nirvāpaḥ kṛto'pyakṛta
eva aśāstrārthatvāt ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu satyaṃ yadyupadeśato'nuṣṭhānaṃ syāt । iha tu kāryato'nuṣṭhānaṃ
kāryaikadeśasya ca sambhave tu tattyāgo niṣpramāṇakaḥ</q> । agnihotrahavaṇyā
abhāve'pi tāvat nirvāya/?/sya kāryaṃ sambhavati । na ca sambhavataḥ kāryaikadeśasya tyāge
pramāṇamasti । tattyāge ca tajjanakatayā nirvāpo'pi kartavya eva kāryaprayuktatvādanu-
ṣṭhānasya । yadyupadeśasampādanāyānuṣṭhānaṃ syāt syādapyananuṣṭhānam । iha tu kāryasampā-
danāyaivānuṣṭhānamiti kartavyo nirvāpaḥ । yadi cāgnihotrahavaṇyeva nirvāpena saṃskriyate
tadā saṃskāryābhāve nirvāpasyākaraṇaṃ syāt na ca tadastītyāha---<q>na(nu) cāgnihotraha-
vaṇī saṃskāryā yena</q> tadabhāve kāryāvalopaḥ <q>syāt</q> । nirvāpasya tu nirupyamāṇadravyaṃ
saṃskāryaṃ1 kāryam । <q>alupte ca tasmin kārye na bādhaḥ śakyate vak‍tumiti
sthito nirvāpaḥ</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 28 ।। muṣṭilopāttu saṅkhālāpastadguṇatvātsyāt ।। 64 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nanu caturo muṣṭīn nirvapatīti catussaṅkhyā muṣṭayaśca nirvāpe
śrūyate । saptadaśasaṅkhyāśarāvadravyantvodanaparimāṇe</q> । tataśca kathaṃ bhinnaviṣayatayā
virodhābhāvena ubhayamubhayasya bādhakamityāśaṅkyata ityatrāha---<q>atra bhinnaviṣayatvepi
śāstrasya kāryata ekaviṣayatāṃ manvānaḥ ubhayorlopaṃ varṇitavān anyathā hi</q>
<note>1. A haviṣyadravyajoṣaṇaṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="355"/>
<q>anyatarasyāpi lopaḥ kena hetunetyabhiprāyaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---yadyapi nirvāpa-
viṣayāt caturo muṣṭīnnirvapatīti śāstrāt saptadaśaśarāvaśāstraṃ odana1 parimāṇavacanaṃ
bhinnaviṣayaṃ tathāpi kāryaparyālocanayā bhavatyevaikaviṣayatvam । tāvatparimāṇanirvāpa-
mantareṇa tāvadodanasyānupapatteḥ2 । tenārthāt tulyārthatāṃ prāpya godohanādineva
puruṣārthena kratvarthasya camasasya saptadaśasaṅkhyāyāḥ śarāvadravyeṇa catussaṅkhyāyāḥ
muṣṭidravyasya ca bādho yuktaḥ । yadi punaḥ kāryataḥ samānaviṣayatā nāśrīyate tadā
anyatarasya bādho rāddhāntābhimato na siddha‍yatīti purvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu---śrutistāvadbhinnaviṣayiṇī saptadaśaśarāvaparimāṇaścaruḥ
śrūyate । caturmuṣṭiparimāṇaśca nirvāpaḥ । tatraikakāryatve pramāṇaṃ nāsti</q> ।
asyārthaḥ-yadi saṅkhyādravyayorvaikṛtayoḥ prākṛtasaṅkhyādravyakārye vidhānaṃ syāt
tadā bhavedeva dvābhyāṃ dvayorbādhaḥ samānaviṣayatve ca sati bādhena bhavi tavyam । na ca
samānaviṣayatāsti prākṛtayoḥ saṅkhyādravyayoḥ nirvāpaviṣayatvena vaikṛtayoścaruviṣayatvena
śravaṇāt ।</p>
<p><q>nanu tāvatparimāṇake nirbāpe sati saptadaśaśarāvaparimāṇatā carorna-
siddha‍yatītyuk‍tam</q> । pariharati---<q>evaṃ tarhyārtho bādhaḥ na tu kṛtakṛtyatayā</q> ।
tathāpi kimityatrāha---<q>ārthaścedayaṃ bādhaḥ tadā</q> yāvadarthaṃ bhavitumarhati । yāvataiva
bādhena vinā caroḥ parimāṇaṃ na siddha‍yati tāvadeva bādhitavyam । saṅkhyādravyayo-
ścānyatarabādhenāpyarthaḥ siddha‍yatīti nobhayabādho bhavitumarhati । tāvataivedamadhikaraṇaṃ
samāptam । dvayorbādha iti pūrvapakṣaḥ । anyatarasya bādha iti rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<p>sa punaḥ anyatarasya kiṃ muṣṭidravyasya uta saṅkhyāyā iti nyāyāntarametatprati-
pāditam । tatrāpi grahaṇameva mukhyasyetyuk‍tam । yathā ādyasyopādānaṃ antyasya
tyāgaḥ tathā'trāpi pūrvabhāvinyā mukhyabhūtāyāssaṅkhyāyāḥ upādānaṃ jadhanyasya dravyasya
lopaḥ ubhayoḥ saṅkhyādravyayoḥ nirvāpaguṇatvāt । yadi saṅkhyā dravya guṇabhūtā bhavet
tato dravyamevānuruddha‍yeta saṅkhyā ca lupyeta । atra tu bhinnaprātipadikābhidheyā saṅkhyā
nirvāpameva prati guṇabhūtā āruṇyamiva krayaṃ prati ।</p>
<note>1. A parimāṇaviṣayaṃ</note> <note>2. A. syāsiddheḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="356"/>
<lg><l>।। 29 ।। autpattike tu dravyato vikāraḥ
syādakāryatvāt ।। 68 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>atropapadasthānīyaṃ codakaṃ manvānaḥ pūrvapakṣavādī nājadravyasya bādhaṃ
manyate</q> । asyārthaḥ---yathā aja ṛṣabha ityatra upapadabhūtājaśabdaśravaṇe aja
eva ṛṣabhaḥ parigṛhyate tathehāpi ajopasthāpini codake sati ajasyaiva ṛṣabhasya
grahaṇamiti ajadravyasyānivṛttiḥ । nanu ṛṣabhādiśabdaśravaṇamātreṇa gauḥ pratīyata
iti ajasya codakaprāptasya bādha eva nyāyya ityatrāha---<q>yadi padoccāraṇasamana-
ntarameva godravyaṃ pratīyata</q> iti manyate tadā aja ṛṣabha ityapi prayogo na
syāt parasparamananvayāt yathā ajo gauriti ।</p>
<p>atha śraute'rthe'nanvayāt gauṇo'yamṛṣabhaśabda iti ghaṭata eva prayogo aja
eva ṛṣabha iti tatrāha---<q>na cāyaṃ gauṇa iti śakyate vak‍tum । svārthāpari-
tyāgāt</q> । yo hi svārthaparityāgenānyatra vartate sa gauṇo'gnirmāṇavaka iti । ṛṣabhā-
dayaśca śabdāḥ ajepi vartamānā na svārthaṃmujjhanti yenaiva ca vayaḥ prabhṛtinārthenābhi-
dheyena ṛṣabhādayaḥ śabdā gavi vartaṃnte tenaiva atrāpyaje vartanta iti na ṛṣabhādi-
śabdaśrutivirodhaḥ ajadravye'pi codakaprāpte'nugṛhyamāṇe ityajasyābādhaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu upadeśaparisamāptau satyāṃ codakaḥ</q> pravartate । <q>avagate hi
aupadeśike śabdārthe paścāt codakasya pravṛttiḥ tena codakānusāreṇa śabdārtho
na śakyo'nyathākartum</q> । dhenvādayastu śabdāḥ gogataguṇavacanāḥ na guṇamātra-
vacanāḥ । na copadeśakāle dhenvādīnāṃ gorūpasvādhiṣṭhānapratyarthibhūtaṃ kiñcidajādi-
dravyamasti yenādhiṣṭhānāntaragatānāṃ anabhidheyānāmapi guṇānāṃ gauṇamabhidhānaṃ kalpyeta ।
codakassu paścādbhāvī na śabdārthaṃ prathamabhāvinamanyathākartumutsahate । <q>yadi gavā-
dhiṣṭhānaguṇavacanā dhenvādayaśśabdāḥ kathaṃ tarhi aja ṛṣabha</q> iti prayogaḥ? uttaraṃ
---<q>upadeśāparisamāptergauṇaḥ prayogo bhaviṣyati</q> । dvayorapi padayoḥ śrutatvāt
anvayaṃ vinā nopadeśaḥ samāpyate । na ca gauṇatvaṃ vinānvayopapattirastīti gauṇatvā-
dhyavasānam ।</p>
<p><q>kathaṃ punastadarthasambhave gauṇatvam ?</q> uttaraṃ---<q>abhidhānādarśanāt</q> ।
yadi guṇamātrābhidhānaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ loke syāt syādguṇamātravācitvam । na ca tadasti ।
﻿<pb n="357"/>
tasmānna1guṇamātraṃ tasya śabdasyārthaḥ । kathaṃ punarabhidhānādarśanaṃ ? kevalapadaśravaṇe
tanmātrānavagamāt gavādhiṣṭhānaguṇāvagamāt । tasmāt vākyabalena kathañcit gauṇyā
vṛttyā ajādhiṣṭhānaguṇapratipattiḥ vaktavyā । iha tu tathā gogatapratipattau pratyarthibhūtaṃ
nāstīti na śrauto'rthaḥ parityak‍tuṃ śakyate । dhenvādayaścaite śabdāḥ gogatatadguṇaṃ
vadanti na gotvamapi ।</p>
<p>nanu yadi gotvamete śabdā nābhidadhati kathaṃ tarhi viśiṣṭaguṇavacanāḥ ।
ucyate । kiñciddhi svata eva viśiṣṭaṃ vastu yadāśrayabhedena bhinnaṃ tatsvata eva viśiṣṭa-
tvānna viśeṣaṇābhidhānamapekṣate । dhānādayaśca pratyāśrayaṃ bhidyante । tatra gavāśritā ye
payodhānādayaste dhenvādiśabdairabhidhīyanta iti na viśeṣaṇatayā āśrayābhidhānamapekṣante ।
kiñcidvastu svato na viśiṣṭaṃ kevalaviśeṣaṇabalenaiva viśiṣṭatāmāpadyate । tattu viśiṣṭa-
mabhidhīyamānaṃ na viśeṣaṇābhidhānamantareṇa tathā'bhidhātuṃ śakyate yathā gotvādi । iha
ca dhānādyupahitagotvādivacanā dhenvādayaḥ śabdā na bhavanti । dhānādyabhidhānamantareṇa
gotvasya viśiṣṭasyābhidhātumaśakteḥ svato gotvasyābhedāt । viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyābhidhāne
śaktikalpanāgauravat । gavāpekṣadhānādivacanatve tu teṣāṃ svato'bhidhānāt viśeṣaṇābhi-
dhānāpekṣā nāstīti lāghavāt dhānāvācitvameva dhānādiśabdānām । tatra yadyapi
guṇavacanāstathāpi śāstrāntareṇa godravyānupādāne guṇavad‌dravyaparatvena prayujyante ।
tasmāt dravyāntaravidhānāt bādhitamajadravyam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 30 ।। naimittike tu kāryatvātprakṛteḥ
syāttadāpatteḥ ।। 69 ।।</l></lg>
<p>iha tu yadi guṇavacanaḥ śabda upadeśe śrūyamāṇaḥ pūrvanyāyena svādhiṣṭhāna-
paryanta eva nimittatāṃ pratipadyate । tarhyayamapi ś‍vetaśabdo dravyamātraṃ anapekṣitajāti-
viśeṣa yadadhiṣṭhānaṃ tatparyantatayā svārthaṃ pratyāyayatīti codakena yad dravyaṃ prāpyate
tadbādha eva । sāmānyaṃ hi dravyamātramupadeśārtha iti viśeṣaścodakaprāpto bādhyate ।</p>
<p><q>atrocyate । tvayaivoktaṃ dravyamātrādhiṣṭhānaṃ svārthaṃ ś‍vetaśabdaḥ pratyā-
yayatīti</q> । tataḥ kimityāha---<q>tarhi[na]viśeṣamavagamayati, nādhiṣṭhāna</q>-
<note>1. R guṇapratipatti</note>
﻿<pb n="358"/>
<q>viśeṣamavaga</q>mayati । viśeṣe'navagate viśeṣāntaranivṛttirdurbhaṇā virodhābhāvāt ।
yadi bhinnamadhiṣṭhānaviśeṣaṃ śvetaśabdo'vagamayet tadā codakaprāptena saha virodhaḥ
syāt । na caitadasti 1tasmādabādhaḥ codakasyeti yuktam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 31 ।। vipratiṣedhe tadvacanāt prākṛtaguṇalopaḥ syāt tena ca
karmasaṃyogāt ।। 70 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>atra bhāṣyakāraḥ khadirādīnāmeva bādhābādhau cintayati</q> । tatra
yāvaduktagrāhiṇaḥ kasyacit tanmātrabuddhirmābhūditi tulyanyāyatayā sarveṣāmeva yūpo-
tpattyarthānāṃ2 dravyāṇāṃ saṃskārāṇāṃ codāharaṇatāmāha---<q>khalevālī</q> yūpo bhavatītyatra
saṃśayaḥ---kiṃ yūpotpattyarthā dharmāḥ sādyaskre kartavyā neti । <q>kathaṃ kartavyāḥ kathaṃ
vā na kartavyā iti</q> ।</p>
<p>uttaraṃ---<q>yadi luptārthāstadā na kartavyāḥ athāluptārthāḥ kartavyāḥ</q> ।
yadyatra yūpo bādhitastadā na kartavyāḥ yūpotpattyarthatvāt । atha na bādhitastadā
kartavyāḥ । <q>kathaṃ punarlopālopāvarthasya</q> ? uttaraṃ---<q>yūpabādhābādhasandehāt ।
yūpasyaiva bādhābādhau kathaṃ sandihyete</q> । uttaraṃ-<q>vacanavyaktibhedāt sandehaḥ
yadā'yaṃ vacanavyaktiḥ yā khalevālī sā yūpo bhavatīti tadā'rthalopaḥ</q> ।
tadā khalevālī yūpakārye vihitā bhavati । tataśca tayaiva yūpakārye kṛte
yūpo lupyeta । atha yūpaḥ khalevālī bhavatītyucyate tadā aluptārthatvāt pravṛttirdharmāṇāṃ,
tadāhi sato yūpasya khalevālītvaṃ vidhīyate । kiṃ punaratra yuktam ? pūrvapakṣaṃ
parigṛhṇāti-<q>yūpaḥ khalevālī kartavya iti vākyārtho yuktaḥ</q> । kā punatra
yuktiḥ ? śrauto yūpaśabdaḥ samarthito bhavati codakaśca na pīḍitaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>nanvasmin pakṣe khalevālīśabdaḥ śrautamarthaṃ tyājitaḥ</q> । kuta ityāha
<q>khalevālīśabdo hi kāṣṭhavacanaḥ</q> khalevārayatīti vyutpattyā yaugikaḥ khalevālī-
śabdo medhikāṣṭhamāha, na punaḥ khalevāraṇakriyāmātram । tathāpi kimityāha---
<q>na ca nirjñātakāṣṭhe yūpe kāṣṭhāntaraṃ vidhātuṃ śakyate</q> । asyārthaḥ---nirjñātaṃ
<note>1. R tasmādapīḍāco</note> 
<note>2. A apūrvotyattyarthānāṃ</note>
﻿<pb n="359"/>
kāṣṭhaṃ khadirādi yasya sa nirjñātakāṣṭho yūpastatra kāṣṭhāntaraṃ vidhātuṃ na śakyate ।
khadirādikāṣṭhaṃ[kāṣṭhā]ntaraṃ bhavatīti vidhātuṃ na śakyate । tasmāt kāṣṭhātmake yūpe
khale vāraṇakriyā kartavyā । yūpaḥ khalevālī kartavyaḥ । yūpe khalevāraṇakriyā
saṃskārārthā kartavyā iti । tataśca śrautasya dravyasya hānaṃ kriyāyāśca vidhānaṃ lakṣaṇayā
yathā pācakaśabde pacikriyāmātrapare ।</p>
<p><q>athā'yamabhiprāyaḥ yadi svārthepi(yūpaḥ) khalevālī sambhavati tasmi-
nnarthe śrautavidhānamupapadyata eveti</q> । asyārthaḥ---yadi kāṣṭhāntaramayīṃ khalevālī
māśritya vidhānamucyate tadā śakyavidhānaṃ syāt । yadi tu khādirīṃ khalevālī-
māśritya yūpe khalevālī vidhirāśrīyate tadā nāsti virodha iti śrautārthavidhāname-
vetyabhiprāyaḥ pūrvapakṣiṇaḥ । ākṣeptā dūṣayati---<q>sutarāṃ tarhi vidhānānupapattiḥ ।
prāptatvātsvadirasya</q> । khadiratā prāptaiva na viṃdheyā । ekagranthena sa eva pūrvapakṣiṇā
śaṅkāmāha---<q>atha khalevāraṇasaṃskṛtaṃ tadvidhīyata ityucyate । yadyapi khadirataḥ
prāptatvānna vidheyā tathāpi khalevāraṇasaṃskṛtatayā vidhīyate</q> । dūṣayati---
<q>saiva tarhī lakṣaṇā khalevālīśabdasya kāṣṭhavacanasya khalevāraṇasaṃskṛta-
paratvāt</q> । evamākṣipte pūrvapakṣe pūrvapakṣī vadati---<q>evaṃ tarhi yaścobhayossamo doṣo
na tamekaścodyo bhavati</q> । tathāhi---viparītāyāmapi siddhāntavacanavyaktau yūpaśabdo
lakṣaṇayā varṇanīyaḥ । punarākṣeptā āha---<q>kastarhi tava pūrvapakṣiṇo viśeṣahetuḥ</q> ।
pūrvapakṣī vadati---<q>ayamasti viśeṣahetuḥ khalevālī yūpo bhavatītyucyamāne</q>-yūpa-
śabdo dharmān lakṣayati, na kāryaṃ, kārye hi lakṣyamāṇe khalevālī vidheyā । tasyāṃ ca
vidhīyamānāyāṃ vyavahitaḥ sambandhaḥ syāt yūpakārye khalevālī bhavatīti yūpaśabdāt
vyavahito bhavati itiśabdaḥ khalevālīśabdena sambandhanīyaḥ । bhavatu dharmalakṣaṇā
tathāpi kimityatrāha---<q>te ca dharmāḥ khalevālyāṃ vidhīyamānāḥ tatsaṃskārakā
eva prāp‍nuvanti</q> khalevālīsaṃskārakā ityarthaḥ । tataśca prakaraṇe khalevālyā asambhavāt
prakaraṇabādhaḥ adhikārāntarakalpanā adṛṣṭakalpanā cetyayameva pakṣo nyāyyaḥ yūpaḥ
khalevālī bhavatīti ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate</q>---avyavadhānāt khalevālī yūpo bhavatīti vākyārthaḥ
na punaryūpaḥ khalevālī bhavatīti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="360"/>
<p><q>nanvevaṃ sati yūpaśabdo lakṣaṇayetyuktam</q> । pariharati---<q>parihṛtamidaṃ
codyaṃ pūrvapakṣiṇaiva yaścobhayordoṣa iti vadatā</q> । yasmāt pūrvapakṣe'pi khalevālī-
śabdo lakṣaṇayā varṇitaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>nanu cādhikārāntarakalpanādayo doṣāḥ</q> । pariharati---<q>dharmalakṣaṇāyāṃ
hyamī doṣāḥ । iha tu kāryaṃ lakṣayati yūpaśabdaḥ</q> । kimiti dharmāneva na
lakṣayatītyatrāha---<q>doṣaparihārāyaivādhikārāntarādidoṣaparihārārthaṃ kāryalakṣaṇā na
dharmalakṣaṇā ।</p>
<p>nanu caivaṃ sati khalevālī bhavatinā sambadhyate [vidhe] yatvāt । kārye hi
khalevālī vidheyā na khalevālyāṃ kāryaṃ tadāha---<q>na yūpaḥ khalevālyāṃ vidheyaḥ
lakṣaṇatvāt uddeśyatvāt</q> । tataśca sa eva vyavahitasambandhaḥ । kathamavyavadhānādi-
tyuktam ? <q>ucyate । kathaṃ vā yūpo bhavatīti</q> kārye hi lakṣyamāṇe na prathamāntatayā
sambandho ghaṭate । na hi bhavati khalevālī yūpakāryaṃ bhavatīti । kintu khalevālī
yūpakārye bhavatīti ।</p>
<p><q>atrocyate---khalevālīviśiṣṭo</q> yūpārthaścodyate । <q>kimidaṃ khalevālī
viśiṣṭo yūpārthaścodyata iti</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>idamidaṃ</q>, yathā dadhnā juhotīti dadhyanu-
rak‍tahomavidhānaṃ evaṃ khalevālyānurak‍tayūpakāryavidhānaṃ bhāvārthaviṣayo vidhiriti bhāvārthā-
tmakaṃ yūpakāryameva khalevālīviśiṣṭaṃ vidhīyata iti na vyavahitānvayaḥ । khalevālī
yūpo bhavatītyartho'sya vākyasya । kuto'yamartho'syetyatrāha---<q>bhavatiyogādyūpasya</q> ।
kathaṃ yūpatīti śabda ityatrāha---yathā śvatigardabhati iti sarvaprātipadikebhya ityeke
ityācāre kvip । evaṃ ca prathamāntaśabdo'pyupapannaḥ । yūpaśabdo'yaṃ gauṇo yūpasadṛśe
vartate । tenāyamarthaḥ---khale vālī yūpasadṛśī bhavatīti । kāryanibandhanaṃ ca sādṛśya-
mucyate । tataśca khalevālyanuraktaḥ yūpaḥ kāryaṃ yadi vidhīyate tadā kathamida-
mucyate yūpakārye khalevālī vidhīyata iti । tatrāha---<q>yāvadaprāptaṃ ca vihitaṃ
bhavati</q> prāptāprāptavivekena khalevālīvidhirucyata iti na prakaraṇabādhādayo doṣāḥ ।
nāpi vyavadhānam । ato luptadvārāṇāṃ khadirādīnāṃ yūpotpattyarthānāmaprāptiḥ ।</p>
<p>atha kasmāt yūpa eva khalevālīkṛtye na vyāpāryate । tathāhi na yūpārthoṃ
bāvito bhavati khalevālyā ca yūpakārya kṛtaṃ bhaviṣyatīti । kuto yūpasyāprāptirityatrāha
﻿<pb n="361"/>
---<q>ākṣiptaviśeṣābhidhānāt khalevālīśabdasya dhenuvat</q> । asyārthaḥ---yathā
dhenuśabdo dravyaparyanto na guṇamātraparyavasāyī tathā khalevālīśabdo'pyākṣiptadravya-
viśeṣavacano na khalevāraṇakriyāmātravacanaḥ । tatra yadi yūpa eva khalevālīkṛtye
vyāpāryaṃte tadā yūpasaṃskārāya khalevāraṇakriyāmātravidhirāpadyate tatra ca lakṣaṇādoṣaḥ ।
tasmādyūpabādhenaiva śrautārthānugraha iti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 31 ।। pareṣāṃ pratiṣedhaḥ syāt ।। 71 ।।</l></lg>
<p>khadirādayastāvadākṣiptaviśeṣavacanatvānnivṛttā ityuk‍tam dravyāntaravidhāne dravyā-
ntaranivṛtteḥ । <q>idānīṃ takṣaṇādayaścintyante kiṃ khalevālyāṃ kartavyā neti ।
tatra pūrvapakṣavādī upadeśāvirodhāt kartavyā iti manyate</q> । khalevālyāṃ
yūpakāryaṃ kartavyamiti yo'yamupadeśārthaḥ asau takṣaṇādiṣu kriyamāṇeṣvapi na viruddha‍yata
iti kartavyāstakṣaṇādayaḥ na hyatropadeśena virodhaḥ khadirādīnāmiva ।</p>
<p><q>nanu kāryaṃ nāsti takṣaṇādīnāṃ kimatrāvirodhaḥ kariṣyati</q> । joṣaṇa-
chedane tāvat joṣitāyāṃ chinnāyāṃ ca khalevālyāṃ luptakārye । takṣaṇamapi khale-
vālīvirodhādavidyamānakāryaṃ kimatrāvirodhaḥ kariṣyati । uttaraṃ---<q>tadeva tu kāryama-
virodhe sati nivṛttamiti na śakyate vak‍tumityabhiprāyaḥ</q> । ayamabhiprāyaḥ---
svarūpatastāvadvirodho nāsti । tenāvirodhe sati kartavyatayā pratibhāsamānānāmeṣāṃ
kāryaṃ kalpayitavyam । tenādṛṣṭārthe na punarapi joṣaṇachedane kariṣyete adṛṣṭārthaṃ ca
takṣaṇamiti । atrocyate । <q>dṛṣṭakāryatvāt tasya khalevālyāṃ cāśakyatvāt na
kāryāntarākāṅkṣā</q> । asyārthaḥ---klṛptakāryāṇāṃ prakṛtitaḥ prāptānāṃ tadeva kāryaṃ
pratibhātīti na kāryāntarākāṅakṣāsti yenāvirodhena kāryāntaraṃ kalpyeta । tasmānna
kāryāvirodhamātreṇa kāryāstitvaṃ śakyate vak‍tum । prākṛtaṃ ca kāryaṃ yattadeṣāṃ luptam ।
yadā caiṣāṃ prākṛtameva kāryaṃ tadā prakṛtau yūpotpattyarthatvāt ihāpi yūpotpattyarthairevai-
tairbhavitavyam । na cātra yūpena prayojanaṃ ayūpasya tatkārye vidhānāt khalevālyā yūpasya
ca bhinnatvāt । tataśca kāryābhāvānna kāryāstakṣaṇādayaḥ । tadāha-<q>kiñca yūpo-
tpattyarthāstakṣaṇādaya iti prakṛtāvuktam । ayūpaścāyaṃ niyojane vihita
iti na takṣaṇādayo bhavitumarhanti joṣaṇādayaśca kṛtatvānna kartavyā iti
pradarśitam</q> ।</p>
﻿<pb n="362"/>
<lg><l>।। 32 ।। arthābhāve saṃskāratvaṃ syāt ।। 73 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>kṛtatvāt kāryasya kāryāntarākāṅkṣā nāstīti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</q> । adbhi-
rava secanādibhiḥ kṛtaṃ tatkāryamiti punaḥ kāryamaparaṃ nākāṅkṣate । tena nivṛttireṣāmiti
pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । <q>satyaṃ yadi dṛṣṭameva kāryaṃ na syāt</q> । dṛṣṭe <q>punaḥ kārye kṛta-
mityeva nāsti khalevāraṇaśithilīkṛtāyāṃ khalevālyām</q> । 1asti ca
dārḍhyāpādanaṃ kāryamiti kṛtakāryatā nāsti kṛtasyāpyananuvartanāt । <q>tasmādaluptārthānāṃ
teṣāmabādhaḥ</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 33 ।। arthena ca viparyāse tādarthyāt tattvameva syāt ।। 74 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>iha pūrvavādī kramapadārtho'pi bādhyata iti manyate</q> । asyārthaḥ---
prakṛtau pākātpūrvamavaghātaḥ iha pākottarakālatā'vaghātasya syāditi kramabādhaḥ । tena
krame bādhite'vaghāto'pi bādhyata iti manyate pūrvapakṣavādī ।</p>
<p><q>nanu cāgnihotrahavaṇyā nirvapatīti na guṇānurodhena pradhānaṃ bādhyata
iti sthitameva । guṇaśca kramaḥ padārthāḥ pradhānabhūtāḥ । tena 2guṇabādhepi
pradhānaṃ kartavyameva kāryataścātra prāptirityuk‍tam</q> । tasya ca tuṣakaṇavimoka-
lakṣaṇasya ca kāryasya darśanādalopo'rthasyeti yuk‍tamevāvaghātānuṣṭhānam । <q>tasmāt
gatārthamevedaṃ pratibhāti uk‍tatvān‍nyāyasya</q> ।</p>
<p>atrocyate---<q>vidhivitānamātraṃ krama ityuk‍tam । na kramo nāmāgni-
hotrahavaṇīvat kaścidva‍yatirik‍to yasya pṛthagbādhaṃ varṇayāmaḥ</q> । tasmādvitānā-
nyatve padārthabādha aivati pūrvapakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>yadi hi svatantraḥ padārthakramaḥ syāt tadā tadabhāve padārthasvarūpānapāyāt
kriyetaivānuṣṭhānam । vitānastu padārthasya svarūpānupraviṣṭaḥ padārthā eva vitatāḥ
pratīyanta iti tadabhāve padārthasvarūpasyāpyabhāva iti kramabādhe padārtho'pi yathā-
codito bādhyate ।</p>
<note>1. R. astye va</note>
<note>2. R. guṇābhāvepi</note>
﻿<pb n="363"/>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu---kāryadarśane sati prayuktaṃ bādhituṃ[na]śakyate</q> । tuṣakaṇa-
vimocanasya kāryasya sambhavādavaghāto na śakyate bādhitum । yadi kāryaprayuk‍to-
'vaghāto na bādhyate <q>kasya tarhi bādhaḥ ?</q> uttaraṃ---<q>anuṣṭhānābhyāsasyeti
vadāmaḥ</q> । prakṛtai triḥphalīkaraṇavidhānāt sābhyāso'vadhātaḥ । iha dhānāsvabhyāse
tasmin kriyamāṇe sak‍tavo bhaveyuḥ tena svarūpavirodhādavaghātasyābhyāso bādhyate ।
sakṛdavadhātastu kriyate tāvanmātreṇa yāvattuṣakaṇavimocanaṃ tāvadeva kāryaṃ kriyate ।
sa cābhyāso'rthaprayuk‍tatvāt guṇa iti śakyate vak‍tuṃ avaghātābhyāsamantareṇa samyak
taṇḍulanirvṛttyabhāvāt arthākṣipto'vaghātābhyāsa iti guṇatvādbādhyate ।</p>
<p><q>kaḥpunarayaṃ vyatikramo bhāṣyakāreṇocyate</p> ? yadi vyatikramaḥ
tadā pūrvoktanyāyenāvadhātasyāpi bādhaḥ prāp‍noti । uttaraṃ---<q>śrutadravyābhiprāyeṇa
taducyate</q> । yacchrutaṃ dhānādravyaṃ tadabhiprāyeṇedamucyate । prakṛtau pākātprāgavaghātaḥ
kriyate । iha tu pākottarakālamiti vyatikramo bhaṇyate ।</p>
<p>paramārthatastu vyatikrama evāyaṃ na bhavati yadeva dravyaṃ śrutaṃ tasyaiva nirvāpa-
prokṣaṇānantaramavaghātaḥ । iha ca na pūrvāvasthā dhānānāṃ śrutā kintu dhānāvasthaiva ।
tadāha---<q>aśrutā tu pūrvāvasthā pradhānānām । tasmātsūktaṃ dhānāsvavahantiḥ
kartavya iti</q> ।</p>
<p>iti ṛjuvimalāyāṃ pañcikāyāṃ</p>
<p>daśamasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।</p>
﻿<pb n="364"/>
<p><q>ṛjuvimalāyāṃ</q></p>
<p><q>।। daśamādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।</q></p>
<p>।। 1 ।। vikṛtau śabdavattvātpradhānasya guṇānāmadhikotpattiḥ
sannidhānāt ।। 1 ।।</p>
<p>atra bhāṣyakāreṇa yāsu vikṛtiṣu prākṛteṣvaṅgeṣu guṇavidhayaḥ tā udāhṛtāḥ ।
tatra yathāśrutamātragrāhī kaścit tanmātrameva māgrahīt ityāha---<q>upadeśavidhāna-
yuktāni sarvāṇyeva vaikṛtānyudāharaṇāni</q> । rāddhānte nāmno'pyanekārthakalpanā
syādityabhyuccayopapattyarthaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇodāharaṇaviśeṣaḥ parigṛhītaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>kaḥpunaratra pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ ?</q> uttaraṃ---<q>ayamabhiprāyaḥ-
kāryataś‍codakaprāptiḥ</q> । tathāpi kimityāha---<q>kāryataś‍cet tadā tatprāp‍tyaiva
nirākāṅkṣaṃ pradhānam</q> । kāryato hi karaṇopakāralakṣaṇāt yā prāptiḥ sā upakāra-
janakatayaiva । tataścopakārajanakapadārthaprāp‍tyaiva nirākāṅkṣaṃ pradhānaṃ, nirākāṅkṣe ca
tasmin vihitasyāpi guṇasya pradhānavidhinā sambandhābhāvāt ananuṣṭhānāpattiḥ1,
guṇavidhyabhāve cānarthakatvaṃ vākyasya । na ca guṇe'dhikārāntarakalpanā sambhavati
prakṛtādhikāraikyāvagamāt । tasmāt guṇavidhyasambhavāt karmāntarāṇyevaitānīti yuktam ।</p>
<p>atra codayati---<q>karmāntarakalpanāyāṃ vā kathaṃ codakasya nirodhaḥ
asati ca nirodhe'rthavattā durbhaṇaiva । tasmāt karmāntaravādināpi pradhāna-
sambandhe samādhirvaktavyaḥ</q> । ucyate । <q>ayamasti samādhiḥ । pradhānaṃ hi vṛttyu-
pāyāpekṣam । yāvadupadeśavidhānanivṛttaṃ prākṛtamupāyamālocayati tāvada-
trāpi prakṛtivadupadeśa evāstīti na paropadeśanibandhanamupāyamapekṣate</q> ।
asyārthaḥ---karmāntaravidhipakṣe niyogaikyena pratipannakāryānupraveśānāṃ prākṛtetikarta-
vyatāsvīkāreṇa nirapekṣatayā aupadeśikānāmanupraveśabādho mābhūditi codako
nāṅgīkriyate । <q>kintu darvihomanyāyena yāvacchrutairupakāraḥ kalpyate; guṇa-
vidhau punaḥ kāryābhinirvṛtternāyaṃ parihārassambhavati</q> ।</p>
<note>1. R āyatteḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="365"/>
<p>asyārthaḥ---guṇavidhipakṣe svāśrayatayā prakṛtapadārthatayā prākṛtapadārthagrahaṇamanu-
mantavyam । tataśca prākṛtenaiva padārthavargeṇa nirākāṅkṣatayā punargaṇānupraveśo na
sambhavati ityukto viśeṣaḥ । prāgeva prayājādayaśca śabdāḥ sphuṭe karmāntaratve prakṛtāviva
bahūnāṃ vācakā ihāpi bhavitumarhanti anekārthatvābhyupagamāt । yathā eka eva
prayājaśabdaḥ prakṛtau bahūnāṃ samidādīnāṃ vācakaḥ tathā'mīṣāmapi karmāntarāṇāmutpadya-
mānānāṃ vācakaḥ prayogabalenānekārthatvāt ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ prāp‍te'bhidhīyate-satyaṃ kāryataḥ kāraṇopakāralakṣaṇāt prākṛtānāṃ
padārthānāṃ atideśo vikṛtyapūrvatādarthyenābhisambandhaḥ, satyaṃ ca nirjñātopā-
yatvāt nairākāṅkṣyam । niyogaikyamapi tu sannidhānānnaivāpanhotuṃ śakyate</q>
1prakṛtivadeva । yathā prakṛtau sannidhānamātreṇāṅgānāṃ pradhānānāṃ ca eka eva niyogaḥ
sādhyo'bhyupeyate tathā vikṛtāvapi tāvattathaiva pratīyate tadaikyāccādhikāṅgopasaṃhāro na
niṣpramāṇakaḥ niyogaikye'vagate yathopadiṣṭāṅgānāmeva prākṛtopakāraṃ prati janakatā
parikalpyate । asati hyupadeśe prākṛtenaiva padārthajātena tasyopakārasyehāpi siddhira-
vasīyate prakṛtiklṛptamevopakārasādhanaṃ vaikṛto vidhiranumanyate । upadiṣṭeṣvadhikeṣvaṅgeṣu
tadanupraveśasiddha‍yarthaṃ teṣāmapi tadupakārajananānupraveśaḥ kalpyate । na ca śaṅka‍yaṃ
codaka eva na pravartiṣyata iti, niyamānavāpteḥ । bhavanti cātra gāthāḥ---</p>
<lg><l>niyamānavāptivikalo liṅgabalopa(hitaṃ)sthitaṃ vidhiḥ prathamam ।</l>
<l>upakāraṃ parakīyaṃ svīkurute tāvaditi siddham ।। 1 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>upakārajanakabhūtaḥ padārthavargo vivakṣitaḥ prakṛtau ।</l>
<l>tādarthyamātreṇa prakārataḥ sannidhimupaiti vikṛtau ।। 2 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>upadeśanipatitāḥ śrūyante katipaye ca ye dharmāḥ ।</l>
<l>2te niyogaikyavaśāt tādarthyaṃ tatra gacchanti ।। 3 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>prākṛtapadārtharāśeḥ vaikṛtamupade(śikīṃ)śaḍhaukitaṃ tu tataḥ ।</l>
<l>vidhirupakārajanane sahāyabhāvena kalpayati ।। 4 ।।</l></lg>
<note>1. R prakṛtivadekavadeva</note>
<note>2. A. tepi niyo</note>
﻿<pb n="366"/>
<p>nanu guṇavidhau vākyena vidhānaṃ, karmavidhau tu śrutyetyatrāha-<q>na ca guṇe karmaṇi
viniyogasya kaścidviśeṣaḥ । guṇavidhāvapi bhāvārthaviṣaya eva vidhirityuktaṃ
yataḥ । ato guṇavidhi1sarūpeṣu vākyeṣu sambhavatpadārtheṣu na viśiṣṭavidhānaṃ
vidhigauravāpādakaṃ ātmānaṃ labhate</q> । codakāccoktaḥ sambhavaḥ । <q>tasmādguṇa-
vidhānānyevaitānīti yuktam । śeṣaṃ sanidarśanamuktam</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 2 ।। hiraṇyagarme pūrvasya mantraliṅgāt ।। 13 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>liṅgāt prakāśanasāmarthyātmakāt pūrvasyaivādhārasya mantravidhiriti
pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । anyathā hi adṛṣṭārtho mantraḥ syāt । indraprakāśa-
nāsāmarthyāt</q> । dvitīye ādhāre etasyaiva viniyogābhyupagame dṛṣṭārtho mantraḥ syāt ।
<quote>‘ūrdhvo adhvara’</quote> iti mantrāntarasya codakaprāptasya bādhaśca na kalpito bhavati ।
<q>atatkāryakaraṇenābhyupagatena tatkāryakaraṇe tvabhyupagamyamāne mantrāntareṇa
mantrāntarasya bādhaḥ syāt</q> ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ prāpte abhidhīyate । na kāryāntarakalpanā sambhavati । upāyā-
ntaramātravidhānopakṣīṇatvādupadeśasya</q> । asyārthaḥ-dvitīya ādhāre mantrakāryaṃ
klṛptamasti pūrvasmiṃścādhāre mantrāntarakāryaṃ kalpayitavyam । na ca kalpanāyāṃ pramāṇa-
masti mantrāntaravidhimātreṇopadeśasyopapatteḥ mantrasya cendrābhidhānepi tulyatvāt ।
<q>darśitaṃ ca bhāṣyakāreṇa tulyatvaṃ ca । tasmāduttarasyaiva mantrāntaravidhiriti
sūk‍tam</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 3 ।। saṃskare tu kriyāntaraṃ tasya vidhāyakatvāt ।। 18 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nanu ca ekādaśa prayājān yajatītyanenaiva gatam । guṇavidhau
sambhavati na viśiṣṭavidhānaṃ sambhavatīti</q> । asyārthaḥ---prākṛtayorevāsādananiyo-
janayorutkaraparidhilakṣaṇaguṇavidhānena vākyayorupapannatvāt na viśiṣṭavidhānaṃ yuk‍ta-
māśrayitum । samādhatte---<q>satyametadevaṃ aśakyatvāttu punarāśaṅkyate</q> yathāvagata-
svarūpayorutkaraparidhyoruttuṅgatīkṣṇāgrakṛśayoḥ prākṛtamāsādanaṃ niyojanaṃ ca dṛṣṭārthaṃ-
maśakyamiti adṛṣṭārthaṃ karmāntaravidhānamiti punarāśaṅkā । tadāha---<q>nāsādana</q>-
<note>1. svarūpeṣu</note>
﻿<pb n="367"/>
<q>niyojane prākṛte dṛṣṭārthe tūtkaraparidhyoḥ</q> tuṅgatīkṣṇāgrakṛśayoḥ sambhavata ityabhi-
prāyaḥ । etacca guṇavidhāvapi vākyabhedo nāstītyabhyupagamyaiva pūrvakṣitam ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu---yāvacchakyaṃ niyogārtho'nuṣṭheyaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---prākṛta-
yoreva guṇavidhirastu । tatra yacchakyaṃ tadanuṣṭhāsyate tatra tuṅgāgratā kṛśatā ca
aśakyeti nāpekṣyate pṛthvagratā sthavimā ca kalpayiṣyate yathā bhaviṣyati śak‍tiḥ ।
tadāha---<q>[sa] ca pṛthvagrakaraṇenotkarasya sthavimnā ca paridheḥ niyogārtho
'nuṣṭhāsyate</q> । ato nādṛṣṭaprayojanakalpanā yuk‍tā, kartavyatāniṣṭhatvānniyogāvagateḥ ।
kartavyatāniṣṭho hi niyogo na prayojananiṣṭhaḥ । tena prayojanāntarakalpanā nāsti ।
klṛptakāryāśrayaṇepi anuṣṭhānopapatteḥ । tasmādatrāpi guṇavidhireva nyāyyaḥ ।</p>
<p>evaṃ samāpte'dhikaraṇe kṛtvācintāmuddhāṭayati---<q>viśiṣṭānuvādādi cātra
nāśaṅkanīyam</q> । nirjñātakāryaviṣayatvādevamāderupadeśasya viśiṣṭavidhānepyadoṣaḥ ।
<q>yadyapyanekaguṇaśravaṇāt nāsādananiyojanāntaravidhiḥ tathāpi prākṛtakārye
vidhānānna doṣaḥ phalasya tulyatvāt</q> । guṇavidhau yādṛśaṃ phalaṃ tādṛśameva viśiṣṭa-
vidhāvapi । sarvatra cedamuk‍tam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 4 ।। ṣaṅ‍‍bhirdīkṣayatīti tāsāṃ mantravikāraḥ
śrutisaṃyogāt ।। 23 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>atra pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ vaikṛtāstāvanmantrāḥ prākṛtakārya eva viniyuktāḥ
śarā iva barhiṣāṃ kārye । ataḥ kāryāpahārāt prākṛtānāṃ nivṛttiḥ</q> ।</p>
<p>nanu homānāmabhyāsāt prākṛtā vaikṛtāśca mantrāḥ samuccīyanta ityatrāha---
<q>na cābhyāse kāryāntaraṃ mantrāṇāṃ sambhavati homānāmabhyāsepi</q> mantrāṇāṃ
kāryāntaraṃ nāsti kāryānyatve hi abhyāsānupapa(ttiḥ)tteḥ tathābhūtasyaiva punaranuṣṭhāna-
mabhyāsaḥ । mantrakāryabhede ca na tathābhūtatvaṃ ekatve ca kāryasya tasminneva mantrāntara-
vidhānam । tasmādvādho nyāyyaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu satyaṃ prākṛtakārye vidhānaṃ kṛtatvāttu kāryasya na mantrā-
bhyāsaṃ nyāyyaṃ manyāmahe</q> । sakṛdupadiṣṭaiḥ kārye kṛte'rthavattā tadupadeśasya jāteti
na mantrābhyāso yuk‍taḥ kāryābhyāsepi । <q>nanu tasminneva kārye satyabhyāsa upa</q>-
﻿<pb n="368"/>
<q>padyate na kāryāntare;</q> pariharati---<q>etadapi satyaṃ na kāryāntare satyabhyāsa
iti । kimiti tarhyanabhyāso mantrāṇām</q> । kāryavanmantrābhyāso'pi 1nyāyya
iti bhāvaḥ । uttaraṃ---<q>kṛtaṃ tadupadeśeneti vadāmaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---mantropadeśena
mantrānuṣṭhānaṃ kṛtam । akṛte ca tasmin mantrābhyāse na pramāṇamasti । <q>upadeśa-
sampattyartho hyatra kāryayogo vaikṛtānām । na kāryataḥ kāryayogaḥ</q> । kārya-
mastītyetāvatā kāryaṃ na kartavyam kintūpadeśasampattaye । tasmāt sakṛtkaraṇenaivo-
padeśaḥ sampanna ityabhyāsāntare bādhāyālaṃ bhavitumarhati । yadi punaḥ kāryata eva
kāryaṃ syāt tadā kāryasya vidyamānatvāt mantraprāpteḥ prākṛtabādha eva syāt । na
caitadasti tadāha---<q>kāryatastu bādha eva । na cāyaṃ kāryata ityuktam ।
tasmātsamuccayaḥ । śeṣamuktam</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 5 ।। agna‍yādheyasya naimittike guṇavikāre dakṣiṇādānamadhikaṃ
syādvākyasaṃyogāt ।। 30 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>atra ekasmin kārye vidhānādanabhyāsācca nivṛttiriti sthite kathaṃ
pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ? punarādhāne yā dakṣiṇā sā prākṛtadakṣiṇākārye vihitā । na
ca punarādheyasyābhyāso'stīti bādha eva yuk‍to na samuccaya iti sthite
kathaṃ pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</q> ? samādhatte---<q>vacanabhrāntyā ubhayīrdadātīti vacanamiti
bhrāmyataḥ pūrvapakṣaḥ । bhrāntipradarśanena ca rāddhāntaḥ</q> । vacanamidamiti bhrānti-
reṣā । kintvanuvādo'yaṃ agnyādheye āgnyādheyikīrdadāti, punarādheye paunarādheyikī-
riti rāddhāntaḥ । <q>liṅgamuk‍tam</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 6 ।। vāsovatsaṃ ca sāpnānyāt ।। 34 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>uttaravivakṣayeti</q>---satyamuttaranyāyaṃ vak‍tumidamuk‍tamiti satyaṃ nānyat ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 7 ।। arthāpattestaddharmā syānnimittasyābhisaṃyogāt ।। 35 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>atra taddharmatve na tāban‍nyāyo'bhidhīyata ityuk‍taṃ bhāṣye । tadayuk‍tam ।
uk‍taṃ hi yo yasya kārye vartate sa taddharmān labhata iti navame</q> । tasmādayuktai-
<note>1. R. kārya iti</note>
﻿<pb n="369"/>
vānvāhāryadharmabādhāśaṅkā vāsovatsayoḥ । ekagranthenāha---<q>yadi dharmaprāptirnāsti
kathaṃ prāptipūrvako bādhaḥ</q> । prāptiścet siddhaṃ tarhi taddharmatvam । samādhatte---<q>prāpti-
ruttaravivakṣayetyetadarthameva tad‍draṣṭavyam । kathaṃ tarhi pūrvamadhikaraṇam ? prāptiḥ
smāraṇīyeti</q> । prāptiṃ smārayitumeva pūrvamadhikaraṇam । 1yadi prāptiḥ smaryate tadā
tatsmṛtau pūrvapakṣāśrayaṇamayuk‍tam । siddha evārthaḥ smaraṇīyaḥ । samādhatte---<q>nāyuk‍taṃ
pūrvapakṣasmāraṇam</q> । sahetukaṃ hi smāraṇaṃ nirviśaṅkamuttaropayogi bhavatīti sapratipakṣa-
muk‍tam । pūrvapakṣe hyasmārite tannirākaraṇapūrvakaḥ siddhāntaheturna śakyate vaditum
anuk‍te ca siddhāntahetau mandabuddheḥ kathametadevamiti śaṅkā syāt । tataścottaracintā
na śakyā kartumiti sapratipakṣamupanyasyate ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 8 ।। dāne pāko'rthalakṣaṇaḥ ।। 36 ।।</l></lg>
<p>yadarthā prāptiḥ smāritā tadevedānīṃ cintyate । <q>tatra 2vatse tāvat pākaś‍ci-
ntyate---kiṃ kartavyo neti । tatra pūrvapakṣavādī nyāyyaṃ pākaṃ manyate । evaṃ
prākṛtaṃ annaṃ sādhanaṃ yasya tadannasādhanaṃ dakṣiṇādānaṃ na pīḍitaṃ bhaviṣyati</q> ।</p>
<p>nanu vatso dakṣiṇeti śrūyate kathaṃ tanmāṃsaṃ dakṣiṇā tatrāha---<q>vatsopadeśaśca
prakṛtidravyatayāpyupapan‍no bhavati vrīhibhiryajetetivat</q> ।</p>
<p>nanu cātra vatsaḥ pacyamāno'pi nānnaṃ bhavatītyatrāha---<q>bhavati ca māṃse
an‍naśabdaḥ paramaṃ vā etadan‍naṃ yanmāṃsaṃ iti</q> ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---vatso dakṣiṇeti vatsasya dakṣi</q>ṇātvaṃ śrūyate । yā
ca dakṣakaraṇī sā dakṣiṇā । yacca dīyate tat dakṣakaram । yadyatra śrapaṇena vatsamāṃsaṃ
dīyate na tarhi vatso dakṣiṇā । na ca pradeyaprakṛtitayā pradeyatā bhavati । tasmānna
māṃsalakṣaṇārtho vatsaśabdo varṇanīyaḥ । vrīhibhiryatetyatra tu yāgaṃ prati karaṇatvaṃ
brīhīṇāmavagamyate । bhavati ca puroḍāśaniṣpattiṃ avāntaravyāpārīkṛtya karaṇatā
vrīhīṇāmapi । tena na tatra lakṣaṇā । iha tu darśitā lakṣaṇā । na ca kāraṇādṛte
lakṣaṇā nyāyyetyuk‍tam ।</p>
<note>1. R. yadi prāptimeva smārayituṃ</note>
<note>2. A. vāsovatsayoḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="370"/>
<p>nanu prakṛtivaditi lakṣaṇākāraṇamupanyastam । na kāraṇaṃ bhavitumarhati prakṛti-
vaditi kāryamātrasyātideśāt । anvāhāryakāryaṃ prakṛtivadityatidiśyate tadākṣepeṇacā-
nvāhāryaṃ tatra । vatsenānvāhāryakārye vihite bādhite'nvāhārye na lakṣaṇākāryamasti
anannasyaivānnakārye vidhānāt । tadāha---<q>vatsena ca tasyānvāhāryakāryasya
siddheḥ na pākaprāptau pramāṇamasti pākasyānnahetutvāt</q> । tasmāt <q>śrutopa-
deśasiddha‍yarthaṃ vatsa eva dātavyaḥ</q> । pāke hi upadiṣṭārthavināśaḥ syāt ।
<q>nanu ca adanīyenānamanaṃ prakṛtau tena vikṛtāvapyadanīyenaivānatiḥ kartavyā ।
tataśca tatsiddha‍yarthaṃ pāko'pi kartavya iti</q> ।</p>
<p>pariharati---<q>na, tasyādanīyatvasyānuṣaṅgikatvāt anvāhāryasvarūpe-
ṇādanīyatvamanuṣajyate na tu pṛthak śabdena tasya vidhānamasti</q> । annamātraṃ
śabdārtho nādanīyatvaṃ; tadidamuktaṃ---<q>na puruṣasaṃskārāyedaṃ dānaṃ bhavatīti</q> । na
puruṣatṛp‍tyarthamidaṃ dānaṃ bhavatītyarthaḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 9 ।। pākasya cānnakāritatvāt ।। 37 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>yuktaṃ vatse upadeśārthavināśāt pāko na kriyata iti</q> । ekagranthenāha
---<q>vāsasi tarhi avināśāt kriyatāṃ pākaḥ</q> । pakvamapi vāso vāsa eva ।
idānīmākṣipati---<q>nanu vāsasyapi kāryābhāvānnivṛttiḥ</q> siddhaiva । pākakārya-
manvāhārye prasiddhaṃ vāsasi nāsti dvāralopāt vāsasyapi pāko bādhanīyaḥ । na ca
śabdārthasampattaye padārthāḥ kriyante, kiṃ tarhi ? kāryārthatayetyuktam । tasmānmandamatra
nirākaraṇīyam । samādhatte---<q>vikāramātrāśaṅkayā kāryasambhavaṃ manyate pūrvapakṣa-
vādī</q> । asyārthaḥ---pūrvapakṣavādī pākyavikāramātraṃ pākakāryaṃ manyate । sambhavati
ca vāsasyapi pākādvikāraḥ tena nāsti dvāralopa iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu viśiṣṭavikārārtho loke pākaḥprasiddhaḥ । ko'sau viśiṣṭo
vikāraḥ ? annaśabdābhidhānanimittamiti brūmaḥ</q> । yasmin sati annaśabdavācyatā
bhavati sa vikāro'nvāhārye kāryatayā sammataḥ । na ca pacyamānaṃ vāso'nnatāṃ
pratipadyate ityatrāpi vatsa iva pākasya nivṛttiḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 10 ।। tathā'bhidhāraṇasya ।। 38 ।।</l></lg>
﻿<pb n="371"/>
<p><q>abhidhāraṇamidānīṃ cintyate - kiṃ vatse vāsasi cābhidhāraṇaṃ kartavyaṃ
neti । atra pūrvapakṣavādī adṛṣṭasaṃskāramabhidhāraṇenānvāhāryasya manvāno-
'bhidhāraṇasya kartavyatāṃ manyate ।</q></p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu---na hi dṛṣṭe sambhavati adṛṣṭakalpanā nyāyyeti hetoḥ
svādimaivābhidhāraṇasya prayojanaṃ ṛtvijāmānatāvupayogāt</q> । yathā hi
svādunā'nnenānamante na tathetareṇeti lokaprasiddham । na ca tena svādimnā vatse vāsasi
ca prayojanamasti anadanīyatvāttayoḥ । adanīyadravyavartī hi svādimā puruṣānatā-
vupayujyate । na punaranadanīyavartyapi iti prayojanābhāvādabhidhāraṇaṃ bādhyate ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 11 ।। dravyavidhisannidhau saṅkhyā teṣāṃ guṇatvātsyāt ।। 39 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>kaḥpunarasyādhikaraṇasya bādhalakṣaṇe prasaṅgaḥ ?</q> uttaraṃ---<q>dakṣiṇābādha-
siddha‍yarthamaupoddhātikamidamadhikaraṇam</q> । varṇayiṣyate hi saṅa‍khyāyuktānāṃ bhāgaśaḥ
kārts‍nyena ca bādhaḥ । yadi hi gavāṃ saṅa‍khyāsambandhaḥ tadā vikṛtiṣu saṅa‍khyāntaraśravaṇe
tāsāmeva bādhaḥ । tatrartvigbhāge saṅa‍khyāntaraśravaṇe gogatasyaiva bhāgasya bādhaḥ kevala-
saṅkhyāntaraśravaṇe kṛts‍nānāmeva gavāṃ bādha iti । na kevalamidamadhikaraṇamevamarthaṃ
<q>vibhāgena ca dānamidamarthatayaiva cintyate</q> । pariṣadadhikaraṇamapyupoddhātabhūta-
mityarthaḥ । tasmādasti bādhalakṣaṇe prasaṅgo'syādhikaraṇasya ।</p> 
<p>nani <quote>‘tasya dvādaśaśataṃ’</quote> iti tacchabdena 1prakṛtatvāt kraturevocyate na gavādiḥ
tatkathaṃ gavādiparaṃ tacchabdaṃ gṛhītvā vicāra iti tatrāha---<q>tasya śabdaṃ kratorapanī-
yaiṣā cintā</q> । dravyāṇāmeva tacchabdenāvamarśa iti cinteyam । abhyupagamyāpi
tasyaśabdāntaḥ pātināṃ dravyāṇāṃ gavāmeva saṅkhyāsambandha iti vak‍tuṃ kṛtvā cinteyam ।
<q>tatrāgṛhyamāṇaviśeṣo vā sarveṣāṃ saṅkhyā sambandhahetuḥ । tena pratyekaṃ
saṅkhyāsambandhaḥ ekena vā kṛtārthatvāt yena kenacit ekenetyayameva
viśeṣahetuḥ ।</q> asyārthaḥ---saṅkhyā gavādayaśca dakṣiṇayā sambadhyante । tatrāruṇaika-
hāyanīnyāyena dravyamāśritya saṅkhyāyā anvayo'nubhavanīya iti yatkiñcid dravya-
māśrīyate na sarvāṇīti । caśabdayogādvā saṃhatiḥ saṅkhyāsambandhinīti pratibhā ।
<note>1. R. prākṛta</note>
﻿<pb n="372"/>
yadyapi saṅkhyā āśrayamātramapekṣate tathāpi caśabdaśravaṇe dravyāṇāṃ samuccayo'vagamyate ।
sa eva ca saṅkhyāsambandhī bhaviṣyatīti pratibhāmātram ।</p> 
<p><q>ānantaryādvā bhāṣāḥ sambandhinaḥ tadanantaraṃ saṅkhyāśravaṇāt ।</q>
saṅkhyāmātravyāvahārikatayā prāṇinaḥ saṅkhyāsambandhinaḥ । saṅkhyāmātreṇa vyāvahā-
rikāḥ vyavahārāya prabhavanti prāṇinaḥ na bhāṣādaya iva kuḍabādyavacchedāpekṣiṇaḥ । tena
sāpekṣatvāt vrīhyādīnāṃ na saṅkhyāsambandhaḥ । kintu prāṇināmeva । upakārādhikyādvā
goṣvaś‍veṣu ca prasaktiḥ । ṛtvijo hi mahatyupakāre vartante । upakurvatāṃ copakāraḥ
kartavya iti sadācāraḥ । tena mahopakārā gāvo'śvā vā saṅkhyāsambandhinaḥ । asmiṃśca
pakṣe'śvaḥ pratiṣedhānnivartate । ubhayatodatāṃ vyavahāro hi vipratiṣiddha iti na
pracuropayogā aśvāḥ । tena te'pi saṅkhyayā na sambadhyante । kintu gāva eva
pracuropayogitvāt । mahābhāgā hi tāḥ ।</p>
<p>atrādhikaraṇe pratyekaṃ 1saṅkhyāsambandho dravyaprādhānyenāśaṅkitaḥ । tatra
codyamāha---<q>nanu dravyaprādhānyapakṣopanyāso'sakṛnnavame nirākṛtaḥ । tena
kimityupanyasyate ।</q> dravyamātrasambandhe hi ānarthakyamuditam । parihāramāha---
<q>upādānata ānarthakyaṃ parihiṛyata ityabhiprāyo dravyaprādhānyavādinaḥ ।</q>
yathā paśvādīnāmekatvādikaṃ dravyamātrasambandhyupādānato'narthakaṃ bhavati upādānaśeṣa-
tvāt tatheyamapi saṅkhyeti । <q>kathaṃ tarhi ayaṃ pakṣo nirākriyate nirākaraṇīya-
ścāyam । anirākṛte hi aruṇānyāyo nāvatarati</q> । anavatīrṇe ca tasmin
gomātrasambandho na saṅkhyāyāḥ syādityatrāha---<q>prātipadikopāttatayā nopā-
dānataḥ śeṣatvaṃ sambhavatīti nirākaraṇam ।</q> prātipadikopāttā hi saṅkhyā
kriyayaiva śabdāt sambandhyate ityaruṇānyāyena viniyogaśeṣatvameva syāt,
nopādānaśeṣatvam । vibhak‍tyabhihitā tu prātipadikamātrasambandhinī śrutyaiva vibhaktyā-
'bhidhīyata iti bhavatyupādānaśeṣaḥ । bhavatvaruṇānyāyaḥ tathāpi caśabdārthaḥ kimiti
saṅkhyāsanbandhī na bhavatītyatrāha---<q>caśabdārthaḥ punaḥ naivānvayī । anvitārthābhi-
dhāyino hyete ।</q> asyārthaḥ---caśabdasyārtho na padārthānvayabhāgbhavati samuccaya-
śabdavat niṣkṛṣṭasyārthasya caśabdenānabhidhānāt । na hi bhavati caḥ śobhana iti ।
kintu parānvitaṃ paropaśliṣṭaṃ svārtha nipātā abhidadhati ।</p>
<note>1. R dravyaṃ prādhānyenāśaṅkitam</note>
﻿<pb n="373"/>
<p>nanu ca yadīha na samuccitānāṃ saṅkhyāsambandhaḥ kutastarhi teṣāṃ samuccayaśca-
śabdena dyotyata ityatrāha---<q>dakṣiṇānvayena caśabdaścaritārthaḥ samuccitānāṃ
dakṣiṇātvamiti vakṣyate</q> iti caśabdārtho nirastaḥ । saṅkhyāsambandhitayā
vyavahārābhāvāt aprāṇito nirastāḥ । na hi kuḍabādinirapekṣaṃ kevalasaṅkhyā-
mātrāvacchinnaiḥ vrīhyādibījaiḥ loke vyavahāro'sti । tena vyavahārānanurūpatvāt na
teṣāṃ saṅkhyāsambandhaḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu sarve prāṇinaḥ saṃhatāḥ saṅkhyayā kimiti na sambadhyante ityatrāha---
<q>ekenāpi prāṇinā saṅkhyopapadyata iti prāṇimātranirāsaḥ । mātraśabdaścātra
sākalyārthaḥ । niraste ca prāṇimātre ekaprāṇimātrasambandhe sthite mukhya-
tvāt prathamopanipātitvāt mahopakāritvāt apratiṣiddhatvācca gāva eva
saṅkhyāsambandhinyaḥ iti nirūpitam ।</q> tathā ca darśanamityuktam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 12 ।। tatra dānaṃ vibhāgena pradānānāṃ pṛthak‍tvāt ।। 50 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nanu parasvatvāpādanānto dadātiriti loke prasiddhatvāt pṛthak‍tvena
cartvijāmutpatteḥ pūrvapakṣa evātra na saṃvartate</q> । yadi hi svatvatyāgamātrarūpo
dadātyarthaḥ syāt tadā vibhāgamantareṇāpi tyāgasya śakyatvāt aniyamena dānaṃ
yuktamevāśaṅikatum । na ca tadasti । na hi tyāgamātre dānaśabdaṃ lokaḥ prayuṅkte ।
kintu ya eva parasvatvāpādanāntaḥ tyāgaḥ tatraiva dānaśabdo loke prasiddhaḥ । yadi ca
bhedenartvijāmutpattiḥ na syāt eka evartvik 1tadāpi vibhāgāniyamena dānaṃ
saṃvarteta । bhinnāścartvijaḥ । tān pratyavibhāgena na śakyaṃ dānaṃ kartu, (m) miti ।</p>
<p>nanu kathamaśaktiḥ ? yadi tāvat svatvāpādanāntatvaṃ na sambhavatītyucyeta
kathamasambhavaḥ । bhavati hi avibhaktamapi madhyagaṃ dravyaṃ 2sambhūyasamutthāyināṃ bhrātṝṇāṃ ca
pitāputrayordempatyośca । anyathā hi kulāyayajñādīnāmanutpattireva3 ārjanaṃ svatvā-
pādakamityuk‍taṃ caturthe । yadā''rjanameva sādhāraṇaṃ tatra svatvamapi sādhāraṇameva
kathamanyadīyamanyasyeti nāśaṅkanīyam । pratipattivirodho'yaṃ na vastuvirodhaḥ । tatra
<note>1. A tada vibhaktamapi madhyagāniyame prāpte</note>
<note>2. R. saṃsṛṣṭānāṃ bhrātṝṇāṃ</note>
<note>3. R. manutpatti</note>
﻿<pb n="074"/>
yanmadhyagaṃ svaṃ tatrānyadīyasya sato nānyadīyatayā'vagatiḥ kintu yugapadeva sādhāraṇa-
tayā; yathā---yadātithyāyāṃ barhiriti ।</p>
<p>athocyeta yadyapi bhavati kiñcitsvaṃ madhyagamapi tathāpi yugapat bahūn
svāminaḥ prati na śakyate svatvamāpādayitumiti nāśak‍tau kāraṇaṃ vācyam ।</p>
<p>idamucyate---paramuddiṃśya tyāgaṃ kurvāṇo hi dātā parasvatvāpādanāntaṃ dadā-
tyarthamabhiniṣpādayati । na ca yugapat bahava ekenoddeṣṭuṃ śakyante anyonyanira-
pekṣāḥ anāpannasamudāyabhāvāśca । deyāstu bahavo'nyonyanirapekṣā api saṅkhyādyavacche-
dāt । gavādayaśca śataṃ sahasraṃ vā śakyanta eva yugapad‌buddhisthīkartum1 paramuddiśya ca
tyak‍tum । krameṇa tūddiśya tyāge tyaktasya punastyāgānupapatteḥ dvitīyādityāgānupapattiḥ ।
nāpyanyonyasāpekṣān yugapaduddiśya tyāgopapattiḥ । tathābhāvena ca teṣāṃ anapekṣa-
tvāt । caitanyena hi svāmī । na caitanye'nyonyāpekṣatvaṃ puruṣāṇām । ato'nyo-
nyāpekṣāṇāṃ svāmitvaṃ na sambhavatīti pūrvapakṣa evātrādhikaraṇe na saṃvartate । samādhatte---
<q>satyaṃ tathāpi loka2vyavahāro'yathārtho dṛśyate</q> vyāmohamūlaḥ । yathā kenacinmī-
māṃsājñānavikalacetasā pariṣade dīyate'dṛṣṭārtham । yadā ca kṛpayā dṛṣṭārthaṃ mahājanāya
dīyate । teca svayameva vibhajanti vibhāgena ca karma kurvate । taddarśanāt kasya
cinmandadhiyaḥ iyamāśaṅkodayate---avibhajyāpi ca dakṣiṇā dātavyeti । tasmāt
vyāvahārādvyāmohamūlāt3 kasyacidavibhajyāpi dātavyeti bhrāntirudayate । tadapanaya-
nārthamidamadhikaraṇam ।</p>
<p>atra codayati---<q>yadyevaṃ yadi loke pariṣadepi dānavyavahāro'sti
tadā kathamidamupagamyate pratyekaṃ dānapadārtho4 niṣpadyate na pariṣadīti ।
yāvatā lokavyavahārabalena evameva kimiti na bhavati ।</q> pariharati---<q>atra
padārthavidaḥ svīkaraṇaparyantaṃ dadātyarthaṃ bruvate ।</q> parasvīkāraparyanto dadātyartha iti
śabdārthaṃvido vadanti । <q>kiṃpunastatra bhavatāṃ pramāṇaṃ</q> svīkāraparyanto dadātirityatreti ।
<note>1. P. buddha‍yā svīkartum</note>
<note>2. A vyavahāre</note>
<note>3. R vyavahāramūlatayā</note>
<note>4. P dadātyarthī</note>
﻿<pb n="375"/>
<q>ṣaṣṭhyantāditarebhyopi dṛśyata iti</q> tral । uttaraṃ---<q>loka evaiṣāṃ pramāṇam tyāga-
mātre dadāteraprayogāt</q> । bhavatu parasvīkaraṇānto dadātiḥ tathāpi kathaṃ pariṣade dānā-
nupapattiḥ ityatrāha-<q>pariṣade yaddattaṃ tatra pariṣadino vaktāro bhavanti pareṇa
prāpitaṃ nāsmākamidamadyāpi svamiti</q> । tathā ca lokayātrāvidaḥ pariṣadyekena
kṛtaṃ dattamakṛtamadattaṃ manyante । tatkasya hetoḥ asvāmitvāditi gamyate । datte pariṣadaḥ1
svāmitvābhāvāt na svīkaraṇānto dadātiḥ pariṣadyupapadyate । pratyekadāne naitad‌dvayaṃ
pūrvoktamasti । tatra pratigrahītāro'smākamidamiti manyante । lokayātrāvidaśca
dattametaditi manyante । tena tatra svīkaraṇamasti । tasmāt padārthavidāṃ sādhunirṇayaḥ
svīkaraṇaparyanto dadātiḥ iti । sa ca pariṣadi nopapadyata iti । yāveva codyaparihārau
tāveva pūrvottarapakṣāviti । śeṣamuktam ।</p>
<p>atra codayati---<q>yuktametatpariṣadi svatvaṃ na niṣpadyata2 iti dānā-
nirvṛttistu kathaṃ ?</q> tyāgamātraṃ dānaṃ manvānasya codyam । tadevāha---<q>ubhayatra
dattamiti prayuñjate dātāraḥ pratigrahītāraśca</q> yatpariṣade dattaṃ yacca pratyekaṃ tatrobhayatrāpi
dattamiti prayogaḥ tena pariṣadyapi dānaṃ niṣpadyata eva । tasmānnāyaṃ nirṇayahetuḥ ।</p>
<p>atrocyate---ayameva nirṇayahetuḥ yāpūrvamuktaḥ yadi hi svīkaraṇādṛtepi
dānānirvṛttiḥ tadā tyāgadānaśabdau paryāyau syātām । paryāyatvaṃ loke prasiddham । nacā-
nyathā paryāyatvasiddhiḥ । tasmāt svīkaraṇānto dadātiḥ । tathā ca laukikāḥ
pareṇāsvīkṛte dattepi svāminā saṅkalpitamidaṃ nādyāpi dīyata iti bruvate । tasmāt
svīkaraṇānto dadātiḥ । ataḥ pariṣade dattamiti yaḥ prayogaḥ asāvupakrama eva samāpti-
paryantasya vācakaḥ prayujyate । tyāgopakramaḥ svīkaraṇaparyanto dadātiriti । tena
tyāgamātre dānopakrame lakṣaṇayā prayujyate । na kevalaṃ lakṣaṇayā tyaktamātre dattaśabdaḥ
api tu saṅkalpite'pi dadātiṃ prayuñjānā dṛśyante dattamedāyuṣmatā yatsaṅkalpitamiti ।
tasmāllakṣaṇayāpi prayogadarśanāt na prayogamātrācchabdārthavyavasthitiḥ । <q>yadi na
prayogācchabdārthavyavasthitiḥ kathaṃ tarhi ?</q> uttaraṃ---<q>yatra na sambandhyantara-
balādavagatiḥ sa śabdārthaḥ iti ।</q> yaḥ padārthāntarasambandhānapekṣaḥ śabdādartho-
<note>1. R tena pariṣādināṃ</note>
<note>2 R. nopapadyata iti</note>
﻿<pb n="376"/>
'vagamyate sa śabdārthaḥ । yaḥ punaḥ sambandhyantarabalenārtho'vagamyate sa gauṇo
lākṣaṇiko vā bhavati । atra ca devadattāya gāvo dīyantāṃ ityukte svīkaraṇānta eva
dadātyarthaḥ pratīyate parityāgamātrepyananvayo nāsti । tathāpi yeyaṃ svīkaraṇāntapratītiḥ
saiva śabdamātranibandhaneti gamyate । pariṣade dattamiti yā tyāgamātrāvagatiḥ pariṣa-
tpadārthasambandhabalāditi nāsau śabdamātranibandhanā । <q>yadi pariṣade dānānupapattiḥ
kathaṃ tarhi pariṣade dānaṃ laukikānām</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>bhrāntyeti vadāmaḥ caitya-
vandanādivat</q> । yathā nirmūlamapi caityavandanāt svargo bhavatīti vyāmohenādriyamāṇā
bhrāntyā caityavandanādikaṃ kurvate tathehāpi nāvaśyamavyāmohādeva laukikavyavahāraḥ
prāyeṇa vyāmohapūrvaka eva laukiko vyavahāraḥ । ata eva parīkṣaṇamapi nyāyavidāṃ
pravṛttam । yadi bhrāntyā loko na vyavaharati tadā kiṃ parīkṣaṇena ? tadāha---
<q>parīkṣaṇaṃ ca nyāyavidāṃ laukikavyavahāramūḍhatayaiva pravṛttam</q> । tasmāt sapramāṇa
evāyaṃ nirṇayaḥ padārthavidāṃ svīkaraṇaparyanto dadātiriti sthitam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 13 ।। samaṃ syādaśrutatvāt ।। 53 ।।</l></lg>
<p>kathaṃ punaḥ pakṣadvayepi samākhyānirdeśaḥ; yadā samaṃ dāna yadā ca karmānurūpyeṇa
tadā kathamardhyādisamākhyānirdeśaḥ ? pariharati---<q>abhyudaya eva dvādaśāha eveti
manyate</q> । asyārthaḥ---dvādaśāhe samākhyānirdeśaḥ tena paraṃ tatraiva bhavatveṣā bhāgakalpanā
na punaḥ kratvantare bhavitumarhati । dvividhaśca dvādaśāhaḥ - satramahīnaśca । tatra yadyapi
satre dānānupapattiḥ tathāpyahīne bhaviṣyati । <q>rāddhāntavādī tvavidhānātprākṛtaṃ
tadityāha</q> । asyārthaḥ - idaṃ vākyaṃ satrabhūte, tatra na dānabhāgavidhiḥ kintu siddha-
vadbhāgasanbandhenāyamṛtvijāṃ vyapadeśo yajamāne prayuktaḥ । na hyanyathā prākṛtaṃ(tikaṃ)vinā
siddhavadabhidhānopapattiḥ । ataḥ samākhyātaḥ tathābhūto bhāga ityavagamyate ।
tathābhūtabhāgasambandhaśca karmakarasyopakāraviśeṣaṃ vinā na bhavatītyupakāraviśeṣo'pi
kalpyate । tadāha---<q>atassamākhyāta upakāravibhāgavat dakṣiṇāvibhāgaḥ ।</q>
kathaṃ punarupakāraviśeṣo'vagamyate karmaviśeṣamantareṇetyāśaṅkyāha---<q>sarvaṃ śabdāvagamyaṃ
codanāsviti sthitam</q> । yadyalpamapi karma kurvāṇo mahāntamupakāraṃ karotīti
śabdāt pratīyate kaḥśaknotyanyathākartumiti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 14 ।। tasya dhenuriti gavāṃ prakṛtau vibhaktacoditatvāt
sāmānyāttadvikāraḥ syāt yatheṣṭirguṇaśabdena ।। 56 ।।</l></lg>
﻿<pb n="377"/>
<p>nanu tasya dhenurdakṣiṇeti śrūyate । tataśca sarveṣāṃ gavādīnāṃ dhenvā nivṛttiryuktā ।
kathamatra saṃśayaḥ? kiṃ dhenurgavāṃ nivartikā uta kṛts‍nakratudākṣiṇyasyeti । atrāha---
<q>atra vibhāgāvibhāganibandhanaḥ saṃśayaḥ</q> । yadi vibhaktā dakṣiṇā tadā goranyāpi
dakṣiṇā1 dhenurgavāṃ nivartikā । atha tvavibhaktā tataḥ sarveṣāṃ nivartiketi । <q>vibhāgā-
vibhāgasaṃśayaḥ punaḥ kathaṃ</q> ? uttaraṃ---<q>viśeṣānavagamāt</q> । ubhayathā ca vākyārthopa-
patteḥ yadi gavādayaḥ ānataya ityucyante tathāpi vākyārtha upapadyate, pratyekaṃ dakṣiṇā-
tvepyupapadyata ityarthaḥ । athānatirgavādaya ityucyate tathāpyupapadyate vākyārthaḥ yadi
samastaṃ dākṣiṇyaṃ tathāpyupapadyata ityarthaḥ । yasmādubhayathāpi vākyārthopapattiḥ tasmādvaraṃ
gavādaya ānataya ityuktam । evaṃ codakānugraho bhaviṣyati dravyāntarāṇāmabādhāt ।
svatantranirdeśaśca samarthito bhaviṣyati । gauścāśvaśceti ।</p>
<p><q>nanu śabdānna svatantrāvagatiḥ । apitu samuccīyamānānāmavagatiḥ ।</q>
pariharati---<q>nāsvatantrāvagatiḥ ।</q> avagamyamānanirdeśārthatvāccakārasya yo'rthaḥ
pramāṇāntareṇa prāptaḥ tameva nipātā vadantītyarthaḥ । tadāha---<q>satyanvaye
yo'rtho'vagamyate tasyāyaṃ pratinirdeśakaḥ 2na punaranvayabhājamarthamācaṣṭe ।</q> 
caśabdābhihito nārthāntareṇānvayaṃ bhajate samuccayaśabdavaditi vaidharmyadṛṣṭāntaḥ । darśitaṃ
caitat । na cātra samāsaḥ yenetaretarayuktāḥ samāhṛtāśca dakṣiṇayā sambadhyante ।
tasmādvibhak‍taṃ dākṣiṇyamiti siddham । ataśca gavāṃ nivartikā dhenuḥ ।</p>
<p>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---<q>ekaṃ dākṣiṇyaṃ, kutaḥ ? ekavacananirdeśāt
