dakṣiṇeti । yadi gavādīnāṃ prādhānyena nirdeśaḥ tadā dakṣiṇāḥ iti
bahuvacanaṃ syāt । guṇavacanānāṃ āśrayato liṅgavacananirdeśāt । yathā
ag‍nīṣomau devateti ।</q> asyārthaḥ---yadi pratyekaṃ dakṣiṇā syāt tadā gavādīnāṃ
dakṣiṇātvaṃ jñāpanīyam । tataśca gavādayaḥ pradhānaṃ pradhānasaṅkhyānurodhena guṇeṣu
saṅkhyāniveśa iti bahuvacanaṃ syāddakṣiṇā iti । yathā ag‍nīṣomau devate । āg‍neye
saumye ca karmaṇi ag‍nīṣomīyacodanārthābhiprāyeṇedamucyate iti matvā codayati---</p>
<note>1. R. gomātrasyāpi dakṣiṇātvāt</note>
<note>2. R. kaḥ punaḥ</note>
﻿<pb n="378"/>
<p><q>nanu cāg‍nīṣomau devatā kimidamucyate devate iti</q> । pariharati---
<q>prādhānyanirdeśapradarśanaparamida bhāṣyakārasya na punarag‍nīṣomīyacodanārthaparam</q> ।
tatrāg‍neḥ somasya ca devatātvaṃ guṇabhūtaṃ nirdiśyate tatpradarśanaparamidaṃ bhāṣyakārasya
vacanaṃ na punarag‍nīṣomīyaṃ paśumityādicodanāsiddho yo'rthaḥ tatparamidamucyate ।
kathamidamavagamyate prādhānyanirdeśapradarśanaparamiti ag‍niradevateti codanārthapare
darśanāt । manotādhikaraṇe'g‍nīṣomīyacodanārthaṃ pradarśayannagneradevatātvamāha bhāṣyakāraḥ ।
tenāgnīṣomīyacodanāsiddhamidaṃ nocyate । anyathāhi tena saha virodhaḥ syāt ।
caśabdabalena samuccitaṃ dakṣiṇetyuktamiti manvānaścodayati---<q>nanu na caśabdo'-
nvayabhājaṃ nirdiśati</q> । pariharati---<q>kenoktaṃ nirdiśatīti । atrāpya-
nyato'nvitasyaiva1 nirdeśakaḥ</q> ekavacanāntadakṣiṇāśabdena yo'vagataḥ sa eva
caśabdena dyotyate ।</p>
<p><q>nanvevaṃ sati itaretarayogaḥ samāhāro vā prāp‍noti</q> । yadi paraspara-
sāpekṣatvaṃ dākṣiṇye tadā itaretarayogaḥ samāhāro vā prāp‍noti । uttaraṃ---<q>prāp‍notu
ko doṣaḥ</q> । doṣaṃ darśayati---<q>samāsena bhavitavyam</q> । pariharati---<q>na bhavitavyaṃ
samāsena vāvacanādbhagavataḥ pāṇineḥ</q> । evaṃ caikaṃ dākṣiṇyaṃ dṛṣṭaprayojanaṃ bhavati
itarathā bahūnāṃ madhye ekenaiva dṛṣṭārthasya siddhatvāt anyeṣāṃ dākṣiṇyānāṃ adṛṣṭārtha-
kalpanā ।</p>
<p><q>nanu vikalpo bhaviṣyati । ucyate । upadeśābhiprāyeṇedamucyate</q> ।
ekasmin‍nupadiṣṭe paropadeśo'dṛṣṭārthaḥ anapekṣitavidhiḥ syādityarthaḥ । eṣa doṣaḥ
parihṛto bhaviṣyati ekasmin dākṣiṇye । ataścaikaṃ dākṣiṇyaṃ kṛts‍nasya ca dhenurnivarti-
keti siddham ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 15 ।। ekāṃ pañ‍ceti dhenuvat ।। 59 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>nanu ca goṣveva saṅkhyāmātravidhiryuktaḥ ataḥ kathaṃ kṛts‍nakratu-
dākṣiṇyasya nivṛttyāśaṅkā</q> ? yadi ca dākṣiṇye gomātravidhiḥ saṅghyāvidhiśca
tadā vākyabhedaḥ tatrāha---<q>atra viśiṣṭāvidhānāt pūrvapakṣaḥ</q> dakṣiṇaiva goviśiṣṭāṃ
<note>1. R. anvaṣāvagatasyaiva</note>
﻿<pb n="379"/>
saṅkhyāviśiṣṭā ca vidhīyate । nanvevaṃ dakṣiṇāntare vihite kathaṃ prākṛtasya nivṛttiḥ
ityatrāha---<q>kṛtatvātprākṛtasya kāryasya dhenvā</q> । nanu te lakṣaṇā syāt kratu-
dākṣiṇyasya prākṛtasya nivṛttiḥ ।</p>
<p>atra bhāṣyakāraḥ <q>trivatsaśca tathā ca liṅgadarśanam</q> iti sūtradvayaṃ antarā-
garbhiṇyāśrayaṇena vyākhyāya punaśca tatparityajya pūrvapakṣe liṅgadarśanaparatvena varṇitavān ।
tadāha---<q>antarāgarbhiṇīnyāyamupanyasya tasyānucitatvāt tatparihārāya
liṅgatvena sūtradvayamupavarṇitavān</q> । tataśca saṅkhyāmātravidhānena rāddhāntamabhidhāya
goṣu saṅkhyāmātraṃ vidhīyata ityevaṃ rāddhāntamabhidhāya na liṅgavaiṣamyamupavarṇitam
yatpūrvapakṣe sūtradvayena liṅgamuktam tena saha vaiṣamyaṃ noktam । tatrāyamabhiprāyaḥ---
antarāgarbhiṇyaiva vaiṣamyamuktaṃ yā sā pūrvamantarāgarbhiṇyuktā tayaiva liṅgavaiṣamyamuk‍taṃ
yuk‍tam । sāṇḍasya krayadravyamātranivartakatvaṃ krīṇātisambandhena vidhānāt tasya । iha
tu na dakṣiṇāsambandhena gavāṃ vidhānam । kintu gosambandhitayā saṅkhyāmātravidhānamiti ।
nanu tyaktā'ntarāgabhiṇī । kathaṃ tayā vaiṣamyamuktaṃ ityatrāha---<q>iha tvantarāgarbhiṇītvaṃ
nirākriyate na punaryuktyabhidhānam</q> । antarānupraveśo nāstītyuktam ।
nyāyastu śobhana eva । tena bhavati vaiṣamyamityuktam ।</p>
<p><q>nanu tatrāpi trivatse'pi vayomātravidhānāt ekāṃ pañ‍cetyanena
tulyam</q> । yathā goṣu saṅkhyāmātravidhiḥ tathā'tra ṛṣabhe trivatsavidhiḥ । pariharati-
<q>na tulyam viśiṣṭavayovacanatvāt</q> । na ca dravyaṃ dravyāntare vidhātuṃ śakyate ।
dravye tu saṅkhyāmātravidhānaṃ sukaram । tasmādvaiṣamyam । kevalaṃ tu vayomātravidhāne'ṅgī-
kriyamāṇe'śabdārthataivābhyupagatā bhavati ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 17 ।। prākāśau tatheti cet ।। 63 ।।</l></lg>
<p>nanu hiraṇmayau prākāśāvadhvaryave dadāti ityadhvaryusambandhe'vagamyamāne kathaṃ
kṛts‍nasya kratudākṣiṇyasya nivṛttyāśaṅkā yāvatā tadbhāgavikāra evetyāśaṅkyāha---<q>atra
viśiṣṭānuvādabhayātpūrvapakṣaḥ</q> । yadyadhvaryuviśiṣṭadānānuvādena prākāśavidhiḥ syāt
tadā viśiṣṭānuvādalakṣaṇo vākyabhedaḥ syāt । tasmādadhvaryuśabdo na viśeṣakaḥ ।
tena dānamātre prākāśavidhiḥ ṛtviṅ‌mātrapradarśanārthaścādhvaryuśabdo yaugikaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="380"/>
<p>nanu cādhvaryuprākāśasambandha eva vidhīyatāmityātrāha---<q>ānantaryaṃ ca
vibhak‍tyoḥ sambandhāyogyatvena nādṛtam</q> । yadyapyānantaryamanayoḥ tathāpi
dvitīyācaturthyoḥ parasparasambandhāyogyatvānnādhvaryuparityāgena prākāśayossambandhaḥ ।
tataścakathaṃ tasya vidhiḥ । tasmāddānamātrasambandhitvena vidhānāt kṛts‍nasya
nivartakau prākāśāviti ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu---pratīyate tāvadvibhāgo dakṣiṇānāṃ na cātra dadātiḥ
padāntaraparityāgenādhvaryuparityāgena prākāśapadena sambadhyata iti pratīti-
rasti</q> । na cādhvaryuḥ prākāśapadena na sambadhyate । bhavati hi kārakayorapi kriyā-
nimittakaḥ sambandhaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>nanu vibhaktyartho vihanyate prathamāṣaṣṭhyau hi tadā syātām । na
dvitīyācaturthyāvityuk‍tam</q> ।</p>
<p>pariharati---<q>na vihanyate'thaprāptatvādvibhaktyarthasya prākāśāvadhbaryu-
sambandhinau kartavyāviti</q> vihite'rthe dvitīyācaturthyorarthaprāptiḥ । yadi hi tau
tasmai dadyāt tau tatsambandhinau kuryāt । tasmādārtho vibhaktyartho vibhaktibhyāmanūdyate ।</p>
<p>kathaṃ punaradhvaryuprākāśayoḥ sambandha ityatrāha---<q>ānantaryasya sambandhahetu-
tvāt</q> । tadidamuktaṃ asatyānantarye sambandho nopapadyata iti । pratyuta caturthīkriyā-
viśeṣasya liṅgaṃ bhaviṣyati । sā kriyā sambandhaheturāśrīyate yasyāṃ satyāṃ caturthyartho
labhyata iti dānameva kriyā kalpyate । eṣā kalpanā'dhvaryuśabdabalenāśritā ।
anyathā'vivakṣitārtho'dhvaryuśabdaḥ syāt । rūḍhiṃ ca parityajya yaugikāśrayaṇe
prakārāntaraṃ cā''ha---<q>viśiṣṭavidhānaṃ vā'bhyupagamyatām</q> । dānamevādhvaryu-
prākāśaviśiṣṭaṃ vidhīyate । na punarbhāgāvagatiḥ śakyate'panhotum tasmādadhvaryubhāgasya
pratyām‍nāyo dānam । tasyāpi dṛṣṭārthatvena tatkāryakaraṇatvāditi sūktam ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 18 ।। dhenuvaccāśvadakṣiṇā sa brahmaṇa iti puruṣāpanayo
yathā hiraṇyasya ।। 65 ।।</l></lg>
﻿<pb n="381"/>
<p><q>kathaṃ punaratra brahmabhāgasya nivartako'śva ityetasmin pūrvapakṣe rukma-
lalāṭo dakṣiṇeti vākyam</q> । asmin vākye sāmānyena dakṣiṇāsambandhaḥ prati-
bhāti । ataḥ kṛts‍nasya kratudākṣiṇyasya nivṛttireva yuktā । uttaraṃ---<q>viśeṣa-
sambandhe'pi sāmānyaṃ na viruddha‍yata ityabhiprāyaḥ</q> । ṛtvigviśeṣadakṣiṇātvepi
dakṣiṇāśabdasya sāmānyavācino na virodhaḥ । ato na kṛts‍nasya kratudākṣiṇyasya
prāptasya nivartako'śvaḥ darśanalobhāt bhramaḥ yathā srajamudgātre dadātītyudgātṛbhāgasya
nivartikā tathā kṛts‍nasya nivartiketi dṛṣṭāntalobhāt bhramo'yaṃ pūrvapakṣiṇaḥ ।
dṛśyate'sminniti darśanam ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu satyaṃ sāmānyasya viśeṣeṇāvirodhaḥ ekavākyatve hetuḥ
saḥ yathā śābaleyo gauriti</q> । vākyabhede punaḥ yathāpratipannameva grahītavyam ।
ekavākyatvepi viśeṣānvitameva sāmānyamabhidhīyate । vākyabhede tu svatantrārthadva‍yā-
vagatiḥ tena prathamavākye'śvasya sāmānyena dakṣiṇātvam । ataḥ kṛts‍nasya kratu-
dākṣiṇyasya nivṛttiḥ । dvitīye tu vākye tasyaiva brahmasambandha iti । yadyaśva eva
kṛts‍nakratudakṣiṇā vrahmaṇa eva deyaḥ । tadā kathaṃ dakṣiṇāmantareṇa ṛtvigantarāṇāṃ
pravartanam tadāha---<q>kathaṃ punarasmin pakṣe kartrantaraṃ pravartanīyam ?</q> uttaraṃ---
<q>nātra ārthasya bādhaḥ । arthādyena kenacitteṣāmānatiḥ vācanikaścāyaṃ pratyā-
m‍nāyaścintyate</q> । vacanādapratihatasvārtho'bhyupāyaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>nanu cārthasyaivāyaṃ niyamaḥ</q> । aptyārthaḥ- parakartṛkaṃ karma dakṣiṇāmantareṇa
na śakyate kartumiti arthādyā dakṣiṇā prāptā tatraivāyaṃ niyama iti । <q>kathamapara
ārtho'bhyupāyaḥ</q> । pariharati---<q>nāyaṃ niyamaḥ । kutaḥ ? varaṇabharaṇanimittatvā-
tparakartṛkāvagateḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---na sākṣātparakartukatvaṃ śrutau śrūyate yena sāmānye-
nānamane1 adoniyamo bhavet । kintu varaṇabharaṇavidhānādeva parakartṛkatāvagamaḥ
tenāyaṃ niyamo bhavatīti varaṇabharaṇavidhānāt prāk sāmānyenāprāpteriti sūktamuktam ।
ataḥ kartrantarāpanaye sarvatra nyāyo draṣṭavyaḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 19 ।। tathā somacamasaḥ ।। 68 ।।</l></lg>
<p>kena viśeṣeṇātra pūrvapakṣa ityatrāha---<q>ekavākyatvenātra sāmānyaṃ viśeṣa-
gataṃ manvānasya pūrvapakṣaḥ</q> । evaṃ hi śrūyate---audumbaraḥ somacamaso dakṣiṇā
﻿<pb n="382"/>
sa priyāya sagotrāya brahmaṇe deyaḥ iti । ekavākyatvāt sāmānyaṃ viśeṣaniṣṭhameva,
tena na kṛts‍nanivṛttiḥ evaṃ prāptasya bādho'nyasya na kalpito bhavati ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu-dakṣiṇāśabdaśravaṇāt deyaṃ sampradānaṃ ca kṛts‍nasambandhi-
tayā'vagamyate</q> । uktaṃ hi avibhaktaṃ dākṣiṇyamiti । yena dakṣiṇāśabda-
śravaṇāt dakṣiṇākārya eva somacamasasyāpi vidhānamavagamyate । tena na dakṣiṇāśabdo
viśeṣe'vasthāpayituṃ śakyate । dvayasya deyasya pradānātmakasya tatsambandhitvenāpi
sāmānyadakṣiṇāsambandhitvenāpyupapatterna lakṣaṇāpramāṇasti । dakṣiṇāśabdena dakṣiṇā-
bhāgalakṣaṇātve pramāṇaṃ nāstīti yuktamuktaṃ kṛts‍nasya nivṛttiriti ।</p>
<p>nanvevaṃ paurastyamadhikaraṇaṃ dūrotsāritam । naivam । iha dakṣiṇāśabdaśravaṇā-
drāddhāntaḥ । pūrvasminnadhikaraṇe tu dakṣiṇāśabdaśravaṇepi vākyabhede kṛts‍nasya nivṛtti-
riti draṣṭavyam ।</p>
<p><q>।। evaṃ vā ।।</q></p>
<q><q>prayojanatvena <quote>“yadi tu brahmaṇa”</quote> iti pūrvatra dvayamupavarṇya evaṃ veti
vadataḥ ko'bhiprāyaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ-nirākaraṇīyābhāvāt pṛthagadhikaraṇāntaraṃ nārabdha
vyam । uttaraṃ---<q>kāryopadeśaṃ varṇayitvā bādho'pi sayuktika eva vaktavya iti
manyate</q> । asyārthaḥ- astyatra nirākaraṇīyaṃ pūrvapakṣī manyate । yadi kṛts‍naṃ dakṣiṇā-
kāryaṃ somacamasena kriyate tadā bhavet kṛts‍nanivṛttiḥ । nacaitadasti somacamasena brahmaṇe
dīyamānena na ṛtvigantaravartinyānatiḥ dakṣiṇākāryaṃ sampadyate tasmānna tena kṛts‍nani-
vṛttirityasyāmākāṅkṣāyāṃ kṛts‍nadakṣiṇākārye somacamasasyopadeśaṃ varṇayitvā bādho'pi
sayuktika eva vaktavyaḥ । ata idamadhikaraṇamārabdham ।</p>
<p>kathaṃ punaḥ kṛts‍nakārye vidhānam । ucyate । dvividhaṃ hi kāryam । ekaṃ
kratau, aparaṃ tadaṅgeṣu । tatra kratau kāryaṃ kevalāgamādavagamyate । tatra yadyapi
somacamasena kratvantarbhūtapuruṣagataṃ kāryaṃ na kriyate tathāpi kratvaṅge kriyata iti āgama-
prāmāṇyādavagamyate । tadarthaṃ cāṅgataṃ kāryam । tena pradhānakārye somacamasena
siddhe dakṣiṇāntaranivṛttiḥ । yadyatra dakṣiṇākāryasampādakatvābhāvāśaṅkyā pūrvapakṣaḥ <q>kathaṃ
tarhi bhāṣyakāra evamāha---<quote>“somacamaso brahmaṇa ityeṣa sambandha iti
﻿<pb n="383"/>
kṛtvā cintā”</quote> iti</q> । evaṃ hi vadan kṛtvācinteti darśayati । na ceyaṃ kṛtvā
cintā । krintu pūrvapakṣabalenaivāyaṃ sambandha iti ।</p>
<p>uttaraṃ---<q>evaṃ kṛtvā pūrvapakṣo'tra varṇyata iti varṇanīyamidaṃ bhāṣyam</q> ।
nyāyabalenaiva somacamaso brahmaṇa iti kṛtvā pūrvapakṣa ityartho bhāṣyasya ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 21 ।। yajuryuk‍te tvadhvaryoḥ dakṣiṇāvikāraḥ syāt ।। 74 ।।</l></lg>
<p>ihādhikaraṇe saptasaptadaśakāni deyāni śrutāni । tathā yajuryuk‍taṃ rathaṃ
adhvaryave dadātīti । ataśca bhāganiyamo'yaṃ bhavati । atha tu svatantraṃ tato bhāga-
vikāra iti । tatra pūrvapakṣī svātantryaṃ manyate । na hi svātantryye sati pāratantryaṃ
yuktamiti bhāgo'dhvaryoḥ tasyāyaṃ vikāraḥ । punardakṣiṇāvikārapakṣe[rathā]dīnāṃ dakṣiṇā-
sambandhaṃ manyate kasmai tāni deyānauti bhāvaḥ ।</p>
<p>uttaraṃ---<q>dīyate tebhyo'dhvaryvādibhyo ye'nye tebhyaḥ tadyugyādika-
miti śakyate vak‍tum</q> । evaṃ pūrvapakṣite ucyate---</p>
<p>nāyaṃ bhāgavikāraśśakyate vak‍tum । aprāptasya viśeṣāvagatau bhāgavikāro
yuktaḥ । yadi rathadāne'dhvaryuḥ prāptaḥ tadā rathaviśeṣavidhānaṃ bhāgavikārāya syāt ।
iha tu prāptānāmadhvaryvādīnāṃ niyamamātreṇaivopadeśasiddheḥ na bhāgāntarānuvṛttiśśakyate
vak‍tuṃ codakānugrahāya । saptadaśarathā ityetadvākyapūrvakamidamiti rāddhāntaḥ
tāvanmātreṇaivopadeśopapatteḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu yadi sāmānyena prāptau satyāṃ viśeṣaśravaṇaṃ niyamamātraphalaṃ, na bhāga-
vikāraḥ tarhi prākāśāvapi niyamārthāveva syātām । aśvamedhepi sāmānyena prākāśa-
vidhirasti hiraṇmayāvadhyaryorniyamyete iti tatrāha---<q>ye punaraśvamedhepyasya prāptiṃ
manyante na te yuk‍tamiva manyante</q> । kutaḥ ? <q>nyāyābhidhānamātravivakṣāyāṃ
hi tadanuguṇamudāharaṇaṃ pradarśyate</q> । tena santamapi sāmānyaṃ prākāśe ekakāryā-
vagamāt । pariharati---<q>udāharaṇamātraṃ tvetaditi nādartavyam</q> adṛṣṭārthamanyārtha-
mapi adṛṣṭārthamapi kṛtvodā [haraṇam] vidhimasantamiva kṛtvodāharaṇaṃ syānna punaḥ
lakṣyanirṇayāyodāharaṇadānam । sāmānyanyāyābhidhitsayedaṃ śāstraṃm । evaṃ sati
﻿<pb n="384"/>
ayaṃ nyāyo bhavatīti yatra sāmānyavacanaṃ nāsti tatra bhāgavikāra iti nyāyaḥ kathyate
na punaḥ granthaviśeṣābhidhitsayā na vākyaviśeṣasyārthaḥ kathyata ityarthaḥ । anyathā hi
paurvāmaryeṇānusaraṇaṃ syāt । yadi hi vedavākyavyākhyārthamidaṃ syāt tadā tathākramaṃ
vedavākyāni vyākhyeyāni nyāyaparatve tu nāyaṃ doṣaḥ । tasmān‍nyāyaniṣṭhaṃ vyākhyāna-
miti na doṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>iti ṛjuvimalāyāṃ pañcikāyāṃ
daśamasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।</p>
﻿<pb n="385"/>
<p><q>ṛjuvimalāyāṃ</q></p>
<p><q>।। daśamādhyāyasya caturthaḥ pādaḥ ।।</q></p>
<lg><l>।। 1 ।। prakṛtiliṅgāsaṃyogāt karmasaṃskāraṃ vikṛtāvadhikaṃ syāt ।। 1 ।।</l></lg>
<p>kathaṃ punaruparhomādibhiḥ nāriṣṭhahomādīnāṃ nivṛttirityatrāha---<q>abhidhāna-
sāmānyena tulyārthatāṃ manvānasya pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ - yathaiṣāmabhidhānaṃ
tulyaṃ tathā kāryamapi bhavitumarhati । abhidhānaikye ca kāryabhedānupapattiḥ ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu vidheyatvādabhidheyānāṃ kāryaikyānavagamācca</q> । asyārthaḥ-
yadyapyabhidhānamekaṃ tathāpi abhidheyānāṃ vidheyatvenānyatvameva । anyatvepi ca
yadi kāryamekaṃ, syāt nivṛttiḥ । na ca kāryaikyamavagamyate । yathā ca kāryaikyaṃ
nāvagamyate tathā darśitamadṛṣṭārthānāmekakāryatvānavagamāditi । nanu ca nivīte vāso-
vinyāsasya dṛṣṭārthatvāt vinyāsāntaropamardena ca vinyāsāntarasya ātmalābhādbādha eva
yuktaḥ । tasmādadoṣaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ vā</q></p>
<p><q>upavarṇanāparihārāt kimabhyadhikamāśaṅkanīyaṃ yannirasyate ?</q> uttaraṃ---
<q>siddhe prakṛtiliṅgatve bhavatūpabarṇaṃnāparihāraḥ iha tu prakṛtiliṅgatvaṃ barhirityasya
sādhyata iti</q> । viśeṣāntaraṃ vyaktameva barhiṣaḥ prakṛtiliṅgatvam । <q>kiṃ paraṃ sādhyate ?</q>
atastatrāśaṅkā । <q>kā punarasau ? iyam</q> । barhiḥ śabdena kuśo'bhidhīyate । tasya
śaramayatā vidhīyate । na punaḥ staraṇe śaravidhirayam । tatra kuśānāṃ śaramayatā
bahutaraśarayogena bhavati <quote>“śālimayā māgadhā janapadā”</quote> iti yathā ।</p>
<p><q>kathaṃ punaridaṃ nirākriyate ?</q> ittham । <q>klṛptakāryāvivakṣayā vaikṛtā
vidhayaḥ । tatra yadi varhiḥ kārye śarāṇāṃ vidhiḥ syāt tadā kāryāntara-
kalpanā nāsti । itasthā tu kāryāntaraṃ prakalpyaṃ syāt</q> । tena barhiḥ śabdaḥ
kāryasamarpaṇārtha eva । śaramayamiti ca mayaṭpratyayo nityaṃ vṛddhaśarādibhya iti
vikāre । yadyapi staraṇaṃ na vikāraḥ tathāpi śarakāryatayā tadvikāra ityupacaryate ।</p>
﻿<pb n="386"/>
<p><q>evaṃ vā</q></p>
<p><q>tatra rathaghoṣeṇeti kiṃ vākyārtho nivartekaḥ uta pratyekaṃ padārtha iti
cintyate</q> । ākṣipati---<q>kimidaṃ pralapyate ?</q> ekagranthenāha---<q>nanu cobhaya-
trāpi vākyārtha eva nivartakaḥ</q> rathaghoṣaśceti pūrvapakṣe'pi vākyārtha eva nivartakaḥ ।
sa tu māhendrastotropākaraṇasambandhī nivartakaḥ tathā rāddhānte'pi rathasambandhī śabdo
vākyārtha eva san mantradarbhanivartaka iti pratigkṣatvābhāvāt saṃśayo'yaṃ pralāpabhūtaḥ
samādhatte---<q>satyamevaṃ śrutābhiprāyeṇedamucyate vākyārthaḥ padārtha iti</q> । ratha-
sambandhī ghoṣo rathaghoṣaśabdābhyāmucyata iti vākyārtha ityucyate । rathastu rathaśabdena
ghoṣaśca ghoṣaśabdenocyata iti padārtha ityucyate । na punarmāhendrastotropākaraṇasambandhā-
bhiprāyeṇa padārthatvaṃ vākyārthatva vā'bhimatam । etameva vivṛṇoti---<q>kiṃ pratipadaṃ
vākyasamāptiruta samudāya iti</q> । ratho'pi stotropākaraṇasambandhī ghoṣo'pīti
pratipadaṃ vākyāsamāptiḥ । yadi rathasambandhī gho/?/ṣaḥ stotropākaraṇasambandhī tadā samudāye
vākyaparisamāptiriti ।</p>
<p><q>kiṃ tāvatprāptam ? pratipadaṃ vākyaparisamāptiḥ</q> dvandvasamāso'yam; tena
pratipadaṃ vākyaparisamāptiḥ । kā yuktirityata āha---<q>evaṃ svārthaparatā dvayorapi
padārthayoḥ</q> । ṣaṣṭhītatpuruṣe tu pūrvapadārtho viśeṣaṇatayā parārthaḥ । svārthatvaṃ parārtha-
tvādyuktam । <q>nanu caivaṃ sati dvivacanena bhavitavyam, rathaghoṣayordvitvāt । na
bhavitavyaṃ dvivacanena dvivacanābhāvāt</q> । vede hi pratipattāro vayaṃ na kartāraḥ । tena
dvivacanopadarśane dvitve'pi dvivacanamatra nāstītyavagamyate । dvivacanābhāve kathaṃ tarhi
dvandvāvagatirityatrāha---<q>etasmādeva kāryāt dvandvāvagamaḥ</q> । yadidaṃ padānāṃ kāryaṃ
svārthasya kāryatvāpādanaṃ etasmādeva dvandvāvagatiḥ ekavadbhavaṃ vā manyate । tena dvivaca-
nānutpattirna doṣaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>evaṃ prāpte'bhidhīyate---tatpuruṣo'yaṃ na dvandvanirdeśaḥ । kutaḥ ?</q> uttaraṃ
-<q>ekavacananirddeśāt । nanu caitasma devakāryā dvandvāvagatirityuktaḥ parihāraḥ ।
nāyaṃ parihāraḥ ।</q> yadi tasmād‌dvandvā/?/vagatiḥ na tarhi dvandva rthasya vidhānaṃ dvandvatve
pramāṇābhāvāt kāryaṃ cetpramāṇaṃ itaretarāśrayam । dvandve'vagate kāryāvagamaḥ kāryāvaga-
mācca dvandvāvagatiriti tatpuruṣāvagatistu abhidhānādeva ekavacanānu(gyā)jñā nyāyyā ।
﻿<pb n="387"/>
<p><q>yatpunarekavadbhāvādapyupapadyata ityuktaṃ siddhaṃ tarhi samudāyavidhānaṃ
vākyārthavidhānaṃ siddham</q> । bhavatvevamityatrāha---<q>iyāṃstu viśeṣaḥ dvandve dvayorapi
padārthayoḥ samāhāraparatvāt guṇabhāvo'bhyupagato bhavati</q> । tatpuruṣe punaḥ
ekasyāpi tāvat prādhānyamiti nyāyyaṃ tadāśrayaṇam । <q>prayojanamuktam</q> । yadi dvandvo
bhavettadā niśśabdo'pi ratho nivartako bhavet anyasambandhyapi ghoṣaḥ । tatpuruṣe tu
rathasambaddhasya nivartakatvamiti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 2 ।। sarvatra tu grahāmnānamadhikaṃ syāt prakṛtivat ।। 3 ।।</l></lg>
<p>atra kecidevaṃ cintayanti vikṛtiṣu graheṣu guṇavidhānāt kiṃ guṇāntaranivṛttiḥ
neti । tadāśrayaṇena codayati---<q>nanu ca yuktaṃ bārhampatyaṃ gṛhṇātītyudāharaṇam</q> ।
atra grahānuvādena bṛhaspatividhirāśaṅkituṃ śakyate tenedamudāharaṇaṃ yuktam । <q>ye punaḥ
nāmaviśiṣṭā grahā udāhṛtāḥ arkaṃ gṛhṇātītyevamādayaḥ teṣāṃ saṃjñā cotpatti-
saṃyogāditi karmāntaratvasiddheḥ nodāharaṇatvamupapadyate । kāryāntarāvagamāt
samuccayasyaiva tatra yuktatvāt</q> ।</p>
<p>paramasiddhāntī vadati---<q>satyamāha bhagavān yadyava guṇanivṛttiścintyate
kiṃ guṇāntaravidhānena prākṛtaguṇanivṛttiruta neti yadyatra cintyate tadā
syādeva pūrvoktadoṣaḥ</q> । iha tu grahā eva nivartyā uta neti cintyate । vaikṛtagrahāntara-
vidhānāt kiṃ prākṛtagrahā nivartante neti cintye । tataśca tatrāpi saṃjñāntarayukta-
grahāntaravidheḥ so'pyudāharaṇam । <q>yadyevaṃ yadi grahāntareṇa grahanivṛttireva
cintyate tarhi guṇavidhipradarśanaṃ kimarthaṃ ?</q> āgneyā grahā iti pūrvapakṣasiddhānta-
yorasadbha‍ūtatvāt ।</p>
<p>uttaraṃ---<q>bādhaprakāradarśanārthaṃ tat svārtham</q> । siddhānte hi samuccayaṃ
varṇayitvā bhāṣyakāreṇa bādhaprakāro darśitaḥ । yadi grahaśabdamuccārya guṇo vidhīyate
tataḥ prākṛtā eva grahāḥ guṇavikṛtā bhaveyuḥ । guṇamātraṃ tadā bādhyeta । atha
grahasambandhenāgrahā vidhīyante tato'graho grahakāryeṃ vartata iti prākṛto nivartate । tatra
yo'yaṃ bādhaprakāraḥ pradarśitaḥ tatsiddha‍yarthaṃma gneyā grahā ityuktam । yāvat guṇamātra-
vidhiratra na sādhyate tāvadidaṃ bādhaprakāradarśanaṃ na ghaṭata iti guṇamātraviviṃ sādhayitvā
āgneyā iti guṇavikṛtipradarśanaṃ kṛtam, na punaḥ pūrvapakṣadṛṣṭāntatvena । <q>yadyatra guṇa-
﻿<pb n="388"/>
nivṛttireva na cintyate kimarthaṃ punaḥ bārhaspatyapunarupanyāsaḥ ? kimiti
uttara vidhātavyam nātrāsyābhidheyaikyamasti</q> । asyābhidheyena saha ekatvaṃ
nāsti kalpanāvirodhastvatantramityuktam । tasmāt bārhaspatyaṃ gṛhṇātīti karmāntaravidhā-
namatra । yadyatra karmāntaravidhānaṃ <q>kathaṃ tarhi idaṃ <quote>“ekādaśa prayājān yajati”</quote>
iti guṇavidhānaṃ</q> ? uttaraṃ---<q>na saṅkhyā'nurañ‍jiketyuktaṃ dvitīye</q> । pṛthaktva-
niveśitvamātraṃ hi <q>vidheyasaṅkhyā prabhavati kartuṃ na punaḥ svānukāri karmāvaga-
mayati yathādravyam</q> । asyārthaḥ---saṅkhyāyāṃ śrutāyāṃ tāvatsaṅkhyākāni karmāṇya-
vagamyante na punasteṣāṃ saṅkhyāto rūpaviśeṣapratipattiḥ । yathā dravyaṃ svānuraktaṃ karmāva-
gamayati na tathā saṅkhyā, ananurañjakatvāt । tatra ca niyogavyāpāra eva vardhate eka
eva niyogo bahūni karmāṇi vidhatta iti । bhavatvevaṃ tathāpi kimitaravidhinetyatrāha---
<q>śaknotyatideśe'pi kalpanāṃ viṣayaviṣayiṇīṃ vārayitum ।</q> asyārthaḥ
---arūpatvātsaṅkhyāyāḥ arūpasya ca yajyarthasya vidhānānupapatteḥ rūpavān yāgo
viṣayabhūtaḥ kalpayitavya । tatra cātideśo'pi kalpanāṃ niroddha‍uṃ śaknotīti ।
yadyupadeśaprāpta eva viṣayo na viṣayāntaraṃ <q>kathaṃ tarhi saṅkhyā śās‍trāntaratve hetuḥ
ekādaśa prayājān yajatīti nedaṃ śāstrāntaraṃ syāt</q> । anuvādaśāstramevedaṃ
bhavatītyarthaḥ ।</p>
<p>pariharati---<q>kena coktaṃ saṅkhyā śāstrāntaratve heturbhavatīti</q> । bhavatye-
vetyarthaḥ । codayitā pṛcchati <q>kathaṃ viṣayādṛte saṅkhyā śās‍traṃ bhinatti</q> ।
samādhātā uttaramāha---viṣayābhyāsādatra saviṣayaḥ siddha‍yati । abhyāsaṃ vidadhadidaṃ
śāstrāntaraṃ bhavati । yathā---ekādaśa prayājāt kuryādityetāvanmātraṃ śrūyate । tatra
yathā'bhyāsaviṣayastathehāpi । yataḥ evamādiṣvabhyāsavidhānaṃ <q>ata eva bhagavataḥ
pāṇineḥ kṛtvasuj vidhānaṃ yathārthamupapannaṃ bhavati anyathā hi pratikṣaṇama-
pavargavataḥ karmaṇā'bhyāsa eva nāsti kriyābhyāsāvṛttyasambhavāt ayathārthaṃ
pāṇinervacamaṃ syāt---<quote>“saṅkhyāḥ kriyābhyāvṛttigaṇane kṛtvasuc”</quote> iti tathā
stome ḍavidha namapyevamepo/?/papadyate saptadaśānyājyānītyāvṛttividhānāt stomāvṛttau iti
vārtikamupapadyate ।</p>
<p>eva svamataṃ nibandhanakāro darśayitvā paramatamāha-<q>atra punaḥ kecit ekā-
daśa prayājāniti parihārāntara bruvate- nāmayogāt prakṛteṣu saṅkhyāvidhānam</q> ।
﻿<pb n="389"/>
anyathāhi nām‍no'nekārthakalpanā syāt । iha punarnāmāntaraṃ grahaśabde nāstīti dhātvartha-
vidhānameva । yataśca grahaśabdābhāvāt karmavidhitayā āgneyā grahā bhavantīti । yatra graha-
śabdāḥ śrūyate tatra guṇavikārassiddho bhavatīti । śaknoti hi vidheyāvagatikalpanāṃ
atideśo vārayitumiti vadantaḥ ।</p>
<p>kecid‌bruvanta iti pūrveṇa sambandhaḥ । pariharati---<q>tadayuktamiti bhāṣya-
vidaḥ</q> prabhākaramiśrāḥ । ihāpi bārhaspatye grahaśabdaśravaṇāt nāmayogāt guṇavidhiḥ
syāt । kiñca dadhigrahe grahaśabdaśravaṇādabhidheyanirodhaḥ syāt । tataśca grahaṇe
kratvaṅgasaṃskārarūpe dadhiśravaṇāt kratāveva dravyāntaravidhāne dadhnā somasya vikāraḥ syāt
pūtīkairivābhiṣave śrutairdravyāntarasya pratinidheyasya vikāraḥ ।</p>
<p><q>nanu somābhāve tena vikāraḥ tena nāsti tulyatā dṛṣṭāntadārṣṭānti-
kayoḥ</q> । pariharati---<q>nātraitadvivakṣitavyam etadabhāve sati vikāra iti na</q>
vivakṣitavyam । kintu dravyavidhānaṃ prāpnotīti । tataśca dravyāntaraṃ vikriyate ।
codakādvā prāptamupādānato vā । sambhavāditi ko viśeṣo vikārāvagatau । tasmāt sahaiva
grahaśabdena pūrvoktaḥ parihāraḥ । yadi vikṛtau karmāntaravidhiḥ <q>kastarhi puroḍāśa-
devatayoḥ havirantara ca sautrāmaṇyāṃ vidhīyate</q> । puroḍāśe'gnīṣomīye codaka-
prāpte devatāntarāṇāmindrādīnāṃ vidhānam devatāyāṃ cāgnīṣomayoḥ havirantarasya grahasya
vidhānaṃ sautrāmaṇyāmayuktam । tatra karmāntaravidhireva yuktaḥ । [uttaraṃ]---<q>yuktamuktaṃ
paśupuroḍāśādhikaraṇe kāryapratyabhijñānāt sa evāyaṃ yāga iti</q> । agneyā
grahā iti kathaṃ tarhi guṇavidhirityatrāha---<q>āgneyā grahā iti vidheyābhidhānamati-
deśo'pi śak‍noti nirod‍dhum</q> । vidheyābhidhānamatra śrūyate grahā ityabhidhānārthatvāt
tena bhāvārtho'tra kalpayitavyaḥ tatkalpanāmatideśo vārayituṃ śaknoti । <q>liṅgamuktam
viraṇyādarśanam</q> । nanu ca yaduktamādhastye'dhikaraṇe pṛthak homavidhānānna mantravidhiḥ ।
samantraśravaṇe tu mantravidhireveti । tadayuktam । samantrakaśravaṇepi karmāntaravidhireva
syāt yadyasau na nāriṣṭhahome guṇavidhirityāśaṅkyāha---<q>yuktamagnau yaduktaṃ bhāṣya-
kāreṇa yasmāt prakṛtireva hi sā । jyotiṣṭoma evāsau</q> । tenopadeśataḥ
sannihiteṣu homeṣu samantrakaśravaṇe mantramātravidhireva syāt yadyasau prakṛtiḥ । kathaṃ
tarhi codakaprāpto nāriṣṭhahoma ityucyate tatrāha---<q>naimittikaṃ tvabhyadhikam</q> ।
asyārthaḥ---naimittiko'yaṃ tasyaiva jyotiṣṭomasya guṇavikāraḥ । tena prakṛtirapi vikṛti-
﻿<pb n="390"/>
rityucyate । yathāgnihotrahomo dadhnondriyakāmasyeti dadhivikṛtau vikṛtirbhavatīti ।
tena na doṣaḥ । nanvevamapi grahāṇāṃ samuccayo na yuktaḥ kintu ekakāryatvādbādha ityā-
śaṅkyāha---<q>kāryaṃ punaḥ yāganirvṛttirgrahāṇāṃ na tāṃ grahacodanayaiveti vaiṣamyaṃ</q>
na grahā yāgoddeśena vidhīyante । kintu yāgārthadravyasambandhena teṣāṃ kratvanupraveśaḥ ।
tena grahāṇāṃ satāṃ yāganirvṛttiḥ kāryaṃ, na punaḥ grahacodanābhireva yāgasādhanatvena
vidhānam । ataśca samuccayasteṣāmiti darśitaṃ dvitīye iti vaiṣamyaṃ sākṣādyāgasādhana-
tvenopadiṣṭaiḥ dravyādibhiḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 3 ।। prājāpatyeṣu cāmnānāt ।। 6 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>paśuśabdaḥ kāryaṃ lakṣayatīti manvānaḥ pūrvapakṣayati</q> । asyārthaḥ---sapta-
daśa prājāpatyān paśūnālabhata iti paśuśabdena prākṛtān kratupaśūn lakṣayitvā
prajāpatidevatāyā vidhiḥ tena paśuśabdaḥ uddeśyaviśeṣaṃ samarpayan prakṛtakārya eva
vidhānametaditi jñāpayati । tenābhiprāyeṇocyate paśuśabdaḥ kāryaṃ lakṣayatīti । nanu
ca saṅkhyāvidhānaṃ nopapadyate devatāyāṃ vidhīyamānāyām kuta ityāha---<q>tadvidhāne ca
vākyabhedaḥ prasajyate yataḥ</q> । pariharati---<q>naiva saṅkhyā vidheyeti manyate</q> ।
kathamityāha---<q>karmaṇi saṅkhyā naiva vidhīyate</q> yathā tis‍tra āhutīrjuhotīti ।
yathā vā's‍minnevodāharaṇe saṅkhyādhikaraṇe dvitīye uktam---karmagatā saṅakhyā naiva
vidhīyata iti ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu satyaṃ na vidheyā saṅakhyā yadi karmāntaravidhānaṃ syāt</q> ।
yadi prajāpatidevatākapaśudravyakakarmavidhiḥsyāt tadā karmabhedakārikā saṅkhyā na
vidhīyeta । karmāntaratve ca paśuśabdopalakṣaṇatve nopapadyate vidheyatvenāvagamāt ।
devatāmātravidhāne punaravidhīyamānārthaḥ saṅkhyāśabdo naivānvetītyasāvapi saṅkhyā
na vidhiśabdārtho vidhātavyaḥ । tataśca vākyabhedaḥ । ataḥ saṅkhyāśabdaśravaṇāt karmā-
ntaravidhānamevaitaditi sthitam । karmāntaravidhāne ca naiva prākṛtakāryāpattiravagamyate
pramāṇābhāvāt । tatra[kathaṃ]guṇavidhirāśaṅkitaḥ pūrvapakṣānaupayikatvāt ? uttaraṃ---
<q>prakāranidarśane sati prasaṅgādidamupajātam</q> । bhāṣyakāreṇa prathamaṃ bādhaprakāre
darśite prasaṅgādidamupajātaṃ prāsaṅgikamidaṃ na punaḥ pūrvapakṣaupayikamityarthaḥ । <q>kaḥ
prasaṅgo yenedamākhyātam</q> ? uttaraṃ---<q>yadyayaṃ bādhaprakāraḥ syāt yo'yaṃ bhāṣya</q>-
﻿<pb n="391"/>
<q>kāreṇoktaḥ</q> । yadi grahaśabdamuccārya guṇo vidhīyeta tataḥ prākṛtā eva grahāḥ guṇa-
vikṛtā bhaveyuriti । <q>na tarhi bārhaspatye samuccayaḥ tatrāpi guṇavikāra eva syāt</q> ।
bhavatu kā kṣatirityatrāha <q>samuccayārthaṃ caitadudāhṛtam । bṛhaspatisave śrūyate---
bārhaspatyaṃ gṛhṇātīti । tasmānna śukravat bārhaspatye samuccayaḥ sambhavati</q>
yathāśukre samuccayaḥ tathā bārhaspatye na sambhavati guṇamātravikāropapatteriti । kathaṃ
tarhi samuccayasiddhirityatrāha---</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu bārhaspatye satyaṃ na siddha‍yati samuccayaḥ yadi gṛhṇātī-
tyasyāṃ codanāyāṃ nām‍ni guṇe vā kaścidviśeṣaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ - gṛhṇa tītyasyāṃ
codanāyāṃ śrutyā grahavidhāna bhātīti rāddhāntayuktiḥ yā, sā guṇaśravaṇe nāmamātra-
śravaṇe vā'viśiṣṭā, tena bārhaspatyepi samuccayaḥ । <q>kathaṃ punaraviśeṣaṃ manyate
yāvatā ādhastya evādhikaraṇe uktam---pṛthageva homavidhānaṃ na mantravidhā-
namiti</q> । tathāpi kimityāha---<q>yadi samantrakaṃ syāt syānmantravidhiriti</q> ।
bhāṣyakāreṇa mantrarahitahomadhidhānāt na mantravidhimātraṃ bhavatīti vadatā uktaṃ---
vikṛtā/?/vapi yatra guṇaḥ śrūyate tatra guṇavidhirbhavati । api ca dadhnā juhotītyevamādibhiḥ
sahāviśeṣo bārhaspatyaṃ gṛhṇātītyasya । yathā tatra homānuvādena dadhividhiḥ tathehāpi
grahānuvādena guṇavidhireva yuktaḥ ।</p>
<p>athāyamabhiprāyaḥ---tatra dadhnā juhotītyevamādau upadeśādeva prakṛtatvāddhomasya
yuktaṃ guṇavidhānaṃ iha punaḥ kāryataḥ prāptau satyāṃ nānuvādo dhātvarthasyeti । yāvadeva
hi kāryataḥ prāptimāśritya guṇavidhirna śakyate darśayituṃ tasya jaghanyatvāditi । tadayu-
ktam । ekādaśa prayājān yajatīti kā kathā । tatrāpi tarhi yāgavidhireva syānna
saṅkhyāvidhiḥ । iṣyate ca saṅkhyāvidhiḥ । kathaṃ vā somaraso grāhyaḥ yadi kāryataḥ
prāptimāśrityopadeśavarṇanā nāsti tadā kathaṃ somaraso vaikṛteṣu graheṣu gṛhyate ।
tasmānnātīva viśeṣo lakṣyate upadeśakāryataḥ prāpta‍yoḥ ।</p>
<p>evaṃ tāvat bārhaspatye samuccayānupapattiḥ yatrāpi śukraṃ gṛhṇātīti saguṇaśravaṇaṃ
tatrāpi nāmaśravaṇaṃ nopapadyata ityāha---<q>śabdasya ca grahalakṣaṇārthatvaṃ na śakyate-
'pahnotum</q> । grahaśabdeta prākṛtaṃ grahakāryaṃ lakṣayitvā grahāntaravidhiryuktaḥ klṛptakārya-
viṣayatvādvaikṛtānāmupadeśānāṃ prakṛtito'pyarthavatā bhavati । prakṛtau hi grahaśabdaḥ
pravṛttiviśeṣakaro na bhavati । iha tu lakṣaṇa(ke)tvena pravṛttiviśeṣakaratvenārthavān
﻿<pb n="392"/>
bhavati । prakṛtau hi arthāsambhavāt kiṃ kriyatām । iha punaḥ sambhavatyarthe nānarthako
grahaśabdo yukta iti pūrvapakṣa eva śreyāniti bruvate ।</p>
<p><q>atrābhidhīyate - gṛhṇātyarthāviśeṣāt grahaśabdasya keyamarthāntara-
kalpanā</q> । asyārthaḥ- yathā prakṛtāvaindravāyavaṃ gṛhṇātīti gṛṇhātiḥ grahaṇaṃ brūte tathā
vikṛtāvapi । (ta)yathā grahaṇaṃ graha iti vyutpattyā prakṛtau grahaśabdo mukhyārthaḥ tathe-
hāpi yuktaḥ na punaryathā grahaśabdo grahaṇamātraṃ brūte tathā kāryamityāha---<q>prayojanaṃ
hi grahakāryaṃ grahaśabdasya nābhidheyaṃ</q> grahakārye lakṣyamāṇe grahaśabdo'rthavān bhavatīti 
prayojanaṃ grahakāryaṃ grahaśabdasya nābhidheyam । abhidheyaṃ tu grahaṇameva । tasmin
vidyamāne na lakṣaṇāpramāṇamasti । abhidheyārthāparityāgena ca kāryaṃ sarve śabdā
lakṣayitu kṣamāḥ na parityajyābhiṃdheyārthamanarthakā lakṣayeyuḥ । atrāpi cāyaṃ gṛhṇātiḥ
śrūyate । abhinnārthaścāyaṃ gṛhṇātinā grahaśabdaḥ prakṛtivat । na cāyaṃ[kiṃ cāyaṃ]
gṛhṇātiḥ yadi kāryalakṣaṇārthastadā grahaśabdā'pi । atha tu vidheyārthaḥ saḥ tadā
sagrahaśabdaka eva vidheyārthaḥ na tu grahaśabdaṃ parityajya । nāmayogāccāvaśyaṃ śukrādiṣu
gṛhṇātipūrvo vidhātavtaḥ । uktaṃ dvitīye - saṃjñā śāstraṃ minattīti । na ca vidheyā-
dbhinnādṛte śāstrabhedaḥ sambhavati, anubandhasya śāstrabhedahetutvāditi siddhaṃ gṛhṇāti-
vidhānam । grahaśabdaśca tatsamānādhikaraṇo na kāryalakṣaṇārthaḥ । kintu mukhya-
vṛttireva । pūrvapakṣyāha---<q>yuktaṃ sāmasu, barhaspatye tu kā kathā</q> tatra guṇavidhānameva
yuktamityarthaḥ । sauvarṇarajatābhyāmiti prākṛtayorbhedo'dhvaryorabhāvāt yuktaḥ guṇavidhi-
parihāra iti manyate । yadi dvau syātāṃ tatra sauvarṇarājatamiti vidhiḥ syāt yathā
vārttadhnī paurṇamāsyāmanūcyete iti । na ca prakṛtau dvau sta iti । tadayuktam । aṃśvadā-
bhyayorvidyamānatvāt aśvadābhyaustaḥ tatra guṇavidhiḥ sambhavatīti । rāddhāntī tvāha---
<q>mahimānāvityanenaikavākyatvātparihāraḥ kevala bārhaspatye parihāro vaktavyaḥ
so'yamabhidhīyate</q> । dadhnā juhotīti dhātvarthavidhānaṃ guṇānuraktamiṣṭam । na kevalaṃ
guṇavidhānaṃ kriyāviṣayatvānniyogānām । yadi homavidhānaṃ tarhi agnihotrahomāddho-
māntaraṃ syādityatrāha---<q>anurajyamānaṃ tu svarūpata evopadiṣṭamastviti kriyā-
ntaravidhānam</q> । prakṛte hi juhotistasmin vartate । ata eva guṇānurakto
vidheyaḥ tadrūpasya tasya vihitatvāditi na homāntaravidhānam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="393"/>
<p>nanvatrāpyevaṃ bhavatvityatrāha---<q>upadeśaś‍copadeśamupodbalayati</q> tad‌buddhihetu-
tvānnātideśaḥ upadeśena sannihite home punarupadeśāntare juhotiḥ śrūyamāṇaḥ tatraiva
buddhiṃ janayatītyupadeśāntarasahāyo bhavati । punaratideśaḥ <q>kāryaniṣṭhatvāt</q> kārya-
pradhānatvāt bhavatu kāryaḥ tathāpi kimityāha---<q>na kāryaṃ karmaṇi buddhimutpādayituṃ
kṣamam atatsvābhāvyāt</q> । aptyārthaḥ---atideśena prāptaṃ tāvat karaṇopakāralakṣaṇaṃ
kāryam na prākṛtakarmaviśeṣe buddhiṃ janayituṃ kṣamam । akarmasvabhāvatvāt । etaduktaṃ
bhavati---vikṛtiṣu śrutamākhyātaṃ, tena kāryabalena padārthā upatiṣṭhanānā na pratyekaṃ
bhedenopatiṣṭhante iti nākhyātaṃ viśeṣe'vasthāpayituṃ śak‍tuvanti ।</p>
<p>nanvevamapi prākṛte padārthe vidyamāne kimiti padārthāntaramabhyupagamyate tena
guṇavidhireva yuktaḥ na karmāntaravidhiḥ । dadhnā juhotītyatrāpi prakṛtābhidhāne ayameva
hetuḥ sannihite home karmāntarakalpanā nopapadyata iti yo manyate tatrāha---<q>na ca
kalpanānirodho dadhnā juhotītyekābhidheyatā agnihotraṃ juhotītyanena</q> । kiṃ
tahiṃ tadbuddha‍yaiva । na cātra tadbuddhirasti kāraṇābhāvāt ।</p>
<p>yadi kalpanāvirodho na bhavati yuktiḥ kimiti tatra bhāṣyakāra evamāha---
<quote>“klṛpte na kalpanopapadyata”</quote> iti atrāha---<q>yatpunaḥ kalpaneti kācidvacovyaktiḥ
sā niyogaviṣayeti mantavyam</q> । klṛpte'dhikāraniyoge niyogāntarakalpanā na
yukteti tatrārthaḥ । <q>iha ca guṇāditi samuccayaḥ kratupaśubhissaha prājāpatyā
nām । liṅgamuktam</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 4 ।। āmane liṅgadarśanāt ।। 7 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>atra saṅkhyā prakṛtiliṅgatve nopapadyata iti manvāno mantravidhānācco-
padeśopapattiṃ anūyājānāṃ nivṛttiṃ manyate</q> । asyārthaḥ---āmanamasyāmanasya
<q>devā ye</q> sajātā iti tisra āhutīriti tisraḥ śabdena trayāṇāmanūyājānāṃ kāryaṃ
lakṣayitvā mantraviśeṣaktya āhutayo vidhīyante tenānūyājānāṃ nivṛttiriti pūrvapakṣaḥ ।
athavā mantra evānūyājāhutiṣu vidhīyata iti prākṛtamantravattayā anūyājānāṃ
nivṛttiriti ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu - na tāvat saṅkhyānūyājakāryaṃ triśabdena lakṣyeta saṅkhyā-
mātravacanastvayaṃ triśabdaḥ</q> । [trisaṅkhyā] nāmāhutīnāṃ....laukikasya karmaṇa
﻿<pb n="394"/>
upapadyata iti na triśabdenānūyājānāmevopādānamiti na tatkārye homāntara-
vidhānam ।</p>
<p>nanu na laukike triśabdo vartate yasmāt prakaraṇasambandhe triśabdo vartata iti
cet tadāha-<q>prakaraṇādavaccheda iti cet</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>vidheye'pi tulyaṃ prakaraṇaṃ
yataḥ</q> । śratra bhāṣyam-liṅgaṃ tvidaṃ prāptirucyatāṃ”</quote> iti । tadākṣipati---<q>evamuktena
nyāyena triśabdasya prakṛtiliṅgatve niraste <quote>“liṅgaṃ tvidaṃ prāptirvaktavyā”</quote>
iti vadataḥ ko'bhiprāyaḥ ? ekagranthenāha---<q>nanu prakṛtiliṅgāsaṃyogāduktaiva
prāptiḥ । uktāyāṃ ca punaḥ</q> praśno nopapadyate । samādhatte---<q>ayamabhiprāyaḥ
kimiti saṅkhyāvantamanṛdya guṇo vidhātuṃ na śakyate</q> । ekagranthenāha---<q>na
nāma saṅkhyā kāryaṃ lakṣayati । saṅkhyāvanta eva hi triśabdāt pratīyante
na saṅkhyāvatāṃ kāryam yajjuhoti tadāmanamasyāmanasya devā ityanena
mantreṇeti । tenānūyājeṣveva mantramātravidhānāt na samuccaya ityucyate
bhāṣyakāreṇeti sambandhaḥ</q> ।</p>
<p><q>parihārastu gṛhṇātivajjuhoteḥ śrutyarthatvādvidhānamityuktam</q> । yathā
bārhaspatyaṃ gṛhṇātīti śrutyā grahaṇavidhānaṃ tathehāpi homavidhāta/?/meva na mantrabivānamiti
parihāraḥ । <q>vājapeyavacca vākyabhedaḥ saṅkhyāmantrayorvidhānāt</q> । yadi tu
rtriśabdārtho na vidhīyeta kintu āhutīrviśinaṣṭi tadā viśiṣṭānuvādalakṣaṇo vākya-
bhedaḥ । tasmāt karmāntarāṇyevaitāni ।</p>
<p>evaṃ ca sati yadā karmāntaravidhānaṃ tadā vidhīyamānakarmāntarabhedāpādakatayāpi
saṅkhyā samarthitaiveti । <q>samuccayaliṅgamuktam</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 5 ।। upageṣu śaravatsyāt prakṛtiliṅgasaṃyogāt ।। 8 ।।</l></lg>
<p>atra bhāṣyakāraḥ pat‍nībhirupagāyantībhiḥ ṛtvijo nivartyante neti cintayati
tadyathāśrutamiti manvāno nyāyyaṃ sandehamāha---<q>prākṛtamupagānaṃ vikriyate neti
cintyata iti</q> । kathaṃ punaryathāśrutamayuktam ? ucyate । yadi hi prākṛte upagāne
pat‍nīmātravidhimāśritya pūrvapakṣāṃ bhavet apūrvopa/?/gānena ca rāddhāntaḥ tadā yukto
yathāśrutassandehaḥ । yadātu (apameva) pūrvameva gānāpacayakaraṃ gānamāśritya pūrvapakṣitaṃ
﻿<pb n="395"/>
tadaṅgīkāreṇaiva ca rāddhāntitaṃ tadā nibandhanokta eva sandeho yuktaḥ । bhāṣyavākyāni
upagānanivṛttāvapi ṛtvijāṃ nivṛttirastītyanenaivābhiprāyeṇa varṇanīyāni ।</p>
<p><q>kathaṃ punarupagānaṃ vikriyate kathaṃ vā na</q> ? uttaraṃ---<q>yadi prakṛti-
liṅgasaṃyogo'sti tadā vikāraḥ atha nāsti tadā samuccayaḥ । kathaṃ prakṛti-
liṅgasaṃyogo bhavati kathaṃ vā na sambhavati</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>yadyatrāpi prakṛti-
gānasyaiva śārīrasya upārtha upacayaścodyate tadā prakṛtiliṅgasaṃyogaḥ
avayavo hyupacayakārye vartata iti yuktam</q> । athāpi gṛhṇa tivanna vikṛtau kevalo-
pārthavidhānaṃ sambhavatīti upārthaviśiṣṭadha tvarthavidhāne'pi tulyakāryatvānnivṛttiḥ
prākṛtasyopagānasya । yadyapi gānopacayakari gānāntaraṃ vidhīyate tathāpi tulyakārya-
tvāt prākṛtamupagānaṃ nivartata iti yathāpūrvaprākāśadānavidhāvapi prākṛtadānanivṛttiḥ ।
<q>kathaṃ punaḥ tulyakāryatvaṃ</q> ? uttaraṃ---<q>upānvayāt । upaśabdo hi upacaya-
kāritāṃ dyotayati</q> । nanūpaśabdo'narthako dṛṣṭaḥ yathā gamanamevāpagamanaṃ tadvadava-
kimiti na bhavatītyatrāha---<q>na hyarthe sambhavatyānarthakyaṃ śakyate kalpayitu-
mityubhayathā upārthavidhau dhātvarthavidhau ca prākṛtaṃ nivartayati</q> । yadi punarvādi-
trasyopagānaṃ vāditramevopagānamiti tadā prakṛtiliṅgāsaṃyogāt samuccayaḥ । yasmādeta-
smin‍nubhayavidhepi pakṣe vāditropacayaḥ kāryaṃ na sāmagānopacayaḥ । <q>yadyevaṃ yadyubhayathāpi
samuccayaḥ tadā rāddhānte dhātvarthopanyāsatantrepi gānaśabdo dṛśyate ityetadeva
vaktavyam । tāvataiva rāddha ntasiddheḥ yadā hi k‍vopa/?/yujyeta</q> । bhāṣyakāraḥ
kimiti dhātvarthavidhānamāhetyarthaḥ । dhātvarthavidhānepi hi prakṛtiliṅgasaṃyoga ukta eva ।
tasmādvāditragānepi gānaśabdo vartata iti tadeva codakānugrahāya vaikṛte vāditre
upacayaḥ kāryamiti śabdāvirodhenāṅgīkriyata iti ।</p>
<p>samādhatte---<q>astyatrābhiprāyaḥ yadi kevalopasargārthaś‍codyate tadā na
prākṛtādgānāt anyacchakyate vak‍tum</q> । asyārthaḥ---vāditrameva gānamityuktaṃ
tanna siddha‍yati yadyupasargārthaḥ kevalo vidhīyate । tadā śrau[tagāna] vidhānamityukte
vākyena prākṛta evopagānopacayaḥ[kṛtaḥ] ihāpi tathaiva mā prasāṅkṣīt ityāghāṭalikādi-
vidhiḥ । dhātvarthavidhāne punaḥ kāryāntareṇāpyupārthānvayaḥ sambhavatīti nāvaśyaṃ prākṛta-
meva kāryaṃ gānopacayakāri । dhātvarthe vidhīyamāne upacayaḥ kāryabhūta āśrayaṇīyaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="396"/>
na ca sa prākṛta eva, dikṣu dundubhayo nadanti ityatrāpi upacayasya kāryasya
sambhavāt । sa eva codakānugrahāyāśrīyate । tadidamuktaṃ vāditrasyopagānamiti ।</p>
<p>kathaṃ tarhi upasargārthavidhānepi rāddhānto darśita ityatrāha---<q>athāti prakṛta-
tvādva ditrasya tasyāpi gānaśabdavācyatvāt vāditra evopacaye</q> upagāyati-
rvartate tadā vāditrasya upārthavidhānepyetatsiddha‍yati vāditropagānamiti । tasmāt
sarvaṃ sūktam । pūrvapakṣottarapakṣāvapi viṣayābhidhānenaivopavarṇitāvityuparamyate । tatra
śārīrameva gānaṃ na vāditramiti pūrvaḥpakṣaḥ । na hi vādayan gāyatītyucyate ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu vāditramapi gānamucyate, svaraviśiṣṭābhivyaktirhi gānaṃ
sā ca vāditre'pi vidyate tadapi gānamiti</q> ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 6 ।। saṃskāre cānyasaṃyogāt ।। 10 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>atra añ‍jata ityupadeśārthatvāt tulyaṃ kāryaṃ manvānasya pūrvaḥpakṣaḥ</q> ।
gauggulavena prātassavane'ñjate ityañjā/?/syeha lepanamātrameva kāryam । navanītasyāpi
lepa/?/nameva kāryamiti manvānaḥ pūrvapakṣī navanītasya nivṛttimāha ।</p>
<p>nanu dīkṣākāle navanītenābhyañjanaṃ sutyākāle ca gauggulavaṃ kaṣāyāñjanaṃ
iti kathaṃ tasya tena nivṛttirityatrāha---<q>tulyakāryatve ca na kālānyatvamupaghāte
hetuḥ</q> kālānyattvaṃ nāvanītasya dhopaghāte hetuḥ prayājavat । yathā kālāntarīyairapi
pāśukaiḥ prayājaiḥ kṛte kārye pauroḍāśikaprayājanivṛttiḥ tathehāpītyabhiprāyaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu nopadeśārtha eva prakṛtau kāryaṃ nāvanītasyābhyañ‍janasya ।
kiṃ tarhi vaiśadyamaṅgānāṃ s‍nehanena navanītena kṛtam</q> । iha gauggulave kaṣāye
s‍nehanaṃ kāryaṃ nāstīti kāryāntarakalpanā । tacca kāryaṃ dṛṣṭamadṛṣṭaṃ vā yathārthaṃ
arthasvarūpānatikrameṇa kalpanīyam । ataḥ kālāntarātsamuccayaḥ na tu kāryānyatvameva
samuccayahetuḥ ।</p>
<p><q>kimidaṃ kālānyatvātsamuccaya ityucyate</q> । samādhatte-<q>ekakālīnānāṃ
hi kāryabhede'pi kālāntarābhāvāt bhavati bādha iti pradarśitaṃ bhavati</q> ।
bhinnakārye api navanītāñjanagauggulavāñjate vaiśadyavirūkṣakaraṇe samānakāle virudhyete
﻿<pb n="397"/>
iti vā etat tyāditi darśayituṃ kālabhede uktaḥ । navanītāñjane sthite gauggulavāñjanaṃ
paścāt virūkṣīkaraṇamiti ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 7 ।। ācchādane tvaikārthyāt prākṛtasya vikāraḥ syāt ।। 13 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>atra kaupīnācchādanārthena vāsaso dṛṣṭārthatvāt bādhaṃ manyate pūrva-
pakṣavādī</q> । tārpyādibhiḥ kaupīnasya guhyadeśācchāditatvāt ahataṃ vāso nivartate ।
dṛṣṭaṃ caitat । idameva kāryaṃ vāsaso'pi kaupīnācchādanamiti rāddhāntavādī manyate ।</p>
<p>uktaṃ vaikṛtamantrepadeśe ṣaṅ‌bhirdīkṣayatītyatra nābhyāsomantrāṇām upadeśārtha-
vattvāya hi te kriyante । kāryaprayuktatvena kāryamastītyetāvatā na kriyante । kintu
upadeśamyārthavattvāyeti । evamatrāpyupadeśasyārthavattā karaṇīyā upadeśataḥ prāpteḥ
svārthādīnām । paridhānaṃ copadeśārthaḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>।। 8 ।। sāmasvarthāntaraśruteravikāraḥ pratīyeta ।। 16 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>sāmāntarāṇiṃ nivartanta iti । ko'bhiprāyo'syāś‍cintāyāḥ ?
yāvatā yuk‍taiva nivṛttiḥ stutau sādhanāntaravidhānena sādhanāntarasya</q> ।
uttaraṃ---<q>nātra kiñcit prākṛtaliṅgaṃ śrūyate yena prākṛtanivṛttiḥ । stutyartha-
syānavagamāt</q> । yadi hi stutimuddiśya sāmāntaravidhānaṃ syāt syāt sāmāntara-
nivṛttiḥ । na caitadasti । tasmāt parisāmādāvanuccāraṇamātraṃ vidhīyamānasāmānta-
rāṇāmadṛṣṭāyeti samuccaya eva yukta iti pūrvaḥpakṣaḥ । rāddhāntastu uk‍taṃ tāvatsām‍nāma-
viśeṣeṇa saṃskārakatvam tena krauñcādayo'pi saṃskārakārakā eva । sāmānyena cāyaṃ
nyāyaḥ---svabhāvataḥ kāryasiddhau sambhavantyāṃ padārthasvabhāvatyāgena kāryāntarakalpanā
na yuk‍teti । <q>evaṃ cākṣarābhivyaktyā stutyabhinirvṛtyā cādṛṣṭe upadeśārthavattve
sambhavati nādṛṣṭakalpanā dravyāṇāṃ sambhavati</q> । asyārthaḥ---sām‍nāṃ hi
sādhanatvaṃ guṇābhidhānasamarthākṣarābhivyaktidvāreṇa । tacca svabhāvāparityāgāt dṛṣṭenaiva
vyāpāreṇa । uccāraṇamātreṇa tvadṛṣṭārthatvam । svabhāvaparityāgena hi tatrākṣarābhi-
vyañjakatvamupayogi । tasmāt stuti [rā]śrīyatām na punaruccāraṇamātreṇādṛṣṭam ।
<q>nanu ca kāryapravṛttirasti</q> । asyārthaḥ---yadyapi sām‍nāmupadeśastathāpi kāryato'pi
sāmāntarāṇāṃ prāptatvāt taissaha samuccaya eva nyāyyaḥ । na bā/?/dhaḥ । uttaraṃ---
﻿<pb n="398"/>
<q>bāḍhamasti kāryāt prāptiḥ</q> । sā tu kāryasiddhāvasatyām । iha tu upadeśata eva
siddhaṃ kāryamiti prati(nivṛttitaṃ)nivartitaṃ vidhestaṃ prati prayojakatvam । tasmād‌bādho
yuk‍taḥ । ayaṃ ca sarvatra nyāyo draṣṭavyaḥ prākṛtapadārthaprayuktibādhena vaikṛtaṃ tatkārye
sādhanāntaraṃ vidhīyata iti ।</p>
<p>nanvevaṃ tarhi parisāmasvapi stutireva syāt ityatrāha---<q>parisāmasu punarupa-
deśāntare vidhānāt dṛṣṭaṃ na sambhavatītyadṛṣṭameva kāryamiti yuk‍ta</q> upadeśāntare
kārye stuteranyasmin kāryāntare vacanenaiva vidhānāt yuk‍taṃ parisām‍nāmadṛṣṭaṃ kāryam ।
yadasmābhiruk‍taṃ tadidamuk‍taṃ devadattavadyajñadattastaileneti । kathamanenaitaduktamityatrāha---
<q>svabhāvāparityāgena tailaṃ s‍nehanarūpaṃ na kāryāntare vartate ityartho'sya
tailadṛṣṭāntasya</q> । tathāpi svabhāvāparityāgenāpi upadeśe siddhe sarveṣāṃ bhāṣyakārīye
sandehe kāraṇasandehamāha-<q>atredānīṃ sthite sāmāntarabādhakatve cintyate । kiṃ</q>
kāryaviśeṣājñānāt stutimātrakāryavijñānāt (sarvakārya) prākṛtasāmakāryārthatvāt
vaikṛtānāṃ sām‍nāmupadeśasya upadeśārthanivṛttimātramevānuṣṭhānenopadeśārthaḥ svīkṛto bhavati
tāvadevānuṣṭhānaṃ kāryamiti ।</p>
<p><q>nanu cāyamasmaduk‍to'rthaḥ upadeśārthanirvṛttimātramevānuṣṭhānamiti
kiṃ cintyate nirṇīṃtatvāt</q> ।</p>
<p>pari/?/harati---<q>satyamuktam kāryāviśeṣānavagamādupadeśamātramevāpratipannaṃ
manyate</q> । yathā ṣaḍ‌ni/?/rdīkṣayatītyādau kāryaviśeṣo jñātaḥ tatheha kāryaviśeṣajñānaṃ nāsti
tenopadeśārtha eva na pratipannaḥ । tena sāmānyupadiṣṭāni tāvatāṃ prayoge yatkāryaṃ
tadetadeva tatkāryaṃ na kāryata upadeśanirṇayaḥ parivāsasyapyupapadyata iti na kāryārthaṃ
kāryataḥ prāptamahataṃ vāso na vihanti kaupīnācchādanādanyad dṛṣṭamapi kāryaṃ sambhavati ।
paridhānasya sambhavāduparivāsasyapi । upadeśe hi śabdārthānuṣṭhānaṃ tataḥkāryam । na
kāryato'nuṣṭhānaṃ yathā kāryataḥ pravṛttānāṃ kāryato'nuṣṭhānaṃ na tathā sākṣādupadiṣṭānāṃ,
kintu teṣāṃ kāryaṃ kalpyam । na ca śabdārthaviśiṣṭasya dadhātyarthasya kaupīnācchādanenaiva
kāryam kāryāntarasyāpyuparivāsasi darśanāt । tenānaikāntikatvāt na kāryaviśeṣā-
vadhāraṇam । <q>darśanamuktam</q> । adṛṣṭārthe hi noparivāsasāpi saha samuccaya iti
vāsāṃsīti bahuvacanaṃ liṅgam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="399"/>
<lg><l>।। 8 ।। sāmasvarthāntaraśruteravikāraḥ pratīyeta ।। 16 ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>atra kālavidhānameva manvāno na śak‍noti pūrvapakṣayitum । vikṛtau
bhāvārthavidhānāt । darśanagrahādhikaraṇavadapratipakṣatvācca bhāvārthavidhānasye-
tyuktam</q> । anekaguṇaśravaṇāccetyapi draṣṭavyam । ataḥ stutyantaramevedaṃ sāmaviśiṣṭaṃ
vidhīyate dānavaddānāntarakārye, stutirapi stutyantarakārye vartata iti pūrvapakṣayati---
<q>samānajātīyatvāt stutyantarakārye vartata iti śakyate vak‍tumiti prākṛta-
stutinivṛttiḥ</q> ।</p>
<p><q>rāddhāntastu syādetadevaṃ yadi guṇamātravidhiḥ stāt krauñ‍cādivat
iha tu viśiṣṭavidhānam</q> । anyathā yadi viśiṣṭavidhānaṃ nāśrīyate tadā yathāśrutānva-
yānupapattiḥ deśaviśiṣṭasyāpyanvayāvagamāt । tataḥ kiṃ ? yadi viśiṣṭavidhānaṃ na
stutyantarakārye vartata iti śakyate vak‍tuṃ adṛṣṭārthatvāt stutīnām । dānena dṛṣṭārtha-
tayā yuk‍to dānāntareṇa vaikṛtena prākṛtadānapratyām‍nāyaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>nanu ca bhāṣyakāreṇa sām‍nāṃ nivṛttirityuk‍taṃ na stutyantareṇa
stutīnāṃ nivṛttirityuk‍tam । ato bhāṣyavirodhaḥ</q> । uttaraṃ - <q>phalatastadva</q>-
[canam] ।</p>
<p><q>।। atra pātaḥ ।।</q></p>
﻿<pb n="400"/>
<p>ṛjuvimalāyāṃ</p>
<p><q>।। dvādaśādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ ।।</q></p>
<p>atra bhāṣyakāraḥ phalamāha---<quote>‘ekādaśādhyāye tantrāvāpalakṣaṇaṃ vyākhyātam ।
adhunā dvādaśe prasaṅgalakṣaṇaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ’</quote> taccaitadvṛttavartiṣyamāṇānukīrtanaṃ sambandha-
kathanārtham । tatra pṛcchati---<q>kaḥpunaranayorlakṣaṇayoḥ sambandhaḥ yatkathanārthaṃidaṃ
bhāṣyamiti</q> । pṛcchataścāyamāśayaḥ tantre'pi sakṛdanuṣṭhānaṃ prasaṅge'pi । tadanayorna hetu-
hetumadbhāvassambhavati । na ca sambandhāntarasya śaṅkāpi yukteti । uttaraṃ---<q>hetuhetu-
madbhāvakṛta eva sambandha iti</q> । kuta ityāha---<q>sthite hyekaprayogavacanāda-
bhinnākāśakālakartṛtve tantramanuṣṭhānamagṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatvāditi idānīṃ gṛhya-
māṇe viśeṣe anyato'pi prayogasiddheḥ deśakālakartṛtvābhede kiṃ tantramevā-
ṣṭhānaṃ uta bhedeneti cintyate</q> । asyārthaḥ-darśapūrṇamāsābhyāṃ svargakāmo yajetetyeka-
smāt prayogavacanāt prayogaviviśeṣabhūtānāṃ deśakālakartṝṇāmabhede sthite prayājādī-
nāmaṅgānāṃ tantramanuṣṭhānamiti yat tadagṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatvāt na prayājādyanuṣṭhānasya viśeṣo
gṛhyate asya pradhānasyedaṃ nāsyeti ।</p>
<p>etaduktaṃ bhavati---yadyekaḥ prayogavacano na syāt tadā prayogacodanāśeṣabhūtā
deśakālakartāro'pi bhedena sambadhyen sauryāryamaṇaprājāpatyeṣviva; yadā tveka
eva prayogavacanaḥ tadā deśatvaṃ deśasya kālatvaṃ kālasya kartṛtvaṃ karturna bhidyate ।
tataśca prayogānubandhabhūtānāṃ teṣāṃ bhedādeka eva prayogo gṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatvāditi ।</p>
<p><q>idānīṃ paśvarthamanuṣṭhānaṃ na puroḍāśārthamiti gṛhyamāṇepi viśeṣe anya-
to'pi prayogasiddheḥ anuṣṭhānasyāgṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatvāt deśakālakartṛtvābheda-
sādhakādanyataḥ tantramadhyavidhānādekaprayogasiddheḥ deśakālakartṛtvābhedepi
kiṃ tantrameva sakṛdevānuṣṭhānaṃ prayājādeḥ uta bhedeneti cintyate</q> yataḥ tato
hetuhetumadbhāvo'stīti । etacca grahaṇavākyam ।</p>
<p>etadeva codyaparihāradvāreṇa vivarītuṃ codayati---<q>kaḥpunaratra pūrvasya
hetvarthaḥ । heturhi bhavan kañcidarthamupakurvan heturbhavati</q> । atra pūrvasya ko
hetvarthaḥ । ekadeśyāha---<q>ekadeśakālakartṛtvasiddhiḥ</q> । deśakālakartṝṇāmekatā
﻿<pb n="401"/>
pūrvādhyāye siddha‍yati । bhavatvevaṃ tathāpi kena hetvarthatetyatrāha---<q>tasyāṃ hi satyāṃ
gṛhyamāṇe viśeṣe sakṛdanuṣṭhānam</q> ।</p>
<p>yadyapi krama(saṅkhyā) [samākhyā ?] apyaviśeṣeṇa gṛhyante viśeṣa[ta]ḥ
pāśukamidamanuṣṭhānamiti tathāpi deśakālakartrekatayā sakṛdanuṣṭhānam । nanvevamapi kathaṃ
pūrvasya hetutvamityatrāha---<q>sā caikaprayogavacanatayā sādhitā'dhastāt</q> ।</p>
<p>ākṣeptā'ha---<q>nanvatrāpi tulyam</q> । asyārthaḥ-yadidaṃ ekaprayogavacanatayā
deśādīnāmekatvasādhanaṃ tattulyamatrāpi । jyotiṣṭoma eva prayogaḥ paśoḥ puroḍāśasya
ca jyotiṣṭomena svargakāmo yajetetyanena pradhānasyāṅgānāṃ ca prayoga ucyata iti ।
upadeśāt jyotiṣṭomāṅgasya paśupuroḍāśasya ca paśvaṅgasyaikaḥ prayogavacanaḥ । <q>pāśuka
eva vā puroḍāśasya tadaṅgatvāt</q> । yadvā pāśuka eva prayogavacanaḥ agnīṣomīyaṃ
paśumālabhata iti puroḍāśasthaprayogaṃ vakti । puroḍāśasya paśvaṅgatvāt sāṅgasya ca
pradhānasya codanāyaiva prayukto'yaṃ iti codayati---<q>sa eva tadaṅgamapīti</q> । yata
evamekaprayogavacanatā'trāpi tannivandhanaśca deśādīnāmabhedaḥ tannibandhanaṃ ca sakṛdanuṣṭhānaṃ
ataḥ tantraprasaṅgyoḥ bheda eva durlabhaḥ hetuhetumadbhāvastu dūrata eva nāstītyāha---
<q>tasmānnānayorhetuhetumadbhābassambhavati</q> ।</p>
<p>idānīmākṣeptā tantraprasaṅgyoḥ bhedamāśaṅkate---<q>athātrāṅgaprāptirbhinnaniyoga-
labhyā prasaṅge । tantre tu punarekaniyogalabhyā iti bhedaḥ</q> । kiṃ tau paśuniyoga-
puroḍāśaniyogāvatideśataḥ prāpayataḥ prasaṅge, tantre punareka eva darśapūrṇamāsādhikāra-
niyogaḥ prayājādikamaṅgajātaṃ prati karaṇaṃ prāpayati । tenaikaniyogaprāpitānāṃ sakṛda-
nuṣṭhānaṃ tantram । bhinnaniyogaprāpitānāṃ tu prasaṅga iti viśeṣaḥ । nirākaroti---
<q>ayamapi viśeṣo naiva śakyate vak‍tuṃ yasmāt jyotiṣṭomaniyogalabhyaiveya-
mubhayoritikartavyatā</q> । asyārthaḥ - yadyapi prāpakabhedaḥ tathāpi prayojakabhedastā-
vannāsti । prasaṅgepi jyotiṣṭomaniyogasya yattantraṃ prayuktiḥ tallabhyaiva tatprayojyaivobhayoḥ
paśupuroḍāśayoritikartavyatā । prayojakaviśeṣanibandhanaścānuṣṭhānaviśeṣo nyāyyaḥ tadadhīna-
tvāttasya । tantraprasaṅgau ca anuṣṭhānasya viśeṣau । tenobhayatrāpi prayojakaviśeṣā-
bhāvānnānuṣṭhānaviśeṣo yuktaḥ । evameva cāyaṃ grantho vyākhyeyaḥ । na jyotiṣṭomasya
prāpakatvamāśritya kṛts‍navidhānādhikaraṇe tasya prāpakatvaniṣedhāt । na cānena prasaṅga
tantrayoḥ viśeṣeṇa hetuhetumadbhāvasiddhiḥ ।‍</p>
﻿<pb n="402"/>
<p>punarapi tantraprasaṅgayoḥ viśeṣamāśaṅkate---<q>athedamucyate guṇādivikārepi
tulyamanuṣṭhānamiti prasaṅgaḥ</q> । yadyapi vṛttādinā saṅkhyayā ca ekādaśādikayā
vikṛtāḥ padārthāḥ tathāpyekamevānuṣṭhānamityevaṃrūpaḥ prasaṅgaḥ । vikāre tu tantramiti kiṃ
tantraprasaṅgayorviśeṣaḥ iti । nirākaroti---<q>yadyapyayaṃ viśeṣaḥ tathāpi hetuhetu-
madbhāvo vaktavyaḥ</q> । sa evāha---<q>kaḥ khalu</q> kṛtasya vikāre hetubhāvaḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu kimatra hetuhetumadbhāvenetyatrāhaṃ-<q>na ca hetuhetumadbhāvaṃ vinā idaṃ vṛttaṃ
idaṃ vatiṃṣyamāṇamiti yuktaṃ vak‍tuṃ</q> sambandhāntarasya[ā]vidyamānatvāt । ākṣeptaiva
śaṅkāmāha---<q>athāṅgānāṃ sakṛdanuṣṭhānalakṣaṇassambandha ucyate</q> । asyārthaḥ-
tantrepi sakṛdanuṣṭhānaṃ prasaṅgepi । tena sakṛdanuṣṭhānarūpatantraprasaṅgāt prasaṅgaścintyata
iti । tena prāsaṅgikassambandha iti । nirākaroti---<q>tathāpi vṛttagrahaṇamakiñci-
tkaram viparītasyāpi prasaṅgasya sambhavāt prasaṅgaprasaṅgena tantrameva
kasmānnocyate</q> tena tantre vṛtte prasaṅga iti vṛttagrahaṇamakiñcitkaram । tattu evamupayogi
syādyadi vṛtta eva tasminnidaṃ vicāryate । yāvatā vartiṣyamāṇepi tasminnidaṃ śakyameva
cintayitum ।</p>
<p>dūṣaṇāntaramāha---<q>taddhetūpajīvanaṃ cātra lakṣyate</q> । 1taddhetūpajīvanañca
prasaṅge kṛte । kasyāsau taddheturityatrāha---<q>abhinnadeśakālakartṛtvamiti</q> । tantre
prasaṅge ca tadeva heturiti samānahetukatayā parasparaṃ hetuhetumadbhāvo nāstītyabhiprāyaḥ ।
upasaṃharati---<q>tasmādvaktavyo'tra hetuhetumadbhāvaḥ</q> ।</p>
<p>samarthayitā āha---<q>ayamabhidhīyate</q> । hetuhetumadbhāvadeśakālakartṛśāstrārthā-
viśeṣeṇa hi tantre sakṛdanuṣṭhānāt tantreṇa kāryasiddhiruktā anuṣṭhānoddeśaviśeṣāgrahaṇā-
diti । same darśapūrṇamāsābhyāṃ yajeta paurṇamāsyāṃ paurṇamāsyā yajeta darśapūrṇamāsayorya-
jñakratvoḥ catvāraṛtvija iti yāni deśakālakartṝṇāṃ śāstrāṇi teṣāṃ yo'rthaḥ
tasyāviśeṣeṇa prayājādīnāṃ sakṛdanuṣṭhānāt kāryasiddhiḥ tantramityanuṣṭhānoddeśe anuṣṭhāne
yaddeśaḥ asmā idamanuṣṭhānamiti tasya viśeṣāgrahaṇāditi tantre tantralakṣaṇe uktam ।</p>
<p><q>idānīmanuṣṭhānoddeśe viśeṣagrahaṇepi deśakālakartṛśāstrārthaviśeṣāt
aṅgakāryasya kimanyatvaṃ bhavati neti saṃśayaḥ</q> । yadi hi aṅgakāryasya bhedo
<note>1. R taddheturupa</note>
﻿<pb n="403"/>
bhavati ekasyārthena kṛtamaṅgajātaṃ aparasyopakartuṃ na śak‍nuyāt tadā bhedenāṅgānā-
manuṣṭhānaṃ bhavati । atha na bhinnaṃ kāryaṃ tadā sakṛdanuṣṭhānamiti anuṣṭhānabhedābhedena
kāryasya bhedābhedau cintyete ।</p>
<p>nanvevamapi pūrvasya kathaṃ hetuhetumadbhāvaḥ ityatrāha---<q>satyaṃ uddeśyāviśeṣeṇa
sarvārthamanuṣṭhānamiti sthitam । kāryāviśeṣastu kartrādyabhedanibandhana eva
iti anuṣṭhānaviśeṣeṇa sādhitastantre prasaṅge hetutāṃ pratipadyata iti so'yaṃ hetu-
hetumadbhāvaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---satyaṃ tatroddeśyāviśeṣeṇa sarvārthamanuṣṭhānamiti sthitam ।
kāryāviśeṣastu yastatra kartrādyabhedanibandhana eva । kartrādīnāṃ hi prayogacodanāśeṣatvāt
sapta[rva]padārtheṣbabhedena kartṛtvaṃ deśatvaṃ kālatvaṃ ca śāstrārthaḥ । tatra yeṣāṃ padārthānāṃ
svarūpabhedaḥ tatra pradhānabhedādaṅgabhūtānāṃ kartrādīnāṃ kartṛtvādikamāvartate pratipradhānamā-
vartante guṇā iti nyāyāt । ye tu padārthāḥ na svarūpato bhinnāḥ tān prati kartṛtvā-
dikaṃ na bhidyata iti balāt sakṛdevānuṣṭhānam । anyathā hi kartṛtvādikamapi bhidyate ।
tataśca sakṛdanuṣṭhāne niścite kāryamapyaṅgānāṃ tantrameveti niścīyate anuṣṭhitānāṃ
kāryāsādhakatvāt । pratipradhānaṃ cāṅgānāṃ viniyogādavaśyābhyupagamanīyatvāt kārya-
syeti । ata idamucyate---kāryādyabhedastu kartrādyabhedanibandhana eveti yo'yaṃ
kāryāviśeṣastantre tantralakṣaṇe anuṣṭhānāviśeṣeṇa sādhitaḥ anuṣṭhānoddeśāviśeṣāt
kartrādyabhedaḥ tadabhedādanuṣṭhānābhedaḥ anuṣṭhānābhedāt kāryābheda iti matvā uktamanu-
ṣṭhāna[ā]viśeṣeṇa sādhitastantre kāryāviśeṣa iti ।</p>
<p>sa cāyaṃ kāryāviśeṣaḥ aṅgakāryaṃ tantratā tantralakṣaṇena sādhitā । sati(tī)-
ca prasaṅge paroddeśānuṣṭhitenāpi paropakāralābhe niścetavye hetutāṃ pratipadyata iti
so'yaṃ hetuhetumadbhāvaḥ ।</p>
<p>tadeṣa saṅkṣepārthaḥ---paśūddeśenānuṣṭhitānāmapyaṅgānāṃ yadavāntakāryaṃ tat paśupuro-
ḍāśayordvayorapi sādhāraṇamiti sthite aṅgāvāntarakāryatantratve tantralakṣaṇe siddhe parārthā-
ṣṭhitairapi padārthaiḥ parasyopakāralakṣaṇakāryasiddheḥ udāsīnā pradhānāntaraprayuktirbhavatīti
prasaṅganiścayo jāyata iti bhavati tantrasya prasaṅgaṃ prati hetubhāvaḥ । dṛṣṭaṃ hi parārthānu-
ṣṭhitasyāpi paraṃ pratyupakāratvamiti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="404"/>
<p>tatra bhavanti ślokāḥ---</p>
<lg><l>paroddeśapravṛttānāmaṅgānāṃ yatparān prati ।</l>
<l>mahopakārasāmarthya/?/ sa prasaṅga udāhṛtaḥ ।। 1 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>aṅgāvāntarakāryāṇāṃ tantratā tasya bodhikā ।</l>
<l>hetutā hetumattā ca tena tantraprasaṅgyoḥ ।। 2 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>kartṛtvādyaviśeṣeṇa kartrādīnāṃ prasiddha‍yati ।</l>
<l>anuṣṭhānasakṛdbhāvaḥ tena kāryasya tantratā ।। 3 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>anuṣṭhānāviśeṣeṇa tantre kartrādyabhinnatā ।</l>
<l>tantramadhyanipātena prasaṅge sā ca siddha‍yati ।। 4 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>ekaprayogatāsiddhiḥ tantramadhyavidhānataḥ ।</l>
<l>aikyena ca prayogasya kartrādīnāmabhinnatā ।। 5 ।।</l></lg>
<p>yata eva tantre anuṣṭhānaviśeṣāgrahaṇāt kāryāviśeṣaḥ ata evātra pūrvaḥpakṣaḥ anuṣṭhāne
viśeṣāgrahaṇāt kāryaviśeṣo nāstītyevaṃrūpaḥ । paśūddeśena hi kriyamāṇāḥ prayā-
jādayaḥ paśūpakārānuguṇamevāvāntarakāryaṃ kurvanti iti yuktam । tena puroḍāśārthaṃ
bhedenānuṣṭhātavyā iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>rāddhāntastu---<q>satyaṃ anuṣṭhāne viśeṣo gṛhyate na punaḥ deśakālakartṝṇāṃ
viśeṣaḥ tatkṛtaścāyaṃ kāryāviśeṣaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ - yadyapyuddeśe viśeṣo gṛhyate
tathāpi deśādīnāṃ deśatvā(nya)dyabhedāt sakṛdanuṣṭhānena bhavitavyam । tataścāṅga-
kāryeṇāpi sakṛdevetyaṅgāvāntaratantratā tāvadgamyate । tataśca paramopakāro'pi tad‌dvāra-
katvāt puroḍāśasyāpi tena siddha‍yati yathā prāsādoddeśenāpi kṛtasya pradīpasya yadavāntara-
kāryaṃ prabhālakṣaṇaṃ tasya sādhāraṇatvāt gamanakāryajanakatā rājamārgepi bhavati ।
tathehāpi praṣṭavyam ।</p>
<p><q>yadyanuṣṭhānaviśeṣagrahaṇe'pi kāryāviśeṣaḥ kimarthaṃ tarhi tantre anuṣṭhāna-
viśeṣāgrahaṇaṃ prayat‍nenocyate</q> । uttaraṃ---<q>kartrādyaviśeṣasiddhaye</q> । yatra hyanuṣṭhāne
viśeṣo gṛhyate tatra kartrādīnāṃ kartṛtvādikaṃ bhidyate yathā saṃsparśiṣu [saṃsarpiṣu ?]
yathā vā āgneyakṛṣṇagrīvayoḥ । tena kartrādīnāmabhedasiddha‍yarthaṃ viśeṣāgrahaṇaṃ sādhyate ।
﻿<pb n="405"/>
yadi viśeṣāgrahaṇe kartrādīnāmabhedaḥ iha tarhi tadabhāvāt viśeṣāgrahaṇā-
bhāvāt kartrādyabhedaḥ [na]prāp‍noti</q> । tataśca kutaḥkāryāviśeṣaḥ kutastarāṃ ca prasaṅgaḥ
iti । pariharati---<q>anyataḥ prayogaikyasiddheḥ na prāp‍noti kartrādīnāṃ bhedaḥ ।
anyataḥ tantramadhya</q>vidhānāt prayogaikyaṃ paśupuroḍāśayoḥ avagamyate । ekaprayogatve
ca prayogaśeṣāṇāṃ kartrādīnāmabhedo'vagamyate । ataḥ aṅgeṣu siddhepi prayogaviśeṣagrahaṇe
anyataḥ kartrādyabhedalābhāt kāryāviśeṣāt tantravatprasaṅgasiddhiriti sthitam ।</p>
<p>tantrepi sakṛdanuṣṭhānenopakārasiddhirevābhedānuṣṭhānahetuḥ ihāpi cok‍tena nyāyena
asti sakṛdanuṣṭhānenāpyupakārasiddhiriti yuktamabhedenānuṣṭhānam । yata eva kartrādīnāma-
bhedenānuṣṭhānasyaikyaniścayaḥ <q>ata eva padārthadvārakāḥ kramasaṅkhyādayaḥ na padārthaṃ-
kāryaṃ vihantuṃ kṣamāḥ tadānuguṇyāt</q> । asyārthaḥ---pūrvapakṣiṇā hyetaduktam tiṣṭhantaṃ
paśuṃ prayajati pṛṣadājyenānūyān yajati ekādaśa prayājān yajati iti paśau prayā-
jādīnāṃ guṇakālavikāravidhānāt vikṛtāḥ paśorupakurvanti na puroḍāśānāmiti ।</p>
<p>tatredamucyate---yadā tantramadhyavidhānasiddhaikaprayoganibandhanakartrādyabhedabalādā-
yātaḥ kāryāviśeṣaḥ paśau puroḍāśe ca prayājādīnāṃ tadā ye padārthadvārakāḥ kramasaṅkhyā-
dayaḥ te padārthakāryaṃ sādhāraṇaṃ na vihantuṃ kṣamāḥ kāryānuguṇatvāt guṇavidhānasya ।
ye hi prayogādvārakāḥ te prayogabhedamāvahanto bhavantyeva kāryābhedavighātakāḥ । yā tu
saṅkhyā yacca dravyaṃ tanna prayogadvārakam । yaḥpunaḥ tiṣṭhantaṃ paśuṃ prayajatīti kālavidhiḥ
sa kālasya vacanāntareṇa sutyālakṣaṇasya vihitatvāt kramamātrapara eveti na bhedenānu-
ṣṭhānamāpādayituṃ kṣamaḥ । ata eva kramasaṅkhyādaya iti kramagrahaṇaṃ kṛtamiti hetoḥ
nānuṣṭhānāntaramāvahanti kramasaṅkhyādayaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>yatpunaridaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa padārthāntaranirākṛtau prayājādayaḥ saṅkhyā-
bhede'pi na prākṛtebhyo'rthāntarabhūtā ityatra yatitaṃ prayājādiṣu</q> । yatiḥ
prakṛtyantaramasti na punaryatī prayat‍ne ityasyedaṃ rūpam, śvīdita iti iḍabhāvaprasaṅgāt ।
tadabuddhipūrvakamiva pratibhāti । <q>padārthāntaratvepi paśāveva tatkāryaṃ bhaviṣyati</q>
tasya padārthāntarasya kāryaṃ paśāveva bhaviṣyati paśoreva tasya vihitatvāt saṅkhyādī-
nāmiva । <q>yathā saṅkhyādīnāṃ paśāveva kāryaṃ tasmāt karmāntaratvepi na puroḍāśe
prakṛtivatkāryavighātaḥ śakyate vak‍tum</q> । asyārthaḥ---prākṛtānāṃ prayājādīnāṃ
paś‍varthaṃmanuṣṭhitānāṃ puroḍāśe prakṛtivatkāryavighāto na śakyate vak‍tuṃ ye prayājādayaḥ
﻿<pb n="406"/>
prakṛtāḥ tadabhiprāyeṇāpi prasaṅgo bhavatyeveti kiṃ padārthāntaranirākaraṇaprayat‍neneti
bhāvaḥ ।</p>
<p>pariharati---<q>satyamāha bhavān kintvatra guṇavikārastantramityuktam ।
tatsiddha‍yarthaṃ prayājādīnāṃ svarūpavat kāryamapi nānyadbhavitumarhati prāpti-
siddha‍yartho'yaṃ yat‍naḥ</q> ।</p>
<p>asyārthaḥ---yadyapi padārthāntaratvepi pṛṣadājyenānūyājān yajatītyevamādīnāṃ
prasaṅgaścintayituṃ śakyate tathāpi bhāṣyakāreṇāpi tu guṇavikārastantramityuktam । guṇena
pṛṣattādinā anūyājādīnāṃ vikāro yasmin aṅgāvāntaropakāre sa guṇavikārastantra-
mityuk‍tam tasya tantratvasiddha‍yartham । kena hetunā tatsiddha‍yarthatvaṃ ityāha---<q>svarūpavat
kāryamapi nānyadbhavitumarhati iti</q> । yathā svarūpaṃ padārthasya tadevetyekarūpatayā
kāryasya tantratāṃ sādhayituṃ prāptisiddha‍yartho anuyājādiprāptipratipādanārtho'yaṃ bhāṣya-
kārasya padārthāntaranirākaraṇe yat‍naḥ । kathaṃ punaḥ prāptisiddha‍yā kāryaikyasiddhirityatrāha
---<q>kāryaviśeṣe hi prāptiḥ yadā prakṛtivikṛtyoḥ । aṅgakāryāviśeṣo
bhavati tadā'stu tāvadaṅgānāṃ prāptirbhavati vikṛtibhūtaśca paśuḥ</q> ।</p>
<p>etāvatyeva mātṛkā ।।</p>
